ye triṣaptāḥ pariyanti viśvā rūpāṇi bibhrataḥ |
vācas patir balā teṣāṃ tanvo adya dadhātu me ||1||

punar ehi vacas pate devena manasā saha |
vasoṣ pate ni ramaya mayy evāstu mayi śrutam ||2||

ihaivābhi vi tanūbhe ārtnī iva jyayā |
vācas patir ni yachatu mayy evāstu mayi śrutam ||3||

upahūto vācas patir upāsmān vācaspatir hvayatām |
saṃ śrutena gamemahi mā śrutena vi rādhiṣi ||4||



vidmā śarasya pitaraṃ parjanyaṃ bhūridhāyasam |
vidmo ṣv asya mātaraṃ pṛthivīṃ bhūrivarpasam ||1||

jyāke pari ṇo namāśmānaṃ tanvaṃ kṛdhi |
vīḍur varīyo 'rātīr apa dveṣāṃsy ā kṛdhi ||2||

vṛkṣaṃ yad gāvaḥ pariṣasvajānā anusphuraṃ śaraṃ arcanty ṛbhum |
śarum asmad yāvaya didyum indra ||3||

yathā dyāṃ ca pṛthivīṃ cāntas tiṣṭhati tejanam |
evā rogaṃ cāsrāvaṃ cāntas tiṣṭhatu muñja it ||4||



vidmā śarasya pitaraṃ parjanyaṃ śatavṛṣṇyaṃ |
tenā te tanve śaṃ karaṃ pṛthivyāṃ te niṣecanaṃ bahiṣ ṭe astu bāl iti ||1||

vidmā śarasya pitaraṃ mitraṃ śatavṛṣṇyaṃ |
tenā te tanve śaṃ karaṃ pṛthivyāṃ te niṣecanaṃ bahiṣ ṭe astu bāl iti ||2||

vidmā śarasya pitaraṃ varuṇaṃ śatavṛṣṇyaṃ |
tenā te tanve śaṃ karaṃ pṛthivyāṃ te niṣecanaṃ bahiṣ ṭe astu bāl iti ||3||

vidmā śarasya pitaraṃ candraṃ śatavṛṣṇyaṃ |
tenā te tanve śaṃ karaṃ pṛthivyāṃ te niṣecanaṃ bahiṣ ṭe astu bāl iti ||4||

vidmā śarasya pitaraṃ sūryaṃ śatavṛṣṇyaṃ |
tenā te tanve śaṃ karaṃ pṛthivyāṃ te niṣecanaṃ bahiṣ ṭe astu bāl iti ||5||

yad āntreṣu gavīnyor yad vastāv adhi saṃśritam |
evā te mūtraṃ mucyatāṃ bahir bāl iti sarvakam ||6||

pra te bhinadmi mehanaṃ vartraṃ veśantyā iva |
evā te mūtraṃ mucyatāṃ bahir bāl iti sarvakam ||7||

viṣitaṃ te vastibilaṃ samudrasyodadher iva |
evā te mūtraṃ mucyatāṃ bahir bāl iti sarvakam ||8||

yatheṣukā parāpatad avasṛṣṭādhi dhanvanaḥ |
evā te mūtraṃ mucyatāṃ bahir bāl iti sarvakam ||9||



ambayo yanty adhvabhir jāmayo adhvarīyatām |
pṛñcatīr madhunā payaḥ ||1||

amūr yā upa sūrye yābhir vā sūryaḥ saha |
tā no hinvantv adhvaram ||2||

apo devīr upa hvaye yatra gāvaḥ pibanti naḥ |
sindhubhyaḥ kartvaṃ haviḥ ||3||

apsv antar amṛtam apsu bheṣajam |
apām uta praśastibhir aśvā bhavatha vājino gāvo bhavatha vājinīḥ ||4||



āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuvas tā na ūrje dadhātana |
mahe raṇāya cakṣase ||1||

yo vaḥ śivatamo rasas tasya bhājayateha naḥ |
uśatīr iva mātaraḥ ||2||

tasmā araṃ gamāma vo yasya kṣayāya jinvatha |
āpo janayathā ca naḥ ||3||

īśānā vāryāṇāṃ kṣayantīś carṣaṇīnām |
apo yācāmi bheṣajam ||4||



śaṃ no devīr abhiṣṭaya āpo bhavantu pītaye |
śaṃ yor abhi sravantu naḥ ||1||

apsu me somo abravīd antar viśvāni bheṣajā |
agniṃ ca viśvaśaṃbhuvam ||2||

āpaḥ pṛṇīta bheṣajaṃ varūthaṃ tanve mama |
jyok ca sūryaṃ dṛśe ||3||

śaṃ na āpo dhanvanyāḥ śam u santv anūpyāḥ |
śaṃ naḥ khanitrimā āpaḥ śam u yāḥ kumbha ābhṛtāḥ |
śivā naḥ santu vārṣikīḥ ||4||



stuvānam agna ā vaha yātudhānaṃ kimīdinam |
tvaṃ hi deva vandito hantā dasyor babhūvitha ||1||

ājyasya parameṣṭhin jātavedas tanūvaśin |
agne taulasya prāśāna yātudhānān vi lāpaya ||2||

vi lapantu yātudhānā attriṇo ye kimīdinaḥ |
athedam agne no havir indraś ca prati haryatam ||3||

agniḥ pūrva ā rabhatāṃ prendro nudatu bāhumān |
bravītu sarvo yātumān ayam asmīty etya ||4||

paśyāma te vīryaṃ jātavedaḥ pra ṇo brūhi yātudhānān nṛcakṣaḥ |
tvayā sarve paritaptāḥ purastāt ta ā yantu prabruvāṇā upedam ||5||

ā rabhasva jātavedo 'smākārthāya jajñiṣe |
dūto no agne bhūtvā yātudhānān vi lāpaya ||6||

tvam agne yātudhānān upabaddhāṃ ihā vaha |
athaiṣām indro vajreṇāpi śīrṣāṇi vṛścatu ||7||



idaṃ havir yātudhānān nādī phenam ivā vahat |
ya idaṃ strī pumān akar iha sa stuvatāṃ janaḥ ||1||

ayaṃ stuvāna āgamad imaṃ sma prati haryata |
bṛhaspate vaśe labdhvāgnīṣomā vi vidhyatam ||2||

yātudhānasya somapa jahi prajāṃ nayasva ca |
ni stuvānasya pātaya param akṣy utāvaram ||3||

yatraiṣām agne janimāni vettha guhā satām attriṇāṃ jātavedaḥ |
tāṃs tvaṃ brahmaṇā vāvṛdhāno jahy eṣāṃ śatatarham agne ||4||



asmin vasu vasavo dhārayantv indraḥ pūṣā varuṇo mitro agniḥ |
imam ādityā uta viśve ca devā uttarasmin jyotiṣi dhārayantu ||1||

asya devāḥ pradiśi jyotir astu sūryo agnir uta vā hiraṇyam |
sapatnā asmad adhare bhavantūttamaṃ nākam adhi rohayemam ||2||

yenendrāya samabharaḥ payāṃsy uttamena brahmaṇā jātavedaḥ |
tena tvam agna iha vardhayemaṃ sajātānāṃ śraiṣṭhya ā dhehy enam ||3||

aiṣāṃ yajñam uta varco dade 'haṃ rāyas poṣam uta cittāny agne |
sapatnā asmad adhare bhavantūttamaṃ nākam adhi rohayemam ||4||



ayaṃ devānām asuro vi rājati vaśā hi satyā varuṇasya rājñaḥ |
tatas pari brahmaṇā śāśadāna ugrasya manyor ud imaṃ nayāmi ||1||

namas te rajan varuṇāstu manyave viśvaṃ hy ugra nicikeṣi drugdham |
sahasram anyān pra suvāmi sākaṃ śataṃ jīvāti śaradas tavāyam ||2||

yad uvakthānṛtam jihvayā vṛjinaṃ bahu |
rājñas tvā satyadharmaṇo muñcāmi varuṇād aham ||3||

muñcāmi tvā vaiśvānarād arṇavān mahatas pari |
sajātān ugrehā vada brahma cāpa cikīhi naḥ ||4||



vaṣaṭ te pūṣann asmint sūtāv aryamā hotā kṛṇotu vedhāḥ |
sisratāṃ nāry ṛtaprajātā vi parvāṇi jihatāṃ sūtavā u ||1||

catasro divaḥ pradiśaś catasro bhūmyā uta |
devā garbhaṃ sam airayan taṃ vy ūrṇuvantu sūtave ||2||

sūṣā vy ūrṇotu vi yoniṃ hāpayāmasi |
śrathayā sūṣaṇe tvam ava tvaṃ biṣkale sṛja ||3||

neva māṃse na pīvasi neva majjasv āhatam |
avaitu pṛśni śevalaṃ śune jarāyv attave 'va jarāyu padyatām ||4||

vi te bhinadmi mehanaṃ vi yoniṃ vi gavīnike |
vi mātaraṃ ca putraṃ ca vi kumāraṃ jarāyuṇāva jarāyu padyatām ||5||

yathā vāto yathā mano yathā patanti pakṣiṇaḥ |
evā tvaṃ daśamāsya sākaṃ jarāyuṇā patāva jarāyu padyatām ||6||



jarāyujaḥ prathama usriyo vṛṣā vātābhrajā stanayann eti vṛṣṭyā |
sa no mṛḍāti tanva ṛjugo rujan ya ekam ojas tredhā vicakrame ||1||

aṅgeaṅge śociṣā śiśriyāṇaṃ namasyantas tvā haviṣā vidhema |
aṅkānt samaṅkān haviṣā vidhema yo agrabhīt parvāsyā grabhītā ||2||

muñca śīrṣaktyā uta kāsa enaṃ paruṣparur āviveśā yo asya |
yo abhrajā vātajā yaś ca śuṣmo vanaspatīnt sacatāṃ parvatāṃś ca ||3||

śaṃ me parasmai gātrāya śam astv avarāya me |
śaṃ me caturbhyo aṅgebhyaḥ śam astu tanve mama ||4||



namas te astu vidyute namas te stanayitnave |
namas te astv aśmane yenā dūḍāśe asyasi ||1||

namas te pravato napād yatas tapaḥ samūhasi |
mṛḍayā nas tanūbhyo mayas tokebhyas kṛdhi ||2||

pravato napān nama evāstu tubhyaṃ namas te hetaye tapuṣe ca kṛṇmaḥ |
vidma te dhāma paramaṃ guhā yat samudre antar nihitāsi nābhiḥ ||3||

yāṃ tvā devā asṛjanta viśva iṣuṃ kṛṇvānā asanāya dhṛṣṇum |
sā no mṛḍa vidathe gṛṇānā tasyai te namo astu devi ||4||



bhagam asyā varca ādiṣy adhi vṛkṣād iva srajam |
mahābudhna iva parvato jyok pitṛṣv āstām ||1||

eṣā te rājan kanyā vadhūr ni dhūyatām yama |
sā mātur badhyatāṃ gṛhe 'tho bhrātur atho pituḥ ||2||

eṣā te kulapā rājan tām u te pari dadmasi |
jyok pitṛṣv āsātā ā śīrṣṇaḥ śamopyāt ||3||

asitasya te brahmaṇā kaśyapasya gayasya ca |
antaḥkośam iva jāmayo 'pi nahyāmi te bhagam ||4 ||



saṃ saṃ sravantu sindhavaḥ saṃ vātāḥ saṃ patatriṇaḥ |
imaṃ yajñaṃ pradivo me juṣantāṃ saṃsrāvyeṇa haviṣā juhomi ||1||

ihaiva havam ā yāta ma iha saṃsrāvaṇā utemaṃ vardhayatā giraḥ |
ihaitu sarvo yaḥ paśur asmin tiṣṭhatu yā rayiḥ ||2||

ye nadīnāṃ saṃsravanty utsāsaḥ sadam akṣitāḥ |
tebhir me sarvaiḥ saṃsrāvair dhanaṃ saṃ srāvayāmasi ||3||

ye sarpiṣaḥ saṃsravanti kṣīrasya codakasya ca
tebhir me sarvaiḥ saṃsrāvair dhanaṃ saṃ srāvayāmasi ||4||
ye 'māvāsyāṃ rātrim udasthur vrājam attriṇaḥ |
agnis turīyo yātuhā so asmabhyam adhi bravat ||1||

sīsāyādhy āha varuṇaḥ sīsāyāgnir upāvati |
sīsaṃ ma indraḥ prāyachat tad aṅga yātucātanam ||2||

idaṃ viṣkandhaṃ sahata idaṃ bādhate attriṇaḥ |
anena viśvā sasahe yā jātāni piśācyāḥ ||3||

yadi no gāṃ haṃsi yady aśvaṃ yadi pūruṣam |
taṃ tvā sīsena vidhyāmo yathā no 'so avīrahā ||4||



amūr yā yanti yoṣito hirā lohitavāsasaḥ |
abhrātara iva jāmayas tiṣṭhantu hatavarcasaḥ ||1||

tiṣṭhāvare tiṣṭha para uta tvaṃ tiṣṭha madhyame |
kaniṣṭhikā ca tiṣṭhati tiṣṭhād id dhamanir mahī ||2||

śatasya dhamanīnāṃ sahasrasya hirāṇām |
asthur in madhyamā imāḥ sākam antā araṃsata ||3||

pari vaḥ sikatāvatī dhanūr bṛhaty akramīt |
tiṣṭhatelayatā su kam ||4||



nir lakṣmyaṃ lalāmyaṃ nir arātiṃ suvāmasi |
atha yā bhadrā tāni naḥ prajāyā arātiṃ nayāmasi ||1||

nir araṇiṃ savitā sāviṣak pador nir hastayor varuṇo mitro aryamā |
nir asmabhyam anumatī rarāṇā premāṃ devā asāviṣuḥ saubhagāya ||2||

yat ta ātmani tanvāṃ ghoram asti yad vā keśeṣu praticakṣaṇe vā |
sarvaṃ tad vācāpa hanmo vayaṃ devas tvā savitā sūdayatu ||3||

riśyapadīṃ vṛṣadatīṃ goṣedhāṃ vidhamām uta |
vilīḍhyaṃ lalāmyaṃ tā asman nāśayāmasi ||4||


mā no vidan vivyādhino mo abhivyādhino vidan |
ārāc charavyā asmad viṣūcīr indra pātaya ||1||

viṣvañco asmac charavaḥ patantu ye astā ye cāsyāḥ |
daivīr manuṣyesavo mamāmitrān vi vidhyata ||2||

yo naḥ svo yo araṇaḥ sajāta uta niṣṭyo yo asmāṃ abhidāsati |
rudraḥ śaravyayaitān mamāmitrān vi vidhyatu ||3||

yaḥ sapatno yo 'sapatno yaś ca dviṣan chapāti naḥ |
devās taṃ sarve dhūrvantu brahma varma mamāntaram ||4||



adārasṛd bhavatu deva somāsmin yajñe maruto mṛḍatā naḥ |
mā no vidad abhibhā mo aśastir mā no vidad vṛjinā dveṣyā yā ||1||

yo adya senyo vadho 'ghāyūnām udīrate |
yuvaṃ taṃ mitrāvaruṇāv asmad yāvayataṃ pari ||2||

itaś ca yad amutaś ca yad vadhaṃ varuṇa yāvaya |
vi mahac charma yacha varīyo yāvayā vadham ||3||

śāsa itthā mahāṃ asy amitrasāho astṛtaḥ |
na yasya hanyate sakhā na jīyate kadā cana ||4||



svastidā viśāṃ patir vṛtrahā vimṛdho vaśī |
vṛṣendraḥ pura etu naḥ somapā abhayaṃkaraḥ ||1||

vi na indra mṛdho jahi nīcā yacha pṛtanyataḥ |
adhamaṃ gamayā tamo yo asmāṃ abhidāsati ||2||

vi rakṣo vi mṛdho jahi vi vṛtrasya hanū ruja |
vi manyum indra vṛtrahann amitrasyābhidāsataḥ ||3||

apendra dviṣato mano 'pa jijyāsato vadham |
vi mahac charma yacha varīyo yāvayā vadham ||4||



anu sūryam ud ayatāṃ hṛddyoto harimā ca te |
go rohitasya varṇena tena tvā pari dadhmasi ||1||

pari tvā rohitair varṇair dīrghāyutvāya dadhmasi |
yathāyam arapā asad atho aharito bhuvat ||2||

yā rohiṇīr devatyā gāvo yā uta rohiṇīḥ |
rūpaṃrūpaṃ vayovayas tābhiṣ ṭvā pari dadhmasi ||3||

śukeṣu te harimāṇaṃ ropaṇākāsu dadhmasi |
atho hāridraveṣu te harimāṇaṃ ni dadhmasi ||4||



naktaṃjātāsi oṣadhe rāme kṛṣṇe asikni ca |
idaṃ rajani rajaya kilāsaṃ palitaṃ ca yat ||1||

kilāsaṃ ca palitaṃ ca nir ito nāśayā pṛṣat |
ā tvā svo viśatāṃ varṇaḥ parā śuklāni pātaya ||2||

asitaṃ te pralayanam āsthānam asitaṃ tava |
asiknī asy oṣadhe nir ito nāśayā pṛṣat ||3||

asthijasya kilāsasya tanūjasya ca yat tvaci |
dūṣyā kṛtasya brahmaṇā lakṣma śvetam anīnaśam ||4||


suparṇo jātaḥ prathamas tasya tvaṃ pittam āsitha |
tad āsurī yudhā jitā rūpaṃ cakre vanaspatīn ||1||
āsurī cakre prathamedaṃ kilāsabheṣajam idaṃ kilāsanāśanam |
anīnaśat kilāsaṃ sarūpām akarat tvacam ||2||

sarūpā nāma te mātā sarūpo nāma te pitā |
sarūpakṛt tvam oṣadhe sā sarūpam idaṃ kṛdhi ||3||

śyāmā sarūpaṃkaraṇī pṛthivyā adhy udbhṛtā |
idam ū ṣu pra sādhaya punā rūpāṇi kalpaya ||4||



yad agnir āpo adahat praviśya yatrākṛṇvan dharmadhṛto namāṃsi |
tatra ta āhuḥ paramaṃ janitraṃ sa naḥ saṃvidvān pari vṛṅgdhi takman ||1||

yady arcir yadi vāsi śociḥ śakalyeṣi yadi vā te janitram |
hrūḍur nāmāsi haritasya deva sa naḥ saṃvidvān pari vṛṅgdhi takman ||2||

yadi śoko yadi vābhiśoko yadi vā rājño varuṇasyāsi putraḥ |
hrūḍur nāmāsi haritasya deva sa naḥ saṃvidvān pari vṛṅgdhi takman ||3||

namaḥ śītāya takmane namo rūrāya śociṣe kṛṇomi |
yo anyedyur ubhayadyur abhyeti tṛtīyakāya namo astu takmane ||4||



āre 'sāv asmad astu hetir devāso asat |
āre aśmā yam asyatha ||1||

sakhāsāv asmabhyam astu rātiḥ sakhendro bhagaḥ |
savitā citrarādhāḥ ||2||

yūyam naḥ pravato napān marutaḥ sūryatvacasaḥ |
śarma yachatha saprathāḥ ||3||

suṣūdata mṛḍata mṛḍayā nas tanūbhyo |
mayas tokebhyas kṛdhi ||4||



amūḥ pāre pṛdākvas triṣaptā nirjarāyavaḥ |
tāsām jarāyubhir vayam akṣyāv api vyayāmasy aghāyoḥ paripanthinaḥ ||1||

viṣūcy etu kṛntatī pinākam iva bibhratī |
viṣvak punarbhuvā mano 'samṛddhā aghāyavaḥ ||2||

na bahavaḥ sam aśakan nārbhakā abhi dādhṛṣuḥ |
veṇor adgā ivābhito 'samṛddhā aghāyavaḥ ||3||

pretaṃ pādau pra sphurataṃ vahataṃ pṛṇato gṛhān |
indrāny etu prathamājītāmuṣitā puraḥ ||4||


upa prāgād devo agnī rakṣohāmīvacātanaḥ |
dahann apa dvayāvino yātudhānān kimīdinaḥ ||1||

prati daha yātudhānān prati deva kimīdinaḥ |
pratīcīḥ kṛṣṇavartane saṃ daha yātudhānyaḥ ||2||

yā śaśāpa śapanena yāghaṃ mūram ādadhe |
yā rasasya haraṇāya jātam ārebhe tokam attu sā ||3||

putram attu yātudhānīḥ svasāram uta naptyam |
adhā mitho vikeśyo vi ghnatāṃ yātudhānyo vi tṛhyantām arāyyaḥ ||4||



abhīvartena maṇinā yenendro abhivavṛdhe |
tenāsmān brahmaṇas pate 'bhi rāṣṭrāya vardhaya ||1||

abhivṛtya sapatnān abhi yā no arātayaḥ |
abhi pṛtanyantaṃ tiṣṭhābhi yo no durasyati ||2||

abhi tvā devaḥ savitābhi ṣomo avīvṛdhat |
abhi tvā viśvā bhūtāny abhīvarto yathāsasi ||3||

abhīvarto abhibhavaḥ sapatnakṣayaṇo maṇiḥ |
rāṣṭrāya mahyaṃ badhyatāṃ sapatnebhyaḥ parābhuve ||4||

ud asau sūryo agād ud idaṃ māmakaṃ vacaḥ |
yathāhaṃ śatruho 'sāny asapatnaḥ sapatnahā ||5||

sapatnakṣayaṇo vṛṣābhiraṣṭro viṣāsahiḥ |
yathāham eṣāṃ vīrāṇāṃ virājāni janasya ca ||6||



viśve devā vasavo rakṣatemam utādityā jāgṛta yūyam asmin |
memaṃ sanābhir uta vānyanābhir memaṃ prāpat pauruṣeyo vadho yaḥ ||1||

ye vo devāḥ pitaro ye ca putrāḥ sacetaso me śṛṇutedam uktam |
sarvebhyo vaḥ pari dadāmy etaṃ svasty enaṃ jarase vahātha ||2||

ye devā divi ṣṭha ye pṛthivyāṃ ye antarikṣa oṣadhīṣu paśuṣv apsv antaḥ |
te kṛṇuta jarasam āyur asmai śatam anyān pari vṛṇaktu mṛtyūn ||3||

yeṣāṃ prayājā uta vānuyājā hutabhāgā ahutādaś ca devāḥ |
yeṣāṃ vaḥ pañca pradiśo vibhaktās tān vo asmai satrasadaḥ kṛṇomi ||4||



āśānām āśāpālebhyaś caturbhyo amṛtebhyaḥ |
idaṃ bhūtasyādhyakṣebhyo vidhema haviṣā vayam ||1||

ya āśānām āśāpālāś catvāra sthana devāḥ |
te no nirṛtyāḥ pāśebhyo muñcatāṃhasoaṃhasaḥ ||2||

asrāmas tvā haviṣā yajāmy aśloṇas tvā ghṛtena juhomi |
ya āśānām āśāpālas turīyo devaḥ sa naḥ subhūtam eha vakṣat ||3||

svasti mātra uta pitre no astu svasti gobhyo jagate puruṣebhyaḥ |
viśvam subhūtam suvidatraṃ no astu jyog eva dṛśema sūryam ||4||


idaṃ janāso vidatha mahad brahma vadiṣyati |
na tat pṛthivyāṃ no divi yena prāṇanti vīrudhaḥ ||1||

antarikṣa āsāṃ sthāma śrāntasadām iva |
āsthānam asya bhūtasya viduṣ ṭad vedhaso na vā ||2||

yad rodasī rejamāne bhūmiś ca niratakṣatam |
ārdraṃ tad adya sarvadā samudrasyeva śrotyāḥ ||3||

viśvam anyām abhīvāra tad anyasyām adhi śritam |
dive ca viśvavedase pṛthivyai cākaraṃ namaḥ ||4||



hiraṇyavarṇāḥ śucayaḥ pāvakā yāsu jātaḥ savitā yāsv agniḥ |
yā agniṃ garbhaṃ dadhire suvarṇās tā na āpaḥ śaṃ syonā bhavantu ||1||

yāsāṃ rājā varuṇo yāti madhye satyānṛte avapaśyan janānām |
yā agniṃ garbhaṃ dadhire suvarṇās tā na āpaḥ śaṃ syonā bhavantu ||2||

yāsāṃ devā divi kṛṇvanti bhakṣaṃ yā antarikṣe bahudhā bhavanti |
yā agniṃ garbhaṃ dadhire suvarṇās tā na āpaḥ śaṃ syonā bhavantu ||3||

śivena mā cakṣuṣā paśyatāpaḥ śivayā tanvopa spṛśata tvacaṃ me |
ghṛtaścutaḥ śucayo yāḥ pāvakās tā na āpaḥ śaṃ syonā bhavantu ||4||



iyaṃ vīrun madhujātā madhunā tvā khanāmasi |
madhor adhi prajātāsi sā no madhumatas kṛdhi ||1||

jihvāyā agre madhu me jihvāmūle madhūlakam |
mamed aha kratāv aso mama cittam upāyasi ||2||

madhuman me nikramaṇaṃ madhuman me parāyaṇam |
vācā vadāmi madhumad bhūyāsaṃ madhusaṃdṛśaḥ ||3||
madhor asmi madhutaro madughān madhumattaraḥ |
mām it kila tvaṃ vanāḥ śākhāṃ madhumatīm iva ||4||

pari tvā paritatnunekṣuṇāgām avidviṣe |
yathā māṃ kaminy aso yathā man nāpagā asaḥ ||5||

yad ābadhnan dākṣāyaṇā hiraṇyaṃ śatānīkāya sumanasyamānāḥ |
tat te badnāmy āyuṣe varcase balāya dīrghāyutvāya śataśāradāya ||1||

nainaṃ rakṣāṃsi na piśācāḥ sahante devānām ojaḥ prathamajam hy etat |
yo bibharti dākṣāyaṇaṃ hiraṇyaṃ sa jīveṣu kṛṇute dīrgham āyuḥ ||2||

apāṃ tejo jyotir ojo balaṃ ca vanaspatīnām uta vīryāṇi |
indra ivendriyāṇy adhi dhārayāmo asmin tad dakṣamāṇo bibharad dhiraṇyam ||3||

samānāṃ māsām ṛtubhiṣ ṭvā vayaṃ saṃvatsarasya payasā piparmi |
indrāgnī viśve devās te 'nu manyantām ahṛṇīyamānāḥ ||4||



venas tat paśyat paramaṃ guhā yad yatra viśvaṃ bhavaty ekarūpam |
idaṃ pṛśnir aduhaj jāyamānāḥ svarvido abhy anūṣata vrāḥ ||1||

pra tad voced amṛtasya vidvān gandharvo dhāma paramaṃ guhā yat |
trīṇi padāni nihitā guhāsya yas tāni veda sa pituṣ pitāsat ||2||

sa naḥ pitā janitā sa uta bandhur dhāmāni veda bhuvanāni viśvā |
yo devānāṃ nāmadha eka eva taṃ saṃpraśnaṃ bhuvanā yanti sarvā ||3||

pari dyāvāpṛthivī sadya āyam upātiṣṭhe prathamajām ṛtasya |
vācam iva vaktari bhuvaneṣṭhā dhāsyur eṣa nanv eṣo agniḥ ||4||

pari viśvā bhuvanāny āyam ṛtasya tantuṃ vitataṃ dṛśe kam |
yatra devā amṛtam ānaśānāḥ samāne yonāv adhy airayanta ||5||



divyo gandharvo bhuvanasya yas patir eka eva namasyo vikṣv īḍyaḥ |
taṃ tvā yaumi brahmaṇā divya deva namas te astu divi te sadhastham ||1||

divi spṛṣṭo yajataḥ sūryatvag avayātā haraso daivyasya |
mṛḍāt gandharvo bhuvanasya yas patir eka eva namasyaḥ suśevāḥ ||2||

anavadyābhiḥ sam u jagma ābhir apsarāsv api gandharva āsīt |
samudra āsāṃ sadanaṃ ma āhur yataḥ sadya ā ca parā ca yanti ||3||

abhriye didyun nakṣatriye yā viśvāvasuṃ gandharvaṃ sacadhve |
tābhyo vo devīr nama it kṛṇomi ||4||

yāḥ klandās tamiṣīcayo 'kṣakāmā manomuhaḥ |
tābhyo gandharvabhyo 'psarābhyo 'karam namaḥ ||5||



ado yad avadhāvaty avatkam adhi parvatāt |
tat te kṛṇomi bheṣajaṃ subheṣajaṃ yathāsasi ||1||

ād aṅgā kuvid aṅga śataṃ yā bheṣajāni te |
teṣām asi tvam uttamam anāsrāvam arogaṇam ||2||

nīcaiḥ khananty asurā arusrāṇam idaṃ mahat |
tad āsrāvasya bheṣajaṃ tad u rogam anīnaśat ||3||

upajīkā ud bharanti samudrād adhi bheṣajam |
tad āsrāvasya bheṣajaṃ tad u rogam aśīśamat ||4||

arusrāṇam idaṃ mahat pṛthivyā adhy udbhṛtam |
tad āsrāvasya bheṣajaṃ tad u rogam anīnaśat ||5||

śaṃ no bhavantv apa oṣadhayaḥ śivāḥ |
indrasya vajro apa hantu rakṣasa ārād visṛṣṭā iṣavaḥ patantu rakṣasām ||6||



dīrghāyutvāya bṛhate raṇāyāriṣyanto dakṣamāṇāḥ sadaiva |
maṇiṃ viṣkandhadūṣaṇaṃ jaṅgiḍaṃ bibhṛmo vayam ||1||

jaṅgiḍo jambhād viśarād viṣkandhād abhiśocanāt |
maṇiḥ sahasravīryaḥ pari ṇaḥ pātu viśvataḥ ||2||

ayaṃ viṣkandhaṃ sahate 'yaṃ bādhate attriṇaḥ |
ayaṃ no viśvabheṣajo jaṅgiḍaḥ pātv aṃhasaḥ ||3||

devair dattena maṇinā jaṅgiḍena mayobhuvā |
viṣkandhaṃ sarvā rakṣāṃsi vyāyāme sahāmahe ||4||

śaṇaś ca mā jaṅgiḍaś ca viṣkandhād abhi rakṣatām |
araṇyād anya ābhṛtaḥ kṛṣyā anyo rasebhyaḥ ||5||

kṛtyādūṣir ayaṃ maṇir atho arātidūṣiḥ |
atho sahasvān jaṅgiḍaḥ pra ṇa āyuṃṣi tāriṣat ||6||



indra juṣasva pra vahā yāhi śūra haribhyām |
pibā sutasya mater iha madhoś cakānaś cārur madāya ||1||

indra jaṭharaṃ navyo na pṛṇasva madhor divo na |
asya sutasya svar ṇopa tvā madāḥ suvāco aguḥ ||2||

indras turāṣāṇ mitro vṛtraṃ yo jaghāna yatīr na |
bibheda valaṃ bhṛgur na sasahe śatrūn made somasya ||3||

ā tvā viśantu sutāsa indra pṛṇasva kukṣī viḍḍhi śakra dhiyehy ā naḥ |
śrudhī havaṃ giro me juṣasvendra svayugbhir matsveha mahe raṇāya ||4||

indrasya nu pra vocaṃ vīryāṇi yāni cakāra prathamāni vajrī |
ahann ahim anu apas tatarda pra vakṣaṇā abhinat parvatānām ||5||

ahann ahiṃ parvate śiśriyāṇaṃ tvaṣṭāsmai vajraṃ svaryaṃ tatakṣa |
vāśrā iva dhenavaḥ syandamānā añjaḥ samudram ava jagmur āpaḥ ||6||

vṛṣāyamāṇo avṛṇīta somaṃ trikadrukeṣu apibat sutasya |
ā sāyakaṃ maghavādatta vajram ahann enaṃ prathamajām ahīnām ||7||



samās tvāgna ṛtavo vardhayantu saṃvatsarā ṛṣayo yāni satyā |
saṃ divyena dīdihi rocanena viśvā ā māhi pradiśaś catasraḥ ||1||

saṃ cedhyasvāgne pra ca vardhayemam uc ca tiṣṭha mahate saubhagāya |
mā te riṣann upasattāro agne brahmāṇas te yaśasaḥ santu mānye ||2||

tvām agne vṛṇate brāhmaṇā ime śivo agne saṃvaraṇe bhavā naḥ |
sapatnahāgne abhimātijid bhava sve gaye jāgṛhy aprayuchan ||3||

kṣatreṇāgne svena saṃ rabhasva mitreṇāgne mitradhā yatasva |
sajātānāṃ madhyameṣṭhā rājñām agne vihavyo dīdihīha ||4||

ati niho ati sṛdho 'ty acittīr ati dviṣaḥ |
viśvā hy agne duritā tara tvam athāsmabhyaṃ sahavīraṃ rayiṃ dāḥ ||5||



aghadviṣṭā devajātā vīruc chapathayopanī |
āpo malam iva prāṇaikṣīt sarvān mac chapathāṃ adhi ||1||

yaś ca sāpatnaḥ śapatho jāmyāḥ śapathaś ca yaḥ |
brahmā yan manyutaḥ śapāt sarvaṃ tan no adhaspadam ||2||

divo mūlam avatataṃ pṛthivyā adhy uttatam |
tena sahasrakāṇḍena pari ṇaḥ pāhi viśvataḥ ||3||

pari māṃ pari me prajāṃ pari ṇaḥ pāhi yad dhanam |
arātir no mā tārīn mā nas tāriśur abhimātayaḥ ||4||

śaptāram etu śapatho yaḥ suhārt tena naḥ saha |
cakṣurmantrasya durhārdaḥ pṛṣṭīr api śṛṇīmasi ||5||


ud agātāṃ bhagavatī vicṛtau nāma tārake |
vi kṣetriyasya muñcatām adhamaṃ pāśam uttamam ||1||

apeyaṃ rātry uchatv apochantv abhikṛtvarīḥ |
vīrut kṣetriyanāśany apa kṣetriyam uchatu ||2||

babhror arjunakāṇḍasya yavasya te palālyā tilasya tilapiñjyā |
vīrut kṣetriyanāśany apa kṣetriyam uchatu ||3||

namas te lāṅgalebhyo nama īṣāyugebhyaḥ |
vīrut kṣetriyanāśany apa kṣetriyam uchatu ||4||

namaḥ sanisrasākṣebhyo namaḥ saṃdeśyebhyaḥ |
namaḥ kṣetrasya pataye vīrut kṣetriyanāśany apa kṣetriyam uchatu ||5||



daśavṛkṣa muñcemaṃ rakṣaso grāhyā adhi yainaṃ jagrāha parvasu |
atho enam vanaspate jīvānāṃ lokam un naya ||1||

āgād ud agād ayaṃ jīvānāṃ vrātam apy agāt |
abhūd u putrāṇāṃ pitā nṛṇāṃ ca bhagavattamaḥ ||2||

adhītīr adhy agād ayam adhi jīvapurā agān |
śataṃ hy asya bhiṣajaḥ sahasram uta vīrudhaḥ ||3||

devās te cītim avidan brahmāṇa uta vīrudhaḥ |
cītiṃ te viśve devā avidan bhūmyām adhi ||4||

yaś cakāra sa niṣ karat sa eva subhiṣaktamaḥ |
sa eva tubhyaṃ bheṣajāni kṛṇavad bhiṣajā śuciḥ ||5||



kṣetriyāt tvā nirṛtyā jāmiśaṃsād druho muñcāmi varuṇasya pāśāt |
anāgasaṃ brahmaṇā tvā kṛṇomi śive te dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe stām ||1||

śaṃ te agniḥ sahādbhir astu śaṃ somaḥ sahauṣadhībhiḥ |
evāhaṃ tvāṃ kṣetriyān nirṛtyā jāmiśaṃsād druho muñcāmi varuṇasya pāśāt |
anāgasaṃ brahmaṇā tvā kṛṇomi śive te dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe stām ||2||

śam te vāto antarikṣe vayo dhāc chaṃ te bhavantu pradiśaś catasraḥ |
evāhaṃ tvāṃ kṣetriyān nirṛtyā jāmiśaṃsād druho muñcāmi varuṇasya pāśāt |
anāgasaṃ brahmaṇā tvā kṛṇomi śive te dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe stām ||3||

imā yā devīḥ pradiśaś catasro vātapatnīr abhi sūryo vicaṣṭe |
evāhaṃ tvāṃ kṣetriyān nirṛtyā jāmiśaṃsād druho muñcāmi varuṇasya pāśāt |
anāgasaṃ brahmaṇā tvā kṛnomi śive te dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe stām ||4||

tāsu tvāntar jarasy ā dadhāmi pra yakṣma etu nirṛtiḥ parācaiḥ |
evāhaṃ tvāṃ kṣetriyān nirṛtyā jāmiśaṃsād druho muñcāmi varuṇasya pāśāt |
anāgasaṃ brahmaṇā tvā kṛṇomi śive te dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe stām ||5||

amukthā yakṣmād duritād avadyād druhaḥ pāśād grāhyāś cod amukthāḥ |
evāhaṃ tvāṃ kṣetriyān nirṛtyā jāmiśaṃsād druho muñcāmi varuṇasya pāśāt |
anāgasaṃ brahmaṇā tvā kṛṇomi śive te dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe stām ||6||

ahā arātim avidaḥ syonam apy abhūr bhadre sukṛtasya loke |
evāhaṃ tvāṃ kṣetriyān nirṛtyā jāmiśaṃsād druho muñcāmi varuṇasya pāśāt |
anāgasaṃ brahmaṇā tvā kṛṇomi śive te dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe stām ||7||

sūryam ṛtaṃ tamaso grāhyā adhi devā muñcanto asṛjan nir enasaḥ |
evāham tvāṃ kṣetriyān nirṛtyā jāmiśaṃsād druho muñcāmi varuṇasya pāśāt |
anāgasam brahmaṇā tvā kṛṇomi śive te dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe stām ||8||



dūṣyā dūṣir asi hetyā hetir asi menyā menir asi |
āpnuhi śreyāṃsam ati samaṃ krāma ||1||

sraktyo 'si pratisaro 'si pratyabhicaraṇo 'si |
āpnuhi śreyāṃsam ati samaṃ krāma ||2||

prati tam abhi cara yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ |
āpnuhi śreyāṃsam ati samaṃ krāma ||3||
sūrir asi varcodhā asi tanūpāno 'si |
āpnuhi śreyāṃsam ati samaṃ krāma ||4||

śukro 'si bhrājo 'si svar asi jyotir asi |
āpnuhi śreyāṃsam ati samaṃ krāma ||5||



dyāvāpṛthivī urv antarikṣaṃ kṣetrasya patny urugāyo 'dbhutaḥ |
utāntarikṣam uru vātagopaṃ ta iha tapyantāṃ mayi tapyamāne ||1||

idaṃ devāḥ śṛṇuta ye yajñiyā stha bharadvājo mahyam ukthāni śaṃsati |
pāśe sa baddho durite ni yujyatāṃ yo asmākaṃ mana idaṃ hinasti ||2||

idam indra śṛṇuhi somapa yat tvā hṛdā śocatā johavīmi |
vṛścāmi taṃ kuliśeneva vṛkṣaṃ yo asmākaṃ mana idaṃ hinasti ||3||

aśītibhis tisṛbhiḥ sāmagebhir ādityebhir vasubhir aṅgirobhiḥ |
iṣṭāpūrtam avatu naḥ pitṝṇām āmuṃ dade harasā daivyena ||4||

dyāvāpṛthivī anu mā dīdhīthāṃ viśve devāso anu mā rabhadhvam |
aṅgirasaḥ pitaraḥ somyāsaḥ pāpam ā ṛchatv apakāmasya kartā ||5||

atīva yo maruto manyate no brahma vā yo nindiṣat kriyamāṇam |
tapūṃṣi tasmai vṛjināni santu brahmadviṣaṃ dyaur abhisaṃtapāti ||6||

sapta prāṇān aṣṭau manyas tāṃs te vṛścāmi brahmaṇā |
ayā yamasya sādanam agnidūto araṃkṛtaḥ ||7||

ā dadhāmi te padaṃ samiddhe jātavedasi |
agniḥ śarīraṃ veveṣṭv asuṃ vāg api gachatu ||8||



āyurdā agne jarasaṃ vṛṇāno ghṛtapratīko ghṛtapṛṣṭho agne |
ghṛtaṃ pītvā madhu cāru gavyaṃ piteva putrān abhi rakṣatād imam ||1||

pari dhatta dhatta no varcasemam jarāmṛtyuṃ kṛṇuta dīrgham āyuḥ |
bṛhaspatiḥ prāyachad vāsa etat somāya rājñe paridhātavā u ||2||
parīdaṃ vāso adhithāḥ svastaye 'bhūr gṛṣṭīnām abhiśastipā u |
śataṃ ca jīva śaradaḥ purūcī rāyaś ca poṣam upasaṃvyayasva ||3||

ehy aśmānam ā tiṣṭhāśmā bhavatu te tanūḥ |
kṛṇvantu viśve devā āyuṣṭe śaradaḥ śatam ||4||

yasya te vāsaḥ prathamavāsyaṃ harāmas taṃ tvā viśve 'vantu devāḥ |
taṃ tvā bhrātaraḥ suvṛdhā vardhamānam anu jāyantāṃ bahavaḥ sujātam ||5||



niḥsālāṃ dhṛṣṇuṃ dhiṣaṇam ekavādyām jighatsvam |
sarvāś caṇḍasya naptyo nāśayāmaḥ sadānvāḥ ||1||

nir vo goṣṭhād ajāmasi nir akṣān nir upānaśāt |
nir vo magundyā duhitaro gṛhebhyaś cātayāmahe ||2||

asau yo adharād gṛhas tatra santv arāyyaḥ |
tatra sedir ny ucyatu sarvāś ca yātudhānyaḥ ||3||

bhūtapatir nir ajatv indraś cetaḥ sadānvāḥ |
gṛhasya budhna āsīnās tā indro vajreṇādhi tiṣṭhatu ||4||

yadi stha kṣetriyāṇāṃ yadi vā puruṣeṣitāḥ |
yadi stha dasyubhyo jātā naśyatetaḥ sadānvāḥ ||5||

pari dhāmāny āsām āśur gāṣṭhām ivāsaram |
ajaiṣaṃ sarvān ājīn vo naśyatetaḥ sadānvāḥ ||6||



yathā dyauś ca pṛthivī ca na bibhīto na riṣyataḥ |
evā me prāṇa mā bibheḥ ||1||

yathāhaś ca rātrī ca na bibhīto na riṣyataḥ |
evā me prāṇa mā bibheḥ ||2||

yathā sūryaś ca candraś ca na bibhīto na riṣyataḥ |
evā me prāṇa mā bibheḥ ||3||

yathā brahma ca kṣatraṃ ca na bibhīto na riṣyataḥ |
evā me prāṇa mā bibheḥ ||4||

yathā satyaṃ cānṛtaṃ ca na bibhīto na riṣyataḥ |
evā me prāṇa mā bibheḥ ||5||

yathā bhūtaṃ ca bhavyaṃ ca na bibhīto na riṣyataḥ |
evā me prāṇa mā bibheḥ ||6||



prāṇāpānau mṛtyor mā pātaṃ svāhā ||1||

dyāvāpṛthivī upaśrutyā mā pātaṃ svāhā ||2||

sūrya cakṣuṣā mā pāhi svāhā ||3||

agne vaiśvānara viśvair mā devaiḥ pāhi svāhā ||4||

viśvambhara viśvena mā bharasā pāhi svāhā ||5||



ojo 'sy ojo me dāḥ svāhā |1||

saho 'si saho me dāḥ svāhā ||2||

balam asi balaṃ dāḥ svāhā ||3||

āyur asy āyur me dāḥ svāha ||4||

śrotram asi śrotraṃ me dāḥ svāha ||5||

cakṣur asi cakṣur me dāḥ svāha ||6||

paripāṇam asi paripāṇaṃ me dāḥ svāha ||7||



bhrātṛvyakṣayaṇam asi bhrātṛvyacātanaṃ me dāḥ svāha ||1||

sapatnakṣayaṇam asi sapatnacātanaṃ me dāḥ svāha ||2||

arāyakṣayaṇam asy arāyacātanaṃ me dāḥ svāha ||3||

piśācakṣayaṇam asi piśācacātanaṃ me dāḥ svāha ||4||

sadānvākṣayaṇam asi sadānvācātanaṃ me dāḥ svāha ||5||



agne yat te tapas tena taṃ prati tapa yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ||1||

agne yat te haras tena taṃ prati hara yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ||2||

agne yat te 'rcis tena taṃ praty arca yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ||3||

agne yat te śocis tena taṃ prati śoca yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ||4||

agne yat te tejas tena tam atejasaṃ kṛṇu yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ||5||



vāyo yat te tapas tena taṃ prati tapa yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ||1||

vāyo yat te haras tena taṃ prati hara yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ||2||

vāyo yat te 'rcis tena taṃ praty arca yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ||3||

vāyo yat te śocis tena taṃ prati śoca yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ||4||

vāyo yat te tejas tena tam atejasaṃ kṛṇu yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ||5||



sūrya yat te tapas tena taṃ prati tapa yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ||1||

sūrya yat te haras tena taṃ prati hara yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ||2||

sūrya yat te 'rcis tena taṃ praty arca yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ||3||

sūrya yat te śocis tena taṃ prati śoca yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ||4||

sūrya yat te tejas tena tam atejasaṃ kṛṇu yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ||5||



candra yat te tapas tena taṃ prati tapa yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ||1||

candra yat te haras tena taṃ prati hara yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ||2||

candra yat te 'rcis tena taṃ praty arca yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ||3||

candra yat te śocis tena taṃ prati śoca yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ||4||

candra yat te tejas tena tam atejasaṃ kṛṇu yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ||5||



āpo yad vas tapas tena taṃ prati tapata yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ||1||

āpo yad vas haras tena taṃ prati harata yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ||2||

āpo yad vas 'rcis tena taṃ prati arcata yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ||3||

āpo yad vas śocis tena taṃ prati śocata yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ||4||

āpo yad vas tejas tena tam atejasaṃ kṛṇuta yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ||5||



śerabhaka śerabha punar vo yantu yātavaḥ punar hetiḥ kimīdinaḥ |
yasya stha tam atta yo vo prāhait tam atta svā māṃsāny atta ||1||

śevṛdhaka śevṛdha punar vo yantu yātavaḥ punar hetiḥ kimīdinaḥ |
yasya stha tam atta yo vo prāhait tam atta svā māṃsāny atta ||2||

mrokānumroka punar vo yantu yātavaḥ punar hetiḥ kimīdinaḥ |
yasya stha tam atta yo vo prāhait tam atta svā māṃsāny atta ||3||

sarpānusarpa punar vo yantu yātavaḥ punar hetiḥ kimīdinaḥ |
yasya stha tam atta yo vo prāhait tam atta svā māṃsāny atta ||4||

jūrṇi punar vo yantu yātavaḥ punar hetiḥ kimīdinaḥ |
yasya stha tam atta yo vo prāhait tam atta svā māṃsāny atta ||5||

upabde punar vo yantu yātavaḥ punar hetiḥ kimīdinaḥ |
yasya stha tam atta yo vo prāhait tam atta svā māṃsāny atta ||6||

arjuni punar vo yantu yātavaḥ punar hetiḥ kimīdinaḥ |
yasya stha tam atta yo vo prāhait tam atta svā māṃsāny atta ||7||

bharūji punar vo yantu yātavaḥ punar hetiḥ kimīdinaḥ |
yasya stha tam atta yo vo prāhait tam atta svā māṃsāny atta ||8||



śaṃ no devī pṛśniparṇy aśaṃ nirṛtyā akaḥ |
ugrā hi kaṇvajambhanī tām abhakṣi sahasvatīm ||1||

sahamāneyaṃ prathamā pṛśniparṇy ajāyata |
tayāhaṃ durṇāmnāṃ śiro vṛścāmi śakuner iva ||2||

arāyam asṛkpāvānaṃ yaś ca sphātiṃ jihīrṣati |
garbhādaṃ kaṇvaṃ nāśaya pṛśniparṇi sahasva ca ||3||

girim enāṃ ā veśaya kaṇvān jīvitayopanān |
tāṃs tvaṃ devi pṛśniparṇy agnir ivānudahann ihi ||4||

parāca enān pra ṇuda kaṇvān jīvitayopanān |
tamāṃsi yatra gachanti tat kravyādo ajīgamam ||5||


eha yantu paśavo ye pareyur vāyur yeṣāṃ sahacāraṃ jujoṣa |
tvaṣṭā yeṣāṃ rūpadheyāni vedāsmin tān goṣṭhe savitā ni yachatu ||1||

imaṃ goṣṭhaṃ paśavaḥ saṃ sravantu bṛhaspatir ā nayatu prajānan |
sinīvālī nayatv āgram eṣām ājagmuṣo anumate ni yacha ||2||

saṃ saṃ sravantu paśavaḥ sam aśvāḥ sam u pūruṣāḥ |
saṃ dhānyasya yā sphātiḥ saṃsrāvyeṇa haviṣā juhomi ||3||

saṃ siñcāmi gavāṃ kṣīram sam ājyena balam rasam |
saṃsiktā asmākaṃ vīrā dhruvā gāvo mayi gopatau ||4||

ā harāmi gavāṃ kṣīram āhārṣaṃ dhānyaṃ rasam |
āhṛtā asmākaṃ vīrā ā patnīr idam astakam ||5||



nec chatruḥ prāśaṃ jayāti sahamānābhibhūr asi |
prāśaṃ pratiprāśo jahy arasān kṛṇv oṣadhe ||1||

suparṇas tvānv avindat sūkaras tvākhanan nasā |
prāśaṃ pratiprāśo jahy arasān kṛṇv oṣadhe ||2||

indro ha cakre tvā bāhāv asurebhya starītave |
prāśaṃ pratiprāśo jahy arasān kṛṇv oṣadhe ||3||

pāṭām indro vy āśnād asurebhya starītave |
prāśaṃ pratiprāśo jahy arasān kṛṇv oṣadhe ||4||

tayāhaṃ śatrūnt sākṣa indraḥ sālāvṛkāṃ iva |
prāśaṃ pratiprāśo jahy arasān kṛṇv oṣadhe ||5||

rudra jalāṣabheṣaja nīlaśikhaṇḍa karmakṛt |
prāśaṃ pratiprāśo jahy arasān kṛṇv oṣadhe ||6||

tasya prāśaṃ tvaṃ jahi yo na indrābhidāsati |
adhi no brūhi śaktibhiḥ prāśi mām uttaraṃ kṛdhi ||7||



tubhyam eva jariman vardhatām ayam memam anye mṛtyavo hiṃsiṣuḥ śataṃ ye |
māteva putraṃ pramanā upasthe mitra enaṃ mitriyāt pātv aṃhasaḥ ||1||

mitra enaṃ varuṇo vā riśādā jarāmṛtyuṃ kṛṇutāṃ saṃvidānau |
tad agnir hotā vayunāni vidvān viśvā devānāṃ janimā vivakti ||2||

tvam īśiṣe paśūnām pārthivānāṃ ye jātā uta vā ye janitrāḥ |
memaṃ prāṇo hāsīn mo apāno memaṃ mitrā vadhiṣur mo amitrāḥ ||3||

dyauṣ ṭvā pitā pṛthivī mātā jarāmṛtyuṃ kṛṇutāṃ saṃvidāne |
yathā jīvā aditer upasthe prāṇāpānābhyāṃ gupitaḥ śataṃ himāḥ ||4||

imam agne āyuṣe varcase naya priyaṃ reto varuṇa mitra rājan |
mātevāsmā adite śarma yacha viśve devā jaradaṣṭir yathāsat ||5||



pārthivasya rase devā bhagasya tanvo bale |
āyuṣyam asmā agniḥ sūryo varca ā dhād bṛhaspatiḥ ||1||

āyur asmai dhehi jātavedaḥ prajāṃ tvaṣṭar adhinidhehi asmai |
rāyas poṣaṃ savitar ā suvāsmai śataṃ jīvāti śaradas tavāyam ||2||

āśīr ṇa ūrjam uta sauprajāstvaṃ dakṣaṃ dhattaṃ draviṇaṃ sacetasau |
jayam kṣetrāṇi sahasāyam indra kṛṇvāno anyān adharānt sapatnān ||3||

indreṇa datto varuṇena śiṣṭo marudbhir ugraḥ prahito no āgan |
eṣa vāṃ dyāvāpṛthivī upasthe mā kṣudhan mā tṛṣat ||4||

ūrjam asmā ūrjasvatī dhattaṃ payo asmai payasvatī dhattam |
ūrjam asmai dyāvapṛthivī adhātāṃ viśve devā maruta ūrjam āpaḥ ||5||

śivābhiṣ ṭe hṛdayaṃ tarpayāmy anamīvo modiṣīṣṭhāḥ suvarcāḥ |
savāsinau pibatāṃ mantham etam aśvino rūpaṃ paridhāya māyām ||6||

indra etāṃ sasṛje viddho agra ūrjāṃ svadhām ajarāṃ sā ta eṣā |
tayā tvaṃ jīva śaradaḥ suvarcā mā ta ā susrod bhiṣajas te akran ||7||


yathedaṃ bhūmyā adhi tṛṇaṃ vāto mathāyati |
evā mathnāmi te mano yathā māṃ kāminy aso yathā man nāpagā asaḥ ||1||

saṃ cen nayātho aśvinā kāminā saṃ ca vakṣathaḥ |
saṃ vāṃ bhagāso agmata saṃ cittāni sam u vratā ||2||

yat suparṇā vivakṣavo anamīvā vivakṣavaḥ |
tatra me gachatād dhavaṃ śalya iva kulmalaṃ yathā ||3||

yad antaraṃ tad bāhyaṃ yad bāhyaṃ tad antaram |
kanyānāṃ viśvarūpāṇāṃ mano gṛbhāyauṣadhe ||4||

eyam agan patikāmā janikāmo 'ham āgamam |
aśvaḥ kanikradad yathā bhagenāhaṃ sahāgamam ||5||



indrasya yā mahī dṛṣat krimer viśvasya tarhaṇī |
tayā pinaṣmi saṃ krimīn dṛṣadā khalvāṃ iva ||1||

dṛṣṭam adṛṣṭam atṛham atho kurūrum atṛham |
algaṇḍūnt sarvān chalunān krimīn vacasā jambhayāmasi ||2||

algaṇḍūn hanmi mahatā vadhena dūnā adūnā arasā abhūvan |
śiṣṭān aśiṣṭān ni tirāmi vācā yathā krimīṇāṃ nakir uchiṣātai ||3||

anvāntryaṃ śīrṣaṇyam atho pārṣṭeyaṃ krimīn |
avaskavaṃ vyadhvaraṃ krimīn vacasā jambhayāmasi ||4||

ye krimayaḥ parvateśu vaneṣv oṣadhīṣu paśuṣv apsv antaḥ |
ye asmākaṃ tanvam āviviśuḥ sarvaṃ tad dhanmi janima krimīṇām ||5||



udyann ādityaḥ krimīn hantu nimrocan hantu raśmibhiḥ |
ye antaḥ krimayo gavi ||1||

viśvarūpaṃ caturakṣaṃ krimiṃ sāraṅgam arjunam |
śṛṇāmy asya pṛṣṭīr api vṛścāmi yac chiraḥ ||2||

atrivad vaḥ krimayo hanmi kaṇvavaj jamadagnivat |
agastyasya brahmaṇā saṃ pinaṣmy ahaṃ krimīn ||3||

hato rājā krimīṇām utaiṣāṃ sthapatir hataḥ |
hato hatamātā krimir hatabhrātā hatasvasā ||4||

hatāso asya veśaso hatāsaḥ pariveśasaḥ |
atho ye kṣullakā iva sarve te krimayo hatāḥ ||5||

pra te śṛṇāmi śṛṅge yābhyāṃ vitudāyasi |
bhinādmi te kuṣumbhaṃ yas te viṣadhānaḥ ||6||



akṣībhyāṃ te nāsikābhyāṃ karṇābhyāṃ chubukād adhi |
yakṣmaṃ śīrṣaṇyaṃ mastiṣkāj jihvāyā vi vṛhāmi te ||1||

grīvābhyas ta uṣṇihābhyaḥ kīkasābhyo anūkyāt |
yakṣmaṃ doṣaṇyam aṃsābhyāṃ bāhubhyāṃ vi vṛhāmi te ||2||

hṛdayāt te pari klomno halīkṣṇāt pārśvābhyām |
yakṣmaṃ matasnābhyāṃ plīhno yaknas te vi vṛhāmasi ||3||

āntrebhyas te gudābhyo vaniṣṭhor udarād adhi |
yakṣmaṃ kukṣibhyām plāśer nābhyā vi vṛhāmi te ||4||

ūrubhyāṃ te aṣṭhīvadbhyāṃ pārṣṇibhyāṃ prapadābhyām |
yakṣmaṃ bhasadyaṃ śroṇibhyāṃ bhāsadaṃ bhaṃsaso vi vṛhāmi te ||5||

asthibhyas te majjabhyaḥ snāvabhyo dhamanibhyaḥ |
yakṣmam pāṇibhyām aṅgulibhyo nakhebhyo vi vṛhāmi te ||6||

aṅgeaṅge lomnilomni yas te parvaṇiparvaṇi |
yakṣmaṃ tvacasyaṃ te vayaṃ kaśyapasya vībarheṇa viṣvañcaṃ vi vṛhāmasi ||7||



ya īśe paśupatiḥ paśūnām catuṣpadām uta yo dvipadām |
niṣkrītaḥ sa yajñiyaṃ bhāgam etu rāyas poṣā yajamānaṃ sacantām ||1||

pramuñcanto bhuvanasya reto gātuṃ dhatta yajamānāya devāḥ |
upākṛtaṃ śaśamānaṃ yad asthāt priyam devānām apy etu pāthaḥ ||2||

ye badhyamānam anu dīdhyānā anvaikṣanta manasā cakṣuṣā ca |
agniṣ ṭān agre pra mumoktu devo viśvakarmā prajayā saṃrarāṇaḥ ||3||

ye grāmyāḥ paśavo viśvarūpā virūpāḥ santo bahudhaikarūpāḥ |
vāyuṣ ṭān agre pra mumoktu devaḥ prajāpatiḥ prajayā saṃrarāṇaḥ ||4||

prajānantaḥ prati gṛhṇantu pūrve prāṇam aṅgebhyaḥ pary ācarantam |
divaṃ gacha prati tiṣṭhā śarīraiḥ svargaṃ yāhi pathibhir devayānaiḥ ||5||



ye bhakṣayanto na vasūny ānṛdhur yān agnayo anvatapyanta dhiṣṇyāḥ |
yā teṣām avayā duriṣṭiḥ sviṣṭiṃ nas tāṃ kṛṇavad viśvakarmā ||1||

yajñapatim ṛṣayaḥ enasāhur nirbhaktaṃ prajā anutapyamānam |
mathavyānt stokān apa yān rarādha saṃ naṣ ṭebhiḥ sṛjatu viśvakarmā ||2||

adānyānt somapān manyamāno yajñasya vidvānt samaye na dhīraḥ |
yad enaś cakṛvān baddha eṣa taṃ viśvakarman pra muñcā svastaye ||3||

ghorā ṛṣayo namo astv ebhyaś cakṣur yad eṣāṃ manasaś ca satyam |
bṛhaspataye mahiṣa dyumann namo viśvakarman namas te pāhy asmān ||4||

yajñasya cakṣuḥ prabhṛtir mukhaṃ ca vācā śrotreṇa manasā juhomi |
imaṃ yajñaṃ vitataṃ viśvakarmaṇā devā yantu sumanasyamānāḥ ||5||


ā no agne sumatiṃ saṃbhalo gamed imāṃ kumārīṃ saha no bhagena |
juṣṭā vareṣu samaneṣu valgur oṣaṃ patyā saubhagam astu asyai ||1||

somajuṣṭaṃ brahmajuṣṭam aryamnā saṃbhṛtaṃ bhagam |
dhātur devasya satyena kṛṇomi pativedanam ||2||

iyam agne nārī patim videṣṭa somo hi rājā subhagāṃ kṛṇoti |
suvānā putrān mahiṣī bhavāti gatvā patiṃ subhagā vi rājatu ||3||

yathākharo maghavaṃś cārur eṣa priyo mṛgāṇāṃ suṣadā babhūva |
evā bhagasya juṣṭeyam astu nārī saṃpriyā patyāvirādhayantī ||4||

bhagasya nāvam ā roha pūrṇām anupadasvatīm |
tayopapratāraya yo varaḥ pratikāmyaḥ ||5||

ā krandaya dhanapate varam āmanasaṃ kṛṇu |
sarvaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛṇu yo varaḥ pratikāmyaḥ ||6||

idaṃ hiraṇyaṃ gulgulv ayam aukṣo atho bhagaḥ |
ete patibhyas tvām aduḥ pratikāmāya vettave ||7
ā te nayatu savitā nayatu patir yaḥ pratikāmyaḥ |



agnir naḥ śatrūn praty etu vidvān pratidahann abhiśastim arātim |
sa senāṃ mohayatu pareṣāṃ nirhastāṃś ca kṛṇavaj jātavedāḥ ||1||

yūyam ugrā maruta īdṛśe sthābhi preta mṛṇata sahadhvam |
amīmṛṇan vasavo nāthitā ime agnir hy eṣāṃ dūtaḥ pratyetu vidvān ||2||

amitrasenāṃ maghavann asmān chatrūyatīm abhi |
yuvaṃ tām indra vṛtrahann agniś ca dahataṃ prati ||3||

prasūta indra pravatā haribhyāṃ pra te vajraḥ pramṛṇann etu śatrūn |
jahi pratīco anūcaḥ parāco viṣvak satyaṃ kṛṇuhi cittam eṣām ||4||

indra senāṃ mohayāmitrāṇām |
agner vātasya dhrājyā tān viṣūco vi nāśaya ||5||

indraḥ senāṃ mohayatu maruto ghnantv ojasā |
cakṣūṃsy agnir ā dattāṃ punar etu parājitā ||6||



agnir no dūtaḥ pratyetu vidvān pratidahann abhiśastim arātim |
sa cittāni mohayatu pareṣāṃ nirhastāṃś ca kṛṇavaj jātavedāḥ ||1||

ayam agnir amūmuhad yāni cittāni vo hṛdi |
vi vo dhamatv okasaḥ pra vo dhamatu sarvataḥ ||2||

indra cittāni mohayann arvāṅ ākūtyā cara |
agner vātasya dhrājyā tān viṣūco vi nāśaya ||3||

vy ākūtaya eṣām itātho cittāni muhyata |
atho yad adyaiṣāṃ hṛdi tad eṣāṃ pari nir jahi ||4||

amīṣāṃ cittāni pratimohayantī gṛhāṇāṅgāny apve parehi |
abhi prehi nir daha hṛtsu śokair grāhyāmitrāṃs tamasā vidhya śatrūn ||5||

asau yā senā marutaḥ pareṣām asmān aity abhy ojasā spardhamānā |
tām vidhyata tamasāpavratena yathaiṣām anyo anyaṃ na jānāt ||6||



acikradat svapā iha bhuvad agne vy acasva rodasī urūcī |
yuñjantu tvā maruto viśvavedasa āmuṃ naya namasā rātahavyam ||1||

dūre cit santam aruṣāsa indram ā cyāvayantu sakhyāya vipram |
yad gāyatrīṃ bṛhatīm arkam asmai sautrāmaṇyā dadhṛṣanta devāḥ ||2||

adbhyas tvā rāja varuṇo hvayatu somas tvā hvayatu parvatebhyaḥ |
indras tvā hvayatu viḍbhya ābhyaḥ śyeno bhūtvā viśa ā patemāḥ ||3|| {4}

śyeno havyaṃ nayatv ā parasmād anyakṣetre aparuddhaṃ carantam |
aśvinā panthāṃ kṛṇutāṃ sugaṃ ta imaṃ sajātā abhisaṃviśadhvam ||4|| {5}

hvayantu tvā pratijanāḥ prati mitrā avṛṣata |
indrāgnī viśve devās te viśi kṣemam adīdharan ||5|| {6}

yas te havaṃ vivadat sajāto yaś ca niṣṭyaḥ |
apāñcam indra taṃ kṛtvāthemam ihāva gamaya ||6|| {7}



ā tvā gan rāṣtraṃ saha varcasod ihi prāṅ viśāṃ patir ekarāṭ tvaṃ vi rāja |
sarvās tvā rājan pradiśo hvayantūpasadyo namasyo bhaveha ||1||

tvāṃ viśo vṛṇatāṃ rājyāya tvām imāḥ pradiśaḥ pañca devīḥ |
varṣman rāṣṭrasya kakudi śrayasva tato na ugro vi bhajā vasūni ||2||

acha tvā yantu havinaḥ sajātā agnir dūto ajiraḥ saṃ carātai |
jāyāḥ putrāḥ sumanaso bhavantu bahuṃ baliṃ prati paśyāsā ugraḥ ||3||

aśvinā tvāgre mitrāvaruṇobhā viśve devā marutas tvā hvayantu |
adhā mano vasudeyāya kṛṇuṣva tato na ugro vi bhajā vasūni ||4||

ā pra drava paramasyāḥ parāvataḥ śive te dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe stām |
tad ayaṃ rājā varuṇas tathāha sa tvāyam ahvat sa upedam ehi ||5||

indrendra manuṣyāḥ parehi saṃ hy ajñāsthā varuṇaiḥ saṃvidānaḥ |
sa tvāyam ahvat sve sadhasthe sa devān yakṣat sa u kalpayad viśaḥ ||6||

pathyā revatīr bahudhā virūpāḥ sarvāḥ saṃgatya varīyas te akran |
tās tvā sarvāḥ saṃvidānā hvayantu daśamīm ugraḥ sumanā vaśeha ||7||



āyam agan parṇamaṇir balī balena pramṛṇant sapatnān |
ojo devānāṃ paya oṣadhīnāṃ varcasā mā jinvantv aprayāvan ||1||

mayi kṣatraṃ parṇamaṇe mayi dhārayatād rayim |
ahaṃ rāṣṭrasyābhīvarge nijo bhūyāsam uttamaḥ ||2||

yaṃ nidadhur vanaspatau guhyaṃ devāḥ priyaṃ maṇim |
tam asmabhyaṃ sahāyuṣā devā dadatu bhartave ||3||

somasya parṇaḥ saha ugram āgann indreṇa datto varuṇena śiṣṭaḥ |
taṃ priyāsaṃ bahu rocamāno dīrghāyutvāya śataśāradāya ||4||

ā mārukṣat parṇamaṇir mahyā ariṣṭatātaye |
yathāham uttaro 'sāny aryamṇa uta saṃvidaḥ ||5||

ye dhīvāno rathakārāḥ karmārā ye manīṣiṇaḥ |
upastīn parṇa mahyaṃ tvaṃ sarvān kṛṇv abhito janān ||6||

ye rājāno rājakṛtaḥ sūtā grāmaṇyaś ca ye |
upastīn parṇa mahyaṃ tvaṃ sarvān kṛṇv abhito janān ||7||

parṇo 'si tanūpānaḥ sayonir vīro vīreṇa mayā |
saṃvatsarasya tejasā tena badhnāmi tvā maṇe ||8||



pumān puṃsaḥ parijāto 'śvatthaḥ khadirād adhi |
sa hantu śatrūn māmakān yān ahaṃ dveṣmi ye ca mām ||1||

tān aśvattha niḥ śṛṇīhi śatrūn vaibādhadodhataḥ |
indreṇa vṛtraghnā medī mitreṇa varuṇena ca ||2||

yathāśvattha nirabhano 'ntar mahaty arṇave |
evā tānt sarvān nir bhaṅgdhi yān ahaṃ dveṣmi ye ca mām ||3||

yaḥ sahamānaś carasi sāsahāna iva ṛṣabhaḥ |
tenāśvattha tvayā vayaṃ sapatnānt sahiṣīmahi ||4||

sinātv enān nirṛtir mṛtyoḥ pāśair amokyaiḥ |
aśvattha śatrūn māmakān yān ahaṃ dveṣmi ye ca mām ||5||

yathāśvattha vānaspatyān ārohan kṛṇuṣe 'dharān |
evā me śatror mūrdhānaṃ viṣvag bhinddhi sahasva ca ||6||

te 'dharāñcaḥ pra plavantāṃ chinnā naur iva bandhanāt |
na vaibādhapraṇuttānāṃ punar asti nivartanam ||7||

praiṇān nude manasā pra cittenota brahmaṇā |
praiṇān vṛkṣasya śākhayāśvatthasya nudāmahe ||8||

hariṇasya raghuṣyado 'dhi śīrṣaṇi bheṣajam |
sa kṣetriyaṃ viṣāṇayā viṣūcīnam anīnaśat ||1||

anu tvā hariṇo vṛṣā padbhiś caturbhir akramīt |
viṣāṇe vi ṣya guṣpitaṃ yad asya kṣetriyaṃ hṛdi ||2||

ado yad avarocate catuṣpakṣam iva chadiḥ |
tenā te sarvaṃ kṣetriyam aṅgebhyo nāśayāmasi ||3||

amū ye divi subhage vicṛtau nāma tārake |
vi kṣetriyasya muñcatām adhamaṃ pāśam uttamam ||4||

āpa id vā u bheṣajīr āpo amīvacātanīḥ |
āpo viśvasya bheṣajīs tās tvā muñcantu kṣetriyāt ||5||

yad āsuteḥ kriyamānāyāḥ kṣetriyaṃ tvā vyānaśe |
vedāhaṃ tasya bheṣajaṃ kṣetriyaṃ nāśayāmi tvat ||6||

apavāse nakṣatrāṇām apavāsa uṣasām uta |
apāsmat sarvaṃ durbhūtam apa kṣetriyam uchatu ||7||



ā yātu mitra ṛtubhiḥ kalpamānaḥ saṃveśayan pṛthivīm usriyābhiḥ |
athāsmabhyam varuṇo vāyur agnir bṛhad rāṣṭraṃ saṃveśyam dadhātu ||1||

dhātā rātiḥ savitedaṃ juśantām indras tvaṣṭā prati haryantu me vacaḥ |
huve devīm aditiṃ śūraputrāṃ sajātānāṃ madhyameṣṭhā yathāsāni ||2||

huve somaṃ savitāraṃ namobhir viśvān ādityāṃ aham uttaratve |
ayam agnir dīdāyad dīrgham eva sajātair iddho 'pratibruvadbhiḥ ||3||

ihed asātha na paro gamātheryo gopāḥ puṣṭapatir va ājat |
asmai kāmāyopa kāminīr viśve vo devā upasaṃyantu ||4||

saṃ vo manāṃsi saṃ vratā sam ākūtīr namāmasi |
amī ye vivratā sthana tān vaḥ saṃ namayāmasi ||5||

ahaṃ gṛbhṇāmi manasā manāṃsi mama cittam anu cittebhir eta |
mama vaśeṣu hṛdayāni vaḥ kṛṇomi mama yātam anuvartmāna eta ||6||



karśaphasya viśaphasya dyauḥ pitā pṛthivī mātā |
yathābhicakra devās tathāpa kṛṇutā punaḥ ||1||

aśreṣmāṇo adhārayan tathā tan manunā kṛtam |
kṛṇomi vadhri viṣkandhaṃ muṣkābarho gavām iva ||2||

piśaṅge sūtre khṛgalaṃ tad ā badhnanti vedhasaḥ |
śravasyuṃ śuṣmaṃ kābavaṃ vadhriṃ kṛṇvantu bandhuraḥ ||3||

yenā śravasyavaś caratha devā ivāsuramāyayā |
śunāṃ kapir iva dūṣaṇo bandhurā kābavasya ca ||4||

duṣṭyai hi tvā bhatsyāmi dūṣayiṣyāmi kābavam |
ud āśavo rathā iva śapathebhiḥ sariṣyatha ||5||

ekaśataṃ viṣkandhāni viṣṭhitā pṛthivīm anu |
teṣāṃ tvām agre uj jaharur maṇiṃ viṣkandhadūṣaṇam ||6||



prathamā ha vy uvāsa sā dhenur abhavad yame |
sā naḥ payasvatī duhām uttarāmuttarām samām ||1||

yāṃ devāḥ pratinandanti rātrim dhenum upāyatīm |
saṃvatsarasya yā patnī sā no astu sumaṅgalī ||2||

saṃvatsarasya pratimāṃ yāṃ tvā rātry upāsmahe |
sā na āyuṣmatīṃ prajāṃ rāyas poṣeṇa saṃ sṛja ||3||

iyam eva sā yā prathamā vyauchad āsv itarāsu carati praviṣṭā |
mahānto asyāṃ mahimāno antar vadhūr jigāya navagaj janitrī ||4||

vānaspatyā grāvāṇo ghoṣam akrata haviṣ kṛṇvantaḥ parivatsarīṇam |
ekāṣṭake suprajasaḥ suvīrā vayaṃ syāma patayo rayīṇām ||5||

iḍāyās padaṃ ghṛtavat sarīsṛpaṃ jātavedaḥ prati havyā gṛbhāya |
ye grāmyāḥ paśavo viśvarūpās teṣāṃ saptānāṃ mayi rantir astu ||6||

ā mā puṣṭe ca poṣe ca rātri devānāṃ sumatau syāma |
pūrṇā darve parā pata supūrṇā punar ā pata |
sarvān yajñānt saṃbhuñjatīṣam ūrjaṃ na ā bhara ||7||

āyam agant saṃvatsaraḥ patir ekāṣṭake tava |
sā na āyuṣmatīṃ prajāṃ rāyas poṣeṇa saṃ sṛja ||8||

ṛtūn yaja ṛtupatīn ārtavān uta hāyanān |
samāḥ saṃvatsarān māsān bhūtasya pataye yaje ||9||

3,10.10a ṛtubhyaṣ ṭvārtavebhyo mādbhyaḥ saṃvatsarebhyaḥ |
3,10.10c dhātre vidhātre samṛdhe bhūtasya pataye yaje ||10||

3,10.11a iḍayā juhvato vayaṃ devān ghṛtavatā yaje |
3,10.11c gṛhān alubhyato vayaṃ saṃ viśemopa gomataḥ ||11||

3,10.12a ekāṣṭakā tapasā tapyamānā jajāna garbhaṃ mahimānam indram |
3,10.12c tena devā vy asahanta śatrūn hantā dasyūnām abhavac chacīpatiḥ ||12||

3,10.13a indraputre somaputre duhitāsi prajāpateḥ |
3,10.13c kāmān asmākaṃ pūraya prati gṛhṇāhi no haviḥ ||13||



muñcāmi tvā haviṣā jīvanāya kam ajñātayakṣmād uta rājayakṣmāt |
grāhir jagrāha yady etad enaṃ tasyā indrāgnī pra mumuktam enam ||1||

yadi kṣitāyur yadi vā pareto yadi mṛtyor antikaṃ eva |
tam ā harāmi nirṛter upasthād aspārśam enaṃ śataśāradāya ||2||

sahasrākṣeṇa śatavīryeṇa śatāyuṣā haviṣāhārṣam enam |
indro yathainaṃ śarado nayāty ati viśvasya duritasya pāram ||3||

śataṃ jīva śarado vardhamānaḥ śataṃ hemantān chatam u vasantān |
śataṃ te indro agniḥ savitā bṛhaspatiḥ śatāyuṣā haviṣāhārṣam enam ||4||

pra viśataṃ prāṇāpānāv anaḍvāhāv iva vrajam |
vy anye yantu mṛtyavo yān āhur itarān chatam ||5||

ihaiva staṃ prāṇāpānau māpa gātam ito yuvam |
śarīram asyāṅgāni jarase vahataṃ punaḥ ||6||

jarāyai tvā pari dadāmi jarāyai ni dhuvāmi tvā |
jarā tvā bhadrā neṣṭa vy anye yantu mṛtyavo yān āhur itarān chatam ||7||

abhi tvā jarimāhita gām ukṣaṇam iva rajjvā |
yas tvā mṛtyur abhyadhatta jāyamānaṃ supāśayā |
taṃ te satyasya hastābhyām ud amuñcad bṛhaspatiḥ ||8||



ihaiva dhruvāṃ ni minomi śālāṃ kṣeme tiṣṭhāti ghṛtam ukṣamāṇā |
tāṃ tvā śāle sarvavīrāḥ suvīrā ariṣṭavīrā upa saṃ carema ||1||

ihaiva dhruvā prati tiṣṭha śāle 'śvāvatī gomatī sūnṛtāvatī |
ūrjasvatī ghṛtavatī payasvaty uc chrayasva mahate saubhagāya ||2||

dharuṇy asi śāle bṛhachandāḥ pūtidhānyā |
ā tvā vatso gamed ā kumāra ā dhenavaḥ sāyam āspandamānāḥ ||3||

imāṃ śālāṃ savitā vāyur indro bṛhaspatir ni minotu prajānan |
ukṣantūdnā maruto ghṛtena bhago no rājā ni kṛṣiṃ tanotu ||4||

mānasya patni śaraṇā syonā devī devebhir nimitāsy agre |
tṛṇaṃ vasānā sumanā asas tvam athāsmabhyaṃ sahavīraṃ rayiṃ dāḥ ||5||

ṛtena sthūṇām adhi roha vaṃśogro virājann apa vṛṅkṣva śatrūn |
mā te riṣann upasattāro gṛhāṇāṃ śāle śataṃ jīvema śaradaḥ sarvavīrāḥ ||6||

emāṃ kumāras taruṇa ā vatso jagatā saha |
emām parisrutaḥ kumbha ā dadhnaḥ kalaśair aguḥ ||7||

pūrṇaṃ nāri pra bhara kumbham etaṃ ghṛtasya dhārām amṛtena saṃbhṛtām |
imāṃ pātṝn amṛtena sam aṅgdhīṣṭāpūrtam abhi rakṣāty enām ||8||

imā āpaḥ pra bharāmy ayakṣmā yakṣmanāśanīḥ |
gṛhān upa pra sīdāmy amṛtena sahāgninā ||9||



yad adaḥ saṃprayatīr ahāv anadatā hate |
tasmād ā nadyo nāma stha tā vo nāmāni sindhavaḥ ||1||

yat preṣitā varuṇenāc chībham samavalgata |
tad āpnod indro vo yatīs tasmād āpo anu ṣṭhana ||2||

apakāmaṃ syandamānā avīvarata vo hi kam |
indro vaḥ śaktibhir devīs tasmād vār nāma vo hitam ||3||

ekaḥ vo devo 'py atiṣṭhat syandamānā yathāvaśam |
ud āniṣur mahīr iti tasmād udakam ucyate ||4||

āpo bhadrā ghṛtam id āpa āsann agnīṣomau bibhraty āpa it tāḥ |
tīvro raso madhupṛcām araṃgama ā mā prāṇena saha varcasā gamet ||5||

ād it paśyāmy uta vā śṛṇomy ā mā ghoṣo gachati vāṅ māsām |
manye bhejāno amṛtasya tarhi hiraṇyavarṇā atṛpaṃ yadā vaḥ ||6||
idaṃ va āpo hṛdayam ayaṃ vatsa ṛtāvarīḥ |
ihettham eta śakvarīr yatredaṃ veśayāmi vaḥ ||7||



saṃ vo goṣṭhena suṣadā saṃ rayyā saṃ subhūtyā |
aharjātasya yan nāma tenā vaḥ saṃ sṛjāmasi ||1||

saṃ vaḥ sṛjatv aryamā saṃ pūṣā saṃ bṛhaspatiḥ |
sam indro yo dhanaṃjayo mayi puṣyata yad vasu ||2||

saṃjagmānā abibhyuṣīr asmin goṣṭhe karīṣiṇīḥ |
bibhratīḥ somyaṃ madhv anamīvā upetana ||3||

ihaiva gāva etaneho śakeva puṣyata |
ihaivota pra jāyadhvaṃ mayi saṃjñānam astu vaḥ ||4||

śivo vo goṣṭho bhavatu śāriśākeva puṣyata |
ihaivota pra jāyadhvaṃ mayā vaḥ saṃ sṛjāmasi ||5||

mayā gāvo gopatinā sacadhvam ayaṃ vo goṣṭha iha poṣayiṣṇuḥ |
rāyas poṣeṇa bahulā bhavantīr jīvā jīvantīr upa vaḥ sadema ||6||



indram ahaṃ vaṇijaṃ codayāmi sa na aitu puraetā no astu |
nudann arātiṃ paripanthinaṃ mṛgaṃ sa īśāno dhanadā astu mahyam ||1||

ye panthāno bahavo devayānā antarā dyāvāpṛthivī saṃcaranti |
te mā juṣantāṃ payasā ghṛtena yathā krītvā dhanam āharāṇi ||2||

idhmenāgna ichamāno ghṛtena juhomi havyaṃ tarase balāya |
yāvad īśe brahmaṇā vandamāna imāṃ dhiyaṃ śataseyāya devīm ||3||

imām agne śaraṇiṃ mīmṛṣo no yam adhvānam agāma dūram |
śunaṃ no astu prapaṇo vikrayaś ca pratipaṇaḥ phalinaṃ mā kṛṇotu |
idaṃ havyaṃ saṃvidānau juṣethāṃ śunaṃ no astu caritam utthitaṃ ca ||4||

yena dhanena prapaṇaṃ carāmi dhanena devā dhanam ichamānaḥ |
tan me bhūyo bhavatu mā kanīyo 'gne sātaghno devān haviṣā ni ṣedha ||5||

yena dhanena prapaṇaṃ carāmi dhanena devā dhanam ichamānaḥ |
tasmin ma indro rucim ā dadhātu prajāpatiḥ savitā somo agniḥ ||6||

upa tvā namasā vayaṃ hotar vaiśvānara stumaḥ |
sa naḥ prajāsv ātmasu goṣu prāṇeṣu jāgṛhi ||7||

viśvāhā te sadam id bharemāśvāyeva tiṣṭhate jātavedaḥ |
rāyas poṣeṇa sam iṣā madanto mā te agne prativeśā riṣāma ||8||



prātar agniṃ prātar indram havāmahe prātar mitrāvaruṇā prātar aśvinā |
prātar bhagaṃ pūṣaṇaṃ brahmaṇas patiṃ prātaḥ somam uta rudraṃ havāmahe ||1||

prātarjitaṃ bhagam ugram havāmahe vayaṃ putram aditer yo vidhartā |
ādhraś cid yaṃ manyamānas turaś cid rājā cid yaṃ bhagaṃ bhakṣīty āha ||2||

bhaga praṇetar bhaga satyarādho bhagemāṃ dhiyam ud avā dadan naḥ |
bhaga pra ṇo janaya gobhir aśvair bhaga pra nṛbhir nṛvantaḥ syāma ||3||

utedānīṃ bhagavantaḥ syāmota prapitva uta madhye ahnām |
utoditau maghavant sūryasya vayaṃ devānāṃ sumatau syāma ||4||

bhaga eva bhagavāṃ astu devas tenā vayaṃ bhagavantaḥ syāma |
taṃ tvā bhaga sarva ij johavīmi sa no bhaga puraetā bhaveha ||5||

sam adhvarāyoṣaso namanta dadhikrāveva śucaye padāya |
arvācīnaṃ vasuvidaṃ bhagaṃ me ratham ivāśvā vājina ā vahantu ||6||

aśvāvatīr gomatīr na uṣāso vīravatīḥ sadam uchantu bhadrāḥ |
ghṛtaṃ duhānā viśvataḥ prapītā yūyaṃ pāta svastibhiḥ sadā naḥ ||7||



sīrā yuñjanti kavayo yugā vi tanvate pṛthak |
dhīrā deveṣu sumnayau ||1||

yunakta sīrā vi yugā tanota kṛte yonau vapateha bījam |
virājaḥ śnuṣṭiḥ sabharā asan no nedīya it sṛṇyaḥ pakvam ā yavan ||2||

lāṅgalaṃ pavīravat suśīmaṃ somasatsaru |
ud id vapatu gām aviṃ prasthāvad rathavāhanaṃ pībarīṃ ca prapharvyam ||3||
indraḥ sītāṃ ni gṛhṇātu tāṃ pūṣābhi rakṣatu |
sā naḥ payasvatī duhām uttarāmuttarāṃ samām ||4||

śunaṃ suphālā vi tudantu bhūmiṃ śunaṃ kīnāśā anu yantu vāhān |
śunāsīrā haviṣā tośamānā supippalā oṣadhīḥ kartam asmai ||5||
śunaṃ vāhāḥ śunaṃ naraḥ śunaṃ kṛṣatu lāṅgalam |
śunaṃ varatrā badhyantāṃ śunam aṣṭrām ud iṅgaya ||6||

śunāsīreha sma me juṣethām |
yad divi cakrathuḥ payas tenemām upa siñcatam ||7||

sīte vandāmahe tvārvācī subhage bhava |
yathā naḥ sumanā aso yathā naḥ suphalā bhuvaḥ ||8||

ghṛtena sītā madhunā samaktā viśvair devair anumatā marudbhiḥ |
sā naḥ sīte payasābhyāvavṛtsvorjasvatī ghṛtavat pinvamānā ||9||



imāṃ khanāmy oṣadhiṃ vīrudhāṃ balavattamām |
yayā sapatnīṃ bādhate yayā saṃvindate patim ||1||

uttānaparṇe subhage devajūte sahasvati |
sapatnīṃ me parā ṇuda patiṃ me kevalaṃ kṛdhi ||2||

nahi te nāma jagrāha no asmin ramase patau |
parām eva parāvataṃ sapatnīṃ gamayāmasi ||3||

uttarāham uttara uttared uttarābhyaḥ |
adhaḥ sapatnī yā mamādharā sādharābhyaḥ ||4||

aham asmi sahamānātho tvam asi sāsahiḥ |
ubhe sahasvatī bhūtvā sapatnīṃ me sahāvahai ||5||

abhi te 'dhāṃ sahamānām upa te 'dhāṃ sahīyasīm |
mām anu pra te mano vatsaṃ gaur iva dhāvatu pathā vār iva dhāvatu ||6||



saṃśitaṃ ma idaṃ brahma saṃśitaṃ vīryaṃ balam |
saṃśitaṃ kṣatram ajaram astu jiṣṇur yeṣām asmi purohitaḥ ||1||

sam aham eṣāṃ rāṣṭraṃ syāmi sam ojo vīryaṃ balam |
vṛścāmi śatrūṇāṃ bāhūn anena haviṣā aham ||2||

nīcaiḥ padyantām adhare bhavantu ye naḥ sūriṃ maghavānaṃ pṛtanyān |
kṣiṇāmi brahmaṇāmitrān un nayāmi svān aham ||3||

tīkṣṇīyāṃsaḥ paraśor agnes tīkṣṇatarā uta |
indrasya vajrāt tīkṣṇīyāṃso yeṣām asmi purohitaḥ ||4||

eṣām aham āyudhā saṃ syāmy eṣāṃ rāṣṭraṃ suvīraṃ vardhayāmi |
eṣām kṣatram ajaram astu jiṣṇv eṣāṃ cittaṃ viśve 'vantu devāḥ ||5||

ud dharṣantāṃ maghavan vājināny ud vīrāṇāṃ jayatām etu ghoṣaḥ |
pṛthag ghoṣā ululayaḥ ketumanta ud īratām |
devā indrajyeṣṭhā maruto yantu senayā ||6||

pretā jayatā nara ugrā vaḥ santu bāhavaḥ |
tīkṣṇeṣavo 'baladhanvano hatogrāyudhā abalān ugrabāhavaḥ ||7||

avasṛṣṭā parā pata śaravye brahmasaṃśite |
jaya amitrān pra padyasva jahy eṣāṃ varaṃvaraṃ māmīṣāṃ moci kaś cana ||8||



ayaṃ te yonir ṛtviyo yato jāto arocathāḥ |
taṃ jānann agna ā rohādhā no vardhaya rayim ||1||

agne achā vadeha naḥ pratyaṅ naḥ sumanā bhava |
pra ṇo yacha viśāṃ pate dhanadā asi nas tvam ||2||

pra ṇo yachatv aryamā pra bhagaḥ pra bṛhaspatiḥ |
pra devīḥ prota sūnṛtā rayiṃ devī dadhātu me ||3||

somaṃ rājānam avase 'gniṃ gīrbhir havāmahe |
ādityam viṣṇum sūryaṃ brahmāṇaṃ ca bṛhaspatim ||4||

tvaṃ no agne agnibhir brahma yajñaṃ vardhaya |
tvaṃ no deva dātave rayiṃ dānāya codaya ||5||

indravāyū ubhāv iha suhaveha havāmahe |
yathā naḥ sarva ij janaḥ saṃgatyāṃ sumanā asad dānakāmaś ca no bhuvat ||6||

aryamaṇaṃ bṛhaspatim indraṃ dānāya codaya |
vātaṃ viṣṇuṃ sarasvatīṃ savitāraṃ ca vājinam ||7||

vājasya nu prasave saṃ babhūvimemā ca viśvā bhuvanāni antaḥ |
utāditsantaṃ dāpayatu prajānan rayiṃ ca naḥ sarvavīraṃ ni yacha ||8||

duhrām me pañca pradiṣo duhrām urvīr yathābalam |
prāpeyaṃ sarvā ākūtīr manasā hṛdayena ca ||9||

3,20.10a gosaniṃ vācam udeyaṃ varcasā mābhyudihi |
3,20.10c ā rundhāṃ sarvato vāyus tvaṣṭā poṣaṃ dadhātu me ||10||



ye agnayo apsv antar ye vṛtre ye puruṣe ye aśmasu |
ya āviveśoṣadhīr yo vanaspatīṃs tebhyo agnibhyo hutam astv etat ||1||

yaḥ some antar yo goṣv antar ya āviṣṭo vayaḥsu yo mṛgeṣu |
ya āviveśa dvipado yas catuṣpadas tebhyo agnibhyo hutam astv etat ||2||

ya indreṇa sarathaṃ yāti devo vaiśvānara uta viśvadāvyaḥ |
yaṃ johavīmi pṛtanāsu sāsahiṃ tebhyo agnibhyo hutam astv etat ||3||

yo devo viśvād yam u kāmam āhur yaṃ dātāraṃ pratigṛhṇantam āhuḥ |
yo dhīraḥ śakraḥ paribhūr adābhyas tebhyo agnibhyo hutam astv etat ||4||

yaṃ tvā hotāraṃ manasābhi saṃvidus trayodaśa bhauvanāḥ pañca mānavāḥ |
varcodhase yaśase sūnṛtāvate tebhyo agnibhyo hutam astv etat ||5||

ukṣānnāya vaśānnāya somapṛṣṭhāya vedhase |
vaiśvānarajyeṣṭhebhyas tebhyo agnibhyo hutam astv etat ||6||

divaṃ pṛthivīm anv antarikṣam ye vidyutam anusaṃcaranti |
ye dikṣv antar ye vāte antas tebhyo agnibhyo hutam astv etat ||7||

hiraṇyapāṇiṃ savitāram indraṃ bṛhaspatiṃ varuṇaṃ mitram agnim |
viśvān devān aṅgiraso havāmahe imaṃ kravyādaṃ śamayantv agnim ||8||

śānto agniḥ kravyāc chāntaḥ puruṣareṣaṇaḥ |
atho yo viśvadāvyas taṃ kravyādam aśīśamam ||9||

3,21.10a ye parvatāḥ somapṛṣṭhā āpa uttānaśīvarīḥ |
3,21.10c vātaḥ parjanya ād agnis te kravyādam aśīśaman ||10||



hastivarcasaṃ prathatāṃ bṛhad yaśo adityā yat tanvaḥ saṃbabhūva |
tat sarve sam adur mahyam etad viśve devā aditiḥ sajoṣāḥ ||1||

mitraś ca varuṇaś cendro rudraś ca cetatu |
devāso viśvadhāyasas te māñjantu varcasā ||2||

yena hastī varcasā saṃbabhūva yena rājā manuṣyesv apsv antaḥ |
yena devā devatām agra āyan tena mām adya varcasāgne varcasvinaṃ kṛṇu ||3||

yat te varco jātavedo bṛhad bhavaty āhuteḥ |
yāvat sūryasya varca āsurasya ca hastinaḥ |
tāvan me aśvinā varca ā dhattāṃ puṣkarasrajā ||4||

yāvac catasraḥ pradiśaś cakṣur yāvat samaśnute |
tāvat samaitv indriyaṃ mayi tad dhastivarcasam ||5||

hastī mṛgāṇāṃ suṣadām atiṣṭhāvān babhūva hi |
tasya bhagena varcasābhi ṣiñcāmi mām aham ||6||



yena vehad babhūvitha nāśayāmasi tat tvat |
idaṃ tad anyatra tvad apa dūre ni dadhmasi ||1||

ā te yoniṃ garbha etu pumān bāṇa iveṣudhim |
ā vīro 'tra jāyatāṃ putras te daśamāsyaḥ ||2||

pumāṃsaṃ putraṃ janaya taṃ pumān anu jāyatām |
bhavāsi putrāṇāṃ mātā jātānāṃ janayāś ca yān ||3||

yāni badrāṇi bījāny ṛṣabhā janayanti ca |
tais tvaṃ putraṃ vindasva sā prasūr dhenukā bhava ||4||

kṛṇomi te prājāpatyam ā yoniṃ garbha etu te |
vindasva tvaṃ putraṃ nāri yas tubhyaṃ śam asac cham u tasmai tvam bhava ||5||

yāsām dyauḥ pitā pṛthivī mātā samudro mūlaṃ vīrudhāṃ babhūva |
tās tvā putravidyāya daivīḥ prāvantv oṣadhayaḥ ||6||



payasvatīr oṣadhayaḥ payasvan māmakaṃ vacaḥ |
atho payasvatīnām ā bhare 'haṃ sahasraśaḥ ||1||

vedāhaṃ payasvantaṃ cakāra dhānyam bahu |
saṃbhṛtvā nāma yo devas taṃ vayaṃ havāmahe yoyo ayajvano gṛhe ||2||

imā yāḥ pañca pradiśo mānavīḥ pañca kṛṣṭayaḥ |
vṛṣṭe śāpaṃ nadīr iveha sphātiṃ samāvahān ||3||

ud utsaṃ śatadhāraṃ sahasradhāram akṣitam |
evāsmākedaṃ dhānyaṃ sahasradhāram akṣitam ||4||

śatahasta samāhara sahasrahasta saṃ kira |
kṛtasya kāryasya ceha sphātiṃ samāvaha ||5||

tisro mātrā gandharvāṇāṃ catasro gṛhapatnyāḥ |
tāsāṃ yā sphātimattamā tayā tvābhi mṛśāmasi ||6||

upohaś ca samūhaś ca kṣattārau te prajāpate |
tāv ihā vahatāṃ sphātiṃ bahuṃ bhūmānam akṣitam ||7||



uttudas tvot tudatu mā dhṛthāḥ śayane sve |
iṣuḥ kāmasya yā bhīmā tayā vidhyāmi tvā hṛdi ||1||

ādhīparṇāṃ kāmaśalyām iṣuṃ saṃkalpakulmalām |
tāṃ susaṃnatāṃ kṛtvā kāmo vidhyatu tvā hṛdi ||2||

yā plīhānaṃ śoṣayati kāmasyeṣuḥ susaṃnatā |
prācīnapakṣā vyoṣā tayā vidhyāmi tvā hṛdi ||3||

śucā viddhā vyoṣayā śuṣkāsyābhi sarpa mā |
mṛdur nimanyuḥ kevalī priyavādiny anuvratā ||4||

ājāmi tvājanyā pari mātur atho pituḥ |
yathā mama kratāv aso mama cittam upāyasi ||5||

vy asyai mitrāvaruṇau hṛdaś cittāny asyatam |
athainām akratuṃ kṛtvā mamaiva kṛṇutaṃ vaśe ||6||



ye 'syāṃ stha prācyāṃ diśi hetayo nāma devās teṣāṃ vo agnir iṣavaḥ |
te no mṛḍata te no 'dhi brūta tebhyo vo namas tebhyo vaḥ svāhā ||1||

ye 'syāṃ stha dakṣiṇāyāṃ diśy aviṣyavo nāma devās teṣāṃ vaḥ kāma iṣavaḥ |
te no mṛḍata te no 'dhi brūta tebhyo vo namas tebhyo vaḥ svāhā ||2||

ye 'syāṃ stha pratīcyāṃ diśi vairājā nāma devās teṣāṃ va āpa iṣavaḥ |
te no mṛḍata te no 'dhi brūta tebhyo vo namas tebhyo vaḥ svāhā ||3||

ye 'syāṃ sthodīcyāṃ diśi pravidhyanto nāma devās teṣāṃ vo vāta iṣavaḥ |
te no mṛḍata te no 'dhi brūta tebhyo vo namas tebhyo vaḥ svāhā ||4||

ye 'syāṃ stha dhruvāyāṃ diśi nilimpā nāma devās teṣāṃ va oṣadhīr iṣavaḥ |
te no mṛḍata te no 'dhi brūta tebhyo vo namas tebhyo vaḥ svāhā ||5||

ye 'syāṃ sthordhvāyāṃ diśy avasvanto nāma devās teṣāṃ vo bṛhaspatir iṣavaḥ |
te no mṛḍata te no 'dhi brūta tebhyo vo namas tebhyo vaḥ svāhā ||6||



prācī dig agnir adhipatir asito rakṣitādityā iṣavaḥ |
tebhyo namo 'dhipatibhyo namo rakṣitṛbhyo nama iṣubhyo nama ebhyo astu |
yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmas taṃ vo jambhe dadhmaḥ ||1||

dakṣiṇā dig indro 'dhipatis tiraścirājī rakṣitā pitara iṣavaḥ |
tebhyo namo 'dhipatibhyo namo rakṣitṛbhyo nama iṣubhyo nama ebhyo astu |
yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmas taṃ vo jambhe dadhmaḥ ||2||

pratīcī dig varuṇo 'dhipatiḥ pṛdākū rakṣitānnam iṣavaḥ |
tebhyo namo 'dhipatibhyo namo rakṣitṛbhyo nama iṣubhyo nama ebhyo astu |
yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmas taṃ vo jambhe dadhmaḥ ||3||

udīcī dik somo 'dhipatiḥ svajo rakṣitāśanir iṣavaḥ |
tebhyo namo 'dhipatibhyo namo rakṣitṛbhyo nama iṣubhyo nama ebhyo astu |
yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmas taṃ vo jambhe dadhmaḥ ||4||

dhruvā dig viṣṇur adhipatiḥ kalmāṣagrīvo rakṣitā vīrudha iṣavaḥ |
tebhyo namo 'dhipatibhyo namo rakṣitṛbhyo nama iṣubhyo nama ebhyo astu |
yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayam dviṣmas taṃ vo jambhe dadhmaḥ ||5||

ūrdhvā dig bṛhaspatir adhipatiḥ śvitro rakṣitā varṣam iṣavaḥ |
tebhyo namo 'dhipatibhyo namo rakṣitṛbhyo nama iṣubhyo nama ebhyo astu |
yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmas taṃ vo jambhe dadhmaḥ ||6||


ekaikayaiṣā sṛṣṭyā saṃ babhūva yatra gā asṛjanta bhūtakṛto viśvarūpāḥ |
yatra vijāyate yaminy apartuḥ sā paśūn kṣiṇāti riphatī ruśatī ||1||

eṣā paśūnt saṃ kṣiṇāti kravyād bhūtvā vyadvarī |
utaināṃ brahmaṇe dadyāt tathā syonā śivā syāt ||2||

śivā bhava puruṣebhyo gobhyo aśvebhyaḥ śivā |
śivāsmai sarvasmai kṣetrāya śivā na ihaidhi ||3||

iha puṣṭir iha rasa iha sahasrasātamā bhava |
paśūn yamini poṣaya ||4||

yatrā suhārdaḥ sukṛto madanti vihāya rogaṃ tanvaḥ svāyāḥ |
taṃ lokaṃ yaminy abhisaṃbabhūva sā no mā hiṃsīt puruṣān paśūṃś ca ||5||

yatrā suhārdāṃ sukṛtām agnihotrahutām yatra lokaḥ |
taṃ lokaṃ yaminy abhisaṃbabhūva sā no mā hiṃsīt puruṣān paśūṃś ca ||6||



yad rājāno vibhajanta iṣṭāpūrtasya ṣoḍaśam yamasyāmī sabhāsadaḥ |
avis tasmāt pra muñcati dattaḥ śitipāt svadhā ||1||

sarvān kāmān pūrayaty ābhavan prabhavan bhavan |
ākūtipro 'vir dattaḥ śitipānn nopa dasyati ||2||

yo dadāti śitipādam aviṃ lokena saṃmitam |
sa nākam abhyārohati yatra śulko na kriyate abalena balīyase ||3||

pañcāpūpaṃ śitipādam aviṃ lokena saṃmitam |
pradātopa jīvati pitṝṇāṃ loke 'kṣitam ||4||

pañcāpūpaṃ śitipādam aviṃ lokena saṃmitam |
pradātopa jīvati sūryāmāsayor akṣitam ||5||

ireva nopa dasyati samudra iva payo mahat |
devau savāsināv iva śitipān nopa dasyati ||6||

ka idaṃ kasmā adāt kāmaḥ kāmāyādāt |
kāmo dātā kāmaḥ pratigrahītā kāmaḥ samudram ā viveśa |
kāmena tvā prati gṛhnāmi kāmaitat te ||7||
bhūmiṣ ṭvā prati gṛhṇātv antarikṣam idaṃ mahat |
māhaṃ prāṇena mātmanā mā prajayā pratigṛhya vi rādhiṣi ||8||



sahṛdayaṃ sāṃmanasyam avidveṣaṃ kṛṇomi vaḥ |
anyo anyam abhi haryata vatsaṃ jātam ivāghnyā ||1||

anuvrataḥ pituḥ putro mātrā bhavatu saṃmanāḥ |
jāyā patye madhumatīṃ vācaṃ vadatu śantivām ||2||

mā bhrātā bhrātaraṃ dvikṣan mā svasāram uta svasā |
samyañcaḥ savratā bhūtvā vācaṃ vadata bhadrayā ||3||

yena devā na viyanti no ca vidviṣate mithaḥ |
tat kṛṇmo brahma vo gṛhe saṃjñānaṃ puruṣebhyaḥ ||4||

jyāyasvantaś cittino mā vi yauṣṭa saṃrādhayantaḥ sadhurāś carantaḥ |
anyo anyasmai valgu vadanta eta sadhrīcīnān vaḥ saṃmanasas krṇomi ||5||

samānī prapā saha vo 'nnabhāgaḥ samāne yoktre saha vo yunajmi |
samyañco 'gniṃ saparyatārā nābhim ivābhitaḥ ||6||

sadhrīcīnān vaḥ saṃmanasas kṛṇomy ekaśnuṣṭīnt saṃvananena sarvān |
devā ivāmṛtaṃ rakṣamāṇāḥ sāyaṃprātaḥ saumanaso vo astu ||7||



vi devā jarasāvṛtan vi tvam agne arātyā |
vy ahaṃ sarveṇa pāpmanā vi yakṣmeṇa sam āyuṣā ||1||

vy ārtyā pavamāno vi śakraḥ pāpakṛtyayā |
vy ahaṃ sarveṇa pāpmanā vi yakṣmeṇa sam āyuṣā ||2||

vi grāmyāḥ paśava āraṇyair vy āpas tṛṣṇayāsaran |
vy ahaṃ sarveṇa pāpmanā vi yakṣmeṇa sam āyuṣā ||3||

vī me dyāvāpṛthivī ito vi panthāno diśaṃdiśam |
vy ahaṃ sarveṇa pāpmanā vi yakṣmeṇa sam āyuṣā ||4||

tvaṣṭā duhitre vahatuṃ yunaktītīdaṃ viśvaṃ bhuvanaṃ vi yāti |
vy ahaṃ sarveṇa pāpmanā vi yakṣmeṇa sam āyuṣā ||5||

agniḥ prāṇānt saṃ dadhāti candraḥ prāṇena saṃhitaḥ |
vy ahaṃ sarveṇa pāpmanā vi yakṣmeṇa sam āyuṣā ||6||

prāṇena viśvatovīryaṃ devāḥ sūryaṃ sam airayan |
vy ahaṃ sarveṇa pāpmanā vi yakṣmeṇa sam āyuṣā ||7||

āyuṣmatām āyuṣkṛtāṃ prāṇena jīva mā mṛthāḥ |
vy ahaṃ sarveṇa pāpmanā vi yakṣmeṇa sam āyuṣā ||8||

prāṇena prāṇatāṃ prāṇehaiva bhava mā mṛthāḥ |
vy ahaṃ sarveṇa pāpmanā vi yakṣmeṇa sam āyuṣā ||9||

3,31.10a ud āyuṣā sam āyuṣod oṣadhīnāṃ rasena |
3,31.10c vy ahaṃ sarveṇa pāpmanā vi yakṣmeṇa sam āyuṣā ||10||

3,31.11a ā parjanyasya vṛṣṭyod asthāmāmṛtā vayam |
3,31.11c vy ahaṃ sarveṇa pāpmanā vi yakṣmeṇa sam āyuṣā ||11||



brahma jajñānaṃ prathamaṃ purastād vi sīmataḥ suruco vena āvaḥ |
sa budhnyā upamā asya viṣṭhāḥ sataś ca yonim asataś ca vi vaḥ ||1||

iyaṃ pitryā rāṣṭry etv agre prathamāya januṣe bhuvaneṣṭhāḥ |
tasmā etaṃ surucaṃ hvāram ahyaṃ gharmaṃ śrīṇantu prathamāya dhāsyave ||2||

pra yo jajñe vidvān asya bandhur viśvā devānāṃ janimā vivakti |
brahma brahmaṇa uj jabhāra madhyān nicair uccaiḥ svadhā abhi pra tasthau ||3||

sa hi vidaḥ sa pṛthivyā ṛtasthā mahī kṣemaṃ rodasī askabhāyat |
mahān mahī askabhāyad vi jāto dyāṃ sadma pārthivaṃ ca rajaḥ ||4||

sa bhudhnyād āṣṭra januṣo 'bhy agram bṛhaspatir devatā tasya samrāṭ |
ahar yac chukraṃ jyotiṣo janiṣṭātha dyumanto vi vasantu viprāḥ ||5||

nūnaṃ tad asya kāvyo hinoti maho devasya pūrvyasya dhāma |
eṣa jajñe bahubhiḥ sākam itthā pūrve ardhe viṣite sasan nu ||6||

yo 'tharvāṇaṃ pitaraṃ devabandhuṃ bṛhaspatiṃ namasāva ca gachāt |
tvaṃ viśveṣāṃ janitā yathāsaḥ kavir devo na dabhāyat svadhāvān ||7||



ya ātmadā baladā yasya viśva upāsate praśiṣaṃ yasya devāḥ |
yo 'syeśe dvipado yaś catuṣpadaḥ kasmai devāya haviṣā vidhema ||1||

yaḥ prāṇato nimiṣato mahitvaiko rājā jagato babhūva |
yasya chāyāmṛtaṃ yasya mṛtyuḥ kasmai devāya haviṣā vidhema ||2||

yaṃ krandasī avataś caskabhāne bhiyasāne rodasī ahvayethām |
yasyāsau panthā rajaso vimānaḥ kasmai devāya haviṣā vidhema ||3||

yasya dyaur urvī pṛthivī ca mahī yasyāda urv antarikṣam |
yasyāsau sūro vitato mahitvā kasmai devāya haviṣā vidhema ||4||

yasya viśve himavanto mahitvā samudre yasya rasām id āhuḥ |
imāś ca pradiśo yasya bāhū kasmai devāya haviṣā vidhema ||5||

āpo agre viśvam āvan garbhaṃ dadhānā amṛtā ṛtajñāḥ |
yāsu devīṣv adhi deva āsīt kasmai devāya haviṣā vidhema ||6||

hiraṇyagarbhaḥ sam avartatāgre bhūtasya jātaḥ patir eka āsīt |
sa dādhāra pṛthivīm uta dyāṃ kasmai devāya haviṣā vidhema ||7||

āpo vatsaṃ janayantīr garbham agre sam airayan |
tasyota jāyamānasyolba āsīd dhiraṇyayaḥ kasmai devāya haviṣā vidhema ||8||



ud itas trayo akraman vyāghraḥ puruṣo vṛkaḥ |
hirug ghi yanti sindhavo hirug devo vanaspatir hiruṅ namantu śatravaḥ ||1||

pareṇaitu pathā vṛkaḥ parameṇota taskaraḥ |
pareṇa datvatī rajjuḥ pareṇāghāyur arṣatu ||2||

akṣyau ca te mukhaṃ ca te vyāghra jambhayāmasi |
āt sarvān viṃśatiṃ nakhān ||3||

vyāghraṃ datvatāṃ vayaṃ prathamaṃ jambhayāmasi |
ād u ṣṭenam atho ahiṃ yātudhānam atho vṛkam ||4||

yo adya stena āyati sa saṃpiṣṭo apāyati |
pathām apadhvaṃsenaitv indro vajreṇa hantu tam ||5||

mūrṇā mṛgasya dantā apiśīrṇā u pṛṣṭayaḥ |
nimruk te godhā bhavatu nīcāyac chaśayur mṛgaḥ ||6||

yat saṃyamo na vi yamo vi yamo yan na saṃyamaḥ |
indrajāḥ somajā ātharvaṇam asi vyāghrajambhanam ||7||



yāṃ tvā gandharvo akhanad varuṇāya mṛtabhraje |
tāṃ tvā vayaṃ khanāmasy oṣadhiṃ śepaharṣaṇīm ||1||

ud uṣā ud u sūrya ud idaṃ māmakaṃ vacaḥ |
ud ejatu prajāpatir vṛṣā śuṣmeṇa vājinā ||2||

yathā sma te virohato 'bhitaptam ivānati |
tatas te śuṣmavattaram iyaṃ kṛṇotv oṣadhiḥ ||3||

uc chuṣmauṣadhīnāṃ sārā ṛṣabhāṇām |
saṃ puṃsām indra vṛṣṇyam asmin dhehi tanūvaśin ||4||

apāṃ rasaḥ prathamajo 'tho vanaspatīnām |
uta somasya bhrātāsy utārśam asi vṛṣṇyam ||5||

adyāgne adya savitar adya devi sarasvati |
adyāsya brahmaṇas pate dhanur ivā tānayā pasaḥ ||6||

āhaṃ tanomi te paso adhi jyām iva dhanvani |
kramasvarśa iva rohitam anavaglāyatā sadā ||7||

aśvasyāśvatarasyājasya petvasya ca |
atha ṛṣabhasya ye vājās tān asmin dhehi tanūvaśin ||8||



sahasraśṛṅgo vṛṣabho yaḥ samudrād udācarat |
tenā sahasyenā vayaṃ ni janānt svāpayāmasi ||1||

na bhūmiṃ vāto ati vāti nāti paśyati kaś cana |
striyaś ca sarvāḥ svāpaya śunaś cendrasakhā caran ||2||

proṣṭheśayās talpeśayā nārīr yā vahyaśīvarīḥ |
striyo yāḥ puṇyagandhayas tāḥ sarvāḥ svāpayāmasi ||3||

ejadejad ajagrabhaṃ cakṣuḥ prāṇam ajagrabham |
aṅgāny ajagrabhaṃ sarvā rātrīṇām atiśarvare ||4||

ya āste yaś carati yaś ca tiṣṭhan vipaśyati |
teṣāṃ saṃ dadhmo akṣīṇi yathedaṃ harmyaṃ tathā ||5||

svaptu mātā svaptu pitā svaptu śvā svaptu viśpatiḥ |
svapantv asyai jñātayaḥ svaptv ayam abhito janaḥ ||6||

svapna svapnābhikaraṇena sarvaṃ ni svāpayā janam |
otsūryam anyānt svāpayāvyuṣaṃ jāgṛtād aham indra ivāriṣṭo akṣitaḥ ||7||



brāhmaṇo jajñe prathamo daśaśīrṣo daśāsyaḥ |
sa somaṃ prathamaḥ papau sa cakārārasaṃ viṣam ||1||

yāvatī dyāvāpṛthivī varimṇā yāvat sapta sindhavo vitaṣṭhire |
vācaṃ viṣasya dūṣaṇīṃ tām ito nir avādiṣam ||2||

suparṇas tvā garutmān viṣa prathamam āvayat |
nāmīmado nārūrupa utāsmā abhavaḥ pituḥ ||3||

yas ta āsyat pañcāṅgurir vakrāc cid adhi dhanvanaḥ |
apaskambhasya śalyān nir avocam ahaṃ viṣam ||4||

śalyād viṣaṃ nir avocam prāñjanād uta parṇadheḥ |
apāṣṭhāc chṛṅgāt kulmalān nir avocam aham viṣam ||5||

arasas ta iṣo śalyo 'tho te arasaṃ viṣam |
utārasasya vṛkṣasya dhanuṣ ṭe arasārasam ||6||

ye apīṣan ye adihan ya āsyan ye avāsṛjan |
sarve te vadhrayaḥ kṛtā vadhrir viṣagiriḥ kṛtaḥ ||7||

vadhrayas te khanitāro vadhris tvam asy oṣadhe |
vadhriḥ sa parvato girir yato jātam idaṃ viṣam ||8||



vār idam vārayātai varaṇāvatyām adhi |
tatrāmṛtasyāsiktaṃ tenā te vāraye viṣam ||1||

arasaṃ prācyaṃ viṣam arasaṃ yad udīcyam |
athedam adharācyaṃ karambheṇa vi kalpate ||2||

karambhaṃ kṛtvā tiryaṃ pībaspākam udārathim |
kṣudhā kila tvā duṣṭano jakṣivānt sa na rūrupaḥ ||3||

vi te madaṃ madāvati śaram iva pātayāmasi |
pra tvā carum iva yeṣantaṃ vacasā sthāpayāmasi ||4||

pari grāmam ivācitaṃ vacasā sthāpayāmasi |
tiṣṭhā vṛkṣa iva sthāmny abhrikhāte na rūrupaḥ ||5||
pavastais tvā pary akrīṇan dūrśebhir ajinair uta |
prakrīr asi tvam oṣadhe 'bhrikhāte na rūrupaḥ ||6||

anāptā ye vaḥ prathamā yāni karmāṇi cakrire |
vīrān no atra mā dabhan tad va etat puro dadhe ||7||


bhūto bhūteṣu paya ā dadhāti sa bhūtānām adhipatir babhūva |
tasya mṛtyuś carati rājasūyaṃ sa rājā anu manyatām idaṃ ||1||

abhi prehi māpa vena ugraś cettā sapatnahā |
ā tiṣṭha mitravardhana tubhyam devā adhi bruvan ||2||

ātiṣṭhantaṃ pari viśve abhūṣaṃ chriyaṃ vasānaś carati svarociḥ |
mahat tad vṛṣṇo asurasya nāmā viśvarūpo amṛtāni tasthau ||3||

vyāghro adhi vaiyāghre vi kramasva diśo mahīḥ |
viśas tvā sarvā vāñchantv āpo divyāḥ payasvatīḥ ||4||

yā āpo divyāḥ payasā madanty antarikṣa uta vā pṛthivyām |
tāsāṃ tvā sarvāsām apām abhi ṣiñcāmi varcasā ||5||

abhi tvā varcasāsicann āpo divyāḥ payasvatīḥ |
yathāso mitravardhanas tathā tvā savitā karat ||6||

enā vyāghraṃ pariṣasvajānāḥ siṃhaṃ hinvanti mahate saubhagāya |
samudraṃ na subhuvas tasthivāṃsaṃ marmṛjyante dvīpinam apsv antaḥ ||7||



ehi jīvaṃ trāyamāṇaṃ parvatasyāsy akṣyam |
viśvebhir devair dattaṃ paridhir jīvanāya kam ||1||

paripāṇaṃ puruṣāṇāṃ paripāṇaṃ gavāṃ asi |
aśvānām arvatām paripāṇāya tasthiṣe ||2||

utāsi paripāṇam yātujambhanam āñjana |
utāmṛtasya tvaṃ vetthātho asi jīvabhojanam atho haritabheṣajam ||3||

yasyāñjana prasarpasy aṅgamaṅgam paruṣparuḥ |
tato yakṣmaṃ vi bādhasa ugro madhyamaśīr iva ||4||

nainaṃ prāpnoti śapatho na kṛtyā nābhiśocanam |
nainaṃ viṣkandham aśnute yas tvā bibharty āñjana ||5||

asanmantrād duṣvapnyād duṣkṛtāc chamalād uta |
durhārdaś cakṣuṣo ghorāt tasmān naḥ pāhy āñjana ||6||

idaṃ vidvān āñjana satyaṃ vakṣyāmi nānṛtam |
saneyam aśvaṃ gām aham ātmānaṃ tava pūruṣa ||7||

trayo dāsā āñjanasya takmā balāsa ād ahiḥ |
varṣiṣṭhaḥ parvatānāṃ trikakun nāma te pitā ||8||

yad āñjanaṃ traikakudam jātaṃ himavatas pari |
yātūṃś ca sarvāñ jambhayat sarvāś ca yātudhānyaḥ ||9||

4,9.10a yadi vāsi traikakudaṃ yadi yāmunam ucyase |
4,9.10c ubhe te bhadre nāmnī tābhyāṃ naḥ pāhy āñjana ||10||



vātāj jāto antarikṣād vidyuto jyotiṣas pari |
sa no hiraṇyajāḥ śaṅkhaḥ kṛśanaḥ pātv aṃhasaḥ ||1||

yo agrato rocanānāṃ samudrād adhi jajñiṣe |
śaṅkhena hatvā rakṣāṃsy attriṇo vi ṣahāmahe ||2||

śaṅkhenāmīvām amatiṃ śaṅkhenota sadānvāḥ |
śaṅkho no viśvabheṣajaḥ kṛśanaḥ pātv aṃhasaḥ ||3||

divi jātaḥ samudrajaḥ sindhutas pary ābhṛtaḥ |
sa no hiraṇyajāḥ śaṅkha āyuṣprataraṇo maṇiḥ ||4||

samudrāj jāto maṇir vṛtrāj jāto divākaraḥ |
so asmānt sarvataḥ pātu hetyā devāsurebhyaḥ ||5||

hiraṇyānām eko 'si somāt tvam adhi jajñiṣe |
rathe tvam asi darśata iṣudhau rocanas tvaṃ pra ṇa āyūṃṣi tāriṣat ||6||

devānām asthi kṛśanaṃ babhūva tad ātmanvac caraty apsv antaḥ |
tat te badhnāmy āyuṣe varcase balāya dīrghāyutvāya śataśāradāya kārśanas tvābhi rakṣatu ||7||



anaḍvān dādhāra pṛthivīm uta dyām anaḍvān dādhārorv antarikṣam |
anaḍvān dādhāra pradiśaḥ ṣaḍ urvīr anaḍvān viśvaṃ bhuvanam ā viveśa ||1||

anaḍvān indraḥ sa paśubhyo vi caṣṭe trayāṃ chakro vi mimīte adhvanaḥ |
bhūtaṃ bhaviṣyad bhuvanā duhānaḥ sarvā devānām carati vratāni ||2||

indro jāto manuṣyeṣv antar gharmas taptaś carati śośucānaḥ |
suprajāḥ sant sa udāre na sarṣad yo nāśnīyād anaḍuho vijānan ||3||

anaḍvān duhe sukṛtasya loka ainaṃ pyāyayati pavamānaḥ purastāt |
parjanyo dhārā maruta ūdho asya yajñaḥ payo dakṣiṇā doho asya ||4||

yasya neśe yajñapatir na yajño nāsya dāteśe na pratigrahītā |
yo viśvajid viśvabhṛd viśvakarmā gharmaṃ no brūta yatamaś catuṣpāt ||5||

yena devāḥ svar āruruhur hitvā śarīram amṛtasya nābhim |
tena geṣma sukṛtasya lokaṃ gharmasya vratena tapasā yaśasyavaḥ ||6||

indro rūpeṇāgnir vahena prajāpatiḥ parameṣṭhī virāṭ |
viśvānare akramata vaiśvānare akramatānaduhy akramata |
so 'dṛṃhayata so 'dhārayata ||7||

madhyam etad anaḍuho yatraiṣa vaha āhitaḥ |
etāvad asya prācīnaṃ yāvān pratyaṅ samāhitaḥ ||8||

yo vedānaduho dohān saptānupadasvataḥ |
prajāṃ ca lokaṃ cāpnoti tathā saptaṛṣayo viduḥ ||9||

4,11.10a padbhiḥ sedim avakrāmann irāṃ jaṅghābhir utkhidan |
4,11.10c srameṇānaḍvān kīlālaṃ kīnāśaś cābhi gachataḥ ||10||

4,11.11a dvādaśa vā etā rātrīr vratyā āhuḥ prajāpateḥ |
4,11.11c tatropa brahma yo veda tad vā anaḍuho vratam ||11||

4,11.12a duhe sāyaṃ duhe prātar duhe madhyaṃdinaṃ pari |
4,11.12c dohā ye asya saṃyanti tān vidmānupadasvataḥ ||12||



rohaṇy asi rohaṇy asthnaś chinnasya rohaṇī |
rohayedam arundhati ||1||

yat te riṣṭaṃ yat te dyuttam asti peṣṭraṃ ta ātmani |
dhātā tad bhadrayā punaḥ saṃ dadhat paruṣā paruḥ ||2||

saṃ te majjā majjñā bhavatu sam u te paruṣā paruḥ |
saṃ te māṃsasya visrastaṃ sam asthy api rohatu ||3||

majjā majñā saṃ dhīyatāṃ carmaṇā carma rohatu |
asṛk te asthi rohatu māṃsaṃ māṃsena rohatu ||4||

loma lomnā saṃ kalpayā tvacā saṃ kalpayā tvacam |
asṛk te asthi rohatu chinnaṃ saṃ dhehy oṣadhe ||5||

sa ut tiṣṭha prehi pra drava rathaḥ sucakraḥ |
supaviḥ sunābhiḥ prati tiṣṭhordhvaḥ ||6||

yadi kartaṃ patitvā saṃśaśre yadi vāśmā prahṛto jaghāna |
ṛbhū rathasyevāṅgāni saṃ dadhat paruṣā paruḥ ||7||



uta devā avahitaṃ devā un nayathā punaḥ |
utāgaś cakruṣaṃ devā devā jīvayathā punaḥ ||1||

dvāv imau vātau vāta ā sindhor ā parāvataḥ |
dakṣaṃ te anya āvātu vy anyo vātu yad rapaḥ ||2||

ā vāta vāhi bheṣajaṃ vi vāta vāhi yad rapaḥ |
tvaṃ hi viśvabheṣaja devānāṃ dūta īyase ||3||
trāyantām imaṃ devās trāyantāṃ marutāṃ gaṇāḥ |
trāyantāṃ viśvā bhūtāni yathāyam arapā asat ||4||

ā tvāgamaṃ śaṃtātibhir atho ariṣṭatātibhiḥ |
dakṣaṃ ta ugram ābhāriṣaṃ parā yakṣmaṃ suvāmi te ||5||

ayaṃ me hasto bhagavān ayaṃ me bhagavattaraḥ |
ayaṃ me viśvabheṣajo 'yaṃ śivābhimarśanaḥ ||6||

hastābhyāṃ daśaśākhābhyāṃ jihvā vācaḥ purogavī |
anāmayitnubhyāṃ hastābhyāṃ tābhyāṃ tvābhi mṛśāmasi ||7||



ajo hy agner ajaniṣṭa śokāt so apaśyaj janitāram agre |
tena devā devatām agrā āyan tena rohān ruruhur medhyāsaḥ ||1||

kramadhvam agninā nākam ukhyān hasteṣu bibhrataḥ |
divas pṛṣṭhaṃ svar gatvā miśrā devebhir ādhvam ||2||

pṛṣṭhāt pṛthivyā aham antarikṣam āruham antarikṣād divam āruham |
divo nākasya pṛṣṭhāt svar jyotir agām aham ||3||

svar yanto nāpekṣanta ā dyāṃ rohanti rodasī |
yajñaṃ ye viśvatodhāraṃ suvidvāṃso vitenire ||4||

agne prehi prathamo devatānāṃ cakṣur devānām uta mānuṣānām |
iyakṣamāṇā bhṛgubhiḥ sajoṣāḥ svar yantu yajamānāḥ svasti ||5||

ajam anajmi payasā ghṛtena divyaṃ suparnaṃ payasaṃ bṛhantam |
tena geṣma sukṛtasya lokaṃ svar ārohanto abhi nākam uttamam ||6||

pañcaudanaṃ pañcabhir aṅgulibhir darvyoddhara pañcadhaitam odanam |
prācyāṃ diśi śiro ajasya dhehi dakṣiṇāyāṃ diśi dakṣiṇaṃ dhehi pārśvam ||7||

pratīcyāṃ diśi bhasadam asya dhehy uttarasyāṃ diśy uttaraṃ dhehi pārśvam |
ūrdhvāyāṃ diśy ajasyānūkaṃ dhehi diśi dhruvāyāṃ dhehi pājasyam antarikṣe madhyato madhyam asya ||8||

śṛtam ajaṃ śṛtayā prorṇuhi tvacā sarvair aṅgaiḥ saṃbhṛtaṃ viśvarūpam |
sa ut tisṭheto abhi nākam uttamaṃ padbhiś caturbhiḥ prati tiṣṭha dikṣu ||9||



samutpatantu pradiśo nabhasvatīḥ sam abhrāṇi vātajūtāni yantu |
mahaṛṣabhasya nadato nabhasvato vāśrā āpaḥ pṛthivīṃ tarpayantu ||1||

sam īkṣayantu taviṣāḥ sudānavo 'pāṃ rasā oṣadhībhiḥ sacantām |
varṣasya sargā mahayantu bhūmiṃ pṛthag jāyantām oṣadhayo viśvarūpāḥ ||2||

sam īkṣayasva gāyato nabhāṃsy apām vegāsaḥ pṛthag ud vijantām |
varṣasya sargā mahayantu bhūmiṃ pṛthag jāyantām vīrudho viśvarūpāḥ ||3||

gaṇās tvopa gāyantu mārutāḥ parjanya ghoṣiṇaḥ pṛthak |
sargā varṣasya varṣato varṣantu pṛthivīm anu ||4||

ud īrayata marutaḥ samudratas tveṣo arko nabha ut pātayātha |
mahaṛṣabhasya nadato nabhasvato vāśrā āpaḥ pṛthivīṃ tarpayantu ||5||

abhi kranda stanayārdayodadhiṃ bhūmiṃ parjanya payasā sam aṅdhi |
tvayā sṛṣṭaṃ bahulam aitu varṣam āśāraiṣī kṛśagur etv astam ||6||

saṃ vo 'vantu sudānava utsā ajagarā uta |
marudbhiḥ pracyutā meghā varṣantu pṛthivīm anu ||7||

āśāmāśāṃ vi dyotatāṃ vātā vāntu diśodiśaḥ |
marudbhiḥ pracyutā meghāḥ saṃ yantu pṛthivīm anu ||8||

āpo vidyud abhraṃ varṣaṃ saṃ vo 'vantu sudānava utsā ajagarā uta |
marudbhiḥ pracyutā meghāḥ prāvantu pṛthivīm anu ||9||

4,15.10a apām agnis tanūbhiḥ saṃvidāno ya oṣadhīnām adhipā babhūva |
4,15.10c sa no varṣaṃ vanutāṃ jātavedāḥ prāṇaṃ prajābhyo amṛtaṃ divas pari ||10||

4,15.11a prajāpatiḥ salilād ā samudrād āpa īrayann udadhim ardayāti |
4,15.11c pra pyāyatāṃ vṛṣṇo aśvasya reto 'rvān etena stanayitnunehi ||11||

4,15.12a apo niṣiñcann asuraḥ pitā naḥ śvasantu gargarā apāṃ varuṇāva nīcīr apaḥ sṛja |
4,15.12c vadantu pṛśnibāhavo maṇḍūkā iriṇānu ||12||

4,15.13a saṃvatsaraṃ śaśayānā brāhmaṇā vratacāriṇaḥ |
4,15.13c vācam parjanyajinvitāṃ pra maṇdūkā avādiṣuḥ ||13||

4,15.14a upapravada maṇḍūki varṣaṃ ā vada tāduri |
4,15.14c madhye hradasya plavasva vigṛhya caturaḥ padaḥ ||14||

4,15.15a khaṇvakhā3i khaimakhā3i madhye taduri |
4,15.15c varṣaṃ vanudhvaṃ pitaro marutāṃ mana ichata ||15||

4,15.16a mahāntaṃ kośam ud acābhi ṣiñca savidyutaṃ bhavatu vātu vātaḥ |
4,15.16c tanvatāṃ yajñaṃ bahudhā visṛṣṭā ānandinīr oṣadhayo bhavantu ||16||



bṛhann eṣām adhiṣṭhātā antikād iva paśyati |
ya stāyan manyate carant sarvaṃ devā idaṃ viduḥ ||1||

yas tiṣṭhati carati yaś ca vañcati yo nilāyaṃ carati yaḥ prataṅkam |
dvau saṃniṣadya yan mantrayete rājā tad veda varuṇas tṛtīyaḥ ||2||

uteyaṃ bhūmir varuṇasya rājña utāsau dyaur bṛhatī dūreantā |
uto samudrau varuṇasya kukṣī utāsminn alpa udake nilīnaḥ ||3||

uta yo dyām atisarpāt parastān na sa mucyātai varuṇasya rājñaḥ |
diva spaśaḥ pra carantīdam asya sahasrākṣā ati paśyanti bhūmim ||4||

sarvaṃ tad rājā varuṇo vi caṣṭe yad antarā rodasī yat parastāt |
saṃkhyātā asya nimiṣo janānām akṣān iva śvaghnī ni minoti tāni ||5||

ye te pāśā varuṇa saptasapta tredhā tiṣṭhanti viṣitā ruṣantaḥ |
chinantu sarve anṛtaṃ vadantaṃ yaḥ satyavādy ati taṃ sṛjantu ||6||

śatena pāśair abhi dhehi varuṇainaṃ mā te mocy anṛtavāṅ nṛcakṣaḥ |
āstāṃ jālma udaraṃ śraṃśayitvā kośa ivābandhaḥ parikṛtyamānaḥ ||7||

yaḥ samābhyo varuṇo yo vyābhyo yaḥ saṃdeśyo varuṇo yo videśyo |
yo daivo varuṇo yaś ca mānuṣaḥ ||8||

tais tvā sarvair abhi ṣyāmi pāśair asāv āmuṣyāyaṇāmuṣyāḥ putra |
tān u te sarvān anusaṃdiśāmi ||9||


īśāṇāṃ tvā bheṣajānām ujjeṣa ā rabhāmahe |
cakre sahasravīryam sarvasmā oṣadhe tvā ||1||

satyajitaṃ śapathayāvanīṃ sahamānāṃ punaḥsarām |
sarvāḥ sam ahvy oṣadhīr ito naḥ pārayād iti ||2||

yā śaśāpa śapanena yāghaṃ mūram ādadhe |
yā rasasya haraṇāya jātam ārebhe tokam attu sā ||3||

yāṃ te cakrur āme pātre yāṃ cakrur nīlalohite |
āme māṃse kṛtyāṃ yāṃ cakrus tayā kṛtyākṛto jahi ||4||

dauṣvapnyaṃ daurjīvityaṃ rakṣo abhvam arāyyaḥ |
durṇāmnīḥ sarvā durvācas tā asman nāśayāmasi ||5||

kṣudhāmāraṃ tṛṣṇāmāram agotām anapatyatām |
apāmārga tvayā vayaṃ sarvaṃ tad apa mṛjmahe ||6||

tṛṣṇāmāraṃ kṣudhāmāraṃ atho akṣaparājayam |
apāmārga tvayā vayaṃ sarvaṃ tad apa mṛjmahe ||7||
