apāmārga oṣadhīnāṃ sarvāsām eka id vaśī |
tena te mṛjma āsthitam atha tvam agadaś cara ||8||



samaṃ jyotiḥ sūryeṇāhnā rātrī samāvatī |
kṛṇomi satyam ūtaye 'rasāḥ santu kṛtvarīḥ ||1||

yo devāḥ kṛtyāṃ kṛtvā harād aviduṣo gṛham |
vatso dhārur iva mātaraṃ taṃ pratyag upa padyatām ||2||

amā kṛtvā pāpmānaṃ yas tenānyaṃ jighāṃsati |
aśmānas tasyāṃ dagdhāyāṃ bahulāḥ phaṭ karikrati ||3||

sahasradhāman viśikhān vigrīvāṃ chāyayā tvam |
prati sma cakruṣe kṛtyāṃ priyāṃ priyāvate hara ||4||

anayāham oṣadhyā sarvāḥ kṛtyā adūduṣam |
yāṃ kṣetre cakrur yāṃ goṣu yāṃ vā te puruṣeṣu ||5||

yaś cakāra na śaśāka kartuṃ śaśre pādam aṅgurim |
cakāra bhadram asmabhyam ātmane tapanam tu saḥ ||6||

apāmārgo 'pa mārṣṭu kṣetriyaṃ śapathaś ca yaḥ |
apāha yātudhānīr apa sarvā arāyyaḥ ||7||

apamṛjya yātudhānān apa sarvā arāyyaḥ |
apāmārga tvayā vayaṃ sarvaṃ tad apa mṛjmahe ||8||



uto asy abandhukṛd uto asi nu jāmikṛt |
uto kṛtyākṛtaḥ prajāṃ nadam ivā chindhi vārṣikam ||1||

brāhmaṇena paryuktāsi kaṇvena nārṣadena |
senevaiṣi tviṣīmatī na tatra bhayam asti yatra prāpnoṣy oṣadhe ||2||

agram eṣy oṣadhīnāṃ jyotiṣevābhidīpayan |
uta trātāsi pākasyātho hantāsi rakṣasaḥ ||3||

yad ado devā asurāṃs tvayāgre nirakurvata |
tatas tvam adhy oṣadhe 'pāmārgo ajāyathāḥ ||4||

vibhindatī śataśākhā vibhindan nāma te pitā |
pratyag vi bhindhi tvaṃ taṃ yo asmāṃ abhidāsati ||5||

asad bhūmyāḥ sam abhavat tad yām eti mahad vyacaḥ |
tad vai tato vidhūpāyat pratyak kartāram ṛchatu ||6||

pratyaṅ hi saṃbabhūvitha pratīcīnaphalas tvam |
sarvān mac chapathām adhi varīyo yāvayā vadham ||7||

śatena mā pari pāhi sahasreṇābhi rakṣā mā |
indras te vīrudhāṃ pata ugra ojmānam ā dadhat ||8||


ā paśyati prati paśyati parā paśyati paśyati |
divam antarikṣam ād bhūmiṃ sarvaṃ tad devi paśyati ||1||

tisro divas tisraḥ pṛthivīḥ ṣaṭ cemāḥ pradiśāḥ pṛthak |
tvayāhaṃ sarvā bhūtāni paśyāni devy oṣadhe ||2||

divyasya suparṇasya tasya hāsi kanīnikā |
sā bhūmim ā rurohitha vahyaṃ śrāntā vadhūr iva ||3||

tāṃ me sahasrākṣo devo dakṣiṇe hasta ā dadhat |
tayāhaṃ sarvaṃ paśyāmi yaś ca śūdra utāryaḥ ||4||

āviṣ kṛṇuṣva rūpāni mātmānam apa gūhathāḥ |
atho sahasracakṣo tvaṃ prati paśyāḥ kimīdinaḥ ||5||

darśaya mā yātudhānān darśaya yātudhānyaḥ |
piśācānt sarvān darśayeti tvā rabha oṣadhe ||6||

kaśyapasya cakṣur asi śunyāś ca caturakṣyāḥ |
vīdhre sūryam iva sarpantaṃ mā piśācaṃ tiras karaḥ ||7||

ud agrabhaṃ paripāṇād yātudhānaṃ kimīdinam |
tenāhaṃ sarvaṃ paśyāmy uta śūdram utāryam ||8||

yo antarikṣeṇa patati divam yaś ca atisarpati |
bhūmiṃ yo manyate nāthaṃ taṃ piśācam pra darśaya ||9||



ā gāvo agmann uta bhadram akrant sīdantu goṣṭhe raṇayantv asme |
prajāvatīḥ pururūpā iha syur indrāya pūrvīr uṣaso duhānāḥ ||1||

indro yajvane gṛṇate ca śikṣata uped dadāti na svaṃ muṣāyati |
bhūyobhūyo rayim id asya vardhayann abhinne khilye ni dadhāti devayum ||2||

na tā naśanti na dabhāti taskaro nāsām āmitro vyathir ā dadharṣati |
devāṃś ca yābhir yajate dadāti ca jyog it tābhiḥ sacate gopatiḥ saha ||3||

na tā arvā reṇukakāṭo 'śnute na saṃskṛtatram upa yanti tā abhi |
urugāyam abhayaṃ tasya tā anu gāvo martasya vi caranti yajvanaḥ ||4||

gāvo bhago gāva indro ma ichād gāva somasya prathamasya bhakṣaḥ |
imā yā gāvaḥ sa janāsa indra ichāmi hṛdā manasā cid indram ||5||

yūyaṃ gāvo medayatha kṛśaṃ cid aśrīraṃ cit kṛṇuthā supratīkam |
bhadraṃ gṛhaṃ kṛṇutha bhadravāco bṛhad vo vaya ucyate sabhāsu ||6||

prajāvatīḥ sūyavase ruśantīḥ śuddhā apaḥ suprapāṇe pibantīḥ |
mā va stena īśata māghaśaṃsaḥ pari vo rudrasya hetir vṛṇaktu ||7||



imam indra vardhaya kṣatriyaṃ me imaṃ viśām ekavṛṣaṃ kṛṇu tvam |
nir amitrān akṣṇuhy asya sarvāṃs tān randhayāsmā ahamuttareṣu ||1||

emaṃ bhaja grāme aśveṣu goṣu niṣ ṭaṃ bhaja yo amitro asya |
varṣma kṣatrāṇām ayam astu rājendra śatruṃ randhaya sarvam asmai ||2||

ayam astu dhanapatir dhanānām ayaṃ viśāṃ viśpatir astu rājā |
asminn indra mahi varcāṃsi dhehy avarcasaṃ kṛṇuhi śatrum asya ||3||

asmai dyāvāpṛthivī bhūri vāmaṃ duhāthāṃ gharmadughe iva dhenū |
ayaṃ rājā priya indrasya bhūyāt priyo gavām oṣadhīnāṃ paśūnām ||4||

yunajmi ta uttarāvantam indraṃ yena jayanti na parājayante |
yas tvā karad ekavṛṣaṃ janānām uta rājñām uttamaṃ mānavānām ||5||

uttaras tvam adhare te sapatnā ye ke ca rājan pratiśatravas te |
ekavṛṣa indrasakhā jigīvāṃ chatrūyatām ā bharā bhojanāni ||6||

siṃhapratīko viśo addhi sarvā vyāghrapratīko 'va bādhasva śatrūn |
ekavṛṣa indrasakhā jigīvāṃ chatrūyatām ā khidā bhojanāni ||7||



agner manve prathamasya pracetasaḥ pāñcajanyasya bahudhā yam indhate |
viśoviśaḥ praviśivāṃsam īmahe sa no muñcatv aṃhasaḥ ||1||

yathā havyaṃ vahasi jātavedo yathā yajñaṃ kalpayasi prajānan |
evā devebhyaḥ sumatiṃ na ā vaha sa no muñcatv aṃhasaḥ ||2||

yāmanyāmann upayuktaṃ vahiṣṭhaṃ karmaṅkarmann ābhagam agnim īḍe |
rakṣohaṇaṃ yajñavṛdhaṃ ghṛtāhutaṃ sa no muñcatv aṃhasaḥ ||3||

sujātaṃ jātavedasam agniṃ vaiśvānaraṃ vibhum |
havyavāhaṃ havāmahe sa no muñcatv aṃhasaḥ ||4||

yena ṛṣayo balam adyotayan yujā yenāsurāṇām ayuvanta māyāḥ |
yenāgninā paṇīn indro jigāya sa no muñcatv aṃhasaḥ ||5||

yena devā amṛtam anvavindan yenauṣadhīr madhumatīr akṛṇvan |
yena devāḥ svar ābharant sa no muñcatv aṃhasaḥ ||6||

yasyedaṃ pradiśi yad virocate yaj jātaṃ janitavyaṃ ca kevalam |
staumy agniṃ nāthito johavīmi sa no muñcatv aṃhasaḥ ||7||



indrasya manmahe śaśvad id asya manmahe vṛtraghna stomā upa mema āguḥ |
yo dāśuṣaḥ sukṛto havam eti sa no muñcatv aṃhasaḥ ||1||

ya ugrīṇām ugrabāhur yayur yo dānavānāṃ balam āruroja |
yena jitāḥ sindhavo yena gāvaḥ sa no muñcatv aṃhasaḥ ||2||

yaś carṣaṇipro vṛṣabhaḥ svarvid yasmai grāvāṇaḥ pravadanti nṛmṇam |
yasyādhvaraḥ saptahotā madiṣṭhaḥ sa no muñcatv aṃhasaḥ ||3||

yasya vaśāsa ṛṣabhāsa ukṣaṇo yasmai mīyante svaravaḥ svarvide |
yasmai śukraḥ pavate brahmaśumbhitaḥ sa no muñcatv aṃhasaḥ ||4||

yasya juṣṭiṃ sominaḥ kāmayante yaṃ havanta iṣumantaṃ gaviṣṭau |
yasminn arkaḥ śiśriye yasminn ojaḥ sa no muñcatv aṃhasaḥ ||5||

yaḥ prathamaḥ karmakṛtyāya jajñe yasya vīryam prathamasyānubuddham |
yenodyato vajro 'bhyāyatāhiṃ sa no muñcatv aṃhasaḥ ||6||

yaḥ saṃgrāmān nayati saṃ yudhe vaśī yaḥ puṣṭāni saṃsṛjati dvayāni |
staumīndraṃ nāthito johavīmi sa no muñcatv aṃhasaḥ ||7||



vāyoḥ savitur vidathāni manmahe yāv ātmanvad viśatho yau ca rakṣathaḥ |
yau viśvasya paribhū babhūvathus tau no muñcatam aṃhasaḥ ||1||

yayoḥ saṃkhyātā varimā pārhivāni yābhyāṃ rajo yupitam antarikṣe |
yayoḥ prāyaṃ nānv ānaśe kaś cana tau no muñcatam aṃhasaḥ ||2||

tava vrate ni viśante janāsas tvayy udite prerate citrabhāno |
yuvaṃ vāyo savitā ca bhuvanāni rakṣathas tau no muñcatam aṃhasaḥ ||3||

apeto vāyo savitā ca duṣkṛtam apa rakṣāṃsi śimidāṃ ca sedhatam |
saṃ hy ūrjayā sṛjathaḥ saṃ balena tau no muñcatam aṃhasaḥ ||4||

rayiṃ me poṣaṃ savitota vāyus tanū dakṣam ā suvatāṃ suśevam |
ayakṣmatātiṃ maha iha dhattaṃ tau no muñcatam aṃhasaḥ ||5||

pra sumatiṃ savitar vāya ūtaye mahasvantaṃ matsaraṃ mādayāthaḥ |
arvāg vāmasya pravato ni yachataṃ tau no muñcatam aṃhasaḥ ||6||

upa śreṣṭhā na āśiṣo devayor dhāmann asthiran |
staumi devaṃ savitāraṃ ca vāyuṃ tau no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ||7||



manve vāṃ dyāvāpṛthivī subhojasau sacetasau ye aprathethām amitā yojanāni |
pratiṣṭhe hy abhavataṃ vasūnāṃ te no muñcatam aṃhasaḥ ||1||

pratiṣṭhe hy abhavataṃ vasūnāṃ pravṛddhe devī subhage urūcī |
dyāvāpṛthivī bhavataṃ me syone te no muñcatam aṃhasaḥ ||2||

asantāpe sutapasau huve 'ham urvī gambhīre kavibhir namasye |
dyāvāpṛthivī bhavataṃ me syone te no muñcatam aṃhasaḥ ||3||

ye amṛtaṃ bibhṛtho ye havīṃṣi ye srotyā bibhṛtho ye manuṣyān |
dyāvāpṛthivī bhavataṃ me syone te no muñcatam aṃhasaḥ ||4||

ye usriyā bibhṛtho ye vanaspatīn yayor vāṃ viśvā bhuvanāny antaḥ |
dyāvāpṛthivī bhavataṃ me syone te no muñcatam aṃhasaḥ ||5||

ye kīlālena tarpayatho ye ghṛtena yābhyām ṛte na kiṃ cana śaknuvanti |
dyāvāpṛthivī bhavataṃ me syone te no muñcatam aṃhasaḥ ||6||

yan medam abhiśocati yenayena vā kṛtaṃ pauruṣeyān na daivāt |
staumi dyāvāpṛthivī nāthito johavīmi te no muñcatam aṃhasaḥ ||7||



marutāṃ manve adhi me bruvantu premaṃ vājaṃ vājasāte avantu |
āśūn iva suyamān ahva ūtaye te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ||1||

utsam akṣitaṃ vyacanti ye sadā ya āsiñcanti rasam oṣadhīṣu |
puro dadhe marutaḥ pṛśnimātṝṃs te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ||2||
payo dhenūnāṃ rasam oṣadhīnāṃ javam arvatāṃ kavayo ya invatha |
śagmā bhavantu maruto naḥ syonās te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ||3||

apaḥ samudrād divam ud vahanti divas pṛthivīm abhi ye sṛjanti |
ye adbhir īśānā marutaś caranti te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ||4||

ye kīlālena tarpayanti ye ghṛtena ye vā vayo medasā saṃsṛjanti |
ye adbhir īśānā maruto varṣayanti te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ||5||

yadīd idaṃ maruto mārutena yadi devā daivyenedṛg āra |
yūyam īśidhve vasavas tasya niṣkṛtes te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ||6||

tigmam anīkam viditaṃ sahasvan mārutaṃ śardhaḥ pṛtanāsūgram |
staumi maruto nāthito johavīmi te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ||7||



bhavāśarvau manve vāṃ tasya vittaṃ yayor vām idaṃ pradiśi yad virocate |
yāv asyeśāthe dvipado yau catuṣpadas tau no muñcatam aṃhasaḥ ||1||

yayor abhyabhva uta yad dūre cid yau viditāv iṣubhṛtām asiṣṭhau |
yāv asyeśathe dvipado yau catuṣpadas tau no muñcatam aṃhasaḥ ||2||

sahasrākṣau vṛtrahanā huvehaṃ dūregavyūtī stuvann emy ugrau |
yāv asyeśathe dvipado yau catuṣpadas tau no muñcatam aṃhasaḥ ||3||

yāv ārebhāthe bahu sākam agre pra ced asrāṣṭram abhibhāṃ janeṣu |
yāv asyeśathe dvipado yau catuṣpadas tau no muñcatam aṃhasaḥ ||4||

yayor vadhān nāpapadyate kaś canāntar deveṣūta mānuṣeṣu |
yāv asyeśathe dvipado yau catuṣpadas tau no muñcatam aṃhasaḥ ||5||

yaḥ kṛtyākṛn mūlakṛd yātudhāno ni tasmin dhattaṃ vajram ugrau |
yāv asyeśathe dvipado yau catuṣpadas tau no muñcatam aṃhasaḥ ||6||

adhi no brūtaṃ pṛtanāsūgrau saṃ vajreṇa sṛjataṃ yaḥ kimīdī |
staumi bhavāśarvau nāthito johavīmi tau no muñcatam aṃhasaḥ ||7||



manve vāṃ mitrāvaruṇāv ṛtāvṛdhau sacetasau druhvaṇo yau nudethe |
pra satyāvānam avatho bhareṣu tau no muñcatam aṃhasaḥ ||1||

sacetasau druhvaṇo yau nudethe pra satyāvānam avatho bhareṣu |
yau gachatho nṛcakṣasau babhruṇā sutaṃ tau no muñcatam aṃhasaḥ ||2||

yāv aṅgirasam avatho yāv agastiṃ mitrāvaruṇā jamadagnim attrim |
yau kaśyapam avatho yau vasiṣṭhaṃ tau no muñcatam aṃhasaḥ ||3||

yau śyāvāśvam avatho vādhryaśvaṃ mitrāvaruṇā purumīḍham attrim |
yau vimadam avatho saptavadhriṃ tau no muñcatam aṃhasaḥ ||4||

yau bharadvājam avatho yau gaviṣṭhiraṃ viśvāmitraṃ varuṇa mitra kutsam |
yau kakṣīvantam avatho prota kaṇvaṃ tau no muñcatam aṃhasaḥ ||5||

yau medhātithim avatho yau triśokaṃ mitrāvaruṇāv uśanām kāvyaṃ yau |
yau gotamam avatho prota mugdalaṃ tau no muñcatam aṃhasaḥ ||6||

yayo rathaḥ satyavartma rjuraśmir mithuyā carantam abhiyāti dūṣayan |
staumi mitrāvaruṇau nāthito johavīmi tau no muñcatam aṃhasaḥ ||7||



ahaṃ rudrebhir vasubhiś carāmy aham ādityair uta viśvadevaiḥ |
ahaṃ mitrāvarunobhā bibharmy aham indrāgnī aham aśvinobhā ||1||

ahaṃ rāṣṭrī saṃgamanī vasūnāṃ cikituṣī prathamā yajñiyānām |
tāṃ mā devā vy adadhuḥ purutrā bhūristhātrāṃ bhūry āveśayantaḥ ||2||

aham eva svayam idaṃ vadāmi juṣṭaṃ devānām uta mānuṣāṇām |
yaṃ kāmaye tantam ugraṃ kṛṇomi taṃ brahmāṇaṃ tam ṛṣiṃ taṃ sumedhām ||3||

mayā so 'nnam atti yo vipaśyati yaḥ prāṇati ya īm śṛṇoty uktam |
amantavo māṃ ta upa kṣiyanti śrudhi śruta śruddheyaṃ te vadāmi ||4||

ahaṃ rudrāya dhanur ā tanomi brahmadviṣe śarave hantavā u |
ahaṃ janāya samadaṃ kṛṇomi aham dyāvāpṛthivī ā viveśa ||5||

ahaṃ somam āhanasaṃ bibharmy ahaṃ tvaṣṭāram uta pūṣaṇaṃ bhagam |
ahaṃ dadhāmi draviṇā haviṣmate suprāvyā yajamānāya sunvate ||6||

ahaṃ suve pitaram asya mūrdhan mama yonir apsv antaḥ samudre |
tato vi tiṣṭhe bhuvanāni viśvotāmūṃ dyāṃ varṣmaṇopa spṛśāmi ||7||

aham eva vātaiva pra vāmy ārabhamāṇā bhuvanāni viśvā |
paro divā para enā pṛthivyaitāvatī mahimnā saṃ babhūva ||8||



tvayā manyo saratham ārujanto harṣamāṇā hṛṣitāso marutvan |
tigmeṣava āyudhā saṃśiśānā upa pra yantu naro agnirūpāḥ ||1||

agnir iva manyo tviṣitaḥ sahasva senānīr naḥ sahure hūta edhi |
hatvāya śatrūn vi bhajasva veda ojo mimāno vi mṛdho nudasva ||2||

sahasva manyo abhimātim asmai rujan mṛṇan pramṛṇan prehi śatrūn |
ugraṃ te pājo nanv ā rurudhre vaśī vaśaṃ nayāsā ekaja tvam ||3||

eko bahūnām asi manya īḍitā viśaṃviśam yuddhāya saṃ śiśādhi |
akṛttaruk tvayā yujā vayaṃ dyumantaṃ ghoṣam vijayāya kṛṇmasi ||4||

vijeṣakṛd indra ivānavabravo 'smākaṃ manyo adhipā bhaveha |
priyaṃ te nāma sahure gṛṇīmasi vidmā tam utsaṃ yata ābabhūtha ||5||

ābhūtyā sahajā vajra sāyaka saho bibharṣi sahabhūta uttaram |
kratvā no manyo saha medy edhi mahādhanasya puruhūta saṃsṛji ||6||

saṃsṛṣṭaṃ dhanam ubhayaṃ samākṛtam asmabhyaṃ dhattāṃ varuṇaś ca manyuḥ |
bhiyo dadhānā hṛdayeṣu śatravaḥ parājitāso apa ni layantām ||7||



yas te manyo 'vidhad vajra sāyaka saha ojaḥ puṣyati viśvam ānuṣak |
sāhyāma dāsam āryaṃ tvayā yujā vayaṃ sahaskṛtena sahasā sahasvatā ||1||

manyur indro manyur evāsa devo manyur hotā varuṇo jātavedāḥ |
manyuṃ viśa īḍate mānuṣīr yāḥ pahi no manyo tapasā sajoṣāḥ ||2||

abhīhi manyo tavasas tavīyān tapasā yujā vi jahi śatrūn |
amitrahā vṛtrahā dasyuhā ca viśvā vasūny ā bharā tvaṃ naḥ ||3||

tvaṃ hi manyo abhibhūtyojāḥ svayaṃbhūr bhāmo abhimātiṣāhaḥ |
viśvacarṣaṇiḥ sahuriḥ sahīyān asmāsv ojaḥ pṛtanāsu dhehi ||4||

abhāgaḥ sann apa pareto asmi tava kratvā taviṣasya pracetaḥ |
taṃ tvā manyo akratur jihīḍāhaṃ svā tanūr baladāvā na ehi ||5||

ayaṃ te asmy upa na ehy arvāṅ pratīcīnaḥ sahure viśvadāvan |
manyo vajrinn abhi na ā vavṛtsva hanāva dasyūṃr uta bodhy āpeḥ ||6||

abhi prehi dakṣiṇato bhavā no 'dhā vṛtrāṇi jaṅghanāva bhūri |
juhomi te dharuṇaṃ madhvo agram ubhāv upāṃśu prathamā pibāva ||7||



apa naḥ śośucad agham agne śuśugdhy ā rayim |
apa naḥ śośucad agham ||1||

sukṣetriyā sugātuyā vasūyā ca yajāmahe |
apa naḥ śośucad agham ||2||

pra yad bhandiṣṭha eṣāṃ prāsmākāsaś ca sūrayaḥ |
apa naḥ śośucad agham ||3||

pra yat te agne sūrayo jāyemahi pra te vayam |
apa naḥ śośucad agham ||4||

pra yad agneḥ sahasvato viśvato yanti bhānavaḥ |
apa naḥ śośucad agham ||5||

tvaṃ hi viśvatomukha viśvataḥ paribhūr asi |
apa naḥ śośucad agham ||6||

dviṣo no viśvatomukhāti nāveva pāraya |
apa naḥ śośucad agham ||7||

sa naḥ sindhum iva nāvāti parṣa svastaye |
apa naḥ śośucad agham ||8||



brahmāsya śīrṣaṃ bṛhad asya pṛṣṭhaṃ vāmadevyam udaram odanasya |
chandāṃsi pakṣau mukham asya satyaṃ viṣṭārī jātas tapaso'dhi yajñaḥ ||1||

anasthāḥ pūtāḥ pavanena śuddhāḥ śucayaḥ śucim api yanti lokam |
naiṣāṃ śiśnaṃ pra dahati jātavedāḥ svarge loke bahu straiṇam eṣām ||2||

viṣṭāriṇam odanaṃ ye pacanti nainān avartiḥ sacate kadā cana |
āste yama upa yāti devānt saṃ gandharvair madate somyebhiḥ ||3||

viṣṭāriṇam odanam ye pacanti nainān yamaḥ pari muṣṇāti retaḥ |
rathī ha bhūtvā rathayāna īyate pakṣī ha bhūtvāti divaḥ sam eti ||4||

eṣa yajñānāṃ vitato vahiṣṭho viṣṭāriṇaṃ paktvā divam ā viveśa |
āṇḍīkaṃ kumudaṃ saṃ tanoti bisaṃ śālūkaṃ śaphako mulālī |
etās tvā dhārā upa yantu sarvāḥ svarge loke madhumat pinvamānā upa tvā tiṣṭhantu puṣkariṇīḥ samantāḥ ||5||

ghṛtahradā madhukūlāḥ surodakāḥ kṣīreṇa pūrṇā udakena dadhnā |
etās tvā dhārā upa yantu sarvāḥ svarge loke madhumat pinvamānā upa tvā tiṣṭhantu puṣkariṇīḥ samantāḥ ||6||

caturaḥ kumbhāṃś caturdhā dadāmi kṣīreṇa pūrnāṃ udakena dadhnā |
etās tvā dhārā upa yantu sarvāḥ svarge loke madhumat pinvamānā upa tvā tiṣṭhantu puṣkariṇīḥ samantāḥ ||7||

imam odanaṃ ni dadhe brāhmaṇeṣu viṣṭāriṇaṃ lokajitaṃ svargam |
sa me mā kṣeṣṭa svadhayā pinvamāno viśvarūpā dhenuḥ kāmadughā me astu ||8||



yam odanaṃ prathamajā ṛtasya prajāpatis tapasā brahmaṇe 'pacat |
yo lokānāṃ vidhṛtir nābhireṣāt tenaudanenāti tarāṇi mṛtyum ||1||

yenātaran bhūtakṛto 'ti mṛtyuṃ yam anvavindan tapasā śrameṇa |
yaṃ papāca brahmaṇe brahma pūrvaṃ tenaudanenāti tarāṇi mṛtyum ||2||

yo dādhāra pṛthivīṃ viśvabhojasaṃ yo antarikṣam āpṛṇād rasena |
yo astabhnād divam ūrdhvo mahimnā tenaudanenāti tarāṇi mṛtyum ||3||

yasmān māsā nirmitās triṃśadarāḥ saṃvatsaro yasmān nirmito dvādaśāraḥ |
ahorātrā yaṃ pariyanto nāpus tenaudanenāti tarāṇi mṛtyum ||4||

yaḥ prāṇadaḥ prāṇadavān babhūva yasmai lokā ghṛtavantaḥ kṣaranti |
jyotiṣmatīḥ pradiśo yasya sarvās tenaudanenāti tarāṇi mṛtyum ||5||

yasmāt pakvād amṛtaṃ saṃbabhūva yo gāyatryā adhipatir babhūva |
yasmin vedā nihitā viśvarūpās tenaudanenāti tarāṇi mṛtyum ||6||

ava bādhe dviṣantaṃ devapīyuṃ sapatnā ye me 'pa te bhavantu |
brahmaudanaṃ viśvajitaṃ pacāmi śṛṇvantu me śraddadhānasya devāḥ ||7||



tānt satyaujāḥ pra dahatv agnir vaiśvānaro vṛṣā |
yo no durasyād dipsāc cātho yo no arātiyāt ||1||

yo no dipsād adipsato dipsato yaś ca dipsati |
vaiśvānarasya daṃṣṭrayor agner api dadhāmi tam ||2||

ya āgare mṛgayante pratikrośe 'māvāsye |
kravyādo anyān dipsataḥ sarvāṃs tānt sahasā sahe ||3||

sahe piśācānt sahasaiṣāṃ draviṇaṃ dade |
sarvān durasyato hanmi saṃ ma ākūtir ṛdhyatām ||4||

ye devās tena hāsante sūryeṇa mimate javam |
nadīṣu parvateṣu ye saṃ taiḥ paśubhir vide ||5||

tapano asmi piśācānāṃ vyāghro gomatām iva |
śvānaḥ siṃham iva dṛṣṭvā te na vindante nyañcanam ||6||

na piśācaiḥ saṃ śaknomi na stenaiḥ na vanargubhiḥ |
piśācās tasmān naśyanti yam ahaṃ grāmam āviśe ||7||

yaṃ grāmam āviśata idam ugraṃ saho mama |
piśācās tasmān naśyanti na pāpam upa jānate ||8||

ye mā krodhayanti lapitā hastinaṃ maśakā iva |
tān ahaṃ manye durhitān jane alpaśayūn iva ||9||

4,36.10a abhi taṃ nirṛtir dhattām aśvam iva aśvābhidhānyā |
4,36.10c malvo yo mahyaṃ krudhyati sa u pāśān na mucyate ||10||



tvayā pūrvam atharvāṇo jaghnū rakṣāṃsy oṣadhe |
tvayā jaghāna kaśyapas tvayā kaṇvo agastyaḥ ||1||

tvayā vayam apsaraso gandharvāṃs cātayāmahe |
ajaśṛṅgy aja rakṣaḥ sarvān gandhena nāśaya ||2||

nadīṃ yantv apsaraso 'pāṃ tāram avaśvasam |
gulgulūḥ pīlā nalady aukṣagandhiḥ pramandanī |
tat paretāpsarasaḥ pratibuddhā abhūtana ||3||

yatrāśvatthā nyagrodhā mahāvṛkṣāḥ śikhaṇḍinaḥ |
tat paretāpsarasaḥ pratibuddhā abhūtana ||4||

yatra vaḥ preṅkhā haritā arjunā uta yatrāghātāḥ karkaryaḥ saṃvadanti |
tat paretāpsarasaḥ pratibuddhā abhūtana ||5||

eyam agann oṣadhīnāṃ vīrudhām vīryāvatī |
ajaśṛṅgy arāṭakī tīkṣṇaśṛṅgī vyṛṣatu ||6||

ānṛtyataḥ śikhaṇḍino gandharvasyāpsarāpateḥ |
bhinadmi muṣkāv api yāmi śepaḥ ||7||

bhīmā indrasya hetayaḥ śataṃ ṛṣṭīr ayasmayīḥ |
tābhir haviradān gandharvān avakādān vyṛṣatu ||8||

bhīmā indrasya hetayaḥ śataṃ ṛṣṭīr hiraṇyayīḥ |
tābhir haviradān gandharvān avakādān vyṛṣatu ||9||
4,37.10a avakādān abhiśocān apsu jyotaya māmakān |
4,37.10c piśācānt sarvān oṣadhe pra mṛṇīhi sahasva ca ||10||

4,37.11a śvevaikaḥ kapir ivaikaḥ kumāraḥ sarvakeśakaḥ |
4,37.11c priyo dṛśa iva bhūtvā gandharvaḥ sacate striyas |
4,37.11e tam ito nāśayāmasi brahmaṇā vīryāvatā ||11||

4,37.12a jāyā id vo apsaraso gandharvāḥ patayo yuyam |
4,37.12c apa dhāvatāmartyā martyān mā sacadhvam ||12||


udbhindatīṃ saṃjayantīm apsarāṃ sādhudevinīm |
glahe kṛtāni kṛṇvānām apsarāṃ tām iha huve ||1||
vicinvatīm ākirantīm apsarāṃ sādhudevinīm |
glahe kṛtāni gṛhṇānām apsarāṃ tām iha huve ||2||

yāyaiḥ parinṛtyaty ādadānā kṛtaṃ glahāt |
sā naḥ kṛtāni sīṣatī prahām āpnotu māyayā |
sā naḥ payasvaty aitu mā no jaiṣur idaṃ dhanam ||3||

yā akṣeṣu pramodante śucaṃ krodhaṃ ca bibhratī |
ānandinīṃ pramodinīm apsarāṃ tām iha huve ||4||

sūryasya raśmīn anu yāḥ sañcaranti marīcīr vā yā anusañcaranti |
yāsām ṛṣabho dūrato vājinīvānt sadyaḥ sarvān lokān paryeti rakṣan |
sa na aitu homam imaṃ jusāṇo 'ntarikṣeṇa saha vājinīvān ||5||

antarikṣena saha vājinīvan karkīṃ vatsām iha rakṣa vājin |
ime te stokā bahulā ehy arvāṅ iyaṃ te karkīha te mano 'stu ||6||

antarikṣeṇa saha vājinīvan karkīṃ vatsām iha rakṣa vājin |
ayaṃ ghāso ayaṃ vraja iha vatsāṃ ni badhnīmaḥ |
yathānāma va īśmahe svāhā ||7||



pṛthivyām agnaye sam anamant sa ārdhnot |
yathā pṛthivyām agnaye samanamann evā mahyaṃ saṃnamaḥ saṃ namantu ||1||

pṛthivī dhenus tasyā agnir vatsaḥ |
sā me 'gninā vatseneṣam ūrjaṃ kāmaṃ duhām |
āyuḥ prathamaṃ prajāṃ poṣaṃ rayiṃ svāhā ||2||

antarikṣe vāyave sam anamant sa ārdhnot |
yathāntarikṣe vāyave samanamann evā mahyaṃ saṃnamaḥ saṃ namantu ||3||

antarikṣaṃ dhenus tasyā vatsaḥ |
sā me vāyunā vatseneṣam ūrjaṃ kāmaṃ duhām |
āyuḥ prathamaṃ prajāṃ poṣaṃ rayiṃ svāhā ||4||

divyādityāya sam anamant sa ārdhnot |
yathā divyādityāya samanamann evā mahyaṃ saṃnamaḥ saṃ namantu ||5||

dyaur dhenus tasyā ādityo vatsaḥ |
sā ma ādityena vatseneṣam ūrjaṃ kāmaṃ duhām |
āyuḥ prathamaṃ prajāṃ poṣaṃ rayiṃ svāhā ||6||

dikṣu candrāya sam anamant sa ārdhnot |
yathā dikṣu candrāya samanamann evā mahyaṃ saṃnamaḥ saṃ namantu ||7||

diśo dhenavas tāsāṃ candro vatsaḥ |
tā me candreṇa vatseneṣam ūrjaṃ kāmaṃ duhām āyuḥ prathamaṃ prajāṃ posaṃ rayiṃ svāhā ||8||

agnāv agniś carati praviṣṭa ṛṣīṇām putro abhiśastipā u |
namaskāreṇa namasā te juhomi mā devānāṃ mithuyā karma bhāgam ||9||

4,39.10a hṛdā pūtam manasā jātavedo viśvāni deva vayunāni vidvān |
4,39.10c saptāsyāni tava jātavedas tebhyo juhomi sa juṣasva havyam ||10||



ye purastāj juhvati jātavedaḥ prācyā diśo 'bhidāsanty asmān |
agnim ṛtvā te parāñco vyathantāṃ pratyag enān pratisareṇa hanmi ||1||

ye dakṣiṇato juhvati jātavedo dakṣiṇāyā diśo 'bhidāsanty asmān |
yamaṃ ṛtvā te parāñco vyathantāṃ pratyag enā pratisareṇa hanmi ||2||

ye paścāj juhvati jātavedaḥ pratīcyā diśo 'bhidāsanty asmān |
varuṇam ṛtvā te parāñco vyathantāṃ pratyag enān pratisareṇa hanmi ||3||

ya uttarato juhvati jātaveda udīcyā diśo 'bhidāsanty asmān |
somam ṛtvā te parāñco vyathantāṃ pratyag enān pratisareṇa hanmi ||4||

ye 'dhastāj juhvati jātaveda udīcyā diśo 'bhidāsanty asmān |
bhūmim ṛtvā te parāñco vyathantāṃ pratyag enān pratisareṇa hanmi ||5||

ye 'ntarikṣāj juhvati jātavedo vyadhvāyā diśo 'bhidāsanty asmān |
vāyum ṛtvā te parāñco vyathantāṃ pratyag enān pratisareṇa hanmi ||6||

ya upariṣṭāj juhvati jātaveda ūrdhvāyā diśo 'bhidāsanty asmān |
sūryam ṛtvā te parāñco vyathantāṃ pratyag enān pratisareṇa hanmi ||7||

ye diśām antardeśebhyo juhvati jātavedaḥ sarvābhyo digbhyo 'bhidāsanti asmān |
brahma rtvā te parāñco vyathantāṃ pratyag enān pratisareṇa hanmi ||8||



ṛdhaṅmantro yoniṃ ya ābabhūvāmṛtāsur vardhamānaḥ sujanmā |
adabdhāsur bhrājamāno 'heva trito dhartā dādhāra trīṇi ||1||

ā yo dharmāṇi prathamaḥ sasāda tato vapūṃṣi kṛṇuṣe purūṇi |
dhāsyur yoniṃ prathama ā viveśā yo vācam anuditāṃ ciketa ||2||

yas te śokāya tanvaṃ rireca kṣarad dhiraṇyaṃ śucayo 'nu svāḥ |
atrā dadhete amṛtāni nāmāsme vastrāṇi viśa erayantām ||3||

pra yad ete prataraṃ pūrvyaṃ guḥ sadaḥsada ātiṣṭhanto ajuryam |
kaviḥ śuṣasya mātarā rihāṇe jāmyai dhuryaṃ patim erayethām ||4||

tad ū ṣu te mahat pṛthujman namaḥ kaviḥ kāvyenā kṛṇomi |
yat samyañcāv abhiyantāv abhi kṣām atrā mahī rodhacakre vāvṛdhete ||5||

sapta maryādāḥ kavayas tatakṣus tāsām id ekām abhy aṃhuro gāt |
āyor ha skambha upamasya nīḍe pathāṃ visarge dharuṇeṣu tasthau ||6||

utāmṛtāsur vrata emi kṛnvann asur ātmā tanvas tat sumadguḥ |
uta vā śakro ratnaṃ dadhāty ūrjayā vā yat sacate havirdāḥ ||7||
uta putraḥ pitaraṃ kṣatram īḍe jyeṣṭhaṃ maryādam ahvayant svastaye |
darśan nu tā varuṇa yās te viṣṭhā āvarvratataḥ kṛṇavo vapūṃṣi ||8||

ardham ardhena payasā pṛṇakṣy ardhena śuṣma vardhase amura |
aviṃ vṛdhāma śagmiyaṃ sakhāyaṃ varuṇaṃ putram adityā iṣiram |
kaviśastāny asmai vapūṃṣy avocāma rodasī satyavācā ||9||



tad id āsa bhuvaneṣu jyeṣṭham yato yajña ugras tveṣanṛmṇaḥ |
sadyo jajñāno ni riṇāti śatrūn anu yad enaṃ madanti viśva ūmāḥ ||1||

vavṛdhānaḥ śavasā bhūryojāḥ śatrur dāsāya bhiyasaṃ dadhāti |
avyanac ca vyanac ca sasni saṃ te navanta prabhṛtā madeṣu ||2||

tve kratum api pṛñcanti bhūri dvir yad ete trir bhavanty ūmāḥ |
svadoḥ svādīyaḥ svādunā sṛjā sam adaḥ su madhu madhunābhi yodhīḥ ||3||

yadi cin nu tvā dhanā jayantaṃ raṇeraṇe anumadanti viprāḥ |
ojīyaḥ śuṣmint sthiram ā tanuṣva mā tvā dabhan durevāsaḥ kaśokāḥ ||4||

tvayā vayaṃ śāśadmahe raṇeṣu prapaśyanto yudhenyāni bhūri |
codayāmi ta āyudhā vacobhiḥ saṃ te śiśāmi brahmaṇā vayāṃsi ||5||

ni tad dadhiṣe 'vare pare ca yasminn āvithāvasā duroṇe |
ā sthāpayata mātaraṃ jigatnum ata invata karvarāṇi bhūri ||6||

stuṣva varṣman puruvartmānaṃ sam ṛbhvāṇam inatamam āptam āptyānām |
ā darśati śavasā bhūryojāḥ pra sakṣati pratimānaṃ pṛthivyāḥ ||7||

imā brahma bṛhaddivaḥ kṛṇavad indrāya śūṣam agriyaḥ svarṣāḥ |
maho gotrasya kṣayati svarājā turaś cid viśvam arṇavat tapasvān ||8||

evā mahān bṛhaddivo atharvāvocat svāṃ tanvam indram eva |
svasārau mātaribhvarī aripre hinvanti caine śavasā vardhayanti ca ||9||



mamāgne varco vihaveṣv astu vayaṃ tvendhānās tanvam puṣema |
mahyaṃ namantāṃ pradiśaś catasras tvayādhyakṣeṇa pṛtanā jayema ||1||

agne manyuṃ pratinudan pareṣāṃ tvaṃ no gopāḥ pari pāhi viśvataḥ |
apāñco yantu nivatā durasyavo 'maiṣāṃ cittaṃ prabudhāṃ vi neśat ||2||

mama devā vihave santu sarva indravanto maruto viṣṇur agniḥ |
mamāntarikṣam urulokam astu mahyaṃ vātaḥ pavatāṃ kāmāyāsmai ||3||

mahyaṃ yajantāṃ mama yānīṣṭākūtiḥ satyā manaso me astu |
eno mā ni gāṃ katamac canāhaṃ viśve devā abhi rakṣantu meha ||4||

mayi devā draviṇam ā yajantāṃ mayi āśīr astu mayi devahūtiḥ |
daivāḥ hotāraḥ saniṣan na etad ariṣṭāḥ syāma tanvā suvīrāḥ ||5||

daivīḥ ṣaḍ urvīr uru naḥ kṛṇota viśve devāsa iha mādayadhvam |
mā no vidad abhibhā mo aśastir mā no vidad vṛjinā dveṣyā yā ||6||

tisro devīr mahi naḥ śarma yachata prajāyai nas tanve yac ca puṣṭam |
mā hāsmahi prajayā mā tanūbhir mā radhāma dviṣate soma rājan ||7||

uruvyacā no mahiṣaḥ śarma yachatv asmin have puruhūtaḥ purukṣu |
sa naḥ prajāyai haryaśva mṛḍendra mā no rīriṣo mā parā dāḥ ||8||

dhātā vidhātā bhuvanasya yas patir devaḥ savitābhimātiṣāhaḥ |
ādityā rudrā aśvinobhā devāḥ pāntu yajamānaṃ nirṛthāt ||9||

5,3.10a ye naḥ sapatnā apa te bhavantv indrāgnibhyām ava bādhāmaha enān |
5,3.10c ādityā rudrā uparispṛśo no ugraṃ cettāram adhirājam akrata ||10||

5,3.11a arvāñcam indram amuto havāmahe yo gojid dhanajid aśvajid yaḥ |
5,3.11c imaṃ no yajñaṃ vihave śṛṇotv asmākam abhūr haryaśva medī ||11||



yo giriṣv ajāyathā vīrudhāṃ balavattamaḥ |
kuṣṭhehi takmanāśana takmānaṃ nāśayann itaḥ ||1||

suparṇasuvane girau jātaṃ himavatas pari |
dhanair abhi śrutvā yanti vidur hi takmanāśanam ||2||

aśvattho devasadanas tṛtīyasyām ito divi |
tatrāmṛtasya cakṣaṇaṃ devāḥ kuṣṭham avanvata ||3||

hiraṇyayī naur acarad dhiraṇyabandhanā divi |
tatrāmṛtasya puṣpaṃ devāḥ kuṣṭham avanvata ||4||

hiraṇyayāḥ panthāna āsann aritrāṇi hiraṇyayā |
nāvo hiraṇyayīr āsan yābhiḥ kuṣṭhaṃ nirāvahan ||5||

imaṃ me kuṣṭha pūruṣaṃ tam ā vaha taṃ niṣ kuru |
tam u me agadaṃ kṛdhi ||6||

devebhyo adhi jāto 'si somasyāsi sakhā hitaḥ |
sa prāṇāya vyānāya cakṣuṣe me asmai mṛḍa ||7||

udaṅ jāto himavataḥ sa prācyāṃ nīyase janam |
tatra kuṣṭhasya nāmāny uttamāni vi bhejire ||8||

uttamo nāma kuṣṭhasy uttamo nāma te pitā |
yakṣmaṃ ca sarvaṃ nāśaya takmānaṃ cārasaṃ kṛdhi ||9||

5,4.10a śīrṣāmayam upahatyām akṣyos tanvo rapaḥ |
5,4.10c kuṣṭhas tat sarvaṃ niṣ karad daivaṃ samaha vṛṣṇyam ||10||



rātrī mātā nabhaḥ pitāryamā te pitāmahaḥ |
silācī nāma vā asi sā devānām asi svasā ||1||

yas tvā pibati jīvati trāyase puruṣaṃ tvam |
bhartrī hi śaśvatām asi janānāṃ ca nyañcanī ||2||

vṛkṣaṃvṛkṣam ā rohasi vṛṣaṇyantīva kanyalā |
jayantī pratyātiṣṭhantī sparaṇī nāma vā asi ||3||

yad daṇḍena yad iṣvā yad vārur harasā kṛtam |
tasya tvam asi niṣkṛtiḥ semaṃ niṣ kṛdhi pūruṣam ||4||

bhadrāt plakṣān nis tiṣṭhasy aśvatthāt khadirād dhavāt |
bhadrān nyagrodhāt parṇāt sā na ehy arundhati ||5||

hiraṇyavarṇe subhage sūryavarṇe vapuṣṭame |
rutaṃ gachāsi niṣkṛte niṣkṛtir nāma vā asi ||6||

hiraṇyavarṇe subhage śuṣme lomaśavakṣane |
apām asi svasā lākṣe vāto hātmā babhūva te ||7||

silācī nāma kānīno 'jababhru pitā tava |
aśvo yamasya yaḥ śyāvas tasya hāsnāsy ukṣitā ||8||

aśvasyāsnaḥ saṃpatitā sā vṛkṣāṃ abhi siṣyade |
sarā patatriṇī bhūtvā sā na ehy arundhati ||9||



brahma jajñānaṃ prathamaṃ purastād vi sīmataḥ suruco vena āvaḥ |
sa budhnyā upamā asya viṣṭhāḥ sataś ca yonim asataś ca vi vaḥ ||1||

anāptā ye vaḥ prathamā yāni karmāṇi cakrire |
vīrān no atra mā dabhan tad va etat puro dadhe ||2||

sahasradhāra eva te sam asvaran divo nāke madhujihvā asaścataḥ |
tasya spaśo na ni miṣanti bhūrṇayaḥ padepade pāśinaḥ santi setave ||3||

pary ū ṣu pra dhanvā vājasātaye pari vṛtrāṇi sakṣaṇiḥ |
dviṣas tad adhy arṇaveneyase sanisraso nāmāsi trayodaśo māsa indrasya gṛhaḥ ||4||

nv etenārātsīr asau svāhā |
tigmāyudhau tigmahetī suśevau somārudrāv iha su mṛḍataṃ naḥ ||5||

avaitenārātsīr asau svāhā |
tigmāyudhau tigmahetī suśevau somārudrāv iha su mṛḍataṃ naḥ ||6||

apaitenārātsīr asau svāhā |
tigmāyudhau tigmahetī suśevau somārudrāv iha su mṛḍataṃ naḥ ||7||

mumuktam asmān duritād avadyāj juṣethām yajñam amṛtam asmāsu dhattam ||8||

cakṣuṣo hete manaso hete brahmaṇo hete tapasaś ca hete |
menyā menir asy amenayas te santu ye 'smāṃ abhyaghāyanti ||9||

5,6.10a yo 'smāṃś cakṣuṣā manasā cittyākūtyā ca yo aghāyur abhidāsāt |
5,6.10c tvaṃ tān agne menyāmenīn kṛṇu svāhā ||10||
5,6.11a indrasya gṛho 'si |
5,6.11c taṃ tvā pra padye taṃ tvā pra viśāmi sarvaguḥ sarvapūruṣaḥ sarvātmā sarvatanūḥ saha yan me 'sti tena ||11||

5,6.12a indrasya śarmāsi |
5,6.12c taṃ tvā pra padye taṃ tvā pra viśāmi sarvaguḥ sarvapūruṣaḥ sarvātmā sarvatanūḥ saha yan me 'sti tena ||12||

5,6.13a indrasya varmāsi |
5,6.13c taṃ tvā pra padye taṃ tvā pra viśāmi sarvaguḥ sarvapūruṣaḥ sarvātmā sarvatanūḥ saha yan me 'sti tena ||13||

5,6.14a indrasya varūtham asi |
5,6.14c taṃ tvā pra padye taṃ tvā pra viśāmi sarvaguḥ sarvapūruṣaḥ sarvātmā sarvatanūḥ saha yan me 'sti tena ||14||



ā no bhara mā pari ṣṭhā arāte mā no rakṣīr dakṣiṇāṃ nīyamānām |
namo vīrtsāyā asamṛddhaye namo astv arātaye ||1||

yam arāte purodhatse puruṣaṃ parirāpiṇam |
namas te tasmai kṛṇmo mā vaniṃ vyathayīr mama ||2||

pra ṇo vanir devakṛtā divā naktaṃ ca kalpatām |
arātim anupremo vayaṃ namo astv arātaye ||3||

sarasvatīm anumatiṃ bhagaṃ yanto havāmahe |
vācam juṣṭāṃ madhumatīm avādiṣaṃ devānāṃ devahūtiṣu ||4||

yaṃ yācāmy ahaṃ vācā sarasvatyā manoyujā |
śraddhā tam adya vindatu dattā somena babhruṇā ||5||

mā vaniṃ mā vācaṃ no vīrtsīr ubhāv indrāgnī ā bharatāṃ no vasūni |
sarve no adya ditsanto 'rātiṃ prati haryata ||6||

paro 'pehy asamṛddhe vi te hetiṃ nayāmasi |
veda tvāhaṃ nimīvantīṃ nitudantīm arāte ||7||

uta nagnā bobhuvatī svapnayā sacase janam |
arāte cittaṃ vīrtsanty ākūtiṃ puruṣasya ca ||8||

yā mahatī mahonmānā viśvā āśā vyānaśe |
tasyai hiraṇyakeśyai nirṛtyā akaraṃ namaḥ ||9||

5,7.10a hiraṇyavarṇā subhagā hiraṇyakaśipur mahī |
5,7.10c tasyai hiraṇyadrāpaye 'rātyā akaraṃ namaḥ ||10||



vaikaṅkatenedhmena devebhya ājyaṃ vaha |
agne tāṃ iha mādaya sarva ā yantu me havam ||1||

indrā yāhi me havam idaṃ kariṣyāmi tac chṛṇu |
ima aindrā atisarā ākūtiṃ saṃ namantu me |
tebhiḥ śakema vīryaṃ jātavedas tanūvaśin ||2||

yad asāv amuto devā adevaḥ saṃścikīrṣati |
mā tasyāgnir havyaṃ vākṣīd dhavaṃ devā asya mopa gur mamaiva havam etana ||3||

ati dhāvatātisarā indrasya vacasā hata |
aviṃ vṛka iva mathnīta sa vo jīvan mā moci prāṇam asyāpi nahyata ||4||

yam amī purodadhire brahmāṇam apabhūtaye |
indra sa te adhaspadaṃ taṃ praty asyāmi mṛtyave ||5||

yadi preyur devapurā brahma varmāṇi cakrire |
tanūpānaṃ paripāṇaṃ kṛṇvānā yad upocire sarvaṃ tad arasaṃ kṛdhi ||6||

yān asāv atisarāṃś cakāra kṛṇavac ca yān |
tvaṃ tān indra vṛtrahan pratīcaḥ punar ā kṛdhi yathāmuṃ tṛṇahāṃ janam ||7||

yathendra udvācanaṃ labdhvā cakre adhaspadam |
kṛṇve 'ham adharān tathā amūñ chaśvatībhyaḥ samābhyaḥ ||8||

atrainān indra vṛtrahann ugro marmaṇi vidhya |
atraivainān abhi tiṣṭhendra medy ahaṃ tava |
anu tvendrā rabhāmahe syāma sumatau tava ||9||



dive svāhā ||1||

pṛthivyai svāhā ||2||

antarikṣāya svāhā ||3||

antarikṣāya svāhā ||4||

dive svāhā ||5||

pṛthivyai svāhā ||6||

sūryo me cakṣur vātaḥ prāṇo 'ntarikṣam ātmā pṛthivī śarīram |
astṛto nāmāham ayam asmi sa ātmānaṃ ni dadhe dyāvāpṛthivībhyāṃ gopīthāya ||7||

ud āyur ud balam ut kṛtam ut kṛtyām un manīṣām ud indriyam |
āyuṣkṛd āyuṣpatnī svadhāvantau gopā me staṃ gopāyataṃ mā |
ātmasadau me staṃ mā mā hiṃsiṣṭam ||8||



aśmavarma me 'si yo mā prācyā diśo 'ghāyur abhidāsāt |
etat sa ṛchāt ||1||

aśmavarma me 'si yo mā dakṣiṇāyā diśo 'ghāyur abhidāsāt |
etat sa ṛchāt ||2||

aśmavarma me 'si yo mā pratīcyā diśo 'ghāyur abhidāsāt |
etat sa ṛchāt ||3||

aśmavarma me 'si yo modīcyā diśo 'ghāyur abhidāsāt |
etat sa ṛchāt ||4||

aśmavarma me 'si yo mā dhruvāyā diśo 'ghāyur abhidāsāt |
etat sa ṛchāt ||5||

aśmavarma me 'si yo mordhvāyā diśo 'ghāyur abhidāsāt |
etat sa ṛchāt ||6||

aśmavarma me 'si yo mā diśām antardeśebhyo 'ghāyur abhidāsāt |
etat sa ṛchāt ||7||

bṛhatā mana upa hvaye mātariśvanā prāṇāpānau |
sūryāc cakṣur antarikṣāc chrotraṃ pṛthivyāḥ śarīram |
sarasvatyā vācam upa hvayāmahe manoyujā ||8||



kathaṃ mahe asurāyābravīr iha kathaṃ pitre haraye tveṣanṛmṇaḥ |
pṛśniṃ varuṇa dakṣiṇāṃ dadāvān punarmagha tvaṃ manasācikitsīḥ ||1||

na kāmena punarmagho bhavāmi saṃ cakṣe kaṃ pṛśnim etām upāje |
kena nu tvam atharvan kāvyena kena jātenāsi jātavedāḥ ||2||

satyam ahaṃ gabhīraḥ kāvyena satyaṃ jātenāsmi jātavedāḥ |
na me dāso nāryo mahitvā vrataṃ mīmāya yad ahaṃ dhariṣye ||3||

na tvad anyaḥ kavitaro na medhayā dhīrataro varuṇa svadhāvan |
tvaṃ tā viśvā bhuvanāni vettha sa cin nu tvaj jano māyī bibhāya ||4||

tvaṃ hy aṅga varuṇa svadhāvan viśvā vettha janima supraṇīte |
kiṃ rajasa enā paro anyad asty enā kiṃ pareṇāvaram amura ||5||

ekaṃ rajasa enā paro anyad asty enā para ekena durṇaśaṃ cid arvāk |
tat te vidvān varuṇa pra bravīmy adhovacasaḥ paṇayo bhavantu nīcair dāsā upa sarpantu bhūmim ||6||

tvaṃ hy aṅga varuṇa bravīṣi punarmagheṣv avadyāni bhūri |
mo ṣu paṇīṃr abhy etāvato bhūn mā tvā vocann arādhasaṃ janāsaḥ ||7||

mā mā vocann arādhasaṃ janāsaḥ punas te pṛśniṃ jaritar dadāmi |
stotraṃ me viśvam ā yāhi śacībhir antar viśvāsu mānuṣīṣu dikṣu ||8||

ā te stotrāṇy udyatāni yantv antar viśvāsu mānuṣīṣu dikṣu |
dehi nu me yan me adatto asi yujyo me saptapadaḥ sakhāsi ||9||

5,11.10a samā nau bandhur varuṇa samā jā vedāhaṃ tad yan nāv eṣā samā jā |
5,11.10c dadāmi tad yat te adatto asmi yujyas te saptapadaḥ sakhāsmi ||10||

5,11.11a devo devāya gṛṇate vayodhā vipro viprāya stuvate sumedhāḥ |
5,11.11c ajījano hi varuṇa svadhāvann atharvāṇaṃ pitaraṃ devabandhum |
5,11.11e tasmā u rādhaḥ kṛṇuhi supraśastaṃ sakhā no asi paramaṃ ca bandhuḥ ||11||



samiddho adya manuṣo duroṇe devo devān yajasi jātavedaḥ |
ā ca vaha mitramahaś cikitvān tvaṃ dūtaḥ kavir asi pracetāḥ ||1||

tanūnapāt patha ṛtasya yānān madhvā samañjant svadayā sujihva |
manmāni dhībhir uta yajñam ṛndhan devatrā ca kṛṇuhy adhvaram naḥ ||2||

ājuhvāna īḍyo bandyaś cā yāhy agne vasubhiḥ sajoṣāḥ |
tvaṃ devānām asi yahva hotā sa enān yakṣīṣito yajīyān ||3||

prācīnaṃ barhiḥ pradiśā pṛthivyā vastor asyā vṛjyate agre ahnām |
vy u prathate vitaraṃ varīyo devebhyo aditaye syonam ||4||

vyacasvatīr urviyā vi śrayantāṃ patibhyo na janayaḥ śumbhamānāḥ |
devīr dvāro bṛhatīr viśvaminvā devebhyo bhavata suprāyaṇāḥ ||5||

ā suṣvayantī yajate upāke uṣāsānaktā sadatāṃ ni yonau |
divye yoṣaṇe bṛhatī surukme adhi śriyaṃ śukrapiśaṃ dadhāne ||6||

daivyā hotārā prathamā suvācā mimānā yajñaṃ manuṣo yajadhyai |
pracodayantā vidatheṣu kārū prācīnaṃ jyotiḥ pradiśā diśantā ||7||

ā no yajñaṃ bhāratī tūyam etv iḍā manuṣvad iha cetayantī |
tisro devīr barhir edaṃ syonaṃ sarasvatīḥ svapasaḥ sadantām ||8||

ya ime dyāvāpṛthivī janitrī rūpair apiṃśad bhuvanāni viśvā |
tam adya hotar iṣito yajīyān devaṃ tvaṣṭāram iha yakṣi vidvān ||9||

5,12.10a upāvasṛja tmanyā samañjan devānāṃ pātha ṛtuthā havīṃṣi |
5,12.10c vanaspatiḥ śamitā devo agniḥ svadantu havyaṃ madhunā ghṛtena ||10||

5,12.11a sadyo jāto vy amimīta yajñam agnir devānām abhavat purogāḥ |
5,12.11c asya hotuḥ praśiṣy ṛtasya vāci svāhākṛtaṃ havir adantu devāḥ ||11||


dadir hi mahyaṃ varuṇo divaḥ kavir vacobhir ugrair ni riṇāmi te viṣam |
khātam akhātam uta saktam agrabham ireva dhanvan ni jajāsa te viṣam ||1||

yat te apodakaṃ viṣaṃ tat ta etāsv agrabham |
gṛhṇāmi te madhyamam uttamaṃ rasam utāvamam bhiyasā neśad ād u te ||2||

vṛṣā me ravo nabhasā na tanyatur ugreṇa te vacasā bādha ād u te |
ahaṃ tam asya nṛbhir agrabham rasaṃ tamasa iva jyotir ud etu sūryaḥ ||3||

cakṣuṣā te cakṣur hanmi viṣeṇa hanmi te viṣam |
ahe mriyasva mā jīvīḥ pratyag abhy etu tvā viṣam ||4||
kairāta pṛśna upatṛṇya babhra ā me śṛṇutāsitā alīkāḥ |
mā me sakhyuḥ stāmānam api ṣṭhātāśrāvayanto ni viṣe ramadhvam ||5||

asitasya taimātasya babhror apodakasya ca |
sātrāsāhasyāhaṃ manyor ava jyām iva dhanvano vi muñcāmi rathāṃ iva ||6||

āligī ca viligī ca pitā ca matā ca |
vidma vaḥ sarvato bandhv arasāḥ kiṃ kariṣyatha ||7||

urugūlāyā duhitā jātā dāsy asiknyā |
prataṅkaṃ dadruṣīṇāṃ sarvāsām arasam viṣam ||8||
karṇā śvāvit tad abravīd girer avacarantikā |
yāḥ kāś cemāḥ khanitrimās tāsām arasatamaṃ viṣam ||9||

5,13.10a tābuvaṃ na tābuvaṃ na ghet tvam asi tābuvam |
5,13.10c tābuvenārasaṃ viṣam ||10||

5,13.11a tastuvaṃ na tastuvaṃ na ghet tvam asi tastuvam |
5,13.11c tastuvenārasaṃ viṣam ||11||



suparṇas tvānv avindat sūkaras tvākhanan nasā |
dipsauṣadhe tvaṃ dipsantam ava kṛtyākṛtaṃ jahi ||1||

ava jahi yātudhānān ava kṛtyākṛtaṃ jahi |
atho yo asmān dipsati tam u tvaṃ jahy oṣadhe ||2||

riśyasyeva parīśāsaṃ parikṛtya pari tvacaḥ |
kṛtyāṃ kṛtyākṛte devā niṣkam iva prati muñcata ||3||

punaḥ kṛtyāṃ kṛtyākṛte hastagṛhya parā ṇaya |
samakṣam asmā ā dhehi yathā kṛtyākṛtam hanat ||4||

kṛtyāḥ santu kṛtyākṛte śapathaḥ śapathīyate |
sukho ratha iva vartatāṃ kṛtyā kṛtyākṛtaṃ punaḥ ||5||

yadi strī yadi vā pumān kṛtyāṃ cakāra pāpmane |
tām u tasmai nayāmasy aśvam ivāśvābhidhānyā ||6||

yadi vāsi devakṛtā yadi vā puruṣaiḥ kṛtā |
tāṃ tvā punar ṇayāmasīndreṇa sayujā vayam ||7||
agne pṛtanāṣāṭ pṛtanāḥ sahasva |
punaḥ kṛtyāṃ kṛtyākṛte pratiharaṇena harāmasi ||8||

kṛtavyadhani vidhya taṃ yaś cakāra tam ij jahi |
na tvām acakruṣe vayaṃ vadhāya saṃ śiśīmahi ||9||

5,14.10a putra iva pitaraṃ gacha svaja ivābhiṣṭhito daśa |
5,14.10c bandham ivāvakrāmī gacha kṛtye kṛtyākṛtaṃ punaḥ ||10||

5,14.11a ud eṇīva vāraṇy abhiskandaṃ mṛgīva |
5,14.11c kṛtyā kartāram ṛchatu ||11||

5,14.12a iṣvā ṛjīyaḥ patatu dyāvāpṛthivī taṃ prati |
5,14.12c sā taṃ mṛgam iva gṛhṇātu kṛtyā kṛtyākṛtaṃ punaḥ ||12||

5,14.13a agnir ivaitu pratikūlam anukūlam ivodakam |
5,14.13c sukho ratha iva vartatāṃ kṛtyā kṛtyākṛtaṃ punaḥ ||13||


ekā ca me daśa ca me 'pavaktāra oṣadhe |
ṛtajāta ṛtāvari madhu me madhulā karaḥ ||1||
dve ca me viṃśatiś ca me 'pavaktāra oṣadhe |
ṛtajāta ṛtāvari madhu me madhulā karaḥ ||2||

tisraś ca me triṃśac ca me 'pavaktāra oṣadhe |
ṛtajāta ṛtāvari madhu me madhulā karaḥ ||3||

catasraś ca me catvāriṃśac ca me 'pavaktāra oṣadhe |
ṛtajāta ṛtāvari madhu me madhulā karaḥ ||4||

pañca ca me pañcāśac ca me 'pavaktāra oṣadhe |
ṛtajāta ṛtāvari madhu me madhulā karaḥ ||5||

ṣaṭ ca me ṣaṣṭiś ca me 'pavaktāra oṣadhe |
ṛtajāta ṛtāvari madhu me madhulā karaḥ ||6||

sapta ca me saptatiś ca me 'pavaktāra oṣadhe |
ṛtajāta ṛtāvari madhu me madhulā karaḥ ||7||

aṣṭa ca me 'śītiś ca me 'pavaktāra oṣadhe |
ṛtajāta ṛtāvari madhu me madhulā karaḥ ||8||

nava ca me navatiś ca me 'pavaktāra oṣadhe |
ṛtajāta ṛtāvari madhu me madhulā karaḥ ||9||

5,15.10a daśa ca me śataṃ ca me 'pavaktāra oṣadhe |
5,15.10c ṛtajāta ṛtāvari madhu me madhulā karaḥ ||10||

5,15.11a śataṃ ca me sahasraṃ cāpavaktāra oṣadhe |
5,15.11c ṛtajāta ṛtāvari madhu me madhulā karaḥ ||11||



yady ekavṛṣo 'si sṛjāraso 'si ||1||

yadi dvivṛṣo 'si sṛjāraso 'si ||2||

yadi trivṛso 'si sṛjāraso 'si ||3||

yadi caturvṛṣo 'si sṛjāraso 'si ||4||

yadi pañcavṛṣo 'si sṛjāraso 'si ||5||

yadi ṣaḍvṛṣo 'si sṛjāraso 'si ||6||

yadi saptavṛṣo 'si sṛjāraso 'si ||7||

yady aṣṭavṛṣo 'si sṛjāraso 'si ||8||

yadi navavṛṣo 'si sṛjāraso 'si ||9||

5,16.10a yadi daśavṛṣo 'si sṛjāraso 'si ||10||

5,16.11a yady ekādaśo 'si so 'podako 'si ||11||



te 'vadan prathamā brahmakilbiṣe 'kūpāraḥ salilo mātariśvā |
vīḍuharās tapa ugraṃ mayobhūr āpo devīḥ prathamajā ṛtasya ||1||

somo rājā prathamo brahmajāyāṃ punaḥ prāyachad ahṛṇīyamānaḥ |
anvartitā varuṇo mitra āsīd agnir hotā hastagṛhyā nināya ||2||

hastenaiva grāhya ādhir asyā brahmajāyeti ced avocat |
na dūtāya praheyā tastha eṣā tathā rāṣṭraṃ gupitaṃ kṣatriyasya ||3||

yām āhus tārakaiṣā vikeśīti duchunāṃ grāmam avapadyamānām |
sā brahmajāyā vi dunoti rāṣṭraṃ yatra prāpādi śaśa ulkuṣīmān ||4||

brahmacārī carati veviṣad viṣaḥ sa devānāṃ bhavaty ekam aṅgam |
tena jāyām anv avindad bṛhaspatiḥ somena nītāṃ juhvaṃ na devāḥ ||5||

devā vā etasyām avadanta pūrve saptaṛṣayas tapasā ye niṣeduḥ |
bhīmā jāyā brāhmaṇasyāpanītā durdhāṃ dadhāti parame vyoman ||6||

ye garbhā avapadyante jagad yac cāpalupyate |
vīrā ye tṛhyante mitho brahmajāyā hinasti tān ||7||

uta yat patayo daśa striyāḥ pūrve abrāhmaṇāḥ |
brahmā ced dhastam agrahīt sa eva patir ekadhā ||8||

brāhmaṇa eva patir na rājanyo na vaiśyaḥ |
tat sūryaḥ prabruvann eti pañcabhyo mānavebhyaḥ ||9||

5,17.10a punar vai devā adaduḥ punar manuṣyā adaduḥ |
5,17.10c rājānaḥ satyaṃ gṛhṇānā brahmajāyāṃ punar daduḥ ||10||

5,17.11a punardāya brahmajāyāṃ kṛtvā devair nikilbiṣam |
5,17.11c ūrjaṃ pṛthivyā bhaktvorugāyam upāsate ||11||

5,17.12a nāsya jāyā śatavāhī kalyāṇī talpam ā śaye |
5,17.12c yasmin rāṣṭre nirudhyate brahmajāyācittyā ||12||

5,17.13a na vikarṇaḥ pṛthuśirās tasmin veśmani jāyate |
5,17.13c yasmin rāṣṭre nirudhyate brahmajāyācittyā ||13||

5,17.14a nāsya kṣattā niṣkagrīvaḥ sūnānām ety agrataḥ |
5,17.14c yasmin rāṣṭre nirudhyate brahmajāyācittyā ||14||

5,17.15a nāsya śvetaḥ kṛṣṇakarṇo dhuri yukto mahīyate |
5,17.15c yasmin rāṣṭre nirudhyate brahmajāyācittyā ||15||

5,17.16a nāsya kṣetre puṣkariṇī nāṇḍīkaṃ jāyate bisam |
5,17.16c yasmin rāṣṭre nirudhyate brahmajāyācittyā ||16||

5,17.17a nāsmai pṛśniṃ vi duhanti ye 'syā doham upāsate |
5,17.17c yasmin rāṣṭre nirudhyate brahmajāyācittyā ||17||

5,17.18a nāsya dhenuḥ kalyāṇī nānaḍvānt sahate dhuram |
5,17.18c vijānir yatra brahmaṇo rātriṃ vasati pāpayā ||18||



naitāṃ te devā adadus tubhyaṃ nṛpate attave |
mā brāhmaṇasya rājanya gāṃ jighatso anādyām ||1||

akṣadrugdho rājanyaḥ pāpa ātmaparājitaḥ |
sa brāhmaṇasya gām adyād adya jīvāni mā śvaḥ ||2||

āviṣṭitāghaviṣā pṛdākūr iva carmaṇā |
sā brāhmaṇasya rājanya tṛṣṭaiṣā gaur anādyā ||3||

nir vai kṣatraṃ nayati hanti varco 'gnir ivārabdho vi dunoti sarvam |
yo brāhmaṇaṃ manyate annam eva sa viṣasya pibati taimātasya ||4||

ya enaṃ hanti mṛduṃ manyamāno devapīyur dhanakāmo na cittāt |
saṃ tasyendro hṛdaye 'gnim indhe ubhe enaṃ dviṣṭo nabhasī carantam ||5||

na brāhmaṇo hiṃsitavyo 'gniḥ priyatanor iva |
somo hy asya dāyāda indro asyābhiśastipāḥ ||6||

śatāpāṣṭhāṃ ni girati tāṃ na śaknoti niḥkhidam |
annaṃ yo brahmaṇām malvaḥ svādv admīti manyate ||7||

jihvā jyā bhavati kulmalaṃ vāṅ nāḍīkā dantās tapasābhidigdhāḥ |
tebhir brahmā vidhyati devapīyūn hṛdbalair dhanurbhir devajūtaiḥ ||8||

tīkṣṇeṣavo brāhmaṇā hetimanto yām asyanti śaravyāṃ na sā mṛṣā |
anuhāya tapasā manyunā cota durād ava bhindanty enam ||9||

5,18.10a ye sahasram arājann āsan daśaśatā uta |
5,18.10c te brāhmaṇasya gāṃ jagdhvā vaitahavyāḥ parābhavan ||10||

5,18.11a gaur eva tān hanyamānā vaitahavyāṃ avātirat |
5,18.11c ye kesaraprābandhāyāś caramājām apeciran ||11||

5,18.12a ekaśataṃ tā janatā yā bhūmir vyadhūnuta |
5,18.12c prajāṃ hiṃsitvā brāhmaṇīm asaṃbhavyaṃ parābhavan ||12||

5,18.13a devapīyuś carati martyeṣu garagīrṇo bhavaty asthibhūyān |
5,18.13c yo brāhmaṇaṃ devabandhuṃ hinasti na sa pitṛyāṇam apy eti lokam ||13||

5,18.14a agnir vai naḥ padavāyaḥ somo dāyāda ucyate |
5,18.14c hantābhiśastendras tathā tad vedhaso viduḥ ||14||

5,18.15a iṣur iva digdhā nṛpate pṛdākūr iva gopate |
5,18.15c sā brāhmaṇasyeṣur ghorā tayā vidhyati pīyataḥ ||15||



atimātram avardhanta nod iva divam aspṛśan |
bhṛguṃ hiṃsitvā sṛñjayā vaitahavyāḥ parābhavan ||1||

ye bṛhatsāmānam āṅgirasam ārpayan brāhmaṇaṃ janāḥ |
petvas teṣām ubhayādam avis tokāny āvayat ||2||

ye brāhmaṇaṃ pratyaṣṭhīvan ye vāsmiñ chulkam īṣire |
asnas te madhye kulyāyāḥ keśān khādanta āsate ||3||

brahmagavī pacyamānā yāvat sābhi vijaṅgahe |
tejo rāṣṭrasya nir hanti na vīro jāyate vṛṣā ||4||

krūram asyā āśasanaṃ tṛṣṭaṃ piśitam asyate |
kṣīraṃ yad asyāḥ pīyate tad vai pitṛṣu kilbiṣam ||5||

ugro rājā manyamāno brāhmaṇaṃ yo jighatsati |
parā tat sicyate rāṣṭraṃ brāhmaṇo yatra jīyate ||6||

aṣṭāpadī caturakṣī catuḥśrotrā caturhanuḥ |
dvyāsyā dvijihvā bhūtvā sā rāṣṭram ava dhūnute brahmajyasya ||7||

tad vai rāṣṭram ā sravati nāvaṃ bhinnām ivodakam |
brahmāṇaṃ yatra hiṃsanti tad rāṣṭraṃ hanti duchunā ||8||

taṃ vṛkṣā apa sedhanti chāyāṃ no mopa gā iti |
yo brāhmaṇasya sad dhanam abhi nārada manyate ||9||

5,19.10a viṣam etad devakṛtaṃ rājā varuṇo 'bravīt |
5,19.10c na brāhmaṇasya gāṃ jagdhvā rāstre jāgāra kaś cana ||10||

5,19.11a navaiva tā navatayo yā bhūmir vyadhūnuta |
5,19.11c prajāṃ hiṃsitvā brāhmaṇīm asaṃbhavyaṃ parābhavan ||11||

5,19.12a yām mṛtāyānubadhnanti kūdyaṃ padayopanīm |
5,19.12c tad vai brahmajya te devā upastaraṇam abruvan ||12||

5,19.13a aśrūṇi kṛpamānasya yāni jītasya vāvṛtuḥ |
5,19.13c taṃ vai brahmajya te devā apāṃ bhāgam adhārayan ||13||

5,19.14a yena mṛtaṃ snapayanti śmaśrūṇi yenondate |
5,19.14c taṃ vai brahmajya te devā apāṃ bhāgam adhārayan ||14||

5,19.15a na varṣaṃ maitrāvaruṇaṃ brahmajyam abhi varṣati |
5,19.15c nāsmai samitiḥ kalpate na mitraṃ nayate vaśam ||15||



uccairghoṣo dundubhiḥ satvanāyan vānaspatyaḥ saṃbhṛta usṛiyābhiḥ |
vācaṃ kṣuṇuvāno damayant sapatnānt siṃha iva jeṣyann abhi taṃstanīhi ||1||

siṃha ivāstānīd druvayo vibaddho 'bhikrandann ṛṣabho vāsitām iva |
vṛṣā tvaṃ vadhrayas te sapatnā aindras te śuṣmo abhimātiṣāhaḥ ||2||

vṛṣeva yūthe sahasā vidāno gavyann abhi ruva saṃdhanājit |
śucā vidhya hṛdayaṃ pareṣāṃ hitvā grāmān pracyutā yantu śatravaḥ ||3||

saṃjayan pṛtanā ūrdhvamāyur gṛhyā gṛhṇāno bahudhā vi cakṣva |
daivīṃ vācaṃ dundubha ā gurasva vedhāḥ śatrūṇām upa bharasva vedaḥ ||4||

dundubher vācaṃ prayatāṃ vadantīm āśṛṇvatī nāthitā ghoṣabuddhā |
nārī putraṃ dhāvatu hastagṛhyāmitrī bhītā samare vadhānām ||5||

pūrvo dundubhe pra vadāsi vācaṃ bhūmyāḥ pṛṣṭhe vada rocamānaḥ |
amitrasenām abhijañjabhāno dyumad vada dundubhe sūnṛtāvat ||6||

antareme nabhasī ghoṣo astu pṛthak te dhvanayo yantu śībham |
abhi kranda stanayotpipānaḥ ślokakṛn mitratūryāya svardhī ||7||

dhībhiḥ kṛtaḥ pra vadāti vācam ud dharṣaya satvanām āyudhāni |
indramedī satvano ni hvayasva mitrair amitrāṃ ava jaṅghanīhi ||8||

saṃkrandanaḥ pravado dhṛṣṇuṣeṇaḥ pravedakṛd bahudhā grāmaghoṣī |
śriyo vanvano vayunāni vidvān kīrtim bahubhyo vi hara dvirāje ||9||

5,20.10a śreyaḥketo vasujit sahīyānt saṃgrāmajit saṃśito brahmaṇāsi |
5,20.10c aṃśūn iva grāvādhiṣavaṇe adrir gavyan dundubhe'dhi nṛtya vedaḥ ||10||

5,20.11a śatrūṣāṇ nīṣād abhimātiṣāho gaveṣaṇaḥ sahamāna udbhit |
5,20.11c vāgvīva mantraṃ pra bharasva vācam sāṃgrāmajityāyeṣam ud vadeha ||11||

5,20.12a acyutacyut samado gamiṣṭho mṛdho jetā puraetāyodhyaḥ |
5,20.12c indreṇa gupto vidathā nicikyad dhṛddyotano dviṣatāṃ yāhi śībham ||12||


vihṛdayaṃ vaimanasyaṃ vadāmitreṣu dundubhe |
vidveṣaṃ kaśmaśaṃ bhayam amitreṣu ni dadhmasy ava enān dundubhe jahi ||1||

udvepamānā manasā cakṣuṣā hṛdayena ca |
dhāvantu bibhyato 'mitrāḥ pratrāsenājye hute ||2||

vānaspatyaḥ saṃbhṛta usriyābhir viśvagotryaḥ |
pratrāsam amitrebhyo vadājyenābhighāritaḥ ||3||

yathā mṛgāḥ saṃvijanta āraṇyāḥ puruṣād adhi |
eva tvaṃ dundubhe 'mitrān abhi kranda pra trāsayātho cittāni mohaya ||4||

yathā vṛkād ajāvayo dhāvanti bahu bibhyatīḥ |
eva tvaṃ dundubhe 'mitrān abhi kranda pra trāsayātho cittāni mohaya ||5||

yathā śyenāt patatriṇaḥ saṃvijante ahardivi siṃhasya stanathor yathā |
eva tvaṃ dundubhe 'mitrān abhi kranda pra trāsayātho cittāni mohaya ||6||

parāmitrān dundubhinā hariṇasyājinena ca |
sarve devā atitrasan ye saṃgrāmasyeṣate ||7||

yair indraḥ prakrīḍate padghoṣaiś chāyayā saha |
tair amitrās trasantu no 'mī ye yanty anīkaśaḥ ||8||
jyāghoṣā dundubhayo 'bhi krośantu yā diśaḥ |
senāḥ parājitā yatīr amitrāṇām anīkaśaḥ ||9||

5,21.10a āditya cakṣur ā datsva marīcayo 'nu dhāvata |
5,21.10c patsaṅginīr ā sajantu vigate bāhuvīrye ||10||

5,21.11a yūyam ugrā marutaḥ pṛśnimātara indreṇa yujā pra mṛnīta śatrūn |
5,21.11c somo rājā varuṇo rājā mahādeva uta mṛtyur indraḥ ||11||

5,21.12a etā devasenāḥ sūryaketavaḥ sacetasaḥ |
5,21.12c amitrān no jayantu svāhā ||12||



agnis takmānam apa bādhatām itaḥ somo grāvā varuṇaḥ pūtadakṣāḥ |
vedir barhiḥ samidhaḥ śośucānā apa dveṣāṃsy amuyā bhavantu ||1||

ayaṃ yo viśvān haritān kṛṇoṣy ucchocayann agnir ivābhidunvan |
adhā hi takmann araso hi bhūyā adhā nyaṅṅ adharān vā parehi ||2||

yaḥ paruṣaḥ pāruṣeyo 'vadhvaṃsa ivāruṇaḥ |
takmānaṃ viśvadhāvīryādharāñcaṃ parā suvā ||3||

adharāñcam pra hiṇomi namaḥ kṛtvā takmane |
śakambharasya muṣṭihā punar etu mahāvṛṣān ||4||

oko asya mūjavanta oko asya mahāvṛṣāḥ |
yāvaj jātas takmaṃs tāvān asi balhikeṣu nyocaraḥ ||5||

takman vyāla vi gada vyaṅga bhūri yāvaya |
dāsīṃ niṣṭakvarīm icha tām vajreṇa sam arpaya ||6||

takman mūjavato gacha balhikān vā parastarām |
śūdrām icha prapharvyaṃ tāṃ takman vīva dhūnuhi ||7||

mahāvṛṣān mūjavato bandhv addhi paretya |
praitāni takmane brūmo anyakṣetrāṇi vā imā ||8||

anyakṣetre na ramase vaśī san mṛḍayāsi naḥ |
abhūd u prārthas takmā sa gamiṣyati balhikān ||9||

5,22.10a yat tvaṃ śīto 'tho rūraḥ saha kāsāvepayaḥ |
5,22.10c bhīmās te takman hetayas tābhiḥ sma pari vṛṅgdhi naḥ ||10||

5,22.11a mā smaitānt sakhīn kuruthā balāsaṃ kāsam udyugam |
5,22.11c mā smāto'rvāṅ aiḥ punas tat tvā takmann upa bruve ||11||

5,22.12a takman bhrātrā balāsena svasrā kāsikayā saha |
5,22.12c pāpmā bhrātṛvyeṇa saha gachāmum araṇaṃ janam ||12||

5,22.13a tṛtīyakaṃ vitṛtīyaṃ sadandim uta śāradam |
5,22.13c takmānaṃ śītaṃ rūraṃ graiṣmaṃ nāśaya vārṣikam ||13||

5,22.14a gandhāribhyo mūjavadbhyo 'ṅgebhyo magadhebhyaḥ |
5,22.14c praiṣyan janam iva śevadhiṃ takmānaṃ pari dadmasi ||14||



ote me dyāvāpṛthivī otā devī sarasvatī |
otau ma indraś cāgniś ca krimiṃ jambhayatām iti ||1||

asyendra kumārasya krimīn dhanapate jahi |
hatā viśvā arātaya ugreṇa vacasā mama ||2||

yo akṣyau parisarpati yo nāse parisarpati |
datāṃ yo madhyaṃ gachati taṃ krimiṃ jambhayāmasi ||3||

sarūpau dvau virūpau dvau kṛṣṇau dvau rohitau dvau |
babhruś ca babhrukarṇaś ca gṛdhraḥ kokaś ca te hatāḥ ||4||

ye krimayaḥ śitikakṣā ye kṛṣṇāḥ śitibāhavaḥ |
ye ke ca viśvarūpās tān krimīn jambhayāmasi ||5||

ut purastāt sūrya eti viśvadṛṣṭo adṛṣṭahā |
dṛṣṭāṃś ca ghnann adṛṣṭāṃś ca sarvāṃś ca pramṛṇan krimīn ||6||

yevāṣāsaḥ kaṣkaṣāsa ejatkāḥ śipavitnukāḥ |
dṛṣṭaś ca hanyatāṃ krimir utādṛṣṭaś ca hanyatām ||7||

hato yevāṣaḥ krimīṇāṃ hato nadanimota |
sarvān ni maṣmaṣākaraṃ dṛṣadā khalvāṃ iva ||8||

triśīrṣāṇaṃ trikakudaṃ krimiṃ sāraṅgam arjunam |
śṛṇāmy asya pṛṣṭīr api vṛścāmi yac chiraḥ ||9||

5,23.10a atrivad vaḥ krimayo hanmi kaṇvavaj jamadagnivat |
5,23.10c agastyasya brahmaṇā saṃ pinaṣmy ahaṃ krimīn ||10||

5,23.11a hato rājā krimīṇām utaiṣāṃ sthapatir hataḥ |
5,23.11c hato hatamātā krimir hatabhrātā hatasvasā ||11||

5,23.12a hatāso asya veśaso hatāsaḥ pariveśasaḥ |
5,23.12c atho ye kṣullakā iva sarve te krimayo hatāḥ ||12||

5,23.13a sarveṣāṃ ca krimīṇāṃ sarvāsāṃ ca krimīnām |
5,23.13c bhinadmy aśmanā śiro dahāmy agninā mukham ||13||



savitā prasavānām adhipatiḥ sa māvatu |
asmin brahmaṇy asmin karmaṇy asyāṃ purodhāyām asyām pratiṣṭhāyām asyāṃ |
cittyām asyām ākūtyām asyām āśiṣy asyāṃ devahūtyāṃ svāhā ||1||

agnir vanaspatīnām adhipatiḥ sa māvatu |
asmin brahmaṇy asmin karmaṇy asyāṃ purodhāyām asyāṃ pratiṣṭhāyām asyāṃ |
cittyām asyām ākūtyām asyām āśiṣy asyāṃ devahūtyāṃ svāhā ||2||

dyāvāpṛthivī dātṝṇām adhipatiḥ sa māvatu |
asmin brahmaṇy asmin karmaṇy asyāṃ purodhāyām asyāṃ pratiṣṭhāyām asyāṃ |
cittyām asyām ākūtyām asyām āśiṣy asyāṃ devahūtyāṃ svāhā ||3||

varuṇo 'pām adhipatiḥ sa māvatu |
asmin brahmaṇy asmin karmaṇy asyāṃ purodhāyām asyāṃ pratiṣṭhāyām asyāṃ |
cittyām asyām ākūtyām asyām āśiṣy asyāṃ devahūtyāṃ svāhā ||4||

mitrāvaruṇau vṛṣṭyādhipatī tau māvatām |
asmin brahmaṇy asmin karmaṇy asyāṃ purodhāyām asyāṃ pratiṣṭhāyām asyāṃ |
cittyām asyām ākūtyām asyām āśiṣy asyāṃ devahūtyāṃ svāhā ||5||

marutaḥ parvatānām adhipatayas te māvantu |
asmin brahmaṇy asmin karmaṇy asyāṃ purodhāyām asyāṃ pratiṣṭhāyām asyāṃ |
cittyām asyām ākūtyām asyām āśiṣy asyāṃ devahūtyāṃ svāhā ||6||

somo vīrudhām adhipatiḥ sa māvatu |
asmin brahmaṇy asmin karmaṇy asyāṃ purodhāyām asyāṃ pratiṣṭhāyām asyāṃ |
cittyām asyām ākūtyām asyām āśiṣy asyāṃ devahūtyāṃ svāhā ||7||

vāyur antarikṣasyādhipatiḥ sa māvatu |
asmin brahmaṇy asmin karmaṇy asyāṃ purodhāyām asyāṃ pratiṣṭhāyām asyāṃ |
cittyām asyām ākūtyām asyām āśiṣy asyāṃ devahūtyāṃ svāhā ||8||

sūryaś cakṣuṣām adhipatiḥ sa māvatu |
asmin brahmaṇy asmin karmaṇy asyāṃ purodhāyām asyāṃ pratiṣṭhāyām asyāṃ |
cittyām asyām ākūtyām asyām āśiṣy asyāṃ devahūtyāṃ svāhā ||9||

5,24.10a candramā nakṣatrāṇām adhipatiḥ sa māvatu |
5,24.10c asmin brahmaṇy asmin karmaṇy asyāṃ purodhāyām asyāṃ pratiṣṭhāyām asyāṃ |
5,24.10e cittyām asyām ākūtyām asyām āśiṣy asyāṃ devahūtyāṃ svāhā ||10||

5,24.11a indro divo 'dhipatiḥ sa māvatu |

5,24.14a yamaḥ pitṝṇām adhipatiḥ sa māvatu |

5,24.15a pitaraḥ pare te māvantu |
5,24.15c asmin brahmaṇy asmin karmaṇy asyāṃ purodhāyām asyāṃ pratiṣṭhāyām asyāṃ |

5,24.16a tatā avare te māvantu |
5,24.16c asmin brahmaṇy asmin karmaṇy asyāṃ purodhāyām asyāṃ pratisṭhāyām asyāṃ |
5,24.16e cittyām asyām ākūtyām asyām āśiṣy asyāṃ devahūtyāṃ svāhā ||16||

5,24.17a tatas tatāmahās te māvantu |
5,24.17c asmin brahmaṇy asmin karmaṇy asyāṃ purodhāyām asyāṃ pratiṣṭhāyām asyāṃ |
5,24.17e cittyām asyām ākūtyām asyām āśiṣy asyāṃ devahūtyāṃ svāhā ||17||



parvatād divo yoner aṅgādaṅgāt samābhṛtam |
śepo garbhasya retodhāḥ sarau parṇam ivā dadhat ||1||

yatheyaṃ pṛthivī mahī bhūtānāṃ garbham ādadhe |
evā dadhāmi te garbhaṃ tasmai tvām avase huve ||2||

garbhaṃ dhehi sinīvāli garbhaṃ dhehi sarasvati |
garbhaṃ te aśvinobhā dhattāṃ puṣkarasrajā ||3||

garbhaṃ te mitrāvaruṇau garbham devo bṛhaspatiḥ |
garbhaṃ ta indraś cāgniś ca garbhaṃ dhātā dadhātu te ||4||

viṣṇur yoniṃ kalpayatu tvaṣṭā rūpāṇi piṃśatu |
ā siñcatu prajāpatir dhātā garbhaṃ dadhātu te ||5||

yad veda rājā varuṇo yad vā devī sarasvatī |
yad indro vṛtrahā veda tad garbhakaraṇaṃ piba ||6||

garbho asy oṣadhīnāṃ garbho vanaspatīnām |
garbho viśvasya bhūtasya so agne garbham eha dhāḥ ||7||

adhi skanda vīrayasva garbham ā dhehi yonyām |
vṛṣāsi vṛṣṇyāvan prajāyai tvā nayāmasi ||8||

vi jihīṣva bārhatsāme garbhas te yonim ā śayām |
aduṣ ṭe devāḥ putraṃ somapā ubhayāvinam ||9||

5,25.10a dhātaḥ śreṣṭhena rūpeṇāsyā nāryā gavīnyoḥ |
5,25.10c pumāṃsaṃ putram ā dhehi daśame māsi sūtave ||10||

5,25.11a tvaṣṭaḥ śreṣṭhena rūpeṇāsyā nāryā gavīnyoḥ |
5,25.11c pumāṃsaṃ putram ā dhehi daśame māsi sūtave ||11||

5,25.12a savitaḥ śreṣṭhena rūpeṇāsyā nāryā gavīnyoḥ |
5,25.12c pumāṃsaṃ putram ā dhehi daśame māsi sūtave ||12||

5,25.13a prajāpate śreṣṭhena rūpeṇāsyā nāryā gavīnyoḥ |
5,25.13c pumāṃsaṃ putram ā dhehi daśame māsi sūtave ||13||



yajūṃṣi yajñe samidhaḥ svāhāgniḥ pravidvān iha vo yunaktu ||1||

yunaktu devaḥ savitā prajānann asmin yajñe mahiṣaḥ svāhā ||2||

indra ukthāmadāny asmin yajñe pravidvān yunaktu suyujaḥ svāhā ||3||

praiṣā yajñe nividaḥ svāhā śiṣṭāḥ patnībhir vahateha yuktāḥ ||4||

chandāṃsi yajñe marutaḥ svāhā māteva putraṃ pipṛteha yuktāḥ ||5||

eyam agan barhiṣā prokṣaṇībhir yajñaṃ tanvānāditiḥ svāhā ||6||

viṣṇur yunaktu bahudhā tapāṃsy asmin yajñe suyujaḥ svāhā ||7||

tvaṣṭā yunaktu bahudhā nu rūpā asmin yajñe yunaktu suyujaḥ svāhā ||8||

bhago yunaktvāśiṣo nv asmā asmin yajñe pravidvān yunaktu suyujaḥ svāhā ||9||

5,26.10a somo yunaktu bahudhā payāṃsy asmin yajñe suyujaḥ svāhā ||10||

5,26.11a indro yunaktu bahudhā payāṃsy asmin yajñe suyujaḥ svāhā ||11||

5,26.12a aśvinā brahmaṇā yātam arvāñcau vaṣaṭkāreṇa yajñaṃ vardhayantau |
5,26.12c bṛhaspate brahmaṇā yāhy arvāṅ yajño ayaṃ svar idaṃ yajamānāya svāhā ||12||



ūrdhvā asya samidho bhavanty ūrdhvā śukrā śocīṣy agneḥ |
dyumattamā supratīkaḥ sasūnus tanūnapād asuro bhūripāṇiḥ ||1||

devo deveṣu devaḥ patho anakti madhvā ghṛtena ||2||

madhvā yajñam nakṣati praiṇāno narāśaṃso agniḥ sukṛd devaḥ savitā viśvavāraḥ ||3||

achāyam eti śavasā ghṛtā cid īdāno vahnir namasā ||4||

agniḥ sruco adhvareṣu prayakṣu sa yakṣad asya mahimānam agneḥ ||5||

tarī mandrāsu prayakṣu vasavaś cātiṣṭhan vasudhātaraś ca ||6||

dvāro devīr anv asya viśve vrataṃ rakṣanti viśvahā ||7||

uruvyacasāgner dhāmnā patyamāne |
ā suṣvayantī yajate upāke uṣāsānaktemaṃ yajñam avatām adhvaram naḥ ||8||
daivā hotāra ūrdhvam adhvaraṃ no 'gner jihvayābhi gṛnata gṛnatā naḥ sviṣṭaye |
tisro devīr barhir edaṃ sadantām iḍā sarasvatī mahī bhāratī gṛṇānā ||9||

5,27.10a tan nas turīpam adbhutaṃ purukṣu |
5,27.10c deva tvaṣṭā rāyas poṣaṃ vi ṣya nābhim asya ||10||

5,27.11a vanaspate 'va sṛjā rarāṇaḥ |
5,27.11c tmanā devebhyo agnir havyaṃ śamitā svadayatu ||11||

5,27.12a agne svāhā kṛṇuhi jātavedaḥ |
5,27.12c indrāya yajñaṃ viśve devā havir idaṃ juṣantām ||12||


nava prāṇān navabhiḥ saṃ mimīte dīrghāyutvāya śataśāradāya |
harite trīṇi rajate trīṇy ayasi trīṇi tapasāviṣṭitāni ||1||

agniḥ sūryaś candramā bhūmir āpo dyaur antarikṣaṃ pradiśo diśaś ca |
ārtavā ṛtubhiḥ saṃvidānā anena mā trivṛtā pārayantu ||2||

trayaḥ poṣās trivṛti śrayantām anaktu pūṣā payasā ghṛtena |
annasya bhūmā puruṣasya bhūmā bhūmā paśūnāṃ ta iha śrayantām ||3||

imam ādityā vasunā sam ukṣatemam agne vardhaya vavṛdhānaḥ |
imam indra saṃ sṛja vīryeṇāsmin trivṛc chrayatāṃ poṣayiṣṇu ||4||

bhūmiṣ ṭvā pātu haritena viśvabhṛd agniḥ pipartv ayasā sajoṣāḥ |
vīrudbhiṣ ṭe arjunaṃ saṃvidānaṃ dakṣaṃ dadhātu sumanasyamānam ||5||

tredhā jātam janmanedaṃ hiraṇyam agner ekaṃ priyatamaṃ babhūva somasyaikaṃ hiṃsitasya parāpatat |
apām ekaṃ vedhasāṃ reta āhus tat te hiraṇyaṃ trivṛd astv āyuṣe ||6||

tryāyuṣaṃ jamadagneḥ kaśyapasya tryāyuṣam |
tredhāmṛtasya cakṣaṇaṃ trīṇy āyūṃṣi te 'karam ||7||

trayaḥ suparṇās trivṛtā yad āyann ekākṣaram abhisaṃbhūya śakrāḥ |
praty auhan mṛtyum amṛtena sākam antardadhānā duritāni viśvā ||8||

divas tvā pātu haritaṃ madhyāt tvā pātv arjunam |
bhūmyā ayasmayaṃ pātu prāgād devapurā ayam ||9||

5,28.10a imās tisro devapurās tās tvā rakṣantu sarvataḥ |
5,28.10c tās tvaṃ bibhrad varcasvy uttaro dviṣatāṃ bhava ||10||

5,28.11a puraṃ devānām amṛtaṃ hiraṇyam ya ābedhe prathamo devo agre |
5,28.11c tasmai namo daśa prācīḥ kṛṇomy anu manyatāṃ trivṛd ābadhe me ||11||

5,28.12a ā tvā cṛtatv aryamā pūṣā bṛhaspatiḥ |
5,28.12c aharjātasya yan nāma tena tvāti cṛtāmasi ||12||

5,28.13a ṛtubhiṣ ṭvārtavair āyuṣe varcase tvā |
5,28.13c saṃvatsarasya tejasā tena saṃhanu kṛṇmasi ||13||

5,28.14a ghṛtād ulluptam madhunā samaktaṃ bhūmidṛṃham acyutam pārayiṣṇu |
5,28.14c bhindat sapatnān adharāṃś ca kṛṇvad ā mā roha mahate saubhagāya ||14||



purastād yukto vaha jātavedo 'gne viddhi kriyamāṇam yathedam |
tvaṃ bhiṣag bheṣajasyāsi kartā tvayā gām aśvaṃ puruṣaṃ sanema ||1||

tathā tad agne kṛṇu jātavedo viśvebhir devaiḥ saha saṃvidānaḥ |
yo no dideva yatamo jaghāsa yathā so asya paridhiṣ patāti ||2||

yathā so asya paridhiṣ patāti tathā tad agne kṛṇu jātavedaḥ |
viśvebhir devair saha saṃvidānaḥ ||3||

akṣyau ni vidhya hṛdayaṃ ni vidhya jihvāṃ ni tṛnddhi pra dato mṛṇīhi |
piśāco asya yatamo jaghāsāgne yaviṣṭha prati śṛṇīhi ||4||

yad asya hṛtaṃ vihṛtaṃ yat parābhṛtam ātmano jagdhaṃ yatamat piśācaiḥ |
tad agne vidvān punar ā bhara tvaṃ śarīre māṃsam asum erayāmaḥ ||5||

āme supakve śabale vipakve yo mā piśāco aśane dadambha |
tad ātmanā prajayā piśācā vi yātayantām agado 'yam astu ||6||

kṣire mā manthe yatamo dadambhākṛṣṭapacye aśane dhānye yaḥ |
tad ātmanā prajayā piśācā vi yātayantām agado 'yam astu ||7||

apāṃ mā pāne yatamo dadambha kravyād yātūnām śayane śayānam |
tad ātmanā prajayā piśācā vi yātayantām agado 'yam astu ||8||

divā mā naktaṃ yatamo dadambha kravyād yātūnām śayane śayānam |
tad ātmanā prajayā piśācā vi yātayantām agado 'yam astu ||9||

kravyādam agne rudhiraṃ piśācaṃ manohanaṃ jahi jātavedaḥ |
tam indro vājī vajreṇa hantu chinattu somaḥ śiro asya dhṛṣṇuḥ ||10||

sanād agne mṛṇasi yātudhānān na tvā rakṣāṃsi pṛtanāsu jigyuḥ |
sahamūrān anu daha kravyādo mā te hetyā mukṣata daivyāyāḥ ||11||

5,29.12a samāhara jātavedo yad dhṛtaṃ yat parābhṛtam |
5,29.12c gātrāṇy asya vardhantām aṃśur ivā pyāyatām ayam ||12||

somasyeva jātavedo aṃśur ā pyāyatām ayam |
agne virapśinaṃ medhyam ayakṣmaṃ kṛṇu jīvatu ||13||

etās te agne samidhaḥ piśācajambhanīḥ |
tās tvaṃ juṣasva prati cainā gṛhāṇa jātavedaḥ ||14||

tārṣṭāghīr agne samidhaḥ prati gṛhṇāhy arciṣā |
jahātu kravyād rūpaṃ yo asya māṃsaṃ jihīrṣati ||15||



āvatas ta āvataḥ parāvatas ta āvataḥ |
ihaiva bhava mā nu gā mā pūrvān anu gāḥ pitṝn asuṃ badhnāmi te dṛḍham ||1||

yat tvābhiceruḥ puruṣaḥ svo yad araṇo janaḥ |
unmocanapramocane ubhe vācā vadāmi te ||2||

yad dudrohitha śepiṣe striyai puṃse acittyā |
unmocanapramocane ubhe vācā vadāmi te ||3||

yat enaso mātṛkṛtāc cheṣe pitṛkṛtāc ca yat |
unmocanapramocane ubhe vācā vadāmi te ||4||

yat te mātā yat te pitā jamir bhrātā ca sarjataḥ |
pratyak sevasva bheṣajaṃ jaradaṣṭiṃ kṛṇomi tvā ||5||

ihaidhi puruṣa sarveṇa manasā saha |
dūtau yamasya mānu gā adhi jīvapurā ihi ||6||

anuhūtaḥ punar ehi vidvān udayanaṃ pathaḥ |
ārohaṇam ākramaṇaṃ jīvatojīvato 'yanam ||7||

mā bibher na mariṣyasi jaradaṣṭiṃ kṛṇomi tvā |
nir avocam ahaṃ yakṣmam aṅgebhyo aṅgajvaraṃ tava ||8||

aṅgabhedo aṅgajvaro yaś ca te hṛdayāmayaḥ |
yakṣmaḥ śyena iva prāpaptad vacā sāḍhaḥ parastarām ||9||

5,30.10a ṛṣī bodhapratībodhāv asvapno yaś ca jāgṛviḥ |
5,30.10c tau te prāṇasya goptārau divā naktaṃ ca jāgṛtām ||10||

5,30.11a ayam agnir upasadya iha sūrya ud etu te |
5,30.11c udehi mṛtyor gambhīrāt kṛṣṇāc cit tamasas pari ||11||

5,30.12a namo yamāya namo astu mṛtyave namaḥ pitṛbhya uta ye nayanti |
5,30.12c utpāraṇasya yo veda tam agniṃ puro dadhe 'smā ariṣṭatātaye ||12||

5,30.13a aitu prāṇa aitu mana aitu cakṣur atho balam |
5,30.13c śarīram asya sam vidāṃ tat padbhyāṃ prati tiṣṭhatu ||13||

5,30.14a prāṇenāgne cakṣuṣā saṃ sṛjemaṃ sam īraya tanvā saṃ balena |
5,30.14c vetthāmṛtasya mā nu gān mā nu bhūmigṛho bhuvat ||14||

5,30.15a mā te prāṇa upa dasan mo apāno 'pi dhāyi te |
5,30.15c sūryas tvādhipatir mṛtyor udāyachatu raśmibhiḥ ||15||

5,30.16a iyam antar vadati jihvā baddhā paniṣpadā |
5,30.16c tvayā yakṣmam nir avocaṃ śataṃ ropīś ca takmanaḥ ||16||

5,30.17a ayaṃ lokaḥ priyatamo devānām aparājitaḥ |
5,30.17c yasmai tvam iha mṛtyave diṣṭaḥ puruṣa jajñiṣe |
5,30.17e sa ca tvānu hvayāmasi mā purā jaraso mṛthāḥ ||17||



yāṃ te cakrur āme pātre yāṃ cakrur miśradhānye |
āme māṃse kṛtyāṃ yāṃ cakruḥ punaḥ prati harāmi tām ||1||

yāṃ te cakruḥ kṛkavākāv aje vā yāṃ kurīriṇi |
avyāṃ te kṛtyāṃ yām cakruḥ punaḥ prati harāmi tām ||2||

yāṃ te cakrur ekaśaphe paśūnām ubhayādati |
gardabhe kṛtyāṃ yāṃ cakruḥ punaḥ prati harāmi tām ||3||

yāṃ te cakrur amūlāyāṃ valagaṃ vā narācyām |
kṣetre te kṛtyāṃ yāṃ cakruḥ punaḥ prati harāmi tām ||4||
yāṃ te cakrur gārhapatye pūrvāgnāv uta duścitaḥ |
śālāyāṃ kṛtyāṃ yām cakruḥ punaḥ prati harāmi tām ||5||

yāṃ te cakruḥ sabhāyāṃ yām cakrur adhidevane |
akṣeṣu kṛtyāṃ yāṃ cakruḥ punaḥ prati harāmi tām ||6||

yāṃ te cakruḥ senāyāṃ yāṃ cakrur iṣvāyudhe |
dundubhau kṛtyāṃ yāṃ cakruḥ punaḥ prati harāmi tām ||7||

yāṃ te kṛtyām kūpe 'vadadhuḥ śmaśāne vā nicakhnuḥ |
sadmani kṛtyām yāṃ cakruḥ punaḥ prati harāmi tām ||8||

yāṃ te cakruḥ puruṣāsthe agnau saṃkasuke ca yām |
mrokaṃ nirdāhaṃ kravyādaṃ punaḥ prati harāmi tām ||9||
5,31.10a apathenā jabhāraināṃ tāṃ pathetaḥ pra hiṇmasi |
5,31.10c adhīro maryādhīrebhyaḥ saṃ jabhārācittyā ||10||

5,31.11a yaś cakāra na śaśāka kartuṃ śaśre pādam aṅgurim |
5,31.11c cakāra bhadram asmabhyam abhago bhagavadbhyaḥ ||11||

5,31.12a kṛtyākṛtaṃ valaginaṃ mūlinaṃ śapatheyyam |
5,31.12c indras taṃ hantu mahatā vadhenāgnir vidhyatv astayā ||12||



doṣo gāya bṛhad gāya dyumad dhehi |
ātharvaṇa stuhi devaṃ savitāram ||1||

tam u ṣṭuhi yo antaḥ sindhau sūnuḥ |
satyasya yuvānam adroghavācaṃ suśevam ||2||

sa ghā no devaḥ savitā sāviṣad amṛtāni bhūri |
ubhe suṣṭutī sugātave ||3||


indrāya somam ṛtvijaḥ sunotā ca dhāvata |
stotur yo vacaḥ śṛṇavad dhavaṃ ca me ||1||

ā yaṃ viśantīndavo vayo na vṛkṣam andhasaḥ |
virapśin vi mṛdho jahi rakṣasvinīḥ ||2||

sunotā somapāvne somam indrāya vajriṇe |
yuvā jeteśānaḥ sa puruṣṭutaḥ ||3||



pātaṃ na indrāpūṣaṇāditiḥ pāntu marutaḥ |
apāṃ napāt sindhavaḥ sapta pātana pātu no viṣṇur uta dyauḥ ||1||

pātāṃ no dyāvāpṛthivī abhiṣṭaye pātu grāvā pātu somo no aṃhasaḥ |
pātu no devī subhagā sarasvatī pātv agniḥ śivā ye asya pāyavaḥ ||2||

pātām no devāśvinā śubhas patī uṣāsānaktota na uruṣyatām |
apāṃ napād abhihrutī gayasya cid deva tvaṣṭar vardhaya sarvatātaye ||3||



tvaṣṭā me daivyaṃ vacaḥ parjanyo brahmaṇas patiḥ |
putrair bhrātṛbhir aditir nu pātu no duṣṭaraṃ trāyamāṇaṃ sahaḥ ||1||

aṃśo bhago varuṇo mitro aryamāditiḥ pāntu marutaḥ |
apa tasya dveṣo gamed abhihruto yāvayac chatrum antitam ||2||

dhiye sam aśvinā prāvataṃ na uruṣyā ṇa urujmann aprayuchan |
dyauṣ pitar yāvaya duchunā yā ||3||



ud enam uttaraṃ nayāgne ghṛtenāhuta |
sam enaṃ varcasā sṛja prajayā ca bahuṃ kṛdhi ||1||

indremaṃ prataraṃ kṛdhi sajātānām asad vaśī |
rāyas poṣeṇa saṃ sṛja jīvātave jarase naya ||2||

yasya kṛṇmo havir gṛhe tam agne vardhayā tvam |
tasmai somo adhi bravad ayaṃ ca brahmaṇas patiḥ ||3||



yo 'smān brahmaṇas pate 'devo abhimanyate |
sarvaṃ tam randhayāsi me yajamānāya sunvate ||1||

yo naḥ soma suśaṃsino duḥśaṃsa ādideśati |
vajreṇāsya mukhe jahi sa saṃpiṣṭo apāyati ||2||

yo naḥ somābhidāsati sanābhir yaś ca niṣṭyaḥ |
apa tasya balaṃ tira mahīva dyaur vadhatmanā ||3||



yena somāditiḥ pathā mitrā vā yanty adruhaḥ |
tenā no 'vasā gahi ||1||

yena soma sāhantyāsurān randhayāsi naḥ |
tenā no adhi vocata ||2||

yena devā asurāṇām ojāṃsy avṛṇīdhvam |
tenā naḥ śarma yachata ||3||



yathā vṛkṣaṃ libujā samantaṃ pariṣasvaje |
evā pari ṣvajasva māṃ yathā māṃ kāminy aso yathā man nāpagā asaḥ ||1||
yathā suparṇaḥ prapatan pakṣau nihanti bhūmyām |
evā ni hanmi te mano yathā māṃ kāminy aso yathā man nāpagā asaḥ ||2||

yatheme dyāvāpṛthivī sadyaḥ paryeti sūryaḥ |
evā pary emi te mano yathā māṃ kāminy aso yathā man nāpagā asaḥ ||3||


vāñcha me tanvaṃ pādau vāñchākṣyau vāñcha sakthyau |
akṣyau vṛṣaṇyantyāḥ keśā māṃ te kāmena śuṣyantu ||1||

mama tvā doṣaṇiśriṣaṃ kṛṇomi hṛdayaśriṣam |
yathā mama kratāv aso mama cittam upāyasi ||2||

yāsāṃ nābhir ārehaṇaṃ hṛdi saṃvananaṃ kṛtam gāvo ghṛtasya mātaro 'mūṃ saṃ vānayantu me ||3||



pṛthivyai śrotrāya vanaspatibhyo 'gnaye 'dhipataye svāhā ||1||

prāṇāyāntarikṣāya vayobhyo vāyave 'dhipataye svāhā ||2||

dive cakṣuṣe nakṣatrebhyaḥ sūryāyādhipataye svāhā ||3||



śamīm aśvattha ārūḍhas tatra puṃsuvanaṃ kṛtam |
tad vai putrasya vedanaṃ tat strīṣv ā bharāmasi ||1||

puṃsi vai reto bhavati tat striyām anu ṣicyate |
tad vai putrasya vedanaṃ tat prajāpatir abravīt ||2||

prajāpatir anumatiḥ sinīvāly acīkḷpat |
straiṣūyam anyatra dadhat pumāṃsam u dadhat iha ||3||



pari dyām iva sūryo 'hīnāṃ janimāgamam |
rātrī jagad ivānyad dhaṃsāt tenā te vāraye viṣam ||1||

yad brahmabhir yad ṛṣibhir yad devair viditaṃ purā |
yad bhūtaṃ bhavyam āsanvat tenā te vāraye viṣam ||2||

madhvā pṛñce nadyaḥ parvatā girayo madhu |
madhu paruṣṇī śīpālā śam āsne astu śaṃ hṛde ||3||



namo devavadhebhyo namo rājavadhebhyaḥ |
atho ye viśyānāṃ vadhās tebhyo mṛtyo namo 'stu te ||1||

namas te adhivākāya parāvākāya te namaḥ |
sumatyai mṛtyo te namo durmatyai te idaṃ namaḥ ||2||

namas te yātudhānebhyo namas te bheṣajebhyaḥ |
namas te mṛtyo mūlebhyo brāhmaṇebhya idaṃ namaḥ ||3||



asthisraṃsaṃ parusraṃsam āsthitam hṛdayāmayam |
balāsaṃ sarvaṃ nāśayāṅgeṣṭhā yaś ca parvasu ||1||

nir balāsaṃ balāsinaḥ kṣiṇomi muṣkaraṃ yathā |
chinadmy asya bandhanaṃ mūlam urvārvā iva ||2||

nir balāsetaḥ pra patāśuṅgaḥ śiśuko yathā |
atho ita iva hāyano 'pa drāhy avīrahā ||3||



uttamo asy oṣadhīnāṃ tava vṛkṣā upastayaḥ |
upastir astu so 'smākaṃ yo asmāṃ abhidāsati ||1||

sabandhuś cāsabandhuś ca yo asmāṃ abhidāsati |
teṣāṃ sā vṛkṣāṇām ivāhaṃ bhūyāsam uttamaḥ ||2||

yathā soma oṣadhīnām uttamo haviṣāṃ kṛtaḥ |
talāśā vṛkṣāṇām ivāhaṃ bhūyāsam uttamaḥ ||3||



ābayo anābayo rasas ta ugra ābayo |
ā te karambham admasi ||1||

vihahlo nāma te pitā madāvatī nāma te mātā |
sa hina tvam asi yas tvam ātmānam āvayaḥ ||2||

tauvilike 'velayāvāyam ailaba ailayīt |
babhruś ca babhrukarṇaś cāpehi nir āla ||3||

alasālāsi pūrva silāñjālāsy uttarā |
nīlāgalasāla ||4||


yatheyam pṛthivī mahī bhūtānāṃ garbham ādadhe |
evā te dhriyatāṃ garbho anu sūtuṃ savitave ||1||

yatheyaṃ pṛthivī mahī dādhāremān vanaspatīn |
evā te dhriyatāṃ garbho anu sūtuṃ savitave ||2||

yatheyaṃ pṛthivī mahī dādhāra parvatān girīn |
evā te dhriyatāṃ garbho anu sūtuṃ savitave ||3||

yatheyaṃ pṛthivī mahī dādhāra viṣṭhitaṃ jagat |
evā te dhriyatāṃ garbho anu sūtuṃ savitave ||4||



īrṣyāyā dhrājiṃ prathamāṃ prathamasyā utāparām |
agniṃ hṛdayyaṃ śokaṃ taṃ te nir vāpayāmasi ||1||

yathā bhūmir mṛtamanā mṛtān mṛtamanastarā |
yathota mamruṣo mana everṣyor mṛtaṃ manaḥ ||2||

ado yat te hṛdi śritaṃ manaskaṃ patayiṣṇukam |
tatas ta īrṣyāṃ muñcāmi nir ūṣmāṇaṃ dṛter iva ||3||


punantu mā devajanāḥ punantu manavo dhiyā |
punantu viśvā bhūtāni pavamānaḥ punātu mā ||1||

pavamānaḥ punātu mā kratve dakṣāya jīvase |
atho ariṣṭatātaye ||2||

ubhābhyāṃ deva savitaḥ pavitreṇa savena ca |
asmān punīhi cakṣase ||3||



agner ivāsya dahata eti śuṣmiṇa uteva matto vilapann apāyati |
anyam asmad ichatu kaṃ cid avratas tapurvadhāya namo astu takmane ||1||

namo rudrāya namo astu takmane namo rājñe varuṇāya tviṣīmate |
namo dive namaḥ pṛthivyai nama oṣadhībhyaḥ ||2||

ayaṃ yo abhiśocayiṣṇur viśvā rūpāṇi haritā kṛṇoṣi |
tasmai te 'ruṇāya babhrave namaḥ kṛṇomi vanyāya takmane ||3||



imā yās tisraḥ pṛthivīs tāsāṃ ha bhūmir uttamā |
tāsām adhi tvaco ahaṃ bheṣajaṃ sam u jagrabham ||1||

śreṣṭham asi bheṣajānāṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ vīrudhānām |
somo bhaga iva yāmeṣu deveṣu varuṇo yathā ||2||

revatīr anādhṛṣaḥ siṣāsavaḥ siṣāsatha |
uta stha keśadṛmhaṇīr atho ha keśavardhanīḥ ||3||



kṛṣṇaṃ niyānaṃ harayaḥ suparṇā apo vasānā divam ut patanti |
ta āvavṛtrant sadanād ṛtasyād id ghṛtena pṛthivīṃ vy ūduḥ ||1||

payasvatīḥ kṛṇuthāpa oṣadhīḥ śivā yad ejathā maruto rukmavakṣasaḥ |
ūrjaṃ ca tatra sumatiṃ ca pinvata yatrā naro marutaḥ siñcathā madhu ||2||

udapruto marutas tāṃ iyarta vṛṣṭir yā viśvā nivatas pṛṇāti |
ejāti glahā kanyeva tunnairuṃ tundānā patyeva jāyā ||3||



sasruṣīs tad apaso divā naktaṃ ca sasruṣīḥ |
vareṇyakratur aham apo devīr upa hvaye ||1||

otā āpaḥ karmaṇyā muñcantv itaḥ praṇītaye |
sadyaḥ kṛṇvantv etave ||2||

devasya savituḥ save karma kṛṇvantu mānuṣāḥ |
śaṃ no bhavantv apa oṣadhīḥ śivāḥ ||3||



himavataḥ pra sravanti sindhau samaha saṅgamaḥ |
āpo ha mahyaṃ tad devīr dadan hṛddyotabheṣajam ||1||

yan me akṣyor ādidyota pārṣṇyoḥ prapadoś ca yat |
āpas tat sarvaṃ niṣ karan bhiṣajāṃ subhiṣaktamāḥ ||2||

sindhupatnīḥ sindhurājñīḥ sarvā yā nadya sthana |
datta nas tasya bheṣajaṃ tenā vo bhunajāmahai ||3||



pañca ca yāḥ pañcāśac ca saṃyanti manyā abhi |
itas tāḥ sarvā naśyantu vākā apacitām iva ||1||

sapta ca yāḥ saptatiś ca saṃyanti graivyā abhi |
itas tāḥ sarvā naśyantu vākā apacitām iva ||2||

nava ca yā navatiś ca saṃyanti skandhyā abhi |
itas tāḥ sarvā naśyantu vākā apacitām iva ||3||



ava mā pāpmant sṛja vaśī san mṛdayāsi naḥ |
ā mā bhadrasya loke pāpman dhehy avihrutam ||1||

yo naḥ pāpman na jahāsi tam u tvā jahimo vayam |
pathām anu vyāvartane 'nyaṃ pāpmānu padyatām ||2||

anyatrāsman ny ucyatu sahasrākṣo amartyaḥ |
yaṃ dveṣāma tam ṛchatu yam u dviṣmas tam ij jahi ||3||



devāḥ kapota iṣito yad ichan dūto nirṛtyā idam ājagāma |
tasmā arcāma kṛṇavāma niṣkṛtiṃ śaṃ no astu dvipade śaṃ catuṣpade ||1||

śivaḥ kapota iṣito no astv anāgā devāḥ śakuno gṛhaṃ naḥ |
agnir hi vipro juṣatām havir naḥ pari hetiḥ pakṣiṇī no vṛṇaktu ||2||

hetiḥ pakṣiṇī na dabhāty asmān āṣṭrī padaṃ kṛṇute agnidhāne |
śivo gobhya uta puruṣebhyo no astu mā no devā iha hiṃsīt kapota ||3||



ṛcā kapotaṃ nudata praṇodam iṣaṃ madantaḥ pari gāṃ nayāmaḥ |
saṃlobhayanto duritā padāni hitvā na ūrjaṃ pra padāt pathiṣṭhaḥ ||1||

parīme 'gnim arṣata parīme gām aneṣata |
deveṣv akrata śravaḥ ka imāṃ ā dadharṣati ||2||

yaḥ prathamaḥ pravatam āsasāda bahubhyaḥ panthām anupaspaśānaḥ |
yo 'syeśe dvipado yaś catuṣpadas tasmai yamāya namo astu mṛtyave ||3||



amūn hetiḥ patatriṇī ny etu yad ulūko vadati mogham etat |
yad vā kapota padam agnau kṛṇoti ||1||

yau te dūtau nirṛta idam eto 'prahitau prahitau vā gṛhaṃ naḥ |
kapotolūkābhyām apadaṃ tad astu ||2||

avairahatyāyedam ā papatyāt suvīratāyā idam ā sasadyāt |
parāṅ eva parā vada parācīm anu saṃvatam |
yathā yamasya tvā gṛhe 'rasaṃ praticākaśān ābhūkaṃ praticākaśān ||3||



devā imaṃ madhunā saṃyutaṃ yavaṃ sarasvatyām adhi maṇāv acarkṛṣuḥ |
indra āsīt sīrapatiḥ śatakratuḥ kīnāśā āsan marutaḥ sudānavaḥ ||1||

yas te mado 'vakeśo vikeśo yenābhihasyaṃ puruṣaṃ kṛṇoṣi |
ārāt tvad anyā vanāni vṛkṣi tvaṃ śami śatavalśā vi roha ||2||

bṛhatpalāśe subhage varṣavṛddha ṛtāvari |
māteva putrebhyo mṛḍa keśebhyaḥ śami ||3||



āyaṃ gauḥ pṛśnir akramīd asadan mātaram puraḥ |
pitaram ca prayant svaḥ ||1||

antaś carati rocanā asya prāṇād apānataḥ |
vy akhyan mahiṣaḥ svaḥ ||2||

triṃśad dhāmā vi rājati vāk pataṅgo aśiśriyat |
prati vastor ahar dyubhiḥ ||3||



antardāve juhuta sv etad yātudhānakṣayaṇaṃ ghṛtena |
ārād rakṣāṃsi prati daha tvam agne na no gṛhāṇām upa tītapāsi ||1||

rudro vo grīvā aśarait piśācāḥ pṛṣṭīr vo 'pi śṛṇātu yātudhānāḥ |
vīrud vo viśvatovīryā yamena sam ajīgamat ||2||

abhayaṃ mitrāvaruṇāv ihāstu no 'rciṣāttriṇo nudataṃ pratīcaḥ |
mā jñātāraṃ mā pratiṣṭhāṃ vidanta mitho vighnānā upa yantu mṛtyum ||3||



yasyedam ā rajo yujas tuje janā navaṃ svaḥ |
indrasya rantyaṃ bṛhat ||1||
nādhṛṣa ā dadhṛṣate dhṛṣāṇo dhṛṣitaḥ śavaḥ |
purā yathā vyathiḥ śrava indrasya nādhṛṣe śavaḥ ||2||

sa no dadātu tāṃ rayim uruṃ piśaṅgasaṃdṛśam |
indraḥ patis tuviṣṭamo janeṣv ā ||3||



prāgnaye vācam īraya vṛṣabhāya kṣitīnām |
sa naḥ parṣad ati dviṣaḥ ||1||

yo rakṣāṃsi nijūrvaty agnis tigmena śociṣā |
sa naḥ parṣad ati dviṣaḥ ||2||

yaḥ parasyāḥ parāvatas tiro dhanvātirocate |
sa naḥ parṣad ati dviṣaḥ ||3||

yo viśvābhi vipaśyati bhuvanā saṃ ca paśyati |
sa naḥ parṣad ati dviṣaḥ ||4||

yo asya pāre rajasaḥ śukro agnir ajāyata |
sa naḥ parṣad ati dviṣaḥ ||5||



vaiśvānaro na ūtaya ā pra yātu parāvataḥ |
agnir naḥ suṣṭutīr upa ||1||

vaiśvānaro na āgamad imaṃ yajñaṃ sajūr upa |
agnir uktheṣv aṃhasu ||2||

vaiśvānaro 'ṅgirasāṃ stomam ukthaṃ ca cākḷpat |
aiṣu dyumnaṃ svar yamat ||3||



ṛtāvānaṃ vaiśvānaram ṛtasya jyotiṣas patim |
ajasraṃ gharmam īmahe ||1||

sa viśvā prati cākḷpa ṛtūṃr ut sṛjate vaśī |
yajñasya vaya uttiran ||2||

agniḥ pareṣu dhāmasu kāmo bhūtasya bhavyasya |
samrād eko vi rājati ||3||



upa prāgāt sahasrākṣo yuktvā śapatho ratham |
śaptāram anvichan mama vṛka ivāvimato gṛham ||1||

pari ṇo vṛṅgdhi śapatha hradam agnir ivā dahan |
śaptāram atra no jahi divo vṛkṣam ivāśaniḥ ||2||

yo naḥ śapād aśapataḥ śapato yaś ca naḥ śapāt |
śune peṣṭram ivāvakṣāmaṃ taṃ praty asyāmi mṛtyave ||3||



siṃhe vyāghra uta yā pṛdākau tviṣir agnau brāhmaṇe sūrye yā |
indraṃ yā devī subhagā jajāna sā na aitu varcasā saṃvidānā ||1||

yā hastini dvīpini yā hiraṇye tviṣir apsu goṣu yā puruṣeṣu |
indraṃ yā devī subhagā jajāna sā na aitu varcasā saṃvidānā ||2||

rathe akṣeṣv ṛṣabhasya vāje vāte parjanye varuṇasya śuṣme |
indram yā devī subhagā jajāna sā na aitu varcasā saṃvidānā ||3||

rājanye dundubhāv āyatāyām aśvasya vāje puruṣasya māyau |
indram yā devī subhagā jajāna sā na aitu varcasā samvidānā ||4||



yaśo havir vardhatām indrajūtaṃ sahasravīryaṃ subhṛtaṃ sahaskṛtam |
prasarsrāṇam anu dīrghāya cakṣase haviṣmantaṃ mā vardhaya jyeṣṭhatātaye ||1||

achā na indraṃ yaśasaṃ yaśobhir yaśasvinaṃ namasānā vidhema |
sa no rāsva rāṣṭram indrajūtaṃ tasya te rātau yaśasaḥ syāma ||2||

yaśā indro yaśā agnir yaśāḥ somo ajāyata |
yaśā viśvasya bhūtasya aham asmi yaśastamaḥ ||3||



abhayaṃ dyāvāpṛthivī ihāstu no 'bhayaṃ somaḥ savitā naḥ kṛṇotu |
abhayaṃ no 'stūrv antarikṣaṃ saptaṛṣīṇāṃ ca haviṣābhayaṃ no astu ||1||

asmai grāmāya pradiśaś catasra ūrjaṃ subhūtaṃ svasti savitā naḥ kṛṇotu |
aśatrv indro abhayaṃ naḥ kṛṇotv anyatra rājñām abhi yātu manyuḥ ||2||

anamitraṃ no adharād anamitraṃ na uttarāt |
indrānamitraṃ naḥ paścād anamitraṃ puras kṛdhi ||3||



manase cetase dhiya ākūtaya uta cittaye |
matyai śrutāya cakṣase vidhema haviṣā vayam ||1||

apānāya vyānāya prāṇāya bhūridhāyase |
sarasvatyā uruvyace vidhema haviṣā vayam ||2||

mā no hāsiṣur ṛṣayo daivyā ye tanūpā ye nas tanvas tanūjāḥ |
amartyā martyāṃ abhi naḥ sacadhvam āyur dhatta prataraṃ jīvase naḥ ||3||



ava jyām iva dhanvano manyuṃ tanomi te hṛdaḥ |
yathā saṃmanasau bhūtvā sakhāyāv iva sacāvahai ||1||

sakhāyāv iva sacāvahā ava manyuṃ tanomi te |
adhas te aśmano manyum upāsyāmasi yo guruḥ ||2||

abhi tiṣṭhāmi te manyuṃ pārṣṇyā prapadena ca |
yathāvaśo na vādiṣo mama cittam upāyasi ||3||



ayaṃ darbho vimanyukaḥ svāya cāraṇāya ca |
manyor vimanyukasyāyaṃ manyuśamana ucyate ||1||

ayaṃ yo bhūrimūlaḥ samudram avatiṣṭhati |
darbhaḥ pṛthivyā utthito manyuśamana ucyate ||2||

vi te hanavyāṃ śaraṇiṃ vi te mukhyāṃ nayāmasi |
yathāvaśo na vādiṣo mama cittam upāyasi ||3||



asthād dyaur asthāt pṛthivy asthād viśvam idaṃ jagat |
asthur vṛkṣā ūrdhvasvapnās tiṣṭhād rogo ayaṃ tava ||1||

śataṃ yā bheṣajāni te sahasraṃ saṃgatāni ca |
śreṣṭham āsrāvabheṣajaṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ roganāśanam ||2||

rudrasya mūtram asy amṛtasya nābhiḥ |
viṣāṇakā nāma vā asi pitṝṇāṃ mūlād utthitā vātīkṛtanāśanī ||3||



paro 'pehi manaspāpa kim aśastāni śaṃsasi |
parehi na tvā kāmaye vṛkṣāṃ vanāni saṃ cara gṛheṣu goṣu me manaḥ ||1||

avaśasā niḥśasā yat parāśasopārima jāgrato yat svapantaḥ |
agnir viśvāny apa duṣkṛtāny ajuṣṭāny āre asmad dadhātu ||2||

yad indra brahmaṇas pate 'pi mṛṣā carāmasi |
pracetā na āṅgiraso duritāt pātv aṃhasaḥ ||3||



yo na jīvo 'si na mṛto devānām amṛtagarbho 'si svapna |
varuṇānī te mātā yamaḥ pitārarur nāmāsi ||1||

vidma te svapna janitraṃ devajāmīnāṃ putro 'si yamasya karaṇaḥ |
antako 'si mṛtyur asi taṃ tvā svapna tathā saṃ vidma sa naḥ svapna duṣvapnyāt pāhi ||2||

yathā kalāṃ yathā śaphaṃ yatharṇaṃ saṃnayanti |
evā duṣvapnyaṃ sarvaṃ dviṣate saṃ nayāmasi ||3||



agniḥ prātaḥsavane pātv asmān vaiśvānaro viśvakṛd viśvaśaṃbhūḥ |
sa naḥ pāvako draviṇe dadhātv āyuṣmantaḥ sahabhakṣāḥ syāma ||1||

viśve devā maruta indro asmān asmin dvitīye savane na jahyuḥ |
āyuṣmantaḥ priyam eṣāṃ vadanto vayaṃ devānāṃ sumatau syāma ||2||

idaṃ tṛtīyaṃ savanaṃ kavīnām ṛtena ye camasam airayanta |
te saudhanvanāḥ svar ānaśānāḥ sviṣṭiṃ no abhi vasyo nayantu ||3||



śyeno 'si gāyatrachandā anu tvā rabhe |
svasti mā saṃ vahāsya yajñasyodṛci svāhā ||1||

ṛbhur asi jagachandā anu tvā rabhe |
svasti mā saṃ vahāsya yajñasyodṛci svāhā ||2||

vṛṣāsi triṣṭupchandā anu tvā rabhe |
svasti mā saṃ vahāsya yajñasyodṛci svāhā ||3||



nahi te agne tanvaḥ krūram ānaṃśa martyaḥ |
kapir babhasti tejanaṃ svaṃ jarāyu gaur iva ||1||

meṣa iva vai saṃ ca vi corv acyase yad uttaradrāv uparaś ca khādataḥ |
śīrṣṇā śiro 'psasāpso ardayann aṃśūn babhasti haritebhir āsabhiḥ ||2||

suparṇā vācam akratopa dyavy ākhare kṛṣṇā iṣirā anartiṣuḥ |
ni yan niyanti uparasya niṣkṛtiṃ purū reto dadhire sūryaśritaḥ ||3||



hataṃ tardaṃ samaṅkam ākhum aśvinā chintaṃ śiro api pṛṣṭīḥ śṛṇītam |
yavān ned adān api nahyataṃ mukham athābhayaṃ kṛṇutaṃ dhānyāya ||1||

tarda hai pataṅga hai jabhya hā upakvasa |
brahmevāsaṃsthitaṃ havir anadanta imān yavān ahiṃsanto apodita ||2||

tardāpate vaghāpate tṛṣṭajambhā ā śṛṇota me |
ya āraṇyā vyadvarā ye ke ca stha vyadvarās tānt sarvān jambhayāmasi ||3||



vāyoḥ pūtaḥ pavitreṇa pratyaṅ somo ati drutaḥ |
indrasya yujaḥ sakhā ||1||

āpo asmān mātaraḥ sūdayantu ghṛtena no ghṛtapvaḥ punantu |
viśvaṃ hi ripraṃ pravahanti devīr ud id ābhyaḥ śucir ā pūta emi ||2||

yat kiṃ cedaṃ varuṇa daivye jane 'bhidrohaṃ manuṣyāś caranti |
acittyā cet tava dharma yuyopima mā nas tasmād enaso deva rīriṣaḥ ||3||


ut sūryo diva eti puro rakṣāṃsi nijūrvan |
ādityaḥ parvatebhyo viśvadṛṣṭo adṛṣṭahā ||1||

ni gāvo goṣṭhe asadan ni mṛgāso avikṣata |
ny ūrmayo nadīnaṃ ny adṛṣṭā alipsata ||2||

āyurdadaṃ vipaścitaṃ śrutāṃ kaṇvasya vīrudham |
ābhāriṣaṃ viśvabheṣajīm asyādṛṣṭān ni śamayat ||3||



dyauś ca ma idaṃ pṛthivī ca pracetasau śukro bṛhan dakṣiṇayā pipartu |
anu svadhā cikitāṃ somo agnir vāyur naḥ pātu savitā bhagaś ca ||1||

punaḥ prāṇaḥ punar ātmā na aitu punaś cakṣuḥ punar asur na aitu |
vaiśvānaro no adabdhas tanūpā antas tiṣṭhāti duritāni viśvā ||2||

saṃ varcasā payasā saṃ tanūbhir aganmahi manasā saṃ śivena |
