tvaṣṭā no atra varīyaḥ kṛṇotv anu no mārṣṭu tanvo yad viriṣṭam ||3||


idaṃ tad yuja uttaram indraṃ śumbhāmy aṣṭaye |
asya kṣatraṃ śriyaṃ mahīṃ vṛṣṭir iva vardhayā tṛṇam ||1||

asmai kṣatram agnīṣomāv asmai dhārayataṃ rayim |
imaṃ rāṣṭrasyābhīvarge kṛṇutam yuja uttaram ||2||

sabandhuś cāsabandhuś ca yo asmāṃ abhidāsati |
sarvaṃ taṃ randhayāsi me yajamānāya sunvate ||3||



ye panthāno bahavo devayānā antarā dyāvāpṛthivī saṃcaranti |
teṣām ajyāniṃ yatamo vahāti tasmai mā devāḥ pari datteha sarve ||1||

grīṣmo hemantaḥ śiśiro vasantaḥ śarad varṣāḥ svite no dadhāta |
ā no goṣu bhajatā prajāyāṃ nivāta id vaḥ śaraṇe syāma ||2||

idāvatsarāya parivatsarāya saṃvatsarāya kṛṇutā bṛhan namaḥ |
teṣāṃ vayaṃ sumatau yajñiyānām api bhadre sau manase syāma ||3||



mā no devā ahir vadhīt satokānt sahapuruṣān |
samyataṃ na vi ṣparad vyāttaṃ na saṃ yaman namo devajanebhyaḥ |

namo 'stv asitāya namas tiraścirājaye |
svajāya babhrave namo namo devajanebhyaḥ ||2||

saṃ te hanmi datā dataḥ sam u te hanvā hanū |
saṃ te jihvayā jihvāṃ sam v āsnāha āsyam ||3||



idam id vā u bheṣajam idaṃ rudrasya bheṣajam |
yeneṣum ekatejanāṃ śataśalyām apabravat ||1||

jālāṣeṇābhi ṣiñcata jālāṣeṇopa siñcata |
jālāṣam ugraṃ bheṣajaṃ tena no mṛḍa jīvase ||2||

śaṃ ca no mayaś ca no mā ca naḥ kiṃ canāmamat |
kṣamā rapo viśvaṃ no astu bheṣajaṃ sarvaṃ no astu bheṣajam ||3||



yaśasaṃ mendro maghavān kṛṇotu yaśasaṃ dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe ime |
yaśasaṃ mā devaḥ savitā kṛṇotu priyo dātur dakṣiṇāyā iha syām ||1||

yathendro dyāvāpṛthivyor yaśasvān yathāpa oṣadhīṣu yaśasvatīḥ |
evā viśveṣu deveṣu vayaṃ sarveṣu yaśasaḥ syāma ||2||

yaśā indro yaśā agnir yaśāḥ somo ajāyata |
yaśā viśvasya bhūtasyāham asmi yaśastamaḥ ||3||



anaḍudbhyas tvaṃ prathamaṃ dhenubhyas tvam arundhati |
adhenave vayase śarma yacha catuṣpade ||1||

śarma yachatv oṣadhiḥ saha devīr arundhatī |
karat payasvantaṃ goṣṭham ayakṣmāṃ uta pūruṣān ||2||

viśvarūpāṃ subhagām achāvadāmi jīvalām |
sā no rudrasyāstāṃ hetiṃ dūraṃ nayatu gobhyaḥ ||3||



ayam ā yāty aryamā purastād viṣitastupaḥ |
asyā ichann agruvai patim uta jāyām ajānaye ||1||

aśramad iyam aryamann anyāsāṃ samanaṃ yatī |
aṅgo nv aryamann asyā anyāḥ samanam āyati ||2||

dhātā dādhāra pṛthivīm dhātā dyām uta sūryam |
dhātāsyā agruvai patim dadhātu pratikāmyam ||3||



mahyam āpo madhumad erayantāṃ mahyaṃ sūro abharaj jyotiṣe kam |
mahyaṃ devā uta viśve tapojā mahyaṃ devaḥ savitā vyaco dhāt ||1||

ahaṃ viveca pṛthivīm uta dyām aham ṛtūṃr ajanayaṃ sapta sākam |
ahaṃ satyam anṛtaṃ yad vadāmy ahaṃ daivīṃ pari vācam viśaś ca ||2||

ahaṃ jajāna pṛthivīm uta dyām aham ṛtūṃr ajanayaṃ sapta sindhūn |
ahaṃ satvam anṛtaṃ yad vadāmi yo agnīṣomāv ajuṣe sakhāyā ||3||



vaiśvānaro raśmibhir naḥ punātu vātaḥ prāṇeneṣiro nabhobhiḥ |
dyāvāpṛthivī payasā payasvatī ṛtāvarī yajñiye na punītām ||1||

vaiśvānarīṃ sūnṛtām ā rabhadhvaṃ yasyā āśās tanvo vītapṛṣṭhāḥ |
tayā gṛṇantaḥ sadhamādeṣu vayaṃ syāma patayo rayīnām ||2||

vaiśvānarīṃ varcasa ā rabhadhvaṃ śuddhā bhavantaḥ śucayaḥ pāvakāḥ |
iheḍayā sadhamādaṃ madanto jyok paśyema sūryam uccarantam ||3||



yat te devī nirṛtir ābabandha dāma grīvāsv avimokyaṃ yat |
tat te vi ṣyāmy āyuṣe varcase balāyādomadam annam addhi prasūtaḥ ||1||

namo 'stu te nirṛte tigmatejo 'yasmayān vi cṛtā bandhapāśān |
yamo mahyam punar it tvām dadāti tasmai yamāya namo astu mṛtyave ||2||

ayasmaye drupade bedhiṣa ihābhihito mṛtyubhir ye sahasram |
yamena tvaṃ pitṛbhiḥ saṃvidāna uttamaṃ nākam adhi rohayemam ||3||

saṃsam id yuvase vṛṣann agne viśvāny arya ā |
iḍas pade sam idhyase sa no vasūny ā bhara ||4||



saṃ jānīdhvaṃ saṃ pṛcyadhvaṃ saṃ vo manāṃsi jānatām |
devā bhāgaṃ yathā pūrve samjānānā upāsate ||1||

samāno mantraḥ samitiḥ samānī samānaṃ vrataṃ saha cittam eṣām |
samānena vo haviṣā juhomi samānaṃ ceto abhisaṃviśadhvam ||2||

samānī va ākūtiḥ samānā hṛdayāni vaḥ |
samānam astu vo manaḥ yathā vaḥ susahāsati ||3||



ava manyur avāyatāva bāhū manoyujā |
parāśara tvaṃ teṣām parāñcaṃ śuṣmam ardayādhā no rayim ā kṛdhi ||1||

nirhastebhyo nairhastam yaṃ devāḥ śarum asyatha |
vṛścāmi śatrūṇāṃ bāhūn anena haviṣā 'ham ||2||

indraś cakāra prathamaṃ nairhastam asurebhyaḥ |
jayantu satvāno mama sthireṇendreṇa medinā ||3||



nirhastaḥ śatrur abhidāsann astu ye senābhir yudham āyanty asmān |
sam arpayendra mahatā vadhena drātv eṣām aghahāro vividdhaḥ ||1||

ātanvānā āyachanto 'syanto ye ca dhāvatha |
nirhastāḥ śatravaḥ sthanendro vo 'dya parāśarīt ||2||

nirhastāḥ santu śatravo 'ṅgaiṣāṃ mlāpayāmasi |
athaiṣām indra vedāṃsi śataśo vi bhajāmahai ||3||


pari vartmāni sarvata indraḥ pūṣā ca sasratuḥ |
muhyantv adyāmūḥ senā amitrāṇāṃ parastarām ||1||

mūḍhā amitrāś caratāśīrṣāṇa ivāhayaḥ |
teṣāṃ vo agnimūḍhānām indro hantu varaṃvaram ||2||

aiṣu nahya vṛṣājinaṃ hariṇasya bhiyaṃ kṛdhi |
parāṅ amitra eṣatv arvācī gaur upeṣatu ||3||



āyam agant savitā kṣureṇoṣṇena vāya udakenehi |
ādityā rudrā vasava undantu sacetasaḥ somasya rājño vapata pracetasaḥ ||1||

aditiḥ śmaśru vapatv āpa undantu varcasā |
cikitsatu prajāpatir dīrghāyutvāya cakṣase ||2||

yenāvapat savitā kṣureṇa somasya rājño varuṇasya vidvān |
tena brahmāṇo vapatedam asya gomān aśvavān ayam astu prajāvān ||3||



girāv aragarāṭeṣu hiranye goṣu yad yaśaḥ |
surāyāṃ sicyamānāyāṃ kīlāle madhu tan mayi ||1||

aśvinā sāragheṇa mā madhunāṅktaṃ śubhas patī |
yathā bhargasvatīṃ vācam āvadāni janāṃ anu ||2||

mayi varco atho yaśo 'tho yajñasya yat payaḥ |
tan mayi prajāpatir divi dyām iva dṛṃhatu ||3||



yathā māṃsam yathā surā yathākṣā adhidevane |
yathā puṃso vṛṣaṇyata striyāṃ nihanyate manaḥ |
evā te aghnye mano 'dhi vatse ni hanyatām ||1||

yathā hastī hastinyāḥ padena padam udyuje |
yathā puṃso vṛṣaṇyata striyāṃ nihanyate manaḥ |
evā te aghnye mano 'dhi vatse ni hanyatām ||2||

yathā pradhir yathopadhir yathā nabhyaṃ pradhāv adhi |
yathā puṃso vṛṣaṇyata striyāṃ nihanyate manaḥ |
evā te aghnye mano 'dhi vatse ni hanyatām ||3||



yad annam admi bahudhā virūpaṃ hiraṇyam aśvam uta gām ajām avim |
yad eva kiṃ ca pratijagrahāham agniṣ ṭad dhotā suhutaṃ kṛnotu ||1||

yan mā hutam ahutam ājagāma dattaṃ pitṛbhir anumataṃ manuṣyaiḥ |
yasmān me mana ud iva rārajīty agniṣ ṭad dhotā suhutaṃ kṛṇotu ||2||

yad annam admy anṛtena devā dāsyann adāsyann uta saṃgṛṇāmi |
vaiśvānarasya mahato mahimnā śivaṃ mahyaṃ madhumad astv annam ||3||



yathāsitaḥ prathayate vaśām anu vapūṃṣi kṛṇvann asurasya māyayā |
evā te śepaḥ sahasāyam arko 'ṅgenāṅgaṃ saṃsamakaṃ kṛṇotu ||1||

yathā pasas tāyādaraṃ vātena sthūlabhaṃ kṛtam |
yāvat parasvataḥ pasas tāvat te vardhatāṃ pasaḥ ||2||

yāvadaṅgīnaṃ pārasvataṃ hāstinaṃ gārdabham ca yat |
yāvad aśvasya vājinas tāvat te vardhatāṃ pasaḥ ||3||



eha yātu varuṇaḥ somo agnir bṛhaspatir vasubhir eha yātu |
asya śriyam upasaṃyāta sarva ugrasya cettuḥ saṃmanasaḥ sajātāḥ ||1||

yo vaḥ śuṣmo hṛdayeṣv antar ākūtir yā vo manasi praviṣṭā |
tānt sīvayāmi haviṣā ghṛtena mayi sajātā ramatir vo astu ||2||

ihaiva sta māpa yātādhy asmat pūṣā parastād apatham vaḥ kṛṇotu |
vāstoṣ patir anu vo johavītu mayi sajātā ramatiḥ vo astu ||3||



saṃ vaḥ pṛcyantāṃ tanvaḥ saṃ manāṃsi sam u vratā |
sam vo 'yam brahmaṇas patir bhagaḥ saṃ vo ajīgamat ||1||

samjñapanaṃ vo manaso 'tho samjñapanam hṛdaḥ |
atho bhagasya yac chrāntaṃ tena saṃjñapayāmi vaḥ ||2||

yathādityā vasubhiḥ sambabhūvur marudbhir ugrā ahṛṇīyamānāḥ |
evā triṇāmann ahṛṇīyamāna imān janānt saṃmanasas kṛdhīha ||3||



nir amuṃ nuda okasaḥ sapatno yaḥ pṛtanyati |
nairbādhyena haviṣendra enaṃ parāśarīt ||1||

paramāṃ taṃ parāvatam indro nudatu vṛtrahā |
yato na punar āyati śaśvatībhyaḥ samābhyaḥ ||2||

etu tisraḥ parāvata etu pañca janāṃ ati |
etu tisro 'ti rocanā yato na punar āyati |
śaśvatībhyaḥ samābhyo yāvat sūryo asad divi ||3||



ya enaṃ pariṣīdanti samādadhati cakṣase |
saṃpreddho agnir jihvābhir ud etu hṛdayād adhi ||1||

agneḥ sāmtapanasyāham āyuṣe padam ā rabhe |
addhātir yasya paśyati dhūmam udyantam āsyataḥ ||2||

yo asya samidhaṃ veda kṣatriyeṇa samāhitām |
nābhihvāre padaṃ ni dadhāti sa mṛtyave ||3||

nainaṃ ghnanti paryāyiṇo na sannāṃ ava gachati |
agner yaḥ kṣatriyo vidvān nāma gṛhnāti āyuṣe ||4||



asthād dyaur asthāt pṛthivy asthād viśvam idaṃ jagat |
āsthāne parvatā asthu sthāmny aśvāṃ atiṣṭhipam ||1||

ya udānat parāyaṇaṃ ya udānaṇ nyāyanam |
āvartanam nivartanaṃ yo gopā api taṃ huve ||2||

jātavedo ni vartaya śataṃ te santv āvṛtaḥ |
sahasraṃ ta upāvṛtas tābhir naḥ punar ā kṛdhi ||3||



tena bhūtena haviṣāyam ā pyāyatāṃ punaḥ |
jāyām yām asmā āvākṣus tām rasenābhi vardhatām ||1||

abhi vardhatāṃ payasābhi rāṣṭreṇa vardhatām |
rayyā sahasravarcasemau stām anupakṣitau ||2||

tvaṣṭā jāyām ajanayat tvaṣṭāsyai tvāṃ patim |
tvaṣṭā sahasram āyuṃṣi dīrgham āyuḥ kṛṇotu vām ||3||



ayaṃ no nabhasas patiḥ saṃsphāno abhi rakṣatu |
asamātim gṛheṣu naḥ ||1||

tvaṃ no nabhasas pate ūrjaṃ gṛhesu dhāraya |
ā puṣṭam etv ā vasu ||2||

deva saṃsphāna sahasrāpoṣasyeśiṣe |
tasya no rāsva tasya no dhehi tasya te bhaktivāmsaḥ syāma ||3||



antarikṣeṇa patati viśvā bhūtāvacākaśat |
śuno divyasya yan mahas tenā te haviṣā vidhema ||1||

ye trayaḥ kālakāñjā divi devā iva śritāḥ |
tānt sarvān ahva ūtaye 'smā ariṣṭatātaye ||2||

apsu te janma divi te sadhasthaṃ samudre antar mahimā te pṛthivyām |
śuno divyasya yan mahas tenā te haviṣā vidhema ||3||



yantāsi yachase hastāv apa rakṣāṃsi sedhasi |
prajāṃ dhanaṃ ca gṛhṇānaḥ parihasto abhūd ayam ||1||

parihasta vi dhāraya yoniṃ garbhāya dhātave |
maryāde putram ā dhehi taṃ tvam ā gamayāgame ||2||

yaṃ parihastam abibhar aditiḥ putrakāmyā |
tvaṣṭā tam asyā ā badhnād yathā putraṃ janād ||3||



āgachata āgatasya nāma gṛhṇāmy āyataḥ |
indrasya vṛtraghno vanve vāsavasya śatakratoḥ ||1||

yena sūryāṃ sāvitrīm aśvinohatuḥ pathā |
tena mām abravīd bhago jayām ā vahatād iti ||2||

yas te 'ṅkuśo vasudāno bṛhann indra hiraṇyayaḥ |
tenā janiyate jāyāṃ mahyaṃ dhehi śacīpate ||3||



apacitaḥ pra patata suparṇo vasater iva |
sūryaḥ kṛṇotu bheṣajaṃ candramā vo 'pochatu ||1||

eny ekā śyeny ekā kṛṣṇaikā rohiṇī dve |
sarvāsām agrabhaṃ nāmāvīraghnīr apetana ||2||

asūtikā rāmāyaṇy apacit pra patiṣyati |
glaur itaḥ pra patiṣyati sa galunto naśiṣyati ||3||

vīhi svām āhutiṃ juṣāno manasā svāhā manasā yad idaṃ juhomi ||4||



yasyās ta āsani ghore juhomy eṣāṃ baddhānām avasarjanāya kam |
bhūmir iti tvābhipramanvate janā nirṛtir iti tvāhaṃ pari veda sarvataḥ ||1||

bhūte haviṣmatī bhavaiṣa te bhāgo yo asmāsu |
muñcemān amūn enasaḥ svāhā ||2||

evo ṣv asman nirṛte 'nehā tvam ayasmayān vi cṛtā bandhapāśān |
yamo mahyaṃ punar it tvāṃ dadāti tasmai yamāya namo astu mṛtyave ||3||

ayasmaye drupade bedhiṣa ihābhihito mṛtyubhir ye sahasram |
yamena tvaṃ pitṛbhiḥ saṃvidāna uttamaṃ nākam adhi rohayemam ||4||



varaṇo vārayātā ayaṃ devo vanaspatiḥ |
yakṣmo yo asminn āviṣṭas tam u devā avīvaran ||1||

indrasya vacasā vayaṃ mitrasya varuṇasya ca |
devānāṃ sarveṣāṃ vācā yakṣmaṃ te vārayāmahe ||2||

yathā vṛtra imā āpas tastambha viśvadhā yatīḥ |
evā te agninā yakṣmaṃ vaiśvānareṇa vāraye ||3||



vṛṣendrasya vṛṣā divo vṛsā pṛthivyā ayam |
vṛṣā viśvasya bhūtasya tvam ekavṛṣo bhava ||1||

samudra īśe sravatām agniḥ pṛthivyā vaśī |
candramā nakṣatrāṇām īśe tvam ekavṛṣo bhava ||2||

samrāḍ asy asurāṇāṃ kakun manuṣyānām |
devānām ardhabhāg asi tvam ekavṛṣo bhava ||3||



ā tvāhārṣam antar abhūr dhruvas tiṣṭhāvicācalat |
viśas tvā sarvā vāñchantu mā tvad rāṣṭram adhi bhraśat ||1||

ihaivaidhi māpa cyoṣṭhāḥ parvata ivāvicācalat |
indra iveha dhruvas tiṣṭheha rāṣṭram u dhāraya ||2||

indra etam adīdharat dhruvaṃ dhruveṇa haviṣā |
tasmai somo adhi bravad ayaṃ ca brahmaṇas patiḥ ||3||



dhruvā dyaur dhruvā pṛthivī dhruvaṃ viśvam idaṃ jagat |
dhruvāsaḥ parvatā ime dhruvo rājā viśām ayam ||1||

dhruvaṃ te rājā varuṇo dhruvam devo bṛhaspatiḥ |
dhruvaṃ ta indraś cāgniś ca rāṣṭraṃ dhārayatāṃ dhruvam ||2||

dhruvo 'cyutaḥ pra mṛṇīhi śatrūn chatrūyato 'dharān pādayasva |
sarvā diśaḥ saṃmanasaḥ sadhrīcīr dhruvāya te samitiḥ kalpatām iha ||3||



idaṃ yat preṇyaḥ śiro dattaṃ somena vṛṣṇyam |
tataḥ pari prajātena hārdiṃ te śocayāmasi ||1||

śocayāmasi te hārdiṃ śocayāmasi te manaḥ |
vātaṃ dhūma iva sadhryaṅ mām evānv etu ye manaḥ ||2||

mahyaṃ tvā mitrāvaruṇau mahyaṃ devī sarasvatī |
mahyaṃ tvā madhyaṃ bhūmyā ubhāv antau sam asyatām ||3||



yāṃ te rudra iṣum āsyad aṅgebhyo hṛdayāya ca |
idaṃ tām adya tvad vayaṃ viṣūcīṃ vi vṛhāmasi ||1||

yās te śataṃ dhamanayo 'ṅgāny anu viṣṭhitāḥ |
tāsāṃ te sarvāsām vayaṃ nir viṣāṇi hvayāmasi ||2||

namas te rudrāsyate namaḥ pratihitāyai |
namo visṛjyamānāyai namo nipatitāyai ||3||



imaṃ yavam aṣṭāyogaiḥ ṣadyogebhir acarkṛṣuḥ |
tenā te tanvo rapo 'pācīnam apa vyaye ||1||

nyag vāto vāti nyak tapati sūryaḥ |
nīcīnam aghnyā duhe nyag bhavatu te rapaḥ ||2||

āpa id vā u bheṣajīr āpo amīvacātanīḥ |
āpo viśvasya bheṣajīs tās te kṛṇvantu bheṣajam ||3||



vātaraṃhā bhava vājin yujamāna indrasya yāhi prasave manojavāḥ |
yuñjantu tvā maruto viśvavedasa ā te tvastā patsu javaṃ dadhātu ||1||

javas te arvan nihito guhā yaḥ śyene vāte uta yo 'carat parīttaḥ |
tena tvaṃ vājin balavān balenājiṃ jaya samane parayiṣṇuḥ ||2||

tanūṣ ṭe vājin tanvaṃ nayantī vāmam asmabhyaṃ dhāvatu śarma tubhyam |
ahruto maho dharuṇāya devo divīva jyotiḥ svam ā mimīyāt ||3||



yamo mṛtyur aghamāro nirṛtho babhruḥ śarvo 'stā nīlaśikhaṇḍaḥ |
devajanāḥ senayottasthivāṃsas te asmākaṃ pari vṛñjantu vīrān ||1||

manasā homair harasā ghṛtena śarvāyāstra uta rājñe bhavāya |
namasyebhyo nama ebhyaḥ kṛṇomy anyatrāsmad aghaviṣā nayantu ||2||

trāyadhvaṃ no aghaviṣābhyo vadhād viśve devā maruto viśvavedasaḥ |
agnīṣomā varuṇaḥ pūtadakṣā vātāparjanyayoḥ sumatau syāma ||3||



saṃ vo manāṃsi saṃ vratā sam ākūtīr namāmasi |
amī ye vivratā sthana tān vaḥ saṃ namayāmasi ||1||

ahaṃ gṛbhṇāmi manasā manāṃsi mama cittam anu cittebhir eta |
mama vaśeṣu hṛdayāni vaḥ kṛṇomi mama yātam anuvartmāna eta ||2||

ote me dyāvāpṛthivī otā devī sarasvatī |
otau ma indraś cāgniś ca rdhyāsmedaṃ sarasvati ||3||



aśvattho devasadanas tṛtīyasyām ito divi |
tatrāmṛtasya cakṣaṇam devāḥ kuṣṭham avanvata ||1||

hiraṇyayī naur acarad dhiraṇyabandhanā divi |
tatrāmṛtasya puṣpaṃ devāḥ kuṣṭham avanvata ||2||

garbho asy oṣadhīnāṃ garbho himavatām uta |
garbho viśvasya bhūtasyemaṃ me agadaṃ kṛdhi ||3||


yā oṣadhayaḥ somarājñīr bahvīḥ śatavicakṣaṇāḥ |
bṛhaspatiprasūtās tā no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ||1||

muñcantu mā śapathyād atho varuṇyād uta |
atho yamasya paḍvīśād viśvasmād devakilbiṣāt ||2||

yac cakṣuṣā manasā yac ca vācopārima jāgrato yat svapantaḥ |
somas tāni svadhayā naḥ punātu ||3||



abhibhūr yajño abhibhūr agnir abhibhūḥ somo abhibhūr indraḥ |
abhy ahaṃ viśvāḥ pṛtanā yathāsāny evā vidhemāgnihotrā idaṃ haviḥ ||1||

svadhāstu mitrāvaruṇā vipaścitā prajāvat kṣatraṃ madhuneha pinvatam |
bādhethāṃ dūraṃ nirṛtiṃ parācaiḥ kṛtaṃ cid enaḥ pra mumuktam asmat ||2||

imaṃ vīram anu harṣadhvam ugram indraṃ sakhāyo anu saṃ rabhadhvam |
grāmajitaṃ gojitaṃ vajrabāhuṃ jayantam ajma pramṛṇantam ojasā ||3||



indro jayāti na parā jayātā adhirājo rājasu rājayātai |
carkṛtya īḍyo vandyaś copasadyo namasyś bhaveha ||1||

tvam indrādhirājaḥ śravasyus tvaṃ bhūr abhibhūtir janānām |
tvaṃ daivīr viśa imā vi rājāyuṣmat kṣatram ajaraṃ te astu ||2||

prācyā diśas tvam indrāsi rājotodīcyā diśo vṛtrahan chatruho 'si |
yatra yanti srotyās taj jitaṃ te dakṣiṇato vṛṣabha eṣi havyaḥ ||3||



abhi tvendra varimataḥ purā tvāṃhūraṇād dhuve |
hvayāmy ugraṃ cettāraṃ puruṇāmānam ekajam ||1||

yo adya senyo vadho jighāṃsan na udīrate |
indrasya tatra bāhū samantaṃ pari dadmaḥ ||2||

pari dadma indrasya bāhū samantaṃ trātus trāyatāṃ naḥ |
deva savitaḥ soma rājant sumanasaṃ mā kṛṇu svastaye ||3||



6,100.1a devā aduḥ sūryo dyaur adāt pṛthivy adāt |
6,100.1c tisraḥ sarasvatir aduḥ sacittā viṣadūṣaṇam ||1||

6,100.2a yad vo devā upajīkā āsiñcan dhanvany udakam |
6,100.2c tena devaprasūtenedaṃ dūṣayatā viṣam ||2||
6,100.3a asurāṇāṃ duhitāsi sā devānām asi svasā |
6,100.3c divas pṛthivyāḥ saṃbhūtā sā cakarthārasaṃ viṣam ||3||



6,101.1a ā vṛṣāyasva śvasihi vardhasva prathayasva ca |
6,101.1c yathāṅgaṃ vardhatāṃ śepas tena yoṣitam ij jahi ||1||

6,101.2a yena kṛṣaṃ vājayanti yena hinvanty āturam |
6,101.2c tenāsya brahmaṇas pate dhanur ivā tānayā pasaḥ ||2||

6,101.3a āhaṃ tanomi te paso adhi jyām iva dhanvani |
6,101.3c kramasva ṛṣa iva rohitam anavaglāyatā sadā ||3||



6,102.1a yathāyaṃ vāho aśvinā samaiti saṃ ca vartate |
6,102.1c evā mām abhi te manaḥ samaitu saṃ ca vartatām ||1||

6,102.2a āhaṃ khidāmi te mano rājāśvaḥ pṛṣṭyām iva |
6,102.2c reṣmachinnam yathā tṛṇaṃ mayi te veṣṭatāṃ manaḥ ||2||

6,102.3a āñjanasya madughasya kuṣṭhasya naladasya ca |
6,102.3c turo bhagasya hastābhyām anurodhanam ud bhare ||3||



6,103.1a saṃdānaṃ vo bṛhaspatiḥ saṃdānaṃ savitā karat |
6,103.1c saṃdānaṃ mitro aryamā saṃdānaṃ bhago aśvinā ||1||

6,103.2a sam paramānt sam avamān atho saṃ dyāmi madhyamān |
6,103.2c indras tān pary ahār dāmnā tān agne saṃ dyā tvam ||2||

6,103.3a amī ye yudham āyanti ketūn kṛtvānīkaśaḥ |
6,103.3c indras tān pary ahār dāmna tān agne saṃ dyā tvam ||3||


6,104.1a ādānena saṃdānenāmitrān ā dyāmasi |
6,104.1c apānā ye caiṣāṃ prāṇā asunāsūnt sam achidan ||1||

6,104.2a idam ādānam akaraṃ tapasendreṇa saṃśitam |
6,104.2c amitrā ye 'tra naḥ santi tān agna ā dyā tvam ||2||

6,104.3a ainān dyatām indrāgnī somo rājā ca medinau |
6,104.3c indro marutvān ādānam amitrebhyaḥ kṛṇotu naḥ ||3||



6,105.1a yathā mano manasketaiḥ parāpataty āśumat |
6,105.1c evā tvaṃ kāse pra pata manaso 'nu pravāyyam ||1||

6,105.2a yathā bāṇaḥ susaṃśitaḥ parāpataty āśumat |
6,105.2c evā tvaṃ kāse pra pata pṛthivyā anu saṃvatam ||2||

6,105.3a yathā sūryasya raśmayaḥ parāpatanty āśumat |
6,105.3c evā tvaṃ kāse pra pata samudrasyānu vikṣaram ||3||



6,106.1a āyane te parāyane dūrvā rohantu puṣpiṇīḥ |
6,106.1c utso vā tatra jāyatām hrado vā puṇḍarīkavān ||1||

6,106.2a apām idaṃ nyayanaṃ samudrasya niveśanam |
6,106.2c madhye hradasya no gṛhāḥ parācīnā mukhā kṛdhi ||2||

6,106.3a himasya tvā jarāyuṇā śāle pari vyayāmasi |
6,106.3c śītahradā hi no bhuvo 'gniṣ kṛṇotu bheṣajam ||3||



6,107.1a viśvajit trāyamāṇāyai mā pari dehi |
6,107.1c trāyamāṇe dvipāc ca sarvaṃ no rakṣa catuṣpāḍ yac ca naḥ svam ||1||

6,107.2a trāyamāṇe viśvajite mā pari dehi |
6,107.2c viśvajid dvipāc ca sarvaṃ no rakṣa catuṣpāḍ yac ca naḥ svam ||2||

6,107.3a viśvajit kalyāṇyai mā pari dehi |
6,107.3c kalyāṇi dvipāc ca sarvaṃ no rakṣa catuṣpāḍ yac ca naḥ svam ||3||

6,107.4a kalyāṇi sarvavide mā pari dehi |
6,107.4c sarvavid dvipāc ca sarvaṃ no rakṣa catuṣpāḍ yac ca naḥ svam ||4||



6,108.1a tvaṃ no medhe prathamā gobhir aśvebhir ā gahi |
6,108.1c tvaṃ sūryasya raśmibhis tvam no asi yajñiyā ||1||

6,108.2a medhām ahaṃ prathamāṃ brahmaṇvatīṃ brahmajūtām ṛṣiṣṭutām |
6,108.2c prapītāṃ brahmacāribhir devānām avase huve ||2||

6,108.3a yāṃ medhām ṛbhavo vidur yāṃ medhām asurā viduḥ |
6,108.3c ṛṣayo bhadrāṃ medhāṃ yāṃ vidus tāṃ mayy ā veśayāmasi ||3||

6,108.4a yām ṛṣayo bhūtakṛto medhāṃ medhāvino viduḥ |
6,108.4c tayā mām adya medhayāgne medhāvinaṃ kṛṇu ||4||

6,108.5a medhāṃ sāyaṃ medhāṃ prātar medhāṃ madhyandinaṃ pari |
6,108.5c medhāṃ sūryasya raśmibhir vacasā veśayāmahe ||5||



6,109.1a pippalī kṣiptabheṣajy utātividdhabheṣajī |
6,109.1c tāṃ devāḥ sam akalpayann iyaṃ jīvitavā alam ||1||

6,109.2a pippalyaḥ sam avadantāyatīr jananād adhi |
6,109.2c yaṃ jīvam aśnavāmahai na sa riṣyāti pūruṣaḥ ||2||

6,109.3a asurās tvā ny akhanan devās tvod avapan punaḥ |
6,109.3c vātīkṛtasya bheṣajīm atho kṣiptasya bheṣajīm ||3||



6,110.1a pratno hi kam īḍyo adhvareṣu sanāc ca hotā navyaś ca satsi |
6,110.1c svām cāgne tanvaṃ piprāyasvāsmabhyaṃ ca saubhagam ā yajasva ||1||

6,110.2a jyeṣṭhaghnyāṃ jāto vicṛtor yamasya mūlabarhaṇāt pari pāhy enam |
6,110.2c aty enam neṣad duritāni viśvā dīrghāyutvāya śataśāradāya ||2||

6,110.3a vyāghre 'hny ajaniṣṭa vīro nakṣatrajā jāyamānaḥ suvīraḥ |
6,110.3c sa mā vadhīt pitaraṃ vardhamāno mā mātaraṃ pra minīj janitrīm ||3||



6,111.1a imam me agne puruṣam mumugdhy ayaṃ yo baddhaḥ suyato lālapīti |
6,111.1c ato 'dhi te kṛṇavad bhāgadheyaṃ yadānunmadito 'sati ||1||

6,111.2a agniṣ ṭe ni śamayatu yadi te mana udyutam |
6,111.2c kṛṇomi vidvān bheṣajaṃ yathānunmadito 'sasi ||2||

6,111.3a devainasād unmaditam unmattam rakṣasas pari |
6,111.3c kṛṇomi vidvān bheṣajaṃ yadānunmadito 'sati ||3||

6,111.4a punas tvā dur apsarasaḥ punar indraḥ punar bhagaḥ |
6,111.4c punas tvā dur viśve devā yathānunmadito 'sasi ||4||


6,112.1a mā jyeṣṭhaṃ vadhīd ayam agna eṣām mūlabarhaṇāt pari pāhy enam |
6,112.1c sa grāhyāḥ pāśān vi cṛta prajānan tubhyaṃ devā anu jānantu viśve ||1||

6,112.2a un muñca pāśāṃs tvam agna eṣāṃ trayas tribhir utsitā yebhir āsan |
6,112.2c sa grāhyāḥ pāśān vi cṛta prajānan pitāputrau mātaraṃ muñca sarvān ||2||

6,112.3a yebhiḥ pāśaiḥ parivitto vibaddho 'ṅgeaṅga ārpita utsitaś ca |
6,112.3c vi te mucyantaṃ vimuco hi santi bhrūṇaghni pūṣan duritāni mṛkṣva ||3||



6,113.1a trite devā amṛjataitad enas trita enan manuṣyeṣu mamṛje |
6,113.1c tato yadi tvā grāhir ānaśe tāṃ te devā brahmaṇā nāśayantu ||1||

6,113.2a marīcīr dhūmān pra viśānu pāpmann udārān gachota vā nīhārān |
6,113.2c nadīnaṃ phenāṃ anu tān vi naśya bhrūṇaghni pūṣan duritāni mṛkṣva ||2||

6,113.3a dvādaśadhā nihitaṃ tritasyāpamṛṣṭam manuṣyainasāni |
6,113.3c tato yadi tvā grāhir ānaśe tāṃ te devā brahmaṇā nāśayantu ||3||



6,114.1a yad devā devaheḍanaṃ devāsaś cakṛma vayam |
6,114.1c ādityās tasmān no yuyam ṛtasya ṛtena muñcata ||1||

6,114.2a ṛtasya ṛtenādityā yajatrā muñcateha naḥ |
6,114.2c yajñaṃ yad yajñavāhasaḥ śikṣanto nopaśekima ||2||

6,114.3a medasvatā yajamānāḥ srucājyāni juhvataḥ |
6,114.3c akāmā viśve vo devāḥ śikṣanto nopa śekima ||3||



6,115.1a yad vidvāṃso yad avidvāṃsa enāṃsi cakṛmā vayam |
6,115.1c yūyaṃ nas tasmān muñcata viśve devāḥ sajoṣasaḥ ||1||

6,115.2a yadi jāgrad yadi svapann ena enasyo 'karam |
6,115.2c bhūtaṃ mā tasmād bhavyaṃ ca drupadād iva muñcatām ||2||

6,115.3a drupadād iva mumucānaḥ svinnaḥ snātvā malād iva |
6,115.3c pūtaṃ pavitreṇevājyaṃ viśve śumbhantu mainasaḥ ||3||



6,116.1a yad yāmaṃ cakrur nikhananto agre kārṣīvaṇā annavido na vidyayā |
6,116.1c vaivasvate rājani taj juhomy atha yajñiyaṃ madhumad astu no 'nnam ||1||

6,116.2a vaivasvataḥ kṛṇavad bhāgadheyaṃ madhubhāgo madhunā saṃ sṛjāti |
6,116.2c mātur yad ena iṣitaṃ na āgan yad vā pitā 'parāddho jihīde ||2||

6,116.3a yadīdaṃ mātur yadi pitur naḥ pari bhrātuḥ putrāc cetasa ena āgan |
6,116.3c yāvanto asmān pitaraḥ sacante teṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ śivo astu manyuḥ ||3||



6,117.1a apamityam apratīttaṃ yad asmi yamasya yena balinā carāmi |
6,117.1c idaṃ tad agne anṛṇo bhavāmi tvaṃ pāśān vicṛtaṃ vettha sarvān ||1||

6,117.2a ihaiva santaḥ prati dadma enaj jīvā jīvebhyo ni harāma enat |
6,117.2c apamitya dhānyaṃ yaj jaghasāham idaṃ tad agne anṛṇo bhavāmi ||2||

6,117.3a anṛṇā asminn anṛṇāḥ parasmin tṛtīye loke anṛṇāḥ syāma |
6,117.3c ye devayānāḥ pitṛyāṇaś ca lokāḥ sarvān patho anṛṇā ā kṣiyema ||3||



6,118.1a yad dhastābhyāṃ cakṛma kilbiṣāṇy akṣāṇāṃ gatnum upalipsamānāḥ |
6,118.1c ugraṃpaśye ugrajitau tad adyāpsarasāv anu dattām ṛṇaṃ naḥ ||1||

6,118.2a ugraṃpaśye rāṣṭrabhṛt kilbiṣāṇi yad akṣavṛttam anu dattam na etat |
6,118.2c ṛṇān no na ṛṇam ertsamāno yamasya loke adhirajjur āyat ||2||

6,118.3a yasmā ṛṇaṃ yasya jāyām upaimi yaṃ yācamāno abhyaimi devāḥ |
6,118.3c te vācaṃ vādiṣur mottarāṃ mad devapatnī apsarasāv adhītam ||3||



6,119.1a yad adīvyann ṛṇam ahaṃ kṛṇomy adāsyann agne uta saṃgṛṇāmi |
6,119.1c vaiśvānaro no adhipā vasiṣṭha ud in nayāti sukṛtasya lokam ||1||

6,119.2a vaiśvānarāya prati vedayāmi yadi ṛṇaṃ saṃgaro devatāsu |
6,119.2c sa etān pāśān vicṛtam veda sarvān atha pakvena saha saṃ bhavema ||2||

6,119.3a vaiśvānaraḥ pavitā mā punātu yat saṃgaram abhidhāvāmy āśām |
6,119.3c anājānan manasā yācamāno yat tatraino apa tat suvāmi ||3||



6,120.1a yad antarikṣaṃ pṛthivīm uta dyām yan mātaraṃ pitaraṃ vā jihiṃsima |
6,120.1c ayaṃ tasmād gārhapatyo no agnir ud in nayāti sukṛtasya lokam ||1||

6,120.2a bhūmir mātāditir no janitraṃ bhrātāntarikṣam abhiśastyā naḥ |
6,120.2c dyaur naḥ pitā pitryāc chaṃ bhavāti jāmim ṛtvā māva patsi lokāt ||2||

6,120.3a yatrā suhārdaḥ sukṛto madanti vihāya rogaṃ tanvaḥ svāyāḥ |
6,120.3c aślonā aṅgair ahrutāḥ svarge tatra paśyema pitarau ca putrān ||3||



6,121.1a viṣāṇā pāśān vi ṣyādhy asmad ya uttamā adhamā vāruṇā ye |
6,121.1c duṣvapnyaṃ duritaṃ ni ṣvāsmad atha gachema sukṛtasya lokam ||1||

6,121.2a yad dāruṇi badhyase yac ca rajjvāṃ yad bhūmyāṃ badhyase yac ca vācā |
6,121.2c ayaṃ tasmād gārhapatyo no agnir ud in nayāti sukṛtasya lokam ||2||

6,121.3a ud agātāṃ bhagavatī vicṛtau nāma tārake |
6,121.3c prehāmṛtasya yachatāṃ praitu baddhakamocanam ||3||

6,121.4a vi jihīṣva lokam kṛṇu bandhān muñcāsi baddhakam |
6,121.4c yonyā iva pracyuto garbhaḥ pathaḥ sarvāṃ anu kṣiya ||4||



6,122.1a etaṃ bhāgaṃ pari dadāmi vidvān viśvakarman prathamajā ṛtasya |
6,122.1c asmābhir dattaṃ jarasaḥ parastād achinnaṃ tantum anu saṃ tarema ||1||

6,122.2a tataṃ tantum anv eke taranti yeṣāṃ dattaṃ pitryam āyanena |
6,122.2c abandhv eke dadataḥ prayachanto dātuṃ cec chikṣānt sa svarga eva ||2||

6,122.3a anvārabhethām anusaṃrabhethām etaṃ lokaṃ śraddadhānāḥ sacante |
6,122.3c yad vāṃ pakvaṃ pariviṣṭam agnau tasya guptaye dampatī saṃ śrayethām ||3||

6,122.4a yajñam yantaṃ manasā bṛhantam anvārohāmi tapasā sayoniḥ |
6,122.4c upahūtā agne jarasaḥ parastāt tṛtīye nāke sadhamādaṃ madema ||4||

6,122.5a śuddhāḥ pūtā yoṣito yajñiyā imā brahmaṇāṃ hasteṣu prapṛthak sādayāmi |
6,122.5c yatkāma idaṃ abhiṣiñcāmi vo 'haṃ indro marutvānt sa dadātu tan me ||5||



6,123.1a etaṃ sadhasthāḥ pari vo dadāmi yaṃ śevadhim āvahāj jātavedaḥ |
6,123.1c anvāgantā yajamānaḥ svasti taṃ sma jānīta parame vyoman ||1||

6,123.2a jānīta smainaṃ parame vyoman devāḥ sadhasthā vida lokam atra |
6,123.2c anvāgantā yajamānaḥ svastīṣṭāpūrtaṃ sma kṛṇutāvir asmai ||2||

6,123.3a devāḥ pitaraḥ pitaro devāḥ |
6,123.3c yo asmi so asmi ||3||

6,123.4a sa pacāmi sa dadāmi |
6,123.4c sa yaje sa dattān mā yūṣam ||4||

6,123.5a nāke rājan prati tiṣṭha tatraitat prati tiṣṭhatu |
6,123.5c viddhi pūrtasya no rājant sa deva sumanā bhava ||5||



6,124.1a divo nu mām bṛhato antarikṣād apāṃ stoko abhy apaptad rasena |
6,124.1c sam indriyena payasāham agne chandobhir yajñaiḥ sukṛtāṃ kṛtena ||1||

6,124.2a yadi vṛkṣād abhyapaptat phalaṃ tad yady antarikṣāt sa u vāyur eva |
6,124.2c yatrāspṛkṣat tanvo yac ca vāsasa āpo nudantu nirṛtiṃ parācaiḥ ||2||

6,124.3a abhyañjanaṃ surabhi sā samṛddhir hiraṇyaṃ varcas tad u pūtrimam eva |
6,124.3c sarvā pavitrā vitatādhy asmat tan mā tārīn nirṛtir mo arātiḥ ||3||



6,125.1a vanaspate vīḍvaṅgo hi bhūyā asmatsakhā prataraṇaḥ suvīraḥ |
6,125.1c gobhiḥ saṃnaddho asi vīḍayasvāsthātā te jayatu jetvāni ||1||

6,125.2a divas pṛthivyāḥ pary oja udbhṛtaṃ vanaspatibhyaḥ pary ābhṛtaṃ sahaḥ |
6,125.2c apām ojmānaṃ pari gobhir āvṛtam indrasya vajraṃ haviṣā rathaṃ yaja ||2||

6,125.3a indrasyaujo marutām anīkaṃ mitrasya garbho varuṇasya nābhiḥ |
6,125.3c sa imāṃ no havyadātiṃ juṣāṇo deva ratha prati havyā gṛbhāya ||3||


6,126.1a upa śvāsaya pṛthivīm uta dyaṃ purutrā te vanvatāṃ viṣṭhitam jagat |
6,126.1c sa dundubhe sajūr indreṇa devair dūrād davīyo apa sedha śatrūn ||1||

6,126.2a ā krandaya balam ojo na ā dhā abhi ṣṭana duritā bādhamānaḥ |
6,126.2c apa sedha dundubhe duchunām ita indrasya muṣṭir asi vīḍayasva ||2||

6,126.3a prāmūṃ jayābhīme jayantu ketumad dundubhir vāvadītu |
6,126.3c sam aśvaparṇāḥ patantu no naro 'smākam indra rathino jayantu ||3||



6,127.1a vidradhasya balāsasya lohitasya vanaspate |
6,127.1c visalpakasyauṣadhe moc chiṣaḥ piśitaṃ cana ||1||

6,127.2a yau te balāsa tiṣṭhataḥ kakṣe muṣkāv apaśritau |
6,127.2c vedāhaṃ tasya bheṣajaṃ cīpudrur abhicakṣaṇam ||2||

6,127.3a yo aṅgyo yaḥ karṇyo yo akṣyor visalpakaḥ |
6,127.3c vi vṛhāmo visalpakaṃ vidradhaṃ hṛdayāmayam |
6,127.3e parā tam ajñātam yakṣmam adharāñcaṃ suvāmasi ||3||



6,128.1a śakadhūmaṃ nakṣatrāṇi yad rājānam akurvata |
6,128.1c bhadrāham asmai prāyachan idaṃ rāṣṭram asād iti ||1||

6,128.2a bhadrāhaṃ no madhyaṃdine bhadrāhaṃ sāyam astu naḥ |
6,128.2c bhadrāhaṃ no ahnāṃ prātā rātrī bhadrāham astu naḥ ||2||

6,128.3a ahorātrābhyāṃ nakṣatrebhyaḥ suryācandramasābhyām |
6,128.3c bhadrāham asmabhyaṃ rājan chakadhūma tvaṃ kṛdhi ||3||

6,128.4a yo no bhadrāham akaraḥ sāyaṃ naktam atho divā |
6,128.4c tasmai te nakṣatrarāja śakadhūma sadā namaḥ ||4||



6,129.1a bhagena mā śāṃśapena sākam indreṇa medinā |
6,129.1c kṛṇomi bhaginaṃ māpa drāntv arātayaḥ ||1||

6,129.2a yena vṛkṣāṃ abhyabhavo bhagena varcasā saha |
6,129.2c tena mā bhaginaṃ kṛṇv apa drāntv arātayaḥ ||2||

6,129.3a yo andho yaḥ punaḥsaro bhago vṛkṣeṣv āhitaḥ |
6,129.3c tena mā bhaginaṃ kṛṇv apa drāntv arātayaḥ ||3||



6,130.1a rathajitāṃ rāthajiteyīnām apsarasām ayaṃ smaraḥ |
6,130.1c devāḥ pra hiṇuta smaram asau mām anu śocatu ||1||

6,130.2a asau me smaratād iti priyo me smaratād iti |
6,130.2c devāḥ pra hiṇuta smaram asau mām anu śocatu ||2||

6,130.3a yathā mama smarād asau nāmuṣyāhaṃ kadā cana |
6,130.3c devāḥ pra hiṇuta smaram asau mām anu śocatu ||3||

6,130.4a un mādayata maruta ud antarikṣa mādaya |
6,130.4c agna un mādayā tvam asau mām anu śocatu ||4||



6,131.1a ni śīrṣato ni pattata ādhyo ni tirāmi te |
6,131.1c devāḥ pra hiṇuta smaram asau mām anu śocatu ||1||

6,131.2a anumate 'nv idaṃ manyasvākute sam idaṃ namaḥ |
6,131.2c devāḥ pra hiṇuta smaram asau mām anu śocatu ||2||

6,131.3a yad dhāvasi triyojanaṃ pañcayojanam āśvinam |
6,131.3c tatas tvaṃ punar āyasi putrāṇāṃ no asaḥ pitā ||3||



6,132.1a yaṃ devāḥ smaram asiñcann apsv antaḥ śośucānaṃ sahādhyā |
6,132.1c taṃ te tapāmi varuṇasya dharmaṇā ||1||

6,132.2a yaṃ viśve devāḥ smaram asiñcann apsv antaḥ śośucānaṃ sahādhyā |
6,132.2c taṃ te tapāmi varuṇasya dharmaṇā ||2||

6,132.3a yam indrāṇī smaram asiñcad apsv antaḥ śośucānaṃ sahādhyā |
6,132.3c taṃ te tapāmi varuṇasya dharmaṇā ||3||

6,132.4a yam indrāgnī smaram asiñcatām apsv antaḥ śośucānaṃ sahādhyā |
6,132.4c taṃ te tapāmi varuṇasya dharmaṇā ||4||

6,132.5a yam mitrāvaruṇau smaram asiñcatām apsv antaḥ śośucānaṃ sahādhyā |
6,132.5c taṃ te tapāmi varuṇasya dharmaṇā ||5||



6,133.1a ya imāṃ devo mekhalām ābabandha yaḥ saṃnanāha ya u no yuyoja |
6,133.1c yasya devasya praśiṣā carāmaḥ sa pāram ichāt sa u no vi muñcāt ||1||

6,133.2a āhutāsy abhihuta ṛṣīṇām asy āyudham |
6,133.2c pūrvā vratasya prāśnatī vīraghnī bhava mekhale ||2||

6,133.3a mṛtyor ahaṃ brahmacārī yad asmi niryācan bhūtāt puruṣaṃ yamāya |
6,133.3c tam ahaṃ brahmaṇā tapasā śrameṇānayainaṃ mekhalayā sināmi ||3||

6,133.4a śraddhāyā duhitā tapaso 'dhi jātā svasā ṛṣīṇāṃ bhūtakṛtāṃ babhūva |
6,133.4c sā no mekhale matim ā dhehi medhām atho no dhehi tapa indriyaṃ ca ||4||

6,133.5a yāṃ tvā pūrve bhūtakṛta ṛṣayaḥ paribedhire |
6,133.5c sā tvaṃ pari ṣvajasva māṃ dīrghāyutvāya mekhale ||5||



6,134.1a ayaṃ vajras tarpayatām ṛtasyāvāsya rāṣṭram apa hantu jīvitam |
6,134.1c śṛṇātu grīvāḥ pra śṛṇātūṣṇihā vṛtrasyeva śacīpatiḥ ||1||

6,134.2a adharo'dhara uttarebhyo gūḍhaḥ pṛthivyā mot sṛpat |
6,134.2c vajreṇāvahataḥ śayām ||2||

6,134.3a yo jināti tam anvicha yo jināti tam ij jahi |
6,134.3c jinato vajra tvaṃ sīmantam anvañcam anu pātaya ||3||



6,135.1a yad aśnāmi balaṃ kurva itthaṃ vajram ā dade |
6,135.1c skandhān amuṣya śātayan vṛtrasyeva śacīpatiḥ ||1||

6,135.2a yat pibāmi saṃ pibāmi samudra iva saṃpibaḥ |
6,135.2c prāṇān amuṣya saṃpāya saṃ pibāmo amuṃ vayam ||2||

6,135.3a yad girāmi saṃ girāmi samudra iva saṃgiraḥ |
6,135.3c prāṇān amuṣya saṃgīrya saṃ girāmo amum vayam ||3||



6,136.1a devī devyām adhi jātā pṛthivyām asy oṣadhe |
6,136.1c tāṃ tvā nitatni keśebhyo dṛṃhaṇāya khanāmasi ||1||

6,136.2a dṛṃha pratnān janayājātān jātān u varṣīyasas kṛdhi ||2||

6,136.3a yas te keśo 'vapadyate samūlo yaś ca vṛścate |
6,136.3c idaṃ taṃ viśvabheṣajyābhi ṣiñcāmi vīrudhā ||3||



6,137.1a yāṃ jamadagnir akhanad duhitre keśavardhanīm |
6,137.1c tāṃ vītahavya ābharad asitasya gṛhebhyaḥ ||1||

6,137.2a abhīśunā meyā āsan vyāmenānumeyāḥ |
6,137.2c keśā naḍā iva vardhantāṃ śīrṣṇas te asitāḥ pari ||2||

6,137.3a dṛṃha mūlam āgraṃ yacha vi madhyaṃ yāmayauṣadhe |
6,137.3c keśā naḍā iva vardhantām śīrṣṇas te asitāḥ pari ||3||



6,138.1a tvaṃ vīrudhāṃ śreṣṭhatamābhiśrutāsy oṣadhe |
6,138.1c imaṃ me adya puruṣaṃ klībam opaśinaṃ kṛdhi ||1||

6,138.2a klībaṃ kṛdhy opaśinam atho kurīriṇaṃ kṛdhi |
6,138.2c athāsyendro grāvabhyām ubhe bhinattv āṇḍyau ||2||

6,138.3a klība klībaṃ tvākaraṃ vadhre vadhriṃ tvākaram arasārasaṃ tvākaram |
6,138.3c kurīram asya śīrṣaṇi kumbaṃ cādhinidadhmasi ||3||

6,138.4a ye te nādyau devakṛte yayos tiṣṭhati vṛṣṇyam |
6,138.4c te te bhinadmi śamyayāmuṣyā adhi muṣkayoḥ ||4||

6,138.5a yathā naḍam kaśipune striyo bhindanty aśmanā |
6,138.5c evā bhinadmi te śepo 'muṣyā adhi muṣkayoḥ ||5||



6,139.1a nyastikā rurohitha subhagaṃkaraṇī mama |
6,139.1c śataṃ tava pratānās trayastriṃśan nitānāḥ ||
6,139.1e tayā sahasraparṇyā hṛdayaṃ śoṣayāmi te ||1||

6,139.2a śuṣyatu mayi te hṛdayam atho śuṣyatv āsyam |
6,139.2c atho ni śuṣya māṃ kāmenātho śuṣkāsyā cara ||2||

6,139.3a saṃvananī samuṣpalā babhru kalyāṇi saṃ nuda |
6,139.3c amūṃ ca māṃ ca saṃ nuda samānaṃ hṛdayaṃ kṛdhi ||3||

6,139.4a yathodakam apapuṣo 'paśuṣyaty āsyam |
6,139.4c evā ni śuṣya māṃ kāmenātho śuṣkāsyā cara ||4||

6,139.5a yathā nakulo vichidya saṃdadhāty ahiṃ punaḥ |
6,139.5c evā kāmasya vichinnaṃ saṃ dhehi vīryāvati ||5||



6,140.1a yau vyāghrāv avarūdhau jighatsataḥ pitaraṃ mātaraṃ ca |
6,140.1c tau dantaṃ brahmaṇas pate śivau kṛṇu jātavedaḥ ||1||

6,140.2a vrīhim attaṃ yavam attam atho māṣam atho tilam |
6,140.2c eṣa vāṃ bhāgo nihito ratnadheyāya dantau mā hiṃsiṣṭaṃ pitaram mātaraṃ ca ||2||

6,140.3a upahūtau sayujau syonau dantau sumaṅgalau |
6,140.3c anyatra vāṃ ghoraṃ tanvaḥ paraitu dantau mā hiṃsiṣṭaṃ pitaraṃ mātaraṃ ca ||3||



6,141.1a vāyur enāḥ samākarat tvaṣṭā poṣāya dhriyatām |
6,141.1c indra ābhyo adhi bravad rudro bhūmne cikitsatu ||1||

6,141.2a lohitena svadhitinā mithunaṃ karṇayoḥ kṛdhi |
6,141.2c akartām aśvinā lakṣma tad astu prajayā bahu ||2||

6,141.3a yathā cakrur devāsurā yathā manuṣyā uta |
6,141.3c evā sahasrapoṣāya kṛṇutaṃ lakṣmāśvinā ||3||


6,142.1a uc chrayasva bahur bhava svena mahasā yava |
6,142.1c mṛṇīhi viśvā pātrāṇi mā tvā divyāśanir vadhīt ||1||

6,142.2a āśṛṇvantaṃ yavaṃ devaṃ yatra tvāchāvadāmasi |
6,142.2c tad uc chrayasva dyaur iva samudra ivaidhy akṣitaḥ ||2||

6,142.3a akṣitās ta upasado 'kṣitāḥ santu rāśayaḥ |
6,142.3c pṛṇanto akṣitāḥ santv attāraḥ santv akṣitāḥ ||3||



dhītī vā ye anayan vāco agraṃ manasā vā ye 'vadann ṛtāni |
tṛtīyena brahmaṇā vāvṛdhānās turīyeṇāmanvata nāma dhenoḥ ||1||

sa veda putraḥ pitaraṃ sa mātaraṃ sa sūnur bhuvat sa bhuvat punarmaghaḥ |
sa dyām aurṇod antarikṣaṃ svaḥ sa idaṃ viśvam abhavat sa ābharat ||2||



atharvāṇaṃ pitaraṃ devabandhuṃ mātur garbhaṃ pitur asuṃ yuvānam |
ya imaṃ yajñam manasā ciketa pra ṇo vocas tam iheha bravaḥ ||1||



ayā viṣṭhā janayan karvarāṇi sa hi ghṛṇir urur varāya gātuḥ |
sa pratyudaid dharuṇaṃ madhvo agraṃ svayā tanvā tanvam airayata ||1||


ekayā ca daśabhiś ca suhute dvābhyām iṣṭaye viṃśatyā ca |
tisṛbhiś ca vahase triṃśatā ca viyugbhir vāya iha tā vi muñca ||1||



yajñena yajñam ayajanta devās tāni dharmāṇi prathamāny āsan |
te ha nākaṃ mahimānaḥ sacanta yatra pūrve sādhyāḥ santi devāḥ ||1||

yajño babhūva sa ā babhūva sa pra jajñe sa u vāvṛdhe punaḥ |
sa devānām adhipatir babhūva so asmāsu draviṇam ā dadhātu ||2||

yad devā devān haviṣā 'yajantāmartyān manasā martyena |
madema tatra parame vyoman paśyema tad uditau sūryasya ||3||

yat puruṣeṇa haviṣā yajñaṃ devā atanvata |
asti nu tasmād ojīyo yad vihavyenejire ||4||

mugdhā devā uta śunā 'yajantota gor aṅgaiḥ purudhā 'yajanta |
ya imaṃ yajñaṃ manasā ciketa pra ṇo vocas tam iheha bravaḥ ||5||



aditir dyaur aditir antarikṣam aditir mātā sa pitā sa putraḥ |
viśve devā aditir pañca janā aditir jātam aditir janitvam ||1||

mahīm ū ṣu mātaraṃ suvratānām ṛtasya patnīm avase havāmahe |
tuvikṣatrām ajarantīm urūcīṃ suśarmāṇam aditiṃ supraṇītim ||2||

sutrāmāṇaṃ pṛthivīṃ dyām anehasaṃ suśarmāṇam aditiṃ supraṇītim |
daivīṃ nāvaṃ svaritrām anāgaso asravantīm ā ruhemā svastaye ||1||

vājasya nu prasave mātaraṃ mahīm aditiṃ nāma vacasā karāmahe |
yasyā upastha urv antarikṣaṃ sā naḥ śarma trivarūthaṃ ni yachāt ||2||



diteḥ putrāṇām aditer akāriṣam ava devānāṃ bṛhatām anarmaṇām |
teṣāṃ hi dhāma gabhiṣak samudriyaṃ nainān namasā paro asti kaścana ||1||



bhadrād adhi śreyaḥ prehi bṛhaspatiḥ puraetā te astu |
athemam asyā vara ā pṛthivyā āreśatruṃ kṛṇuhi sarvavīram ||1||



prapathe pathām ajaniṣṭa pūṣā prapathe divaḥ prapathe pṛthivyāḥ |
ubhe abhi priyatame sadhasthe ā ca parā ca carati prajānan ||1||

pūṣemā āśā anu veda sarvāḥ so asmāṃ abhayatamena neṣat |
svastidā āghṛṇiḥ sarvavīro 'prayuchan pura etu prajānan ||2||

pūṣan tava vrate vayaṃ na riṣyema kadā cana |
stotāras ta iha smasi ||3||

pari pūṣā parastād dhastaṃ dadhātu dakṣiṇam |
punar no naṣṭam ājatu saṃ naṣṭena gamemahi ||4||



yas te stanaḥ śaśayur yo mayobhūr yaḥ sumnayuḥ suhavo yaḥ sudatraḥ |
yena viśvā puṣyasi vāryāṇi sarasvati tam iha dhātave kaḥ ||1||



yas te pṛthu stanayitnur ya ṛṣvo daivaḥ ketur viśvam ābhūṣatīdam |
mā no vadhīr vidyutā deva sasyaṃ mota vadhī raśmibhiḥ sūryasya ||1||



sabhā ca mā samitiś cāvatāṃ prajāpater duhitarau saṃvidāne |
yenā saṃgachā upa mā sa śikṣāc cāru vadāni pitaraḥ saṃgateṣu ||1||

vidma te sabhe nāma nariṣṭā nāma vā asi |
ye te ke ca sabhāsadas te me santu savācasaḥ ||2||

eṣām ahaṃ samāsīnānāṃ varco vijñānam ā dade |
asyāḥ sarvasyāḥ saṃsado mām indra bhaginaṃ kṛṇu ||3||

yad vo manaḥ parāgataṃ yad baddham iha veha vā |
tad va ā vartayāmasi mayi vo ramatāṃ manaḥ ||4||



yathā sūryo nakṣatrāṇām udyaṃs tejāṃsy ādade |
evā strīṇāṃ ca puṃsāṃ ca dviṣatāṃ varca ā dade ||1||

yāvanto mā sapatnānām āyantaṃ pratipaśyatha |
udyant sūrya iva suptānāṃ dviṣatām varca ā dade ||2||



abhi tyaṃ devaṃ savitāram oṇyoḥ kavikratum |
arcāmi satyasavaṃ ratnadhām abhi priyaṃ matim ||1||

urdhvā yasyāmatir bhā adidyutat savīmani |
hiraṇyapāṇir amimīta sukratuḥ kṛpāt svaḥ ||2||

sāvīr hi deva prathamāya pitre varṣmāṇam asmai varimāṇam asmai |
athāsmabhyaṃ savitar vāryāṇi divodiva ā suvā bhūri paśvaḥ ||3||

damūnā devaḥ savitā vareṇyo dadhad ratnaṃ pitṛbhya āyūṃṣi |
pibāt somaṃ mamadad enam iṣṭe parijmā cit kramate asya dharmaṇi ||4||



tāṃ savitaḥ satyasavāṃ sucitrām āhaṃ vṛṇe sumatiṃ viśvavārām |
yām asya kaṇvo aduhat prapīnāṃ sahasradhārāṃ mahiṣo bhagāya ||1||



bṛhaspate savitar vardhayainaṃ jyotayainaṃ mahate saubhagāya |
saṃśitaṃ cit saṃtaraṃ saṃ śiśādhi viśva enam anu madantu devāḥ ||1||



dhātā dadhātu no rayim īśāno jagatas patiḥ |
sa naḥ pūrṇena yachatu ||1||

dhātā dadhātu dāśuṣe prācīṃ jīvātum akṣitām |
vayam devasya dhīmahi sumatiṃ viśvarādhasaḥ ||2||

dhātā viśvā vāryā dadhātu prajākāmāya dāśuṣe duroṇe |
tasmai devā amṛtaṃ saṃ vyayantu viśve devā aditiḥ sajoṣāḥ ||3||

dhātā rātiḥ savitedaṃ juṣantāṃ prajāpatir nidhipatir no agniḥ |
tvaṣṭā viṣṇuḥ prajayā saṃrarāṇo yajamānāya draviṇaṃ dadhātu ||4||



pra nabhasva pṛthivi bhinddhīdaṃ divyaṃ nabhaḥ |
udno divyasya no dhātar īśāno vi ṣyā dṛtim ||1||

na ghraṃs tatāpa na himo jaghāna pra nabhatāṃ pṛthivī jīradānuḥ |
āpaś cid asmai ghṛtam it kṣaranti yatra somaḥ sadam it tatra bhadram ||2||



prajāpatir janayati prajā imā dhātā dadhātu sumanasyamānaḥ |
saṃjānānāḥ saṃmanasaḥ sayonayo mayi puṣṭaṃ puṣṭapatir dadhātu ||1||



anv adya no 'numatir yajñaṃ deveṣu manyatām |
agniś ca havyavāhano bhavatāṃ dāśuṣe mama ||1||

anv id anumate tvaṃ maṃsase śaṃ ca nas kṛdhi |
juṣasva havyam āhutaṃ prajāṃ devi rarāsva naḥ ||2||

anu manyatām anumanyamānaḥ prajāvantaṃ rayim akṣīyamāṇam |
tasya vayaṃ heḍasi māpi bhūma sumṛḍīke asya sumatau syāma ||3||

yat te nāma suhavaṃ supraṇīte 'numate anumataṃ sudānu |
tenā no yajñaṃ pipṛhi viśvavāre rayiṃ no dhehi subhage suvīram ||4||

emaṃ yajñam anumatir jagāma sukṣetratāyai suvīratāyai sujātam |
bhadrā hy asyāḥ pramatir babhūva semam yajñam avatu devagopā ||5||

anumatiḥ sarvam idaṃ babhūva yat tiṣṭhati carati yad u ca viśvam ejati |
tasyās te devi sumatau syāmānumate anu hi maṃsase naḥ ||6||



sameta viśve vacasā patiṃ diva eko vibhūr atithir janānām |
sa pūrvyo nūtanam āvivāsat taṃ vartanir anu vāvṛta ekam it puru ||1||

ayaṃ sahasram ā no dṛśe kavīnāṃ matir jyotir vidharmaṇi ||1||

bradhnaḥ samīcīr uṣasaḥ sam airayan |
arepasaḥ sacetasaḥ svasare manyumattamāś cite goḥ ||2||



dauṣvapnyam daurjīvityaṃ rakṣo abhvam arāyyaḥ |
durṇāmnīḥ sarvā durvācas tā asman nāśayāmasi ||1||



yan na indro akhanad yad agnir viśve devā maruto yat svarkāḥ |
tad asmabhyaṃ savitā satyadharmā prajāpatir anumatir ni yachāt ||1||



yayor ojasā skabhitā rajāṃsi yau vīryair vīratamā śaviṣṭhā |
yau patyete apratītau sahobhir viṣṇum agan varuṇaṃ pūrvahūtiḥ ||1||

yasyedaṃ pradiśi yad virocate pra cānati vi ca caṣṭe śacībhiḥ |
purā devasya dharmaṇā sahobhir viṣṇum agan varuṇaṃ pūrvahūtiḥ ||2||



viṣṇor nu kaṃ prā vocaṃ vīryāṇi yaḥ pārthivāni vimame rajāṃsi |
yo askabhāyad uttaraṃ sadhasthaṃ vicakramāṇas tredhorugāyaḥ ||1||

pra tad viṣṇu stavate vīryāṇi mṛgo na bhīmaḥ kucaro giriṣṭhāḥ |
parāvata ā jagamyāt parasyāḥ ||2||

yasyoruṣu triṣu vikramaneṣv adhikṣiyanti bhuvanāni viśvā |
uru viṣṇo vi kramasvoru kṣayāya nas kṛdhi |
ghṛtam ghṛtayone piba prapra yajñapatiṃ tira ||3||

idaṃ viṣṇur vi cakrame tredhā ni dadhe padā |
samūḍham asya paṃsure ||4||

trīṇi padā vi cakrame viṣṇur gopā adābhyaḥ |
ito dharmāṇi dhārayan ||5||

viṣṇoḥ karmāṇi paśyata yato vratāni paspaśe |
indrasya yujyaḥ sakhā ||6||

tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padaṃ sadā paśyanti sūrayaḥ |
divīva cakṣur ātatam ||7||

divo viṣṇa uta pṛthivyā maho viṣṇa uror antarikṣāt |
hastau pṛṇasva bahubhir vasavyair āprayacha dakṣiṇād ota savyāt ||8||


iḍaivāsmāṃ anu vastāṃ vratena yasyāḥ pade punate devayantaḥ |
ghṛtapadī śakvarī somapṛṣṭhopa yajñam asthita vaiśvadevī ||1||


vedaḥ svastir drughaṇaḥ svastiḥ paraśur vediḥ paraśur naḥ svasti |
haviṣkṛto yajñiyā yajñakāmās te devāso yajñam imaṃ juṣantām ||1||



agnāviṣṇū mahi tad vāṃ mahitvam pātho ghṛtasya guhyasya nāma |
damedame sapta ratnā dadhānau prati vāṃ jihvā ghṛtam ā caraṇyāt ||1||

agnāviṣṇū mahi dhāma priyam vāṃ vītho ghṛtasya guhyā juṣāṇau |
damedame suṣṭutyā vāvṛdhānau prati vāṃ jihvā ghṛtam uc caraṇyāt ||2||



svāktaṃ me dyāvāpṛthivī svāktaṃ mitro akar ayam |
svāktaṃ me brahmaṇas patiḥ svāktaṃ savitā karat ||1||


indrotibhir bahulābhir no adya yāvacchreṣṭhābhir maghavan chūra jinva |
yo no dveṣṭy adhara sas padīṣṭa yam u dviṣmas tam u prāṇo jahātu ||1||



upa priyaṃ panipnatam yuvānam āhutīvṛdham |
aganma bibhrato namo dīrgham āyuḥ kṛṇotu me ||1||



saṃ mā siñcantu marutaḥ saṃ pūṣā saṃ bṛhaspatiḥ |
saṃ māyam agniḥ siñcatu prajayā ca dhanena ca dīrgham āyuḥ kṛṇotu me ||1||



agne jātān pra ṇudā me sapatnān praty ajātān jātavedo nudasva |
adhaspadaṃ kṛṇuṣva ye pṛtanyavo 'nāgasas te vayam aditaye syāma ||1||



prānyānt sapatnānt sahasā sahasva praty ajātān jātavedo nudasva |
idaṃ rāṣṭraṃ pipṛhi saubhagāya viśva enam anu madantu devāḥ ||1||

imā yās te śataṃ hirāḥ sahasraṃ dhamanīr uta |
tāsāṃ te sarvāsām aham aśmanā bilam apy adhām ||2||

paraṃ yoner avaraṃ te kṛṇomi mā tvā prajābhi bhūn mota sūtuḥ |
asvaṃ tvāprajasaṃ kṛṇomy aśmānaṃ te apidhānam kṛṇomi ||3||



akṣyau nau madhusaṃkāśe anīkam nau samañjanam |
antaḥ kṛṣṇuṣva māṃ hṛdi mana in nau sahāsati ||1||



abhi tvā manujātena dadhāmi mama vāsasā |
yāthā 'so mama kevalo nānyāsāṃ kīrtayāś cana ||1||


idam khanāmi bheṣajaṃ māṃpaśyam abhirorudam |
parāyato nivartanam āyataḥ pratinandanam ||1||
yenā nicakra āsurīndraṃ devebhyas pari |
tenā ni kurve tvām ahaṃ yathā te 'sāni supriyā ||2||

pratīcī somam asi pratīcī uta sūryam |
pratīcī viśvān devān tāṃ tvāchāvadāmasi ||3||

ahaṃ vadāmi net tvaṃ sabhāyām aha tvaṃ vada |
mamed asas tvaṃ kevalo nānyāsāṃ kīrtayāś cana ||4||
yadi vāsi tirojanaṃ yadi vā nadyas tiraḥi |
iyaṃ ha mahyaṃ tvām oṣadhir baddhveva nyānayat ||5||



divyaṃ suparṇaṃ payasaṃ bṛhantam apāṃ garbhaṃ vṛṣabham oṣadhīnām |
abhīpato vṛṣṭyā tarpayantam ā no goṣṭhe rayiṣṭhāṃ sthāpayāti ||1||


yasya vrataṃ paśavo yanti sarve yasya vrata upatiṣṭhanta āpaḥ |
yasya vrate puṣṭapatir niviṣṭas taṃ sarasvantam avase havāmahe ||1||

ā pratyañcaṃ dāśuṣe dāśvaṃsaṃ sarasvantaṃ puṣṭapatiṃ rayiṣṭhām |
rāyas poṣaṃ śravasyuṃ vasānā iha sadanaṃ rayīṇām ||2||



ati dhanvāny aty apas tatarda śyeno nṛcakṣā avasānadarśaḥ |
taran viśvāny avarā rajaṃsīndreṇa sakhyā śiva ā jagamyāt ||1||

śyeno nṛcakṣā divyaḥ suparṇaḥ sahasrapāc chatayonir vayodhāḥ |
sa no ni yachād vasu yat parābhṛtam asmākam astu pitṛṣu svadhāvat ||2||



somārudrā vi vṛhataṃ viṣūcīm amīvā yā no gayam āviveśa |
bādhethāṃ dūraṃ nirṛtim parācaiḥ kṛtaṃ cid enaḥ pra mumuktam asmat ||1||

somārudrā yuvam etāny asmad viśvā tanūṣu bheṣajāni dhattam |
ava syataṃ muñcataṃ yan no asat tanūṣu baddhaṃ kṛtam eno asmat ||2||



śivās ta ekā aśivās ta ekāḥ sarvā bibharṣi sumanasyamānaḥ |
tisro vāco nihitā antar asmin tāsām ekā vi papātānu ghoṣam ||1||



ubhā jigyathur na parā jayethe na parā jigye kataraś canainayoḥ |
indraś ca viṣṇo yad apaspṛdhethāṃ tredhā sahasraṃ vi tad airayethām ||1||



janād viśvajanīnāt sindhutas pary ābhṛtam |
dūrāt tvā manya udbhṛtam īrṣyāyā nāma bheṣajam ||1||

agner ivāsya dahato dāvasya dahataḥ pṛthak |
etām etasyerṣyām udrāgnim iva śamaya ||1||


sinīvāli pṛthuṣṭuke yā devānām asi svasā |
juṣasva havyam āhutaṃ prajāṃ devi didiḍḍhi naḥ ||1||

yā subāhuḥ svaṅguriḥ suṣūmā bahusūvarī |
tasyai viśpatnyai haviḥ sinīvālyai juhotana ||2||

yā viśpatnīndram asi pratīcī sahasrastukābhiyantī devī |
viṣṇoḥ patni tubhyaṃ rātā havīṃṣi patiṃ devi rādhase codayasva ||3||



kuhūṃ devīṃ sukṛtaṃ vidmanāpasam asmin yajñe suhavā johavīmi |
sā no rayiṃ viśvavāraṃ ni yachād dadātu vīram śatadāyam ukthyam ||1||

kuhūr devānām amṛtasya patnī havyā no asya haviṣo juṣeta |
śṛnotu yajñam uśatī no adya rāyas poṣaṃ cikituṣī dadhātu ||2||



rākām ahaṃ suhavā suṣṭutī huve śṛṇotu naḥ subhagā bodhatu tmanā |
sīvyatv apaḥ sūcyāchidyamānayā dadātu vīraṃ śatadāyam ukthyam ||1||

yās te rāke sumatayaḥ supeśaso yābhir dadāsi dāśuṣe vasūni |
tābhir no adya sumanā upāgahi sahasrāpoṣam subhage rarāṇā ||2||



devānāṃ patnīr uśatīr avantu naḥ prāvantu nas tujaye vājasātaye |
yāḥ pārthivāso yā apām api vrate tā no devīḥ suhavāḥ śarma yachantu ||1||

uta gnā vyantu devapatnīr indrāṇy agnāyy aśvinī rāṭ |
ā rodasī varunānī śṛṇotu vyantu devīr ya ṛtur janīnām ||2||



yathā vṛkṣam aśanir viśvāhā hanty aprati |
evāham adya kitavān akṣair badhyāsam aprati ||1||

turāṇām aturāṇāṃ viśām avarjuṣīṇām |
samaitu viśvato bhago antarhastaṃ kṛtaṃ mama ||2||

īḍe agniṃ svāvasuṃ namobhir iha prasakto vi cayat kṛtaṃ naḥ |
rathair iva pra bhare vājayadbhiḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ marutāṃ stomam ṛdhyām ||3||

vayaṃ jayema tvayā yujā vṛtam asmākam aṃśam ud ava bharebhare |
asmabhyam indra varīyaḥ sugaṃ kṛdhi pra śatrūṇāṃ maghavan vṛṣṇyā ruja ||4||

ajaiṣaṃ tvā saṃlikhitam ajaiṣam uta saṃrudham |
aviṃ vṛko yathā mathad evā mathnāmi te kṛtam ||5||

uta prahām atidīvā jayati kṛtam iva śvaghnī vi cinoti kāle |
yo devakāmo na dhanam ruṇaddhi sam it taṃ rāyaḥ sṛjati svadhābhiḥ ||6||

gobhiṣ ṭaremāmatiṃ durevāṃ yavena vā kṣudhaṃ puruhūta viśve |
vayaṃ rājasu prathamā dhanāny ariṣṭāso vṛjanībhir jayema ||7||

kṛtaṃ me dakṣiṇe haste jayo me savya āhitaḥ |
gojid bhūyāsam aśvajid dhanaṃjayo hiraṇyajit ||8||

akṣāḥ phalavatīm dyuvaṃ datta gāṃ kṣīriṇīm iva |
saṃ mā kṛtasya dhārayā dhanuḥ snāvneva nahyata ||9||



bṛhaspatir naḥ pari pātu paścād utottarasmād adharād aghayoḥ |
indraḥ purastād uta madhyato naḥ sakhā sakhibhyo varīyaḥ kṛṇotu ||1||



saṃjñānaṃ naḥ svebhiḥ saṃjñānam araṇebhiḥ |
saṃjñānam aśvinā yuvam ihāsmāsu ni yachatam ||1||

saṃ jānāmahai manasā saṃ cikitvā mā yuṣmahi manasā daivyena |
mā ghoṣā ut sthur bahule vinirhate meṣuḥ paptad indrasyāhany āgate ||2||



amutrabhūyād adhi yad yamasya bṛhaspate abhiśaster amuñcaḥ |
praty auhatām aśvinā mṛtyum asmad devānām agne bhiṣajā śacībhiḥ ||1||

saṃ krāmataṃ mā jahītaṃ śarīraṃ prāṇāpānau te sayujāv iha stām |
śataṃ jīva śarado vardhamāno 'gniṣ ṭe gopā adhipā vasiṣṭhaḥ ||2||

āyur yat te atihitaṃ parācair apānaḥ prāṇaḥ punar ā tāv itām |
agniṣ ṭad āhār nirṛter upasthāt tad ātmani punar ā veśayāmi te ||3||

memaṃ prāṇo hāsīn mo apāno 'vahāya parā gāt |
saptarṣibhya enaṃ pari dadāmi te enaṃ svasti jarase vahantu ||4||

pra viṣataṃ prāṇāpānāv anaḍvāhāv iva vrajam |
ayaṃ jarimnaḥ śevadhir ariṣṭa iha vardhatām ||5||

ā te prāṇaṃ suvāmasi parā yakṣmaṃ suvāmi te |
āyur no viśvato dadhad ayam agnir vareṇyaḥ ||6||

ud vayaṃ tamasas pari rohanto nākam uttamam |
devaṃ devatrā sūryam aganma jyotir uttamam ||7||



ṛcaṃ sāma yajāmahe yābhyāṃ karmāṇi kurvate |
ete sadasi rājato yajñaṃ deveṣu yachataḥ ||1||

ṛcaṃ sāma yad aprākṣaṃ havir ojo yajur balam |
eṣa mā tasmān mā hiṃsīd vedaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ śacīpate ||1||



ye te panthāno 'va divo yebhir viśvam airayaḥ |
tebhiḥ sumnayā dhehi no vaso ||2||



tiraścirājer asitāt pṛdākoḥ pari saṃbhṛtam |
tat kaṅkaparvaṇo viṣam iyaṃ vīrud anīnaśat ||1||

iyaṃ vīrun madhujātā madhuścun madhulā madhūḥ |
sā vihrutasya bheṣajy atho maśakajambhanī ||2||

yato daṣṭaṃ yato dhītaṃ tatas te nir hvayāmasi |
arbhasya tṛpradaṃśino maśakasyārasaṃ viṣam ||3||

ayaṃ yo vakro viparur vyaṅgo mukhāni vakrā vṛjinā kṛṇoṣi |
tāni tvaṃ brahmaṇas pate iṣīkām iva saṃ namaḥ ||4||

arasasya śarkoṭasya nīcīnasyopasarpataḥ |
viṣaṃ hy asyādiṣy atho enam ajījabham ||5||

na te bāhvor balam asti na śīrṣe nota madhyataḥ |
atha kiṃ pāpayā 'muyā puche bibharṣy arbhakam ||6||

adanti tvā pipīlikā vi vṛścanti mayūryaḥ |
sarve bhala bravātha śārkoṭam arasaṃ viṣam ||7||

ya ubhābhyāṃ praharasi puchena cāsyena ca |
āsye na te viṣaṃ kim u te puchadhāv asat ||8||



yad āśasā vadato me vicukṣubhe yad yācamānasya carato janāṃ anu |
yad ātmani tanvo me viriṣṭaṃ sarasvatī tad ā pṛṇad ghṛtena ||1||

sapta kṣaranti siśave marutvate pitre putrāso apy avīvṛtann ṛtāni |
ubhe id asyobhe asya rājata ubhe yatete ubhe asya puṣyataḥ ||2||



indrāvaruṇā sutapāv imaṃ sutaṃ somaṃ pibataṃ madyaṃ dhṛtavratau |
yuvo ratho adhvaro devavītaye prati svasaram upa yātu pītaye ||1||

indrāvaruṇā madhumattamasya vṛṣṇaḥ somasya vṛṣaṇā vṛṣethām |
idaṃ vām andhaḥ pariṣiktam āsadyāsmin barhiṣi mādayethām ||2||



yo naḥ śapād aśapataḥ śapato yaś ca naḥ śapāt |
vṛkṣa iva vidyutā hata ā mūlād anu śuṣyatu ||1||



ūrjaṃ bibhrad vasuvaniḥ sumedhā aghoreṇa cakṣuṣā mitriyeṇa |
gṛhān aimi sumanā vandamāno ramadhvam mā bibhīta mat ||1||

ime gṛhā mayobhuva ūrjasvantaḥ payasvantaḥ |
pūrṇā vāmena tiṣṭhantas te no jānantv āyataḥ ||2||

yeṣām adhyeti pravasan yeṣu saumanaso bahuḥ |
gṛhān upa hvayāmahe te no jānantv āyataḥ ||3||

upahūtā bhūridhanāḥ sakhāyaḥ svādusaṃmudaḥ |
akṣudhyā atṛṣyā sta gṛhā māsmad bibhītana ||4||

upahūtā iha gāva upahūtā ajāvayaḥ |
atho annasya kīlāla upahūto gṛheṣu ||5||

sūnṛtāvantaḥ subhagā irāvanto hasāmudāḥ |
atṛṣyā akṣudhyā sta gṛhā māsmad bibhītana ||6||

ihaiva sta mānu gāta viśvā rūpāṇi puṣyata |
aiṣyāmi bhadreṇā saha bhūyāṃso bhavatā mayā ||7||



yad agne tapasā tapa upatapyāmahe tapaḥ |
priyāḥ śrutasya bhūyāsmāyuṣmantaḥ sumedhasaḥ ||1||

agne tapas tapyāmaha upa tapyāmahe tapaḥ |
śrutāni śṛṇvantaḥ vayam āyuṣmantaḥ sumedhasaḥ ||2||


ayam agniḥ satpatir vṛddhavṛṣṇo rathīva pattīn ajayat purohitaḥ |
nābhā pṛthivyāṃ nihito davidyutad adhaspadaṃ kṛṇutāṃ ye pṛtanyavaḥ ||1||



pṛtanājitaṃ sahamānam agnim ukthyair havāmahe paramāt sadhasthāt |
sa naḥ parṣad ati durgāṇi viśvā kṣāmad devo 'ti duritāny agniḥ ||1||



idaṃ yat kṛṣṇaḥ śakunir abhiniṣpatann apīpatat |
āpo mā tasmāt sarvasmād duritāt pāntv aṃhasaḥ ||1||

idaṃ yat kṛṣṇaḥ śakunir avāmṛkṣan nirṛte te mukhena |
agnir mā tasmād enaso gārhapatyaḥ pra muñcatu ||2||


pratīcīnaphalo hi tvam apāmārga rurohitha |
sarvān mac chapathām adhi varīyo yavayā itaḥ ||1||

yad duṣkṛtaṃ yac chamalaṃ yad vā cerima pāpayā |
tvayā tad viśvatomukhāpāmārgāpa mṛjmahe ||2||

śyāvadatā kunakhinā baṇḍena yat sahāsima |
apāmārga tvayā vayaṃ sarvaṃ tad apa mṛjmahe ||3||


yady antarikṣe yadi vāta āsa yadi vṛkṣeṣu yadi volapeṣu |
yad aśravan paśava udyamānaṃ tad brāhmaṇaṃ punar asmān upaitu ||1||



punar maitv indriyaṃ punar ātmā draviṇaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ ca |
punar agnayo dhiṣṇyā yathāsthāma kalpayantām ihaiva ||1||


sarasvati vrateṣu te divyeṣu devi dhāmasu |
juṣasva havyam āhutaṃ prajām devi rarāsva naḥ ||1||

idaṃ te havyaṃ ghṛtavat sarasvatīdaṃ pitṝṇāṃ havir āsyaṃ yat |
imāni ta uditā śamtamāni tebhir vayaṃ madhumantaḥ syāma ||2||

śivā naḥ śaṃtamā bhava sumṛḍīkā sarasvati |
mā te yuyoma saṃdṛśaḥ ||1||



śaṃ no vāto vātu śaṃ nas tapatu sūryaḥ |
ahāni śaṃ bhavantu naḥ śaṃ rātrī prati dhīyatāṃ |
śaṃ uṣā no vy uchatu ||1||


yat kiṃ cāsau manasā yac ca vācā yajñair juhoti haviṣā yajuṣā |
tan mṛtyunā nirṛtiḥ saṃvidānā purā satyād āhutiṃ hantv asya ||1||

yātudhānā nirṛtir ād u rakṣas te asya ghnantv anṛtena satyam |
indreṣitā devā ājam asya mathnantu mā tat saṃ pādi yad asau juhoti ||2||

ajirādhirājau śyenau saṃpātināv iva |
ājyaṃ pṛtanyato hatāṃ yo naḥ kaścābhyaghāyati ||3||

apāñcau ta ubhau bāhū api nahyāmy āsyam |
agner devasya manyunā tena te 'vadhiṣaṃ haviḥ ||4||
api nahyāmi te bāhū api nahyāmy āsyam |
agner ghorasya manyunā tena 'vadhiṣaṃ haviḥ ||5||



pari tvāgne puraṃ vayaṃ vipraṃ sahasya dhīmahi |
dhṛṣadvarṇaṃ divedive hantāraṃ bhaṅgurāvataḥ ||1||



ut tiṣṭhatāva paśyatendrasya bhāgam ṛtviyam |
yadi śrātam juhotana yady aśrātaṃ mamattana ||1||

śrātam havir o ṣv indra pra yāhi jagāma sūro adhvano vi madhyam |
pari tvāsate nidhibhiḥ sakhāyaḥ kulapā na vrājapatim carantam ||2||

śrātaṃ manya ūdhani śrātam agnau suśṛtaṃ manye tad ṛtaṃ navīyaḥ |
mādhyandinasya savanasya dadhnaḥ pibendra vajrin purukṛj juṣāṇaḥ ||1||


samiddho agnir vṛṣaṇā rathī divas tapto gharmo duhyate vām iṣe madhu |
vayaṃ hi vāṃ purudamāso aśvinā havāmahe sadhamādeṣu kāravaḥ ||1||

samiddho agnir aśvinā tapto vāṃ gharma ā gatam |
duhyante nūnaṃ vṛṣaṇeha dhenavo dasrā madanti vedhasaḥ ||2||

ivāhākṛtaḥ śucir deveṣu yajño yo aśvinoś camaso devapānaḥ |
tam u viśve amṛtāso juṣāṇā gandharvasya praty āsnā rihanti ||3||

yad usriyāsv āhutaṃ ghṛtaṃ payo 'yaṃ sa vām aśvinā bhāga ā gatam |
mādhvī dhartārā vidathasya satpatī taptaṃ gharmaṃ pibatam divaḥ ||4||

tapto vāṃ gharmo nakṣatu svahotā pra vām adhvaryuś caratu payasvān |
madhor dugdhasyāśvinā tanāyā vītaṃ pātaṃ payasa usriyāyāḥ ||5||

upa drava payasā godhug oṣam ā gharme siñca paya usriyāyāḥ |
vi nākam akhyat savitā vareṇyo 'nuprayāṇam uṣaso vi rājati ||6||

upa hvaye sudughāṃ dhenum etāṃ suhasto godhug uta dohad enām |
śreṣṭhaṃ savaṃ savitā sāviṣan no 'bhīddho gharmas tad u ṣu pra vocat ||7||

hiṅkṛṇvatī vasupatnī vasūnāṃ vatsam ichantī manasā nyāgan |
duhām aśvibhyāṃ payo aghnyeyaṃ sā vardhatāṃ mahate saubhagāya ||8||

juṣṭo damūnā atithir duroṇa imaṃ no yajñam upa yāhi vidvān |
viśvā agne abhiyujo vihatya śatrūyatām ā bharā bhojanāni ||9||

7,73.10a agne śardha mahate saubhagāya tava dyumnāny uttamāni santu |
7,73.10c saṃ jāspatyaṃ suyamam ā kṛṇuṣva śatrūyatām abhi tiṣṭhā mahāṃsi ||10||

7,73.11a sūyavasād bhagavatī hi bhūyā adhā vayaṃ bhagavantaḥ syāma |
7,73.11c addhi tṛṇam aghnye viśvadānīṃ piba śuddham udakam ācarantī ||11||



apacitāṃ lohinīnāṃ kṛṣṇā māteti śuśruma |
muner devasya mūlena sarvā vidhyāmi tā aham ||1||

vidhyāmy āsāṃ prathamāṃ vidhyāmi uta madhyamām |
idaṃ jaghanyām āsām ā chinadmi stukām iva ||2||

tvāṣṭreṇāhaṃ vacasā vi ta īrṣyām amīmadam |
atho yo manyuṣ ṭe pate tam u te śamayāmasi ||3||

vratena tvaṃ vratapate samakto viśvāhā sumanā dīdihīha |
taṃ tvā vayaṃ jātavedaḥ samiddhaṃ prajāvanta upa sadema sarve ||4||



prajāvatīḥ sūyavase ruśantīḥ śuddhā apaḥ suprapāṇe pibantīḥ |
mā va stena īśata māghaśaṃsaḥ pari vo rudrasya hetir vṛṇaktu ||1||

padajñā stha ramatayaḥ saṃhitā viśvanāmnīḥ |
upa mā devīr devebhir eta |
imaṃ goṣṭham idaṃ sado ghṛtenāsmānt sam ukṣata ||2||



ā susrasaḥ susraso asatībhyo asattarāḥ |
sehor arasatarā havaṇād vikledīyasīḥ ||1||

yā graivyā apacito 'tho yā upapakṣyāḥ |
vijāmni yā apacitaḥ svayaṃsrasaḥ ||2||

yaḥ kīkasāḥ praśṛṇāti talīdyam avatiṣṭhati |
nir hās taṃ sarvaṃ jāyānyam yaḥ kaś ca kakudi śritaḥ ||3||

pakṣī jāyānyaḥ patati sa ā viśati pūruṣam |
tad akṣitasya bheṣajam ubhayoḥ sukṣatasya ca ||4||

vidma vai te jāyānya jānaṃ yato jāyānya jāyase |
kathaṃ ha tatra tvam hano yasya kṛṇmo havir gṛhe ||1||

dhṛṣat piba kalaśe somam indra vṛtrahā śūra samare vasūnām |
mādhyandine savana ā vṛṣasva rayiṣṭhāno rayim asmāsu dhehi ||2||



sāṃtapanā idaṃ havir marutas taj jujuṣṭana |
asmākotī riśādasaḥ ||1||

yo no marto maruto durhṛṇāyus tiraś cittāni vasavo jighāṃsati |
druhaḥ pāśān prati muñcatāṃ sas tapiṣṭhena tapasā hantanā tam ||2||

samvatsarīṇā marutaḥ svarkā urukṣayāḥ sagaṇā mānuṣāsaḥ |
te asmat pāśān pra muñcantv enasas sāṃtapanā matsarā mādayiṣṇavaḥ ||3||



vi te muñcāmi raśanāṃ vi yoktraṃ vi niyojanam |
ihaiva tvam ajasra edhy agne ||1||

asmai kṣatrāṇi dhārayantam agne yunajmi tvā brahmaṇā daivyena |
dīdihy asmabhyaṃ draviṇeha bhadraṃ premaṃ voco havirdām devatāsu ||2||



yat te devā akṛṇvan bhāgadheyam amāvāsye saṃvasanto mahitvā |
tenā no yajñaṃ pipṛhi viśvavāre rayiṃ no dhehi subhage suvīram ||1||

aham evāsmy amāvāsyā mām ā vasanti sukṛto mayīme |
mayi devā ubhaye sādyāś cendrajyeṣṭhāḥ sam agachanta sarve ||2||

āgan rātrī saṅgamanī vasūnām ūrjaṃ puṣṭaṃ vasv āveśayantī |
amāvāsyāyai haviṣa vidhemorjaṃ duhānā payasā na āgan ||3||

amāvāsye na tvad etāny anyo viśvā rūpāṇi paribhūr jajāna |
yatkāmās te juhumas tan no astu vayaṃ syāma patayo rayiṇām ||4||



paurṇamāsī jigāya |
tasyāṃ devaiḥ saṃvasanto mahitvā nākasya pṛṣṭhe sam iṣā madema ||1||

vṛṣabhaṃ vājinaṃ vayaṃ paurṇamāsaṃ yajāmahe |
sa no dadātv akṣitāṃ rayim anupadasvatīm ||2||

prajāpate na tvad etāny anyo viśvā rūpāṇi paribhūr jajāna |
yatkāmās te juhumas tan no astu vayaṃ syāma patayo rayīṇām ||3||

paurṇamāsī prathamā yajñiyāsīd ahnāṃ rātrīṇām atiśarvareṣu |
ye tvām yajñair yajñiye ardhayanty amī te nāke sukṛtaḥ praviṣṭāḥ ||4||



pūrvāparaṃ carato mayayaitau śiśū krīḍantau pari yāto 'rṇavam |
viśvānyo bhuvanā vicaṣṭa ṛtūṃr anyo vidadhaj jāyase navaḥ ||1||

navonavo bhavasi jāyamāno 'hnāṃ ketur uṣasām eṣy agram |
bhāgaṃ devebhyo vi dadhāsy āyan pra candramas tirase dhīrgham āyuḥ ||2||

somasyāmśo yudhāṃ pate 'nūno nāma vā asi |
anūnam darśa mā kṛdhi prajayā ca dhanena ca ||3||

darśo 'si darśato 'si samagro 'si samantaḥ |
samagraḥ samanto bhūyāsaṃ gobhir aśvaiḥ prajayā paśubhir gṛhair dhanena ||4||

yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmas tasya tvaṃ prāṇenā pyāyasva |
ā vayaṃ pyāsiṣīmahi gobhir aśvaiḥ prajayā paśubhir gṛhair dhanena ||5||

yaṃ devā aṃśum āpyāyayanti yam akṣitam akṣitā bhakṣayanti |
tenāsmān indro varuṇo bṛhaspatir ā pyāyayantu bhuvanasya gopāḥ ||6||



abhy arcata suṣṭutiṃ gavyam ājim asmāsu bhadrā draviṇāni dhatta |
imaṃ yajñaṃ nayata devatā no ghṛtasya dhārā madhumat pavantām ||1||

mayy agre agniṃ gṛhṇāmi saha kṣatreṇa varcasā balena |
mayi prajāṃ mayy āyur dadhāmi svāhā mayy agnim ||2||

ihaivāgne adhy dhārayā rayim mā tvā ni kran pūrvacittā nikāriṇaḥ |
kṣatreṇāgne suyamam astu tubhyam upasattā vardhatāṃ te aniṣṭṛtaḥ ||3||

anv agnir uṣasām agram akhyad anv ahāni prathamo jātavedāḥ |
anu sūrya uṣaso anu raśmīn anu dyāvāpṛthivī ā viveśa ||4||

praty agnir uṣasām agram akhyat prati ahāni prathamo jātavedāḥ |
prati sūryasya purudhā ca raśmīn prati dyāvāpṛthivī ā tatāna ||5||

ghṛtaṃ te agne divye sadhasthe ghṛtena tvāṃ manur adyā sam indhe |
ghṛtaṃ te devīr naptya ā vahantu ghṛtaṃ tubhyaṃ duhratāṃ gāvo agne ||6||



apsu te rājan varuṇa gṛho hiraṇyayo mitaḥ |
tato dhṛtavrato rājā sarvā dhāmāni muñcatu ||1||

dāmnodāmno rājann ito varuṇa muñca naḥ |
yad āpo aghnyā iti varuṇeti yad ūcima tato varuṇa muñca naḥ ||2||

ud uttamaṃ varuṇa pāśam asmad avādhamaṃ vi madhyamaṃ śrathāya |
adhā vayam āditya vrate tavānāgaso aditaye syāma ||3||

prāsmat pāśān varuṇa muñca sarvān ya uttamā adhamā vāruṇā ye |
duṣvapnyaṃ duritaṃ ni ṣvāsmad atha gachema sukṛtasya lokam ||4||



anādhṛṣyo jātavedā amartyo virāḍ agne kṣatrabhṛd dīdihīha |
viśvā amīvāḥ pramuñcan mānuṣībhiḥ śivābhir adya pari pāhi no gayam ||1||

indra kṣatram abhi vāmam ojo 'jāyathā vṛṣabha carṣaṇīnām |
apānudo janam amitrayantam uruṃ devebhyo akṛṇor u lokam ||2||

mṛgo na bhīmaḥ kucaro giriṣṭhāḥ parāvata ā jagamyāt parasyāḥ |
sṛkaṃ saṃśāya pavim indra tigmaṃ vi śatrūn tāḍhi vi mṛdho nudasva ||3||



tyam ū ṣu vājinaṃ devajūtaṃ sahovānaṃ tarutāraṃ rathānām |
ariṣṭanemiṃ pṛtanājim āśuṃ svastaye tārkṣyam ihā huvema ||1||



trātāram indram avitāram indraṃ havehave suhavaṃ śūram indram |
huve nu śakraṃ puruhūtam indraṃ svasti na indro maghavān kṛṇotu ||1||


yo agnau rudro yo apsv antar ya oṣadhīr vīrudha āviveśa |
ya imāviśvā bhuvanāni cākḷpe tasmai rudrāya namo astv agnaye ||1||



apehy arir asy arir vā asi viṣe viṣam apṛkthā viṣam id vā apṛkthāḥ |
ahim evābhyapehi taṃ jahi ||1||


apo divyā acāyiṣam rasena sam apṛkṣmahi |
payasvān agna āgamaṃ tam mā saṃ sṛja varcasā ||1||

saṃ māgne varcasā sṛja saṃ prajayā sam āyuṣā |
vidyur me asya devā indro vidyāt saha ṛṣibhiḥ ||2||

idam āpaḥ pra vahatāvadyaṃ ca malaṃ ca yat |
yac cābhidudrohānṛtaṃ yac ca śepe abhīruṇam ||3||

edho 'sy edhiṣīya samid asi sam edhiṣīya |
tejo 'si tejo mayi dhehi ||4||



api vṛśca purāṇavad vratater iva guṣpitam |
ojo dāsasya dambhaya ||1||

vayaṃ tad asya sambhṛtaṃ vasv indrena vi bhajāmahai |
mlāpayāmi bhrajaḥ śibhraṃ varuṇasya vratena te ||2||

yathā śepo apāyātai strīṣu cāsad anāvayāḥ |
avasthasya knadīvataḥ śāṅkurasya nitodinaḥ |
yad ātatam ava tat tanu yad uttataṃ ni tat tanu ||3||



indraḥ sutrāmā svavāṃ avobhiḥ sumṛḍīko bhavatu viśvavedāḥ |
bādhatāṃ dveṣo abhayaṃ naḥ kṛṇotu suvīryasya patayaḥ syāma ||1||



sa sutrāmā svavāṃ indro asmad ārāc cid dveṣaḥ sanutar yuyotu |
tasya vayaṃ sumatau yajñiyasyāpi bhadre saumanase syāma ||1||



indreṇa manyunā vayam abhi ṣyāma pṛtanyataḥ |
ghnanto vṛtrāṇy aprati ||1||



dhruvaṃ dhruveṇa haviṣāva somaṃ nayāmasi |
yathā na indraḥ kevalīr viśaḥ saṃmanasas karat ||1||



ud asya śyāvau vithurau gṛdhrau dyām iva petatuḥ |
ucchocanapraśocanav asyocchocanau hṛdaḥ ||1||

aham enāv ud atiṣṭhipaṃ gāvau śrāntasadāv iva |
kurkurāv iva kūjantāv udavantau vṛkāv iva ||2||

ātodinau nitodināv atho saṃtodināv uta |
api nahyāmy asya meḍhraṃ ya itaḥ strī pumān jabhāra ||3||



asadan gāvaḥ sadane 'paptad vasatiṃ vayaḥ |
āsthāne parvatā asthuḥ sthāmni vṛkkāv atiṣṭhipam ||1||



yad adya tvā prayati yajñe asmin hotaś cikitvann avṛṇīmahīha |
dhruvam ayo dhruvam utā śaviṣṭhaipravidvān yajñam upa yāhi somam ||1||

sam indra no manasā neṣa gobhiḥ saṃ sūribhir harivant saṃ svastyā |
saṃ brahmaṇā devahitaṃ yad asti saṃ devānāṃ sumatau yajñiyānām ||2||

yān āvaha uśato deva devāṃs tān preraya sve agne sadhasthe |
jakṣivāṃsaḥ papivāṃso madhūny asmai dhatta vasavo vasūni ||3||

sugā vo devāḥ sadanā akarma ya ājagma savane mā juṣāṇāḥ |
vahamānā bharamāṇāḥ svā vasūni vasuṃ gharmaṃ divam ā rohatānu ||4||

yajña yajñaṃ gacha yajñapatiṃ gacha |
svāṃ yoniṃ gacha svāhā ||5||

eṣa te yajño yajñapate sahasūktavākaḥ |
suvīryaḥ svāhā ||6||

vaṣaḍ dhutebhyo vaṣaḍ ahutebhyaḥ |
devā gātuvido gātuṃ vittvā gātum ita ||7||



manasas pata imaṃ no divi deveṣu yajñam |
svāhā divi svāhā pṛthivyāṃ svāhāntarikṣe svāhā vāte dhāṃ svāhā ||8||



saṃ barhir aktaṃ haviṣā ghṛtena sam indreṇa vasunā saṃ marudbhiḥ |
saṃ devair viśvadevebhir aktam indraṃ gachatu haviḥ svāhā ||1||



pari stṛṇīhi pari dhehi vediṃ mā jāmiṃ moṣīr amuyā śayānām |
hotṛṣadanam haritaṃ hiraṇyayaṃ niṣkā ete yajamānasya loke ||1||



7,100.1a paryāvarte duṣvapnyāt pāpāt svapnyād abhūtyāḥ |
7,100.1c brahmāham antaraṃ kṛṇve parā svapnamukhāḥ śucaḥ ||1||



7,101.1a yat svapne annam aśnāmi na prātar adhigamyate |
7,101.1c sarvaṃ tad astu me śivaṃ nahi tad dṛṣyate divā ||1||



7,102.1a namaskṛtya dyāvāpṛthivībhyām antarikṣāya mṛtyave |
7,102.1c mekṣāmy ūrdhvas tiṣṭhan mā mā hiṃsiṣur īśvarāḥ ||1||



7,103.1a ko asyā no druho 'vadyavatyā un neṣyati kṣatriyo vasya ichan |
7,103.1c ko yajñakāmaḥ ka u pūrtikāmaḥ ko deveṣu vanute dīrgham āyuḥ ||1||



7,104.1a kaḥ pṛśniṃ dhenuṃ varuṇena dattām atharvane sudughāṃ nityavatsām |
7,104.1c bṛhaspatinā sakhyaṃ juṣaṇo yathāvaśaṃ tanvaḥ kalpayāti ||1||



7,105.1a apakrāman pauruṣeyād vṛṇāno daivyaṃ vacaḥ |
7,105.1c praṇītīr abhyāvartasva viśvebhiḥ sakhibhiḥ saha ||1||



7,106.1a yad asmṛti cakṛma kiṃ cid agna upārima caraṇe jātavedaḥ |
7,106.1c tataḥ pāhi tvaṃ naḥ pracetaḥ śubhe sakhibhyo amṛtatvam astu naḥ ||1||



7,107.1a ava divas tārayanti sapta sūryasya raśmayaḥ |
7,107.1c āpaḥ samudriyā dhārās tās śalyam asisrasan ||1||



7,108.1a yo na stāyad dipsati yo na āviḥ svo vidvān araṇo vā no agne |
7,108.1c pratīcy etv araṇī datvatī tān maiṣām agne vāstu bhūn mo apatyam ||1||

7,108.2a yo naḥ suptān jāgrato vābhidāsāt tiṣṭhato vā carato jātavedaḥ |
7,108.2c vaiśvānareṇa sayujā sajoṣās tān pratīco nir daha jātavedaḥ ||2||



7,109.1a idam ugrāya babhrave namo yo akṣeṣu tanūvaśī |
7,109.1c ghṛtena kaliṃ śikṣāmi sa no mṛḍātīdṛśe ||1||

7,109.2a ghṛtam apsarābhyo vaha tvam agne pāṃsūn akṣebhyaḥ sikatā apaś ca |
7,109.2c yathābhagaṃ havyadātiṃ juṣāṇā madanti devā ubhayāni havyā ||2||

7,109.3a apsarasaḥ sadhamādaṃ madanti havirdhānam antarā sūryaṃ ca |
7,109.3c tā me hastau saṃ sṛjantu ghṛtena sapatnaṃ me kitavam randhayantu ||3||

7,109.4a ādinavaṃ pratidīvne ghṛtenāsmāṃ abhi kṣara |
7,109.4c vṛkṣam ivāśanyā jahi yo asmān pratidīvyati ||4||

7,109.5a yo no dyuve dhanam idaṃ cakāra yo akṣāṇāṃ glahanaṃ śeṣaṇaṃ ca |
7,109.5c sa no devo havir idaṃ juṣāṇo gandharvebhiḥ sadhamādaṃ madema ||5||

7,109.6a saṃvasava iti vo nāmadheyam ugraṃpaśyā rāṣṭrabhṛto hy akṣāḥ |
7,109.6c tebhyo va indavo haviṣā vidhema vayaṃ syāma patayo rayīṇām ||6||

7,109.7a devān yan nāthito huve brahmacaryaṃ yad ūṣima |
7,109.7c akṣān yad babhrūn ālabhe te no mṛḍantv īdṛśe ||7||


7,110.1a agna indraś ca dāśuṣe hato vṛtrāṇy aprati |
7,110.1c ubhā hi vṛtrahantamā ||1||

7,110.2a yābhyām ajayant svar agra eva yāv ātasthatur bhuvanāni viśvā |
7,110.2c pra carṣaṇīvṛṣaṇā vajrabāhū agnim indram vṛtrahaṇā huve 'ham ||2||

7,110.3a upa tvā devo agramīc camasena bṛhaspatiḥ |
7,110.3c indra gīrbhir na ā viśa yajamānāya sunvate ||3||



7,111.1a indrasya kukṣir asi somadhāna ātmā devānām uta mānuṣāṇām |
7,111.1c iha prajā janaya yās ta āsu yā anyatreha tās te ramantām ||1||



7,112.1a śumbhanī dyāvāpṛthivī antisumne mahivrate |
7,112.1c āpaḥ sapta susruvur devīs tā no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ||1||

7,112.2a muñcantu mā śapathyād atho varuṇyād uta |
7,112.2c atho yamasya paḍvīśād viśvasmād devakilbiṣāt ||2||


7,113.1a tṛṣṭike tṛṣṭavandana ud amūṃ chindhi tṛṣṭike |
7,113.1c yathā kṛtadviṣṭāso 'muṣmai śepyāvate ||1||

7,113.2a tṛṣṭāsi tṛṣṭikā viṣā viṣātaky asi |
7,113.2c parivṛktā yathāsasy ṛṣabhasya vaśeva ||2||



7,114.1a ā te dade vakṣaṇābhya ā te 'haṃ hṛdayād dade |
7,114.1c ā te mukhasya saṅkāśāt sarvaṃ te varca ā dade ||1||

7,114.2a preto yantu vyādhyaḥ prānudhyāḥ pro aśastayaḥ |
7,114.2c agnī rakṣasvinīr hantu somo hantu durasyatīḥ ||2||



7,115.1a pra patetaḥ pāpi lakṣmi naśyetaḥ prāmutaḥ pata |
7,115.1c ayasmayenāṅkena dviṣate tvā sajāmasi ||1||

7,115.2a yā mā lakṣmīḥ patayālūr ajuṣṭābhicaskanda vandaneva vṛkṣam |
7,115.2c anyatrāsmat savitas tām ito dhā hiraṇyahasto vasu no rarāṇaḥ ||2||

7,115.3a ekaśataṃ lakṣmyo martyasya sākaṃ tanvā januṣo 'dhi jātāḥ |
7,115.3c tāsāṃ pāpiṣṭhā nir itaḥ pra hiṇmaḥ śivā asmabhyaṃ jātavedo niyacha ||3||

7,115.4a etā enā vyākaraṃ khile gā viṣṭhitā iva |
7,115.4c ramantāṃ puṇyā lakṣmīr yāḥ pāpīs tā anīnaśam ||4||



7,116.1a namo rūrāya cyavanāya nodanāya dhṛṣṇave |
7,116.1c namaḥ śītāya pūrvakāmakṛtvane ||1||

7,116.2a yo anyedyur ubhayadyur abhyetīmaṃ maṇḍūkam |
7,116.2c abhy etv avrataḥ ||2||



7,117.1a ā mandrair indra haribhir yāhi mayūraromabhiḥ |
7,117.1c mā tvā ke cid vi yaman viṃ na pāśino 'ti dhanveva tāṃ ihi ||1||

7,118.1a marmāṇi te varmaṇā chādayāmi somas tvā rājāmṛtenānu vastām |
7,118.1c uror varīyo varuṇas te kṛṇotu jayantaṃ tvānu devā madantu ||1||



antakāya mṛtyave namaḥ prānā apānā iha te ramantām |
ihāyam astu puruṣaḥ sahāsunā sūryasya bhāge amṛtasya loke ||1||

ud enaṃ bhago agrabhīd ud enaṃ somo aṃśumān |
ud enaṃ maruto devā ud indrāgnī svastaye ||2||

iha te 'sur iha prāṇa ihāyur iha te manaḥ |
ut tvā nirṛtyāḥ pāśebhyo daivyā vacā bharāmasi ||3||

ut krāmātaḥ puruṣa māva patthā mṛtyoḥ paḍvīṣam avamuñcamānaḥ |
mā chitthā asmāl lokād agneḥ sūryasya saṃdṛśaḥ ||4||

tubhyaṃ vātaḥ pavatāṃ mātariśvā tubhyaṃ varṣantv amṛtāny āpaḥ |
sūryas te tanve śaṃ tapāti tvām mṛtyur dayatāṃ mā pra meṣṭhāḥ ||5||

udyānaṃ te puruṣa nāvayānaṃ jīvātuṃ te dakṣatātiṃ kṛnomi |
ā hi rohemam amṛtaṃ sukhaṃ ratham atha jirvir vidatham ā vadāsi ||6||

mā te manas tatra gān mā tiro bhūn mā jīvebhyaḥ pra mado mānu gāḥ pitṝn |
viśve devā abhi rakṣantu tveha ||7||

mā gatānām ā dīdhīthā ye nayanti parāvatam |
ā roha tamaso jyotir ehy ā te hastau rabhāmahe ||8||

śyāmaś ca tvā mā śabalaś ca preṣitau yamasya yau pathirakṣī śvānau |
arvāṅ ehi mā vi dīdhyo mātra tiṣṭhaḥ parāṅmanāḥ ||9||
8,1.10a maitaṃ panthām anu gā bhīma eṣa yena pūrvaṃ neyatha taṃ bravīmi |
8,1.10c tama etat puruṣa mā pra patthā bhayaṃ parastād abhayaṃ te arvāk ||10|| {1}

8,1.11a rakṣantu tvāgnayo ye apsv antā rakṣatu tvā manuṣyā yam indhate |
8,1.11c vaiśvānaro rakṣatu jātavedā divyas tvā mā pra dhāg vidyutā saha ||11||

8,1.12a mā tvā kravyād abhi maṃstārāt saṃkasukāc cara rakṣatu tvā dyau rakṣatu |
8,1.12c pṛthivī sūryaś ca tvā rakṣatāṃ candramāś ca |
8,1.12e antarikṣaṃ rakṣatu devahetyāḥ ||12||

8,1.13a bodhaś ca tvā pratibodhaś ca rakṣatām asvapnaś ca tvānavadrāṇaś ca rakṣatām |
8,1.13c gopāyaṃś ca tvā jāgṛviś ca rakṣatām ||13||

8,1.14a te tvā rakṣantu te tvā gopāyantu tebhyo namas tebhyaḥ svāhā ||14||

8,1.15a jīvebhyas tvā samude vāyur indro dhātā dadhātu savitā trāyamāṇaḥ |
8,1.15c mā tvā prāṇo balaṃ hāsīd asuṃ te 'nu hvayāmasi ||15||

8,1.16a mā tvā jambhaḥ saṃhanur mā tamo vidan mā jihvā barhis pramayuḥ kathā syāḥ |
8,1.16c ut tvādityā vasavo bharantūd indrāgnī svastaye ||16||

8,1.17a ut tvā dyaur ut pṛthivy ut prajāpatir agrabhīt |
8,1.17c ut tvā mṛtyor oṣadhayaḥ somarājñīr apīparan ||17||

8,1.18a ayaṃ devā ihaivāstv ayaṃ māmutra gād itaḥ |
8,1.18c imaṃ sahasravīryeṇa mṛtyor ut pārayāmasi ||18||

8,1.19a ut tvā mṛtyor apīparaṃ saṃ dhamantu vayodhasaḥ |
8,1.19c mā tvā vyastakeśyo mā tvāgharudo rudan ||19||

8,1.20a āhārṣam avidaṃ tvā punar āgāḥ punarṇavaḥ |
8,1.20c sarvāṅga sarvaṃ te cakṣuḥ sarvam āyuś ca te 'vidam ||20||

8,1.21a vy avāt te jyotir abhūd apa tvat tamo akramīt |
8,1.21c apa tvan mṛtyuṃ nirṛtim apa yakṣmaṃ ni dadhmasi ||21|| {2}



ā rabhasvemām amṛtasya śnuṣṭim achidyamānā jaradaṣṭir astu te |
asuṃ ta āyuḥ punar ā bharāmi rajas tamo mopa gā mā pra meṣṭhāḥ ||1||

jīvatāṃ jyotir abhyehy arvāṅ ā tvā harāmi śataśāradāya |
avamuñcan mṛtyupāśān aśastiṃ drāghīya āyuḥ prataraṃ te dadhāmi ||2||

vātāt te prānam avidaṃ sūryāc cakṣur ahaṃ tava |
yat te manas tvayi tad dhārayāmi saṃ vitsvāṅgair vada jihvayālapan ||3||

prāṇena tvā dvipadāṃ catuṣpadām agnim iva jātam abhi saṃ dhamāmi |
namas te mṛtyo cakṣuṣe namaḥ prāṇāya te 'karam ||4||

ayaṃ jīvatu mā mṛtemaṃ sam īrayāmasi |
kṛṇomy asmai bheṣajaṃ mṛtyo mā puruṣaṃ vadhīḥ ||5||

jīvalāṃ naghāriṣāṃ jīvantīm oṣadhīm aham |
trāyamāṇāṃ sahamānāṃ sahasvatīm iha huve 'smā ariṣṭatātaye ||6||

adhi brūhi mā rabhathāḥ sṛjemaṃ tavaiva sant sarvahāyāḥ ihāstu |
bhavāśarvau mṛḍataṃ śarma yachatam apasidhya duritaṃ dhattam āyuḥ ||7||

asmai mṛtyo adhi brūhīmaṃ dayasvod ito 'yam etu |
ariṣṭaḥ sarvāṅgaḥ suśruj jarasā śatahāyana ātmanā bhujam aśnutām ||8||

devānāṃ hetiḥ pari tvā vṛṇaktu pārayāmi tvā rajasa ut tvā mṛtyor apīparam |
ārād agniṃ kravyādaṃ nirūhaṃ jīvātave te paridhiṃ dadhāmi ||9||

8,2.10a yat te niyānaṃ rajasaṃ mṛtyo anavadharṣyam |
8,2.10c patha imaṃ tasmād rakṣanto brahmāsmai varma kṛṇmasi ||10|| {3}

8,2.11a kṛṇomi te prāṇāpānau jarāṃ mṛtyuṃ dīrgham āyuḥ svasti |
8,2.11c vaivasvatena prahitān yamadūtāṃś carato 'pa sedhāmi sarvān ||11||

8,2.12a ārād arātiṃ nirṛtiṃ paro grāhiṃ kravyādaḥ piśācān |
8,2.12c rakṣo yat sarvaṃ durbhūtaṃ tat tama ivāpa hanmasi ||12||

8,2.13a agneṣ ṭa prānam amṛtād āyuṣmato vanve jātavedasaḥ |
8,2.13c yathā na riṣyā amṛtaḥ sajūr asas tat te kṛṇomi tad u te sam ṛdhyatām ||13||

8,2.14a śive te stāṃ dyāvāpṛthivī asaṃtāpe abhiśriyau |
8,2.14c śaṃ te sūrya ā tapatu śaṃ vāto vātu te hṛde |
8,2.14e śivā abhi kṣarantu tvāpo divyāḥ payasvatīḥ ||14||

8,2.15a śivās te santv oṣadhaya ut tvāhārṣam adharasyā uttarāṃ pṛthivīm abhi |
8,2.15c tatra tvādityau rakṣatāṃ sūryācandramasāv ubhā ||15||

8,2.16a yat te vāsaḥ paridhānaṃ yāṃ nīviṃ kṛṇuṣe tvam |
8,2.16c śivaṃ te tanve tat kṛṇmaḥ saṃsparśe 'drūkṣṇam astu te ||16||

8,2.17a yat kṣureṇa marcayatā sutejasā vaptā vapasi keśaśmaśru |
8,2.17c śubhaṃ mukhaṃ mā na āyuḥ pra moṣīḥ ||17||

8,2.18a śivau te stāṃ vrīhiyavāv abalāsāv adomadhau |
8,2.18c etau yakṣmaṃ vi bādhete etau muñcato aṃhasaḥ ||18||

8,2.19a yad aśnāsi yat pibasi dhānyaṃ kṛṣyāḥ payaḥ |
8,2.19c yad ādyaṃ yad anādyaṃ sarvaṃ te annam aviṣaṃ kṛṇomi ||19||

8,2.20a ahne ca tvā rātraye cobhābhyāṃ pari dadmasi |
8,2.20c arāyebhyo jighatsubhya imaṃ me pari rakṣata ||20|| {4}

8,2.21a śataṃ te 'yutaṃ hāyanān dve yuge trīṇi catvāri kṛṇmaḥ |
8,2.21c indrāgnī viśve devās te 'nu manyantām ahṛṇīyamānāḥ ||21||

8,2.22a śarade tvā hemantāya vasantāya grīṣmāya pari dadmasi |
8,2.22c varṣāṇi tubhyaṃ syonāni yeṣu vardhanta oṣadhīḥ ||22||

8,2.23a mṛtyur īśe dvipadāṃ mṛtyur īśe catuṣpadām |
8,2.23c tasmāt tvāṃ mṛtyor gopater ud bharāmi sa mā bibheḥ ||23||

8,2.24a so 'riṣṭa na mariṣyasi na mariṣyasi mā bibheḥ |
8,2.24c na vai tatra mriyante no yanti adhamaṃ tamaḥ ||24||

8,2.25a sarvo vai tatra jīvati gaur aśvaḥ puruṣaḥ paśuḥ |
8,2.25c yatredaṃ brahma kriyate paridhir jīvanāya kam ||25||

8,2.26a pari tvā pātu samānebhyo 'bhicārāt sabandhubhyaḥ |
8,2.26c amamrir bhavāmṛto 'tijīvo mā te hāsiṣur asavaḥ śarīram ||26||

8,2.27a ye mṛtyava ekaśataṃ yā nāṣṭrā atitāryāḥ |
8,2.27c muñcantu tasmāt tvāṃ devā agner vaiśvānarād adhi ||27||

8,2.28a agneḥ śarīram asi pārayiṣṇu rakṣohāsi sapatnahā |
8,2.28c atho amīvacātanaḥ pūtudrur nāma bheṣajam ||28|| {5}



rakṣohaṇaṃ vājinam ā jigharmi mitraṃ prathiṣṭham upa yāmi śarma |
śiśāno agniḥ kratubhiḥ samiddhaḥ sa no divā sa riṣaḥ pātu naktam ||1||

ayodaṃṣṭro arciṣā yātudhānān upa spṛśa jātavedaḥ samiddhaḥ |
ā jihvayā mūradevān rabhasva kravyādo vṛṣṭvāpi dhatsvāsan ||2||

ubhobhayāvinn upa dhehi daṃṣṭrau hiṃsraḥ śiśāno 'varaṃ paraṃ ca |
utāntarikṣe pari yāhy agne jambhaiḥ saṃ dhehy abhi yātudhānān ||3||

agne tvacaṃ yātudhānasya bhindhi hiṃsrāśanir harasā hantv enam |
pra parvāṇi jātavedaḥ śṛṇīhi kravyāt kraviṣṇur vi cinotv enam ||4||

yatredānīṃ paśyasi jātavedas tiṣṭhantam agna uta vā carantam |
utāntarikṣe patantaṃ yātudhānaṃ tam astā vidhya śarvā śiśānaḥ ||5||

yajñair iṣūḥ saṃnamamāno agne ivācā śalyāṃ aśanibhir dihānaḥ |
tābhir vidhya hṛdaye yātudhānān pratīco bāhūn prati bhaṅgdhy eṣām ||6||

utārabdhānt spṛnuhi jātaveda utārebhāṇāṃ ṛṣṭibhir yātudhānān |
agne pūrvo ni jahi śośucāna āmādaḥ kṣviṅkās tam adantv enīḥ ||7||

iha pra brūhi yatamaḥ so agne yātudhāno ya idaṃ kṛṇoti |
tam ā rabhasva samidhā yaviṣṭha nṛcakṣasaś cakṣuṣe randhayainam ||8||

tīkṣṇenāgne cakṣuṣā rakṣa yajñaṃ prāñcaṃ vasubhyaḥ pra ṇaya pracetaḥ |
hiṃsraṃ rakṣāṃsy abhi śośucānaṃ mā tvā dabhan yātudhānā nṛcakṣaḥ ||9||

8,3.10a nṛcakṣā rakṣaḥ pari paśya vikṣu tasya trīṇi prati śṛṇīhy agrā |
8,3.10c tasyāgne pṛṣṭīr harasā śṛṇīhi tredhā mūlaṃ yātudhānasya vṛśca ||10|| {6}

8,3.11a trir yātudhānaḥ prasitiṃ ta etv ṛtaṃ yo agne anṛtena hanti |
8,3.11c tam arciṣā sphūrjayan jātavedaḥ samakṣam enam gṛṇate ni yuṅgdhi ||11||

8,3.12a yad agne adya mithunā śapāto yad vācas tṛṣṭaṃ janayanta rebhāḥ |
8,3.12c manyor manasaḥ śaravyā jāyate yā tayā vidhya hṛdaye yātudhānān ||12||

8,3.13a parā śṛṇīhi tapasā yātudhānān parāgne rakṣo harasā śṛṇīhi |
8,3.13c parārciṣā mūradevān chṛṇīhi parāsutṛpaḥ śośucataḥ śṛṇīhi ||13||

8,3.14a parādya devā vṛjinaṃ śṛṇantu pratyag enaṃ śapathā yantu sṛṣṭāḥ |
8,3.14c vācāstenaṃ śarava ṛchantu marman viśvasyaitu prasitiṃ yātudhānaḥ ||14||

8,3.15a yaḥ pauruṣeyeṇa kraviṣā samaṅkte yo aśvyena paśunā yātudhānaḥ |
8,3.15c yo aghnyāyā bharati kṣīram agne teṣāṃ śīrṣāṇi harasāpi vṛśca ||15||

8,3.16a viṣaṃ gavāṃ yātudhānā bharantām ā vṛścantām aditaye durevāḥ |
8,3.16c paraiṇān devaḥ savitā dadātu parā bhāgam oṣadhīnāṃ jayantām ||16||

8,3.17a saṃvatsarīṇaṃ paya usriyāyās tasya māśīd yātudhāno nṛcakṣaḥ |
8,3.17c pīyūṣam agne yatamas titṛpsāt taṃ pratyañcam arciṣā vidhya marmaṇi ||17||

8,3.18a sanād agne mṛṇasi yātudhānān na tvā rakṣāṃsi pṛtanāsu jigyuḥ |
8,3.18c sahamūrān anu daha kravyādo mā te hetyā mukṣata daivyāyāḥ ||18||

8,3.19a tvaṃ no agne adharād udaktas tvaṃ paścād uta rakṣā purastāt |
8,3.19c prati tye te ajarāsas tapiṣṭhā aghaśaṃsaṃ śośucato dahantu ||19||

8,3.20a paścāt purastād adharād utottarāt kaviḥ kāvyena pari pāhy agne |
8,3.20c sakhā sakhāyam ajaro jarimne agne martāṃ amartyas tvaṃ naḥ ||20|| {7}

8,3.21a tad agne cakṣuḥ prati dhehi rebhe śaphārujo yena paśyasi yātudhānān |
8,3.21c atharvavaj jyotiṣā daivyena satyaṃ dhūrvantam acitaṃ nyoṣa ||21||

8,3.22a pari tvāgne puraṃ vayaṃ vipraṃ sahasya dhīmahi |
8,3.22c dhṛṣadvarṇaṃ divedive hantāraṃ bhaṅgurāvataḥ ||22||

8,3.23a viṣeṇa bhaṅgurāvataḥ prati sma rakṣaso jahi |
8,3.23c agne tigmena śociṣā tapuragrābhir arcibhiḥ ||23||

8,3.24a vi jyotiṣā bṛhatā bhāty agnir āvir viśvāni kṛṇute mahitvā |
8,3.24c prādevīr māyāḥ sahate durevāḥ śiśīte śṛṅge rakṣobhyo vinikṣe ||24||

8,3.25a ye te śṛṅge ajare jātavedas tigmahetī brahmasaṃśite |
8,3.25c tābhyāṃ durhārdam abhidāsantaṃ kimīdinaṃ |
8,3.25e pratyañcam arciṣā jātavedo vi nikṣva ||25||

8,3.26a agnī rakṣāṃsi sedhati śukraśocir amartyaḥ |
8,3.26c śuciḥ pāvaka īḍyaḥ ||26|| {8}



indrāsomā tapataṃ rakṣa ubjataṃ ny arpayataṃ vṛṣaṇā tamovṛdhaḥ |
parā śṛṇītam acito ny oṣataṃ hataṃ nudethāṃ ni śiśītam attriṇaḥ ||1||

indrāsomā sam aghaśaṃsam abhy aghaṃ tapur yayastu carur agnimāṃ iva |
brahmadviṣe kravyāde ghoracakṣase dveṣo dhattam anavāyaṃ kimīdine ||2||

indrāsomā duṣkṛto vavre antar anārambhaṇe tamasi pra vidhyatam |
yato naiṣāṃ punar ekaś canodayat tad vām astu sahase manyumac chavaḥ ||3||

indrāsomā vartayataṃ divo vadhaṃ saṃ pṛthivyā aghaśaṃsāya tarhaṇam |
ut takṣataṃ svaryaṃ1 parvatebhyo yena rakṣo vāvṛdhānaṃ nijūrvathaḥ ||4||

indrāsomā vartayataṃ divas pary agnitaptebhir yuvam aśmahanmabhiḥ |
tapurvadhebhir ajarebhir attriṇo ni parśāne vidhyataṃ yantu nisvaram ||5||

indrāsomā pari vāṃ bhūtu viśvata iyaṃ matiḥ kakṣyāśveva vājinā |
yāṃ vāṃ hotrāṃ parihinomi medhayemā brahmāṇi nṛpatī iva jinvatam ||6||

prati smarethāṃ tujayadbhir evair hataṃ druho rakṣaso bhaṅgurāvataḥ |
indrāsomā duṣkṛte mā sugaṃ bhūd yo mā kadā cid abhidāsati druhuḥ ||7||

yo mā pākena manasā carantam abhicaṣṭe anṛtebhir vacobhiḥ |
āpa iva kāśinā samgṛbhītā asann astv asataḥ indra vaktā ||8||

ye pākaśaṃsaṃ viharanta evair ye vā bhadraṃ dūṣayanti svadhābhiḥ |
ahaye vā tān pradadātu soma ā vā dadhātu nirṛter upaṣṭhe ||9||

8,4.10a yo no rasaṃ dipsati pitvo agne aśvānāṃ gavāṃ yas tanūnām |
8,4.10c ripu stena steyakṛd dabhram etu ni ṣa hīyatāṃ tanvā tanā ca ||10|| {9}

8,4.11a paraḥ so astu tanvā tanā ca tisraḥ pṛthivīr adho astu viśvāḥ |
8,4.11c prati śuṣyatu yaśo asya devā yo mā divā dipsati yaś ca naktam ||11||

8,4.12a suvijñānaṃ cikituṣe janāya sac cāsac ca vacasī paspṛdhāte |
8,4.12c tasyor yat satyaṃ yatarad ṛjīyas tad it somo 'vati hanty asat ||12||

8,4.13a na vā u somo vṛjinaṃ hinoti na kṣatriyam mithuyā dhārayantam |
8,4.13c hanti rakṣo hanty āsad vadantam ubhāv indrasya prasitau śayāte ||13||

8,4.14a yadi vāham anṛtadevo asmi moghaṃ vā devāṃ apyūhe agne |
8,4.14c kim asmabhyaṃ jātavedo hṛṇīṣe droghavācas te nirṛthaṃ sacantām ||14||

8,4.15a adyā murīya yadi yātudhāno asmi yadi vāyus tatapa puruṣasya |
8,4.15c adhā sa vīrair daśabhir vi yūyā yo mā moghaṃ yātudhānety āha ||15||

8,4.16a yo māyātuṃ yātudhānety āha yo vā rakṣāḥ śicir asmīty āha |
8,4.16c indras taṃ hantu mahatā vadhena viśvasya jantor adhamas padīṣṭa ||16||

8,4.17a pra yā jigāti khargaleva naktam apa druhus tanvaṃ1 gūhamānā |
8,4.17c vavram anantam ava sā padīṣṭia grāvāṇo ghnantu rakṣasa upabdaiḥ ||17||

8,4.18a vi tiṣṭhadhvam maruto vikṣv ichata gṛbhāyata rakṣasaḥ saṃ pinaṣṭan |
8,4.18c vayo ye bhūtvā patayanti naktabhir ye vā ripo dadhire deve adhvare ||18||

8,4.19a pra vartaya divo 'śmānam indra somaśitaṃ maghavant saṃ śiśādhi |
