8,4.19c prākto apākto adharād udakto 'bhi jahi rakṣasaḥ parvatena ||19||

8,4.20a eta u tye patayanti śvayātava indraṃ dipsanti dipsavo 'dābhyam |
8,4.20c śiśīte śakraḥ piśunebhyo vadhaṃ nunaṃ sṛjad aśaniṃ yātumadbhyaḥ ||20|| {10}

8,4.21a indro yātūnām abhavat parāśaro havirmathīnām abhy āvivāsatām |
8,4.21c abhīd u śakraḥ paraśur yathā vanaṃ pātreva bhindant sata etu rakṣasaḥ ||21||

8,4.22a ulūkayātuṃ śuśulūkayātuṃ jahi śvayātum uta kokayātum |
8,4.22c suparṇayātum uta gṛdhrayātuṃ dṛṣadeva pra mṛṇa rakṣa indra ||22||

8,4.23a mā no rakṣo abhi naḍ yātumāvad apochantu mithunā ye kimīdinaḥ |
8,4.23c pṛthivī naḥ pārthivāt pātv aṃhaso 'ntarikṣaṃ divyāt pātv asmān ||23||

8,4.24a indra jahi pumāṃsaṃ yātudhānam uta striyaṃ māyayā śāśadānām |
8,4.24c vigrīvāso mūradevā ṛdantu mā te dṛśant sūryam uccarantam ||24||
8,4.25a prati cakṣva vi cakṣvendraś ca soma jāgṛtam |
8,4.25c rakṣobhyo vadham asyatam aśaniṃ yātumadbhyaḥ ||25|| {11}



ayaṃ pratisaro maṇir vīro vīrāya badhyate |
vīryavānt sapatnahā śūravīraḥ paripāṇaḥ sumaṅgalaḥ ||1||

ayaṃ maṇiḥ sapatnahā suvīraḥ sahasvān vājī sahamāna ugraḥ |
pratyak kṛtyā dūṣayann eti vīraḥ ||2||

anenendro maṇinā vṛtram ahann anenāsurān parābhāvayan manīṣī |
anenājayad dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe ime anenājayat pradiśaś catasraḥ ||3||

ayaṃ srāktyo maṇiḥ pratīvartaḥ pratisaraḥ |
ojasvān vimṛdho vaśī so asmān pātu sarvataḥ ||4||

tad agnir āha tad u soma āha bṛhaspatiḥ savitā tad indraḥ |
te me devāḥ purohitāḥ pratīcīḥ kṛtyāḥ pratisarair ajantu ||5||

antar dadhe dyāvāpṛthivī utāhar uta sūryam |
te me devāḥ purohitāḥ pratīcīḥ kṛtyāḥ pratisarair ajantu ||6||

ye srāktyaṃ maṇiṃ janā varmāṇi kṛṇvate |
sūrya iva divam āruhya vi kṛtyā bādhate vaśī ||7||

srāktyena maṇinā ṛṣiṇeva manīṣiṇā |
ajaiṣaṃ sarvāḥ pṛtanā vi mṛdho hanmi rakṣasaḥ ||8||

yāḥ kṛtyā āṅgirasīr yāḥ kṛtyā āsurīr yāḥ |
kṛtyāḥ svayaṃkṛtā yā u cānyebhir ābhṛtāḥ |
ubhayīs tāḥ parā yantu parāvato navatiṃ nāvyā ati ||9||

8,5.10a asmai maṇiṃ varma badhnantu devā indro viṣṇuḥ savitā rudro agniḥ |
8,5.10c prajāpatiḥ parameṣṭhī virāḍ vaiśvānara ṛṣayaś ca sarve ||10|| {12}

8,5.11a uttamo asy oṣadhīnām anaḍvān jagatām iva vyāghraḥ śvapadām iva |
8,5.11ḍ yam aichāmāvidāma taṃ pratispāśanam antitam ||11||

8,5.12a sa id vyāghro bhavaty atho siṃho atho vṛṣā |
8,5.12c atho sapatnakarśano yo bibhartīmaṃ maṇim ||12||

8,5.13a nainaṃ ghnanty apsaraso na gandharvā na martyāḥ |
8,5.13c sarvā diśo vi rājati yo bibhartīmaṃ maṇim ||13||

8,5.14a kaśyapas tvām asṛjata kaśyapas tvā sam airayat |
8,5.14c abibhas tvendro mānuṣe bibhrat saṃśreṣiṇe 'jayat |
8,5.14e maṇiṃ sahasravīryaṃ varma devā akṛṇvata ||14||

8,5.15a yas tvā kṛtyābhir yas tvā dīkṣābhir yajñair yas tvā jighāṃsati |
8,5.15c pratyak tvam indra taṃ jahi vajreṇa śataparvaṇā ||15||

8,5.16a ayam id vai pratīvarta ojasvān saṃjayo maṇiḥ |
8,5.16c prajāṃ dhanaṃ ca rakṣatu paripāṇaḥ sumaṅgalaḥ ||16||

8,5.17a asapatnaṃ no adharād asapatnaṃ na uttarāt |
8,5.17c indrāsapatnaṃ naḥ paścāj jyotiḥ śūra puras kṛdhi ||17||

8,5.18a varma me dyāvāpṛthivī varmāhar varma sūryaḥ |
8,5.18c varma ma indraś cāgniś ca varma dhātā dadhātu me ||18||

8,5.19a aindrāgnaṃ varma bahulaṃ yad ugraṃ viśve devā nātividhyanti sarve |
8,5.19c tan me tanvaṃ trāyatāṃ sarvato bṛhad āyuṣmāṃ jaradaṣṭir yathāsāni ||19||

8,5.20a ā mārukṣad devamaṇir mahyā ariṣṭatātaye |
8,5.20c imaṃ methim abhisaṃviśadhvaṃ tanūpānaṃ trivarūtham ojase ||20||

8,5.21a asminn indro ni dadhātu nṛmṇam imaṃ devāso abhisaṃviśadhvam |
8,5.21c dīrghāyutvāya śataśāradāyāyuṣmān jaradaṣṭir yathāsat ||21||

8,5.22a svastidā viśāṃ patir vṛtrahā vimṛdho vaśī |
8,5.22c indro badhnātu te maṇiṃ jigīvāṃ aparājitaḥ |
8,5.22e somapā abhayaṅkaro vṛṣā |



yau te mātonmamārja jātāyāḥ pativedanau |
durṇāmā tatra mā gṛdhad aliṃśa uta vatsapaḥ ||1||

palālānupalālau śarkuṃ kokaṃ malimlucaṃ palījakam |
āśreṣaṃ vavrivāsasam ṛkṣagrīvaṃ pramīlinam ||2||

mā saṃ vṛto mopa sṛpa ūrū māva sṛpo 'ntarā |
kṛṇomy asyai bheṣajaṃ bajaṃ durṇāmacātanam ||3||

durṇāmā ca sunāmā cobhā samvṛtam ichataḥ |
arāyān apa hanmaḥ sunāmā straiṇam ichatām ||4||

yaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ keśy asura stambaja uta tuṇḍikaḥ |
arāyān asyā muṣkābhyāṃ bhaṃsaso 'pa hanmasi ||5||

anujighraṃ pramṛśantaṃ kravyādam uta reriham |
arāyāṃ chvakiṣkiṇo bajaḥ piṅgo anīnaśat ||6||

yas tvā svapne nipadyate bhrātā bhūtvā piteva ca |
bajas tānt sahatām itaḥ klībarūpāṃs tirīṭinaḥ ||7||

yas tvā svapantīṃ tsarati yas tvā dipsati jāgratīm |
chāyām iva pra tānt sūryaḥ parikrāmann anīnaśat ||8||

yaḥ kṛṇoti mṛtavatsām avatokām imāṃ striyam |
tam oṣadhe tvaṃ nāśayāsyāḥ kamalam añjivam ||9||

8,6.10a ye śālāḥ parinṛtyanti sāyaṃ gardabhanādinaḥ |
8,6.10c kusūlā ye ca kukṣilāḥ kakubhāḥ karumāḥ srimāḥ |
8,6.10e tān oṣadhe tvaṃ gandhena viṣūcīnān vi nāśaya ||10|| {14}

8,6.11a ye kukundhāḥ kukirabhāḥ kṛttīr dūrśāni bibhrati |
8,6.11c klībā iva pranṛtyanto vane ye kurvate ghoṣaṃ tān ito nāśayāmasi ||11||

8,6.12a ye sūryaṃ na titikṣanta ātapantam amuṃ divaḥ |
8,6.12c arāyān bastavāsino durgandhīṃl lohitāsyān makakān nāśayāmasi ||12||

8,6.13a ya ātmānam atimātram aṃsa ādhāya bibhrati |
8,6.13c strīṇāṃ śroṇipratodina indra rakṣāṃsi nāśaya ||13||

8,6.14a ye pūrve badhvo yanti haste śṛṅgāni bibhrataḥ |
8,6.14c āpākesthāḥ prahāsina stambe ye kurvate jyotis tān ito nāśayāmasi ||14||

8,6.15a yeṣām paścāt prapadāni puraḥ pārṣṇīḥ puro mukhā |
8,6.15c khalajāḥ śakadhūmajā uruṇḍā ye ca maṭmaṭāḥ kumbhamuṣkā ayāśavaḥ |
8,6.15e tān asyā brahmaṇas pate pratībodhena nāśaya ||15||

8,6.16a paryastākṣā apracaṅkaśā astraiṇāḥ santu paṇḍagāḥ |
8,6.16c ava bheṣaja pādaya ya imāṃ saṃvivṛtsaty apatiḥ svapatiṃ striyam ||16||

8,6.17a uddharṣiṇaṃ munikeśaṃ jambhayantaṃ marīmṛśam |
8,6.17c upeṣantam udumbalaṃ tuṇḍelam uta śāluḍam |
8,6.17e padā pra vidhya pārṣṇyā sthālīṃ gaur iva spandanā ||17||

8,6.18a yas te garbhaṃ pratimṛśāj jātaṃ vā mārayāti te |
8,6.18c piṅgas tam ugradhanvā kṛṇotu hṛdayāvidham ||18||

8,6.19a ye amno jatān mārayanti sūtikā anuśerate |
8,6.19c strībhāgān piṅgo gandharvān vāto abhram ivājatu ||19||

8,6.20a parisṛṣṭaṃ dharayatu yad dhitaṃ māva pādi tat |
8,6.20c garbhaṃ ta ugrau rakṣatām bheṣajau nīvibhāryau ||20|| {15}

8,6.21a pavīnasāt taṅgalvāc chāyakād uta nagnakāt |
8,6.21c prajāyai patye tvā piṅgaḥ pari pātu kimīdinaḥ ||21||

8,6.22a dvyāsyāc caturakṣāt pañcapadād anaṅgureḥ |
8,6.22c vṛntād abhi prasarpataḥ pari pāhi varīvṛtāt ||22||

8,6.23a ya āmaṃ māṃsam adanti pauruṣeyaṃ ca ye kraviḥ |
8,6.23c garbhān khādanti keśavās tān ito nāśayāmasi ||23||

8,6.24a ye sūryāt parisarpanti snuṣeva śvaśurād adhi |
8,6.24c bajaś ca teṣāṃ piṅgaś ca hṛdaye 'dhi ni vidhyatām ||24||

8,6.25a piṅga rakṣa jāyamānaṃ mā pumāṃsaṃ striyaṃ kran |
8,6.25c āṇḍādo garbhān mā dabhan bādhasvetaḥ kimīdinaḥ ||25||

8,6.26a aprajāstvaṃ mārtavatsam ād rodam agham āvayam |
8,6.26c vṛkṣād iva srajam kṛtvāpriye prati muñca tat ||26|| {16}



yā babhravo yāś ca śukrā rohiṇīr uta pṛśnayaḥ |
asiknīḥ kṛṣṇā oṣadhīḥ sarvā achāvadāmasi ||1||

trāyantām imaṃ purusaṃ yakṣmād deveṣitād adhi |
yāsām dyauḥ pitā pṛthivī mātā samudro mūlaṃ vīrudhāṃ babhūva ||2||

āpo agraṃ divyā oṣadhayaḥ |
tās te yakṣmam enasyam aṅgādaṅgād anīnaśan ||3||

prastṛṇatī stambinīr ekaśuṅgāḥ pratanvatīr oṣadhīr ā vadāmi |
aṃśumatīḥ kaṇḍinīr yā viśākhā hvayāmi te vīrudho vaiśvadevīr ugrāḥ puruṣajīvanīḥ ||4||

yad vaḥ sahaḥ sahamānā vīryaṃ1 yac ca vo balam |
tenemam asmād yakṣmāt puruṣaṃ muñcatauṣadhīr atho kṛṇomi bheṣajam ||5||

jīvalāṃ naghāriṣāṃ jīvantīm oṣadhīm aham |
arundhatīm unnayantīṃ puṣpām madhumatīm iha huve 'smā ariṣṭatātaye ||6||

ihā yantu pracetaso medinīr vacaso mama |
yathemaṃ pārayāmasi puruṣaṃ duritād adhi ||7||

agner ghāso apāṃ garbho yā rohanti punarṇavāḥ |
dhruvāḥ sahasranāmnīr bheṣajīḥ santv ābhṛtāḥ ||8||

avakolbā udakātmāna oṣadhayaḥ |
vyṛṣantu duritaṃ tīkṣṇaśṛṅgyaḥ ||9||

8,7.10a unmuñcantīr vivaruṇā ugrā yā viṣadūṣanīḥ |
8,7.10c atho balāsanāśanīḥ kṛtyādūṣaṇīś ca yās tā ihā yantv oṣadhīḥ ||10|| {17}

8,7.11a apakrītāḥ sahīyasīr vīrudho yā abhiṣṭutāḥ |
8,7.11c trāyantām asmin grāme gām aśvaṃ puruṣaṃ paśum ||11||

8,7.12a madhuman mūlaṃ madhumad agram āsām madhuman madhyaṃ vīrudhāṃ babhūva |
8,7.12c madhumat parṇaṃ madhumat puṣpam āsāṃ madhoḥ sambhaktā amṛtasya bhakṣo ghṛtam annaṃ duhratāṃ gopurogavam ||12||

8,7.13a yāvatīḥ kiyatīś cemāḥ pṛthivyām adhy oṣadhīḥ |
8,7.13c tā mā sahasraparṇyo mṛtyor muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ||13||

8,7.14a vaiyāghro maṇir vīrudhāṃ trāyamāno 'bhiśastipāḥ |
8,7.14c amīvāḥ sarvā rakṣāṃsy apa hantv adhi dūram asmat ||14||

8,7.15a siṃhasyeva stanathoḥ saṃ vijante 'gner iva vijante ābhṛtābhyaḥ |
8,7.15c gavāṃ yakṣmaḥ puruṣāṇāṃ vīrudbhir atinutto nāvyā etu srotyāḥ ||15||

8,7.16a mumucānā oṣadhayo 'gner vaiśvānarād adhi |
8,7.16c bhūmiṃ saṃtanvatīr ita yāsāṃ rājā vanaspatiḥ ||16||

8,7.17a yā rohanty āṅgirasīḥ parvateṣu sameṣu ca |
8,7.17c tā naḥ payasvatīḥ śivā oṣadhīḥ santu śaṃ hṛde ||17||

8,7.18a yāś cāhaṃ veda vīrudho yāś ca paśyāmi cakṣuṣā |
8,7.18c ajñātā jānīmaś ca yā yāsu vidma ca saṃbhṛtam ||18||

8,7.19a sarvāḥ samagrā oṣadhīr bodhantu vacaso mama |
8,7.19c yathemaṃ pārayāmasi puruṣam duritād adhi ||19||

8,7.20a aśvattho darbho vīrudhāṃ somo rājāmṛtaṃ haviḥ |
8,7.20c vrīhir yavaś ca bheṣajau divasi putrāv amartyau ||20|| {18}

8,7.21a uj jihīdhve stanayaty abhikrandaty oṣadhīḥ |
8,7.21c yadā vaḥ pṛśnimātaraḥ parjanyo retasāvati ||21||
8,7.22a tasyāmṛtasyemaṃ balaṃ puruṣaṃ payayāmasi |
8,7.22c atho kṛṇomi bheṣajaṃ yathāsac chatahāyanaḥ ||22||

8,7.23a varāho veda vīrudhaṃ nakulo veda bheṣajīm |
8,7.23c sarpā gandharvā yā vidus tā asmā avase huve ||23||

8,7.24a yāḥ suparṇā āṅgirasīr divyā yā raghato viduḥ |
8,7.24c vayāṃsi haṃsā yā vidur yās ca sarve patatriṇaḥ |
8,7.24e mṛgā yā vidur oṣadhīs tā asmā avase huve ||24||

8,7.25a yāvatīnām oṣadhīnāṃ gāvaḥ prāśnanty aghnyā yavatīnām ajāvayaḥ |
8,7.25c tāvatīs tubhyam oṣadhīḥ śarma yachantv ābhṛtāḥ ||25||

8,7.26a yāvatīṣu manuṣyā bheṣajaṃ bhiṣajo viduḥ |
8,7.26c tāvatīr viśvabheṣajīr ā bharāmi tvām abhi ||26||

8,7.27a puṣpavatīḥ prasūmatīḥ phalinīr aphalā uta |
8,7.27c saṃmātara iva duhrām asmā ariṣṭatātaye ||27||

8,7.28a ut tvāhārṣaṃ pañcaśalād atho daśaśalād uta |
8,7.28c atho yamasya paḍvīśād viśvasmād devakilbiṣāt ||28|| {19}


indro manthatu manthitā śakraḥ śūraḥ puraṃdaraḥ |
yathā hanāma senā amitrāṇāṃ sahasraśaḥ ||1||

pūtirajjur upadhmānī pūtiṃ senāṃ kṛṇotv amūm |
dhūmam agnim parādṛśyā 'mitrā hṛtsv ā dadhatāṃ bhayam ||2||

amūn aśvattha niḥ śṛṇīhi khādāmūn khadirājiram |
tājadbhaṅga iva bhajantāṃ hantv enān vadhako vadhaiḥ ||3||

paruṣān amūn paruṣāhvaḥ kṛṇotu hantv enān vadhako vadhaiḥ |
kṣipraṃ śara iva bhajantāṃ bṛhajjālena saṃditāḥ ||4||

antarikṣaṃ jālam āsīj jāladaṇḍā diśo mahīḥ |
tenābhidhāya dasyūnāṃ śakraḥ senām apāvapat ||5||

bṛhad dhi jālaṃ bṛhataḥ śakrasya vājinīvataḥ |
tena śatrūn abhi sarvān ny ubja yathā na mucyātai katamaś canaiṣām ||6||

bṛhat te jālaṃ bṛhata indra śūra sahasrārghasya śatavīryasya |
tena śataṃ sahasram ayutaṃ nyarbudaṃ jaghāna śakro dasyūnām abhidhāya senayā ||7||

ayaṃ loko jālam āsīc chakrasya mahato mahān |
tenāham indrajālenāmūṃs tamasābhi dadhāmi sarvān ||8||

sedir ugrā vyṛddhir ārtiś cānapavācanā |
śramas tandrīś ca mohaś ca tair amūn abhi dadhāmi sarvān ||9||

8,8.10a mṛtyave 'mūn pra yachāmi mṛtyupāśair amī sitāḥ |
8,8.10c mṛtyor ye aghalā dūtās tebhya enān prati nayāmi baddhvā ||10|| {20}

8,8.11a nayatāmūn mṛtyudūtā yamadūtā apombhata |
8,8.11c paraḥsahasrā hanyantāṃ tṛṇeḍhv enān matyaṃ bhavasya ||11||

8,8.12a sādhyā ekaṃ jāladaṇḍam udyatya yanty ojasā |
8,8.12c rudrā ekaṃ vasava ekam ādityair eka udyataḥ ||12||

8,8.13a viśve devāḥ upariṣṭād ubjanto yantv ojasā |
8,8.13c madhyena ghnanto yantu senām aṅgiraso mahīm ||13||

8,8.14a vanaspatīn vānaspatyān oṣadhīr uta vīrudhaḥ |
8,8.14c dvipāc catuṣpād iṣṇāmi yathā senām amūṃ hanan ||14||

8,8.15a gandharvāpsarasaḥ sarpān devān puṇyajanān pitṝn |
8,8.15c dṛṣṭān adṛṣṭān iṣṇāmi yathā senām amūṃ hanan ||15||

8,8.16a ima uptā mṛtyupāśā yān ākramya na mucyase |
8,8.16c amuṣyā hantu senāyā idaṃ kūṭaṃ sahasraśaḥ ||16||

8,8.17a gharmaḥ samiddho agnināyaṃ homaḥ sahasrahaḥ |
8,8.17c bhavaś ca pṛśnibāhuś ca śarva senām amūṃ hatam ||17||

8,8.18a mṛtyor āṣam ā padyantāṃ kṣudhaṃ sediṃ vadham bhayam |
8,8.18c indraś cākṣujālābhyāṃ śarva senām amūṃ hatam ||18||

8,8.19a parājitāḥ pra trasatāmitrā nuttā dhāvata brahmaṇā |
8,8.19c bṛhaspatipranuttānāṃ māmīṣāṃ moci kaś cana ||19||

8,8.20a ava padyantām eṣām āyudhāni mā śakan pratidhām iṣum |
8,8.20c athaiṣāṃ bahu bibhyatām iṣavaḥ ghnantu marmaṇi ||20||

8,8.21a saṃ krośatām enān dyāvāpṛthivī sam antarikṣaṃ saha devatābhiḥ |
8,8.21c mā jñātāraṃ mā pratiṣṭhāṃ vidanta mitho vighnānā upa yantu mṛtyum ||21||

8,8.22a diśaś catasro 'śvataryo devarathasya purodāśāḥ śaphā antarikṣam uddhiḥ |
8,8.22c dyāvāpṛthivī pakṣasī ṛtavo 'bhīśavo 'ntardeśāḥ kimkarā vāk parirathyam ||22||

8,8.23a saṃvatsaro rathaḥ parivatsaro rathopastho virāḍ īṣāgnī rathamukham |
8,8.23c indraḥ savyaṣṭhāś candramāḥ sārathiḥ ||23||

8,8.24a ito jayeto vi jaya saṃ jaya jaya svāhā |
8,8.24c ime jayantu parāmī jayantāṃ svāhaibhyo durāhāmībhyaḥ |
8,8.24e nīlalohitenāmūn abhyavatanomi ||24|| {21}



kutas tau jātau katamaḥ so ardhaḥ kasmāl lokāt katamasyāḥ pṛthivyāḥ |
vatsau virājaḥ salilād ud aitāṃ tau tvā pṛchāmi katareṇa dugdhā ||1||

yo akrandayat salilaṃ mahitvā yoniṃ kṛtvā tribhujaṃ śayānaḥ |
vatsaḥ kāmadugho virājaḥ sa guhā cakre tanvaḥ parācaiḥ ||2||

yāni trīṇi bṛhanti yeṣāṃ caturthaṃ viyunakti vācam |
brahmainad vidyāt tapasā vipaścid yasminn ekaṃ yujyate yasminn ekam ||3||

bṛhataḥ pari sāmāni ṣaṣṭhāt pañcādhi nirmitā |
bṛhad bṛhatyā nirmitaṃ kuto 'dhi bṛhatī mitā ||4||

bṛhatī pari mātrāyā mātur mātrādhi nirmitā |
māyā ha jajñe māyāyā māyāyā mātalī pari ||5||

vaiśvānarasya pratimopari dyaur yāvad rodasī vibabādhe agniḥ |
tataḥ ṣaṣṭhād āmuto yanti stomā ud ito yanty abhi ṣaṣṭham ahnaḥ ||6||

ṣaṭ tvā pṛchāma ṛṣayaḥ kaśyapeme tvaṃ hi yuktaṃ yuyukṣe yogyaṃ ca |
virājam āhur brahmaṇaḥ pitaraṃ tāṃ no vi dhehi yatidhā sakhibhyaḥ ||7||

yāṃ pracyutām anu yajñāḥ pracyavanta upatiṣṭhanta upatiṣṭhamānām |
yasyā vrate prasave yakṣam ejati sā virāṭ ṛṣayaḥ parame vyoman ||8||

aprāṇaiti prāṇena prāṇatīnāṃ virāṭ svarājam abhy eti paścāt |
viśvaṃ mṛśantīm abhirūpāṃ virājaṃ paśyanti tve na tve paśyanty enām ||9||

8,9.10a ko virājo mithunatvaṃ pra veda ka ṛtūn ka u kalpam asyāḥ |
8,9.10c kramān ko asyāḥ katidhā vidugdhān ko asyā dhāma katidhā vyuṣṭīḥ ||10|| {22}

8,9.11a iyam eva sā yā prathamā vyauchad āsv itarāsu carati praviṣṭā |
8,9.11c mahānto asyāṃ mahimāno antar vadhūr jigāya navagaj janitrī ||11||

8,9.12a chandaḥpakṣe uṣasā pepiśāne samānaṃ yonim anu saṃ careme |
8,9.12c sūryapatnī saṃ carataḥ prajānatī ketumatī ajare bhūriretasā ||12||

8,9.13a ṛtasya panthām anu tisra āgus trayo gharmā anu reta āguḥ |
8,9.13c prajām ekā jinvaty ūrjam ekā rāṣṭram ekā rakṣati devayūnām ||13||

8,9.14a agnīṣomāv adadhur yā turīyāsīd yajñasya pakṣāv ṛṣayaḥ kalpayantaḥ |
8,9.14c gāyatrīṃ triṣṭubhaṃ jagatīm anuṣṭubhaṃ bṛhadarkīṃ yajamānāya svar ābharantīm ||14||

8,9.15a pañca vyuṣṭīr anu pañca dohā gāṃ pañcanāmnīm ṛtavo 'nu pañca |
8,9.15c pañca diśaḥ pañcadaśena kḷptās tā ekamūrdhnīr abhi lokam ekam ||15||

8,9.16a ṣaṭ jātā bhūtā prathamajā ṛtasya ṣaṭ u sāmāni ṣaṭahaṃ vahanti |
8,9.16c ṣaṭyogaṃ sīram anu sāmasāma ṣaṭ āhur dyāvāpṛthivīḥ ṣaṭ urvīḥ ||16||

8,9.17a ṣaḍ āhuḥ śītān ṣaḍ u māsa uṣṇān ṛtuṃ no brūta yatamo 'tiriktaḥ |
8,9.17c sapta suparṇāḥ kavayo ni ṣeduḥ sapta chandāṃsy anu sapta dīkṣāḥ ||17||

8,9.18a sapta homāḥ samidho ha sapta madhūni sapta ṛtavo ha sapta |
8,9.18c saptājyāni pari bhūtam āyan tāḥ saptagṛdhrā iti śuśrumā vayam ||18||

8,9.19a sapta chandāṃsi caturuttarāṇy anyo anyasminn adhy ārpitāni |
8,9.19c kathaṃ stomāḥ prati tiṣṭhanti teṣu tāni stomeṣu katham ārpitāni ||19||

8,9.20a kathaṃ gāyatrī trivṛtaṃ vy āpa kathaṃ triṣṭup pañcadaśena kalpate |
8,9.20c trayastriṃśena jagatī katham anuṣṭup katham ekaviṃśaḥ ||20|| {23}

8,9.21a aṣṭa jātā bhūtā prathamajā ṛtasyāṣṭendra ṛtvijo daivyā ye |
8,9.21c aṣṭayonir aditir aṣṭaputrāstamīṃ rātrim abhi havyam eti ||21||

8,9.22a itthaṃ śreyo manyamānedam āgamaṃ yuṣmākaṃ sakhye aham asmi śevā |
8,9.22c samānajanmā kratur asti vaḥ śivaḥ sa vaḥ sarvāḥ saṃ carati prajānan ||22||
8,9.23a aṣṭendrasya ṣaḍ yamasya ṛṣīṇāṃ sapta saptadhā |
8,9.23c apo manuṣyān oṣadhīs tāṃ u pañcānu secire ||23||

8,9.24a kevalīndrāya duduhe hi gṛṣṭir vaśam pīyūṣaṃ prathamaṃ duhānā |
8,9.24c athātarpayac caturaś caturdhā devān manuṣyāṃ asurān uta ṛṣīn ||24||

8,9.25a ko nu gauḥ ka ekaṛṣiḥ kim u dhāma kā āśiṣaḥ |
8,9.25c yakṣam pṛthivyām ekavṛd ekartuḥ katamo nu saḥ ||25||

8,9.26a eko gaur eka ekaṛṣir ekaṃ dhāmaikadhāśiṣaḥ |
8,9.26c yakṣaṃ pṛthivyām ekavṛd ekartur nāti ricyate ||26|| {24}



virāḍ vā idam agra āsīt tasyā jātāyāḥ sarvam abibhed iyam evedaṃ bhaviṣyatīti ||1||

sod akrāmat sā gārhapatye ny akrāmat |
gṛhamedhī gṛhapatir bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||2||

sod akrāmat sāhavanīye ny akrāmat |
yanty asya devā devahūtiṃ priyo devānāṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||3||

sod akrāmat sā dakṣiṇāgnau ny akrāmat |
yajñarto dakṣiṇīyo vāsateyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||4||

sod akrāmat sā sabhāyāṃ ny akrāmat |
yanty asya sabhāṃ sabhyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||5||

sod akrāmat sā samitau ny akrāmat |
yanty asya samitiṃ sāmityo bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||6||

sod akrāmat sāmantraṇe ny akrāmat |
yanty asyāmantraṇam āmantraṇīyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||7|| {25}

sod akrāmat sāntarikṣe caturdhā vikrāntātiṣṭhat ||8||

tāṃ devamanuṣyā abruvann iyam eva tad veda yad ubhaya upajīvememām upa hvayāmahā iti ||9||

8,10.10a tām upāhvayanta ||10||

8,10.11a ūrja ehi svadha ehi sūnṛta ehīrāvaty ehīti ||11||

8,10.12a tasyā indro vatsa āsīd gāyatry abhidhāny abhram ūdhaḥ ||12||

8,10.13a bṛhac ca rathaṃtaraṃ ca dvau stanāv āstāṃ yajñāyajñiyaṃ ca vāmadevyaṃ ca dvau ||13||

8,10.14a oṣadhīr eva rathaṃtareṇa devā aduhran vyaco bṛhatā ||14||

8,10.15a apo vāmadevyena yajñaṃ yajñāyajñiyena ||15||

8,10.16a oṣadhīr evāsmai rathaṃtaraṃ duhe vyaco bṛhat ||16||

8,10.17a apo vāmadevyaṃ yajñaṃ yajñāyajñiyaṃ ya veda ||17|| {26}

8,10.18a sod akrāmat sā vanaspatīn āgachat tāṃ vanaspatayo 'ghnata sā saṃvatsare sam abhavat |
8,10.18c tasmād vanaspatīnāṃ saṃvatsare vṛkṇam api rohati vṛścate 'syāpriyo bhrātṛvyo ya evaṃ veda ||18||

8,10.19a sod akrāmat sā pitṝn āgachat tāṃ pitaro 'ghnata sā māsi sam abhavat |
8,10.19c tasmāt pitṛbhyo māsy upamāsyaṃ dadati pra pitṛyāṇaṃ panthāṃ jānāti ya evaṃ veda ||19||

8,10.20a sod akrāmat sā devān āgachat tāṃ devā aghnata sārdhamāse sam abhavat |
8,10.20c tasmād devebhyo 'rdhamāse vaṣaṭ kurvanti pra devayānaṃ panthāṃ jānāti ya evaṃ veda ||20||

8,10.21a sod akrāmat sā manuṣyān āgachat tāṃ manuṣyā aghnata sā sadyaḥ sam abhavat |
8,10.21c tasmān manuṣyebhya ubhayadyur upa haranty upāsya gṛhe haranti ya evaṃ veda ||21|| {27}

8,10.22a sod akrāmat sāsurān āgachat tām asurā upāhvayanta māya ehīti |
8,10.22c tasyā virocanaḥ prāhrādir vatsa āsīd ayaspātraṃ pātram |
8,10.22e tāṃ dvimūrdhārtvyo 'dhok tāṃ māyām evādhok ||
8,10.22g tāṃ māyām asurā upa jīvanty upajīvanīyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||22||

8,10.23a sod akrāmat sā pitṝn āgachat tāṃ pitara upāhvayanta svadha ehīti |
8,10.23c tasyā yamo rājā vatsa āsīd rajatapātraṃ pātram |
8,10.23e tām antako mārtyavo 'dhok tāṃ svadhām evādhok |
8,10.23g tāṃ svadhāṃ pitara upa jīvanty upajīvanīyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||23||

8,10.24a sod akrāmat sā manuṣyān āgachat tāṃ manuṣyā upāhvayanterāvaty ehīti |
8,10.24c tasyā manur vaivasvato vatsa āsīt pṛthivī pātram |
8,10.24e tāṃ pṛthī vainyo 'dhok tāṃ kṛṣiṃ ca sasyaṃ cādhok |
8,10.24g te svadhāṃ kṛṣiṃ ca sasyaṃ ca manuṣyā upa jīvanti kṛṣṭarādhir upajīvanīyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||24||

8,10.25a sod akrāmat sā saptaṛṣīn āgachat tāṃ saptaṛṣaya upāhvayanta brahmaṇvaty ehīti |
8,10.25c tasyāḥ somo rājā vatsa āsīc chandaḥ pātram |
8,10.25e tāṃ bṛhaspatir āṅgiraso 'dhok tāṃ brahma ca tapaś cādhok |
8,10.25g tad brahma ca tapaś ca saptaṛṣaya upa jīvanti brahmavarcasy upajīvanīyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||25|| {28}

8,10.26a sod akrāmat sā devān āgachat tāṃ devā upāhvayantorja ehīti |
8,10.26c tasyā indro vatsa āsīc camasaḥ pātram |
8,10.26e tāṃ devaḥ savitādhok tām ūrjām evādhok |
8,10.26g tāṃ ūrjāṃ devā upa jīvanty upajīvanīyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||26||

8,10.27a sod akrāmat sā gandharvāpsarasa āgachat tāṃ gandharvāpsarasa upāhvayanta puṇyagandha ehīti |
8,10.27c tasyāś citrarathaḥ sauryavarcaso vatsa āsīt puṣkaraparṇaṃ pātram |
8,10.27e tāṃ vasuruciḥ sauryavarcaso 'dhok tāṃ puṇyam eva gandham adhok |
8,10.27g taṃ puṇyaṃ gandhaṃ gandharvāpsarasa upa jīvanti puṇyagandhir upajīvanīyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||27||

8,10.28a sod akrāmat setarajanān āgachat tām itarajanā upāhvayanta tirodha ehīti |
8,10.28c tasyāḥ kubero vaiśravaṇo vatsa āsīd āmapātraṃ pātram |
8,10.28e tāṃ rajatanābhiḥ kaberako 'dhok tāṃ tirodhām evādhok |
8,10.28g tāṃ tirodhām atirajanā pitara upa jīvanti tiro dhatte sarvaṃ pāpmānam upajīvanīyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||28||

8,10.29a sod akrāmat sā sarpān āgachat tāṃ sarpā upāhvayanta viṣavaty ehīti |
8,10.29c tasyās takṣako vaiśaleyo vatsa āsīd alābupātraṃ pātraṃ |
8,10.29e tāṃ dhṛtarāṣṭra airāvato 'dhok tāṃ viṣam evādhok |
8,10.29g tad viṣaṃ sarvā upa jīvanty upajīvanīyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||29|| {29}

8,10.30a tad yasmā evaṃ viduṣe 'lābunābhiṣiñcet pratyāhanyāt ||30||

8,10.31a na ca pratyāhanyān manasā tvā pratyāhanmīti pratyāhanyāt ||31||

8,10.32a yat pratyāhanti viṣam eva tat pratyāhanti ||32||

8,10.33a viṣam evāsyāpriyaṃ bhrātṛvyam anuviṣicyate ya evaṃ veda ||33|| {30}


divas pṛthivyā antarikṣāt samudrād agner vātān madhukaśā hi jajñe |
tāṃ cāyitvāmṛtaṃ vasānāṃ hṛdbhiḥ prajāḥ prati nandanti sarvāḥ ||1||

mahat payo viśvarūpam asyāḥ samudrasya tvota reta āhuḥ |
yata aiti madhukaśā rarāṇā tat prāṇas tad amṛtaṃ niviṣṭam ||2||

paśyanty asyāś caritaṃ pṛthivyāṃ pṛthaṅ naro bahudhā mīmāṃsamānāḥ |
agner vātān madhukaśā hi jajñe marutām ugrā naptiḥ ||3||

mātādityānāṃ duhitā vasūnāṃ prāṇaḥ prajānām amṛtasya nābhiḥ |
hiraṇyavarṇā madhukaśā ghṛtācī mahān bhargaś carati martyeṣu ||4||

madhoḥ kaśām ajanayanta devās tasyā garbho abhavad viśvarūpaḥ |
taṃ jātaṃ taruṇaṃ piparti mātā sa jāto viśvā bhuvanā vi caṣṭe ||5||

kas taṃ pra veda ka u taṃ ciketa yo asyā hṛdaḥ kalaśaḥ somadhāno akṣitaḥ |
brahmā sumedhāḥ so asmin madeta ||6||

sa tau pra veda sa u tau ciketa yāv asyāḥ stanau sahasradhārāv akṣitau |
ūrjaṃ duhāte anapasphurantau ||7||

hiṅkarikratī bṛhatī vayodhā uccairghoṣābhyeti yā vratam |
trīn gharmān abhi vāvaśānā mimāti māyuṃ payate payobhiḥ ||8||

yām āpīnām upasīdanty āpaḥ śākvarā vṛṣabhā ye svarājaḥ |
te varṣanti te varṣayanti tadvide kāmam ūrjam āpaḥ ||9||

9,1.10a stanayitnus te vāk prajāpate vṛṣā śuṣmaṃ kṣipasi bhūmyām adhi |
9,1.10c agner vātān madhukaśā hi jajñe marutām ugrā naptiḥ ||10|| {1}

9,1.11a yathā somaḥ prātaḥsavane aśvinor bhavati priyaḥ |
9,1.11c evā me aśvinā varca ātmani dhriyatām ||11||

9,1.12a yathā somo dvitīye savana indrāgnyor bhavati priyaḥ |
9,1.12c evā ma indrāgnī varca ātmani dhriyatām ||12||

9,1.13a yathā somas tṛtīye savana ṛbhūṇāṃ bhavati priyaḥ |
9,1.13c evā ma ṛbhavo varca ātmani dhriyatām ||13||

9,1.14a madhu janiṣīya madhu vaṃsiṣīya |
9,1.14c payasvān agna āgamaṃ taṃ mā saṃ sṛja varcasā ||14||

9,1.15a saṃ māgne varcasā sṛja saṃ prajayā sam āyuṣā |
9,1.15c vidyur me asya devā indro vidyāt saha ṛṣibhiḥ ||15||

9,1.16a yathā madhu madhukṛtaḥ saṃbharanti madhāv adhi |
9,1.16c evā me aśvinā varca ātmani dhriyatām ||16||

9,1.17a yathā makṣāḥ idaṃ madhu nyañjanti madhāv adhi |
9,1.17c evā me aśvinā varcas tejo balam ojaś ca dhriyatām ||17||

9,1.18a yad giriṣu parvateṣu goṣv aśveṣu yan madhu |
9,1.18c surāyāṃ sicyamānāyāṃ yat tatra madhu tan mayi ||18||

9,1.19a aśvinā sāragheṇa mā madhunāṅktaṃ śubhas patī |
9,1.19c yathā varcasvatīṃ vācam āvadāni janāṃ anu ||19||

9,1.20a stanayitnus te vāk prajāpate vṛṣā śuṣmaṃ kṣipasi bhūmyāṃ divi |
9,1.20c tāṃ paśava upa jīvanti sarve teno seṣam ūrjaṃ piparti ||20||

9,1.21a pṛthivī daṇḍo 'ntarikṣaṃ garbho dyauḥ kaśā vidyut prakaśo hiraṇyayo binduḥ ||21||

9,1.22a yo vai kaśāyāḥ sapta madhūni veda madhumān bhavati |
9,1.22c brāhmaṇaś ca rājā ca dhenuś cānaḍvāṃś ca vrīhiś ca yavaś ca madhu saptamam ||22||

9,1.23a madhumān bhavati madhumad asyāhāryaṃ bhavati |
9,1.23c madhumato lokān jayati ya evaṃ veda ||23||

9,1.24a yad vīdhre stanayati prajāpatir eva tat prajābhyaḥ prādur bhavati |
9,1.24c tasmāt prācīnopavītas tiṣṭhe prajāpate 'nu mā budhyasveti |
9,1.24e anv enaṃ prajā anu prajāpatir budhyate ya evaṃ veda ||24|| {2}



sapatnahanam ṛṣabhaṃ ghṛtena kāmaṃ śikṣāmi haviṣājyena |
nīcaiḥ sapatnān mama padaya tvam abhiṣṭuto mahatā vīryeṇa ||1||

yan me manaso na priyaṃ cakṣuṣo yan me babhasti nābhinandati |
tad duṣvapnyaṃ prati muñcāmi sapatne kāmaṃ stutvod ahaṃ bhideyam ||2||

duṣvapnyaṃ kāma duritaṃ ca kamāprajastām asvagatām avartim |
ugra īśānaḥ prati muñca tasmin yo asmabhyam aṃhūraṇā cikitsāt ||3||

nudasva kāma pra ṇudasva kāmāvartiṃ yantu mama ye sapatnāḥ |
teṣāṃ nuttānām adhamā tamāṃsy agne vāstūni nir daha tvam ||4||

sā te kāma duhitā dhenur ucyate yām āhur vācaṃ kavayo virājam |
tayā sapatnān pari vṛṅgdhi ye mama pary enān prāṇaḥ paśavo jīvanaṃ vṛṇaktu ||5||

kāmasyendrasya varuṇasya rājño viṣṇor balena savituḥ savena |
agner hotreṇa pra ṇude sapatnāṃ chambīva nāvam udakeṣu dhīraḥ ||6||

adhyakṣo vājī mama kāma ugraḥ kṛṇotu mahyam asapatnam eva |
viśve devā mama nāthaṃ bhavantu sarve devā havam ā yantu ma imam ||7||

idam ājyaṃ ghṛtavaj juṣāṇāḥ kāmajyeṣṭhā iha mādayadhvam |
kṛṇvanto mahyam asapatnam eva ||8||

indrāgnī kāma sarathaṃ hi bhūtvā nīcaiḥ sapatnān mama pādayāthaḥ |
teṣāṃ pannānām adhamā tamāṃsy agne vāstūny anunirdaha tvam ||9||

9,2.10a jahi tvam kāma mama ye sapatnā andhā tamāṃsy ava pādayainān |
9,2.10c nirindriyā arasāḥ santu sarve mā te jīviṣuḥ katamac canāhaḥ ||10|| {3}

9,2.11a avadhīt kāmo mama ye sapatnā uruṃ lokam akaran mahyam edhatum |
9,2.11c mahyaṃ namantāṃ pradiśaś catasro mahyaṃ ṣaḍ urvīr ghṛtam ā vahantu ||11||

9,2.12a te 'dharāñcaḥ pra plavantāṃ chinnā naur iva bandhanāt |
9,2.12c na sāyakapraṇuttānāṃ punar asti nivartanam ||12||

9,2.13a agnir yava indro yavaḥ somo yavaḥ |
9,2.13c yavayāvāno devā yavayantv enam ||13||

9,2.14a asarvavīraś caratu praṇutto dveṣyo mitrānāṃ parivargyaḥ svānām |
9,2.14c uta pṛthivyām ava syanti vidyuta ugro vo devaḥ pra mṛṇat sapatnān ||14||

9,2.15a cyutā ceyaṃ bṛhaty acyutā ca vidyud bibharti stanayitnūṃś ca sarvān |
9,2.15c udyann ādityo draviṇena tejasā nīcaiḥ sapatnān nudatāṃ me sahasvān ||15||

9,2.16a yat te kāma śarma trivarūtham udbhu brahma varma vitatam anativyādhyaṃ kṛtam |
9,2.16c tena sapatnān pari vṛṅgdhi ye mama pary enān prāṇaḥ paśavo jīvanaṃ vṛṇaktu ||16||

9,2.17a yena devā asurān prāṇudanta yenendro dasyūn adhamaṃ tamo nināya |
9,2.17c tena tvaṃ kāma mama ye sapatnās tān asmāl lokāt pra ṇudasva dūram ||17||

9,2.18a yathā devā asurān prāṇudanta yathendro dasyūn adhamaṃ tamo babādhe |
9,2.18c tathā tvaṃ kāma mama ye sapatnās tān asmāl lokāt pra ṇudasva dūram ||18||

9,2.19a kāmo jajñe prathamo nainaṃ devā āpuḥ pitaro na martyāḥ |
9,2.19c tatas tvam asi jyāyān viśvahā mahāṃs tasmai te kāma nama it kṛnomi ||19||

9,2.20a yāvatī dyāvāpṛthivī varimṇā yāvad āpaḥ siṣyadur yāvad agniḥ |
9,2.20c tatas tvam asi jyāyān viśvahā mahāṃs tasmai te kāma nama it kṛṇomi ||20|| {4}

9,2.21a yāvatīr diśaḥ pradiśo viṣūcīr yāvatīr āśā abhicakṣaṇā divaḥ |
9,2.21c tatas tvam asi jyāyān viśvahā mahāṃs tasmai te kāma nama it kṛṇomi ||21||

9,2.22a yāvatīr bhṛṅgā jatvaḥ kurūravo yāvatīr vaghā vṛkṣasarpyo babhūvuḥ |
9,2.22c tatas tvam asi jyāyān viśvahā mahāṃs tasmai te kāma nama it kṛṇomi ||22||

9,2.23a jyāyān nimiṣato 'si tiṣṭhato jyāyānt samudrād asi kāma manyo |
9,2.23c tatas tvam asi jyāyān viśvahā mahāṃs tasmai te kāma nama it kṛnomi ||23||

9,2.24a na vai vātaś cana kāmam āpnoti nāgniḥ sūryo nota candramāḥ |
9,2.24c tatas tvam asi jyāyān viśvahā mahāṃs tasmai te kāma nama it kṛṇomi ||24||

9,2.25a yās te śivās tanvaḥ kāma bhadrā yābhiḥ satyaṃ bhavati yad vṛṇiṣe |
9,2.25c tābhiṣ ṭvam asmāṃ abhisaṃviśasvānyatra pāpīr apa veśayā dhiyaḥ ||25|| {5}


upamitāṃ pratimitām atho parimitām uta |
śālāyā viśvavārāyā naddhāni vi cṛtāmasi ||1||

yat te naddhaṃ viśvavāre pāśo granthiś ca yaḥ kṛtaḥ |
bṛhaspatir ivāhaṃ balaṃ vācā vi sraṃsayāmi tat ||2||

ā yayāma saṃ babarha granthīṃś cakāra te dṛḍhān |
parūṃṣi vidvāṃ chastevendreṇa vi cṛtāmasi ||3||

vaṃśānāṃ te nahanānāṃ prāṇāhasya tṛṇasya ca |
pakṣāṇāṃ viśvavāre te naddhāni vi cṛtāmasi ||4||

saṃdaṃśānāṃ paladānāṃ pariṣvañjalyasya ca |
idaṃ mānasya patnyā naddhāni vi cṛtāmasi ||5||

yāni te 'ntaḥ śikyāny ābedhū raṇyāya kam |
pra te tāni cṛtāmasi śivā mānasya patni na uddhitā tanve bhava ||6||

havirdhānam agniśālaṃ patnīnāṃ sadanaṃ sadaḥ |
sado devānām asi devi śāle ||7||

akṣum opaśaṃ vitataṃ sahasrākṣaṃ viṣūvati |
avanaddham abhihitaṃ brahmaṇā vi cṛtāmasi ||8||

yas tvā śāle pratigṛhṇāti yena cāsi mitā tvam |
ubhau mānasya patni tau jīvatāṃ jaradaṣṭī ||9||

9,3.10a amutrainam ā gachatād dṛḍhā naddhā pariṣkṛtā |
9,3.10c yasyās te vicṛtāmasy aṅgamaṅgaṃ paruṣparuḥ ||10|| {6}

9,3.11a yas tvā śāle nimimāya saṃjabhāra vanaspatīn |
9,3.11c prajāyai cakre tvā śāle parameṣṭhī prajāpatiḥ ||11||

9,3.12a namas tasmai namo dātre śālāpataye ca kṛṇmaḥ |
9,3.12c namo 'gnaye pracarate puruṣāya ca te namaḥ ||12||

9,3.13a gobhyo aśvebhyo namo yac chālāyāṃ vijāyate |
9,3.13c vijāvati prajāvati vi te pāśāṃś cṛtāmasi ||13||

9,3.14a agnim antaś chādayasi puruṣān paśubhiḥ saha |
9,3.14c vijāvati prajāvati vi te pāśāṃś cṛtāmasi ||14||

9,3.15a antarā dyāṃ ca pṛthivīṃ ca yad vyacas tena śālāṃ prati gṛhṇāmi ta imām |
9,3.15c yad antarikṣaṃ rajaso vimānaṃ tat kṛṇve 'ham udaraṃ śevadhibhyaḥ |
9,3.15e tena śālāṃ prati gṛhṇāmi tasmai ||15||

9,3.16a ūrjasvatī payasvatī pṛthivyāṃ nimitā mitā |
9,3.16c viśvānnaṃ bibhratī śāle mā hiṃsīḥ pratigṛhṇataḥ ||16||

9,3.17a tṛṇair āvṛtā paladān vasānā rātrīva śālā jagato niveśanī |
9,3.17c mitā pṛthivyāṃ tiṣṭhasi hastinīva padvatī ||17||

9,3.18a iṭasya te vi cṛtāmy apinaddham aporṇuvan |
9,3.18c varuṇena samubjitāṃ mitraḥ prātar vy ubjatu ||18||

9,3.19a brahmaṇā śālāṃ nimitāṃ kavibhir nimitāṃ mitām |
9,3.19c indrāgnī rakṣatāṃ śālām amṛtau somyaṃ sadaḥ ||19||

9,3.20a kulāye 'dhi kulāyaṃ kośe kośaḥ samubjitaḥ |
9,3.20c tatra marto vi jāyate yasmād viśvaṃ prajāyate ||20|| {7}

9,3.21a yā dvipakṣā catuṣpakṣā ṣaṭpakṣā yā nimīyate |
9,3.21c aṣṭāpakṣāṃ daśapakṣāṃ śālāṃ mānasya patnīm agnir garbha ivā śaye ||21||

9,3.22a pratīcīṃ tvā pratīcīnaḥ śāle praimy ahiṃsatīm |
9,3.22c agnir hy antar āpaś ca ṛtasya prathamā dvāḥ ||22||

9,3.23a imā āpaḥ pra bharāmy ayakṣmā yakṣmanāśanīḥ |
9,3.23c gṛhān upa pra sīdāmy amṛtena sahāgninā ||23||

9,3.24a mā naḥ pāśaṃ prati muco gurur bhāro laghur bhava |
9,3.24c vadhūm iva tvā śāle yatrakāmaṃ bharāmasi ||24||

9,3.25a prācyā diśaḥ śālāyā namo mahimne svāhā devebhyaḥ svāhyebhyaḥ ||25||

9,3.26a dakṣiṇāyā diśaḥ śālāyā namo mahimne svāhā devebhyaḥ svāhyebhyaḥ ||26||

9,3.27a pratīcyā diśaḥ śālāyā namo mahimne svāhā devebhyaḥ svāhyebhyaḥ ||27||

9,3.28a udīcyā diśaḥ śālāyā namo mahimne svāhā devebhyaḥ svāhyebhyaḥ ||28||

9,3.29a dhruvāyā diśaḥ śālāyā namo mahimne svāhā devebhyaḥ svāhyebhyaḥ ||29||

9,3.30a ūrdhvāyā diśaḥ śālāyā namo mahimne svāhā devebhyaḥ svāhyebhyaḥ ||30||

9,3.31a diśodiśaḥ śālāyā namo mahimne svāhā devebhyaḥ svāhyebhyaḥ ||31|| {8}



sāhasras tveṣa ṛṣabhaḥ payasvān viśvā rūpāṇi vakṣaṇāsu bibhrat |
bhadraṃ dātre yajamānāya śīkṣan bārhaspatya usriyas tantum ātān ||1||

apāṃ yo agne pratimā babhūva prabhūḥ sarvasmai pṛthivīva devī |
pitā vatsānāṃ patir aghnyānāṃ sāhasre poṣe api naḥ kṛṇotu ||2||

pumān antarvānt sthaviraḥ payasvān vasoḥ kabandhaṃ ṛṣabho bibharti |
tam indrāya pathibhir devayānair hutam agnir vahatu jātavedāḥ ||3||

pitā vatsānāṃ patir aghnyānāṃ atho pitā mahatāṃ gargarāṇām |
vatso jarāyu pratidhuk pīyūṣa āmikṣā ghṛtaṃ tad v asya retaḥ ||4||

devānāṃ bhāga upanāha eṣo 'pāṃ rasa oṣadhīnāṃ ghṛtasya |
somasya bhakṣam avṛṇīta śakro bṛhann adrir abhavad yac charīram ||5||

somena pūrṇaṃ kalaśaṃ bibharṣi tvastā rupāṇāṃ janitā paśūnām |
śivās te santu prajanva iha yā imā ny asmabhyaṃ svadhite yacha yā amūḥ ||6||

ājaṃ bibharti ghṛtam asya retaḥ sāhasraḥ poṣas tam u yajñam āhuḥ |
indrasya rūpam ṛṣabho vasānaḥ so asmān devāḥ śiva aitu dattaḥ ||7||

indrasyaujo varuṇasya bāhū aśvinor aṃsau marutām iyaṃ kakut |
bṛhaspatiṃ saṃbhṛtam etam āhur ye dhīrāsaḥ kavayo ye manīṣiṇaḥ ||8||

daivīr viśaḥ payasvān ā tanoṣi tvām indraṃ tvāṃ sarasvantam āhuḥ |
sahasraṃ sa ekamukhā dadāti yo brāhmaṇa ṛṣabham ājuhoti ||9||
9,4.10a bṛhaspatiḥ savitā te vayo dadhau tvaṣṭur vāyoḥ pary ātmā ta ābhṛtaḥ |
9,4.10c antarikṣe manasā tvā juhomi barhiṣ ṭe dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe stām ||10|| {9}

9,4.11a ya indra iva deveṣu goṣv eti vivāvadat |
9,4.11c tasya ṛṣabhasyāṅgāni brahmā saṃ stautu bhadrayā ||11||

9,4.12a pārśve āstām anumatyā bhagasyāstām anūvṛjau |
9,4.12c aṣṭhīvantāv abravīn mitro mamaitau kevalāv iti ||12||

9,4.13a bhasad āsīd ādityānāṃ śroṇī āstāṃ bṛhaspateḥ |
9,4.13c puchaṃ vātasya devasya tena dhūnoty oṣadhīḥ ||13||

9,4.14a gudā āsant sinīvālyāḥ sūryāyās tvacam abruvan |
9,4.14c utthātur abruvan pada ṛṣabhaṃ yad akalpayan ||14||

9,4.15a kroḍa āsīj jāmiśaṃsasya somasya klaśo dhṛtaḥ |
9,4.15c devāḥ saṃgatya yat sarva ṛṣabhaṃ vyakalpayan ||15||

9,4.16a te kuṣṭhikāḥ saramāyai kurmebhyo adadhuḥ śaphān |
9,4.16c ūbadhyam asya kītebhyaḥ śvavartebhyo adhārayan ||16||

9,4.17a śṛṅgābhyāṃ rakṣa ṛṣaty avartim hanti cakṣuṣā |
9,4.17c śṛṇoti bhadraṃ karṇābhyāṃ gavāṃ yaḥ patir aghnyaḥ ||17||

9,4.18a śatayājaṃ sa yajate nainaṃ dunvanty agnayaḥ |
9,4.18c jinvanti viśve taṃ devā yo brāhmaṇa ṛṣabham ājuhoti ||18||

9,4.19a brāhmaṇebhya ṛṣabhaṃ dattvā varīyaḥ kṛṇute manaḥ |
9,4.19c puṣṭiṃ so aghnyānāṃ sve goṣṭhe 'va paśyate ||19||

9,4.20a gāvaḥ santu prajāḥ santv atho astu tanūbalam |
9,4.20c tat sarvam anu manyantāṃ devā ṛṣabhadāyine ||20||

9,4.21a ayaṃ pipāna indra id rayiṃ dadhātu cetanīm |
9,4.21c ayaṃ dhenuṃ sudughāṃ nityavatsāṃ vaśaṃ duhāṃ vipaścitaṃ paro divaḥ ||21||

9,4.22a piśaṅgarūpo nabhaso vayodhā aindraḥ śuṣmo viśvarūpo na āgan |
9,4.22c āyur asmabhyaṃ dadhat prajāṃ ca rāyaś ca poṣair abhi naḥ sacatām ||22||

9,4.23a upehopaparcanāsmin goṣṭha upa pṛñca naḥ |
9,4.23c upa ṛṣabhasya yad reta upendra tava vīryam ||23||

9,4.24a etaṃ vo yuvānaṃ prati dadhmo atra tena krīḍantīś carata vaśāṃ anu |
9,4.24c mā no hāsiṣṭa januṣā subhāgā rāyaś ca poṣair abhi naḥ sacadhvam ||24|| {10}



ā nayaitam ā rabhasva sukṛtāṃ lokam api gachatu prajānan |
tīrtvā tamāṃsi bahudhā mahānty ajo nākam ā kramatāṃ tṛtīyam ||1||

indrāya bhāgaṃ pari tvā nayāmy asmin yajñe yajamānāya sūrim |
ye no dviṣanty anu tān rabhasvānāgaso yajamānasya vīrāḥ ||2||

pra pado 'va nenigdhi duścaritaṃ yac cacāra śuddhaiḥ śaphair ā kramatāṃ prajānan |
tīrtvā tamāṃsi bahudhā vipaśyann ajo nākam ā kramatāṃ tṛtīyam ||3||

anuchya śyāmena tvacam etāṃ viśastar yathāparv asinā mābhi maṃsthāḥ |
mābhi druhaḥ paruśaḥ kalpayainaṃ tṛtīye nāke adhi vi śrayainam ||4||

ṛcā kumbhīm adhy agnau śrayāmy ā siñcodakam ava dhehy enam |
paryādhattāgninā śamitāraḥ śṛto gachatu sukṛtāṃ yatra lokaḥ ||5||

ut krāmātaḥ pari ced ataptas taptāc caror adhi nākaṃ tṛtīyam |
agner agnir adhi saṃ babhūvitha jyotiṣmantam abhi lokaṃ jayaitam ||6||

ajo agnir ajam u jyotir āhur ajaṃ jīvatā brahmaṇe deyam āhuḥ |
ajas tamāṃsy apa hanti dūram asmiṃl loke śraddadhānena dattaḥ ||7||

pañcaudanaḥ pañcadhā vi kramatām ākraṃsyamānas trīṇi jyotīṃṣi |
ījānānāṃ sukṛtāṃ prehi madhyaṃ tṛtīye nāke adhi vi śrayasva ||8||

ajā roha sukṛtāṃ yatra lokaḥ śarabho na catto 'ti durgāny eṣaḥ |
pañcaudano brahmaṇe dīyamānaḥ sa dātāraṃ tṛptyā tarpayāti ||9||

9,5.10a ajas trināke tridive tripṛṣṭhe nākasya pṛṣṭhe dadivāṃsaṃ dadhāti |
9,5.10c pañcaudano brahmaṇe dīyamāno viśvarūpā dhenuḥ kāmadughāsy ekā ||10|| {11}

9,5.11a etad vo jyotiḥ pitaras tṛtīyaṃ pañcaudanaṃ brahmaṇe 'jaṃ dadāti |
9,5.11c ajas tamāṃsy apa hanti dūram asmiṃl loke śraddadhānena dattaḥ ||11||

9,5.12a ījānānāṃ sukṛtāṃ lokam īpsan pañcaudanaṃ brahmaṇe 'jaṃ dadāti |
9,5.12c sa vyāptim abhi lokaṃ jayaitaṃ śivo 'smabhyaṃ pratigṛhīto astu ||12||

9,5.13a ajo hy agner ajaniṣṭa śokād vipro viprasya sahaso vipaścit |
9,5.13c iṣṭaṃ pūrtam abhipūrtaṃ vaṣaṭkṛtaṃ tad devā ṛtuśaḥ kalpayantu ||13||

9,5.14a amotaṃ vāso dadyād dhiraṇyam api dakṣiṇām |
9,5.14c tathā lokānt sam āpnoti ye divyā ye ca pārthivāḥ ||14||

9,5.15a etās tvājopa yantu dhārāḥ somyā devīr ghṛtapṛṣṭhā madhuścutaḥ |
9,5.15c stabhān pṛthivīm uta dyāṃ nākasya pṛṣṭhe 'dhi saptaraśmau ||15||

9,5.16a ajo 'sy aja svargo 'si tvayā lokam aṅgirasaḥ prājānan |
9,5.16c taṃ lokaṃ puṇyaṃ pra jñeṣam ||16||

9,5.17a yenā sahasraṃ vahasi yenāgne sarvavedasam |
9,5.17c tenemaṃ yajñaṃ no vaha svar deveṣu gantave ||17||

9,5.18a ajaḥ pakvaḥ svarge loke dadhāti pañcaudano nirṛtiṃ bādhamānaḥ |
9,5.18c tena lokānt sūryavato jayema ||18||

9,5.19a yaṃ brāhmaṇe nidadhe yaṃ ca vikṣu yā vipruṣa odanānām ajasya |
9,5.19c sarvaṃ tad agne sukṛtasya loke jānītān naḥ saṃgamane pathīnām ||19||

9,5.20a ajo vā idam agne vy akramata tasyora iyam abhavad dyauḥ pṛṣṭiham |
9,5.20c antarikṣaṃ madhyam diśaḥ pārśve samudrau kukṣī ||20|| {12}

9,5.21a satyaṃ ca rtaṃ ca cakṣuṣī viśvaṃ satyaṃ śraddhā prāṇo virāṭ śiraḥ |
9,5.21c eṣa vā aparimito yajño yad ajaḥ pañcaudanaḥ ||21||

9,5.22a aparimitam eva yajñam āpnoty aparimitaṃ lokam ava runddhe |
9,5.22c yo 'jaṃ pañcaudanaṃ dakṣiṇājyotiṣaṃ dadāti ||22||

9,5.23a nāsyāsthīni bhindyān na majjño nir dhayet |
9,5.23c sarvam enaṃ samādāyedamidaṃ pra veśayet ||23||

9,5.24a idamidam evāsya rūpaṃ bhavati tenainaṃ saṃ gamayati |
9,5.24c iṣaṃ maha ūrjam asmai duhe yo 'jaṃ pañcaudanam dakṣiṇājyotiṣaṃ dadāti ||24||

9,5.25a pañca rukmā pañca navāni vastrā pañcāsmai dhenavaḥ kāmadughā bhavanti |
9,5.25c yo 'jaṃ pañcaudanaṃ dakṣiṇājyotiṣaṃ dadāti ||25||

9,5.26a pañca rukmā jyotir asmai bhavanti varma vāsāṃsi tanve bhavanti |
9,5.26c svargaṃ lokam aśnute yo 'jaṃ pañcaudanaṃ dakṣiṇājyotiṣam dadāti ||26||

9,5.27a yā pūrvaṃ patiṃ vittvā 'thānyaṃ vindate 'param |
9,5.27c pañcaudanaṃ ca tāv ajaṃ dadāto na vi yoṣataḥ ||27||

9,5.28a samānaloko bhavati punarbhuvāparaḥ patiḥ |
9,5.28c yo 'jaṃ pañcaudanam dakṣiṇājyotiṣaṃ dadāti ||28||

9,5.29a anupūrvavatsāṃ dhenum anaḍvāham upabarhaṇam |
9,5.29c vāso hiraṇyaṃ dattvā te yanti divam uttamām ||29||

9,5.30a ātmānaṃ pitaraṃ putraṃ pautraṃ pitāmaham |
9,5.30c jāyāṃ janitrīṃ mātaraṃ ye priyās tān upa hvaye ||30|| {13}

9,5.31a yo vai naidāghaṃ nāma rtuṃ veda |
9,5.31c eṣa vai naidāgho nāma rtur yad ajaḥ pañcaudanaḥ |
9,5.31e nir evāpriyasya bhrātṛvyasya śriyaṃ dahati bhavaty ātmanā |

9,5.32a yo vai kurvantaṃ nāma rtuṃ veda |
9,5.32c kurvatīṃkurvatīm evāpriyasya bhrātṛvyasya śriyaṃ ā datte |
9,5.32e eṣa vai kurvan nāma rtur yad ajaḥ pañcaudanaḥ |

9,5.33a yo vai saṃyantaṃ nāma rtuṃ veda |
9,5.33c saṃyatīṃsaṃyatīm evāpriyasya bhrātṛvyasya śriyaṃ ā datte |
9,5.33e eṣa vai saṃyan nāma rtur yad ajaḥ pañcaudanaḥ |

9,5.34a yo vai pinvantaṃ nāma rtum veda |
9,5.34c pinvatīṃpinvatīm evāpriyasya bhrātṛvyasya śriyaṃ ā datte |
9,5.34e eṣa vai pinvan nāma rtur yad ajaḥ pañcaudanaḥ |

9,5.35a yo vā udyantaṃ nāma rtuṃ veda |
9,5.35c udyatīṃudyatīm evāpriyasya bhrātṛvyasya śriyaṃ ā datte |
9,5.35e eṣa vā udyann nāma rtur yad ajaḥ pañcaudanaḥ |

9,5.36a yo vā abhibhuvaṃ nāma rtuṃ veda |
9,5.36c abhibhavantīmabhibhavantīm evāpriyasya bhrātṛvyasya śriyaṃ ā datte |
9,5.36e eṣa vā abhibhūr nāma rtur yad ajaḥ pañcaudanaḥ |

9,5.37a ajaṃ ca pacata pañca caudanān |
9,5.37c sarvā diśaḥ saṃmanasaḥ sadhrīcīḥ sāntardeśāḥ prati gṛhnantu ta etam ||37||

9,5.38a tās te rakṣantu tava tubhyam etaṃ tābhya ājyaṃ havir idaṃ juhomi ||38|| {14}



yo vidyād brahma pratyakṣaṃ parūṃṣi yasya saṃbhārā ṛco yasyānūkyam ||1||

sāmāni yasya lomāni yajur hṛdayam ucyate paristaraṇam id dhaviḥ ||2||

yad vā atithipatir atithīn pratipaśyati devayajanaṃ prekṣate ||3||

yad abhivadati dīkṣām upaiti yad udakaṃ yācaty apaḥ pra ṇayati ||4||

yā eva yajña āpaḥ praṇīyante tā eva tāḥ ||5||

yat tarpaṇam āharanti ya evāgnīṣomīyaḥ paśur badhyate sa eva saḥ ||6||

yad āvasathān kalpayanti sadohavirdhānāny eva tat kalpayanti ||7||

yad upastṛṇanti barhir eva tat ||8||

yad upariśayanam āharanti svargam eva tena lokam ava runddhe ||9||

9,6.10a yat kaśipūpabarhaṇam āharanti paridhaya eva te ||10||

9,6.11a yad āñjanābhyañjanam āharanty ājyam eva tat ||11||

9,6.12a yat purā pariveṣāt svādam āharanti purodāśāv eva tau ||12||

9,6.13a yad aśanakṛtaṃ hvayanti haviṣkṛtam eva tad dhvayanti ||13||

9,6.14a ye vrīhayo yavā nirupyante 'ṃśava eva te ||14||

9,6.15a yāny ulūkhalamusalāni grāvāṇa eva te ||15||

9,6.16a śūrpaṃ pavitraṃ tuṣā ṛjīṣābhiṣavaṇīr āpaḥ ||16||

9,6.17a srug darvir nekṣaṇam āyavanaṃ droṇakalaśāḥ kumbhyo vāyavyāni pātrāṇīyam eva kṛṣṇājinam ||17|| {15}

9,6.18a yajamānabrāhmaṇaṃ vā etad atithipatiḥ kurute yad āhāryāṇi prekṣata idaṃ bhūyā3 idā3m iti ||18||

9,6.19a yad āha bhūya ud dhareti prāṇam eva tena varṣīyāṃsaṃ kurute ||19||

9,6.20a upa harati havīṃṣy ā sādayati ||20||

9,6.21a teṣām āsannānām atithir ātman juhoti ||21||

9,6.22a srucā hastena prāṇe yūpe srukkāreṇa vaṣaṭkāreṇa ||22||

9,6.23a ete vai priyāś cāpriyāś ca rtvijaḥ svargaṃ lokaṃ gamayanti yad atithayaḥ ||23||

9,6.24a sa ya evaṃ vidvān na dviṣann aśnīyān na dviṣato 'nnam aśnīyān na mīmāṃsitasya na mīmāṃsamānasya ||24||

9,6.25a sarvo vā eṣa jagdhapāpmā yasyānnam aśnanti ||25||

9,6.26a sarvo vā eso 'jagdhapāpmā yasyānnam nāśnanti ||26||

9,6.27a sarvadā vā eṣa yuktagrāvārdrapavitro vitatādhvara āhṛtayajñakratur ya upaharati ||27||

9,6.28a prājāpatyo vā etasya yajño vitato ya upaharati ||28||

9,6.29a prajāpater vā eṣa vikramān anuvikramate ya upaharati ||29||

9,6.30a yo 'tithīnāṃ sa āhavanīyo yo veśmani sa gārhapatyo yasmin pacanti sa dakṣiṇāgniḥ ||30|| {16}

9,6.31a iṣṭaṃ ca vā eṣa pūrtaṃ ca gṛhāṇām aśnāti yaḥ pūrvo 'tither aśnāti ||31||

9,6.32a payaś ca vā eṣa rasaṃ ca gṛhāṇām aśnāti yaḥ pūrvo 'tither aśnāti ||32||

9,6.33a ūrjāṃ ca vā eṣa sphātiṃ ca gṛhāṇām aśnāti yaḥ pūrvo 'tither aśnāti ||33||

9,6.34a prajāṃ vā eṣa paśūṃś ca gṛhāṇām aśnāti yaḥ pūrvo 'tither aśnāti ||34||

9,6.35a kīrtiṃ vā eṣa yaśaś ca gṛhāṇām aśnāti yaḥ pūrvo 'tither aśnāti ||35||

9,6.36a śriyaṃ vā eṣa saṃvidaṃ ca gṛhāṇām aśnāti yaḥ pūrvo 'tither aśnāti ||36||

9,6.37a eṣa vā atithir yac chrotriyas tasmāt pūrvo nāśnīyāt ||37||

9,6.38a aśitāvaty atithāv aśnīyād yajñasya sātmatvāya yajñasyāvichedāya tad vratam ||38||

9,6.39a etad vā u svādīyo yad adhigavaṃ kṣīraṃ vā māṃsaṃ vā tad eva nāśnīyāt ||39|| {17}

9,6.40a sa ya evaṃ vidvān kṣīram upasicyopaharati |
9,6.40c yāvad agniṣṭomeneṣṭvā susamṛddhenāvarunddhe tāvad enenāva runddhe ||40||

9,6.41a sa ya evaṃ vidvānt sarpir upasicyopaharati |
9,6.41c yāvad atirātreṇeṣṭvā susamṛddhenāvarunddhe tāvad enenāva runddhe ||41||

9,6.42a sa ya evaṃ vidvān madhūpasicyopaharati |
9,6.42c yāvad sattrasadyeneṣṭvā susamṛddhenāvarunddhe tāvad enenāva runddhe ||42||

9,6.43a sa ya evaṃ vidvān māṃsam upasicyopaharati |
9,6.43c yāvad dvādaśāheneṣṭvā susamṛddhenāvarunddhe tāvad enenāva runddhe ||43||

9,6.44a sa ya evaṃ vidvān udakam upasicyopaharati |
9,6.44c prajānāṃ prajananāya gachati pratiṣṭhāṃ priyaḥ prajānāṃ bhavati ya evaṃ vidvān upasicyopaharati ||44|| {18}

9,6.45a tasmā uṣā hiṅ kṛṇoti savitā pra stauti |
9,6.45c bṛhaspatir ūrjayod gāyati tvaṣṭā puṣṭyā prati harati viśve devā nidhanam ||2||
9,6.45e nidhanaṃ bhūtyāḥ prajāyāḥ paśūnāṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||45||

9,6.46a tasmā udyant sūryo hiṅ kṛṇoti saṃgavaḥ pra stauti |
9,6.46c madhyandina ud gāyaty aparāhṇaḥ prati haraty astaṃyan nidhanam |
9,6.46e nidhanaṃ bhūtyāḥ prajāyāḥ paśūnāṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||46||

9,6.47a tasmā abhro bhavan hiṅ kṛṇoti stanayan pra stauti |
9,6.47c vidyotamānaḥ prati harati varṣann ud gāyaty udgṛhṇan nidhanam |
9,6.47e nidhanaṃ bhūtyāḥ prajāyāḥ paśūnāṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||47||

9,6.48a atithīn prati paśyati hiṅ kṛṇoty abhi vadati pra stauty udakam yācaty ud gāyati |
9,6.48c upa harati prati haraty ucchiṣṭaṃ nidhanam |
9,6.48e nidhanaṃ bhūtyāḥ prajāyāḥ paśūnāṃ bhavati ya evam veda ||48|| {19}
9,6.48a yat kṣattāraṃ hvayaty ā śrāvayaty eva tat ||49||

9,6.50a yat pratiśṛṇoti pratyāśrāvayaty eva tat ||50||

9,6.51a yat pariveṣṭāraḥ pātrahastāḥ pūrve cāpare ca prapadyante camasādhvaryava eva te ||51||

9,6.52a teṣāṃ na kaś canāhotā ||52||

9,6.53a yad vā atithipatir atithīn pariviṣya gṛhān upodaity avabhṛtham eva tad upāvaiti ||53||

9,6.54a yat sabhāgayati dakṣiṇāḥ sabhāgayati yad anutiṣṭhata udavasyaty eva tat ||54||

9,6.55a sa upahūtaḥ pṛthivyāṃ bhakṣayaty upahūtas tasmin yat pṛthivyāṃ viśvarūpam ||55||

9,6.56a sa upahūto 'ntarikṣe bhakṣayaty upahūtas tasmin yad divi viśvarūpam ||56||

9,6.57a sa upahūto divi bhakṣayaty upahūtas tasmin yad divi viśvarūpam ||57||

9,6.58a sa upahūto deveṣu bhakṣayaty upahūtas tasmin yad divi viśvarūpam ||58||

9,6.59a sa upahūto lokeṣu bhakṣayaty upahūtas tasmin yad divi viśvarūpam ||59||

9,6.60a sa upahūta upahūtaḥ ||60||

9,6.61a āpnotīmaṃ lokam āpnoty amum ||61||

9,6.62a jyotiṣmato lokān jayati ya evaṃ veda ||62|| {20}



prajāpatiś ca parameṣṭhī ca śṛṅge indraḥ śiro agnir lalāṭaṃ yamaḥ kṛkāṭam ||1||

somo rājā mastiṣko dyaur uttarahanuḥ pṛthivy adharahanuḥ ||2||

vidyuj jihvā maruto dantā revatir grīvāḥ kṛttikā skandhā gharmo vahaḥ ||3||

viśvaṃ vāyuḥ svargo lokaḥ kṛṣṇadraṃ vidharaṇī niveṣyaḥ ||4||

śyenaḥ kroto 'ntarikṣaṃ pājasyaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ kakud bṛhatīḥ kīkasāḥ ||5||

devānāṃ patnīḥ pṛṣṭaya upasadaḥ parśavaḥ ||6||

mitraś ca varuṇaś cāṃsau tvaṣṭā cāryamā ca doṣaṇī mahādevo bāhū ||7||

indrāṇī bhasad vāyuḥ puchaṃ pavamāno bālāḥ ||8||

brahma ca kṣatraṃ ca śroṇī balam ūrū ||9||

9,7.10a dhātā ca savitā cāṣṭhīvantau jaṅghā gandharvā apsarasaḥ kuṣṭhikā aditiḥ śaphāḥ ||10||

9,7.11a ceto hṛdayaṃ yakṛn medhā vrataṃ purītat ||11||

9,7.12a kṣut kukṣir irā vaniṣṭhuḥ parvatāḥ plāśayaḥ ||12||

9,7.13a krodho vṛkkau manyur āṇḍau prajā śepaḥ ||13||

9,7.14a nadī sūtrī varṣasya pataya stanā stanayitnur ūdhaḥ ||14||

9,7.15a viśvavyacās carmauṣadhayo lomāni nakṣatrāṇi rūpam ||15||

9,7.16a devajanā gudā manuṣyā āntrāṇy atrā udaram ||16||

9,7.17a rakṣāṃsi lohitam itarajanā ūbadhyam ||17||

9,7.18a abhraṃ pībo majjā nidhanam ||18||

9,7.19a agnir āsīna utthito 'śvinā ||19||

9,7.20a indraḥ prāṅ tiṣṭhan dakṣiṇā tiṣṭhan yamaḥ ||20||

9,7.21a pratyaṅ tiṣṭhan dhātodaṅ tiṣṭhant savitā ||21||

9,7.22a tṛṇāni prāptaḥ somo rājā ||22||

9,7.23a mitra īkṣamāṇa āvṛtta ānandaḥ ||23||

9,7.24a yujyamāno vaiśvadevo yuktaḥ prajāpatir vimuktaḥ sarvam ||24||

9,7.25a etad vai viśvarūpaṃ sarvarūpaṃ gorūpam ||25||

9,7.26a upainaṃ viśvarūpāḥ sarvarūpāḥ paśavas tiṣṭhanti ya evaṃ veda ||26|| {21}



śīrṣaktiṃ śīrṣāmayaṃ karṇaśūlaṃ vilohitam |
sarvaṃ śīrṣanyaṃ te rogaṃ bahir nir mantrayāmahe ||1||

karṇābhyāṃ te kaṅkūṣebhyaḥ karṇaśūlaṃ visalpakam |
sarvaṃ śīrṣanyaṃ te rogaṃ bahir nir mantrayāmahe ||2||

yasya hetoḥ pracyavate yakṣmaḥ karṇato āsyataḥ |
sarvaṃ śīrṣanyaṃ te rogaṃ bahir nir mantrayāmahe ||3||
yaḥ kṛṇoti pramotam andhaṃ kṛṇoti pūruṣam |
sarvaṃ śīrṣanyaṃ te rogaṃ bahir nir mantrayāmahe ||4||

aṅgabhedam aṅgajvaram viśvāṅgyaṃ visalpakam |
sarvaṃ śīrṣanyaṃ te rogaṃ bahir nir mantrayāmahe ||5||

yasya bhīmaḥ pratīkāśa udvepayati pūruṣam |
takmānaṃ viśvaśāradaṃ bahir nir mantrayāmahe ||6||

ya ūrū anusarpaty atho eti gavīnike |
yakṣmaṃ te antar aṅgebhyo bahir nir mantrayāmahe ||7||

yadi kāmād apakāmād dhṛdayāj jāyate pari |
hṛdo balāsam aṅgebhyo bahir nir mantrayāmahe ||8||

harimāṇaṃ te aṅgebhyo 'pvām antarodarāt |
yakṣmodhām antar ātmano bahir nir mantrayāmahe ||9||

9,8.10a āso balāso bhavatu mūtraṃ bhavatv āmayat |
9,8.10c yakṣmāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ viṣaṃ nir avocam ahaṃ tvat ||10|| {22}

9,8.11a bahir bilaṃ nir dravatu kāhābāhaṃ tavodarāt |
9,8.11c yakṣmāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ viṣaṃ nir avocam ahaṃ tvat ||11||

9,8.12a udarāt te klomno nābhyā hṛdayād adhi |
9,8.12c yakṣmāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ viṣaṃ nir avocam ahaṃ tvat ||12||

9,8.13a yāḥ sīmānaṃ virujanti mūrdhānaṃ praty arṣanīḥ |
9,8.13c ahiṃsantīr anāmayā nir dravantu bahir bilam ||13||

9,8.14a yā hṛdayam uparṣanty anutanvanti kīkasāḥ |
9,8.14c ahiṃsantīr anāmayā nir dravantu bahir bilam ||14||

9,8.15a yāḥ pārśve uparṣanty anunikṣanti pṛṣṭīḥ |
9,8.15c ahiṃsantīr anāmayā nir dravantu bahir bilam ||15||

9,8.16a yās tiraścīḥ uparṣanty arṣaṇīr vakṣaṇāsu te |
9,8.16c ahiṃsantīr anāmayā nir dravantu bahir bilam ||16||

9,8.17a yā gudā anusarpanty āntrāṇi mohayanti ca |
9,8.17c ahiṃsantīr anāmayā nir dravantu bahir bilam ||17||

9,8.18a yā majjño nirdhayanti parūṃṣi virujanti ca |
9,8.18c ahiṃsantīr anāmayā nir dravantu bahir bilam ||18||

9,8.19a ye aṅgāni madayanti yakṣmāso ropaṇās tava |
9,8.19c yakṣmāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ viṣaṃ nir avocam ahaṃ tvat ||19||

9,8.20a visalpasya vidradhasya vātīkārasya vālajeḥ |
9,8.20c yakṣmāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ viṣaṃ nir avocam ahaṃ tvat ||20||

9,8.21a pādābhyāṃ te jānubhyāṃ śroṇibhyāṃ pari bhaṃsasaḥ |
9,8.21c anūkād arṣaṇīr uṣṇihābhyaḥ śīrṣṇo rogam anīnaśam ||21||

9,8.22a saṃ te śīrṣṇaḥ kapālāni hṛdayasya ca yo vidhuḥ |
9,8.22c udyann āditya raśmibhiḥ śīrṣṇo rogam anīnaśo 'ṅgabhedam aśīśamaḥ ||22|| {23}



asya vāmasya palitasya hotus tasya bhrātā madhyamo asty aśnaḥ |
tṛtīyo bhrātā ghṛtapṛṣṭho asyātrāpaśyaṃ viśpatiṃ saptaputram ||1||

sapta yuñjanti ratham ekacakram eko aśvo vahati saptanāmā |
trinābhi cakram ajaram anarvaṃ yatremā viśvā bhuvanādhi tasthuḥ ||2||

imaṃ ratham adhi ye sapta tasthuḥ saptacakraṃ sapta vahanty aśvāḥ |
sapta svasāro abhi saṃ navanta yatra gavām nihitā sapta nāma ||3||

ko dadarśa prathamaṃ jāyamānam asthanvantaṃ yad anasthā bibharti |
bhūmyā asur asṛg ātmā kva svit ko vidvāṃsam upa gāt praṣṭum etat ||4||

iha bravītu ya īm aṅga vedāsya vāmasya nihitaṃ padaṃ veḥ |
śīrṣṇaḥ kṣīraṃ duhrate gāvo asya vavriṃ vasānā udakaṃ padā 'puḥ ||5||

pākaḥ pṛchāmi manasā 'vijānan devānām enā nihitā padāni |
vatse baṣkaye 'dhi sapta tantūn vi tatnire kavaya otavā u ||6||

acikitvāṃs cikituṣaś cid atra kavīn pṛchāmi vidvano na vidvān |
vi yas tastambha ṣaṭ imā rajāṃsy ajasya rūpe kiṃ api svid ekam ||7||

mātā pitaram ṛta ā babhāja 'dhīty agre manasā saṃ hi jagme |
sā bībhatsur garbharasā nividdhā namasvanta id upavākam īyuḥ ||8||

yuktā mātāsid dhuri dakṣiṇāyā atiṣṭhad garbho vṛjanīṣv antaḥ |
amīmed vatso anu gām apaśyad viśvarūpyaṃ triṣu yoganeṣu ||9||

9,9.10a tisro matṝs trīn pitṝn bibhrad eka urdhvas tasthau nem ava glāpayanta |
9,9.10c mantrayante divo amuṣya pṛṣṭhe viśvavido vācam aviśvavinnām ||10|| {24}

9,9.11a pañcāre cakre parivartamāne yasminn ātasthur bhuvanāni viśvā |
9,9.11c tasya nākṣas tapyate bhūribhāraḥ sanād eva na chidyate sanābhiḥ ||11||

9,9.12a pañcapādaṃ pitaraṃ dvādaśākṛtiṃ diva āhuḥ pare ardhe purīṣiṇam |
9,9.12c atheme anya upare vicakṣaṇe saptacakre ṣaḍara āhur arpitam ||12||

9,9.13a dvādaśāraṃ nahi taj jarāya varvarti cakraṃ pari dyām ṛtasya |
9,9.13c ā putrā agne mithunāso atra sapta śatāni viṃśatiś ca tasthuḥ ||13||

9,9.14a sanemi cakram ajaraṃ vi vavṛta uttānāyāṃ daśa yuktā vahanti |
9,9.14c sūryasya cakṣū rajasaity āvṛtaṃ yasminn ātasthur bhuvanāni viśvā ||14||

9,9.15a striyaḥ satīs tām u me puṃsaḥ āhuḥ paśyad akṣaṇvānn vi cetad andhaḥ |
9,9.15c kavir yaḥ putraḥ sa īm ā ciketa yas tā vijānāt sa pituṣ pitāsat ||15||

9,9.16a sākaṃjānāṃ saptatham āhur ekajaṃ ṣaḍ id yamā ṛṣayo devajā iti |
9,9.16c teṣām iṣṭāni vihitāni dhāmaśa sthātre rejante vikṛtāni rūpaśaḥ ||16||

9,9.17a avaḥ pareṇa para enā avareṇa padā vatsaṃ bibhratī gaur ud asthāt |
9,9.17c sā kadrīcī kaṃ svid ardhaṃ parāgāt kva svit sūte nahi yūthe asmin ||17||

9,9.18a avaḥ pareṇa pitaraṃ yo asya vedāvaḥ pareṇa para enāvareṇa |
9,9.18c kavīyamānaḥ ka iha pra vocad devaṃ manaḥ kuto adhi prajātam ||18||

9,9.19a ye arvāñcas tām u parāca āhur ye parāñcas tāṃ u arvāca āhuḥ |
9,9.19c indraś ca yā cakrathuḥ soma tāni dhurā na yuktā rajaso vahanti ||19||

9,9.20a dvā suparṇā sayujā sakhāyā samānaṃ vṛkṣaṃ pari ṣasvajāte |
9,9.20c tayor anyaḥ pippalaṃ svādv atty anaśnann anyo abhi cākaśīti ||20||

9,9.21a yasmin vṛkṣe madhvadaḥ suparṇā niviśante suvate cādhi viśve |
9,9.21c tasya yad āhuḥ pippalaṃ svādv agre tan non naśad yaḥ pitaraṃ na veda ||21||

9,9.22a yatrā suparṇā amṛtasya bhakṣam animeṣaṃ vidathābhisvaranti |
9,9.22c enā viśvasya bhuvanasya gopāḥ sa mā dhīraḥ pākam atrā viveśa ||22|| {25}



yad gāyatre adhi gāyatram āhitaṃ traiṣṭubhaṃ vā traiṣṭubhān niratakṣata |
yad vā jagaj jagaty āhitaṃ padaṃ ya it tad vidus te amṛtatvam ānuśuḥ ||1||

gāyatreṇa prati mimīte arkam arkeṇa sāma traiṣṭubhena vākam |
vākena vākaṃ dvipadā catuṣpadākṣareṇa mimate sapta vāṇīḥ ||2||

jagatā sindhuṃ divy askabhāyad rathaṃtare sūryaṃ pary apaśyat |
gāyatrasya samidhas tisra āhus tato mahnā pra ririce mahitvā ||3||

upa hvaye sudughāṃ dhenum etāṃ suhasto godhug uta dohad enām |
śreṣṭhaṃ savaṃ savitā sāviṣan no 'bhīddho gharmas tad u ṣu pra vocat ||4||

hiṅkṛṇvatī vasupatnī vasūnāṃ vatsam ichantī manasābhyāgāt |
duhām aśvibhyāṃ payo aghnyeyaṃ sā vardhatāṃ mahate saubhagāya ||5||

gaur amīmed abhi vatsaṃ miṣantaṃ mūrdhānaṃ hiṅṅ akṛṇon mātavā u |
sṛkvāṇaṃ gharmam abhi vāvaśānā mimāti māyuṃ payate payobhiḥ ||6||

ayaṃ sa śiṅkte yena gaur abhivṛtā mimāti mayuṃ dhvasanāv adhi śritā |
sā cittibhir ni hi cakāra martyān vidyud bhavantī prati vavrim auhata ||7||

anac chaye turagātu jīvam ejad dhruvaṃ madhya ā pastyānām |
jīvo mṛtasya carati svadhābhir amartyo martyenā sayoniḥ ||8||

vidhuṃ dadrāṇaṃ salilasya pṛṣṭhe yuvānaṃ santaṃ palito jagāra |
devasya paśya kāvyaṃ mahitvādya mamāra sa hyaḥ sam āna ||9||

9,10.10a ya īṃ cakāra na so asya veda ya īṃ dadarśa hirug in nu tasmāt |
9,10.10c sa mātur yonā parivīto antar bahuprajā nirṛtir ā viveśa ||10|| {26}

9,10.11a apaśyaṃ gopām anipadyamānam ā ca parā ca pathibhiś carantam |
9,10.11c sa sadhrīcīḥ sa viṣūcīr vasāna ā varīvarti bhuvaneṣv antaḥ ||11||

9,10.12a dyaur naḥ pitā janitā nābhir atra bandhur no mātā pṛthivī mahīyam |
9,10.12c uttānayoś camvor yonir antar atrā pitā duhitur garbham ādhāt ||12||

9,10.13a pṛchāmi tvā param antaṃ pṛthivyāḥ pṛchāmi vṛṣṇo aśvasya retaḥ |
9,10.13c pṛchāmi viśvasya bhuvanasya nābhiṃ pṛchāmi vācaḥ paramaṃ vyoma ||13||
9,10.14a iyaṃ vediḥ paro antaḥ pṛthivyā ayaṃ somo vṛṣṇo aśvasya retaḥ |
9,10.14c ayaṃ yajño viśvasya bhuvanasya nābhir brahmāyaṃ vācaḥ paramaṃ vyoma ||14||
9,10.15a na vi jānāmi yad ivedam asmi niṇyaḥ saṃnaddho manasā carāmi |
9,10.15c yadā māgan prathamajā ṛtasyād id vāco aśnuve bhāgam asyāḥ ||15||

9,10.16a apāṅ prāṅ eti svadhayā gṛbhīto 'martyo martyenā sayoniḥ |
9,10.16c tā śaśvantā viṣūcīnā viyantā ny anyaṃ cikyur na ni cikyur anyam ||16||

9,10.17a saptārdhagarbhā bhuvanasya reto viṣṇos tiṣṭhanti pradiśā vidharmaṇi |
9,10.17c te dhītibhir manasā te vipaścitaḥ paribhuvaḥ pari bhavanti viśvataḥ ||17||

9,10.18a ṛco akṣare parame vyoman yasmin devā adhi viśve niṣeduḥ |
9,10.18c yas tan na veda kim ṛcā kariṣyati ya it tad vidus te amī sam āsate ||18||

9,10.19a ṛcaḥ padaṃ mātrayā kalpayanto 'rdharcena cakḷpur viśvam ejat |
9,10.19c tripād brahma pururūpaṃ vi taṣṭhe tena jīvanti pradiśaś catasraḥ ||19||

9,10.20a sūyavasād bhagavatī hi bhūyā adhā vayaṃ bhagavantaḥ syāma |
9,10.20c addhi tṛṇam aghnye viśvadānīṃ piba śuddham udakam ācarantī ||20|| {27}

9,10.21a gaur in mimāya salilāni takṣatī ekapadī dvipadī sā catuṣpadī |
9,10.21c aṣṭāpadī navapadī babhūvuṣī sahasrākṣarā bhuvanasya paṅktis tasyāḥ samudrā adhi vi kṣaranti ||21||

9,10.22a kṛṣṇaṃ niyānaṃ harayaḥ suparṇā apo vasānā divam ut patanti |
9,10.22c taṃ āvavṛtrant sadanād ṛtasyād id ghṛtena pṛthivīṃ vy ūduḥ ||22||

9,10.23a apād eti prathamā padvatīnāṃ kas tad vāṃ mitrāvaruṇā ciketa |
9,10.23c garbho bhāraṃ bharaty ā cid asyā ṛtaṃ piparti anṛtaṃ ni pāti ||23||

9,10.24a virāḍ vāg virāṭ pṛthivī virāḍ antarikṣaṃ virāṭ prajāpatiḥ |
9,10.24c virāṇ mṛtyuḥ sādhyānām adhirājo babhūva tasya bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ vaśe sa me bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ vaśe kṛṇotu ||24||

9,10.25a śakamayaṃ dhūmam ārād apaśyaṃ viṣūvatā para enāvareṇa |
9,10.25c ukṣāṇaṃ pṛśnim apacanta vīrās tāni dharmāṇi prathamāny āsan ||25||

9,10.26a trayaḥ keśina ṛtuthā vi cakṣate saṃvatsare vapata eka eṣām |
9,10.26c viśvam anyo abhicaṣṭe śacībhir dhrājir ekasya dadṛśe na rūpam ||26||

9,10.27a catvāri vāk parimitā padāni tāni vidur brāhmaṇā ye manīṣiṇaḥ |
9,10.27c guhā trīṇi nihitā neṅgayanti turīyaṃ vāco manuṣyā vadanti ||27||

9,10.28a indraṃ mitraṃ varuṇam agnim āhur atho divyaḥ sa suparṇo garutmān |
9,10.28c ekaṃ sad viprā bahudhā vadanty agniṃ yamaṃ mātariśvānam āhuḥ ||28|| {28}



1yāṃ kalpayanti vahatau vadhūm iva viśvarūpāṃ hastakṛtāṃ cikitsavaḥ |
1sārād etv apa nudāma enām ||1||

1śīrṣaṇvatī nasvatī karṇiṇī kṛtyākṛtā saṃbhṛtā viśvarūpā |
1sārād etv apa nudāma enām ||2||

1śūdrakṛtā rājakṛtā strīkṛtā brahmabhiḥ kṛtā |
1jāyā patyā nutteva kartāraṃ bandhv ṛchatu ||3||

1anayāham oṣadhyā sarvāḥ kṛtyā adūduṣam |
1yāṃ kṣetre cakrur yāṃ goṣu yāṃ vā te puruṣeṣu ||4||

1agham astv aghakṛte śapathaḥ śapathīyate |
1pratyak pratiprahiṇmo yathā kṛtyākṛtaṃ hanat ||5||

1pratīcīna āṅgiraso 'dhyakṣo naḥ purohitaḥ |
1pratīcīḥ kṛtyā ākṛtyāmūn kṛtyākṛto jahi ||6||

1yas tvovāca parehīti pratikūlam udāyyam |
1taṃ kṛtye 'bhinivartasva māsmān icho anāgasaḥ ||7||

1yas te parūṃṣi saṃdadhau rathasyeva rbhur dhiyā |
1taṃ gacha tatra te 'yanam ajñātas te 'yaṃ janaḥ ||8||

1ye tvā kṛtvālebhire vidvalā abhicāriṇaḥ |
1śaṃbhv idaṃ kṛtyādūṣaṇaṃ prativartma punaḥsaraṃ tena tvā snapayāmasi ||9||

10,1.10a yad durbhagāṃ prasnapitāṃ mṛtavatsām upeyima |
10,1.10c apaitu sarvaṃ mat pāpaṃ draviṇaṃ mopa tiṣṭhatu ||10|| {1}

10,1.11a yat te pitṛbhyo dadato yajñe vā nāma jagṛhuḥ |
10,1.11c saṃdeśyāt sarvasmāt pāpād imā muñcantu tvauṣadhīḥ ||11||

10,1.12a devainasāt pitryān nāmagrāhāt saṃdeśyād abhiniṣkṛtāt |
10,1.12c muñcantu tvā vīrudho vīryeṇa brahmaṇā ṛgbhiḥ payasā ṛṣīṇām ||12||

10,1.13a yathā vātaś cyāvayati bhūmyā reṇum antarikṣāc cābhram |
10,1.13c evā mat sarvaṃ durbhūtaṃ brahmanuttam apāyati ||13||

10,1.14a apa krāma nānadatī vinaddhā gardabhīva |
10,1.14c kartṝn nakṣasveto nuttā brahmaṇā vīryāvatā ||14||

10,1.15a ayaṃ panthāḥ kṛtyeti tvā nayāmo 'bhiprahitāṃ prati tvā pra hiṇmaḥ |
10,1.15c tenābhi yāhi bhañjaty anasvatīva vāhinī viśvarūpā kurūtinī ||15||

10,1.16a parāk te jyotir apathaṃ te arvāg anyatrāsmad ayanā kṛṇuṣva |
10,1.16c pareṇehi navatiṃ nāvyā ati durgāḥ srotyā mā kṣaṇiṣṭhāḥ parehi ||16||

10,1.17a vāta iva vṛkṣān ni mṛṇīhi pādaya mā gām aśvaṃ puruṣam uc chiṣa eṣām |
10,1.17c kartṝn nivṛtyetaḥ kṛtye 'prajāstvāya bodhaya ||17||

10,1.18a yāṃ te barhiṣi yāṃ śmaśāne kṣetre kṛtyāṃ valagaṃ vā nicakhnuḥ |
10,1.18c agnau vā tvā gārhapatye 'bhiceruḥ pākaṃ santaṃ dhīratarā anāgasam ||18||

10,1.19a upāhṛtam anubuddhaṃ nikhātaṃ vairaṃ tsāry anv avidāma kartram |
10,1.19c tad etu yata ābhṛtaṃ tatrāśva iva vi vartatāṃ hantu kṛtyākṛtaḥ prajām ||19||

10,1.20a svāyasā asayaḥ santi no gṛhe vidmā te kṛtye yatidhā parūṃṣi |
10,1.20c ut tiṣṭhaiva parehīto 'jñāte kim ihechasi ||20|| {2}

10,1.21a grīvās te kṛtye pādau cāpi kartsyāmi nir drava |
10,1.21c indrāgnī asmān rakṣatāṃ yau prajānāṃ prajāvatī ||21||

10,1.22a somo rājādhipā mṛḍitā ca bhūtasya naḥ patayo mṛḍayantu ||22||

10,1.23a bhavāśarvāv asyatāṃ pāpakṛte kṛtyākṛte |
10,1.23c duṣkṛte vidyutaṃ devahetim ||23||

10,1.24a yady eyatha dvipadī catuṣpadī kṛtyākṛtā saṃbhṛtā viśvarūpā |
10,1.24c seto 'ṣṭāpadī bhūtvā punaḥ parehi duchune ||24||

10,1.25a abhyaktāktā svaraṃkṛtā sarvaṃ bharantī duritaṃ parehi |
10,1.25c jānīhi kṛtye kartāraṃ duhiteva pitaraṃ svam ||25||

10,1.26a parehi kṛtye mā tiṣṭho viddhasyeva padaṃ naya |
10,1.26c mṛgaḥ sa mṛgayus tvaṃ na tvā nikartum arhati ||26||

10,1.27a uta hanti pūrvāsinaṃ pratyādāyāpara iṣvā |
10,1.27c uta pūrvasya nighnato ni hanty aparaḥ prati ||27||

10,1.28a etad dhi śṛṇu me vaco 'thehi yata eyatha |
10,1.28c yas tvā cakāra taṃ prati ||28||

10,1.29a anāgohatyā vai bhīmā kṛtye mā no gām aśvaṃ puruṣaṃ vadhīḥ |
10,1.29c yatrayatrāsi nihitā tatas tvot thāpayāmasi parṇāl laghīyasī bhava ||29||

10,1.30a yadi stha tamasāvṛtā jālenabhihitā iva |
10,1.30c sarvāḥ saṃlupyetaḥ kṛtyāḥ punaḥ kartre pra hiṇmasi ||30||

10,1.31a kṛtyākṛto valagino 'bhiniṣkāriṇaḥ prajām |
10,1.31c mṛṇīhi kṛtye moc chiṣo 'mūn kṛtyākṛto jahi ||31||

10,1.32a yathā sūryo mucyate tamasas pari rātriṃ jahāty uṣasaśca ketūn |
10,1.32c evāhaṃ sarvaṃ durbhūtaṃ kartraṃ kṛtyākṛtā kṛtaṃ hastīva rajo duritaṃ jahāmi ||32|| {3}



1kena pārṣṇī ābhṛte pūruṣasya kena māṃsaṃ saṃbhṛtaṃ kena gulphau |
1kenāṅgulīḥ peśanīḥ kena khāni kenocchlaṅkhau madhyataḥ kaḥ pratiṣṭhām ||1||

1kasmān nu gulphāv adharāv akṛṇvann aṣṭhīvantāv uttarau puruṣasya |
1jaṅghe nirṛtya ny adadhuḥ kva svij jānunoḥ saṃdhī ka u tac ciketa ||2||

1catuṣṭayaṃ yujate saṃhitāntaṃ jānubhyām ūrdhvaṃ śithiraṃ kabandham |
1śroṇī yad ūrū ka u taj jajāna yābhyāṃ kusindhaṃ sudṛḍhaṃ babhūva ||3||

1kati devāḥ katame ta āsan ya uro grīvāś cikyuḥ puruṣasya |
1kati stanau vy adadhuḥ kaḥ kaphodau kati skandhān kati pṛṣṭīr acinvan ||4||

1ko asya bāhū sam abharad vīryāṃ karavād iti |
1aṃsau ko asya tad devaḥ kusindhe adhy ā dadhau ||5||

1kaḥ sapta khāni vi tatarda śīrṣaṇi karṇāv imau nāsike cakṣaṇī mukham |
1yeṣāṃ purutrā vijayasya mahnani catuṣpādo dvipado yanti yāmam ||6||

1hanvor hi jihvām adadhāt purūcīm adhā mahīm adhi śiśrāya vācam |
1sa ā varīvarti bhuvaneṣv antar apo vasānaḥ ka u tac ciketa ||7||

1mastiṣkam asya yatamo lalātaṃ kakāṭikāṃ prathamo yaḥ kapālam |
1citvā cityaṃ hanvoḥ pūruṣasya divaṃ ruroha katamaḥ sa devaḥ ||8||

1priyāpriyāṇi bahulā svapnaṃ saṃbādhatandyaḥ |
1ānandān ugro nandāṃś ca kasmād vahati pūruṣaḥ ||9||

10,2.10a ārtir avartir nirṛtiḥ kuto nu puruṣe 'matiḥ |
10,2.10c rāddhiḥ samṛddhir avyṛddhir matir uditayaḥ kutaḥ ||10|| {4}

10,2.11a ko asminn āpo vy adadhāt viṣūvṛtaḥ purūvṛtaḥ sindhusṛtyāya jātāḥ |
10,2.11c tīvrā aruṇā lohinīs tāmradhūmrā ūrdhvā avācīḥ puruṣe tiraścīḥ ||11||

10,2.12a ko asmin rūpam adadhāt ko mahmānaṃ ca nāma ca |
10,2.12c gātuṃ ko asmin kaḥ ketuṃ kaś caritrāni puruṣe ||12||

10,2.13a ko asmin prāṇaṃ avayat ko apānaṃ vyānam u |
10,2.13c samānam asmin ko devo 'dhi śiśrāya puruṣe ||13||

10,2.14a ko asmin yajñam adadhād eko devo 'dhi puruṣe |
10,2.14c ko asmint satyaṃ ko 'nṛtaṃ kuto mṛtyuḥ kuto 'mṛtam ||14||

10,2.15a ko asmai vāsaḥ pary adadhāt ko asyāyur akalpayat |
10,2.15c balaṃ ko asmai prāyachat ko asyākalpayaj javam ||15||

10,2.16a kenāpo anv atanuta kenāhar akarod ruce |
10,2.16c uṣasaṃ kenānv ainddha kena sāyaṃbhavaṃ dade ||16||

10,2.17a ko asmin reto ny adadhāt tantur ā tāyatām iti |
10,2.17c medhāṃ ko asminn adhy auhat ko bāṇaṃ ko nṛto dadhau ||17||

10,2.18a kenemāṃ bhūmim aurṇot kena pary abhavad divam |
10,2.18c kenābhi mahnā parvatān kena karmāṇi puruṣaḥ ||18||

10,2.19a kena parjanyam anv eti kena somaṃ vicakṣaṇam |
10,2.19c kena yajñam ca śraddhāṃ ca kenāsmin nihitaṃ manaḥ ||19||

10,2.20a kena śrotriyam āpnoti kenemaṃ parameṣṭhinam |
10,2.20c kenemam agniṃ pūruṣaḥ kena saṃvatsaraṃ mame ||20|| {5}

10,2.21a brahma śrotriyam āpnoti brahmemaṃ parameṣṭhinam |
10,2.21c brahmemam agniṃ pūruṣo brahma saṃvatsaraṃ mame ||21||

10,2.22a kena devāṃ anu kṣiyati kena daivajanīr viśaḥ |
10,2.22c kenedam anyan nakṣatraṃ kena sat kṣatram ucyate ||22||

10,2.23a brahma devāṃ anu kṣiyati brahma daivajanīr viśaḥ |
10,2.23c brahmedam anyan nakṣatraṃ brahma sat kṣatram ucyate ||23||

10,2.24a keneyaṃ bhūmir vihitā kena dyaur uttarā hitā |
10,2.24c kenedam ūrdhvaṃ tiryak cāntarikṣam vyaco hitam ||24||

10,2.25a brahmaṇā bhūmir vihitā brahma dyaur uttarā hitā |
10,2.25c brahmedam ūrdhvaṃ tiryak cāntarikṣaṃ vyaco hitam ||25||

10,2.26a mūrdhānam asya saṃsīvyātharvā hṛdayaṃ ca yat |
10,2.26c mastiṣkād ūrdhvaḥ prairayat pavamāno 'dhi śīrṣataḥ ||26||

10,2.27a tad vā atharvaṇaḥ śiro devakośaḥ samubjitaḥ |
10,2.27c tat prāṇo abhi rakṣati śiro annam atho manaḥ ||27||

10,2.28a ūrdhvo nu sṛṣṭā3s tiryaṅ nu sṛṣṭā3s sarvā diśaḥ puruṣa ā babhūvā3ṃ |
10,2.28c puraṃ yo brahmaṇo veda yasyāḥ puruṣa ucyate ||28||

10,2.29a yo vai tāṃ brahmaṇo vedāmṛtenāvṛtāṃ puram |
10,2.29c tasmai brahma ca brāhmāś ca cakṣuḥ prāṇaṃ prajāṃ daduḥ ||29||

10,2.30a na vai tam cakṣur jahāti na prāṇo jarasaḥ purā |
10,2.30c puraṃ yo brahmaṇo veda yasyāḥ puruṣa ucyate ||30||

10,2.31a aṣṭācakrā navadvārā devānāṃ pūr ayodhyā |
10,2.31c tasyāṃ hiraṇyayaḥ kośaḥ svargo jyotiṣāvṛtaḥ ||31||

10,2.32a tasmin hiraṇyaye kośe tryare tripratiṣṭhite |
10,2.32c tasmin yad yakṣam ātmanvat tad vai brahmavido viduḥ ||32||

10,2.33a prabhrājamānāṃ hariṇīṃ yaśasā saṃparīvṛtām |
10,2.33c puraṃ hiraṇyayīṃ brahmā viveśāparājitām ||33|| {6}



1ayaṃ me varaṇo maṇiḥ sapatnakṣayaṇo vṛṣā |
1tenā rabhasva tvaṃ śatrūn pra mṛṇīhi durasyataḥ ||1||

1praiṇān chṛṇīhi pra mṛṇā rabhasva maṇis te astu puraetā purastāt |
1avārayanta varaṇena devā abhyācāram asurāṇāṃ śvaḥśvaḥ ||2||

1ayaṃ maṇir varaṇo viśvabheṣajaḥ sahasrākṣo harito hiraṇyayaḥ |
1sa te śatrūn adharān pādayāti pūrvas tān dabhnuhi ye tvā dviṣanti ||3||

1ayaṃ te kṛtyāṃ vitatām pauruṣeyād ayaṃ bhayāt |
1ayaṃ tvā sarvasmāt pāpād varaṇo vārayiṣyate ||4||

1varaṇo vārayātā ayaṃ devo vanaspatiḥ |
1yakṣmo yo asminn āviṣṭas tam u devā avīvaran ||5||

1svapnaṃ suptvā yadi paśyāsi pāpaṃ mṛgaḥ sṛtiṃ yati dhāvād ajuṣṭām |
1parikṣavāc chakuneḥ pāpavādād ayaṃ maṇir varaṇo vārayiṣyate ||6||

1arātyās tvā nirṛtyā abhicārād atho bhayāt |
1mṛtyor ojīyaso vadhād varaṇo vārayiṣyate ||7||

1yan me mātā yan me pitā bhrātaro yac ca me svā yad enaś cakṛmā vayam |
1tato no vārayiṣyate 'yaṃ devo vanaspatiḥ ||8||

1varaṇena pravyathitā bhrātṛvyā me sabandhavaḥ |
1asūrtaṃ rajo apy agus te yantv adhamaṃ tamaḥ ||9||

10,3.10a ariṣṭo 'ham ariṣṭagur āyuṣmānt sarvapūruṣaḥ |
10,3.10c tam māyaṃ varaṇo maṇiḥ pari pātu diśodiśaḥ ||10|| {7}

10,3.11a ayaṃ me varaṇa urasi rājā devo vanaspatiḥ |
10,3.11c sa me śatrūn vi bādhatām indro dasyūn ivāsurān ||11||

10,3.12a imaṃ bibharmi varaṇam āyuṣmān chataśāradaḥ |
10,3.12c sa me rāṣṭraṃ ca kṣatraṃ ca paśūn ojaś ca me dadhat ||12||

10,3.13a yathā vāto vanaspatīn vṛkṣān bhanakty ojasā |
10,3.13c evā sapatnān me bhaṅgdhi pūrvān jātāṃ utāparān varaṇas tvābhi rakṣatu ||13||

10,3.14a yathā vātaś cāgniś ca vṛkṣān psāto vanaspatīn |
10,3.14c evā sapatnān me psāhi pūrvān jātāṃ utāparān varaṇas tvābhi rakṣatu ||14||

10,3.15a yathā vātena prakṣīṇā vṛkṣāḥ śere nyarpitāḥ |
10,3.15c evā sapatnāṃs tvaṃ mama pra kṣiṇīhi ny arpaya |
10,3.15e pūrvān jātāṃ utāparān varaṇas tvābhi rakṣatu ||15||

10,3.16a tāṃs tvaṃ pra chinddhi varaṇa purā diṣṭāt purāyuṣaḥ |
10,3.16c ya enaṃ paśuṣu dipsanti ye cāsya rāṣṭradipsavaḥ ||16||

10,3.17a yathā sūryo atibhāti yathāsmin teja āhitam |
10,3.17c evā me varaṇo maṇiḥ kīrtiṃ bhūtiṃ ni yachatu |
10,3.17e tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā ||17||

10,3.18a yathā yaśaś candramasy āditye ca nṛcakṣasi |
10,3.18c evā me varaṇo maṇiḥ kīrtiṃ bhūtiṃ ni yachatu |
10,3.18e tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā ||18||

10,3.19a yathā yaśaḥ pṛthivyāṃ yathāsmin jātavedasi |
10,3.19c evā me varaṇo maṇiḥ kīrtiṃ bhūtiṃ ni yachatu |
10,3.19e tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā ||19||

10,3.20a yathā yaśaḥ kanyāyāṃ yathāsmint saṃbhṛte rathe |
10,3.20c evā me varaṇo maṇiḥ kīrtiṃ bhūtiṃ ni yachatu |
10,3.20e tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā ||20|| {8}

10,3.21a yathā yaśaḥ somapīthe madhuparke yathā yaśaḥ |
10,3.21c evā me varaṇo maṇiḥ kīrtiṃ bhūtiṃ ni yachatu |
10,3.21e tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā ||21||

10,3.22a yathā yaśo 'gnihotre vaṣaṭkāre yathā yaśaḥ |
10,3.22c evā me varaṇo maṇiḥ kīrtiṃ bhūtiṃ ni yachatu |
10,3.22e tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā ||22||

10,3.23a yathā yaśo yajamāne yathāsmin yajña āhitam |
10,3.23c evā me varaṇo maṇiḥ kīrtiṃ bhūtiṃ ni yachatu |
10,3.23e tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā ||23||

10,3.24a yathā yaśaḥ prajāpatau yathāsmin parameṣṭhini |
10,3.24c evā me varaṇo maṇiḥ kīrtiṃ bhūtiṃ ni yachatu |
10,3.24e tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā ||24||

10,3.25a yathā deveṣv amṛtaṃ yathaiṣu satyam āhitam |
10,3.25c evā me varaṇo maṇiḥ kīrtiṃ bhūtiṃ ni yachatu |
10,3.25e tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā ||25|| {9}



1indrasya prathamo ratho devānām aparo ratho varuṇasya tṛtīya it |
1ahīnām apamā ratha sthānum ārad athārṣat ||1||

1darbhaḥ śocis tarūṇakam aśvasya vāraḥ paruṣasya vāraḥ |
1rathasya bandhuram ||2||

1ava śveta padā jahi pūrveṇa cāpareṇa ca |
1udaplutam iva dārv ahīnām arasaṃ viṣaṃ vār ugram ||3||

1araṃghuṣo nimajyonmaja punar abravīt |
1udaplutam iva dārv ahīnām arasaṃ viṣaṃ vār ugram ||4||

1paidvo hanti kasarṇīlaṃ paidvaḥ śvitram utāsitam |
1paidvo ratharvyāḥ śiraḥ saṃ bibheda pṛdākvāḥ ||5||

1paidva prehi prathamo 'nu tvā vayam emasi |
1ahīn vy asyatāt patho yena smā vayam emasi ||6||

1idaṃ paidvo ajāyatedam asya parāyaṇam |
1imāny arvataḥ padāhighnyo vājinīvataḥ ||7||

1saṃyataṃ na vi ṣparad vyāttaṃ na saṃ yamat |
1asmin kṣetre dvāv ahī strī ca pumāṃś ca tāv ubhāv arasā ||8||

1arasāsa ihāhayo ye anti ye ca dūrake |
1ghanena hanmi vṛścikam ahiṃ daṇḍenāgatam ||9||

10,4.10a aghāśvasyedaṃ bheṣajam ubhayo svajasya ca |
10,4.10c indro me 'him aghāyantam ahiṃ paidvo arandhayat ||10|| {10}

10,4.11a paidvasya manmahe vayaṃ sthirasya sthiradhāmnaḥ |
10,4.11c ime paścā pṛdākavaḥ pradīdhyata āsate ||11||

10,4.12a naṣṭāsavo naṣṭaviṣā hatā indreṇa vajriṇā |
10,4.12c jaghānendro jaghnimā vayam ||12||

10,4.13a hatās tiraścirājayo nipiṣṭāsaḥ pṛdākavaḥ |
10,4.13c darviṃ karikrataṃ śvitraṃ darbheṣv asitaṃ jahi ||13||

10,4.14a kairātikā kumārikā sakā khanati bheṣajam |
10,4.14c hiraṇyayībhir abhribhir girīnām upa sānuṣu ||14||

10,4.15a āyam agan yuvā bhiṣak pṛśnihāparājitaḥ |
10,4.15c sa vai svajasya jambhana ubhayor vṛścikasya ca ||15||

10,4.16a indro me 'him arandhayan mitraś ca varuṇaś ca |
10,4.16c vātāparjanyobhā ||16||

10,4.17a indro me 'him arandhayat pṛdākuṃ ca pṛdākvam |
10,4.17c svajaṃ tiraścirājiṃ kasarṇīlaṃ daśonasim ||17||

10,4.18a indro jaghāna prathamaṃ janitāram ahe tava |
10,4.18c teṣām u tṛhyamāṇānāṃ kaḥ svit teṣām asad rasaḥ ||18||

10,4.19a saṃ hi śīrṣāṇy agrabhaṃ pauñjiṣṭha iva karvaram |
10,4.19c sindhor madhyaṃ paretya vy anijam aher viṣam ||19||

10,4.20a ahīnāṃ sarveṣāṃ viṣaṃ parā vahantu sindhavaḥ |
10,4.20c hatās tiraścirājayo nipiṣṭāsaḥ pṛdākavaḥ ||20|| {11}

10,4.21a oṣadhīnām ahaṃ vṛṇa urvarīr iva sādhuyā |
10,4.21c nayāmy arvatīr ivāhe niraitu viṣam ||21||

10,4.22a yad agnau sūrye viṣaṃ pṛthivyām oṣadhīṣu yat |
10,4.22c kāndāviṣaṃ kanaknakaṃ niraitv aitu te viṣam ||22||

10,4.23a ye agnijā oṣadhijā ahīnāṃ ye apsujā vidyuta ābabhūvuḥ |
10,4.23c yeṣāṃ jātāni bahudhā mahānti tebhyaḥ sarpebhyo namasā vidhema ||23||

10,4.24a taudī nāmāsi kanyā ghṛtācī nāma vā asi |
10,4.24c adhaspadena te padam ā dade viṣadūṣaṇam ||24||

10,4.25a aṅgādaṅgāt pra cyāvaya hṛdayam pari varjaya |
10,4.25c adhā viṣasya yat tejo 'vācīnaṃ tad etu te ||25||

10,4.26a āre abhūd viṣam araud viṣe viṣam aprāg api |
10,4.26c agnir viṣam aher nir adhāt somo nir aṇayīt |
10,4.26e daṃṣṭāram anv agād viṣam ahir amṛta ||26|| {12}



1indrasyauja sthendrasya saha sthendrasya balaṃ sthendrasya vīryaṃ sthendrasya nṛmṇaṃ stha |
1jiṣṇave yogāya brahmayogair vo yunajmi ||1||

1indrasyauja sthendrasya saha sthendrasya balaṃ sthendrasya vīryaṃ sthendrasya nṛmṇaṃ stha |
1jiṣṇave yogāya kṣatrayogair vo yunajmi ||2||

1indrasyauja sthendrasya saha sthendrasya balaṃ sthendrasya vīryaṃ sthendrasya nṛmṇaṃ stha |
1jiṣṇave yogāyendrayogair vo yunajmi ||3||

1indrasyauja sthendrasya saha sthendrasya balaṃ sthendrasya vīryaṃ sthendrasya nṛmṇaṃ stha |
1jiṣṇave yogāya somayogair vo yunajmi ||4||

1indrasyauja sthendrasya saha sthendrasya balaṃ sthendrasya vīryaṃ sthendrasya nṛmṇaṃ stha |
1jiṣṇave yogāyāpsuyogair vo yunajmi ||5||

1indrasyauja sthendrasya saha sthendrasya balaṃ sthendrasya vīryaṃ sthendrasya nṛmṇaṃ stha |
1jiṣṇave yogāya viśvāni mā bhūtāny upa tiṣṭhantu yuktā ma āpa stha ||6||

1agner bhāga stha apāṃ śukram āpo devīr varco asmāsu dhatta |
1prajāpater vo dhāmnāsmai lokāya sādaye ||7||

1indrasya bhāga stha apāṃ śukram āpo devīr varco asmāsu dhatta |
1prajāpater vo dhāmnāsmai lokāya sādaye ||8||

1somasya bhāga stha apāṃ śukram āpo devīr varco asmāsu dhatta |
1prajāpater vo dhāmnāsmai lokāya sādaye ||9||

10,5.10a varuṇasya bhāga stha apāṃ śukram āpo devīr varco asmāsu dhatta |
10,5.10c prajāpater vo dhāmnāsmai lokāya sādaye ||10|| {13}

10,5.11a mitrāvaruṇayor bhāga stha apāṃ śukram āpo devīr varco asmāsu dhatta |
10,5.11c prajāpater vo dhāmnāsmai lokāya sādaye ||11||

10,5.12a yamasya bhāga stha apām śukram āpo devīr varco asmāsu dhatta |
10,5.12c prajāpater vo dhāmnāsmai lokāya sādaye ||12||

10,5.13a pitṝṇāṃ bhāga stha apāṃ śukram āpo devīr varco asmāsu dhatta |
10,5.13c prajāpater vo dhāmnāsmai lokāya sādaye ||13||

10,5.14a devasya savitur bhāga stha apāṃ śukram āpo devīr varco asmāsu dhatta |
10,5.14c prajāpater vo dhāmnāsmai lokāya sādaye ||14||

10,5.15a yo va āpo 'pāṃ bhāgo 'psv antar yajuṣyo devayajanaḥ |
10,5.15c idaṃ tam ati sṛjāmi taṃ mābhyavanikṣi |
10,5.15e tena tam abhyatisṛjāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ |
10,5.15g taṃ vadheyaṃ taṃ stṛṣīyānena brahmaṇānena karmaṇānayā menyā || 15 ||

10,5.16a yo va āpo 'pām ūrmir apsv antar yajuṣyo devayajanaḥ |
10,5.16c idaṃ tam ati sṛjāmi taṃ mābhyavanikṣi |
10,5.16e tena tam abhyatisṛjāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ |
10,5.16g taṃ vadheyaṃ taṃ stṛṣīyānena brahmaṇānena karmaṇānayā menyā || 16 ||

10,5.17a yo va āpo 'pām vatso 'psv antar yajuṣyo devayajanaḥ |
10,5.17c idaṃ tam ati sṛjāmi taṃ mābhyavanikṣi |
10,5.17e tena tam abhyatisṛjāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ |
10,5.17g taṃ vadheyaṃ taṃ stṛṣīyānena brahmaṇānena karmaṇānayā menyā || 17 ||

10,5.18a yo va āpo 'pāṃ vṛṣabho 'psv antar yajuṣyo devayajanaḥ ||
10,5.18c idaṃ tam ati sṛjāmi taṃ mābhyavanikṣi |
10,5.18e tena tam abhyatisṛjāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ||
10,5.18g taṃ vadheyaṃ taṃ stṛṣīyānena brahmaṇānena karmaṇānayā menyā || 18 ||

10,5.19a yo va āpo 'pāṃ hiraṇyagarbho 'psv antar yajuṣyo devayajanaḥ |
10,5.19c idaṃ tam ati sṛjāmi taṃ mābhyavanikṣi |
10,5.19e tena tam abhyatisṛjāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ |
10,5.19g taṃ vadheyaṃ taṃ stṛṣīyānena brahmaṇānena karmaṇānayā menyā || 19 ||

10,5.20a yo va āpo 'pāṃ aśmā pṛśnir divyo 'psv antar yajuṣyo devayajanaḥ |
10,5.20c idaṃ tam ati sṛjāmi taṃ mābhyavanikṣi |
10,5.20e tena tam abhyatisṛjāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ |
10,5.20g taṃ vadheyaṃ taṃ stṛṣīyānena brahmaṇānena karmaṇānayā menyā || 20 ||

10,5.21a yo va āpo 'pāṃ agnayo 'psv antar yajuṣyo devayajanaḥ |
10,5.21c idaṃ tam ati sṛjāmi taṃ mābhyavanikṣi |
10,5.21e tena tam abhyatisṛjāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ |
10,5.21g taṃ vadheyaṃ taṃ stṛṣīyānena brahmaṇānena karmaṇānayā menyā || 21 ||

10,5.22a yad arvācīnaṃ traihāyaṇād anṛtaṃ kiṃ codima |
10,5.22c āpo mā tasmāt sarvasmād duritāt pāntv aṃhasaḥ ||22||

10,5.23a samudraṃ vaḥ pra hiṇomi svāṃ yonim apītana |
10,5.23c ariṣṭāḥ sarvahāyaso mā ca naḥ kiṃ canāmamat ||23||

10,5.24a ariprā āpo apa ripram asmat |
10,5.24c prāsmad eno duritaṃ supratīkāḥ pra duṣvapnyam pra malaṃ vahantu ||24||

10,5.25a viṣṇoḥ kramo 'si sapatnahā pṛthivīsaṃśito 'gnitejāḥ |
10,5.25c pṛthivīm anu vi krame 'haṃ pṛthivyās taṃ nir bhajāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ |
10,5.25e sa mā jīvīt taṃ prāno jahātu ||25||

10,5.26a viṣṇoḥ kramo 'si sapatnahāntarikṣasaṃśito vāyutejāḥ |
10,5.26c antarikṣam anu vi krame 'haṃ antarikṣāt taṃ nir bhajāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ |
10,5.26e sa mā jīvīt taṃ prāno jahātu ||26||

10,5.27a viṣṇoḥ kramo 'si sapatnahā dyausaṃśitaḥ sūryatejāḥ |
10,5.27c divam anu vi krame 'haṃ divas taṃ nir bhajāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ |
10,5.27e sa mā jivīt taṃ prāno jahātu ||27||

10,5.28a viṣṇoḥ kramo 'si sapatnahā diksaṃśito manastejāḥ |
10,5.28c diśo anu vi krame 'haṃ digbhyas taṃ nir bhajāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ |
10,5.28e sa mā jīvīt taṃ prāno jahātu ||28||

10,5.29a viṣṇoḥ kramo 'si sapatnahāśāsaṃśito vātatejāḥ |
10,5.29c āśā anu vi krame 'haṃ āśābhyas taṃ nir bhajāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ |
10,5.29e sa mā jīvīt taṃ prāno jahātu ||29||

10,5.30a viṣṇoḥ kramo 'si sapatnahā ṛksaṃśito sāmatejāḥ |
10,5.30c ṛco 'nu vi krame 'haṃ ṛgbhyas taṃ nir bhajāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ |
10,5.30e sa mā jīvīt taṃ prāno jahātu ||30|| {15}

10,5.31a viṣṇoḥ kramo 'si sapatnahā yajñasaṃśito brahmatejāḥ |
10,5.31c yajñam anu vi krame 'haṃ yajñāt taṃ nir bhajāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ |
10,5.31e sa mā jīvīt taṃ prāno jahātu ||31||

10,5.32a viṣṇoḥ kramo 'si sapatnahauṣadhīsaṃśito somatejāḥ |
10,5.32c oṣadhīr anu vi krame 'haṃ oṣadhībhyas taṃ nir bhajāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ |
10,5.32e sa mā jīvīt taṃ prāno jahātu ||32||

10,5.33a viṣṇoḥ kramo 'si sapatnahāpsusaṃśito varuṇatejāḥ |
10,5.33c apo 'nu vi krame 'haṃ adbhyas taṃ nir bhajāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ |
10,5.33e sa mā jīvīt taṃ prāno jahātu ||33||

10,5.34a viṣṇoḥ kramo 'si sapatnahā kṛṣisaṃśito 'nnatejāḥ |
10,5.34c kṛṣim anu vi krame 'haṃ kṛṣyās taṃ nir bhajāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ |
10,5.34e sa mā jīvīt taṃ prāno jahātu ||34||

10,5.35a visṇoḥ kramo 'si sapatnahā prāṇasaṃśitaḥ puruṣatejāḥ |
10,5.35c prāṇam anu vi krame 'haṃ prāṇāt taṃ nir bhajāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ |
10,5.35e sa mā jīvīt taṃ prāno jahātu ||35||
10,5.36a jitam asmākam udbhinnam asmākam abhy aṣṭhāṃ viśvāḥ pṛtanā arātīḥ |
10,5.36c idam aham āmuṣyāyaṇasyāmuṣyāḥ putrasya varcas tejaḥ prāṇam āyur ni veṣṭayāmīdam enam adharāñcaṃ pādayāmi ||36||

10,5.37a sūryasyāvṛtam anvāvarte dakṣiṇām anv āvṛtam |
10,5.37c sā me draviṇaṃ yachatu sā me brāhmaṇavarcasam ||37||

10,5.38a diśo jyotiṣmatīr abhyāvarte |
10,5.38c tā me draviṇaṃ yachantu tā me brāhmaṇavarcasam ||38||

10,5.39a saptaṛṣīn abhyāvarte |
10,5.39c te me draviṇaṃ yachantu te me brāhmaṇavarcasam ||39||

10,5.40a brahmābhyāvarte |
10,5.40c tan me draviṇaṃ yachantu tan me brāhmaṇavarcasam ||40|| {16}

10,5.41a brāhmaṇāṃ abhyāvarte |
10,5.41c te me draviṇaṃ yachantu te me brāhmaṇavarcasam ||41||

10,5.42a yam vayaṃ mṛgayāmahe taṃ vadhai stṛṇavāmahai |
10,5.42c vyātte parameṣṭhino brahmaṇāpīpadāma tam ||42||

10,5.43a vaiśvānarasya daṃṣṭrābhyāṃ hetis taṃ sam adhād abhi |
10,5.43c iyaṃ taṃ psātv āhutiḥ samid devī sahīyasī ||43||

10,5.44a rājño varuṇasya bandho 'si |
10,5.44c so 'mum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putram anne prāṇe badhāna ||44||

10,5.45a yat te annaṃ bhuvas pata ākṣiyati pṛthivīm anu |
10,5.45c tasya nas tvaṃ bhuvas pate saṃprayacha prajāpate ||45||

10,5.46a apo divyā acāyiṣaṃ rasena sam apṛkṣmahi |
10,5.46c payasvān agna āgamaṃ taṃ mā saṃ sṛja varcasā ||46||

10,5.47a saṃ māgne varcasā sṛja saṃ prajayā sam āyuṣā |
10,5.47c vidyur me asya devā indro vidyāt saha ṛṣibhiḥ ||47||

10,5.48a yad agne adya mithunā śapato yad vācas tṛṣṭaṃ janayanta rebhāḥ |
10,5.48c manyor manasaḥ śaravyā jāyate yā tayā vidhya hṛdaye yātudhānān ||48||

10,5.49a parā śṛṇīhi tapasā yātudhānān parāgne rakṣo harasā śṛṇīhi |
10,5.49c parārciṣā mūradevāṃ chṛṇīhi parāsutṛpaḥ śośucataḥ śṛṇīhi ||49||

10,5.50a apām asmai vajraṃ pra harāmi caturbhṛṣṭiṃ śīrṣabhidyāya vidvān |
10,5.50c so asyāṅgāni pra śṛṇātu sarvā tan me devā anu jānantu viśve ||50|| {17}



1arātīyor bhrātṛvyasya durhārdo dviṣataḥ śiraḥ |
1api vṛścāmy ojasā ||1||

1varma mahyam ayaṃ maṇiḥ phālāj jātaḥ kariṣyati |
1pūrṇo manthena māgamad rasena saha varcasā ||2||

1yat tvā śikvaḥ parāvadhīt takṣā hastena vāsyā |
1āpas tvā tasmaj jīvalāḥ punantu śucayaḥ śucim ||3||

1hiraṇyasrag ayaṃ maṇiḥ śraddhāṃ yajñaṃ maho dadhat |
1gṛhe vasatu no 'tithiḥ ||4||

1tasmai ghṛtaṃ suraṃ madhv annamannam kṣadāmahe |
1sa naḥ piteva putrebhyaḥ śreyaḥśreyaś cikitsatu bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvo devebhyo maṇir etya ||5||

1yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir maṇiṃ phālaṃ ghṛtaścutam ugraṃ kadhiram ojase |
1tam agniḥ praty amuñcata so asmai duha ājyaṃ bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi ||6||

1yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir maṇiṃ phālaṃ ghṛtaścutam ugraṃ kadhiram ojase |
1tam indraḥ praty amuñcataujase vīryāya kam |
1so asmai balam id duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi ||7||

1yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir maṇiṃ phālaṃ ghṛtaścutam ugram kadhiram ojase |
1taṃ somaḥ praty amuñcata mahe śrotrāya cakṣase |
1so asmai varca id duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvam dviṣato jahi ||8||

1yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir maṇiṃ phālaṃ ghṛtaścutam ugraṃ khadiram ojase |
1taṃ sūryaḥ praty amuñcata tenemā ajayad diśaḥ |
1so asmai bhūtim id duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi ||9||

10,6.10a yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir maṇiṃ phālaṃ ghṛtaścutam ugram khadiram ojase |
10,6.10c tam bibhrac candramā maṇim asurāṇāṃ puro 'jayad dānavānāṃ hiraṇyayīḥ |
