10,6.10e so asmai śriyam id duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi ||10|| {18}

10,6.11a yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir vātāya maṇim āśave |
10,6.11c so asmai vājinam id duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi ||11||

10,6.12a yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir vātāya maṇim āśave |
10,6.12c tenemāṃ maṇinā kṛṣim aśvināv abhi rakṣataḥ |
10,6.12e sa bhiṣagbhyāṃ maho duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi ||12||

10,6.13a yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir vātāya maṇim āśave |
10,6.13c tam bibhrat savitā maṇiṃ tenedam ajayat svaḥ |
10,6.13e so asmai sūnṛtāṃ duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi ||13||

10,6.14a yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir vātāya maṇim āśave |
10,6.14c tam āpo bibhratīr maṇiṃ sadā dhāvanty akṣitāḥ |
10,6.14e sa ābhyo 'mṛtam id duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi ||14||

10,6.15a yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir vātāya maṇim āśave |
10,6.15c tam rājā varuṇo maṇiṃ praty amuñcata śaṃbhuvam |
10,6.15e so asmai satyam id duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi ||15||

10,6.16a yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir vātāya maṇim āśave |
10,6.16c taṃ devā bibhrato maṇiṃ sarvāṃl lokān yudhājayan |
10,6.16e sa ebhyo jitim id duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi ||16||

10,6.17a yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir vātāya maṇim āśave |
10,6.17c tam imaṃ devatā maṇiṃ praty amuñcanta śambhuvam |
10,6.17e sa ābhyo viśvam id duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi ||17||

10,6.18a ṛtavas tam abadhnatārtavās tam abadhnata |
10,6.18c saṃvatsaras taṃ baddhvā sarvaṃ bhūtaṃ vi rakṣati ||18||

10,6.19a antardeśā abadhnata pradiśas tam abadhnata |
10,6.19c prajāpatisṛṣṭo maṇir dviṣato me 'dharāṃ akaḥ ||19||

10,6.20a atharvāṇo abadhnatātharvaṇā abadhnata |
10,6.20c tair medino aṅgiraso dasyūnāṃ bibhiduḥ puras tena tvam dviṣato jahi ||20|| {19}

10,6.21a taṃ dhātā praty amuñcata sa bhūtaṃ vy akalpayat |
10,6.21c tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi ||21||

10,6.22a yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir devebhyo asurakṣitim |
10,6.22c sa māyaṃ maṇir āgamad rasena saha varcasā ||22||

10,6.23a yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir devebhyo asurakṣitim |
10,6.23c sa māyaṃ maṇir āgamat saha gobhir ajāvibhir annena prajayā saha ||23||

10,6.24a yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir devebhyo asurakṣitim |
10,6.24c sa māyaṃ maṇir āgamat saha vrīhiyavābhyāṃ mahasā bhūtyā saha ||24||

10,6.25a yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir devebhyo asurakṣitim |
10,6.25c sa māyaṃ maṇir āgaman madhor ghṛtasya dhārayā kīlālena maṇiḥ saha ||25||

10,6.26a yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir devebhyo asurakṣitim |
10,6.26c sa māyaṃ maṇir āgamad ūrjayā payasā saha draviṇena śriyā saha ||26||

10,6.27a yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir devebhyo asurakṣitim |
10,6.27c sa māyaṃ maṇir āgamat tejasā tviṣyā saha yaśasā kīrtyā saha ||27||

10,6.28a yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir devebhyo asurakṣitim |
10,6.28c sa māyaṃ maṇir āgamat sarvābhir bhūtibhiḥ saha ||28||

10,6.29a tam imaṃ devatā maṇiṃ mahyaṃ dadatu puṣṭaye |
10,6.29c abhibhuṃ kṣatravardhanaṃ sapatnadambhanaṃ maṇim ||29||

10,6.30a brahmaṇā tejasā saha prati muñcāmi me śivam |
10,6.30c asapatnaḥ sapatnahā sapatnān me 'dharāṃ akaḥ ||30|| {20}

10,6.31a uttaraṃ dviṣato mām ayaṃ maṇiḥ kṛṇotu devajāḥ |
10,6.31c yasya lokā ime trayaḥ payo dugdham upāsate |
10,6.31e sa māyam adhi rohatu maṇiḥ śraiṣṭhyāya mūrdhataḥ ||31||

10,6.32a yaṃ devāḥ pitaro manuṣyā upajīvanti sarvadā |
10,6.32c sa māyam adhi rohatu maṇiḥ śraiṣṭhyāya mūrdhataḥ ||32||

10,6.33a yathā bījam urvarāyāṃ kṛṣṭe phālena rohati |
10,6.33c evā mayi prajā paśavo 'nnamannaṃ vi rohatu ||33||

10,6.34a yasmai tvā yajñavardhana maṇe pratyamucaṃ śivam |
10,6.34c taṃ tvaṃ śatadakṣiṇa maṇe śraiṣṭhyāya jinvatāt ||34||

10,6.35a etam idhmaṃ samāhitaṃ juṣaṇo agne prati harya homaiḥ |
10,6.35c tasmin vidhema sumatiṃ svasti prajām cakṣuḥ paśūnt samiddhe jātavedasi brahmaṇā ||35|| {21}



1kasminn aṅge tapo asyādhi tiṣṭhati kasminn aṅga ṛtam asyādhy āhitam |
1kva vrataṃ kva śraddhāsya tiṣṭhati kasminn aṅge satyam asya pratiṣṭhitam ||1||

1kasmād aṅgād dīpyate agnir asya kasmād aṅgāt pavate mātariśva |
1kasmād aṅgād vi mimīte 'dhi candramā maha skambhasya mimāno aṅgam ||2||

1kasminn aṅge tiṣṭhati bhūmir asya kasminn aṅge tiṣṭhaty antarikṣam |
1kasminn aṅge tiṣṭhaty āhitā dyauḥ kasminn aṅge tiṣṭhaty uttaraṃ divaḥ ||3||

1kva prepsan dīpyata ūrdhvo agniḥ kva prepsan pavate mātariśvā |
1yatra prepsantīr abhiyanty āvṛtaḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ ||4||

1kvārdhamāsāḥ kva yanti māsāḥ saṃvatsareṇa saha saṃvidānāḥ |
1yatra yanty ṛtavo yatrārtavāḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ ||5||

1kva prepsantī yuvatī virūpe ahorātre dravataḥ saṃvidāne |
1yatra prepsantīr abhiyanty āpaḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ ||6||

1yasmint stabdhvā prajāpatir lokānt sarvāṃ adhārayat |
1skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ ||7||

1yat paramam avamam yac ca madhyamaṃ prajāpatiḥ sasṛje viśvarūpam |
1kiyatā skambhaḥ pra viveśa tatra yan na prāviśat kiyat tad babhūva ||8||

1kiyatā skambhaḥ pra viveśa bhūtam kiyad bhaviṣyad anvāśaye 'sya |
1ekaṃ yad aṅgam akṛṇot sahasradhā kiyatā skambhaḥ pra viveśa tatra ||9||

10,7.10a yatra lokāmś ca kośāṃś cāpo brahma janā viduḥ |
10,7.10c asac ca yatra sac cānta skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ ||10|| {22}

10,7.11a yatra tapaḥ parākramya vrataṃ dhārayaty uttaram |
10,7.11c ṛtaṃ ca yatra śraddhā cāpo brahma samāhitāḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ ||11||

10,7.12a yasmin bhūmir antarikṣaṃ dyaur yasminn adhy āhitā |
10,7.12c yatrāgniś candramāḥ sūryo vātas tiṣṭhanty ārpitāḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ ||12||

10,7.13a yasya trayastriṃśad devā aṅge sarve samāhitāḥ |
10,7.13c skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ ||13||

10,7.14a yatra ṛṣayaḥ prathamajā ṛcaḥ sāma yajur mahī |
10,7.14c ekarṣir yasminn ārpitaḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ ||14||

10,7.15a yatrāmṛtaṃ ca mṛtyuś ca puruṣe 'dhi samāhite |
10,7.15c samudro yasya nāḍyaḥ puruṣe 'dhi samāhitāḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ ||15||

10,7.16a yasya catasraḥ pradiśo nāḍyas tiṣṭhanti prathamāḥ |
10,7.16c yajño yatra parākrāntaḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ ||16||

10,7.17a ye puruṣe brahma vidus te viduḥ parameṣṭhinam |
10,7.17c yo veda parameṣṭhinaṃ yaś ca veda prajāpatim |
10,7.17e jyeṣṭhaṃ ye brāhmaṇaṃ vidus te skambham anusaṃviduḥ ||17||

10,7.18a yasya śiro vaiśvānaraś cakṣur aṅgiraso 'bhavan |
10,7.18c aṅgāni yasya yātavaḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ ||18||

10,7.19a yasya brahma mukham āhur jihvāṃ madhukaśām uta |
10,7.19c virājam ūdho yasyāhuḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ ||19||

10,7.20a yasmād ṛco apātakṣan yajur yasmād apākaṣan |
10,7.20c sāmāni yasya lomāny atharvāṅgiraso mukhaṃ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ ||20|| {23}

10,7.21a asaccākhāṃ pratiṣṭhantīṃ paramam iva janā viduḥ |
10,7.21c uto san manyante 'vare ye te śākhām upāsate ||21||

10,7.22a yatrādityāś ca rudrāś ca vasavaś ca samāhitāḥ |
10,7.22c bhūtaṃ ca yatra bhavyaṃ ca sarve lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ ||22||

10,7.23a yasya trayastriṃśad devā nidhiṃ rakṣanti sarvadā |
10,7.23c nidhiṃ tam adya ko veda yaṃ devā abhirakṣatha ||23||

10,7.24a yatra devā brahmavido brahma jyeṣṭham upāsate |
10,7.24c yo vai tān vidyāt pratyakṣaṃ sa brahmā veditā syāt ||24||

10,7.25a bṛhanto nāma te devā ye 'sataḥ pari jajñire |
10,7.25c ekaṃ tad aṅgaṃ skambhasyāsad āhuḥ paro janāḥ ||25||

10,7.26a yatra skambhaḥ prajanayan purāṇaṃ vyavartayat |
10,7.26c ekaṃ tad aṅgaṃ skambhasya purāṇam anusaṃviduḥ ||26||

10,7.27a yasya trayastriṃśad devā aṅge gātrā vibhejire |
10,7.27c tān vai trayastriṃśad devān eke brahamvido viduḥ ||27||

10,7.28a hiraṇyagarbham paramam anatyudyaṃ janā viduḥ |
10,7.28c skambhas tad agre prāsiñcad dhiraṇyaṃ loke antarā ||28||

10,7.29a skambhe lokāḥ skambhe tapaḥ skambhe 'dhy ṛtam āhitam |
10,7.29c skambha tvā veda pratyakṣam indre sarvaṃ samāhitam ||29||

10,7.30a indre lokā indre tapa indre 'dhy ṛtam āhitam |
10,7.30c indraṃ tvā veda pratyakṣaṃ skambhe sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ||30|| {24}

10,7.31a nāma nāmnā johavīti purā sūryāt puroṣasaḥ |
10,7.31c yad ajaḥ prathamaṃ saṃbabhūva sa ha tat svarājyam iyāya yasmān nānyat param asti bhūtam ||31||

10,7.32a yasya bhūmiḥ pramāntarikṣam utodaram |
10,7.32c divaṃ yaś cakre mūrdhānaṃ tasmai jyeṣṭhāya brahmaṇe namaḥ ||32||

10,7.33a yasya sūryaś cakṣuś candramāś ca punarṇavaḥ |
10,7.33c agniṃ yaś cakra āsyaṃ tasmai jyeṣṭhāya brahmaṇe namaḥ ||33||

10,7.34a yasya vātaḥ prāṇāpānau cakṣur aṅgiraso 'bhavan |
10,7.34c diśo yaś cakre prajñānīs tasmai jyeṣṭhāya brahmaṇe namaḥ ||34||
10,7.35a skambho dādhāra dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe ime skambho dādhārorv antarikṣam |
10,7.35c skambho dādhāra pradiśaḥ ṣaḍ urvīḥ skambha idaṃ viśvaṃ bhuvanam ā viveśa ||35||

10,7.36a yaḥ śramāt tapaso jāto lokānt sarvānt samānaśe |
10,7.36c somaṃ yaś cakre kevalaṃ tasmai jyeṣṭhāya brahmaṇe namaḥ ||36||

10,7.37a kathaṃ vāto nelayati kathaṃ na ramate manaḥ |
10,7.37c kim āpaḥ satyaṃ prepsantīr nelayanti kadā cana ||37||

10,7.38a mahad yakṣaṃ bhuvanasya madhye tapasi krāntaṃ salilasya pṛṣṭhe |
10,7.38c tasmin chrayante ya u ke ca devā vṛkṣasya skandhaḥ parita iva śākhāḥ ||38||
10,7.39a yasmai hastābhyāṃ pādābhyāṃ vācā śrotreṇa cakṣuṣā |
10,7.39c yasmai devāḥ sadā baliṃ prayachanti vimite 'mitaṃ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ ||39||

10,7.40a apa tasya hataṃ tamo vyāvṛttaḥ sa pāpmanā |
10,7.40c sarvāṇi tasmin jyotīṃṣi yāni trīṇi prajāpatau ||40||

10,7.41a yo vetasaṃ hiraṇyayaṃ tiṣṭhantaṃ salile veda |
10,7.41c sa vai guhyaḥ prajāpatiḥ ||41||

10,7.42a tantram eke yuvatī virūpe abhyākrāmaṃ vayataḥ ṣaṇmayūkham |
10,7.42c prānyā tantūṃs tirate dhatte anyā nāpa vṛñjāte na gamāto antam ||42||

10,7.43a tayor ahaṃ parinṛtyantyor iva na vi jānāmi yatarā parastāt |
10,7.43c pumān enad vayaty ud gṛṇanti pumān enad vi jabhārādhi nāke ||43||

10,7.44a ime mayūkhā upa tastabhur divaṃ sāmāni cakrus tasarāṇi vātave ||44|| {25}



1yo bhūtaṃ ca bhavyaṃ ca sarvaṃ yaś cādhitiṣṭhati |
1sv aryasya ca kevalaṃ tasmai jyeṣṭhāya brahmaṇe namaḥ ||1||

1skambheneme viṣṭabhite dyauś ca bhūmiś ca tiṣṭhataḥ |
1skambha idaṃ sarvam ātmanvad yat prāṇan nimiṣac ca yat ||2||

1tisro ha prajā atyāyam āyan ny anyā arkam abhito 'viśanta |
1bṛhan ha tasthau rajaso vimāno harito hariṇīr ā viveśa ||3||

1dvādaśa pradhayaś cakram ekaṃ trīṇi nabhyāni ka u tac ciketa |
1tatrāhatās trīṇi śatāni śaṅkavaḥ ṣaṣṭiś ca khīlā avicācalā ye ||4||

1idaṃ savitar vi jānīhi ṣaḍ yamā eka ekajaḥ |
1tasmin hāpitvam ichante ya eṣām eka ekajaḥ ||5||

1āviḥ san nihitaṃ guhā jaran nāma mahat padam |
1tatredaṃ sarvam ārpitam ejat prāṇat pratiṣṭhitam ||6||

1ekacakraṃ vartata ekanemi sahasrākṣaraṃ pra puro ni paścā |
1ardhena viśvaṃ bhuvanaṃ jajāna yad asyārdhaṃ kva tad babhūva ||7||

1pañcavāhī vahatyagram eṣāṃ praṣṭayo yuktā anusaṃvahanti |
1ayātam asya dadṛśe na yātaṃ paraṃ nedīyo 'varaṃ davīyaḥ ||8||

1tiryagbilaś camasa ūrdhvabudhnas tasmin yaśo nihitaṃ viśvarūpam |
1tad āsata ṛṣayaḥ sapta sākaṃ ye asya gopā mahato babhūvuḥ ||9||

10,8.10a yā purastād yujyate yā ca paścād yā viśvato yujyate yā ca sarvataḥ |
10,8.10c yayā yajñaḥ prāṅ tāyate tāṃ tvā pṛchāmi katamā sā ṛcām ||10|| {26}

10,8.11a yad ejati patati yac ca tiṣṭhati prāṇad aprāṇan nimiṣac ca yad bhuvat |
10,8.11c tad dādhāra pṛthivīṃ viśvarūpaṃ tat saṃbhūya bhavaty ekam eva ||11||

10,8.12a anantaṃ vitataṃ purutrānantam antavac cā samante |
10,8.12c te nākapālaś carati vicinvan vidvān bhūtam uta bhavyam asya ||12||

10,8.13a prajāpatiś carati garbhe antar adṛśyamāno bahudhā vi jāyate |
10,8.13c ardhena viśvaṃ bhuvanaṃ jajāna yad asyārdhaṃ katamaḥ sa ketuḥ ||13||

10,8.14a ūrdhvaṃ bharantam udakaṃ kumbhenevodahāryam |
10,8.14c paśyanti sarve cakṣuṣā na sarve manasā viduḥ ||14||

10,8.15a dūre pūrṇena vasati dūra ūnena hīyate |
10,8.15c mahad yakṣaṃ bhuvanasya madhye tasmai baliṃ rāṣṭrabhṛto bharanti ||15||

10,8.16a yataḥ sūryaḥ udety astaṃ yatra ca gachati |
10,8.16c tad eva manye 'haṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ tad u nāty eti kiṃ cana ||16||

10,8.17a ye arvāṅ madhya uta vā purāṇaṃ vedaṃ vidvāṃsam abhito vadanti |
10,8.17c ādityam eva te pari vadanti sarve agniṃ dvitīyaṃ trivṛtaṃ ca haṃsam ||17||

10,8.18a sahasrāhṇyaṃ viyatāv asya pakṣau harer haṃsasya patataḥ svargam |
10,8.18c sa devānt sarvān urasy upadadya saṃpaśyan yāti bhuvanāni viśvā ||18||

10,8.19a satyenordhvas tapati brahmaṇārvāṅ vi paśyati |
10,8.19c prāṇena tiryaṅ prāṇati yasmin jyeṣṭham adhi śritam ||19||

10,8.20a yo vai te vidyād araṇī yābhyāṃ nirmathyate vasu |
10,8.20c sa vidvān jyeṣṭhaṃ manyeta sa vidyād brāhmaṇaṃ mahat ||20|| {27}

10,8.21a apād agre sam abhavat so agre svar ābharat |
10,8.21c catuṣpād bhūtvā bhogyaḥ sarvam ādatta bhojanam ||21||

10,8.22a bhogyo bhavad atho annam adad bahu |
10,8.22c yo devam uttarāvantam upāsātai sanātanam ||22||

10,8.23a sanātanam enam āhur utādya syāt punarṇavaḥ |
10,8.23c ahorātre pra jāyete anyo anyasya rūpayoḥ ||23||

10,8.24a śataṃ sahasram ayutaṃ nyarbudam asaṃkhyeyaṃ svam asmin niviṣṭam |
10,8.24c tad asya ghnanty abhipaśyata eva tasmād devo rocat eṣa etat ||24||

10,8.25a bālād ekam aṇīyaskam utaikaṃ neva dṛśyate |
10,8.25c tataḥ pariṣvajīyasī devatā sā mama priyā ||25||

10,8.26a iyaṃ kalyāṇy ajarā martyasyāmṛtā gṛhe |
10,8.26c yasmai kṛtā śaye sa yaś cakāra jajāra saḥ ||26||

10,8.27a tvaṃ strī tvaṃ pumān asi tvaṃ kumāra uta vā kumārī||
10,8.27b tvaṃ jīrṇo daṇḍena vañcasi tvaṃ jāto bhavasi viśvatomukhaḥ ||27||

10,8.28a utaiṣāṃ pitota vā putra eṣām utaiṣāṃ jyeṣṭha uta vā kaniṣṭhaḥ |
10,8.28c eko ha devo manasi praviṣṭaḥ prathamo jātaḥ sa u garbhe antaḥ ||28||

10,8.29a pūrṇāt pūrṇam ud acati pūrṇaṃ pūrṇena sicyate |
10,8.29c uto tad adya vidyāma yatas tat pariṣicyate ||29||

10,8.30a eṣā sanatnī sanam eva jātaiṣā purāṇī pari sarvaṃ babhūva |
10,8.30c mahī devy uṣaso vibhātī saikenaikena miṣatā vi caṣṭe ||30|| {28}

10,8.31a avir vai nāma devatartenāste parīvṛtā |
10,8.31c tasyā rūpeṇeme vṛkṣā haritā haritasrajaḥ ||31||

10,8.32a anti santaṃ na jahāty anti santaṃ na paśyati |
10,8.32c devasya paśya kāvyaṃ na mamāra na jīryati ||32||

10,8.33a apūrveṇeṣitā vācas tā vadanti yathāyatham |
10,8.33c vadantīr yatra gachanti tad āhur brāhmaṇaṃ mahat ||33||

10,8.34a yatra devāś ca manuṣyāś cārā nābhāv iva śritāḥ |
10,8.34c apāṃ tvā puṣpaṃ pṛchāmi yatra tan māyayā hitam ||34||

10,8.35a yebhir vāta iṣitaḥ pravāti ye dadante pañca diśaḥ sadhrīcīḥ |
10,8.35c ya āhutim atyamanyanta devā apāṃ netāraḥ katame ta āsan ||35||

10,8.36a imām eṣāṃ pṛthivīṃ vasta eko 'ntarikṣaṃ pary eko babhūva |
10,8.36c divam eṣāṃ dadate yo vidhartā viśvā āśāḥ prati rakṣanty eke ||36||

10,8.37a yo vidyāt sūtraṃ vitataṃ yasminn otāḥ prajā imāḥ |
10,8.37c sūtraṃ sūtrasya yo vidyād sa vidyād brāhmaṇaṃ mahat ||37||

10,8.38a vedāhaṃ sūtraṃ vitataṃ yasminn otāḥ prajā imāḥ |
10,8.38c sūtraṃ sūtrasyāhaṃ vedātho yad brāhmaṇaṃ mahad ||38||

10,8.39a yad antarā dyāvāpṛthivī agnir ait pradahan viśvadāvyaḥ |
10,8.39c yatrātiṣṭhann ekapatnīḥ parastāt kvevāsīn mātariśvā tadānīm ||39||

10,8.40a apsv āsīn mātariśvā praviṣṭaḥ praviṣṭā devāḥ salilāny āsan||
10,8.40b bṛhan ha tasthau rajaso vimānaḥ pavamāno harita ā viveśa ||40||

10,8.41a uttareṇeva gayatrīm amṛte 'dhi vi cakrame |
10,8.41c sāmnā ye sāma saṃvidur ajas tad dadṛśe kva ||41||

10,8.42a niveśanaḥ saṃgamano vasūnāṃ deva iva savitā satyadharmā |
10,8.42c indro na tasthau samare dhanānām ||42||

10,8.43a puṇḍarīkaṃ navadvāraṃ tribhir guṇebhir āvṛtam |
10,8.43c tasmin yad yakṣam ātmanvat tad vai brahmavido viduḥ ||43||

10,8.44a akāmo dhīro amṛtaḥ svayaṃbhū rasena tṛpto na kutaś canonaḥ |
10,8.44c tam eva vidvān na bibhāya mṛtyor ātmānaṃ dhīram ajaraṃ yuvānam ||44|| {29}



1aghāyatām api nahyā mukhāni sapatneṣu vajram arpayaitam |
1indreṇa dattā prathamā śataudanā bhrātṛvyaghnī yajamānasya gātuḥ ||1||

1vediṣ ṭe carma bhavatu barhir lomāni yāni te |
1eṣā tvā raśanāgrabhīd grāvā tvaiṣo 'dhi nṛtyatu ||2||

1bālās te prokṣaṇīḥ santu jīhvā saṃ mārṣṭu aghnye |
1śuddhā tvaṃ yajñiyā bhūtvā divaṃ prehi śataudane ||3||

1yaḥ śataudanāṃ pacati kāmapreṇa sa kalpate |
1prītā hy asya ṛtvijaḥ sarve yanti yathāyatham ||4||

1sa svargam ā rohati yatrādas tridivaṃ divaḥ |
1apūpanābhiṃ kṛtvā yo dadāti śataudanām ||5||
1sa tāṃl lokānt sam āpnoti ye divyā ye ca pārthivāḥ |
1hiraṇyajyotiṣaṃ kṛtvā yo dadāti śataudanām ||6||

1ye te devi śamitāraḥ paktāro ye ca te janāḥ |
1te tvā sarve gopsyanti maibhyo bhaiṣīḥ śataudane ||7||

1vasavas tvā dakṣiṇata uttarān marutas tvā |
1ādityāḥ paścād gopsyanti sāgniṣṭomam ati drava ||8||

1devāḥ pitaro manuṣyā gandharvāpsarasaś ca ye |
1te tvā sarve gopsyanti sātirātram ati drava ||9||

10,9.10a antarikṣaṃ divaṃ bhūmim ādityān maruto diśaḥ |
10,9.10c lokānt sa sarvān āpnoti yo dadāti śataudanām ||10|| {30}

10,9.11a ghṛtaṃ prokṣantī subhagā devī devān gamiṣyati |
10,9.11c paktāram aghnye mā hiṃsīr divaṃ prehi śataudane ||11||

10,9.12a ye devā diviṣado antarikṣasadaś ca ye ye ceme bhūmyām adhi |
10,9.12c tebhyas tvaṃ dhukṣva sarvadā kṣīraṃ sarpir atho madhu ||12||

10,9.13a yat te śiro yat te mukhaṃ yau karṇau ye ca te hanū |
10,9.13c āmikṣāṃ duhratāṃ dātre kṣīraṃ sarpir atho madhu ||13||

10,9.14a yau ta oṣṭhau ye nāsike ye śṛṅge ye ca te 'kṣiṇī |
10,9.14c āmikṣāṃ duhratāṃ dātre kṣīraṃ sarpir atho madhu ||14||

10,9.15a yat te klomā yad dhṛdayaṃ purītat sahakaṇṭhikā |
10,9.15c āmikṣāṃ duhratāṃ dātre kṣīraṃ sarpir atho madhu ||15||

10,9.16a yat te yakṛd ye matasne yad āntram yāś ca te gudāḥ |
10,9.16c āmikṣāṃ duhratāṃ dātre kṣīraṃ sarpir atho madhu ||16||

10,9.17a yas te plāśir yo vaniṣṭhur yau kukṣī yac ca carma te |
10,9.17c āmikṣāṃ duhratāṃ dātre kṣīraṃ sarpir atho madhu ||17||

10,9.18a yat te majjā yad asthi yan maṃsaṃ yac ca lohitam |
10,9.18c āmikṣāṃ duhratāṃ dātre kṣīraṃ sarpir atho madhu ||18||

10,9.19a yau te bāhū ye doṣaṇī yāv aṃsau yā ca te kakut |
10,9.19c āmikṣāṃ duhratāṃ dātre kṣīraṃ sarpir atho madhu ||19||

10,9.20a yās te grīvā ye skandhā yāḥ pṛṣṭīr yāś ca parśavaḥ |
10,9.20c āmikṣāṃ duhratāṃ dātre kṣīraṃ sarpir atho madhu ||20|| {31}

10,9.21a yau ta urū aṣṭhīvantau ye śroṇī yā ca te bhasat |
10,9.21c āmikṣāṃ duhratāṃ dātre kṣīraṃ sarpir atho madhu ||21||

10,9.22a yat te puchaṃ ye te bālā yad ūdho ye ca te stanāḥ |
10,9.22c āmikṣāṃ duhratāṃ dātre kṣīraṃ sarpir atho madhu ||22||

10,9.23a yās te jaṅghāḥ yāḥ kuṣṭhikā ṛcharā ye ca te śaphāḥ |
10,9.23c āmikṣāṃ duhratāṃ dātre kṣīraṃ sarpir atho madhu ||23||

10,9.24a yat te carma śataudane yāni lomāny aghnye |
10,9.24c āmikṣāṃ duhratāṃ dātre kṣīraṃ sarpir atho madhu ||24||

10,9.25a kroḍau te stāṃ purodāśāv ājyenābhighāritau |
10,9.25c tau pakṣau devi kṛtvā sā paktāraṃ divaṃ vaha ||25||

10,9.26a ulūkhale musale yaś ca carmaṇi yo vā śūrpe taṇḍulaḥ kaṇaḥ |
10,9.26c yaṃ vā vāto mātariśvā pavamāno mamāthāgniṣ ṭad dhotā suhutaṃ kṛṇotu ||26||

10,9.27a apo devīr madhumatīr ghṛtaścuto brahmaṇāṃ hasteṣu prapṛthak sādayāmi |
10,9.27c yatkāma idam abhiṣiñcāmi vo 'haṃ tan me sarvaṃ saṃ padyatāṃ vayaṃ syāma patayo rayīṇām ||27|| {32}



1namas te jāyamānāyai jātāyā uta te namaḥ |
1bālebhyaḥ śaphebhyo rūpāyāghnye te namaḥ ||1||

1yo vidyāt sapta pravataḥ sapta vidyāt parāvataḥ |
1śiro yajñasya yo vidyāt sa vaśāṃ prati gṛhṇīyāt ||2||

1vedāhaṃ sapta pravataḥ sapta veda parāvataḥ |
1śiro yajñasyāhaṃ veda somaṃ cāsyāṃ vicakṣaṇam ||3||

1yayā dyaur yayā pṛthivī yayāpo gupitā imāḥ |
1vaśāṃ sahasradhārāṃ brahmaṇāchāvadāmasi ||4||

1śataṃ kaṃsāḥ śataṃ dogdhāraḥ śataṃ goptāro adhi pṛṣṭhe asyāḥ |
1ye devās tasyāṃ prāṇanti te vaśāṃ vidur ekadhā ||5||

1yajñapadīrākṣīrā svadhāprāṇā mahīlukā |
1vaśā parjanyapatnī devāṃ apy eti brahmaṇā ||6||

1anu tvāgniḥ prāviśad anu somo vaśe tvā |
1ūdhas te bhadre parjanyo vidyutas te stanā vaśe ||7||

1apas tvaṃ dhukṣe prathamā urvarā aparā vaśe |
1tṛtīyaṃ rāṣṭraṃ dhukṣe 'nnaṃ kṣīraṃ vaśe tvam ||8||

1yad ādityair hūyamānopātiṣṭha ṛtavari |
1indraḥ sahasraṃ pātrānt somaṃ tvāpāyayad vaśe ||9||

10,10.10a yad anūcīndram air āt tvā ṛṣabho 'hvayat |
10,10.10c tasmāt te vṛtrahā payaḥ kṣīraṃ kruddho 'harad vaśe ||10|| {33}

10,10.11a yat te kruddho dhanapatir ā kṣīram aharad vaśe |
10,10.11c idaṃ tad adya nākas triṣu pātreṣu rakṣati ||11||

10,10.12a triṣu pātreṣu taṃ somam ā devy aharad vaśā |
10,10.12c atharvā yatra dīkṣito barhiṣy āsta hiraṇyaye ||12||

10,10.13a saṃ hi somenāgata sam u sarveṇa padvatā |
10,10.13c vaśā samudram adhy aṣṭhad gandharvaiḥ kalibhiḥ saha ||13||

10,10.14a saṃ hi vātenāgata sam u sarvaiḥ patatribhiḥ |
10,10.14c vaśā samudre prānṛtyad ṛcaḥ sāmāni bibhratī ||14||

10,10.15a saṃ hi sūryeṇāgata sam u sarveṇa cakṣuṣā |
10,10.15c vaśā samudram aty akhyad bhadrā jyotīṃṣi bibhratī ||15||

10,10.16a abhīvṛtā hiraṇyena yad atiṣṭha ṛtāvari |
10,10.16c aśvaḥ samudro bhūtvādhy askandad vaśe tvā ||16||

10,10.17a tad bhadrāḥ sam agachanta vaśā deṣṭry atho svadhā |
10,10.17c atharvā yatra dīkṣito barhiṣy āsta hiraṇyaye ||17||

10,10.18a vaśā mātā rājanyasya vaśā mātā svadhe tava |
10,10.18c vaśāyā yajña āyudhaṃ tataś cittam ajāyata ||18||

10,10.19a ūrdhvo bindur ud acarad brahmaṇaḥ kakudād adhi |
10,10.19c tatas tvaṃ jajñiṣe vaśe tato hotājāyata ||19||

10,10.20a āsnas te gāthā abhavann uṣṇihābhyo balaṃ vaśe |
10,10.20c pājasyāj jajñe yajña stanebhyo raśmayas tava ||20|| {34}

10,10.21a īrmābhyām ayanaṃ jātaṃ sakthibhyāṃ ca vaśe tava |
10,10.21c āntrebhyo jajñire atrā udarād adhi vīrudhaḥ ||21||

10,10.22a yad udaraṃ varuṇasyānuprāviśathā vaśe |
10,10.22c tatas tvā brahmod ahvayat sa hi netram avet tava ||22||

10,10.23a sarve garbhād avepanta jāyamānād asūsvaḥ |
10,10.23c sasūva hi tām āhu vaśeti brahmabhiḥ kḷptaḥ sa hy asyā bandhuḥ ||23||

10,10.24a yudha ekaḥ saṃ sṛjati yo asyā eka id vaśī |
10,10.24c tarāṃsi yajñā abhavan tarasāṃ cakṣur abhavad vaśā ||24||

10,10.25a vaśā yajñaṃ praty agṛhṇād vaśā sūryam adhārayat |
10,10.25c vaśāyām antar aviśad odano brahmaṇā saha ||25||

10,10.26a vaśām evāmṛtam āhur vaśāṃ mṛtyum upāsate |
10,10.26c vaśedaṃ sarvam abhavad devā manuṣyā asurāḥ pitara ṛṣayaḥ ||26||

10,10.27a ya evaṃ vidyāt sa vaśāṃ prati gṛhṇīyāt |
10,10.27c tathā hi yajñaḥ sarvapād duhe dātre 'napasphuran ||27||

10,10.28a tisro jihvā varuṇasyāntar dīdyaty āsani |
10,10.28c tāsāṃ yā madhye rājati sā vaśā duṣpratigrahā ||28||

10,10.29a caturdhā reto abhavad vaśāyāḥ |
10,10.29c āpas turīyam amṛtaṃ turīyaṃ yajñas turīyaṃ paśavas turīyam ||29||

10,10.30a vaśā dyaur vaśā pṛthivī vaśā viṣṇuḥ prajāpatiḥ |
10,10.30c vaśāyā dugdham apibant sādhyā vasavaś ca ye ||30||

10,10.31a vaśāyā dugdhaṃ pītvā sādhyā vasavaś ca ye |
10,10.31c te vai bradhnasya viṣṭapi payo asyā upāsate ||31||

10,10.32a somam enām eke duhre ghṛtam eka upāsate |
10,10.32c ya evaṃ viduṣe vaśāṃ dadus te gatās tridivaṃ divaḥ ||32||

10,10.33a brāhmaṇebhyo vaśāṃ dattvā sarvāṃl lokānt sam aśnute |
10,10.33c ṛtaṃ hy asyām ārpitam api brahmātho tapaḥ ||33||

10,10.34a vaśāṃ devā upa jīvanti vaśāṃ manuṣyā uta |
10,10.34c vaśedaṃ sarvam abhavad yāvat sūryo vipaśyati ||34|| {35}




1agne jāyasvāditir nāthiteyaṃ brahmaudanaṃ pacati putrakāmā |
1saptaṛṣayo bhūtakṛtas te tvā manthantu prajayā saheha ||1||

1kṛṇuta dhūmaṃ vṛṣaṇaḥ sakhāyo 'droghāvitā vācam acha |
1ayam agniḥ pṛtanāṣāṭ suvīro yena devā asahanta dasyūn ||2||

1agne 'janiṣṭhā mahate vīryāya brahmaudanāya paktave jātavedaḥ |
1saptaṛṣayo bhūtakṛtas te tvājījanann asyai rayiṃ sarvavīraṃ ni yacha ||3||

1samiddho agne samidhā sam idhyasva vidvān devān yajñiyāṃ eha vakṣaḥ |
1tebhyo haviḥ śrapayaṃ jātaveda uttamaṃ nākam adhi rohayemam ||4||

1tredhā bhāgo nihito yaḥ purā vo devānāṃ pitṝṇāṃ martyānām |
1aṃśāṃ jānīdhvaṃ vi bhajāmi tān vo yo devānāṃ sa imāṃ pārayāti ||5||

1agne sahasvān abhibhūr abhīd asi nīco ny ubja dviṣataḥ sapatnān |
1iyaṃ mātrā mīyamānā mitā ca sajātāṃs te balihṛtaḥ kṛṇotu ||6||

1sākaṃ sajātaiḥ payasā sahaidhy ud ubjaināṃ mahate vīryāya |
1ūrdhvo nākasyādhi roha viṣṭapaṃ svargo loka iti yaṃ vadanti ||7||

1iyaṃ mahī prati gṛhṇātu carma pṛthivī devī sumanasyamānā |
1atha gachema sukṛtasya lokam ||8||

1etau grāvāṇau sayujā yuṅdhi carmaṇi nirbindhy aṃśūn yajamānāya sādhu |
1avaghnatī ni jahi ya imāṃ pṛtanyava ūrdhvaṃ prajām udbharanty ud ūha ||9||

11,1.10a gṛhāṇa grāvāṇau sakṛtau vīra hasta ā te devā yajñiyā yajñam aguḥ |
11,1.10c trayo varā yatamāṃs tvaṃ vṛṇīṣe tās te samṛddhīr iha rādhayāmi ||10|| {1}

11,1.11a iyaṃ te dhītir idam u te janitraṃ gṛhṇātu tvām aditiḥ śūraputrā |
11,1.11c parā punīhi ya imāṃ pṛtanyavo 'syai rayiṃ sarvavīraṃ ni yacha ||11||

11,1.12a upaśvase druvaye sīdatā yūyaṃ vi vicyadhvaṃ yajñiyāsas tuṣaiḥ |
11,1.12c śriyā samānān ati sarvānt syāmādhaspadaṃ dviṣatas pādayāmi ||12||

11,1.13a parehi nāri punar ehi kṣipram apāṃ tvā goṣṭho adhy arukṣad bharāya |
11,1.13c tāsāṃ gṛhṇītād yatamā yajñiyā asan vibhājya dhīrītarā jahītāt ||13||

11,1.14a emā agur yoṣitaḥ śumbhamānā ut tiṣṭha nāri tavasaṃ rabhasva |
11,1.14c supatnī patyā prajayā prajāvaty ā tvāgan yajñaḥ prati kumbhaṃ gṛbhāya ||14||

11,1.15a ūrjo bhāgo nihito yaḥ purā va ṛṣipraśiṣṭāpa ā bharaitāḥ |
11,1.15c ayaṃ yajño gātuvin nāthavit prajāvid ugraḥ paśuvid vīravid vo astu ||15||

11,1.16a agne carur yajñiyas tvādhy arukṣac chucis tapiṣṭhas tapasā tapainam |
11,1.16c ārṣeyā daivā abhisaṃgatya bhāgam imaṃ tapiṣṭhā ṛtubhis tapantu ||16||

11,1.17a śuddhāḥ pūtā yoṣito yajñiyā imā āpaś carum ava sarpantu śubhrāḥ |
11,1.17c aduḥ prajāṃ bahulāṃ paśūn naḥ paktaudanasya sukṛtām etu lokam ||17||

11,1.18a brahmaṇā śuddhā uta pūtā ghṛtena somasyāṃśavas taṇḍulā yajñiyā ime |
11,1.18c apaḥ pra viśata prati gṛhṇātu vaś carur imaṃ paktvā sukṛtām eta lokam ||18||

11,1.19a uruḥ prathasva mahatā mahimnā sahasrapṛṣṭhaḥ sukṛtasya loke |
11,1.19c pitāmahāḥ pitaraḥ prajopajāhaṃ paktā pañcadaśas te asmi ||19||

11,1.20a sahasrapṛṣṭhaḥ śatadhāro akṣito brahmaudano devayānaḥ svargaḥ |
11,1.20c amūṃs ta ā dadhāmi prajayā reṣayainān balihārāya mṛḍatān mahyam eva ||20|| {2}

11,1.21a udehi vediṃ prajayā vardhayaināṃ nudasva rakṣaḥ prataraṃ dhehy enām |
11,1.21c śriyā samānān ati sarvānt syāmādhaspadaṃ dviṣatas pādayāmi ||21||

11,1.22a abhyāvartasva paśubhiḥ sahaināṃ pratyaṅṅ enāṃ devatābhiḥ sahaidhi |
11,1.22c mā tvā prāpac chapatho mābhicāraḥ sve kṣetre anamīvā vi rāja ||22||

11,1.23a ṛtena taṣṭā manasā hitaiṣā brahmaudanasya vihitā vedir agre |
11,1.23c aṃsadhrīṃ śuddhām upa dhehi nāri tatraudanaṃ sādaya daivānām ||23||

11,1.24a aditer hastāṃ srucam etāṃ dvitīyāṃ saptaṛṣayo bhūtakṛto yām akṛṇvan |
11,1.24c sā gātrāṇi viduṣy odanasya darvir vedyām adhy enaṃ cinotu ||24||

11,1.25a śṛtaṃ tvā havyam upa sīdantu daivā niḥsṛpyāgneḥ punar enān pra sīda |
11,1.25c somena pūto jaṭhare sīda brahmaṇām ārṣeyās te mā riṣan prāśitāraḥ ||25||

11,1.26a soma rājant saṃjñānam ā vapaibhyaḥ subrāhmaṇā yatame tvopasīdān |
11,1.26c ṛṣīn ārṣeyāṃs tapaso 'dhi jātān brahmaudane suhavā johavīmi ||26||

11,1.27a śuddhāḥ pūtā yoṣito yajñiyā imā brahmaṇāṃ hasteṣu prapṛthak sādayāmi |
11,1.27c yatkāma idam abhiṣiñcāmi vo 'ham indro marutvānt sa dadād idaṃ me ||27||

11,1.28a idaṃ me jyotir amṛtaṃ hiraṇyaṃ pakvaṃ kṣetrāt kāmadughā ma eṣā |
11,1.28c idaṃ dhanaṃ ni dadhe brāhmaṇeṣu kṛṇve panthāṃ pitṛṣu yaḥ svargaḥ ||28||

11,1.29a agnau tuṣān ā vapa jātavedasi paraḥ kambūkāṃ apa mṛḍḍhi dūram |
11,1.29c etaṃ śuśruma gṛharājasya bhāgam atho vidma nirṛter bhāgadheyam ||29||

11,1.30a śrāmyataḥ pacato viddhi sunvataḥ panthāṃ svargam adhi rohayainam |
11,1.30c yena rohāt param āpadya yad vaya uttamaṃ nākaṃ paramaṃ vyoma ||30|| {3}

11,1.31a babhrer adhvaryo mukham etad vi mṛḍḍhy ājyāya lokaṃ kṛṇuhi pravidvān |
11,1.31c ghṛtena gātrānu sarvā vi mṛḍḍhi kṛṇve panthāṃ pitṛṣu yaḥ svargaḥ ||31||

11,1.32a babhre rakṣaḥ samadam ā vapaibhyo 'brāhmaṇā yatame tvopasīdān |
11,1.32c purīṣiṇaḥ prathamānāḥ purastād ārṣeyās te mā riṣan prāśitāraḥ ||32||

11,1.33a ārṣeyeṣu ni dadha odana tvā nānārṣeyāṇām apy asty atra |
11,1.33c agnir me goptā marutaś ca sarve viśve devā abhi rakṣantu pakvam ||33||

11,1.34a yajñaṃ duhānaṃ sadam it prapīnaṃ pumāṃsaṃ dhenuṃ sadanaṃ rayīṇām |
11,1.34c prajāmṛtatvam uta dīrgham āyū rāyaś ca poṣair upa tvā sadema ||34||

11,1.35a vṛṣabho 'si svarga ṛṣīn ārṣeyān gacha |
11,1.35c sukṛtāṃ loke sīda tatra nau saṃskṛtam ||35||

11,1.36a samācinuṣvānusaṃprayāhy agne pathaḥ kalpaya devayānān |
11,1.36c etaiḥ sukṛtair anu gachema yajñaṃ nāke tiṣṭhantam adhi saptaraśmau ||36||

11,1.37a yena devā jyotiṣā dyām udāyan brahmaudanaṃ paktvā sukṛtasya lokam |
11,1.37c tena geṣma sukṛtasya lokaṃ svar ārohanto abhi nākam uttamam ||37|| {4}



1bhavāśarvau mṛḍataṃ mābhi yātaṃ bhūtapatī paśupatī namo vām |
1pratihitām āyatāṃ mā vi srāṣṭaṃ mā no hiṃsiṣṭaṃ dvipado mā catuṣpadaḥ ||1||

1śune kroṣṭre mā śarīrāṇi kartam aliklavebhyo gṛdhrebhyo ye ca kṛṣṇā aviṣyavaḥ |
1makṣikās te paśupate vayāṃsi te vighase mā vidanta ||2||

1krandāya te prāṇāya yāś ca te bhava ropayaḥ |
1namas te rudra kṛṇmaḥ sahasrākṣāyāmartya ||3||

1purastāt te namaḥ kṛṇma uttarād adharād uta |
1abhīvargād divas pary antarikṣāya te namaḥ ||4||

1mukhāya te paśupate yāni cakṣūṃṣi te bhava |
1tvace rūpāya saṃdṛśe pratīcīnāya te namaḥ ||5||

1aṅgebhyas ta udarāya jihvāyā āsyāya te |
1dadbhyo gandhāya te namaḥ ||6||

1astrā nīlaśikhaṇḍena sahasrākṣeṇa vājinā |
1rudreṇārdhakaghātinā tena mā sam arāmahi ||7||

1sa no bhavaḥ pari vṛṇaktu viśvata āpa ivāgniḥ pari vṛṇaktu no bhavaḥ |
1mā no 'bhi māṃsta namo astv asmai ||8||

1catur namo aṣṭakṛtvo bhavāya daśa kṛtvaḥ paśupate namas te |
1taveme pañca paśavo vibhaktā gāvo aśvāḥ puruṣā ajāvayaḥ ||9||

11,2.10a tava catasraḥ pradiśas tava dyaus tava pṛthivī tavedam ugrorv antarikṣam |
11,2.10c tavedaṃ sarvam ātmanvad yat prāṇat pṛthivīm anu ||10|| {5}

11,2.11a uruḥ kośo vasudhānas tavāyaṃ yasminn imā viśvā bhuvanāny antaḥ |
11,2.11c sa no mṛḍa paśupate namas te paraḥ kroṣṭāro abhibhāḥ śvānaḥ paro yantv agharudo vikeśyaḥ ||11||

11,2.12a dhanur bibharṣi haritaṃ hiraṇyayaṃ sahasraghniṃ śatavadhaṃ śikhaṇḍin |
11,2.12c rudrasyeṣuś carati devahetis tasyai namo yatamasyāṃ diśītaḥ ||12||

11,2.13a yo 'bhiyāto nilayate tvāṃ rudra nicikīrṣati |
11,2.13c paścād anuprayuṅkṣe taṃ viddhasya padanīr iva ||13||

11,2.14a bhavārudrau sayujā saṃvidānāv ubhāv ugrau carato vīryāya |
11,2.14c tābhyāṃ namo yatamasyāṃ diśītaḥ ||14||

11,2.15a namas te astv āyate namo astu parāyate |
11,2.15c namas te rudra tiṣṭhata āsīnāyota te namaḥ ||15||

11,2.16a namaḥ sāyaṃ namaḥ prātar namo rātryā namo divā |
11,2.16c bhavāya ca śarvāya cobhābhyām akaraṃ namaḥ ||16||

11,2.17a sahasrākṣam atipaśyaṃ purastād rudram asyantaṃ bahudhā vipaścitam |
11,2.17c mopārāma jihvayeyamānam ||17||

11,2.18a śyāvāśvaṃ kṛṣṇam asitaṃ mṛṇantaṃ bhīmaṃ rathaṃ keśinaḥ pādayantam |
11,2.18c pūrve pratīmo namo astv asmai ||18||

11,2.19a mā no 'bhi srā matyaṃ devahetiṃ mā naḥ krudhaḥ paśupate namas te |
11,2.19c anyatrāsmad divyāṃ śākhāṃ vi dhūnu ||19||

11,2.20a mā no hiṃsīr adhi no brūhi pari ṇo vṛṅdhi mā krudhaḥ |
11,2.20c mā tvayā sam arāmahi ||20|| {6}

11,2.21a mā no goṣu puruṣeṣu mā gṛdho no ajāviṣu |
11,2.21c anyatrogra vi vartaya piyārūṇāṃ prajāṃ jahi ||21||

11,2.22a yasya takmā kāsikā hetir ekam aśvasyeva vṛṣaṇaḥ kranda eti |
11,2.22c abhipūrvaṃ nirṇayate namo astv asmai ||22||

11,2.23a yo 'ntarikṣe tiṣṭhati viṣṭabhito 'yajvanaḥ pramṛṇan devapīyūn |
11,2.23c tasmai namo daśabhiḥ śakvarībhiḥ ||23||

11,2.24a tubhyam āraṇyāḥ paśavo mṛgā vane hitā haṃsāḥ suparṇāḥ śakunā vayāṃsi |
11,2.24c tava yakṣaṃ paśupate apsv antas tubhyaṃ kṣaranti divyā āpo vṛdhe ||24||

11,2.25a śiṃśumārā ajagarāḥ purīkayā jaṣā matsyā rajasā yebhyo asyasi |
11,2.25c na te dūraṃ na pariṣṭhāsti te bhava sadyaḥ sarvāṃ pari paśyasi bhūmiṃ pūrvasmād dhaṃsy uttarasmint samudre ||25||

11,2.26a mā no rudra takmanā mā viṣeṇa mā naḥ saṃ srā divyenāgninā |
11,2.26c anyatrāsmad vidyutaṃ pātayaitām ||26||

11,2.27a bhavo divo bhava īśe pṛthivyā bhava ā papra urv antarikṣam |
11,2.27c tasyai namo yatamasyāṃ diśītaḥ ||27||

11,2.28a bhava rājan yajamānāya mṛḍa paśūnāṃ hi paśupatir babhūtha |
11,2.28c yaḥ śraddadhāti santi devā iti catuṣpade dvipade 'sya mṛḍa ||28||

11,2.29a mā no mahāntam uta mā no arbhakaṃ mā no vahantam uta mā no vakṣyataḥ |
11,2.29c mā no hiṃsīḥ pitaraṃ mātaraṃ ca svāṃ tanvaṃ rudra mā rīriṣo naḥ ||29||

11,2.30a rudrasyailabakārebhyo 'saṃsūktagilebhyaḥ |
11,2.30c idaṃ mahāsyebhyaḥ śvabhyo akaraṃ namaḥ ||30||

11,2.31a namas te ghoṣiṇībhyo namas te keśinībhyaḥ |
11,2.31c namo namaskṛtābhyo namaḥ saṃbhuñjatībhyaḥ |
11,2.31e namas te deva senābhyaḥ svasti no abhayaṃ ca naḥ ||31|| {7}


1tasyaudanasya bṛhaspatiḥ śiro brahma mukham ||1||

1dyāvāpṛthivī śrotre sūryācandramasāv akṣiṇī saptaṛṣayaḥ prāṇāpānāḥ ||2||

1cakṣur musalaṃ kāma ulūkhalam ||3||

1ditiḥ śūrpam aditiḥ śūrpagrāhī vāto 'pāvinak ||4||

1aśvāḥ kaṇā gāvas taṇḍulā maśakās tuṣāḥ ||5||

1kabru phalīkaraṇāḥ śaro 'bhram ||6||

1śyāmam ayo 'sya māṃsāni lohitam asya lohitam ||7||

1trapu bhasma haritaṃ varṇaḥ puṣkaram asya gandhaḥ ||8||

1khalaḥ pātraṃ sphyāv aṃsāv īṣe anūkye ||9||

11,3.10a āntrāṇi jatravo gudā varatrāḥ ||10||

11,3.11a iyam eva pṛthivī kumbhī bhavati rādhyamānasyaudanasya dyaur apidhānam ||11||

11,3.12a sītāḥ parśavaḥ sikatā ūbadhyam ||12||

11,3.13a ṛtaṃ hastāvanejanaṃ kulyopasecanam ||13||

11,3.14a ṛcā kumbhy adhihitārtvijyena preṣitā ||14||

11,3.15a brahmaṇā parigṛhītā sāmnā paryūḍhā ||15||

11,3.16a bṛhad āyavanaṃ rathantaraṃ darviḥ ||16||

11,3.17a ṛtavaḥ paktāra ārtavāḥ sam indhate ||17||

11,3.18a caruṃ pañcabilam ukhaṃ gharmo 'bhīndhe ||18|| [note CORRIGENDA ed. ŚPP]
11,3.19a odanena yajñavataḥ sarve lokāḥ samāpyāḥ ||19||

11,3.20a yasmint samudro dyaur bhūmis trayo 'varaparaṃ śritāḥ ||20||

11,3.21a yasya devā akalpantocchiṣṭe ṣaḍ aśītayaḥ ||21||

11,3.22a taṃ tvaudanasya pṛchāmi yo asya mahimā mahān ||22||

11,3.23a sa ya odanasya mahimānaṃ vidyāt ||23||

11,3.24a nālpa iti brūyān nānupasecana iti nedaṃ ca kiṃ ceti ||24||

11,3.25a yāvad dātābhimanasyeta tan nāti vadet ||25||

11,3.26a brahmavādino vadanti parāñcam odanaṃ prāśī3ḥ pratyañcā3m iti ||26||

11,3.27a tvam odanaṃ prāśī3s tvām odanā3 iti ||27||

11,3.28a parāñcaṃ cainaṃ prāśīḥ prāṇās tvā hāsyantīty enam āha ||28||

11,3.29a pratyañcaṃ cainaṃ prāśīr apānās tvā hāsyantīty enam āha ||29||

11,3.30a naivāham odanaṃ na mām odanaḥ ||30||

11,3.31a odana evaudanaṃ prāśīt ||31|| {8}



11,3.32[4.1]a tataś cainam anyena śīrṣṇā prāśīr yena caitaṃ pūrva ṛṣayaḥ prāśnan |
11,3.32[4.1]b jyeṣṭhatas te prajā mariṣyatīty enam āha |
11,3.32[4.1]c taṃ vā ahaṃ nārvāñcaṃ na parāñcaṃ na pratyañcam |
11,3.32[4.1]d bṛhaspatinā śīrṣṇā |
11,3.32[4.1]e tenainaṃ prāśiṣaṃ tenainam ajīgamam |
11,3.32[4.1]f eṣa vā odanaḥ sarvāṅgaḥ sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ |
11,3.32[4.1]g sarvāṅga eva sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ saṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||32|| [1]

11,3.33[4.2]a tataś cainam anyābhyāṃ śrotrābhyāṃ prāśīr yābhyāṃ caitaṃ pūrva ṛṣayaḥ prāśnan |

11,3.33[4.2]e tābhyām enaṃ prāśiṣaṃ tābhyām enam ajīgamam |

11,3.46[4.15]e tābhyām enaṃ prāśiṣaṃ tābhyām enam ajīgamam |
11,3.46[4.15]f eṣa vā odanaḥ sarvāṅgaḥ sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ |
11,3.46[4.15]g sarvāṅga eva sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ saṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||46|| [15]

11,3.47[4.16]a tataś cainam anyābhyāṃ prapadābhyāṃ prāśīr yābhyāṃ caitaṃ pūrva ṛṣayaḥ prāśnan |
11,3.47[4.16]b sarpas tvā haniṣyatīty enam āha |
11,3.47[4.16]c taṃ vā ahaṃ nārvāñcaṃ na parāñcaṃ na pratyañcam |
11,3.47[4.16]d savituḥ prapadābhyām |
11,3.47[4.16]e tābhyām enaṃ prāśiṣaṃ tābhyām enam ajīgamam |
11,3.47[4.16]f eṣa vā odanaḥ sarvāṅgaḥ sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ |
11,3.47[4.16]g sarvāṅga eva sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ saṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||47|| [16]

11,3.48[4.17]a tataś cainam anyābhyāṃ hastābhyāṃ prāśīr yābhyāṃ caitaṃ pūrva ṛṣayaḥ prāśnan |
11,3.48[4.17]b brāhmaṇaṃ haniṣyasīty enam āha |
11,3.48[4.17]c taṃ vā ahaṃ nārvāñcaṃ na parāñcaṃ na pratyañcam |
11,3.48[4.17]d ṛtasya hastābhyām |
11,3.48[4.17]e tābhyām enaṃ prāśiṣaṃ tābhyām enam ajīgamam |
11,3.48[4.17]f eṣa vā odanaḥ sarvāṅgaḥ sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ |
11,3.48[4.17]g sarvāṅga eva sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ saṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||48|| [17]

11,3.49[4.18]a tataś cainam anyayā pratiṣṭhayā prāśīr yayā caitaṃ pūrva ṛṣayaḥ prāśnan |
11,3.49[4.18]b apratiṣṭhāno 'nāyatano mariṣyasīty enam āha |
11,3.49[4.18]c taṃ vā ahaṃ nārvāñcaṃ na parāñcaṃ na pratyañcam |
11,3.49[4.18]d satye pratiṣṭhāya |
11,3.49[4.18]e tayainaṃ prāśiṣaṃ tayainam ajīgamam |
11,3.49[4.18]f eṣa vā odanaḥ sarvāṅgaḥ sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ |
11,3.49[4.18]g sarvāṅga eva sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ saṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||49|| [18] {9}



11,3.50[5.1]a etad vai bradhnasya viṣṭapaṃ yad odanaḥ ||50|| [1]

11,3.51[5.2]a bradhnaloko bhavati bradhnasya viṣṭapi śrayate ya evaṃ veda ||51|| [2]

11,3.52[5.3]a etasmād vā odanāt trayastriṃśataṃ lokān nir amimīta prajāpatiḥ ||52|| [3]

11,3.53[5.4]a teṣāṃ prajñānāya yajñam asṛjata ||53|| [4]

11,3.54[5.5]a sa ya evaṃ viduṣa upadraṣṭā bhavati prāṇaṃ ruṇaddhi ||54|| [5]

11,3.55[5.6]a na ca prāṇaṃ ruṇaddhi sarvajyāniṃ jīyate ||55|| [6]

11,3.56[5.7]a na ca sarvajyāniṃ jīyate purainaṃ jarasaḥ prāṇo jahāti ||56|| [7] {10}



11,4[6].1a prāṇāya namo yasya sarvam idaṃ vaśe |
11,4[6].1c yo bhūtaḥ sarvasyeśvaro yasmint sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ||1||

11,4[6].2a namas te prāṇa krandāya namas te stanayitnave |
11,4[6].2c namas te prāṇa vidyute namas te prāṇa varṣate ||2||

11,4[6].3a yat prāṇa stanayitnunābhikrandaty oṣadhīḥ |
11,4[6].3c pra vīyante garbhān dadhate 'tho bahvīr vi jāyante ||3||

11,4[6].4a yat prāṇa ṛtāv āgate 'bhikrandaty oṣadhīḥ |
11,4[6].4c sarvaṃ tadā pra modate yat kiṃ ca bhūmyām adhi ||4||
11,4[6].5a yadā prāṇo abhyavarṣīd varṣeṇa pṛthivīṃ mahīm |
11,4[6].5c paśavas tat pra modante maho vai no bhaviṣyati ||5||

11,4[6].6a abhivṛṣṭā oṣadhayaḥ prāṇena sam avādiran |
11,4[6].6c āyur vai naḥ prātītaraḥ sarvā naḥ surabhīr akaḥ ||6||

11,4[6].7a namas te astv āyate namo astu parāyate |
11,4[6].7c namas te prāṇa tiṣṭhata āsīnāyota te namaḥ ||7||

11,4[6].8a namas te prāṇa prāṇate namo astv apānate |
11,4[6].8c parācīnāya te namaḥ pratīcīnāya te namaḥ sarvasmai ta idaṃ namaḥ ||8||

11,4[6].9a yā te prāṇa priyā tanūr yo te prāṇa preyasī |
11,4[6].9c atho yad bheṣajaṃ tava tasya no dhehi jīvase ||9||
11,4[6].10a prāṇaḥ prajā anu vaste pitā putram iva priyam |
11,4[6].10c prāṇo ha sarvasyeśvaro yac ca prāṇati yac ca na ||10|| {11}

11,4[6].11a prāṇo mṛtyuḥ prāṇas takmā prāṇaṃ devā upāsate |
11,4[6].11c prāṇo ha satyavādinam uttame loka ā dadhat ||11||

11,4[6].12a prāṇo virāṭ prāṇo deṣṭrī prāṇaṃ sarva upāsate |
11,4[6].12c prāṇo ha sūryaś candramāḥ prāṇam āhuḥ prajāpatim ||12||

11,4[6].13a prāṇāpānau vrīhiyavāv anaḍvān prāṇa ucyate |
11,4[6].13c yave ha prāṇa āhito 'pāno vrīhir ucyate ||13||

11,4[6].14a apānati prāṇati puruṣo garbhe antarā |
11,4[6].14c yadā tvaṃ prāṇa jinvasy atha sa jāyate punaḥ ||14||

11,4[6].15a prāṇam āhur mātariśvānaṃ vāto ha prāṇa ucyate |
11,4[6].15c prāṇe ha bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ ca prāṇe sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ||15||

11,4[6].16a ātharvaṇīr āṅgirasīr daivīr manuṣyajā uta |
11,4[6].16c oṣadhayaḥ pra jāyante yadā tvaṃ prāṇa jinvasi ||16||

11,4[6].17a yadā prāṇo abhyavarṣīd varṣeṇa pṛthivīṃ mahīm |
11,4[6].17c oṣadhayaḥ pra jāyante 'tho yāḥ kāś ca vīrudhaḥ ||17||

11,4[6].18a yas te prāṇedaṃ veda yasmiṃś cāsi pratiṣṭhitaḥ |
11,4[6].18c sarve tasmai baliṃ harān amuṣmiṃl loka uttame ||18||

11,4[6].19a yathā prāṇa balihṛtas tubhyaṃ sarvāḥ prajā imāḥ |
11,4[6].19c evā tasmai baliṃ harān yas tvā śṛṇavat suśravaḥ ||19||

11,4[6].20a antar garbhaś carati devatāsv ābhūto bhūtaḥ sa u jāyate punaḥ |
11,4[6].20c sa bhūto bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyat pitā putraṃ pra viveśā śacībhiḥ ||20|| {12}

11,4[6].21a ekaṃ pādaṃ not khidati salilād dhaṃsa uccaran |
11,4[6].21c yad aṅga sa tam utkhiden naivādya na śvaḥ syāt |
11,4[6].21e na rātrī nāhaḥ syān na vy uchet kadā cana ||21||

11,4[6].22a aṣṭācakraṃ vartata ekanemi sahasrākṣaraṃ pra puro ni paścā |
11,4[6].22c ardhena viśvaṃ bhuvanaṃ jajāna yad asyārdhaṃ katamaḥ sa ketuḥ ||22||

11,4[6].23a yo asya viśvajanmana īśe viśvasya ceṣṭataḥ |
11,4[6].23c anyeṣu kṣipradhanvane tasmai prāṇa namo 'stu te ||23||

11,4[6].24a yo asya sarvajanmana īśe sarvasya ceṣṭataḥ |
11,4[6].24c atandro brahmaṇā dhīraḥ prāṇo mānu tiṣṭhatu ||24||

11,4[6].25a ūrdhvaḥ supteṣu jāgāra nanu tiryaṅ ni padyate |
11,4[6].25c na suptam asya supteṣv anu śuśrāva kaś cana ||25||

11,4[6].26a prāṇa mā mat paryāvṛto na mad anyo bhaviṣyasi |
11,4[6].26c apāṃ garbham iva jīvase prāṇa badhnāmi tvā mayi ||26|| {13}



11,5[7].1a brahmacārīṣṇaṃś carati rodasī ubhe tasmin devāḥ saṃmanaso bhavanti |
11,5[7].1c sa dādhāra pṛthivīṃ divaṃ ca sa ācāryaṃ tapasā piparti ||1||

11,5[7].2a brahmacāriṇaṃ pitaro devajanāḥ pṛthag devā anusaṃyanti sarve |
11,5[7].2c gandharvā enam anv āyan trayastriṃśat triśatāḥ ṣaṭsahasrāḥ sarvānt sa devāṃs tapasā piparti ||2||

11,5[7].3a ācārya upanayamāno brahmacāriṇaṃ kṛṇute garbham antaḥ |
11,5[7].3c taṃ rātrīs tisra udare bibharti taṃ jātaṃ draṣṭum abhisaṃyanti devāḥ ||3||

11,5[7].4a iyaṃ samit pṛthivī dyaur dvitīyotāntarikṣaṃ samidhā pṛṇāti |
11,5[7].4c brahmacārī samidhā mekhalayā śrameṇa lokāṃs tapasā piparti ||4||

11,5[7].5a pūrvo jāto brahmaṇo brahmacārī gharmaṃ vasānas tapasod atiṣṭhat |
11,5[7].5c tasmāj jātaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ brahma jyeṣṭhaṃ devāś ca sarve amṛtena sākam ||5||

11,5[7].6a brahmacāry eti samidhā samiddhaḥ kārṣṇaṃ vasāno dīkṣito dīrghaśmaśruḥ |
11,5[7].6c sa sadya eti pūrvasmād uttaraṃ samudraṃ lokānt saṃgṛbhya muhur ācarikrat ||6||

11,5[7].7a brahmacārī janayan brahmāpo lokaṃ prajāpatiṃ parameṣṭhinaṃ virājam |
11,5[7].7c garbho bhūtvāmṛtasya yonāv indro ha bhūtvāsurāṃs tatarha ||7||

11,5[7].8a ācāryas tatakṣa nabhasī ubhe ime urvī gambhīre pṛthivīṃ divaṃ ca |
11,5[7].8c te rakṣati tapasā brahmacārī tasmin devāḥ saṃmanaso bhavanti ||8||

11,5[7].9a imāṃ bhūmiṃ pṛthivīṃ brahmacārī bhikṣām ā jabhāra prathamo divaṃ ca |
11,5[7].9c te kṛtvā samidhāv upāste tayor ārpitā bhuvanāni viśvā ||9||

11,5[7].10a arvāg anyaḥ paro anyo divas pṛṣṭhād guhā nidhī nihitau brāhmaṇasya |
11,5[7].10c tau rakṣati tapasā brahmacārī tat kevalaṃ kṛṇute brahma vidvān ||10|| {14}

11,5[7].11a arvāg anya ito anyaḥ pṛthivyā agnī sameto nabhasī antareme |
11,5[7].11c tayoḥ śrayante raśmayo 'dhi dṛḍhās tān ā tiṣṭhati tapasā brahmacārī ||11||

11,5[7].12a abhikrandan stanayann aruṇaḥ śitiṅgo bṛhac chepo 'nu bhūmau jabhāra |
11,5[7].12c brahmacārī siñcati sānau retaḥ pṛthivyāṃ tena jīvanti pradiśaś catasraḥ ||12||

11,5[7].13a agnau sūrye candramasi mātariśvan brahmacāry apsu samidham ā dadhāti |
11,5[7].13c tāsām arcīṃṣi pṛthag abhre caranti tāsām ājyaṃ puruṣo varṣam āpaḥ ||13||

11,5[7].14a ācāryo mṛtyur varuṇaḥ soma oṣadhayaḥ payaḥ |
11,5[7].14c jīmūtā āsant satvānas tair idaṃ svar ābhṛtam ||14||

11,5[7].15a amā ghṛtaṃ kṛṇute kevalam ācāryo bhūtvā varuṇaḥ |
11,5[7].15c yadyad aichat prajāpatau tad brahmacārī prāyachat svān mitro adhy ātmanaḥ ||15||

11,5[7].16a ācāryo brahmacārī brahmacārī prajāpatiḥ |
11,5[7].16c prajāpatir vi rājati virāḍ indro 'bhavad vaśī ||16||

11,5[7].17a brahmacaryeṇa tapasā rājā rāṣṭraṃ vi rakṣati |
11,5[7].17c ācāryo brahmacaryeṇa brahmacāriṇam ichate ||17||

11,5[7].18a brahmacaryeṇa kanyā yuvānaṃ vindate patim |
11,5[7].18c anaḍvān brahmacaryeṇāśvo ghāsaṃ jigīṣati ||18||

11,5[7].19a brahmacaryeṇa tapasā devā mṛtyum apāghnata |
11,5[7].19c indro ha brahmacaryeṇa devebhyaḥ svar ābharat ||19||

11,5[7].20a oṣadhayo bhūtabhavyam ahorātre vanaspatiḥ |
11,5[7].20c saṃvatsaraḥ saha ṛtubhis te jātā brahmacāriṇaḥ ||20|| {15}

11,5[7].21a pārthivā divyāḥ paśava āraṇyā grāmyāś ca ye |
11,5[7].21c apakṣāḥ pakṣiṇaś ca ye te jātā brahmacāriṇaḥ ||21||

11,5[7].22a pṛthak sarve prājāpatyāḥ prāṇān ātmasu bibhrati |
11,5[7].22c tānt sarvān brahma rakṣati brahmacāriṇy ābhṛtam ||22||

11,5[7].23a devānām etat pariṣūtam anabhyārūḍhaṃ carati rocamānam |
11,5[7].23c tasmāj jātaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ brahma jyeṣṭhaṃ devāś ca sarve amṛtena sākam ||23||

11,5[7].24a brahmacārī brahma bhrājad bibharti tasmin devā adhi viśve samotāḥ |
11,5[7].24c prāṇāpānau janayann ād vyānaṃ vācaṃ mano hṛdayaṃ brahma medhām ||24||

11,5[7].25a cakṣuḥ śrotraṃ yaśo asmāsu dhehy annaṃ reto lohitam udaram ||25||

11,5[7].26a tāni kalpan brahmacārī salilasya pṛṣṭhe tapo 'tiṣṭhat tapyamānaḥ samudre |
11,5[7].26c sa snāto babhruḥ piṅgalaḥ pṛthivyāṃ bahu rocate ||26|| {16}



11,6[8].1a agniṃ brūmo vanaspatīn oṣadhīr uta vīrudhaḥ |
11,6[8].1c indraṃ bṛhaspatiṃ sūryaṃ te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ||1||

11,6[8].2a brūmo rājānaṃ varuṇaṃ mitraṃ viṣṇum atho bhagam |
11,6[8].2c aṃśaṃ vivasvantaṃ brūmas te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ||2||

11,6[8].3a brūmo devaṃ savitāraṃ dhātāram uta pūṣaṇam |
11,6[8].3c tvaṣṭāram agriyaṃ brūmas te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ||3||

11,6[8].4a gandharvāpsaraso brūmo aśvinā brahmaṇaspatim |
11,6[8].4c aryamā nāma yo devas te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ||4||

11,6[8].5a ahorātre idaṃ brūmaḥ sūryācandramasāv ubhā |
11,6[8].5c viśvān ādityān brūmas te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ||5||

11,6[8].6a vātaṃ brūmaḥ parjanyam antarikṣam atho diśaḥ |
11,6[8].6c āśāś ca sarvā brūmas te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ||6||

11,6[8].7a muñcantu mā śapathyād ahorātre atho uṣāḥ |
11,6[8].7c somo mā devo muñcatu yam āhuś candramā iti ||7||

11,6[8].8a pārthivā divyāḥ paśava āraṇyā uta ye mṛgāḥ |
11,6[8].8c śakuntān pakṣiṇo brūmas te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ||8||

11,6[8].9a bhavāśarvāv idaṃ brūmo rudraṃ paśupatiś ca yaḥ |
11,6[8].9c iṣūr yā eṣāṃ saṃvidma tā naḥ santu sadā śivāḥ ||9||

11,6[8].10a divaṃ brūmo nakṣatrāṇi bhūmiṃ yakṣāṇi parvatān |
11,6[8].10c samudrā nadyo veśantās te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ||10|| {17}

11,6[8].11a saptaṛṣīn vā idaṃ brūmo 'po devīḥ prajāpatim |
11,6[8].11c pitṝn yamaśreṣṭhān brūmas te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ |11||

11,6[8].12a ye devā diviṣado antarikṣasadaś ca ye |
11,6[8].12c pṛthivyāṃ śakrā ye śritās te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ||12||

11,6[8].13a ādityā rudrā vasavo divi devā atharvāṇaḥ |
11,6[8].13c aṅgiraso manīṣiṇas te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ||13||

11,6[8].14a yajñaṃ brūmo yajamānam ṛcaḥ sāmāni bheṣajā |
11,6[8].14c yajūṃṣi hotrā brūmas te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ||14||

11,6[8].15a pañca rājyāni vīrudhāṃ somaśreṣṭhāni brūmaḥ |
11,6[8].15c darbho bhaṅgo yavaḥ sahas te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ||15||

11,6[8].16a arāyān brūmo rakṣāṃsi sarpān puṇyajanān pitṝn |
11,6[8].16c mṛtyūn ekaśataṃ brūmas te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ||16||

11,6[8].17a ṛtūn brūma ṛtupatīn ārtavān uta hāyanān |
11,6[8].17c samāḥ saṃvatsarān māsāṃs te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ||17||

11,6[8].18a eta devā dakṣiṇataḥ paścāt prāñca udeta |
11,6[8].18c purastād uttarāc chakrā viśve devāḥ sametya te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ||18||

11,6[8].19a viśvān devān idaṃ brūmaḥ satyasandhān ṛtāvṛdhaḥ |
11,6[8].19c viśvābhiḥ patnībhiḥ saha te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ||19||

11,6[8].20a sarvān devān idaṃ brūmaḥ satyasandhān ṛtāvṛdhaḥ |
11,6[8].20c sarvābhiḥ patnībhiḥ saha te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ||20||

11,6[8].21a bhūtaṃ brūmo bhūtapatiṃ bhūtānām uta yo vaśī |
11,6[8].21c bhūtāni sarvā saṃgatya te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ||21||

11,6[8].22a yā devīḥ pañca pradiśo ye devā dvādaśa ṛtavaḥ |
11,6[8].22c saṃvatsarasya ye daṃṣṭrās te naḥ santu sadā śivāḥ ||22||

11,6[8].23a yan mātalī rathakrītam amṛtaṃ veda bheṣajam |
11,6[8].23c tad indro apsu prāveśayat tad āpo datta bheṣajam ||23|| {18}



11,7[9].1a ucchiṣṭe nāma rūpaṃ cocchiṣṭe loka āhitaḥ |
11,7[9].1c ucchiṣṭa indraś cāgniś ca viśvam antaḥ samāhitam ||1||

11,7[9].2a ucchiṣṭe dyāvāpṛthivī viśvaṃ bhūtaṃ samāhitam |
11,7[9].2c āpaḥ samudra ucchiṣṭe candramā vāta āhitaḥ ||2||

11,7[9].3a sann ucchiṣṭe asaṃś cobhau mṛtyur vājaḥ prajāpatiḥ |
11,7[9].3c laukyā ucchiṣṭa āyattā vraś ca draś cāpi śrīr mayi ||3||

11,7[9].4a dṛḍho dṛṃha sthiro nyo brahma viśvasṛjo daśa |
11,7[9].4c nābhim iva sarvataś cakram ucchiṣṭe devatāḥ śritāḥ ||4||

11,7[9].5a ṛk sāma yajur ucchiṣṭa udgīthaḥ prastutaṃ stutam |
11,7[9].5c hiṅkāra ucchiṣṭe svaraḥ sāmno meḍiś ca tan mayi ||5||

11,7[9].6a aindrāgnaṃ pāvamānaṃ mahānāmnīr mahāvratam |
11,7[9].6c ucchiṣṭe yajñasyāṅgāny antar garbha iva mātari ||6||

11,7[9].7a rājasūyaṃ vājapeyam agniṣṭomaṣ tad adhvaraḥ |
11,7[9].7c arkāśvamedhāv ucchiṣṭe jīvabarhir madintamaḥ ||7||

11,7[9].8a agnyādheyam atho dīkṣā kāmapraś chandasā saha |
11,7[9].8c utsannā yajñāḥ satrāṇy ucchiṣṭe 'dhi samāhitāḥ ||8||

11,7[9].9a agnihotraṃ ca śraddhā ca vaṣaṭkāro vrataṃ tapaḥ |
11,7[9].9c dakṣiṇeṣṭaṃ pūrtaṃ cocchiṣṭe 'dhi samāhitāḥ ||9||

11,7[9].10a ekarātro dvirātraḥ sadyaḥkrīḥ prakrīr ukthyaḥ |
11,7[9].10c otaṃ nihitam ucchiṣṭe yajñasyāṇūni vidyayā ||10|| {19}

11,7[9].11a catūrātraḥ pañcarātraḥ ṣaḍrātraś cobhayaḥ saha |
11,7[9].11c ṣoḍaśī saptarātraś cocchiṣṭāj jajñire sarve ye yajñā amṛte hitāḥ ||11||

11,7[9].12a pratīhāro nidhanaṃ viśvajic cābhijic ca yaḥ |
11,7[9].12c sāhnātirātrāv ucchiṣṭe dvādaśāho 'pi tan mayi ||12||

11,7[9].13a sūnṛtā saṃnatiḥ kṣemaḥ svadhorjāmṛtaṃ sahaḥ |
11,7[9].13c ucchiṣṭe sarve pratyañcaḥ kāmāḥ kāmena tātṛpuḥ ||13||

11,7[9].14a nava bhūmīḥ samudrā ucchiṣṭe 'dhi śritā divaḥ |
11,7[9].14c ā sūryo bhāty ucchiṣṭe 'horātre api tan mayi ||14||
11,7[9].15a upahavyaṃ viṣūvantaṃ ye ca yajñā guhā hitāḥ |
11,7[9].15c bibharti bhartā viśvasyocchiṣṭo janituḥ pitā ||15||

11,7[9].16a pitā janitur ucchiṣṭo 'soḥ pautraḥ pitāmahaḥ |
11,7[9].16c sa kṣiyati viśvasyeśāno vṛṣā bhūmyām atighnyaḥ ||16||

11,7[9].17a ṛtaṃ satyaṃ tapo rāṣṭraṃ śramo dharmaś ca karma ca |
11,7[9].17c bhūtaṃ bhaviṣyad ucchiṣṭe vīryaṃ lakṣmīr balaṃ bale ||17||

11,7[9].18a samṛddhir oja ākūtiḥ kṣatraṃ rāṣṭraṃ ṣaḍ urvyaḥ |
11,7[9].18c saṃvatsaro 'dhy ucchiṣṭa iḍā praiṣā grahā haviḥ ||18||

11,7[9].19a caturhotāra āpriyaś cāturmāsyāni nīvidaḥ |
11,7[9].19c ucchiṣṭe yajñā hotrāḥ paśubandhās tad iṣṭayaḥ ||19||

11,7[9].20a ardhamāsāś ca māsāś cārtavā ṛtubhiḥ saha |
11,7[9].20c ucchiṣṭe ghoṣiṇīr āpa stanayitnuḥ śrutir mahī ||20|| {20}

11,7[9].21a śarkarāḥ sikatā aśmāna oṣadhayo vīrudhas tṛṇā |
11,7[9].21c abhrāṇi vidyuto varṣam ucchiṣṭe saṃśritā śritā ||21||

11,7[9].22a rāddhiḥ prāptiḥ samāptir vyāptir maha edhatuḥ |
11,7[9].22c atyāptir ucchiṣṭe bhūtiś cāhitā nihitā hitā ||22||

11,7[9].23a yac ca prāṇati prāṇena yac ca paśyati cakṣuṣā |
11,7[9].23c ucchiṣṭāj jajñire sarve divi devā diviśritaḥ ||23||

11,7[9].24a ṛcaḥ sāmāni chandāṃsi purāṇaṃ yajuṣā saha |
11,7[9].24c ucchiṣṭāj jajñire sarve divi devā diviśritaḥ ||24||

11,7[9].25a prāṇāpānau cakṣuḥ śrotram akṣitiś ca kṣitiś ca yā |
11,7[9].25c ucchiṣṭāj jajñire sarve divi devā diviśritaḥ ||25||

11,7[9].26a ānandā modāḥ pramudo 'bhīmodamudaś ca ye |
11,7[9].26c ucchiṣṭāj jajñire sarve divi devā diviśritaḥ ||26||

11,7[9].27a devāḥ pitaro manuṣyā gandharvāpsarasaś ca ye |
11,7[9].27c ucchiṣṭāj jajñire sarve divi devā diviśritaḥ ||27|| {21}



11,8[10].1a yan manyur jāyām āvahat saṃkalpasya gṛhād adhi |
11,8[10].1c ka āsaṃ janyāḥ ke varāḥ ka u jyeṣṭhavaro 'bhavat ||1||

11,8[10].2a tapaś caivāstāṃ karma cāntar mahaty arṇave |
11,8[10].2c ta āsaṃ janyās te varā brahma jyeṣṭhavaro 'bhavat ||2||

11,8[10].3a daśa sākam ajāyanta devā devebhyaḥ purā |
11,8[10].3c yo vai tān vidyāt pratyakṣaṃ sa vā adya mahad vadet ||3||

11,8[10].4a prāṇāpānau cakṣuḥ śrotram akṣitiś ca kṣitiś ca yā |
11,8[10].4c vyānodānau vāṅ manas te vā ākūtim āvahan ||4||

11,8[10].5a ajātā āsann ṛtavo 'tho dhātā bṛhaspatiḥ |
11,8[10].5c indrāgnī aśvinā tarhi kaṃ te jyeṣṭham upāsata ||5||

11,8[10].6a tapaś caivāstāṃ karma cāntar mahaty arṇave |
11,8[10].6c tapo ha jajñe karmaṇas tat te jyeṣṭham upāsata ||6||

11,8[10].7a yeta āsīd bhūmiḥ pūrvā yām addhātaya id viduḥ |
11,8[10].7c yo vai tāṃ vidyān nāmathā sa manyeta purāṇavit ||7||

11,8[10].8a kuta indraḥ kutaḥ somaḥ kuto agnir ajāyata |
11,8[10].8c kutas tvaṣṭā sam abhavat kuto dhātājāyata ||8||

11,8[10].9a indrād indraḥ somāt somo agner agnir ajāyata |
11,8[10].9c tvaṣṭā ha jajñe tvaṣṭur dhātur dhātājāyata ||9||

11,8[10].10a ye ta āsan daśa jātā devā devebhyaḥ purā |
11,8[10].10c putrebhyo lokaṃ dattvā kasmiṃs te loka āsate ||10|| {22}

11,8[10].11a yadā keśān asthi snāva māṃsaṃ majjānam ābharat |
11,8[10].11c śarīraṃ kṛtvā pādavat kaṃ lokam anu prāviśat ||11||

11,8[10].12a kutaḥ keśān kutaḥ snāva kuto asthīny ābharat |
11,8[10].12c aṅgā parvāṇi majjānaṃ ko māṃsaṃ kuta ābharat ||12||

11,8[10].13a saṃsico nāma te devā ye saṃbhārānt samabharan |
11,8[10].13c sarvaṃ saṃsicya martyaṃ devāḥ puruṣam āviśan ||13||

11,8[10].14a ūrū pādāv aṣṭhīvantau śiro hastāv atho mukham |
11,8[10].14c pṛṣṭīr barjahye pārśve kas tat sam adadhād ṛṣiḥ ||14||

11,8[10].15a śiro hastāv atho mukhaṃ jihvāṃ grīvāś ca kīkasāḥ |
11,8[10].15c tvacā prāvṛtya sarvaṃ tat saṃdhā sam adadhān mahī ||15||

11,8[10].16a yat tac charīram aśayat saṃdhayā saṃhitaṃ mahat |
11,8[10].16c yenedam adya rocate ko asmin varṇam ābharat ||16||

11,8[10].17a sarve devā upāśikṣan tad ajānād vadhūḥ satī |
11,8[10].17c īśā vaśasya yā jāyā sāsmin varṇam ābharat ||17||

11,8[10].18a yadā tvaṣṭā vyatṛṇat pitā tvaṣṭur ya uttaraḥ |
11,8[10].18c gṛhaṃ kṛtvā martyaṃ devāḥ puruṣam āviśan ||18||

11,8[10].19a svapno vai tandrīr nirṛtiḥ pāpmāno nāma devatāḥ |
11,8[10].19c jarā khālatyaṃ pālityaṃ śarīram anu prāviśan ||19||

11,8[10].20a steyaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ vṛjinaṃ satyaṃ yajño yaśo bṛhat |
11,8[10].20c balaṃ ca kṣatram ojaś ca śarīram anu prāviśan ||20|| {23}

11,8[10].21a bhūtiś ca vā abhūtiś ca rātayo 'rātayaś ca yāḥ |
11,8[10].21c kṣudhaś ca sarvās tṛṣṇāś ca śarīram anu prāviśan ||21||

11,8[10].22a nindāś ca vā anindāś ca yac ca hanteti neti ca |
11,8[10].22c śarīraṃ śraddhā dakṣiṇāśraddhā cānu prāviśan ||22||

11,8[10].23a vidyāś ca vā avidyāś ca yac cānyad upadeśyam |
11,8[10].23c śarīraṃ brahma prāviśad ṛcaḥ sāmātho yajuḥ ||23||

11,8[10].24a ānandā modāḥ pramudo 'bhīmodamudaś ca ye |
11,8[10].24c haso nariṣṭā nṛttāni śarīram anu prāviśan ||24||

11,8[10].25a ālāpāś ca pralāpāś cābhīlāpalapaś ca ye |
11,8[10].25c śarīraṃ sarve prāviśann āyujaḥ prayujo yujaḥ ||25||

11,8[10].26a prāṇāpānau cakṣuḥ śrotram akṣitiś ca kṣitiś ca yā |
11,8[10].26c vyānodānau vāṅ manaḥ śarīreṇa ta īyante ||26||

11,8[10].27a āśiṣaś ca praśiṣaś ca saṃśiṣo viśiṣaś ca yāḥ |
11,8[10].27c cittāni sarve saṃkalpāḥ śarīram anu prāviśan ||27||

11,8[10].28a āsteyīś ca vāsteyīś ca tvaraṇāḥ kṛpaṇāś ca yāḥ |
11,8[10].28c guhyāḥ śukrā sthūlā apas tā bībhatsāv asādayan ||28||

11,8[10].29a asthi kṛtvā samidhaṃ tad aṣṭāpo asādayan |
11,8[10].29c retaḥ kṛtvājyaṃ devāḥ puruṣam āviśan ||29||

11,8[10].30a yā āpo yāś ca devatā yā virāḍ brahmaṇā saha |
11,8[10].30c śarīraṃ brahma prāviśac charīre 'dhi prajāpatiḥ ||30||

11,8[10].31a sūryaś cakṣur vātaḥ prāṇaṃ puruṣasya vi bhejire |
11,8[10].31c athāsyetaram ātmānaṃ devāḥ prāyachann agnaye ||31||

11,8[10].32a tasmād vai vidvān puruṣam idaṃ brahmeti manyate |
11,8[10].32c sarvā hy asmin devatā gāvo goṣṭha ivāsate ||32||

11,8[10].33a prathamena pramāreṇa tredhā viṣvaṅ vi gachati |
11,8[10].33c ada ekena gachaty ada ekena gachatīhaikena ni ṣevate ||33||

11,8[10].34a apsu stīmāsu vṛddhāsu śarīram antarā hitam |
11,8[10].34c tasmiṃ chavo 'dhy antarā tasmāc chavo 'dhy ucyate ||34|| {24}



11,9[11].1a ye bāhavo yā iṣavo dhanvanāṃ vīryāṇi ca |
11,9[11].1c asīn paraśūn āyudhaṃ cittākūtaṃ ca yad dhṛdi |
11,9[11].1e sarvaṃ tad arbude tvam amitrebhyo dṛśe kurūdārāṃś ca pra darśaya ||1||

11,9[11].2a ut tiṣṭhata saṃ nahyadhvaṃ mitrā devajanā yūyam |
11,9[11].2c saṃdṛṣṭā guptā vaḥ santu yā no mitrāṇy arbude ||2||

11,9[11].3a ut tiṣṭhatam ā rabhetām ādānasaṃdānābhyām |
11,9[11].3c amitrāṇāṃ senā abhi dhattam arbude ||3||

11,9[11].4a arbudir nāma yo deva īśānaś ca nyarbudiḥ |
11,9[11].4c yābhyām antarikṣam āvṛtam iyaṃ ca pṛthivī mahī |
11,9[11].4e tābhyām indramedibhyām ahaṃ jitam anv emi senayā ||4||

11,9[11].5a ut tiṣṭha tvaṃ devajanārbude senayā saha |
11,9[11].5c bhañjann amitrāṇāṃ senāṃ bhogebhiḥ pari vāraya ||5||

11,9[11].6a sapta jātān nyarbuda udārāṇāṃ samīkṣayan |
11,9[11].6c tebhiṣ ṭvam ājye hute sarvair ut tiṣṭha senayā ||6||

11,9[11].7a pratighnānāśrumukhī kṛdhukarṇī ca krośatu |
11,9[11].7c vikeśī puruṣe hate radite arbude tava ||7||

11,9[11].8a saṃkarṣantī karūkaraṃ manasā putram ichantī |
11,9[11].8c patiṃ bhrātaram āt svān radite arbude tava ||8||

11,9[11].9a aliklavā jāṣkamadā gṛdhrāḥ śyenāḥ patatriṇaḥ |
11,9[11].9c dhvāṅkṣāḥ śakunayas tṛpyantv amitreṣu samīkṣayan radite arbude tava ||9||

11,9[11].10a atho sarvaṃ śvāpadaṃ makṣikā tṛpyatu krimiḥ |
11,9[11].10c pauruṣeye 'dhi kuṇape radite arbude tava ||10|| {25}

11,9[11].11a ā gṛhṇītaṃ saṃ bṛhataṃ prāṇāpānān nyarbude |
11,9[11].11c nivāśā ghoṣāḥ saṃ yantv amitreṣu samīkṣayan radite arbude tava ||11||

11,9[11].12a ud vepaya saṃ vijantāṃ bhiyāmitrānt saṃ sṛja |
11,9[11].12c urugrāhair bāhvaṅkair vidhyāmitrān nyarbude ||12||

11,9[11].13a muhyantv eṣāṃ bāhavaś cittākūtaṃ ca yad dhṛdi |
11,9[11].13c maiṣām uc cheṣi kiṃ cana radite arbude tava ||13||

11,9[11].14a pratighnānāḥ saṃ dhāvantūraḥ paṭaurāv āghnānāḥ |
11,9[11].14c aghāriṇīr vikeśyo rudatyaḥ puruṣe hate radite arbude tava ||14||

11,9[11].15a śvanvatīr apsaraso rūpakā utārbude |
11,9[11].15c antaḥpātre rerihatīṃ riśāṃ durṇihitaiṣiṇīm |
11,9[11].15e sarvās tā arbude tvam amitrebhyo dṛśe kurūdārāṃś ca pra darśaya ||15||

11,9[11].16a khaḍūre 'dhicaṅkramāṃ kharvikāṃ kharvavāsinīm |
11,9[11].16c ya udārā antarhitā gandharvāpsarasaś ca ye | 
11,9[11].16e sarpā itarajanā rakṣāṃsi ||16||

11,9[11].17a caturdaṃṣṭrāṃ chyāvadataḥ kumbhamuṣkāṃ asṛṅmukhān |
11,9[11].17c svabhyasā ye codbhyasāḥ ||17||

11,9[11].18a ud vepaya tvam arbude 'mitrāṇām amūḥ sicaḥ |
11,9[11].18c jayaṃś ca jiṣṇuś cāmitrāṃ jayatām indramedinau ||18||

11,9[11].19a prablīno mṛditaḥ śayāṃ hato 'mitro nyarbude |
11,9[11].19c agnijihvā dhūmaśikhā jayantīr yantu senayā ||19||

11,9[11].20a tayārbude praṇuttānām indro hantu varaṃvaram |
11,9[11].20c amitrāṇāṃ śacīpatir māmīṣāṃ moci kaś cana ||20|| {26}

11,9[11].21a ut kasantu hṛdayāny ūrdhvaḥ prāṇa ud īṣatu |
11,9[11].21c śauṣkāsyam anu vartatām amitrān mota mitriṇaḥ ||21||

11,9[11].22a ye ca dhīrā ye cādhīrāḥ parāñco badhirāś ca ye |
11,9[11].22c tamasā ye ca tūparā atho bastābhivāsinaḥ |
11,9[11].22e sarvāṃs tāṃ arbude tvam amitrebhyo dṛśe kurūdārāṃś ca pra darśaya ||22||

11,9[11].23a arbudiś ca triṣandhiś cāmitrān no vi vidhyatām |
11,9[11].23c yathaiṣām indra vṛtrahan hanāma śacīpate 'mitrāṇāṃ sahasraśaḥ ||23||

11,9[11].24a vanaspatīn vānaspatyān oṣadhīr uta vīrudhaḥ |
11,9[11].24c gandharvāpsarasaḥ sarpān devān puṇyajanān pitṝn |
11,9[11].24e sarvāṃs tāṃ arbude tvam amitrebhyo dṛśe kurūdārāṃś ca pra darśaya ||24||

11,9[11].25a īśāṃ vo maruto deva ādityo brahmaṇaspatiḥ |
11,9[11].25c īśāṃ va indraś cāgniś ca dhātā mitraḥ prajāpatiḥ |
11,9[11].25e īśāṃ va ṛṣayaś cakrur amitreṣu samīkṣayan radite arbude tava ||25||

11,9[11].26a teṣāṃ sarveṣām īśānā ut tiṣṭhata saṃ nahyadhvam |
11,9[11].26c mitrā devajanā yūyam imaṃ saṃgrāmaṃ saṃjitya yathālokaṃ vi tiṣṭhadhvam ||26|| {27}



11,10[12].1a ut tiṣṭhata saṃ nahyadhvam udārāḥ ketubhiḥ saha |
11,10[12].1c sarpā itarajanā rakṣāṃsy amitrān anu dhāvata ||1||

11,10[12].2a īśāṃ vo veda rājyaṃ triṣandhe aruṇaiḥ ketubhiḥ saha |
11,10[12].2c ye antarikṣe ye divi pṛthivyāṃ ye ca mānavāḥ |
11,10[12].2e triṣandhes te cetasi durṇāmāna upāsatām ||2||

11,10[12].3a ayomukhāḥ sūcīmukhā atho vikaṅkatīmukhāḥ |
11,10[12].3c kravyādo vātaraṃhasa ā sajantv amitrān vajreṇa triṣandhinā ||3||

11,10[12].4a antar dhehi jātaveda āditya kuṇapaṃ bahu |
11,10[12].4c triṣandher iyaṃ senā suhitāstu me vaśe ||4||

11,10[12].5a ut tiṣṭha tvaṃ devajanārbude senayā saha |
11,10[12].5c ayaṃ balir va āhutas triṣandher āhutiḥ priyā ||5||

11,10[12].6a śitipadī saṃ dyatu śaravyeyaṃ catuṣpadī |
11,10[12].6c kṛtye 'mitrebhyo bhava triṣandheḥ saha senayā ||6||

11,10[12].7a dhūmākṣī saṃ patatu kṛdhukarṇī ca krośatu |
11,10[12].7c triṣandheḥ senayā jite aruṇāḥ santu ketavaḥ ||7||

11,10[12].8a avāyantāṃ pakṣiṇo ye vayāṃsy antarikṣe divi ye caranti |
11,10[12].8c śvāpado makṣikāḥ saṃ rabhantām āmādo gṛdhrāḥ kuṇape radantām ||8||

11,10[12].9a yām indreṇa saṃdhāṃ samadhatthā brahmaṇā ca bṛhaspate |
11,10[12].9c tayāham indrasaṃdhayā sarvān devān iha huva ito jayata māmutaḥ ||9||

11,10[12].10a bṛhaspatir āṅgirasa ṛṣayo brahmasaṃśitāḥ |
11,10[12].10c asurakṣayaṇaṃ vadhaṃ triṣandhiṃ divy āśrayan ||10|| {28}

11,10[12].11a yenāsau gupta āditya ubhāv indraś ca tiṣṭhataḥ |
11,10[12].11c triṣandhiṃ devā abhajantaujase ca balāya ca ||11||

11,10[12].12a sarvāṃl lokānt sam ajayan devā āhutyānayā |
11,10[12].12c bṛhaspatir āṅgiraso vajraṃ yam asiñcatāsurakṣayaṇaṃ vadham ||12||

11,10[12].13a bṛhaspatir āṅgiraso vajraṃ yam asiñcatāsurakṣayaṇaṃ vadham |
11,10[12].13c tenāham amūṃ senāṃ ni limpāmi bṛhaspate 'mitrān hanmy ojasā ||13||

11,10[12].14a sarve devā atyāyanti ye aśnanti vaṣaṭkṛtam |
11,10[12].14c imāṃ juṣadhvam āhutim ito jayata māmutaḥ ||14||

11,10[12].15a sarve devā atyāyantu triṣandher āhutiḥ priyā |
11,10[12].15c saṃdhāṃ mahatīṃ rakṣata yayāgre asurā jitāḥ ||15||

11,10[12].16a vāyur amitrāṇām iṣvagrāṇy āñcatu |
11,10[12].16c indra eṣāṃ bāhūn prati bhanaktu mā śakan pratidhām iṣum |
11,10[12].16e āditya eṣām astraṃ vi nāśayatu candramā yutām agatasya panthām ||16||

11,10[12].17a yadi preyur devapurā brahma varmāṇi cakrire |
11,10[12].17c tanūpānaṃ paripāṇaṃ kṛṇvānā yad upocire sarvaṃ tad arasaṃ kṛdhi ||17||

11,10[12].18a kravyādānuvartayan mṛtyunā ca purohitam |
11,10[12].18c triṣandhe prehi senayā jayāmitrān pra padyasva ||18||
11,10[12].19a triṣandhe tamasā tvam amitrān pari vāraya |
11,10[12].19c pṛṣadājyapraṇuttānāṃ māmīṣāṃ moci kaś cana ||19||

11,10[12].20a śitipadī saṃ patatv amitrāṇām amūḥ sicaḥ |
11,10[12].20c muhyantv adyāmūḥ senā amitrāṇāṃ nyarbude ||20|| {29}

11,10[12].21a mūḍhā amitrā nyarbude jahy eṣāṃ varaṃvaram |
11,10[12].21c anayā jahi senayā ||21||

11,10[12].22a yaś ca kavacī yaś cākavaco 'mitro yaś cājmani |
11,10[12].22c jyāpāśaiḥ kavacapāśair ajmanābhihataḥ śayām ||22||

11,10[12].23a ye varmiṇo ye 'varmāṇo amitrā ye ca varmiṇaḥ |
11,10[12].23c sarvāṃs tāṃ arbude hatāṃ chvāno 'dantu bhūmyām ||23||

11,10[12].24a ye rathino ye arathā asādā ye ca sādinaḥ |
11,10[12].24c sarvān adantu tān hatān gṛdhrāḥ śyenāḥ patatriṇaḥ ||24||

11,10[12].25a sahasrakuṇapā śetām āmitrī senā samare vadhānām |
11,10[12].25c vividdhā kakajākṛtā ||25||

11,10[12].26a marmāvidhaṃ roruvataṃ suparṇair adantu duścitaṃ mṛditaṃ śayānam |
11,10[12].26c ya imāṃ pratīcīm āhutim amitro no yuyutsati ||26||

11,10[12].27a yāṃ devā anutiṣṭhanti yasyā nāsti virādhanam |
11,10[12].27c tayendro hantu vṛtrahā vajreṇa triṣandhinā ||27|| {30}



1satyaṃ bṛhad ṛtam ugraṃ dīkṣā tapo brahma yajñaḥ pṛthivīṃ dhārayanti |
1sā no bhūtasya bhavyasya patny uruṃ lokaṃ pṛthivī naḥ kṛṇotu ||1||

1asaṃbādhaṃ madhyato mānavānāṃ yasyā udvataḥ pravataḥ samaṃ bahu |
1nānāvīryā oṣadhīr yā bibharti pṛthivī naḥ prathatāṃ rādhyatāṃ naḥ ||2||

1yasyāṃ samudra uta sindhur āpo yasyām annaṃ kṛṣṭayaḥ saṃbabhūvuḥ |
1yasyām idaṃ jinvati prāṇad ejat sā no bhūmiḥ pūrvapeye dadhātu ||3||

1yasyāś catasraḥ pradiśaḥ pṛthivyā yasyām annam kṛṣṭayaḥ saṃbabhūvuḥ |
1yā bibharti bahudhā prāṇad ejat sā no bhūmir goṣv apy anne dadhātu ||4||

1yasyāṃ pūrve pūrvajanā vicakrire yasyāṃ devā asurān abhyavartayan |
1gavām aśvānāṃ vayasaś ca viṣṭhā bhagaṃ varcaḥ pṛthivī no dadhātu ||5||

1viśvaṃbharā vasudhānī pratiṣṭhā hiraṇyavakṣā jagato niveśanī |
1vaiśvānaraṃ bibhratī bhūmir agnim indraṛṣabhā draviṇe no dadhātu ||6||

1yāṃ rakṣanty asvapnā viśvadānīṃ devā bhūmiṃ pṛthivīm apramādam |
1sā no madhu priyaṃ duhām atho ukṣatu varcasā ||7||

1yārṇave 'dhi salilam agra āsīt yāṃ māyābhir anvacaran manīṣiṇaḥ |
1yasyā hṛdayaṃ parame vyomant satyenāvṛtam amṛtaṃ pṛthivyāḥ |
1sā no bhūmis tviṣiṃ balaṃ rāṣṭre dadhātūttame ||8||

1yasyām āpaḥ paricarāḥ samānīr ahorātre apramādaṃ kṣaranti |
1sā no bhūmir bhūridhārā payo duhām atho ukṣatu varcasā ||9||

12,1.10a yām aśvināv amimātāṃ viṣṇur yasyāṃ vicakrame |
12,1.10c indro yāṃ cakra ātmane 'namitrāṃ śacīpatiḥ |
12,1.10e sā no bhūmir vi sṛjatāṃ mātā putrāya me payaḥ ||10|| {1}

12,1.11a girayas te parvatā himavanto 'raṇyaṃ te pṛthivi syonam astu |
12,1.11c babhruṃ kṛṣṇāṃ rohiṇīṃ viśvarūpāṃ dhruvāṃ bhūmiṃ pṛthivīm indraguptām |
12,1.11e ajīto 'hato akṣato 'dhy aṣṭhām pṛthivīm aham ||11||

12,1.12a yat te madhyaṃ pṛthivi yac ca nabhyaṃ yās ta ūrjas tanvaḥ saṃbabhūvuḥ |
12,1.12c tāsu no dhehy abhi naḥ pavasva mātā bhūmiḥ putro ahaṃ pṛthivyāḥ parjanyaḥ pitā sa u naḥ pipartu ||12||

12,1.13a yasyāṃ vediṃ parigṛhṇanti bhūmyāṃ yasyāṃ yajñaṃ tanvate viśvakarmāṇaḥ |
12,1.13c yasyāṃ mīyante svaravaḥ pṛthivyām ūrdhvāḥ śukrā āhutyāḥ purastāt |
12,1.13e sā no bhūmir vardhayad vardhamānā ||13||

12,1.14a yo no dveṣat pṛthivi yaḥ pṛtanyād yo 'bhidāsān manasā yo vadhena |
12,1.14c taṃ no bhūme randhaya pūrvakṛtvari ||14||

12,1.15a tvaj jātās tvayi caranti martyās tvaṃ bibharṣi dvipadas tvaṃ catuṣpadaḥ |
12,1.15c taveme pṛthivi pañca mānavā yebhyo jyotir amṛtaṃ martyebhya udyant sūryo raśmibhir ātanoti ||15||

12,1.16a tā naḥ prajāḥ saṃ duhratāṃ samagrā vāco madhu pṛthivi dhehi mahyam ||16||

12,1.17a viśvasvaṃ mātaram oṣadhīnāṃ dhruvāṃ bhūmiṃ pṛthivīṃ dharmaṇā dhṛtām |
12,1.17c śivāṃ syonām anu carema viśvahā ||17||

12,1.18a mahat sadhasthaṃ mahatī babhūvitha mahān vega ejathur vepathuṣ ṭe |
12,1.18c mahāṃs tvendro rakṣaty apramādam |
12,1.18e sā no bhūme pra rocaya hiraṇyasyeva saṃdṛśi mā no dvikṣata kaś cana ||18||

12,1.19a agnir bhūmyām oṣadhīṣv agnim āpo bibhraty agnir aśmasu |
12,1.19c agnir antaḥ puruṣeṣu goṣv aśveṣv agnayaḥ ||19||

12,1.20a agnir diva ā tapaty agner devasyorv antarikṣam |
12,1.20c agniṃ martāsa indhate havyavāhaṃ ghṛtapriyam ||20|| {2}

12,1.21a agnivāsāḥ pṛthivy asitajñūs tviṣīmantaṃ saṃśitaṃ mā kṛṇotu ||21||

12,1.22a bhūmyāṃ devebhyo dadati yajñaṃ havyam araṃkṛtam |
12,1.22c bhūmyāṃ manuṣyā jīvanti svadhayānnena martyāḥ |
12,1.22e sā no bhūmiḥ prāṇam āyur dadhātu jaradaṣṭiṃ mā pṛthivī kṛṇotu ||22||

12,1.23a yas te gandhaḥ pṛthivi saṃbabhūva yaṃ bibhraty oṣadhayo yam āpaḥ |
12,1.23c yaṃ gandharvā apsarasaś ca bhejire tena mā surabhiṃ kṛṇu mā no dvikṣata kaś cana ||23||

12,1.24a yas te gandhaḥ puṣkaram āviveśa yaṃ saṃjabhruḥ sūryāyā vivāhe |
12,1.24c amartyāḥ pṛthivi gandham agre tena mā surabhiṃ kṛṇu mā no dvikṣata kaś cana ||24||

12,1.25a yas te gandhaḥ puruṣeṣu strīṣu puṃsu bhago ruciḥ |
12,1.25c yo aśveṣu vīreṣu yo mṛgeṣūta hastiṣu |
12,1.25e kanyāyāṃ varco yad bhūme tenāsmāṃ api saṃ sṛja mā no dvikṣata kaś cana ||25||

12,1.26a śilā bhūmir aśmā pāṃsuḥ sā bhūmiḥ saṃdhṛtā dhṛtā |
12,1.26c tasyai hiraṇyavakṣase pṛthivyā akaraṃ namaḥ ||26||

12,1.27a yasyāṃ vṛkṣā vānaspatyā dhruvās tiṣṭhanti viśvahā |
12,1.27c pṛthivīṃ viśvadhāyasaṃ dhṛtām achāvadāmasi ||27||

12,1.28a udīrāṇā utāsīnās tiṣṭhantaḥ prakrāmantaḥ |
12,1.28c padbhyāṃ dakṣiṇasavyābhyāṃ mā vyathiṣmahi bhūmyām ||28||

12,1.29a vimṛgvarīṃ pṛthivīm ā vadāmi kṣamāṃ bhūmiṃ brahmaṇā vāvṛdhānām |
12,1.29c ūrjaṃ puṣṭaṃ bibhratīm annabhāgaṃ ghṛtaṃ tvābhi ni ṣīdema bhūme ||29||

12,1.30a śuddhā na āpas tanve kṣarantu yo naḥ sedur apriye taṃ ni dadhmaḥ |
12,1.30c pavitreṇa pṛthivi mot punāmi ||30|| {3}

12,1.31a yās te prācīḥ pradiśo yā udīcīr yās te bhūme adharād yāś ca paścāt |
12,1.31c syonās tā mahyaṃ carate bhavantu mā ni paptaṃ bhuvane śiśriyāṇaḥ ||31||

12,1.32a mā naḥ paścān mā purastān nudiṣṭhā mottarād adharād uta |
12,1.32c svasti bhūme no bhava mā vidan paripanthino varīyo yāvayā vadham ||32||

12,1.33a yāvat te 'bhi vipaśyāmi bhūme sūryeṇa medinā |
12,1.33c tāvan me cakṣur mā meṣṭottarāmuttarāṃ samām ||33||

12,1.34a yac chayānaḥ paryāvarte dakṣiṇaṃ sakhyam abhi bhūme pārśvam uttānās tvā pratīcīṃ yat pṛṣṭībhir adhiśemahe |
12,1.34c mā hiṃsīs tatra no bhūme sarvasya pratiśīvari ||34||

12,1.35a yat te bhūme vikhanāmi kṣipraṃ tad api rohatu |
12,1.35c mā te marma vimṛgvari mā te hṛdayam arpipam ||35||

12,1.36a grīṣmas te bhūme varṣāṇi śarad dhemantaḥ śiśiro vasantaḥ |
12,1.36c ṛtavas te vihitā hāyanīr ahorātre pṛthivi no duhātām ||36||

12,1.37a yāpa sarpaṃ vijamānā vimṛgvarī yasyām āsann agnayo ye apsv antaḥ |
12,1.37c parā dasyūn dadatī devapīyūn indraṃ vṛṇānā pṛthivī na vṛtram śakrāya dadhre vṛṣabhāya vṛṣṇe ||37||

12,1.38a yasyāṃ sadohavirdhāne yūpo yasyāṃ nimīyate |
12,1.38c brahmāṇo yasyām arcanty ṛgbhiḥ sāmnā yajurvidaḥ yujyante yasyām ṛtvijaḥ somam indrāya pātave ||38||

12,1.39a yasyāṃ pūrve bhūtakṛta ṛṣayo gā udānṛcuḥ |
12,1.39c sapta satreṇa vedhaso yajñena tapasā saha ||39||

12,1.40a sā no bhūmir ā diśatu yad dhanaṃ kāmayāmahe |
12,1.40c bhago anuprayuṅktām indra etu purogavaḥ ||40|| {4}

12,1.41a yasyāṃ gāyanti nṛtyanti bhūmyāṃ martyā vyailabāḥ |
12,1.41c yudhyante yasyām ākrando yasyām vadati dundubhiḥ |
12,1.41e sā no bhūmiḥ pra ṇudatāṃ sapatnān asapatnaṃ mā pṛthivī kṛṇotu ||41||

12,1.42a yasyām annaṃ vrīhiyavau yasyā imāḥ pañca kṛṣṭayaḥ |
12,1.42c bhūmyai parjanyapatnyai namo 'stu varṣamedase ||42||

12,1.43a yasyāḥ puro devakṛtāḥ kṣetre yasyā vikurvate |
12,1.43c prajāpatiḥ pṛthivīṃ viśvagarbhām āśāmāśāṃ raṇyāṃ naḥ kṛṇotu ||43||

12,1.44a nidhiṃ bibhratī bahudhā guhā vasu maṇiṃ hiraṇyaṃ pṛthivī dadātu me |
12,1.44c vasūni no vasudā rāsamānā devī dadhātu sumanasyamānā ||44||

12,1.45a janaṃ bibhratī bahudhā vivācasaṃ nānādharmāṇaṃ pṛthivī yathaukasam |
12,1.45c sahasraṃ dhārā draviṇasya me duhāṃ dhruveva dhenur anapasphurantī ||45||

12,1.46a yas te sarpo vṛścikas tṛṣṭadaṃśmā hemantajabdho bhṛmalo guhā śaye |
12,1.46c krimir jinvat pṛthivi yadyad ejati prāvṛṣi tan naḥ sarpan mopa sṛpad yac chivaṃ tena no mṛḍa ||46||

12,1.47a ye te panthāno bahavo janāyanā rathasya vartmānasaś ca yātave |
12,1.47c yaiḥ saṃcaranty ubhaye bhadrapāpās taṃ panthānaṃ jayemānamitram ataskaraṃ yac chivaṃ tena no mṛḍa ||47||

12,1.48a malvaṃ bibhratī gurubhṛd bhadrapāpasya nidhanaṃ titikṣuḥ |
12,1.48c varāheṇa pṛthivī saṃvidānā sūkarāya vi jihīte mṛgāya ||48||

12,1.49a ye ta āraṇyāḥ paśavo mṛgā vane hitāḥ siṃhā vyāghrāḥ puruṣādaś caranti |
12,1.49c ulaṃ vṛkaṃ pṛthivi duchunām ita ṛkṣīkāṃ rakṣo apa bādhayāsmat ||49||

12,1.50a ye gandharvā apsaraso ye cārāyāḥ kimīdinaḥ |
12,1.50c piśācānt sarvā rakṣāṃsi tān asmad bhūme yāvaya ||50|| {5}

12,1.51a yāṃ dvipādaḥ pakṣiṇaḥ saṃpatanti haṃsāḥ suparṇāḥ śakunā vayāṃsi |
12,1.51c yasyāṃ vāto mātariśveyate rajāṃsi kṛṇvaṃś cyāvayaṃś ca vṛkṣān |
12,1.51e vātasya pravām upavām anu vāty arciḥ ||51||

12,1.52a yasyāṃ kṛṣṇam aruṇaṃ ca saṃhite ahorātre vihite bhūmyām adhi |
12,1.52c varṣeṇa bhūmiḥ pṛthivī vṛtāvṛtā sā no dadhātu bhadrayā priye dhāmanidhāmani ||52||

12,1.53a dyauś ca ma idaṃ pṛthivī cāntarikṣaṃ ca me vyacaḥ |
12,1.53c agniḥ sūrya āpo medhāṃ viśve devāś ca saṃ daduḥ ||53||

12,1.54a aham asmi sahamāna uttaro nāma bhūmyām |
12,1.54c abhīṣāḍ asmi viśvāṣāḍ āśāmāśāṃ viṣāsahiḥ ||54||

12,1.55a ado yad devi prathamānā purastād devair uktā vyasarpo mahitvam |
12,1.55c ā tvā subhūtam aviśat tadānīm akalpayathāḥ pradiśaś catasraḥ ||55||

12,1.56a ye grāmā yad araṇyaṃ yāḥ sabhā adhi bhūmyām |
12,1.56c ye saṃgrāmāḥ samitayas teṣu cāru vadema te ||56||

12,1.57a aśva iva rajo dudhuve vi tān janān ya ākṣiyan pṛthivīṃ yād ajāyata |
12,1.57c mandrāgretvarī bhuvanasya gopā vanaspatīnāṃ gṛbhir oṣadhīnām ||57||

12,1.58a yad vadāmi madhumat tad vadāmi yad īkṣe tad vananti mā |
12,1.58c tviṣīmān asmi jūtimān avānyān hanmi dodhataḥ ||58||

12,1.59a śantivā surabhiḥ syonā kīlālodhnī payasvatī |
12,1.59c bhūmir adhi bravītu me pṛthivī payasā saha ||59||

12,1.60a yām anvaichad dhaviṣā viśvakarmāntar arṇave rajasi praviṣṭām |
12,1.60c bhujiṣyaṃ pātraṃ nihitaṃ guhā yad āvir bhoge abhavan mātṛmadbhyaḥ ||60||

12,1.61a tvam asy āvapanī janānām aditiḥ kāmadughā paprathānā |
12,1.61c yat ta ūnaṃ tat ta ā pūrayāti prajāpatiḥ prathamajā ṛtasya ||61||

12,1.62a upasthās te anamīvā ayakṣmā asmabhyaṃ santu pṛthivi prasūtāḥ |
12,1.62c dīrghaṃ na āyuḥ pratibudhyamānā vayaṃ tubhyaṃ balihṛtaḥ syāma ||62||

12,1.63a bhūme mātar ni dhehi mā bhadrayā supratiṣṭhitam |
12,1.63c saṃvidānā divā kave śriyāṃ mā dhehi bhūtyām ||63|| {6}



1naḍam ā roha na te atra loka idaṃ sīsaṃ bhāgadheyaṃ ta ehi |
1yo goṣu yakṣmaḥ puruṣeṣu yakṣmas tena tvaṃ sākam adharāṅ parehi ||1||

1aghaśaṃsaduḥśaṃsābhyāṃ kareṇānukareṇa ca |
1yakṣmaṃ ca sarvaṃ teneto mṛtyuṃ ca nir ajāmasi ||2||

1nir ito mṛtyuṃ nirṛtiṃ nir arātim ajāmasi |
1yo no dveṣṭi tam addhy agne akravyād yam u dviṣmas tam u te pra suvāmasi ||3||

1yady agniḥ kravyād yadi vā vyāghra imaṃ goṣṭhaṃ praviveśānyokāḥ |
1taṃ māṣājyaṃ kṛtvā pra hiṇomi dūraṃ sa gachatv apsuṣado 'py agnīn ||4||

1yat tvā kruddhāḥ pracakrur manyunā puruṣe mṛte |
1sukalpam agne tat tvayā punas tvod dīpayāmasi ||5||

1punas tvādityā rudrā vasavaḥ punar brahmā vasunītir agne |
1punas tvā brahmaṇas patir ādhād dīrghāyutvāya śataśāradāya ||6||
1yo agniḥ kravyāt praviveśa no gṛham imaṃ paśyann itaraṃ jātavedasam |
1taṃ harāmi pitṛyajñāya dūraṃ sa gharmam indhāṃ parame sadhasthe ||7||

1kravyādam agniṃ pra hiṇomi dūram yamarājño gachatu ripravāhaḥ |
1ihāyam itaro jātavedā devo devebhyo havyaṃ vahatu prajānan ||8||

1kravyādam agnim iṣito harāmi janān dṛṃhantaṃ vajreṇa mṛtyum |
1ni taṃ śāsmi gārhapatyena vidvān pitṝṇāṃ loke 'pi bhāgo astu ||9||

12,2.10a kravyādam agniṃ śaśamānam ukthyaṃ pra hiṇomi pathibhiḥ pitṛyāṇaiḥ |
12,2.10c mā devayānaiḥ punar ā gā atraivaidhi pitṛṣu jāgṛhi tvam ||10|| {7}

12,2.11a sam indhate saṃkasukaṃ svastaye śuddhā bhavantaḥ śucayaḥ pāvakāḥ |
12,2.11c jahāti ripram aty ena eti samiddho agniḥ supunā punāti ||11||

12,2.12a devo agniḥ saṃkasuko divas pṛṣṭhāny āruhat |
12,2.12c mucyamāno nir eṇaso 'mog asmāṃ aśastyāḥ ||12||

12,2.13a asmin vayaṃ saṃkasuke agnau riprāṇi mṛjmahe |
12,2.13c abhūma yajñiyāḥ śuddhāḥ pra ṇa āyūṃṣi tāriṣat ||13||

12,2.14a saṃkasuko vikasuko nirṛtho yaś ca nisvaraḥ |
12,2.14c te te yakṣmaṃ savedaso dūrād dūram anīnaśan ||14||

12,2.15a yo no aśveṣu vīreṣu yo no goṣv ajāviṣu |
12,2.15c kravyādaṃ nir ṇudāmasi yo agnir janayopanaḥ ||15||

12,2.16a anyebhyas tvā puruṣebhyo gobhyo aśvebhyas tvā |
12,2.16c niḥ kravyādaṃ nudāmasi yo agnir jīvitayopanaḥ ||16||

12,2.17a yasmin devā amṛjata yasmin manuṣyā uta |
12,2.17c tasmin ghṛtastāvo mṛṣṭvā tvam agne divaṃ ruha ||17||

12,2.18a samiddho agna āhuta sa no mābhyapakramīḥ |
12,2.18c atraiva dīdihi dyavi jyok ca sūryaṃ dṛśe ||18||

12,2.19a sīse mṛḍḍhvaṃ naḍe mṛḍḍhvam agnau saṃkasuke ca yat |
12,2.19c atho avyāṃ rāmāyāṃ śīrṣaktim upabarhaṇe ||19||

12,2.20a sīse malaṃ sādayitvā śīrṣaktim upabarhaṇe |
12,2.20c avyām asiknyāṃ mṛṣṭvā śuddhā bhavata yajñiyāḥ ||20|| {8}

12,2.21a paraṃ mṛtyo anu parehi panthāṃ yas ta eṣa itaro devayānāt |
12,2.21c cakṣuṣmate śṛṇvate te bravīmīheme vīrā bahavo bhavantu ||21||

12,2.22a ime jīvā vi mṛtair āvavṛtrann abhūd bhadrā devahutir no adya |
12,2.22c prāñco agāma nṛtaye hasāya suvīrāso vidatham ā vadema ||22||

12,2.23a imaṃ jīvebhyaḥ paridhiṃ dadhāmi maiṣāṃ nu gād aparo artham etam |
12,2.23c śataṃ jīvantaḥ śaradaḥ purūcīs tiro mṛtyuṃ dadhatām parvatena ||23||

12,2.24a ā rohatāyur jarasaṃ vṛṇānā anupūrvaṃ yatamānā yati stha |
12,2.24c tān vas tvaṣṭā sujanimā sajoṣāḥ sarvam āyur nayatu jīvanāya ||24||

12,2.25a yathāhāny anupūrvaṃ bhavanti yatha rtava ṛtubhir yanti sākam |
12,2.25c yathā na pūrvam aparo jahāty evā dhātar āyūṃṣi kalpayaiṣām ||25||

12,2.26a aśmanvatī rīyate saṃ rabhadhvaṃ vīrayadhvaṃ pra taratā sakhāyaḥ |
12,2.26c atrā jahīta ye asan durevā anamīvān ut taremābhi vājān ||26||

12,2.27a ut tiṣṭhatā pra taratā sakhāyo 'śmanvatī nadī syandata iyam |
12,2.27c atrā jahīta ye asann aśivāḥ śivānt syonān ut taremābhi vājān ||27||

12,2.28a vaiśvadevīṃ varcasā ā rabhadhvaṃ śuddhā bhavantaḥ śucayaḥ pāvakāḥ |
12,2.28c atikrāmanto duritā padāni śataṃ himāḥ sarvavīrā madema ||28||

12,2.29a udīcīnaiḥ pathibhir vāyumadbhir atikrāmanto 'varān parebhiḥ |
12,2.29c triḥ sapta kṛtva ṛṣayaḥ paretā mṛtyuṃ praty auhan padayopanena ||29||

12,2.30a mṛtyoḥ padaṃ yopayanta eta drāghīya āyuḥ prataraṃ dadhānāḥ |
12,2.30c āsīnā mṛtyuṃ nudatā sadhasthe 'tha jīvāso vidatham ā vadema ||30|| {9}

12,2.31a imā nārīr avidhavāḥ supatnīr āñjanena sarpiṣā saṃ spṛśantām |
12,2.31c anaśravo anamīvāḥ suratnā ā rohantu janayo yonim agre ||31||

12,2.32a vyākaromi haviṣāham etau tau brahmaṇā vy ahaṃ kalpayāmi |
12,2.32c svadhāṃ pitṛbhyo ajarāṃ kṛṇomi dīrgheṇāyuṣā sam imānt sṛjāmi ||32||

12,2.33a yo no agniḥ pitaro hṛtsv antar āviveśāmṛto martyeṣu |
12,2.33c mayy ahaṃ taṃ pari gṛhṇāmi devaṃ mā so asmān dvikṣata mā vayaṃ tam ||33||

12,2.34a apāvṛtya gārhapatyāt kravyādā preta dakṣiṇā |
12,2.34c priyaṃ pitṛbhya ātmane brahmabhyaḥ kṛṇutā priyam ||34||

12,2.35a dvibhāgadhanam ādāya pra kṣiṇāty avartyā |
12,2.35c agniḥ putrasya jyeṣṭhasya yaḥ kravyād anirāhitaḥ ||35||

12,2.36a yat kṛṣate yad vanute yac ca vasnena vindate |
12,2.36c sarvaṃ martyasya tan nāsti kravyāc ced anirāhitaḥ ||36||

12,2.37a ayajñiyo hatavarcā bhavati nainena havir attave |
12,2.37c chinatti kṛṣyā gor dhanād yaṃ kravyād anuvartate ||37||

12,2.38a muhur gṛdhyaiḥ pra vadaty ārtim martyo nītya |
12,2.38c kravyād yān agnir antikād anuvidvān vitāvati ||38||

12,2.39a grāhyā gṛhāḥ saṃ sṛjyante striyā yan mriyate patiḥ |
12,2.39c brahmaiva vidvān eṣyo yaḥ kravyādaṃ nirādadhat ||39||
12,2.40a yad ripraṃ śamalaṃ cakṛma yac ca duṣkṛtam |
12,2.40c āpo mā tasmāc chumbhantv agneḥ saṃkasukāc ca yat ||40|| {10}

12,2.41a tā adharād udīcīr āvavṛtran prajānaitīḥ pathibhir devayānaiḥ |
12,2.41c parvatasya vṛṣabhasyādhi pṛṣṭhe navāś caranti saritaḥ purāṇīḥ ||41||

12,2.42a agne akravyān niḥ kravyādaṃ nudā devayajanaṃ vaha ||42||

12,2.43a imaṃ kravyād ā viveśāyaṃ kravyādam anv agāt |
12,2.43c vyāghrau kṛtvā nānānaṃ taṃ harāmi śivāparam ||43||

12,2.44a antardhir devānāṃ paridhir manuṣyāṇām agnir gārhapatya ubhayān antarā śritaḥ ||44||

12,2.45a jīvānām āyuḥ pra tira tvam agne pitṝṇāṃ lokam api gachantu ye mṛtāḥ |
12,2.45c sugārhapatyo vitapann arātim uṣāmuṣāṃ śreyasīṃ dhehy asmai ||45||

12,2.46a sarvān agne sahamānaḥ sapatnān aiṣām ūrjaṃ rayim asmāsu dhehi ||46||

12,2.47a imam indraṃ vahniṃ paprim anvārabhadhvaṃ sa vo nir vakṣad duritād avadyāt |
12,2.47c tenāpa hata śarum āpatantaṃ tena rudrasya pari pātāstām ||47||

12,2.48a anaḍvāhaṃ plavam anvārabhadhvaṃ sa vo nir vakṣad duritād avadyāt |
12,2.48c ā rohata savitur nāvam etāṃ ṣaḍbhir urvībhir amatiṃ tarema ||48||

12,2.49a ahorātre anv eṣi bibhrat kṣemyas tiṣṭhan prataraṇaḥ suvīraḥ |
12,2.49c anāturānt sumanasas talpa bibhraj jyog eva naḥ puruṣagandhir edhi ||49||

12,2.50a te devebhya ā vṛścante pāpaṃ jīvanti sarvadā |
12,2.50c kravyād yān agnir antikād aśva ivānuvapate naḍam ||50|| {11}

12,2.51a ye 'śraddhā dhanakāmyā kravyādā samāsate |
12,2.51c te vā anyeṣāṃ kumbhīṃ paryādadhati sarvadā ||51||

12,2.52a preva pipatiṣati manasā muhur ā vartate punaḥ |
12,2.52c kravyād yān agnir antikād anuvidvān vitāvati ||52||

12,2.53a aviḥ kṛṣṇā bhāgadheyaṃ paśūnāṃ sīsaṃ kravyād api candraṃ ta āhuḥ |
12,2.53c māṣāḥ piṣṭā bhāgadheyaṃ te havyam araṇyānyā gahvaraṃ sacasva ||53||

12,2.54a iṣīkāṃ jaratīm iṣṭvā tilpiñjaṃ daṇḍanaṃ naḍam |
12,2.54c tam indra idhmam kṛtvā yamasyāgniṃ nirādadhau ||54||

12,2.55a pratyañcam arkaṃ pratyarpayitvā pravidvān panthāṃ vi hy āviveśa |
12,2.55c parāmīṣām asūn dideśa dīrgheṇāyuṣā sam imānt sṛjāmi ||55|| {12}



1pumān puṃso 'dhi tiṣṭha carmehi tatra hvayasva yatamā priyā te |
1yāvantāv agre prathamaṃ sameyathus tad vāṃ vayo yamarājye samānam ||1||

1tāvad vāṃ cakṣus tati vīryāṇi tāvat tejas tatidhā vājināni |
1agniḥ śarīraṃ sacate yadaidho 'dhā pakvān mithunā saṃ bhavāthaḥ ||2||

1sam asmiṃl loke sam u devayāne saṃ smā sametaṃ yamarājyeṣu |
1pūtau pavitrair upa tad dhvayethāṃ yadyad reto adhi vāṃ saṃbabhūva ||3||

1āpas putrāso abhi saṃ viśadhvam imaṃ jīvaṃ jīvadhanyāḥ sametya |
1tāsāṃ bhajadhvam amṛtaṃ yam āhur odanaṃ pacati vāṃ janitrī ||4||

1yaṃ vāṃ pitā pacati yaṃ ca mātā riprān nirmuktyai śamalāc ca vācaḥ |
1sa odanaḥ śatadhāraḥ svarga ubhe vy āpa nabhasī mahitvā ||5||

1ubhe nabhasī ubhayāṃś ca lokān ye yajvanām abhijitāḥ svargāḥ |
1teṣāṃ jyotiṣmān madhumān yo agre tasmin putrair jarasi saṃ śrayethām ||6||

1prācīṃprācīṃ pradiśam ā rabhethām etaṃ lokaṃ śraddadhānāḥ sacante |
1yad vāṃ pakvaṃ pariviṣṭam agnau tasya guptaye daṃpatī saṃ śrayethām ||7||

1dakṣiṇāṃ diśam abhi nakṣamāṇau paryāvartethām abhi pātram etat |
1tasmin vāṃ yamaḥ pitṛbhiḥ saṃvidānaḥ pakvāya śarma bahulaṃ ni yachāt ||8||

1pratīcī diśām iyam id varaṃ yasyāṃ somo adhipā mṛḍitā ca |
1tasyāṃ śrayethāṃ sukṛtaḥ sacethām adhā pakvān mithunā saṃ bhavāthaḥ ||9||

12,3.10a uttaraṃ rāṣṭraṃ prajayottarāvad diśām udīcī kṛṇavan no agram |
12,3.10c pāṅktaṃ chandaḥ puruṣo babhūva viśvair viśvāṅgaiḥ saha saṃ bhavema ||10|| {13}

12,3.11a dhruveyaṃ virāṇ namo astv asyai śivā putrebhya uta mahyam astu |
12,3.11c sā no devy adite viśvavāra irya iva gopā abhi rakṣa pakvam ||11||

12,3.12a piteva putrān abhi saṃ svajasva naḥ śivā no vātā iha vāntu bhūmau |
12,3.12c yam odanaṃ pacato devate iha taṃ nas tapa uta satyaṃ ca vettu ||12||
