12,3.13a yadyad kṛṣṇaḥ śakuna eha gatvā tsaran viṣaktaṃ bila āsasāda |
12,3.13c yad vā dāsy ārdrahastā samaṅkta ulūkhalaṃ musalaṃ śumbhatāpaḥ ||13||

12,3.14a ayaṃ grāvā pṛthubudhno vayodhāḥ pūtaḥ pavitrair apa hantu rakṣaḥ |
12,3.14c ā roha carma mahi śarma yacha mā daṃpatī pautram aghaṃ ni gātām ||14||

12,3.15a vanaspatiḥ saha devair na āgan rakṣaḥ piśācāṃ apabādhamānaḥ |
12,3.15c sa uc chrayātai pra vadāti vācaṃ tena lokāṃ abhi sarvān jayema ||15||

12,3.16a sapta medhān paśavaḥ pary agṛhṇan ya eṣāṃ jyotiṣmāṃ uta yaś cakarśa |
12,3.16c trayastriṃśad devatās tānt sacante sa naḥ svargam abhi neṣa lokam ||16||

12,3.17a svargaṃ lokam abhi no nayāsi saṃ jāyayā saha putraiḥ syāma |
12,3.17c gṛhṇāmi hastam anu maitv atra mā nas tārīn nirṛtir mo arātiḥ ||17||

12,3.18a grāhiṃ pāpmānam ati tāṃ ayāma tamo vy asya pra vadāsi valgu |
12,3.18c vānaspatya udyato mā jihiṃsīr mā taṇḍulaṃ vi śarīr devayantam ||18||

12,3.19a viśvavyacā ghṛtapṛṣṭho bhaviṣyant sayonir lokam upa yāhy etam |
12,3.19c varṣavṛddham upa yacha śūrpaṃ tuṣaṃ palāvān apa tad vinaktu ||19||

12,3.20a trayo lokāḥ saṃmitā brāhmaṇena dyaur evāsau pṛthivy antarikṣam |
12,3.20c aṃśūn gṛbhītvānvārabhethām ā pyāyantāṃ punar ā yantu śūrpam ||20|| {14}

12,3.21a pṛthag rūpāṇi bahudhā paśūnām ekarūpo bhavasi saṃ samṛddhyā |
12,3.21c etāṃ tvacaṃ lohinīṃ tāṃ nudasva grāvā śumbhāti malaga iva vastrā ||21||

12,3.22a pṛthivīṃ tvā pṛthivyām ā veśayāmi tanūḥ samānī vikṛtā ta eṣā |
12,3.22c yadyad dyuttaṃ likhitam arpaṇena tena mā susror brahmaṇāpi tad vapāmi ||22||

12,3.23a janitrīva prati haryāsi sūnuṃ saṃ tvā dadhāmi pṛthivīṃ pṛthivyā |
12,3.23c ukhā kumbhī vedyāṃ mā vyathiṣṭhā yajñāyudhair ājyenātiṣaktā ||23||

12,3.24a agniḥ pacan rakṣatu tvā purastād indro rakṣatu dakṣiṇato marutvān |
12,3.24c varuṇas tvā dṛṃhād dharuṇe pratīcyā uttarāt tvā somaḥ saṃ dadātai ||24||

12,3.25a pūtāḥ pavitraiḥ pavante abhrād divaṃ ca yanti pṛthivīṃ ca lokān |
12,3.25c tā jīvalā jīvadhanyāḥ pratiṣṭhāḥ pātra āsiktāḥ pary agnir indhām ||25||

12,3.26a ā yanti divaḥ pṛthivīṃ sacante bhūmyāḥ sacante adhy antarikṣam |
12,3.26c śuddhāḥ satīs tā u śumbhanta eva tā naḥ svargam abhi lokaṃ nayantu ||26||

12,3.27a uteva prabhvīr uta saṃmitāsa uta śukrāḥ śucayaś cāmṛtāsaḥ |
12,3.27c tā odanaṃ daṃpatibhyāṃ praśiṣṭā āpaḥ śikṣantīḥ pacatā sunāthāḥ ||27||

12,3.28a saṃkhyātā stokāḥ pṛthivīṃ sacante prāṇāpānaiḥ saṃmitā oṣadhībhiḥ |
12,3.28c asaṃkhyātā opyamānāḥ suvarṇāḥ sarvaṃ vyāpuḥ śucayaḥ śucitvam ||28||

12,3.29a ud yodhanty abhi valganti taptāḥ phenam asyanti bahulāṃś ca bindūn |
12,3.29c yoṣeva dṛṣṭvā patim ṛtviyāyaitais taṇḍulair bhavatā sam āpaḥ ||29||

12,3.30a ut thāpaya sīdato budhna enān adbhir ātmānam abhi saṃ spṛśantām |
12,3.30c amāsi pātrair udakaṃ yad etan mitās taṇḍulāḥ pradiśo yadīmāḥ ||30|| {15}

12,3.31a pra yacha parśuṃ tvarayā harausam ahiṃsanta oṣadhīr dāntu parvan |
12,3.31c vāsāṃ somaḥ pari rājyaṃ babhūvāmanyutā no vīrudho bhavantu ||31||

12,3.32a navaṃ barhir odanāya stṛṇīta priyaṃ hṛdaś cakṣuṣo valgv astu |
12,3.32c tasmin devāḥ saha daivīr viśantv imaṃ prāśnantv ṛtubhir niṣadya ||32||

12,3.33a vanaspate stīrṇam ā sīda barhir agniṣṭobhaiḥ saṃmito devatābhiḥ |
12,3.33c tvaṣṭreva rūpaṃ sukṛtaṃ svadhityainā ehāḥ pari pātre dadṛśrām ||33||

12,3.34a ṣaṣṭyāṃ śaratsu nidhipā abhīchāt svaḥ pakvenābhy aśnavātai |
12,3.34c upainaṃ jīvān pitaraś ca putrā etaṃ svargaṃ gamayāntam agneḥ ||34||

12,3.35a dhartā dhriyasva dharuṇe pṛthivyā acyutaṃ tvā devatāś cyāvayantu |
12,3.35c taṃ tvā daṃpatī jīvantau jīvaputrāv ud vāsayātaḥ pary agnidhānāt ||35||

12,3.36a sarvānt samāgā abhijitya lokān yāvantaḥ kāmāḥ sam atītṛpas tān |
12,3.36c vi gāhethām āyavanaṃ ca darvir ekasmin pātre adhy ud dharainam ||36||

12,3.37a upa stṛṇīhi prathaya purastād ghṛtena pātram abhi ghārayaitat |
12,3.37c vāśrevosrā taruṇaṃ stanasyum imaṃ devāso abhihiṅkṛṇota ||37||

12,3.38a upāstarīr akaro lokam etam uruḥ prathatām asamaḥ svargaḥ |
12,3.38c tasmiṃ chrayātai mahiṣaḥ suparṇo devā enaṃ devatābhyaḥ pra yachān ||38||

12,3.39a yadyaj jāyā pacati tvat paraḥparaḥ patir vā jāye tvat tiraḥ |
12,3.39c saṃ tat sṛjethāṃ saha vāṃ tad astu saṃpādayantau saha lokam ekam ||39||

12,3.40a yāvanto asyāḥ pṛthivīṃ sacante asmat putrāḥ pari ye saṃbabhūvuḥ |
12,3.40c sarvāṃs tāṃ upa pātre hvayethāṃ nābhiṃ jānānāḥ śiśavaḥ samāyān ||40|| {16}

12,3.41a vasor yā dhārā madhunā prapīnā ghṛtena miśrā amṛtasya nābhayaḥ |
12,3.41c sarvās tā ava rundhe svargaḥ ṣaṣṭyāṃ śaratsu nidhipā abhīchāt ||41||

12,3.42a nidhiṃ nidhipā abhy enam ichād anīśvarā abhitaḥ santu ye 'nye |
12,3.42c asmābhir datto nihitaḥ svargas tribhiḥ kāṇḍais trīnt svargān arukṣat ||42||

12,3.43a agnī rakṣas tapatu yad videvaṃ kravyād piśāca iha mā pra pāsta |
12,3.43c nudāma enam apa rudhmo asmad ādityā enam aṅgirasaḥ sacantām ||43||
12,3.44a ādityebhyo aṅgirobhyo madhv idaṃ ghṛtena miśraṃ prati vedayāmi |
12,3.44c śuddhahastau brāhmaṇasyānihatyaitaṃ svargaṃ sukṛtāv apītam ||44||

12,3.45a idaṃ prāpam uttamaṃ kāṇḍam asya yasmāl lokāt parameṣṭhī samāpa |
12,3.45c ā siñca sarpir ghṛtavat sam aṅgdhy eṣa bhāgo aṅgiraso no atra ||45||

12,3.46a satyāya ca tapase devatābhyo nidhiṃ śevadhiṃ pari dadma etam |
12,3.46c mā no dyūte 'va gān mā samityāṃ mā smānyasmā ut sṛjatā purā mat ||46||

12,3.47a ahaṃ pacāmy ahaṃ dadāmi mamed u karman karuṇe 'dhi jāyā |
12,3.47c kaumāro loko ajaniṣṭa putro 'nvārabhethāṃ vaya uttarāvat ||47||

12,3.48a na kilbiṣam atra nādhāro asti na yan mitraiḥ samamamāna eti |
12,3.48c anūnaṃ pātraṃ nihitaṃ na etat paktāraṃ pakvaḥ punar ā viśāti ||48||

12,3.49a priyaṃ priyāṇāṃ kṛṇavāma tamas te yantu yatame dviṣanti |
12,3.49c dhenur anaḍvān vayovaya āyad eva pauruṣeyam apa mṛtyuṃ nudantu ||49||

12,3.50a sam agnayaḥ vidur anyo anyaṃ ya oṣadhīḥ sacate yaś ca sindhūn |
12,3.50c yāvanto devā divy ātapanti hiraṇyaṃ jyotiḥ pacato babhūva ||50|| {17}

12,3.51a eṣā tvacāṃ puruṣe saṃ babhūvānagnāḥ sarve paśavo ye anye |
12,3.51c kṣatreṇātmānaṃ pari dhāpayātho 'motaṃ vāso mukham odanasya ||51||

12,3.52a yad akṣeṣu vadā yat samityāṃ yad vā vadā anṛtaṃ vittakāmyā |
12,3.52c samānaṃ tantum abhi samvasānau tasmint sarvaṃ śamalaṃ sādayāthaḥ ||52||

12,3.53a varṣaṃ vanuṣvāpi gacha devāṃs tvaco dhūmaṃ pary ut pātayāsi |
12,3.53c viśvavyacā ghṛtapṛṣṭho bhaviṣyant sayonir lokam upa yāhy etam ||53||

12,3.54a tanvaṃ svargo bahudhā vi cakre yathā vida ātmann anyavarṇām |
12,3.54c apājait kṛṣṇāṃ ruśatīṃ punāno yā lohinī tāṃ te agnau juhomi ||54||

12,3.55a prācyai tvā diśe 'gnaye 'dhipataye 'sitāya rakṣitra ādityāyeṣumate |
12,3.55c etaṃ pari dadmas taṃ no gopāyatāsmākam aitoḥ |
12,3.55e diṣṭaṃ no atra jarase ni neṣaj jarā mṛtyave pari ṇo dadātv atha pakvena saha saṃ bhavema ||55||

12,3.56a dakṣiṇāyai tvā diśa indrāyādhipataye tiraścirājaye rakṣitre yamāyeṣumate |
12,3.56c etaṃ pari dadmas taṃ no gopāyatāsmākam aitoḥ |
12,3.56e diṣṭaṃ no atra jarase ni neṣaj jarā mṛtyave pari ṇo dadātv atha pakvena saha saṃ bhavema ||56||

12,3.57a pratīcyai tvā diśe varuṇāyādhipataye pṛdākave rakṣitre 'nnāyeṣumate |
12,3.57c etaṃ pari dadmas taṃ no gopāyatāsmākam aitoḥ |
12,3.57e diṣṭaṃ no atra jarase ni neṣaj jarā mṛtyave pari ṇo dadātv atha pakvena saha saṃ bhavema ||57||

12,3.58a udīcyai tvā diśe somāyādhipataye svajāya rakṣitre 'śanyā iṣumatyai |
12,3.58c etaṃ pari dadmas taṃ no gopāyatāsmākam aitoḥ |
12,3.58e diṣṭaṃ no atra jarase ni neṣaj jarā mṛtyave pari ṇo dadātv atha pakvena saha saṃ bhavema ||58||

12,3.59a dhruvāyai tvā diśe viṣṇave 'dhipataye kalmāṣagrīvāya rakṣitra oṣadhībhya iṣumatībhyaḥ |
12,3.59c etaṃ pari dadmas taṃ no gopāyatāsmākam aitoḥ |
12,3.59e diṣṭaṃ no atra jarase ni neṣaj jarā mṛtyave pari ṇo dadātv atha pakvena saha saṃ bhavema ||59||

12,3.60a ūrdhvāyai tvā diśe bṛhaspataye 'dhipataye śvitrāya rakṣitre varṣāyeṣumate |
12,3.60c etaṃ pari dadmas taṃ no gopāyatāsmākam aitoḥ |
12,3.60e diṣṭaṃ no atra jarase ni neṣaj jarā mṛtyave pari ṇo dadātv atha pakvena saha saṃ bhavema ||60|| {18}



1dadāmīty eva brūyād anu cainām abhutsata |
1vaśāṃ brahmabhyo yācadbhyas tat prajāvad apatyavat ||1||

1prajayā sa vi krīṇīte paśubhiś copa dasyati |
1ya ārṣeyebhyo yācadbhyo devānāṃ gāṃ na ditsati ||2||

1kūṭayāsya saṃ śīryante śloṇayā kāṭam ardati |
1baṇḍayā dahyante gṛhāḥ kāṇayā dīyate svam ||3||

1vilohito adhiṣṭhānāc chakno vindati gopatim |
1tathā vaśāyāḥ saṃvidyaṃ duradabhnā hy ucyase ||4||

1pador asyā adhiṣṭhānād viklindur nāma vindati |
1anāmanāt saṃ śīryante yā mukhenopajighrati ||5||

1yo asyāḥ karṇāv āskunoty ā sa deveṣu vṛścate |
1lakṣma kurva iti manyate kanīyaḥ kṛṇute svam ||6||

1yad asyāḥ kasmai cid bhogāya bālān kaś cit prakṛntati |
1tataḥ kiśorā mriyante vatsāṃś ca ghātuko vṛkaḥ ||7||

1yad asyā gopatau satyā loma dhvāṅkṣo ajīhiḍat |
1tataḥ kumārā mriyante yakṣmo vindaty anāmanāt ||8||

1yad asyāḥ palpūlanaṃ śakṛd dāsī samasyati |
1tato 'parūpaṃ jāyate tasmād avyeṣyad enasaḥ ||9||

12,4.10a jāyamānābhi jāyate devānt sabrāhmaṇān vaśā |
12,4.10c tasmād brahmabhyo deyaiṣā tad āhuḥ svasya gopanam ||10|| {19}

12,4.11a ya enāṃ vanim āyanti teṣāṃ devakṛtā vaśā |
12,4.11c brahmajyeyaṃ tad abruvan ya enāṃ nipriyāyate ||11||

12,4.12a ya ārṣeyebhyo yācadbhyo devānāṃ gāṃ na ditsati |
12,4.12c ā sa deveṣu vṛścate brāhmaṇānāṃ ca manyave ||12||

12,4.13a yo asya syād vaśābhogo anyām icheta tarhi saḥ |
12,4.13c hiṃste adattā puruṣaṃ yācitāṃ ca na ditsati ||13||

12,4.14a yathā śevadhir nihito brāhmaṇānāṃ tathā vaśā |
12,4.14c tām etad achāyanti yasmin kasmiṃś ca jāyate ||14||

12,4.15a svam etad achāyanti yad vaśāṃ brāhmaṇā abhi |
12,4.15c yathainān anyasmin jinīyād evāsyā nirodhanam ||15||

12,4.16a cared evā traihāyaṇād avijñātagadā satī |
12,4.16c vaśāṃ ca vidyān nārada brāhmaṇās tarhy eṣyāḥ ||16||

12,4.17a ya enām avaśām āha devānāṃ nihitaṃ nidhim |
12,4.17c ubhau tasmai bhavāśarvau parikramyeṣum asyataḥ ||17||

12,4.18a yo asyā ūdho na vedātho asyā stanān uta |
12,4.18c ubhayenaivāsmai duhe dātuṃ ced aśakad vaśām ||18||

12,4.19a duradabhnainam ā śaye yācitāṃ ca na ditsati |
12,4.19c nāsmai kāmāḥ sam ṛdhyante yām adattvā cikīrṣati ||19||

12,4.20a devā vaśām ayācan mukhaṃ kṛtvā brāhmaṇam |
12,4.20c teṣāṃ sarveṣām adadad dheḍaṃ ny eti mānuṣaḥ ||20|| {20}

12,4.21a heḍaṃ paśūnāṃ ny eti brāhmaṇebhyo 'dadad vaśām |
12,4.21c devānāṃ nihitaṃ bhāgaṃ martyaś cen nipriyāyate ||21||

12,4.22a yad anye śataṃ yāceyur brāhmaṇā gopatiṃ vaśām |
12,4.22c athaināṃ devā abruvann evaṃ ha viduṣo vaśā ||22||

12,4.23a ya evaṃ viduṣe 'dattvāthānyebhyo dadad vaśām |
12,4.23c durgā tasmā adhiṣṭhāne pṛthivī sahadevatā ||23||

12,4.24a devā vaśām ayācan yasminn agre ajāyata |
12,4.24c tām etāṃ vidyān nāradaḥ saha devair ud ājata ||24||

12,4.25a anapatyam alpapaśuṃ vaśā kṛṇoti pūruṣam |
12,4.25c brāhmaṇaiś ca yācitām athaināṃ nipriyāyate ||25||

12,4.26a agnīṣomābhyāṃ kāmāya mitrāya varuṇāya ca |
12,4.26c tebhyo yācanti brāhmaṇās teṣv ā vṛścate 'dadat ||26||

12,4.27a yāvad asyā gopatir nopaśṛṇuyād ṛcaḥ svayam |
12,4.27c cared asya tāvad goṣu nāsya śrutvā gṛhe vaset ||27||

12,4.28a yo asyā ṛca upaśrutyātha goṣv acīcarat |
12,4.28c āyuś ca tasya bhūtiṃ ca devā vṛścanti hīḍitāḥ ||28||

12,4.29a vaśā carantī bahudhā devānāṃ nihito nidhiḥ |
12,4.29c āviṣ kṛṇuṣva rūpāṇi yadā sthāma jighāṃsati ||29||

12,4.30a āvir ātmānaṃ kṛṇute yadā sthāma jighāṃsati |
12,4.30c atho ha brahmabhyo vaśā yāñcyāya kṛṇute manaḥ ||30|| {21}

12,4.31a manasā saṃ kalpayati tad devāṃ api gachati |
12,4.31c tato ha brahmāṇo vaśām upaprayanti yācitum ||31||

12,4.32a svadhākāreṇa pitṛbhyo yajñena devatābhyaḥ |
12,4.32c dānena rājanyo vaśāyā mātur heḍam na gachati ||32||

12,4.33a vaśā mātā rājanyasya tathā saṃbhūtam agraśaḥ |
12,4.33c tasyā āhur anarpaṇaṃ yad brahmabhyaḥ pradīyate ||33||

12,4.34a yathājyaṃ pragṛhītam ālumpet sruco agnaye |
12,4.34c evā ha brahmabhyo vaśām agnaya ā vṛścate 'dadat ||34||

12,4.35a puroḍāśavatsā sudughā loke 'smā upa tiṣṭhati |
12,4.35c sāsmai sarvān kāmān vaśā pradaduṣe duhe ||35||

12,4.36a sarvān kāmān yamarājye vaśā pradaduṣe duhe |
12,4.36c athāhur nārakaṃ lokaṃ nirundhānasya yācitām ||36||

12,4.37a pravīyamānā carati kruddhā gopataye vaśā |
12,4.37c vehataṃ mā manyamāno mṛtyoḥ pāśeṣu badhyatām ||37||

12,4.38a yo vehataṃ manyamāno 'mā ca pacate vaśām |
12,4.38c apy asya putrān pautrāṃś ca yācayate bṛhaspatiḥ ||38||

12,4.39a mahad eṣāva tapati carantī goṣu gaur api |
12,4.39c atho ha gopataye vaśādaduṣe viṣaṃ duhe ||39||

12,4.40a priyaṃ paśūnāṃ bhavati yad brahmabhyaḥ pradīyate |
12,4.40c atho vaśāyās tat priyaṃ yad devatrā haviḥ syāt ||40|| {22}

12,4.41a yā vaśā udakalpayan devā yajñād udetya |
12,4.41c tāsāṃ viliptyaṃ bhīmām udākuruta nāradaḥ ||41||

12,4.42a tāṃ devā amīmāṃsanta vaśeyā3m avaśeti |
12,4.42c tām abravīn nārada eṣā vaśānāṃ vaśatameti ||42||

12,4.43a kati nu vaśā nārada yās tvaṃ vettha manuṣyajāḥ |
12,4.43c tās tvā pṛchāmi vidvāṃsaṃ kasyā nāśnīyād abrāhmaṇaḥ ||43||

12,4.44a viliptyā bṛhaspate yā ca sūtavaśā vaśā |
12,4.44c tasyā nāśnīyād abrāhmaṇo ya āśaṃseta bhūtyām ||44||

12,4.45a namas te astu nāradānuṣṭhu viduṣe vaśā |
12,4.45c katamāsāṃ bhīmatamā yām adattvā parābhavet ||45||

12,4.46a viliptī yā bṛhaspate 'tho sūtavaśā vaśā |
12,4.46c tasyā nāśnīyād abrāhmaṇo ya āśaṃseta bhūtyām ||46||

12,4.47a trīṇi vai vaśājātāni viliptī sūtavaśā vaśā |
12,4.47c tāḥ pra yached brahmabhyaḥ so 'nāvraskaḥ prajāpatau ||47||

12,4.48a etad vo brāhmaṇā havir iti manvīta yācitaḥ |
12,4.48c vaśāṃ ced enaṃ yāceyur yā bhīmādaduṣo gṛhe ||48||

12,4.49a devā vaśāṃ pary avadan na no 'dād iti hīḍitāḥ |
12,4.49c etābhir ṛgbhir bhedaṃ tasmād vai sa parābhavat ||49||

12,4.50a utaināṃ bhedo nādadād vaśām indreṇa yācitaḥ |
12,4.50c tasmāt taṃ devā āgaso 'vṛścann ahamuttare ||50||

12,4.51a ye vaśāyā adānāya vadanti parirāpiṇaḥ |
12,4.51c indrasya manyave jālmā ā vṛścante acittyā ||51||

12,4.52a ye gopatiṃ parāṇīyāthāhur mā dadā iti |
12,4.52c rudrasyāstāṃ te hetīṃ pari yanty acittyā ||52||

12,4.53a yadi hutaṃ yady ahutām amā ca pacate vaśām |
12,4.53c devānt sabrāhmaṇān ṛtvā jihmo lokān nir ṛchati ||53|| {23}


12,5.53a śrameṇa tapasā sṛṣṭā brahmaṇā vittā rte śritā ||1||

1satyenāvṛtā śriyā prāvṛtā yaśasā parīvṛtā ||2||

1svadhayā parihitā śraddhayā paryūḍhā dīkṣayā guptā yajñe pratiṣṭhitā loko nidhanam ||3||

1brahma padavāyaṃ brāhmaṇo 'dhipatiḥ ||4||

1tām ādadānasya brahmagavīṃ jinato brāhmaṇaṃ kṣatriyasya ||5||

1apa krāmati sūnṛtā vīryaṃ punyā lakṣmīḥ ||6|| {24}

1ojaś ca tejaś ca sahaś ca balaṃ ca vāk cendriyaṃ ca śrīś ca dharmaś ca ||7||

1brahma ca kṣatraṃ ca rāṣṭraṃ ca viśaś ca tviṣiś ca yaśaś ca varcaś ca draviṇaṃ ca ||8||

1āyuś ca rūpaṃ ca nāma ca kīrtiś ca prāṇaś cāpānaś ca cakṣuś ca śrotraṃ ca ||9||

12,5.10a payaś ca rasaś cānnaṃ cānnādyaṃ ca rtaṃ ca satyaṃ ceṣṭaṃ ca pūrtaṃ ca prajā ca paśavaś ca ||10||

12,5.11a tāni sarvāṇy apa krāmanti brahmagavīm ādadānasya jinato brāhmaṇaṃ kṣatriyasya ||11|| {25}

12,5.12a saiṣā bhīmā brahmagavy aghaviṣā sākṣāt kṛtyā kūlbajam āvṛtā ||12||

12,5.13a sarvāṇy asyāṃ ghorāṇi sarve ca mṛtyavaḥ ||13||

12,5.14a sarvāṇy asyāṃ krūrāṇi sarve puruṣavadhāḥ ||14||

12,5.15a sā brahmajyaṃ devapīyuṃ brahmagavy ādīyamānā mṛtyoḥ padvīṣa ā dyati ||15||

12,5.16a meniḥ śatavadhā hi sā brahmajyasya kṣitir hi sā ||16||

12,5.17a tasmād vai brāhmaṇānāṃ gaur durādharṣā vijānatā ||17||

12,5.18a vajro dhāvantī vaiśvānara udvītā ||18||

12,5.19a hetiḥ śaphān utkhidantī mahādevo 'pekṣamāṇā ||19||

12,5.20a kṣurapavir īkṣamāṇā vāśyamānābhi sphūrjati ||20||

12,5.21a mṛtyur hiṅkṛṇvaty ugro devaḥ puchaṃ paryasyantī ||21||

12,5.22a sarvajyāniḥ karṇau varīvarjayantī rājayakṣmo mehantī ||22||

12,5.23a menir duhyamānā śīrṣaktir dugdhā ||23||

12,5.24a sedir upatiṣṭhantī mithoyodhaḥ parāmṛṣṭā ||24||
12,5.25a śaravyā mukhe 'pinahyamāna ṛtir hanyamānā ||25||

12,5.26a aghaviṣā nipatantī tamo nipatitā ||26||

12,5.27a anugachantī prāṇān upa dāsayati brahmagavī brahmajyasya ||27|| {26}

12,5.28a vairaṃ vikṛtyamānā pautrādyaṃ vibhājyamānā ||28||

12,5.29a devahetir hriyamāṇā vyṛddhir hṛtā ||29||

12,5.30a pāpmādhidhīyamānā pāruṣyam avadhīyamānā ||30||

12,5.31a viṣaṃ prayasyantī takmā prayastā ||31||

12,5.32a aghaṃ pracyamānā duṣvapnyaṃ pakvā ||32||
12,5.33a mūlabarhaṇī paryākriyamāṇā kṣitiḥ paryākṛtā ||33||

12,5.34a asaṃjñā gandhena śug uddhriyamāṇāśīviṣa uddhṛtā ||34||

12,5.35a abhūtir upahriyamāṇā parābhūtir upahṛtā ||35||

12,5.36a śarvaḥ kruddhaḥ piśyamānā śimidā piśitā ||36||

12,5.37a avartir aśyamānā nirṛtir aśitā ||37||

12,5.38a aśitā lokāc chinatti brahmagavī brahmajyam asmāc cāmuṣmāc ca ||38|| {27}

12,5.39a tasyā āhananaṃ kṛtyā menir āśasanaṃ valaga ūbadhyam ||39||

12,5.40a asvagatā parihṇutā ||40||

12,5.41a agniḥ kravyād bhūtvā brahmagavī brahmajyaṃ praviśyātti ||41||

12,5.42a sarvāsyāṅgā parvā mūlāni vṛścati ||42||

12,5.43a chinatty asya pitṛbandhu parā bhāvayati mātṛbandhu ||43||

12,5.44a vivāhāṃ jñātīnt sarvān api kṣāpayati brahmagavī brahmajyasya kṣatriyeṇāpunardīyamānā ||44||

12,5.45a avāstum enam asvagam aprajasaṃ karoty aparāparaṇo bhavati kṣīyate ||45||

12,5.46a ya evaṃ viduṣo brāhmaṇasya kṣatriyo gām ādatte ||46|| {28}

12,5.47a kṣipraṃ vai tasyāhanane gṛdhrāḥ kurvata ailabam ||47||

12,5.48a kṣipraṃ vai tasyādahanaṃ pari nṛtyanti keśinīr āghnānāḥ pāṇinorasi kurvāṇāḥ pāpam ailabam ||48||

12,5.49a kṣipraṃ vai tasya vāstuṣu vṛkāḥ kurvata ailabam ||49||

12,5.50a kṣipraṃ vai tasya pṛchanti yat tad āsī3d idaṃ nu tā3d iti ||50||

12,5.51a chindhy ā chindhi pra chindhy api kṣāpaya kṣāpaya ||51||

12,5.52a ādadānam āṅgirasi brahmajyam upa dāsaya ||52||

12,5.53a vaiśvadevī hy ucyase kṛtyā kūlbajam āvṛtā ||53||

12,5.54a oṣantī samoṣantī brahmaṇo vajraḥ ||54||

12,5.55a kṣurapavir mṛtyur bhūtvā vi dhāva tvam ||55||

12,5.56a ā datse jinatāṃ varca iṣṭaṃ pūrtaṃ cāśiṣaḥ ||56||

12,5.57a ādāya jītaṃ jītāya loke 'muṣmin pra yachasi ||57||

12,5.58a aghnye padavīr bhava brāhmaṇasyābhiśastyā ||58||

12,5.59a meniḥ śaravyā bhavāghād aghaviṣā bhava ||59||

12,5.60a aghnye pra śiro jahi brahmajyasya kṛtāgaso devapīyor arādhasaḥ ||60||

12,5.61a tvayā pramūrṇaṃ mṛditam agnir dahatu duścitam ||61|| {29}

12,5.62a vṛśca pra vṛśca saṃ vṛśca daha pra daha saṃ daha ||62||

12,5.63a brahmajyaṃ devy aghnya ā mūlād anusaṃdaha ||63||

12,5.64a yathāyād yamasādanāt pāpalokān parāvataḥ ||64||

12,5.65a evā tvaṃ devy aghnye brahmajyasya kṛtāgaso devapīyor arādhasaḥ ||65||

12,5.66a vajreṇa śataparvaṇā tīkṣṇena kṣurabhṛṣṭinā ||66||

12,5.67a pra skandhān pra śiro jahi ||67||

12,5.68a lomāny asya saṃ chindhi tvacam asya vi veṣṭaya ||68||

12,5.69a māṃsāny asya śātaya snāvāny asya saṃ vṛha ||69||

12,5.70a asthīny asya pīḍaya majjānam asya nir jahi ||70||

12,5.71a sarvāsyāṅgā parvāṇi vi śrathaya ||71||

12,5.72a agnir enaṃ kravyāt pṛthivyā nudatām ud oṣatu vāyur antarikṣān mahato varimṇaḥ ||72||

12,5.73a sūrya enaṃ divaḥ pra ṇudatāṃ ny oṣatu ||73|| {30}



1udehi vājin yo apsv antar idaṃ rāṣṭraṃ pra viśa sūnṛtāvat |
1yo rohito viśvam idaṃ jajāna sa tvā rāṣṭrāya subhṛtaṃ bibhartu ||1||

1ud vāja ā gan yo apsv antar viśa ā roha tvadyonayo yāḥ |
1somaṃ dadhāno 'pa oṣadhīr gāś catuṣpado dvipada ā veśayeha ||2||

1yūyam ugrā marutaḥ pṛśnimātara indreṇa yujā pra mṛṇīta śatrūn |
1ā vo rohitaḥ śṛṇavat sudānavas triṣaptāso marutaḥ svādusaṃmudaḥ ||3||

1ruho ruroha rohita ā ruroha garbho janīnāṃ januṣām upastham |
1tābhiḥ saṃrabdham anv avindan ṣaḍ urvīr gātuṃ prapaśyann iha rāṣṭram āhāḥ ||4||

1ā te rāṣṭram iha rohito 'hārṣīd vy āsthan mṛdho abhayaṃ te abhūt |
1tasmai te dyāvāpṛthivī revatībhiḥ kāmaṃ duhātām iha śakvarībhiḥ ||5||

1rohito dyāvāpṛthivī jajāna tatra tantuṃ parameṣṭhī tatāna |
1tatra śiśriye 'ja ekapādo 'dṛṃhad dyāvāpṛthivī balena ||6||

1rohito dyāvāpṛthivī adṛṃhat tena sva stabhitaṃ tena nākaḥ |
1tenāntarikṣaṃ vimitā rajāṃsi tena devā amṛtam anv avindan ||7||

1vi rohito amṛśad viśvarūpaṃ samākurvāṇaḥ praruho ruhaś ca |
1divaṃ rūḍhvā mahatā mahimnā saṃ te rāṣṭram anaktu payasā ghṛtena ||8||

1yās te ruhaḥ praruho yās ta āruho yābhir āpṛṇāsi divam antarikṣam |
1tāsāṃ brahmaṇā payasā vavṛdhāno viśi rāṣṭre jāgṛhi rohitasya ||9||

13,1.10a yas te viśas tapasaḥ saṃbabhūvur vatsaṃ gāyatrīm anu tā ihāguḥ |
13,1.10c tās tvā viśantu manasā śivena saṃmātā vatso abhy etu rohitaḥ ||10|| {1}

13,1.11a ūrdhvo rohito adhi nāke asthād viśvā rūpāṇi janayan yuvā kaviḥ |
13,1.11c tigmenāgnir jyotiṣā vi bhāti tṛtīye cakre rajasi priyāṇi ||11||

13,1.12a sahasraśṛṅgo vṛṣabho jātavedā ghṛtāhutaḥ somapṛṣṭhaḥ suvīraḥ |
13,1.12c mā mā hāsīn nāthito net tvā jahāni gopoṣaṃ ca me vīrapoṣaṃ ca dhehi ||12||

13,1.13a rohito yajñasya janitā mukhaṃ ca rohitāya vācā śrotreṇa manasā juhomi |
13,1.13c rohitaṃ devā yanti sumanasyamānāḥ sa mā rohaiḥ sāmityai rohayatu ||13||

13,1.14a rohito yajñaṃ vy adadhād viśvakarmaṇe tasmāt tejāṃsy upa memāny āguḥ |
13,1.14c voceyaṃ te nābhiṃ bhuvanasyādhi majmani ||14||

13,1.15a ā tvā ruroha bṛhaty uta paṅktir ā kakub varcasā jātavedaḥ |
13,1.15c ā tvā rurohoṣṇihākṣaro vaṣaṭkāra ā tvā ruroha rohito retasā saha ||15||

13,1.16a ayaṃ vaste garbhaṃ pṛthivyā divaṃ vaste 'yam antarikṣam |
13,1.16c ayaṃ bradhnasya viṣṭapi svar lokān vy ānaśe ||16||

13,1.17a vācas pate pṛthivī naḥ syonā syonā yonis talpā naḥ suśevā |
13,1.17c ihaiva prāṇaḥ sakhye no astu taṃ tvā parameṣṭhin pary agnir āyuṣā varcasā dadhātu ||17||

13,1.18a vācas pata ṛtavaḥ pañca ye nau vaiśvakarmaṇāḥ pari ye saṃbabhūvuḥ |
13,1.18c ihaiva prāṇaḥ sakhye no astu taṃ tvā parameṣṭhin pari rohita āyuṣā varcasā dadhātu ||18||

13,1.19a vācas pate saumanasaṃ manaś ca goṣṭhe no gā janaya yoniṣu prajāḥ |
13,1.19c ihaiva prāṇaḥ sakhye no astu taṃ tvā parameṣṭhin pary aham āyuṣā varcasā dadhātu ||19||

13,1.20a pari tvā dhāt savitā devo agnir varcasā mitrāvaruṇāv abhi tvā |
13,1.20c sarvā arātīr avakrāmann ehīdaṃ rāṣṭram akaraḥ sunṛtāvat ||20|| {2}

13,1.21a yaṃ tvā pṛṣatī rathe praṣṭir vahati rohita |
13,1.21c śubhā yāsi riṇann apaḥ ||21||

13,1.22a anuvratā rohiṇī rohitasya sūriḥ suvarṇā bṛhatī suvarcāḥ |
13,1.22c tayā vājān viśvarūpāṃ jayema tayā viśvāḥ pṛtanā abhi ṣyāma ||22||

13,1.23a idaṃ sado rohiṇī rohitasyāsau panthāḥ pṛṣatī yena yāti |
13,1.23c tāṃ gandharvāḥ kaśyapā un nayanti tāṃ rakṣanti kavayo 'pramādam ||23||

13,1.24a sūryasyāśvā harayaḥ ketumantaḥ sadā vahanty amṛtāḥ sukhaṃ ratham |
13,1.24c ghṛtapāvā rohito bhrājamāno divaṃ devaḥ pṛṣatīm ā viveśa ||24||

13,1.25a yo rohito vṛṣabhas tigmaśṛṅgaḥ pary agniṃ pari sūryaṃ babhūva |
13,1.25c yo viṣṭabhnāti pṛthivīṃ divaṃ ca tasmād devā adhi sṛṣṭīḥ sṛjante ||25||

13,1.26a rohito divam āruhan mahataḥ pary arṇavāt |
13,1.26c sarvo ruroha rohito ruhaḥ ||26||

13,1.27a vi mimīṣva payasvatīṃ ghṛtācīṃ devānāṃ dhenur anapaspṛg eṣā |
13,1.27c indraḥ somaṃ pibatu kṣemo astv agniḥ pra stautu vi mṛdho nudasva ||27||

13,1.28a samiddho agniḥ samidhāno ghṛtavṛddho ghṛtāhutaḥ |
13,1.28c abhīṣāṭ viśvāṣāḍ agniḥ sapatnān hantu ye mama ||28||

13,1.29a hantv enān pra dahatv arir yo naḥ pṛtanyati |
13,1.29c kravyādāgninā vayaṃ sapatnān pra dahāmasi ||29||

13,1.30a avācīnān ava jahīndra vajreṇa bāhumān |
13,1.30c adhā sapatnān māmakān agnes tejobhir ādiṣi ||30|| {3}

13,1.31a agne sapatnān adharān pādayāsmad vyathayā sajātam utpipānaṃ bṛhaspate |
13,1.31c indrāgnī mitrāvaruṇāv adhare padyantām apratimanyūyamānāḥ ||31||

13,1.32a udyaṃs tvaṃ deva sūrya sapatnān ava me jahi |
13,1.32c avainān aśmanā jahi te yantv adhamaṃ tamaḥ ||32||

13,1.33a vatso virājo vṛṣabho matīnām ā ruroha śukrapṛṣṭho 'ntarikṣam |
13,1.33c ghṛtenārkam abhy arcanti vatsaṃ brahma santaṃ brahmaṇā vardhayanti ||33||

13,1.34a divaṃ ca roha pṛthivīṃ ca roha rāṣṭraṃ ca roha draviṇaṃ ca roha |
13,1.34c prajāṃ ca rohāmṛtaṃ ca roha rohitena tanvaṃ saṃ spṛṣasva ||34||

13,1.35a ye devā rāṣṭrabhṛto 'bhito yanti sūryam |
13,1.35c taiṣ ṭe rohitaḥ samvidāno rāṣṭraṃ dadhātu sumanasyamānaḥ ||35||

13,1.36a ut tvā yajñā brahmapūtā vahanty adhvagato harayas tvā vahanti |
13,1.36c tiraḥ samudram ati rocase 'rṇavam ||36||

13,1.37a rohite dyāvāpṛthivī adhi śrite vasujiti gojiti saṃdhanājiti |
13,1.37c sahasraṃ yasya janimāni sapta ca voceyaṃ te nābhiṃ bhuvanasyādhi majmani ||37||

13,1.38a yaśā yāsi pradiśo diśaś ca yaśāḥ paśūnām uta carṣaṇīnām |
13,1.38c yaśāḥ pṛthivyā adityā upasthe 'haṃ bhūyāsaṃ saviteva cāruḥ ||38||

13,1.39a amutra sann iha vetthetaḥ saṃs tāni paśyasi |
13,1.39c itaḥ paśyanti rocanaṃ divi sūryaṃ vipaścitam ||39||

13,1.40a devo devān marcayasy antaś carasy arṇave |
13,1.40c samānam agnim indhate taṃ viduḥ kavayaḥ pare ||40|| {4}

13,1.41a avaḥ pareṇa para enāvareṇa padā vatsaṃ bibratī gaur ud asthāt |
13,1.41c sā kadrīcī kaṃ svid ardhaṃ parāgāt kva svit sūte nahi yūthe asmin ||41||

13,1.42a ekapadī dvipadī sā catuṣpady aṣṭāpadī navapadī babhūvuṣī |
13,1.42c sahasrākṣarā bhuvanasya paṅktis tasyāḥ samudrā adhi vi kṣaranti ||42||

13,1.43a ārohan dyām amṛtaḥ prāva me vacaḥ |
13,1.43c ut tvā yajñā brahmapūtā vahanty adhvagato harayas tvā vahanti ||43||

13,1.44a veda tat te amartya yat ta ākramaṇaṃ divi |
13,1.44c yat te sadhasthaṃ parame vyoman ||44||

13,1.45a sūryo dyāṃ sūryaḥ pṛṭhivīṃ sūrya āpo'ti paśyati |
13,1.45c sūryo bhūtasyaikaṃ cakṣur ā ruroha divaṃ mahīm ||45||

13,1.46a urvīr āsan paridhayo vedir bhūmir akalpata |
13,1.46c tatraitāv agnī ādhatta himaṃ ghraṃsaṃ ca rohitaḥ ||46||

13,1.47a himaṃ ghraṃsaṃ cādhāya yūpān kṛtvā parvatān |
13,1.47c varṣājyāv agnī ījāte rohitasya svarvidaḥ ||47||

13,1.48a svarvido rohitasya brahmaṇāgniḥ sam idhyate |
13,1.48c tasmād ghraṃsas tasmād dhimas tasmād yajño 'jāyata ||48||

13,1.49a brahmaṇāgnī vāvṛdhānau brahmavṛddhau brahmāhutau |
13,1.49c brahmeddhāv agnī ījāte rohitasya svarvidaḥ ||49||

13,1.50a satye anyaḥ samāhito 'psv anyaḥ sam idhyate |
13,1.50c brahmeddhāv agnī ījāte rohitasya svarvidaḥ ||50|| {5}

13,1.51a yaṃ vātaḥ pariśumbhati yaṃ vendro brahmaṇaspatiḥ |
13,1.51c brahmeddhāvagnī ījāte rohitasya svarvidaḥ ||51||

13,1.52a vediṃ bhūmiṃ kalpayitvā divaṃ kṛtvā dakṣiṇām |
13,1.52c ghraṃsaṃ tad agniṃ kṛtvā cakāra viśvam ātmanvad varṣeṇājyena rohitaḥ ||52||

13,1.53a varṣam ājam ghraṃso agnir vedir bhūmir akalpata |
13,1.53c tatraitān parvatān agnir gīrbhir ūrdhvāṃ akalpayat ||53||

13,1.54a gīrbhir ūrdhvān kalpayitvā rohito bhūmim abravīt |
13,1.54c tvayīdaṃ sarvaṃ jāyatāṃ yad bhūtaṃ yac ca bhāvyam ||54||

13,1.55a sa yajñaḥ prathamo bhūto bhavyo ajāyata |
13,1.55c tasmād dha jajña idaṃ sarvaṃ yat kiṃ cedaṃ virocate rohitena ṛṣiṇābhṛtam ||55||

13,1.56a yaś ca gāṃ padā sphurati pratyaṅ sūryaṃ ca mehati |
13,1.56c tasya vṛścāmi te mūlaṃ na chāyāṃ karavo 'param ||56||

13,1.57a yo mābhichāyam atyeṣi māṃ cāgniṃ cāntarā |
13,1.57c tasya vṛścāmi te mūlaṃ na chāyāṃ karavo 'param ||57||

13,1.58a yo adya deva sūrya tvāṃ ca māṃ cāntarāyati |
13,1.58c duṣvapnyaṃ tasmiṃ chamalaṃ duritāni ca mṛjmahe ||58||

13,1.59a mā pra gāma patho vayaṃ mā yajñād indra sominaḥ |
13,1.59c mānta sthur no arātayaḥ ||59||

13,1.60a yo yajñasya prasādhanas tantur deveṣv ātataḥ |
13,1.60c tam āhutam aśīmahi ||60|| {6}



1ud asya ketavo divi śukrā bhrājanta īrate |
1ādityasya nṛcakṣaso mahivratasya mīḍhuṣaḥ ||1||

1diśāṃ prajñānāṃ svarayantam arciṣā supakṣam āśuṃ patayantam arṇave |
1stavāma sūryaṃ bhuvanasya gopāṃ yo raśmibhir diśa ābhāti sarvāḥ ||2||

1yat prāṅ pratyaṅ svadhayā yāsi śībhaṃ nānārūpe ahanī karṣi māyayā |
1tad āditya mahi tat te mahi śravo yad eko viśvaṃ pari bhūma jāyase ||3||

1vipaścitaṃ taraṇiṃ bhrājamānaṃ vahanti yaṃ haritaḥ sapta bahvīḥ |
1srutād yam attrir divam unnināya taṃ tvā paśyanti pariyāntam ājim ||4||

1mā tvā dabhan pariyāntam ājiṃ svasti durgāṃ ati yāhi śībham |
1divaṃ ca sūrya pṛthivīṃ ca devīm ahorātre vimimāno yad eṣi ||5||

1svasti te sūrya carase rathāya yenobhāv antau pariyāsi sadyaḥ |
1yaṃ te vahanti harito vahiṣṭhāḥ śatam aśvā yadi vā sapta bahvīḥ ||6||

1sukhaṃ sūrya ratham aṃśumantaṃ syonaṃ suvahnim adhi tiṣṭha vājinam |
1yaṃ te vahanti harito vahiṣṭhāḥ śatam aśvā yadi vā sapta bahvīḥ ||7||

1sapta sūryo harito yātave rathe hiraṇyatvacaso bṛhatīr ayukta |
1amoci śukro rajasaḥ parastād vidhūya devas tamo divam āruhat ||8||

1ut ketunā bṛhatā deva āgann apāvṛk tamo 'bhi jyotir aśrait |
1divyaḥ suparṇaḥ sa vīro vy akhyad aditeḥ putro bhuvanāni viśvā ||9||

13,2.10a udyan raśmīn ā tanuṣe viśvā rupāṇi puṣyasi |
13,2.10c ubhā samudrau kratunā vi bhāsi sarvāṃl lokān paribhūr bhrājamānaḥ ||10|| {7}

13,2.11a pūrvāparaṃ carato māyayaitau śiśū krīḍantau pari yāto 'rṇavam |
13,2.11c viśvānyo bhuvanā vicaṣṭe hairaṇyair anyaṃ harito vahanti ||11||

13,2.12a divi tvāttrir adhārayat sūryā māsāya kartave |
13,2.12c sa eṣi sudhṛtas tapan viśvā bhūtāvacākaśat ||12||

13,2.13a ubhāv antau sam arṣasi vatsaḥ saṃmātarāv iva |
13,2.13c nanv etad itaḥ purā brahma devā amī viduḥ ||13||

13,2.14a yat samudram anu śritaṃ tat siṣāsati sūryaḥ |
13,2.14c adhvāsya vitato mahān pūrvaś cāparaś ca yaḥ ||14||

13,2.15a taṃ sam āpnoti jūtibhis tato nāpa cikitsati |
13,2.15c tenāmṛtasya bhakṣaṃ devānāṃ nāva rundhate ||15||

13,2.16a ud u tyaṃ jātavedasaṃ devaṃ vahanti ketavaḥ |
13,2.16c dṛśe viśvāya sūryam ||16||

13,2.17a apa tye tāyavo yathā nakṣatrā yanty aktubhiḥ |
13,2.17c sūrāya viśvacakṣase ||17||

13,2.18a adṛśrann asya ketavo vi raśmayo janāṃ anu |
13,2.18c bhrājanto agnayo yathā ||18||

13,2.19a taraṇir viśvadarśato jyotiṣkṛd asi sūrya |
13,2.19c viśvam ā bhāsi rocana ||19||

13,2.20a pratyaṅ devānāṃ viśaḥ pratyaṅṅ ud eṣi mānuṣīḥ |
13,2.20c pratyaṅ viśvaṃ svar dṛśe ||20|| {8}

13,2.21a yenā pāvaka cakṣasā bhuraṇyantaṃ janāṃ anu |
13,2.21c tvaṃ varuṇa paśyasi ||21||

13,2.22a vi dyām eṣi rajas pṛthv ahar mimāno aktubhiḥ |
13,2.22c paśyan janmāni sūrya ||22||

13,2.23a sapta tvā harito rathe vahanti deva sūrya |
13,2.23c śociṣkeśaṃ vicakṣaṇam ||23||

13,2.24a ayukta sapta śundhyuvaḥ sūro rathasya naptyaḥ |
13,2.24c tābhir yāti svayuktibhiḥ ||24||

13,2.25a rohito divam āruhat tapasā tapasvī |
13,2.25c sa yonim aiti sa u jāyate punaḥ sa devānām adhipatir babhūva ||25||

13,2.26a yo viśvacarṣaṇir uta viśvatomukho yo viśvataspāṇir uta viśvataspṛthaḥ |
13,2.26c saṃ bāhubhyāṃ bharati saṃ patatrair dyāvāpṛthivī janayan deva ekaḥ ||26||

13,2.27a ekapād dvipado bhūyo vi cakrame dvipāt tripādam abhy eti paścāt |
13,2.27c dvipād dha ṣaṭpado bhūyo vi cakrame ta ekapadas tanvaṃ sam āsate ||27||

13,2.28a atandro yāsyan harito yad āsthād dve rūpe kṛṇute rocamānaḥ |
13,2.28c ketumān udyant sahamāno rajāṃsi viśvā āditya pravato vi bhāsi ||28||

13,2.29a baṇ mahāṃ asi sūrya baḍ āditya mahāṃ asi |
13,2.29c mahāṃs te mahato mahimā tvam āditya mahāṃ asi ||29||

13,2.30a rocase divi rocase antarikṣe pataṅga pṛthivyāṃ rocase rocase apsv antaḥ |
13,2.30c ubhā samudrau rucyā vy āpitha devo devāsi mahiṣaḥ svarjit ||30|| {9}

13,2.31a arvāṅ parastāt prayato vyadhva āśur vipaścit patayan pataṅgaḥ |
13,2.31c viṣṇur vicittaḥ śavasādhitiṣṭhan pra ketunā sahate viśvam ejat ||31||

13,2.32a citrāś cikitvān mahiṣaḥ suparṇa ārocayan rodasī antarikṣam |
13,2.32c ahorātre pari sūryaṃ vasāne prāsya viśvā tirato vīryāṇi ||32||

13,2.33a tigmo vibhrājan tanvaṃ śiśāno 'raṃgamāsaḥ pravato rarāṇaḥ |
13,2.33c jyotiṣmān pakṣī mahiṣo vayodhā viśvā āsthāt pradiśaḥ kalpamānaḥ ||33||

13,2.34a citraṃ devānām ketur anīkaṃ jyotiṣmān pradiśaḥ sūrya udyan |
13,2.34c divākaro 'ti dyumnais tamāṃsi viśvātārīd duritāni śukraḥ ||34||

13,2.35a citraṃ devānām ud agād anīkaṃ cakṣur mitrasya varuṇasyāgneḥ |
13,2.35c āprād dyāvāpṛthivī antarikṣaṃ sūrya ātmā jagatas tasthuṣaś ca ||35||

13,2.36a uccā patantam aruṇaṃ suparṇaṃ madhye divas taraṇiṃ bhrājamānam |
13,2.36c paśyama tvā savitāraṃ yam āhur ajasraṃ jyotir yad avindad attriḥ ||36||

13,2.37a divas pṛṣṭhe dhāvamānaṃ suparṇam adityāḥ putraṃ nāthakāma upa yāmi bhītaḥ |
13,2.37c sa naḥ sūrya pra tira dīrgham āyur mā riṣāma sumatau te syāma ||37||

13,2.38a sahasrāhṇyaṃ viyatāv asya pakṣau harer haṃsasya patataḥ svargam |
13,2.38c sa devānt sarvān urasy upadadya saṃpaśyan yāti bhuvanāni viśvā ||38||

13,2.39a rohitaḥ kālo abhavad rohito 'gre prajāpatiḥ |
13,2.39c rohito yajñānāṃ mukhaṃ rohitaḥ svar ābharat ||39||

13,2.40a rohito loko abhavad rohito 'ty atapad divam |
13,2.40c rohito raśmibhir bhūmiṃ samudram anu saṃ carat ||40|| {10}

13,2.41a sarvā diśaḥ sam acarad rohito 'dhipatir divaḥ |
13,2.41c divaṃ samudram ād bhūmiṃ sarvaṃ bhūtaṃ vi rakṣati ||41||

13,2.42a ārohan chukro bṛhatīr atandro dve rūpe kṛṇute rocamānaḥ |
13,2.42c citraś cikitvān mahiṣo vātamāyā yāvato lokān abhi yad vibhāti ||42||

13,2.43a abhy anyad eti pary anyad asyate 'horātrābhyāṃ mahiṣaḥ kalpamānaḥ |
13,2.43c sūryaṃ vayaṃ rajasi kṣiyantaṃ gātuvidaṃ havāmahe nādhamānāḥ ||43||

13,2.44a pṛthivīpro mahiṣo nādhamānasya gātur adabdhacakṣuḥ pari viśvaṃ babhūva |
13,2.44c viśvaṃ saṃpaśyant suvidatro yajatra idaṃ śṛṇotu yad ahaṃ bravīmi ||44||

13,2.45a pary asya mahimā pṛthivīṃ samudraṃ jyotiṣā vibhrājan pari dyām antarikṣam |
13,2.45c sarvaṃ saṃpaśyant suvidatro yajatra idaṃ śṛṇotu yad ahaṃ bravīmi ||45||

13,2.46a abodhy agniḥ samidhā janānāṃ prati dhenum ivāyatīm uṣasam |
13,2.46c yahvā iva pra vayām ujjihānāḥ pra bhānavaḥ sisrate nākam acha ||46|| {11}



1ya ime dyāvāpṛthivī jajāna yo drāpim kṛtvā bhuvanāni vaste |
1yasmin kṣiyanti pradiśaḥ ṣaḍ urvīr yāḥ pataṅgo anu vicākaśīti |
1tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti |

1yasmād vātā ṛtuthā pavante yasmāt samudrā adhi vikṣaranti |
1tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti |
1ud vepaya rohita pra kṣiṇīhi brahmajyasya prati muñca pāśān ||2||

1yo mārayati prāṇayati yasmāt prāṇanti bhuvanāni viśvā |
1tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti |
1ud vepaya rohita pra kṣiṇīhi brahmajyasya prati muñca pāśān ||3||

1yaḥ prāṇena dyāvāpṛthivī tarpayaty apānena samudrasya jaṭharaṃ yaḥ piparti |
1tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti |
1ud vepaya rohita pra kṣiṇīhi brahmajyasya prati muñca pāśān ||4||

1yasmin virāṭ parameṣṭhī prajāpatir agnir vaiśvānaraḥ saha paṅktyā śritaḥ |
1yaḥ parasya prāṇaṃ paramasya teja ādade |
1tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti |

1yasmin ṣaḍ urvīḥ pañca diśo adhiśritāś catasra āpo yajñasya trayo 'kṣarāḥ |
1yo antarā rodasī kruddhaś cakṣuṣaikṣata |
1tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇam jināti |

1yo annādo annapatir babhūva brahmaṇas patir uta yaḥ |
1bhūto bhaviṣyat bhuvanasya yas patiḥ |
1tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti |

1ahorātrair vimitaṃ triṃśadaṅgaṃ trayodaśaṃ māsaṃ yo nirmimīte |
1tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti |
1ud vepaya rohita pra kṣiṇīhi brahmajyasya prati muñca pāśān ||8||

1kṛsṇaṃ niyānaṃ harayaḥ suparṇā apo vasānā divam ut patanti |
1ta āvavṛtrant sadanād ṛtasya |
1tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti |

13,3.10a yat te candraṃ kaśyapa rocanāvad yat saṃhitaṃ puṣkalaṃ citrabhānu yasmint sūryā ārpitāḥ sapta sākam |
13,3.10c tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti |
13,3.10e ud vepaya rohita pra kṣiṇīhi brahmajyasya prati muñca pāśān ||10|| {12}

13,3.11a bṛhad enam anu vaste purastād rathaṃtaraṃ prati gṛhṇāti paścāt |
13,3.11c jyotir vasāne sadam apramādam |
13,3.11e tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti |

13,3.12a bṛhad anyataḥ pakṣa āsīd rathaṃtaram anyataḥ sabale sadhrīcī |
13,3.12c yad rohitam ajanayanta devāḥ |
13,3.12e tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti |

13,3.13a sa varuṇaḥ sāyam agnir bhavati sa mitro bhavati prātar udyan |
13,3.13c sa savitā bhūtvāntarikṣeṇa yāti sa indro bhūtvā tapati madhyato divam |
13,3.13e tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti |

13,3.14a sahasrāhṇyaṃ viyatāv asya pakṣau harer haṃsasya patataḥ svargam |
13,3.14c sa devānt sarvān urasy upadadya saṃpaśyan yāti bhuvanāni viśvā |
13,3.14e tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti |

13,3.15a ayaṃ sa devo apsv antaḥ sahasramūlaḥ paruśāko attriḥ |
13,3.15c ya idaṃ viśvaṃ bhuvanaṃ jajāna |
13,3.15e tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti |

13,3.16a śukraṃ vahanti harayo raghuṣyado devaṃ divi varcasā bhrājamānam |
13,3.16c yasyordhvā divaṃ tanvas tapanty arvāṅ suvarṇaiḥ paṭarair vi bhāti |
13,3.16e tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti |

13,3.17a yenādityān haritaḥ samvahanti yena yajñena bahavo yanti prajānantaḥ |
13,3.17c yad ekaṃ jyotir bahudhā vibhāti |
13,3.17e tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti |

13,3.18a sapta yuñjanti ratham ekacakram eko aśvo vahati saptanāmā |
13,3.18c trinābhi cakram ajaram anarvaṃ yatremā viśvā bhuvanādhi tasthuḥ |
13,3.18e tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti |

13,3.19a aṣṭadhā yukto vahati vahnir ugraḥ pitā devānāṃ janitā matīnām |
13,3.19c ṛtasya tantuṃ manasā mimānaḥ sarvā diśaḥ pavate mātariśvā |
13,3.19e tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti |

13,3.20a saṃyañcaṃ tantuṃ pradiśo 'nu sarvā antar gāyatryām amṛtasya garbhe |
13,3.20c tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti |
13,3.20e ud vepaya rohita pra kṣiṇīhi brahmajyasya prati muñca pāśān ||20|| {13}

13,3.21a nimrucas tisro vyuṣo ha tisras trīṇi rajāṃsi divo aṅga tisraḥ |
13,3.21c vidmā te agne tredhā janitraṃ tredhā devānāṃ janimāni vidma |
13,3.21e tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti |

13,3.22a vi ya aurṇot pṛthivīṃ jāyamāna ā samudram adadhāt antarikṣe |
13,3.22c tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti |
13,3.22e ud vepaya rohita pra kṣiṇīhi brahmajyasya prati muñca pāśān ||22||

13,3.23a tvam agne kratubhiḥ ketubhir hito 'rkaḥ samiddha ud arocathā divi |
13,3.23c kim abhy ārcan marutaḥ pṛśnimātaro yad rohitam ajanayanta devāḥ |
13,3.23e tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti |

13,3.24a ya ātmadā baladā yasya viśva upāsate praśiṣaṃ yasya devāḥ |
13,3.24c yo 'syeśe dvipado yaś catuṣpadaḥ |
13,3.24e tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti |

13,3.25a ekapād dvipado bhūyo vi cakrame dvipāt tripādam abhy eti paścāt |
13,3.25c catuṣpāc cakre dvipadām abhisvare saṃpaśyan paṅktim upatiṣṭhamānaḥ |
13,3.25e tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti |

13,3.26a kṛṣṇāyaḥ putro arjuno rātryā vatso 'jāyata |
13,3.26c sa ha dyām adhi rohati ruho ruroha rohitaḥ ||26|| {14}


13,4.26a sa eti savitā svar divas pṛṣṭhe 'vacākaśat ||1||

1raśmibhir nabha ābhṛtaṃ mahendra ety āvṛtaḥ ||2||

1sa dhātā sa vidhartā sa vāyur nabha ucchritam ||3||

1so 'ryamā sa varuṇaḥ sa rudraḥ sa mahādevaḥ ||4||

1so agniḥ sa u sūryaḥ sa u eva mahāyamaḥ ||5||

1taṃ vatsā upa tiṣṭhanty ekaśīrṣāṇo yutā daśa ||6||

1paścāt prāñca ā tanvanti yad udeti vi bhāsati ||7||

1tasyaiṣa māruto gaṇaḥ sa eti śikyākṛtaḥ ||8||

1raśmibhir nabha ābhṛtaṃ mahendra ety āvṛtaḥ ||9||

13,4.10a tasyeme nava kośā viṣṭambhā navadhā hitāḥ ||10||

13,4.11a sa prajābhyo vi paśyati yac ca prāṇati yac ca na ||11||

13,4.12a tam idaṃ nigataṃ sahaḥ sa eṣa eka ekavṛd eka eva ||12||

13,4.13a ete asmin devā ekavṛto bhavanti ||13|| {15}

13,4.14a kīrtiś ca yaśaś cāmbhaś ca nabhaś ca brāhmaṇavarcasaṃ cānnaṃ cānnādyaṃ ca ||14||

13,4.15a ya etaṃ devam ekavṛtaṃ veda ||15||

13,4.16a na dvitīyo na tṛtīyaś caturtho nāpy ucyate ||16||

13,4.17a na pañcamo na ṣaṣṭhaḥ saptamo nāpy ucyate ||17||

13,4.18a nāṣṭamo na navamo daśamo nāpy ucyate ||18||

13,4.19a sa sarvasmai vi paśyati yac ca prāṇati yac ca na ||19||

13,4.20a tam idaṃ nigataṃ sahaḥ sa eṣa eka ekavṛd eka eva ||20||

13,4.21a sarve asmin devā ekavṛto bhavanti ||21|| {16}

13,4.22a brahma ca tapaś ca kīrtiś ca yaśaś cāmbhaś ca nabhaś ca brāhmaṇavarcasaṃ cānnaṃ cānnādyaṃ ca ||2||

13,4.23a bhūtaṃ ca bhavyaṃ ca śraddhā ca ruciś ca svargaś ca svadhā ca ||23||

13,4.24a ya etaṃ devam ekavṛtaṃ veda ||24||

13,4.25a sa eva mṛtyuḥ so 'mṛtaṃ so 'bhvaṃ sa rakṣaḥ ||25||

13,4.26a sa rudro vasuvanir vasudeye namovāke vaṣaṭkāro 'nu saṃhitaḥ ||26||

13,4.27a tasyeme sarve yātava upa praśiṣam āsate ||27||

13,4.28a tasyāmū sarvā nakṣatrā vaśe candramasā saha ||28|| {17}

13,4.29a sa vā ahno 'jāyata tasmād ahar ajāyata ||29||

13,4.30a sa vai rātryā ajāyata tasmād rātrir ajāyata ||30||

13,4.31a sa vā antarikṣād ajāyata tasmād antarikṣam ajāyata ||31||

13,4.32a sa vai vāyor ajāyata tasmād vāyur ajāyata ||32||

13,4.33a sa vai divo 'jāyata tasmād dyaur adhi ajāyata ||33||

13,4.34a sa vai digbhyo 'jāyata tasmād diśo 'jāyanta ||34||

13,4.35a sa vai bhūmer ajāyata tasmād bhūmir ajāyata ||35||

13,4.36a sa vā agner ajāyata tasmād agnir ajāyata ||36||

13,4.37a sa vā adbhyo 'jāyata tasmād āpo 'jāyanta ||37||

13,4.38a sa vā ṛgbhyo 'jāyata tasmād ṛco 'jāyanta ||38||

13,4.39a sa vai yajñād ajāyata tasmād yajño 'jāyata ||39||

13,4.40a sa yajñas tasya yajñaḥ sa yajñasya śiras kṛtam ||40||

13,4.41a sa stanayati sa vi dyotate sa u aśmānam asyati ||41||

13,4.42a pāpāya vā bhadrāya vā puruṣāyāsurāya vā ||42||

13,4.43a yad vā kṛṇoṣy oṣadhīr yad vā varṣasi bhadrayā yad vā janyam avīvṛdhaḥ ||43||

13,4.44a tāvāṃs te maghavan mahimopo te tanvaḥ śatam ||44||

13,4.45a upo te badhve baddhāni yadi vāsi nyarbudam ||45|| {18}

13,4.46a bhūyān indro namurād bhūyān indrāsi mṛtyubhyaḥ ||46||

13,4.47a bhūyān arātyāḥ śacyāḥ patis tvam indrāsi vibhūḥ prabhūr iti tvopāsmahe vayam ||47||

13,4.48a namas te astu paśyata paśya mā paśyata ||48||

13,4.49a annādyena yaśasā tejasā brāhmaṇavarcasena ||49||

13,4.50a ambho amo mahaḥ saha iti tvopāsmahe vayam ||50||

13,4.51a ambho aruṇaṃ rajataṃ rajaḥ saha iti tvopāsmahe vayam ||51|| {19}

13,4.52a uruḥ pṛthuḥ subhūr bhuva iti tvopāsmahe vayam ||52||

13,4.53a pratho varo vyaco loka iti tvopāsmahe vayam ||53||

13,4.54a bhavadvasur idadvasuḥ saṃyadvasur āyadvasur iti tvopāsmahe vayam ||54||

13,4.55a namas te astu paśyata paśya mā paśyata ||55||

13,4.56a annādyena yaśasā tejasā brāhmaṇavarcasena ||56|| {20}



1satyenottabhitā bhūmiḥ sūryeṇottabhitā dyauḥ |
1ṛtenādityās tiṣṭhanti divi somo adhi śritaḥ ||1||

1somenādityā balinaḥ somena pṛthivī mahī |
1atho nakṣatrāṇām eṣām upasthe soma āhitaḥ ||2||

1somaṃ manyate papivān yat saṃpiṃṣanty oṣadhim |
1somaṃ yaṃ brahmāṇo vidur na tasyāśnāti pārthivaḥ ||3||

1yat tvā soma prapibanti tata ā pyāyase punaḥ |
1vāyuḥ somasya rakṣitā samānāṃ māsa ākṛtiḥ ||4||

1āchadvidhānair gupito bārhataiḥ soma rakṣitaḥ |
1grāvṇām ic chṛṇvan tiṣṭhasi na te aśnāti pārthivaḥ ||5||

1cittir ā upabarhaṇaṃ cakṣur ā abhyañjanam |
1dyaur bhūmiḥ kośa āsīd yad ayāt sūryā patim ||6||

1raibhy āsīd anudeyī nārāśaṃsī nyocanī |
1suryāyā bhadram id vāso gāthayati pariṣkṛtā ||7||

1stomā āsan pratidhayaḥ kurīraṃ chanda opaśaḥ |
1sūryāyā aśvinā varāgnir āsīt purogavaḥ ||8||

1somo vadhūyur abhavad aśvināstām ubhā varā |
1sūryāṃ yat patye śaṃsantīṃ manasā savitādadāt ||9||

14,1.10a mano asyā ana āsīd dyaur āsīd uta chadiḥ |
14,1.10c śukrāv anaḍvāhāv āstāṃ yad ayāt sūryā patim ||10|| {1}

14,1.11a ṛksāmābhyām abhihitau gāvau te sāmanāv aitām |
14,1.11c śrotre te cakre āstāṃ divi panthāś carācaraḥ ||11||

14,1.12a śucī te cakre yātyā vyāno akṣa āhataḥ |
14,1.12c ano manasmayaṃ sūryārohat prayatī patim ||12||

14,1.13a sūryāyā vahatuḥ prāgāt savitā yam avāsṛjat |
14,1.13c maghāsu hanyante gāvaḥ phalgunīṣu vy uhyate ||13||

14,1.14a yad aśvinā pṛchamānāv ayātaṃ tricakreṇa vahatuṃ sūryāyāḥ |
14,1.14c kvaikaṃ cakraṃ vām āsīt kva deṣṭrāya tasthathuḥ ||14||

14,1.15a yad ayātaṃ śubhas patī vareyaṃ sūryām upa |
14,1.15c viśve devā anu tad vām ajānan putraḥ pitaram avṛṇīta pūṣā ||15||

14,1.16a dve te cakre sūrye brahmāṇa ṛtuthā viduḥ |
14,1.16c athaikaṃ cakraṃ yad guhā tad addhātaya id viduḥ ||16||

14,1.17a aryamaṇaṃ yajāmahe subandhuṃ pativedanam |
14,1.17c urvārukam iva bandhanāt preto muñcāmi nāmutaḥ ||17||

14,1.18a preto muñcāmi nāmutaḥ subaddhām amutas karam |
14,1.18c yatheyam indra mīḍhvaḥ suputrā subhagāsati ||18||

14,1.19a pra tvā muñcāmi varuṇasya pāśād yena tvābadhnāt savitā suśevāḥ |
14,1.19c ṛtasya yonau sukṛtasya loke syonaṃ te astu sahasaṃbhalāyai ||19||
14,1.20a bhagas tveto nayatu hastagṛhyāśvinā tvā pra vahatāṃ rathena |
14,1.20c gṛhān gacha gṛhapatnī yathāso vaśinī tvaṃ vidatham ā vadāsi ||20|| {2}

14,1.21a iha priyaṃ prajāyai te sam ṛdhyatām asmin gṛhe gārhapatyāya jāgṛhi |
14,1.21c enā patyā tanvaṃ saṃ spṛśasvātha jirvir vidatham ā vadāsi ||21||

14,1.22a ihaiva staṃ mā vi yauṣṭaṃ viśvam āyur vy aśnutam |
14,1.22c krīḍantau putrair naptṛbhir modamānau svastakau ||22||

14,1.23a pūrvāparaṃ carato māyaitau śiśū krīḍantau pari yāto 'rṇavam |
14,1.23c viśvānyo bhuvanā vicaṣṭa ṛtūṃr anyo vidadhaj jāyase navaḥ ||23||

14,1.24a navonavo bhavasi jāyamāno 'hnāṃ ketur uṣasām eṣy agram |
14,1.24c bhāgaṃ devebhyo vi dadhāsy āyan pra candramas tirase dīrgham āyuḥ ||24||
14,1.25a parā dehi śāmulyaṃ brahmabhyo vi bhajā vasu |
14,1.25c kṛtyaiṣā padvatī bhūtvā jāyā viśate patim ||25||

14,1.26a nīlalohitaṃ bhavati kṛtyāsaktir vy ajyate |
14,1.26c edhante asyā jñātayaḥ patir bandheṣu badhyate ||26||

14,1.27a aślīlā tanūr bhavati ruśatī pāpayāmuyā |
14,1.27c patir yad vadhvo vāsasaḥ svam aṅgam abhyūrṇute ||27||

14,1.28a āśasanaṃ viśasanam atho adhivikartanam |
14,1.28c sūryāyāḥ paśya rūpāṇi tāni brahmota śumbhati ||28||

14,1.29a tṛṣṭam etat kaṭukam apāṣṭhavad viṣavan naitad attave |
14,1.29c sūryāṃ yo brahmā veda sa id vādhūyam arhati ||29||

14,1.30a sa it tat syonaṃ harati brahmā vāsaḥ sumaṅgalam |
14,1.30c prāyaścittiṃ yo adhyeti yena jāyā na riṣyati ||30|| {3}

14,1.31a yuvaṃ bhagaṃ saṃ bharataṃ samṛddham ṛtaṃ vadantāv ṛtodyeṣu |
14,1.31c brahmaṇas pate patim asyai rocaya cāru saṃbhalo vadatu vācam etām ||31||

14,1.32a ihed asātha na paro gamāthemaṃ gāvaḥ prajayā vardhayātha |
14,1.32c śubhaṃ yatīr usriyāḥ somavarcaso viśve devāḥ krann iha vo manāṃsi ||32||

14,1.33a imaṃ gāvaḥ prajayā saṃ viśāthāyaṃ devānāṃ na mināti bhāgam |
14,1.33c asmai vaḥ pūṣā marutaś ca sarve asmai vo dhātā savitā suvāti ||33||

14,1.34a anṛkṣarā ṛjavaḥ santu panthano yebhiḥ sakhāyo yanti no vareyam |
14,1.34c saṃ bhagena sam aryamṇā saṃ dhātā sṛjatu varcasā ||34||

14,1.35a yac ca varco akṣeṣu surāyāṃ ca yad āhitam |
14,1.35c yad goṣv aśvinā varcas tenemāṃ varcasāvatam ||35||

14,1.36a yena mahānaghnyā jaghanam aśvinā yena vā surā |
14,1.36c yenākṣā abhyaṣicyanta tenemāṃ varcasāvatam ||36||

14,1.37a yo anidhmo dīdayad apsv antar yaṃ viprāsa īḍate adhvareṣu |
14,1.37c apāṃ napān madhumatīr apo dā yābhir indro vāvṛdhe vīryāvān ||37||

14,1.38a idam ahaṃ ruśantaṃ grābhaṃ tanūdūṣim apohāmi |
14,1.38c yo bhadro rocanas tam ud acāmi ||38||

14,1.39a āsyai brāhmaṇāḥ snapanīr harantv avīraghnīr ud ajantv āpaḥ |
14,1.39c aryamṇo agniṃ pary etu pūṣan pratīkṣante śvaśuro devaraś ca ||39||

14,1.40a śaṃ te hiraṇyaṃ śam u santv āpaḥ śaṃ methir bhavatu śaṃ yugasya tardma |
14,1.40c śaṃ ta āpaḥ śatapavitrā bhavantu śam u patyā tanvaṃ saṃ spṛśasva ||40|| {4}

14,1.41a khe rathasya khe 'nasaḥ khe yugasya śatakrato |
14,1.41c apālām indra triṣ pūtvākṛṇoḥ sūryatvacam ||41||

14,1.42a āśāsānā saumanasaṃ prajāṃ saubhāgyaṃ rayim |
14,1.42c patyur anuvratā bhūtvā saṃ nahyasvāmṛtāya kam ||42||

14,1.43a yathā sindhur nadīnāṃ sāmrājyaṃ suṣuve vṛṣā |
14,1.43c evā tvaṃ samrājñy edhi patyur astaṃ paretya ||43||

14,1.44a samrājñy edhi śvaśureṣu samrājñy uta devṛṣu |
14,1.44c nanānduḥ samrājñy edhi samrājñy uta śvaśrvāḥ ||44||

14,1.45a yā akṛntann avayan yāś ca tatnire yā devīr antāṃ abhito 'dadanta |
14,1.45c tās tvā jarase saṃ vyayantv āyuṣmatīdaṃ pari dhatsva vāsaḥ ||45||

14,1.46a jīvaṃ rudanti vi nayanty adhvaraṃ dīrghām anu prasitiṃ dīdhyur naraḥ |
14,1.46c vāmaṃ pitṛbhyo ya idaṃ samīrire mayaḥ patibhyo janaye pariṣvaje ||46||

14,1.47a syonaṃ dhruvaṃ prajāyai dhārayāmi te 'śmānaṃ devyāḥ pṛthivyā upasthe |
14,1.47c tam ā tiṣṭhānumādyā suvarcā dīrghaṃ ta āyuḥ savitā kṛṇotu ||47||

14,1.48a yenāgnir asyā bhūmyā hastaṃ jagrāha dakṣiṇam |
14,1.48c tena gṛhṇāmi te hastaṃ mā vyathiṣṭhā mayā saha prajayā ca dhanena ca ||48||

14,1.49a devas te savitā hastaṃ gṛhṇātu somo rājā suprajasaṃ kṛṇotu |
14,1.49c agniḥ subhagāṃ jatavedāḥ patye patnīṃ jaradaṣṭim kṛṇotu ||49||

14,1.50a gṛhṇāmi te saubhagatvāya hastaṃ mayā patyā jaradaṣṭir yathāsaḥ |
14,1.50c bhago aryamā savitā puraṃdhir mahyaṃ tvādur gārhapatyāya devāḥ ||50|| {5}
14,1.51a bhagas te hastam agrahīt savitā hastam agrahīt |
14,1.51c patnī tvam asi dharmaṇāhaṃ gṛhapatis tava ||51||

14,1.52a mameyam astu poṣyā mahyaṃ tvādād bṛhaspatiḥ |
14,1.52c mayā patyā prajāvati saṃ jīva śaradaḥ śatam ||52||

14,1.53a tvaṣṭā vāso vy adadhāc chubhe kaṃ bṛhaspateḥ praśiṣā kavīnām |
14,1.53c tenemāṃ nārīṃ savitā bhagaś ca sūryām iva pari dhattāṃ prajayā ||53||

14,1.54a indrāgnī dyāvāpṛthivī mātariśvā mitrāvaruṇā bhago aśvinobhā |
14,1.54c bṛhaspatir maruto brahma soma imāṃ nāriṃ prajayā vardhayantu ||54||
14,1.55a bṛhaspatiḥ prathamaḥ sūryāyāḥ śīrṣe keśāṃ akalpayat |
14,1.55c tenemām aśvinā nārīṃ patye saṃ śobhayāmasi ||55||

14,1.56a idaṃ tad rūpaṃ yad avasta yoṣā jāyāṃ jijñāse manasā carantīm |
14,1.56c tām anv artiṣye sakhibhir navagvaiḥ ka imān vidvān vi cacarta pāśān ||56||

14,1.57a ahaṃ vi ṣyāmi mayi rūpam asyā vedad it paśyan manasaḥ kulāyam |
14,1.57c na steyam admi manasod amucye svayaṃ śrathnāno varuṇasya pāśān ||57||

14,1.58a pra tvā muñcāmi varuṇasya pāśād yena tvābadhnāt savitā suśevāḥ |
14,1.58c uruṃ lokaṃ sugam atra panthāṃ kṛṇomi tubhyaṃ sahapatnyai vadhu ||58||

14,1.59a ud yachadhvam apa rakṣo hanāthemaṃ nārīṃ sukṛte dadhāta |
14,1.59c dhātā vipaścit patim asyai viveda bhago rājā pura etu prajānan ||59||

14,1.60a bhagas tatakṣa caturaḥ pādān bhagas tatakṣa catvāry uṣpalāni |
14,1.60c tvaṣṭā pipeśa madhyato 'nu vardhrānt sā no astu sumaṅgalī ||60||

14,1.61a sukiṃśukaṃ vahatuṃ viśvarūpaṃ hiraṇyavarṇaṃ suvṛtaṃ sucakram |
14,1.61c ā roha sūrye amṛtasya lokaṃ syonaṃ patibhyo vahatuṃ kṛṇu tvam ||61||

14,1.62a abhrātṛghnīṃ varuṇāpaśughnīṃ bṛhaspate |
14,1.62c indrāpatighnīm putriṇīm āsmabhyaṃ savitar vaha ||62||

14,1.63a mā hiṃsiṣṭaṃ kumāryaṃ sthūṇe devakṛte pathi |
14,1.63c śālāyā devyā dvāraṃ syonaṃ kṛṇmo vadhūpatham ||63||

14,1.64a brahmāparaṃ yujyatāṃ brahma pūrvaṃ brahmāntato madhyato brahma sarvataḥ |
14,1.64c anāvyādhāṃ devapurāṃ prapadya śivā syonā patiloke vi rāja ||64|| {6}



1tubhyam agre pary avahant sūryāṃ vahatunā saha |
1sa naḥ patibhyo jāyāṃ dā agne prajayā saha ||1||

1punaḥ patnīm agnir adād āyuṣā saha varcasā |
1dīrghāyur asyā yaḥ patir jīvāti śaradaḥ śatam ||2||

1somasya jāyā prathamaṃ gandharvas te 'paraḥ patiḥ |
1tṛtīyo agniṣ ṭe patis turīyas te manuṣyajāḥ ||3||

1somo dadad gandharvāya gandharvo dadad agnaye |
1rayiṃ ca putrāṃs cādād agnir mahyam atho imām ||4||

1ā vām agant sumatir vājinīvasū ny aśvinā hṛtsu kāmā araṃsata |
1abhūtaṃ gopā mithunā śubhas patī priyā aryamṇo duryāṃ aśīmahi ||5||

1sā mandasānā manasā śivena rayiṃ dhehi sarvavīraṃ vacasyam |
1sugaṃ tīrthaṃ suprapāṇaṃ śubhas patī sthāṇuṃ pathiṣṭhām apa durmatiṃ hatam ||6||

1yā oṣadhayo yā nadyo yāni kṣetrāṇi yā vanā |
1tās tvā vadhu prajāvatīṃ patye rakṣantu rakṣasaḥ ||7||

1emaṃ panthām arukṣāma sugaṃ svastivāhanam |
1yasmin vīro na riṣyaty anyeṣāṃ vindate vasu ||8||

1idaṃ su me naraḥ śṛṇuta yayāśiṣā daṃpatī vāmam aśnutaḥ |
1ye gandharvā apsarasaś ca devīr eṣu vānaspatyeṣu ye 'dhi tasthuḥ |
1syonās te asyai vadhvai bhavantu mā hiṃsiṣur vahatum uhyamānam ||9||

14,2.10a ye vadhvaś candraṃ vahatuṃ yakṣmā yanti janāṃ anu |
14,2.10c punas tān yajñiyā devā nayantu yata āgatāḥ ||10|| {7}

14,2.11a mā vidan paripanthino ya āsīdanti daṃpatī |
14,2.11c sugena durgam atītām apa drāntv arātayaḥ ||11||

14,2.12a saṃ kāśayāmi vahatuṃ brahmaṇā gṛhair aghoreṇa cakṣuṣā mitriyeṇa |
14,2.12c paryāṇaddhaṃ viśvarūpaṃ yad asti syonaṃ patibhyaḥ savitā tat kṛṇotu ||12||

14,2.13a śivā nārīyam astam āgann imaṃ dhātā lokam asyai dideśa |
14,2.13c tām aryamā bhago aśvinobhā prajāpatiḥ prajayā vardhayantu ||13||

14,2.14a ātmanvaty urvarā nārīyam āgan tasyāṃ naro vapata bījam asyām |
14,2.14c sā vaḥ prajāṃ janayad vakṣaṇābhyo bibhratī dugdham ṛṣabhasya retaḥ ||14||

14,2.15a prati tiṣṭha virāḍ asi viṣṇur iveha sarasvati |
14,2.15c sinīvāli pra jāyatāṃ bhagasya sumatāv asat ||15||

14,2.16a ud va ūrmiḥ śamyā hantv āpo yoktrāṇi muñcata |
14,2.16c māduṣkṛtau vyenasāv aghnyāv aśunam āratām ||16||

14,2.17a aghoracakṣur apatighnī syonā śagmā suśevā suyamā gṛhebhyaḥ |
14,2.17c vīrasūr devṛkāmā saṃ tvayaidhiṣīmahi sumasyamānā ||17||

14,2.18a adevṛghny apatighnīhaidhi śivā paśubhyaḥ suyamā suvarcāḥ |
14,2.18c prajāvatī vīrasūr devṛkāmā syonemam agniṃ gārhapatyaṃ saparya ||18||

14,2.19a ut tiṣṭhetaḥ kim ichantīdam āgā ahaṃ tveḍe abhibhūḥ svād gṛhāt |
14,2.19c śūnyaiṣī nirṛte yājaganthot tiṣṭhārāte pra pata meha raṃsthāḥ ||19||

14,2.20a yadā gārhapatyam asaparyait pūrvam agniṃ vadhūr iyam |
14,2.20c adhā sarasvatyai nāri pitṛbhyaś ca namas kuru ||20|| {8}

14,2.21a śarma varmaitad ā harāsyai nāryā upastire |
14,2.21c sinīvāli pra jāyatāṃ bhagasya sumatāv asat ||21||

14,2.22a yaṃ balbajaṃ nyasyatha carma copastṛṇīthana |
14,2.22c tad ā rohatu suprajā yā kanyā vindate patim ||22||

14,2.23a upa stṛṇīhi balbajam adhi carmaṇi rohite |
14,2.23c tatropaviśya suprajā imam agniṃ saparyatu ||23||

14,2.24a ā roha carmopa sīdāgnim eṣa devo hanti rakṣāṃsi sarvā |
14,2.24c iha prajāṃ janaya patye asmai sujyaiṣṭhyo bhavat putras ta eṣaḥ ||24||

14,2.25a vi tiṣṭhantāṃ mātur asyā upasthān nānārūpāḥ paśavo jāyamānāḥ |
14,2.25c sumaṅgaly upa sīdemam agniṃ saṃpatnī prati bhūṣeha devān ||25||

14,2.26a sumaṅgalī prataraṇī gṛhāṇāṃ suśevā patye śvaśurāya śaṃbhūḥ |
14,2.26c syonā śvaśrvai pra gṛhān viśemān ||26||

14,2.27a syonā bhava śvaśurebhyaḥ syonā patye gṛhebhyaḥ |
14,2.27c syonāsyai sarvasyai viśe syonā puṣṭāyaiṣāṃ bhava ||27||

14,2.28a sumaṅgalīr iyaṃ vadhūr imāṃ sameta paśyata |
14,2.28c saubhāgyam asyai dattvā daurbhāgyair viparetana ||28||

14,2.29a yā durhārdo yuvatayo yāś ceha jaratīr api |
14,2.29c varco nv asyai saṃ dattāthāstaṃ viparetana ||29||

14,2.30a rukmaprastaraṇaṃ vahyaṃ viśvā rūpāṇi bibhratam |
14,2.30c ārohat sūryā sāvitrī bṛhate saubhagāya kam ||30|| {9}

14,2.31a ā roha talpaṃ sumanasyamāneha prajāṃ janaya patye asmai |
14,2.31c indrāṇīva subudhā budhyamānā jyotiragrā uṣasaḥ prati jāgarāsi ||31||

14,2.32a devā agre ny apadyanta patnīḥ sam aspṛśanta tanvas tanūbhiḥ |
14,2.32c sūryeva nāri viśvarūpā mahitvā prajāvatī patyā saṃ bhaveha ||32||

14,2.33a ut tiṣṭheto viśvāvaso namaseḍāmahe tvā |
14,2.33c jāmim icha pitṛṣadaṃ nyaktāṃ sa te bhāgo januṣā tasya viddhi ||33||

14,2.34a apsarasaḥ sadhamādaṃ madanti havirdhānam antarā sūryaṃ ca |
14,2.34c tās te janitram abhi tāḥ parehi namas te gandharvartunā kṛṇomi ||34||

14,2.35a namo gandharvasya namase namo bhāmāya cakṣuṣe ca kṛṇmaḥ |
14,2.35c viśvāvaso brahmaṇā te namo 'bhi jāyā apsarasaḥ parehi ||35||

14,2.36a rāyā vayaṃ sumanasaḥ syāmod ito gandharvam āvīvṛtāma |
14,2.36c agant sa devaḥ paramaṃ sadhastham aganma yatra pratiranta āyuḥ ||36||

14,2.37a saṃ pitarāv ṛtviye sṛjethāṃ mātā pitā ca retaso bhavāthaḥ |
14,2.37c marya iva yoṣām adhi rohayaināṃ prajāṃ kṛṇvāthām iha puṣyataṃ rayim ||37||

14,2.38a tāṃ pūṣaṃ chivatamām erayasva yasyāṃ bījaṃ manuṣyā vapanti |
14,2.38c yā na ūrū uśatī viśrayāti yasyām uśantaḥ praharema śepaḥ ||38||

14,2.39a ā rohorum upa dhatsva hastaṃ pari ṣvajasva jāyāṃ sumanasyamānaḥ |
14,2.39c prajāṃ kṛṇvāthām iha modamānau dīrghaṃ vām āyuḥ savitā kṛṇotu ||39||

14,2.40a ā vāṃ prajāṃ janayatu prajāpatir ahorātrābhyāṃ sam anaktv aryamā |
14,2.40c adurmaṅgalī patilokam ā viśemaṃ śaṃ no bhava dvipade śaṃ catuṣpade ||40|| {10}

14,2.41a devair dattaṃ manunā sākam etad vādhūyaṃ vāso vadhvaś ca vastram |
14,2.41c yo brahmaṇe cikituṣe dadāti sa id rakṣāṃsi talpāni hanti ||41||

14,2.42a yaṃ me datto brahmabhāgaṃ vadhūyor vādhūyaṃ vāso vadhvaś ca vastram |
14,2.42c yuvaṃ brahmaṇe 'numanyamānau bṛhaspate sākam indraś ca dattam ||42||

14,2.43a syonād yoner adhi badhyamānau hasāmudau mahasā modamānau |
14,2.43c sugū suputrau sugṛhau tarātho jīvāv uṣaso vibhātīḥ ||43||

14,2.44a navaṃ vasānaḥ surabhiḥ suvāsā udāgāṃ jīva uṣaso vibhātīḥ |
14,2.44c āṇḍāt patatrīvāmukṣi viśvasmād enasas pari ||44||

14,2.45a śumbhanī dyāvāpṛthivī antisumne mahivrate |
14,2.45c āpaḥ sapta susruvur devīs tā no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ ||45||

14,2.46a sūryāyai devebhyo mitrāya varuṇāya ca |
14,2.46c ye bhūtasya pracetasas tebhya idam akaraṃ namaḥ ||46||

14,2.47a ya ṛte cid abhiśriṣaḥ purā jatrubhya ātṛdaḥ |
14,2.47c saṃdhātā saṃdhiṃ maghavā purūvasur niṣkartā vihrutaṃ punaḥ ||47||

14,2.48a apāsmat tama uchatu nīlaṃ piśaṅgam uta lohitaṃ yat |
14,2.48c nirdahanī yā pṛṣātaky asmin tāṃ sthāṇāv adhy ā sajāmi ||48||

14,2.49a yāvatīḥ kṛtyā upavāsane yāvanto rājño varuṇasya pāśāḥ |
14,2.49c vyṛddhayo yā asamṛddhayo yā asmin tā sthāṇāv adhi sādayāmi ||49||

14,2.50a yā me priyatamā tanūḥ sā me bibhāya vāsasaḥ |
14,2.50c tasyāgre tvaṃ vanaspate nīviṃ kṛṇuṣva mā vayaṃ riṣāma ||50|| {11}

14,2.51a ye antā yāvatīḥ sico ya otavo ye ca tantavaḥ |
14,2.51c vāso yat patnībhir utaṃ tan na syonam upa spṛśāt ||51||

14,2.52a uśatīḥ kanyalā imāḥ pitṛlokāt patiṃ yatīḥ |
14,2.52c ava dīkṣām asṛkṣata svāhā ||52||

14,2.53a bṛhaspatināvasṛṣṭāṃ viśve devā adhārayan |
14,2.53c varco goṣu praviṣṭaṃ yat tenemāṃ saṃ sṛjāmasi ||53||

14,2.54a bṛhaspatināvasṛṣṭāṃ viśve devā adhārayan |
14,2.54c tejo goṣu praviṣṭaṃ yat tenemāṃ saṃ sṛjāmasi ||54||

14,2.55a bṛhaspatināvasṛṣṭāṃ viśve devā adhārayan |
14,2.55c bhajo goṣu praviṣṭo yas tenemāṃ saṃ sṛjāmasi ||55||

14,2.56a bṛhaspatināvasṛṣṭāṃ viśve devā adhārayan |
14,2.56c yaśo goṣu praviṣṭaṃ yat tenemāṃ saṃ sṛjāmasi ||56||

14,2.57a bṛhaspatināvasṛṣṭāṃ viśve devā adhārayan |
14,2.57c payo goṣu praviṣṭaṃ yat tenemāṃ saṃ sṛjāmasi ||57||

14,2.58a bṛhaspatināvasṛṣṭāṃ viśve devā adhārayan |
14,2.58c raso goṣu praviṣṭo yas tenemāṃ saṃ sṛjāmasi ||58||

14,2.59a yadīme keśino janā gṛhe te samanartiṣū rodena kṛṇvanto 'gham |
14,2.59c agniṣ ṭvā tasmād enasaḥ savitā ca pra muñcatām ||59||

14,2.60a yadīyaṃ duhitā tava vikeśy arudad gṛhe rodena kṛṇvaty agham |
14,2.60c agniṣ ṭvā tasmād enasaḥ savitā ca pra muñcatām ||60|| {12}

14,2.61a yaj jāmayo yad yuvatayo gṛhe te samanartiṣū rodena kṛṇvatīr agham |
14,2.61c agniṣ ṭvā tasmād enasaḥ savitā ca pra muñcatām ||61||

14,2.62a yat te prajāyāṃ paśuṣu yad vā gṛheṣu niṣṭhitam aghakṛdbhir aghaṃ kṛtam |
14,2.62c agniṣ ṭvā tasmād enasaḥ savitā ca pra muñcatām ||62||

14,2.63a iyaṃ nāry upa brūte pūlyāny āvapantikā |
14,2.63c dīrghāyur astu me patir jīvāti śaradaḥ śatam ||63||

14,2.64a ihemāv indra saṃ nuda cakravākeva daṃpatī |
14,2.64c prajayainau svastakau viśvam āyur vy aśnutām ||64||

14,2.65a yad āsandyām upadhāne yad vopavāsane kṛtam |
14,2.65c vivāhe kṛtyāṃ yāṃ cakrur āsnāne tāṃ ni dadhmasi ||65||

14,2.66a yad duṣkṛtaṃ yac chamalaṃ vivāhe vahatau ca yat |
14,2.66c tat saṃbhalasya kambale mṛjmahe duritaṃ vayam ||66||

14,2.67a saṃbhale malaṃ sādayitvā kambale duritaṃ vayam |
14,2.67c abhūma yajñiyāḥ śuddhāḥ pra ṇa āyūṃṣi tāriṣat ||67||

14,2.68a kṛtrimaḥ kaṇṭakaḥ śatadan ya eṣaḥ |
14,2.68c apāsyāḥ keśyaṃ malam apa śīrṣaṇyaṃ likhāt ||68||

14,2.69a aṅgādaṅgād vayam asyā apa yakṣmaṃ ni dadhmasi |
14,2.69c tan mā prāpat pṛthivīṃ mota devān divaṃ mā prāpad urv antarikṣam |
14,2.69e apo mā prāpan malam etad agne yamam mā prāpat pitṝṃś ca sarvān ||69||

14,2.70a saṃ tvā nahyāmi payasā pṛthivyāḥ saṃ tvā nahyāmi payasauṣadhīnām |
14,2.70c saṃ tvā nahyāmi prajayā dhanena sā saṃnaddhā sanuhi vājam emam ||70|| {13}

14,2.71a amo 'ham asmi sā tvaṃ sāmāham asmy ṛk tvaṃ dyaur ahaṃ pṛthivī tvam |
14,2.71c tāv iha saṃ bhavāva prajām ā janayāvahai ||71||

14,2.72a janiyanti nāv agravaḥ putriyanti sudānavaḥ |
14,2.72c ariṣṭāsū sacevahi bṛhate vājasātaye ||72||

14,2.73a ye pitaro vadhūdarśā imaṃ vahatum āgaman |
14,2.73c te asyai vadhvai saṃpatnyai prajāvac charma yachantu ||73||

14,2.74a yedaṃ pūrvāgan raśanāyamānā prajām asyai draviṇaṃ ceha dattvā |
14,2.74c tāṃ vahantv agatasyānu panthāṃ virāḍ iyaṃ suprajā aty ajaiṣīt ||74||

14,2.75a pra budhyasva subudhā budhyamānā dīrghāyutvāya śataśāradāya |
14,2.75c gṛhān gacha gṛhapatnī yathāso dīrghaṃ ta āyuḥ savitā kṛṇotu ||75|| {14}


1vrātya āsīd īyamāna eva sa prajāpatiṃ sam airayat ||1||

1sa prajāpatiḥ suvarṇam ātmann apaśyat tat prājanayat ||2||

1tad ekam abhavat tal lalāmam abhavat tan mahad abhavat taj jyeṣṭham abhavat tad brahmābhavat tat tapo 'bhavat tat satyam abhavat tena prājāyata ||3||

1so 'vardhata sa mahān abhavat sa mahādevo 'bhavat ||4||

1sa devānām īśāṃ pary ait sa īśāno 'bhavat ||5||

1sa ekavrātyo 'bhavat sa dhanur ādatta tad evendradhanuḥ ||6||

1nīlam asyodaraṃ lohitaṃ pṛṣṭham ||7||

1nīlenaivāpriyaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ prorṇoti lohitena dviṣantaṃ vidhyatīti brahmavādino vadanti ||8||



15,2.1[2.1]a sa ud atiṣṭhat sa prācīṃ diśam anu vy acalat | [1]
15,2.1[2.2]b taṃ bṛhac ca rathantaraṃ cādityāś ca viśve ca devā anuvyacalan | [2]
15,2.1[2.3]c bṛhate ca vai sa rathantarāya cādityebhyaś ca viśvebhyaś ca devebhya ā vṛścate ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ vrātyam upavadati | [3]
15,2.1[2.4]d bṛhataś ca vai sa rathantarasya cādityānāṃ ca viśveṣāṃ ca devānāṃ priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [4]
15,2.1[2.5]e tasya prācyāṃ diśi śraddhā puṃścalī mitro māgadho vijñānaṃ vāso 'har uṣṇīṣaṃ rātrī keśā haritau pravartau kalmalir maṇiḥ | [5]
15,2.1[2.6-7]f bhūtaṃ ca bhaviṣyac ca pariṣkandau mano vipathaṃ mātariśvā ca pavamānaś ca vipathavāhau vātaḥ sārathī reṣmā pratodaḥ kīrtiś ca yaśaś ca puraḥsarau | [6-7]
15,2.1[2.8]g ainaṃ kīrtir gachaty ā yaśo gachati ya evaṃ veda ||1|| [8]

15,2.2[2.9]a sa ud atiṣṭhat sa dakṣiṇāṃ diśam anu vy acalat | [9]
15,2.2[2.10]b taṃ yajñāyajñiyaṃ ca vāmadevyaṃ ca yajñaś ca yajamānaś ca paśavaś cānuvyacalan | [10]
15,2.2[2.11]c yajñāyajñiyāya ca vai sa vāmadevyāya ca yajñāya ca yajamānāya ca paśubhyaś cā vṛścate ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ vrātyam upavadati | [11]
15,2.2[2.12]d yajñāyajñiyasya ca vai sa vāmadevyasya ca yajñasya ca yajamānasya ca paśūnāṃ ca priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [12]
15,2.2[2.13]e tasya dakṣiṇāyāṃ diśy uṣāḥ puṃścalī mantro māgadho vijñānaṃ vāso 'har uṣṇīṣaṃ rātrī keśā haritau pravartau kalmalir maṇiḥ | [13]
15,2.2[2.14]f amāvāsyā ca paurṇamāsī ca pariṣkandau mano vipathaṃ mātariśvā ca pavamānaś ca vipathavāhau vātaḥ sārathī reṣmā pratodaḥ kīrtiś ca yaśaś ca puraḥsarau |
15,2.2[2.14]g ainaṃ kīrtir gachaty ā yaśo gachati ya evaṃ veda ||2|| [14]

15,2.3[2.15]a sa ud atiṣṭhat sa pratīcīṃ diśam anu vy acalat | [15]
15,2.3[2.16]b taṃ vairūpaṃ ca vairājaṃ cāpaś ca varuṇaś ca rājānuvyacalan | [16]
15,2.3[2.17]c vairūpāya ca vai sa vairājāya cādbhyaś ca varuṇāya ca rājña ā vṛścate ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ vrātyam upavadati | [17]
15,2.3[2.18]d vairūpasya ca vai sa vairājasya cāpāṃ ca varuṇasya ca rājñaḥ priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [18]
15,2.3[2.19]e tasya pratīcyāṃ diśīrā puṃścalī haso māgadho vijñānaṃ vāso 'har uṣṇīṣaṃ rātrī keśā haritau pravartau kalmalir maṇiḥ | [19]
15,2.3[2.20]f ahaś ca rātrī ca pariṣkandau mano vipathaṃ mātariśvā ca pavamānaś ca vipathavāhau vātaḥ sārathī reṣmā pratodaḥ kīrtiś ca yaśaś ca puraḥsarau |
15,2.3[2.20]g ainaṃ kīrtir gachaty ā yaśo gachati ya evaṃ veda ||3|| [20]

15,2.4[2.21]a sa ud atiṣṭhat sa udīcīṃ diśam anu vy acalat | [21]
15,2.4[2.22]b taṃ śyaitaṃ ca naudhasaṃ ca saptarṣayaś ca somaś ca rājānuvyacalan | [22]
15,2.4[2.23]c śyaitāya ca vai sa naudhasāya ca saptarṣibhyaś ca somāya ca rājña ā vṛścate ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ vrātyam upavadati | [23]
15,2.4[2.24]d śyaitasya ca vai sa naudhasasya ca saptarṣīṇāṃ ca somasya ca rājñaḥ priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [24]
15,2.4[2.25]e tasyodīcyāṃ diśi vidyut puṃścalī stanayitnur māgadho vijñānaṃ vāso 'har uṣṇīṣaṃ rātrī keśā haritau pravartau kalmalir maṇiḥ | [25]
15,2.4[2.26-27]f śrutaṃ ca viśrutaṃ ca pariṣkandau mano vipathaṃ mātariśvā ca pavamānaś ca vipathavāhau vātaḥ sārathī reṣmā pratodaḥ kīrtiś ca yaśaś ca puraḥsarau | [26-27]
15,2.4[2.28]g ainaṃ kīrtir gachaty ā yaśo gachati ya evaṃ veda ||4|| [28]



1sa saṃvatsaram ūrdhvo 'tiṣṭhat taṃ devā abruvan vrātya kiṃ nu tiṣṭhasīti ||1||

1so 'bravīd āsandīṃ me saṃ bharantv iti ||2||

1tasmai vrātyāyāsandīṃ sam abharan ||3||

1tasyā grīṣmaś ca vasantaś ca dvau pādāv āstāṃ śarac ca varṣāś ca dvau ||4||

1bṛhac ca rathantaraṃ cānūcye āstāṃ yajñāyajñiyaṃ ca vāmadevyaṃ ca tiraścye ||5||

1ṛcaḥ prāñcas tantavo yajūṃṣi tiryañcaḥ ||6||

1veda āstaraṇaṃ brahmopabarhaṇam ||7||

1sāmāsāda udgītho 'paśrayaḥ ||8||

1tām āsandīṃ vrātya ārohat ||9||

15,3.10a tasya devajanāḥ pariṣkandā āsant saṃkalpāḥ prahāyyā viśvāni bhūtāny upasadaḥ ||10||

15,3.11a viśvāny evāsya bhūtāny upasado bhavanti ya evaṃ veda ||11||



15,4.1[4.1]a tasmai prācyā diśaḥ | [1]
15,4.1[4.2]b vāsantau māsau goptārāv akurvan bṛhac ca rathantaraṃ cānuṣṭhātārau | [2]
15,4.1[4.3]c vāsantāv enaṃ māsau prācyā diśo gopāyato bṛhac ca rathantaraṃ cānu tiṣṭhato ya evaṃ veda ||1|| [3]

15,4.2[4.4]a tasmai dakṣiṇāyā diśaḥ | [4]
15,4.2[4.5]b graiṣmau māsau goptārāv akurvan yajñāyajñiyaṃ ca vāmadevyaṃ cānuṣṭhātārau | [5]
15,4.2[4.6]c graiṣmāv enaṃ māsau dakṣiṇāyā diśo gopāyato yajñāyajñiyaṃ ca vāmadevyaṃ cānu tiṣṭhato ya evaṃ veda ||2|| [6]

15,4.3[4.7]a tasmai pratīcyā diśaḥ | [7]
15,4.3[4.8]b vārṣikau māsau goptārāv akurvan vairūpaṃ ca vairājaṃ cānuṣṭhātārau | [8]
15,4.3[4.9]c vārṣikāv enaṃ māsau pratīcyā diśo gopāyato vairūpaṃ ca vairājaṃ cānu tiṣṭhato ya evaṃ veda ||3|| [9]

15,4.4[4.10]a tasmā udīcyā diśaḥ | [10]
15,4.4[4.11]b śāradau māsau goptārāv akurvaṃ chyaitaṃ ca naudhasaṃ cānuṣṭhātārau | [11]
15,4.4[4.12]c śāradāv enaṃ māsāv udīcyā diśo gopāyataḥ śyaitaṃ ca naudhasaṃ cānu tiṣṭhato ya evaṃ veda ||4|| [12]

15,4.5[4.13]a tasmai dhruvāyā diśaḥ | [13]
15,4.5[4.14]b haimanau māsau goptārāv akurvan bhūmiṃ cāgniṃ cānuṣṭhātārau | [14]
15,4.5[4.15]c haimanāv enaṃ māsau dhruvāyā diśo gopāyato bhūmiś cāgniś cānu tiṣṭhato ya evaṃ veda ||5|| [15]

15,4.6[4.16]a tasmā ūrdhvāyā diśaḥ | [16]
15,4.6[4.17]b śaiśirau māsau goptārāv akurvan divaṃ cādityaṃ cānuṣṭhātārau | [17]
15,4.6[4.18]c śaiśirāv enaṃ māsāv ūrdhvāyā diśo gopāyato dyauś cādityaś cānu tiṣṭhato ya evaṃ veda ||6|| [18]



15,5.1[5.1]a tasmai prācyā diśo antardeśād bhavam iṣvāsam anuṣṭhātāram akurvan | [1]
15,5.1[5.2-3]b bhava enam iṣvāsaḥ prācyā diśo antardeśād anuṣṭhātānu tiṣṭhati nainaṃ śarvo na bhavo neśāno nāsya paśūn na samānān hinasti ya evaṃ veda ||1|| [2-3]

15,5.2[5.4]a tasmai dakṣiṇāyā diśo antardeśāc charvam iṣvāsam anuṣṭhātāram akurvan | [4]
15,5.2[5.5]b śarva enam iśvāso dakṣiṇāyā diśo antardeśād anuṣṭhātānu tiṣṭhati nainaṃ śarvo na bhavo neśāno nāsya paśūn na samānān hinasti ya evaṃ veda ||2|| [5]

15,5.3[5.6]a tasmai pratīcyā diśo antardeśāt paśupatim iṣvāsam anuṣṭhātāram akurvan | [6]
15,5.3[5.7]b paśupatir enam iṣvāsaḥ pratīcyā diśo antardeśād anuṣṭhātānu tiṣṭhati nainaṃ śarvo na bhavo neśāno nāsya paśūn na samānān hinasti ya evaṃ veda ||3|| [7]

15,5.4[5.8]a tasmā udīcyā diśo antardeśād ugraṃ devam iṣvāsam anuṣṭhātāram akurvan | [8]
15,5.4[5.9]b ugra enaṃ deva iṣvāsa udīcyā diśo antardeśād anuṣṭhātānu tiṣṭhati nainaṃ śarvo na bhavo neśāno nāsya paśūn na samānān hinasti ya evaṃ veda ||4|| [9]

15,5.5[5.10]a tasmai dhruvāyā diśo antardeśād rudram iṣvāsam anuṣṭhātāram akurvan | [10]
15,5.5[5.11]b rudra enam iṣvāso dhruvāyā diśo antardeśād anuṣṭhātānu tiṣṭhati nainaṃ śarvo na bhavo neśāno nāsya paśūn na samānān hinasti ya evaṃ veda ||5|| [11]

15,5.6[5.12]a tasmā ūrdhvāyā diśo antardeśān mahādevam iṣvāsam anuṣṭhātāram akurvan | [12]
15,5.6[5.13]b mahādeva enam iṣvāsa ūrdhvāyā diśo antardeśād anuṣṭhātānu tiṣṭhati nainaṃ śarvo na bhavo neśāno nāsya paśūn na samānān hinasti ya evaṃ veda ||6|| [13]

15,5.7[5.14]a tasmai sarvebhyo antardeśebhya īśānam iṣvāsam anuṣṭhātāram akurvan | [14]
15,5.7[5.15-16]b īśāna enam iṣvāsaḥ sarvebhyo antardeśebhyo 'nuṣṭhātānu tiṣṭhati nainaṃ śarvo na bhavo neśāno nāsya paśūn na samānān hinasti ya evaṃ veda ||7|| [15-16]



15,6.1[6.1]a sa dhruvāṃ diśam anu vy acalat | [1]
15,6.1[6.2]b taṃ bhūmiś cāgniś cauṣadhayaś ca vanaspatayaś ca vānaspatyāś ca vīrudhaś cānuvyacalan | [2]
15,6.1[6.3]c bhūmeś ca vai so 'gneś cauṣadhīnāṃ ca vanaspatīnāṃ ca vānaspatyānāṃ ca vīrudhāṃ ca priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||1|| [3]

15,6.2[6.4]a sa ūrdhvāṃ diśam anu vy acalat | [4]
15,6.2[6.5]b tam ṛtaṃ ca satyaṃ ca sūryaś ca candraś ca nakṣatrāṇi cānuvyacalan | [5]
15,6.2[6.6]c ṛtasya ca vai sa satyasya ca sūryasya ca candrasya ca nakṣatrāṇāṃ ca priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||2|| [6]

15,6.3[6.7]a sa uttamāṃ diśam anu vy acalat | [7]
15,6.3[6.8]b tam ṛcaś ca sāmāni ca yajūṃṣi ca brahma cānuvyacalan | [8]
15,6.3[6.9]c ṛcāṃ ca vai sa sāmnāṃ ca yajuṣāṃ ca brahmaṇaś ca priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||3|| [9]

15,6.4[6.10]a sa bṛhatīṃ diśam anu vy acalat | [10]
15,6.4[6.11]b tam itihāsaś ca purāṇaṃ ca gāthāś ca nārāśaṃsīś cānuvyacalan | [11]
15,6.4[6.12]c itihāsasya ca vai sa purāṇasya ca gāthānāṃ ca nārāśaṃsīnāṃ ca priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||4|| [12]

15,6.5[6.13]a sa paramāṃ diśam anu vy acalat | [13]
15,6.5[6.14]b tam āhavanīyaś ca gārhapatyaś ca dakṣiṇāgniś ca yajñaś ca yajamānaś ca paśavaś cānuvyacalan | [14]
15,6.5[6.15]c āhavanīyasya ca vai sa gārhapatyasya ca dakṣiṇāgneś ca yajñasya ca yajamānasya ca paśūnāṃ ca priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||5|| [15]

15,6.6[6.16]a so 'nādiṣṭāṃ diśam anu vy acalat | [16]
15,6.6[6.17]b tam ṛtavaś cārtavāś ca lokāś ca laukyāś ca māsāś cārdhamāsāś cāhorātre cānuvyacalan | [17]
15,6.6[6.18]c ṛtūnāṃ ca vai sa ārtavānāṃ ca lokānāṃ ca laukyānāṃ ca māsānāṃ cārdhamāsānāṃ cāhorātrayoś ca priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||6|| [18]

15,6.7[6.19]a so 'nāvṛttāṃ diśam anu vy acalat tato nāvartsyann amanyata | [19]
15,6.7[6.20]b taṃ ditiś cāditiś ceḍā cendrāṇī cānuvyacalan | [20]
15,6.7[6.21]c diteś ca vai so 'diteś ceḍāyāś cendrāṇyāś ca priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||7|| [21]

15,6.8[6.22]a sa diśo 'nu vy acalat taṃ virāḍ anu vy acalat sarve ca devāḥ sarvāś ca devatāḥ | [22]
15,6.8[6.23]b virājaś ca vai sa sarveṣāṃ ca devānāṃ sarvāsāṃ ca devatānāṃ priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||8|| [23]

15,6.9[6.24]a sa sarvān antardeśān anu vy acalat | [24]
15,6.9[6.25]b taṃ prajāpatiś ca parameṣṭhī ca pitā ca pitāmahaś cānuvyacalan | [25]
15,6.9[6.26]c prajāpateś ca vai sa parameṣṭhinaś ca pituś ca pitāmahasya ca priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||9|| [26]



1sa mahimā sadrur bhūtvāntaṃ pṛthivyā agachat samudro 'bhavat ||1||

1taṃ prajāpatiś ca parameṣṭhī ca pitā ca pitāmahaś cāpaś ca śraddhā ca varṣaṃ bhūtvānuvyavartayanta ||2||

1ainam āpo gachanty ainaṃ śraddhā gachaty ainaṃ varṣaṃ gachati ya evaṃ veda ||3||

1taṃ śraddhā ca yajñaś ca lokaś cānnaṃ cānnādyaṃ ca bhūtvābhiparyāvartanta ||4||

1ainaṃ śraddhā gachaty ainaṃ yajño gachaty ainaṃ loko gachaty ainam annaṃ gachaty ainam annādyaṃ gachati ya evaṃ veda ||5||



1so 'rajyata tato rājanyo 'jāyata ||1||

1sa viśaḥ sabandhūn annam annādyam abhyudatiṣṭhat ||2||

1viśāṃ ca vai sa sabandhūnāṃ cānnasya cānnādyasya ca priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||3||



1sa viśo 'nu vy acalat ||1||

1taṃ sabhā ca samitiś ca senā ca surā cānuvyacalan ||2||

1sabhāyāś ca vai sa samiteś ca senāyāś ca surāyāś ca priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||3||



1tad yasyaivaṃ vidvān vrātyo rājño 'tithir gṛhān āgachet ||1||

1śreyāṃsam enam ātmano mānayet tathā kṣatrāya nā vṛścate tathā rāṣṭrāya nā vṛścate ||2||

1ato vai brahma ca kṣatraṃ cod atiṣṭhatāṃ te abrūtāṃ kaṃ pra viśāveti ||3||

1bṛhaspatim eva brahma praviśatv indraṃ kṣatraṃ tathā vā iti ||4||

1ato vai bṛhaspatim eva brahma prāviśad indraṃ kṣatram ||5||

1iyaṃ vā u pṛthivī bṛhaspatir dyaur evendraḥ ||6||

1ayaṃ vā u agnir brahmāsāv ādityaḥ kṣatram ||7||

1ainaṃ brahma gachati brahmavarcasī bhavati ||8||

1yaḥ pṛthivīṃ bṛhaspatim agniṃ brahma veda ||9||

15,10.10a ainam indriyaṃ gachatīndriyavān bhavati ||10||

15,10.11a ya ādityaṃ kṣatraṃ divam indraṃ veda ||11||



1tad yasyaivaṃ vidvān vrātyo 'tithir gṛhān āgachet ||1||

1svayam enam abhyudetya brūyād vrātya kvāvātsīr vrātyodakaṃ vrātya tarpayantu vrātya yathā te priyaṃ tathāstu vrātya yathā te vaśas tathāstu vrātya yathā te nikāmas tathāstv iti ||2||

1yad enam āha vrātya kvāvātsīr iti patha eva tena devayānān ava rundhe ||3||

1yad enam āha vrātyodakam ity apa eva tenāva rundhe ||4||

1yad enam āha vrātya tarpayantv iti prāṇam eva tena varṣīyāṃsaṃ kurute ||5||

1yad enam āha vrātya yathā te priyaṃ tathāstv iti priyam eva tenāva rundhe ||6||

1ainaṃ priyaṃ gachati priyaḥ priyasya bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||7||

1yad enam āha vrātya yathā te vaśas tathāstv iti vaśam eva tenāva rundhe ||8||

1ainaṃ vaśo gachati vaśī vaśināṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||9||

15,11.10a yad enam āha vrātya yathā te nikāmas tathāstv iti nikāmam eva tenāva rundhe ||10||

15,11.11a ainaṃ nikāmo gachati nikāme nikāmasya bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||11||



1tad yasyaivaṃ vidvān vrātya uddhṛteṣv agniṣv adhiśrite 'gnihotre 'tithir gṛhān āgachet ||1||

1svayam enam abhyudetya brūyād vrātyāti sṛja hoṣyāmīti ||2||

1sa cātisṛjej juhuyān na cātisṛjen na juhuyāt ||3||

1sa ya evaṃ viduṣā vrātyenātisṛṣṭo juhoti ||4||

1pra pitṛyāṇaṃ panthāṃ jānāti pra devayānam ||5||

1na deveṣv ā vṛścate hutam asya bhavati ||6||

1pary asyāsmiṃl loka āyatanaṃ śiṣyate ya evaṃ viduṣā vrātyenātisṛṣṭo juhoti ||7||

1atha ya evaṃ viduṣā vrātyenānatisṛṣṭo juhoti ||8||

1na pitṛyāṇaṃ panthāṃ jānāti na devayānam ||9||

15,12.10a ā deveṣu vṛścate ahutam asya bhavati ||10||

15,12.11a nāsyāsmiṃl loka āyatanaṃ śiṣyate ya evaṃ viduṣā vrātyenānatisṛṣṭo juhoti ||11||


15,13.1[13.1]a tad yasyaivaṃ vidvān vrātya ekāṃ rātrim atithir gṛhe vasati | [1]
15,13.1[13.2]b ye pṛthivyāṃ puṇyā lokās tān eva tenāva rundhe ||1|| [2]

15,13.2[13.3]a tad yasyaivaṃ vidvān vrātyo dvitīyāṃ rātrim atithir gṛhe vasati | [3]
15,13.2[13.4]b ye 'ntarikṣe puṇyā lokās tān eva tenāva rundhe ||2|| [4]
15,13.3[13.5]a tad yasyaivaṃ vidvān vrātyas tṛtīyāṃ rātrim atithir gṛhe vasati | [5]
15,13.3[13.6]b ye divi puṇyā lokās tān eva tenāva rundhe ||3|| [6]

15,13.4[13.7]a tad yasyaivaṃ vidvān vrātyaś caturthīṃ rātrim atithir gṛhe vasati | [7]
15,13.4[13.8]b ye puṇyānāṃ puṇyā lokās tān eva tenāva rundhe ||4|| [8]

15,13.5[13.9]a tad yasyaivaṃ vidvān vrātyo 'parimitā rātrīr atithir gṛhe vasati | [9]
15,13.5[13.10]b ya evāparimitāḥ puṇyā lokās tān eva tenāva rundhe ||5|| [10]

15,13.6[13.11]a atha yasyāvrātyo vrātyabruvo nāmabibhraty atithir gṛhān āgachet ||6|| [11]

15,13.7[13.12]a karṣed enaṃ na cainaṃ karṣet ||7|| [12]

15,13.8[13.13]a asyai devatāyā udakaṃ yācāmīmāṃ devatāṃ vāsaya imām imāṃ devatāṃ pari veveṣmīty enaṃ pari veviṣyāt ||8|| [13]

15,13.9[13.14]a tasyām evāsya tad devatāyāṃ hutaṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda ||9|| [14]



15,14.1[14.1]a sa yat prācīṃ diśam anu vyacalan mārutaṃ śardho bhūtvānuvyacalan mano 'nnādaṃ kṛtvā | [1]
15,14.1[14.2]b manasānnādenānnam atti ya evaṃ veda ||1|| [2]

15,14.2[14.3]a sa yad dakṣiṇāṃ diśam anu vyacalad indro bhūtvānuvyacalad balam annādaṃ kṛtvā | [3]
15,14.2[14.4]b balenānnādenānnam atti ya evaṃ veda ||2|| [4]

15,14.3[14.5]a sa yat pratīcīṃ diśam anu vyacalad varuṇo rājā bhūtvānuvyacalad apo 'nnādīḥ kṛtvā | [5]
15,14.3[14.6]b adbhir annādībhir annam atti ya evaṃ veda ||3|| [6]

15,14.4[14.7]a sa yad udīcīṃ diśam anu vyacalat somo rājā bhūtvānuvyacalat saptarṣibhir huta āhutim annādīṃ kṛtvā | [7]
15,14.4[14.8]b āhutyānnādyānnam atti ya evaṃ veda ||4|| [8]

15,14.5[14.9]a sa yad dhruvāṃ diśam anu vyacalad viṣṇur bhūtvānuvyacalad virājam annādīṃ kṛtvā | [9]
15,14.5[14.10]b virājānnādyānnam atti ya evaṃ veda ||5|| [10]

15,14.6[14.11]a sa yat paśūn anu vyacalad rudro bhūtvānuvyacalad oṣadhīr annādīḥ kṛtvā | [11]
15,14.6[14.12]b oṣadhībhir annādībhir annam atti ya evaṃ veda ||6|| [12]

15,14.7[14.13]a sa yat pitṝn anu vyacalad yamo rājā bhūtvānuvyacalat svadhākāram annādaṃ kṛtvā | [13]
15,14.7[14.14]b svadhākāreṇānnādenānnam atti ya evaṃ veda ||7|| [14]

15,14.8[14.15]a sa yan manuṣyān anu vyacalad agnir bhūtvānuvyacalat svāhākāram annādaṃ kṛtvā | [15]
15,14.8[14.16]b svāhākāreṇānnādenānnam atti ya evaṃ veda ||8|| [16]

15,14.9[14.17]a sa yad ūrdhvāṃ diśam anu vyacalad bṛhaspatir bhūtvānuvyacalad vaṣaṭkāram annādaṃ kṛtvā | [17]
15,14.9[14.18]b vaṣaṭkāreṇānnādenānnam atti ya evaṃ veda ||9|| [18]

15,14.10[14.19]a sa yad devān anu vyacalad īśāno bhūtvānuvyacalan manyum annādaṃ kṛtvā | [19]
15,14.10[14.20]b manyunānnādenānnam atti ya evaṃ veda ||10|| [20]

15,14.11[14.21]a sa yat prajā anu vyacalat prajāpatir bhūtvānuvyacalat prāṇam annādaṃ kṛtvā | [21]
15,14.11[14.22]b prāṇenānnādenānnam atti ya evaṃ veda ||11|| [22]

15,14.12[14.23]a sa yat sarvān antardeśān anu vyacalat parameṣṭhī bhūtvānuvyacalad brahmānnādaṃ kṛtvā | [23]
15,14.12[14.24]b brahmaṇānnādenānnam atti ya evaṃ veda ||12|| [24]



1tasya vrātyasya ||1||

1sapta prāṇāḥ saptāpānāḥ sapta vyānāḥ ||2||

1yo 'sya prathamaḥ prāṇa ūrdhvo nāmāyaṃ so agniḥ ||3||

1yo 'sya dvitīyaḥ prāṇaḥ prauḍho nāmāsau sa ādityaḥ ||4||

1yo 'sya tṛtīyaḥ prāṇo 'bhyūḍho nāmāsau sa candramāḥ ||5||

1yo 'sya caturthaḥ prāṇo vibhūr nāmāyaṃ sa pavamānaḥ ||6||

1yo 'sya pañcamaḥ prāṇo yonir nāma tā imā āpaḥ ||7||

1yo 'sya ṣaṣṭhaḥ prāṇaḥ priyo nāma ta ime paśavaḥ ||8||

1yo 'sya saptamaḥ prāṇo 'parimito nāma tā imāḥ prajāḥ ||9||



1yo 'sya prathamo 'pānaḥ sā paurṇamāsī ||1||

1yo 'sya dvitīyo 'pānaḥ sāṣṭakā ||2||

1yo 'sya tṛtīyo 'pānaḥ sāmāvāsyā ||3||

1yo 'sya caturtho 'pānaḥ sā śraddhā ||4||

1yo 'sya pañcamo 'pānaḥ sā dīkṣā ||5||

1yo 'sya ṣaṣṭho 'pānaḥ sa yajñaḥ ||6||

1yo 'sya saptamo 'pānas tā imā dakṣiṇāḥ ||7||



1yo 'sya prathamo vyānaḥ seyaṃ bhūmiḥ ||1||

1yo 'sya dvitīyo vyānas tad antarikṣam ||2||

1yo 'sya tṛtīyo vyānaḥ sā dyauḥ ||3||

1yo 'sya caturtho vyānas tāni nakṣatrāṇi ||4||

1yo 'sya pañcamo vyānas ta ṛtavaḥ ||5||

1yo 'sya ṣaṣṭho vyānas ta ārtavāḥ ||6||

1yo 'sya saptamo vyānaḥ sa saṃvatsaraḥ ||7||

1samānam arthaṃ pari yanti devāḥ saṃvatsaraṃ vā etad ṛtavo 'nupariyanti vrātyaṃ ca ||8||

1yad ādityam abhisaṃviśanty amāvāsyāṃ caiva tat paurṇamāsīṃ ca ||9||

15,17.10a ekaṃ tad eṣām amṛtatvam ity āhutir eva ||10||



1tasya vrātyasya ||1||

1yad asya dakṣiṇam akṣy asau sa ādityo yad asya savyam akṣy asau sa candramāḥ ||2||

1yo 'sya dakṣiṇaḥ karṇo 'yaṃ so agnir yo 'sya savyaḥ karṇo 'yaṃ sa pavamānaḥ ||3||

1ahorātre nāsike ditiś cāditiś ca śīrṣakapāle saṃvatsaraḥ śiraḥ ||4||

1ahnā pratyaṅ vrātyo rātryā prāṅ namo vrātyāya ||5||


1atisṛṣṭo apāṃ vṛṣabho 'tisṛṣṭā agnayo divyāḥ ||1||

1rujan parirujan mṛṇan pramṛṇan ||2||

1mroko manohā khano nirdāha ātmadūṣis tanūdūṣiḥ ||3||

1idaṃ tam ati sṛjāmi taṃ mābhyavanikṣi ||4||

1tena tam abhyatisṛjāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ ||5||

1apām agram asi samudraṃ vo 'bhyavasṛjāmi ||6||

1yo 'psv agnir ati taṃ sṛjāmi mrokaṃ khaniṃ tanūdūṣim ||7||

1yo va āpo 'gnir āviveśa sa eṣa yad vo ghoraṃ tad etat ||8||

1indrasya va indriyeṇābhi ṣiñcet ||9||

16,1.10a ariprā āpo apa ripram asmat ||10||
16,1.11a prāsmad eno vahantu pra duṣvapnyaṃ vahantu ||11||

16,1.12a śivena mā cakṣuṣā paśyatāpaḥ śivayā tanvopa spṛśata tvacaṃ me ||12||

16,1.13a śivān agnīn apsuṣado havāmahe mayi kṣatraṃ varca ā dhatta devīḥ ||13||



1nir durarmaṇya ūrjā madhumatī vāk ||1||

1madhumatī stha madhumatīṃ vācam udeyam ||2||

1upahūto me gopāḥ upahūto gopīthaḥ ||3||

1suśrutau karṇau bhadraśrutau karṇau bhadraṃ ślokaṃ śrūyāsam ||4||

1suśrutiś ca mopaśrutiś ca mā hāsiṣṭāṃ sauparṇaṃ cakṣur ajasraṃ jyotiḥ ||5||

1ṛṣīṇāṃ prastaro 'si namo 'stu daivāya prastarāya ||6||



1mūrdhāhaṃ rayīṇāṃ mūrdhā samānānāṃ bhūyāsam ||1||

1rujaś ca mā venaś ca mā hāsiṣṭāṃ mūrdhā ca mā vidharmā ca mā hāsiṣṭām ||2||

1urvaś ca mā camasaś ca mā hāsiṣṭāṃ dhartā ca mā dharuṇaś ca mā hāsiṣṭām ||3||

1vimokaś ca mārdrapaviś ca mā hāsiṣṭām ārdradānuś ca mā mātariśvā ca mā hāsiṣṭām ||4||

1bṛhaspatir ma ātmā nṛmaṇā nāma hṛdyaḥ ||5||

1asaṃtāpaṃ me hṛdayam urvī gavyūtiḥ samudro asmi vidharmaṇā ||6||



1nābhir ahaṃ rayīṇāṃ nābhiḥ samānānāṃ bhūyāsam ||1||

1svāsad asi sūṣā amṛto martyeśv ā ||2||

1mā māṃ prāṇo hāsīn mo apāno 'vahāya parā gāt ||3||

1sūryo māhnaḥ pātv agniḥ pṛthivyā vāyur antarikṣād yamo manuṣyebhyaḥ sarasvatī pārthivebhyaḥ ||4||

1prāṇāpanau mā mā hāsiṣṭam mā jane pra meṣi ||5||

1svasty adyoṣaso doṣasaś ca sarva āpaḥ sarvagaṇo aśīya ||6||

1śakvarī stha paśavo mopa stheṣur mitrāvaruṇau me prāṇāpānāv agnir me dakṣaṃ dadhātu ||7||



1vidma te svapna janitraṃ grāhyāḥ putro 'si yamasya karaṇaḥ |
1antako 'si mṛtyur asi |
1taṃ tvā svapna tathā saṃ vidma sa naḥ svapna duṣvapnyāt pāhi ||1||

1vidma te svapna janitraṃ nirṛtyāḥ putro 'si yamasya karaṇaḥ | [...] || 2 ||

1vidma te svapna janitraṃ abhūtyāḥ putro 'si yamasya [...] || 3 ||

1vidma te svapna janitraṃ nirbhūtyāḥ putro 'si [...] || 4 ||
