1vidma te svapna janitraṃ parābhūtyāḥ putro 'si [...] || 5 ||

1vidma te svapna janitraṃ devajāmīnāṃ putro 'si yamasya karaṇaḥ |
1antako 'si mṛtyur asi |
1taṃ tvā svapna tathā saṃ vidma sa naḥ svapna duṣvapnyāt pāhi ||6||



1ajaiṣmādyāsanām adyāmūm anāgaso vayam ||1||

1uṣo yasmād duṣvapnyād abhaiṣmāpa tad uchatu ||2||

1dviṣate tat parā vaha śapate tat parā vaha ||3||

1yaṃ dviṣmo yaś ca no dveṣṭi tasmā enad gamayāmaḥ ||4||

1uṣā devī vācā saṃvidānā vāg devy uṣasā saṃvidānā ||5||

1uṣas patir vācas patinā saṃvidāno vācas patinā saṃvidānaḥ ||6||

1te 'muṣmai parā vahantv arāyān durṇāmnaḥ sadānvāḥ ||7||

1kumbhīkāḥ dūṣīkāḥ pīyakān ||8||

1jāgradduṣvapnyaṃ svapneduṣvapnyam ||9||

16,6.10a anāgamiṣyato varān avitteḥ saṃkalpān amucyā druhaḥ pāśān ||10||

16,6.11a tad amuṣmā agne devāḥ parā vahantu vaghrir yathāsad vithuro na sādhuḥ ||11||



1tenainaṃ vidhyāmy abhūtyainaṃ vidhyāmi nirbhūtyainaṃ vidhyāmi parābhūtyainaṃ vidhyāmi grāhyainaṃ vidhyāmi tamasainaṃ vidhyāmi ||1||

1devānām enaṃ ghoraiḥ krūraiḥ praiṣair abhipreṣyāmi ||2||

1vaiśvānarasyainaṃ daṃṣṭrayor api dadhāmi ||3||

1evānevāva sā garat ||4||

1yo 'smān dveṣṭi tam ātmā dveṣṭu yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ sa ātmānaṃ dveṣṭu ||5||

1nir dviṣantaṃ divo niḥ pṛthivyā nir antarikṣād bhajāma ||6||

1suyāmaṃś cākṣuṣa ||7||

1idam aham āmuṣyāyaṇe 'muṣyāḥ putre duṣvapnyaṃ mṛje ||8||

1yad adoado abhyagachaṃ yad doṣā yat pūrvāṃ rātrim ||9||

16,7.10a yaj jāgrad yat supto yad divā yan naktam ||10||

16,7.11a yad aharahar abhigachāmi tasmād enam ava daye ||11||

16,7.12a taṃ jahi tena mandasva tasya pṛṣṭīr api śṛṇīhi ||12||

16,7.13a sa mā jīvīt taṃ prāṇo jahātu ||13||

1jitam asmākam udbhinnam asmākam ṛtam asmākaṃ tejas asmākaṃ brahmāsmākaṃ svar asmākaṃ yajño 'smākaṃ paśavo 'smākaṃ prajā asmākaṃ vīrā asmākam ||1||

1jitam asmākam udbhinnam asmākam ṛtam asmākaṃ tejo 'smākaṃ brahmāsmākaṃ svar asmākaṃ yajño 'smākaṃ paśavo 'smākaṃ prajā asmākaṃ vīrā asmākam |
1tasmād amuṃ nir bhajāmo 'mum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putram asau yaḥ |
1sa nirṛtyāḥ pāśān mā moci ||2||

1jitam asmākam udbhinnam asmākam ṛtam asmākaṃ tejo 'smākaṃ brahmāsmākaṃ svar asmākaṃ yajño 'smākaṃ paśavo 'smākaṃ prajā asmākaṃ vīrā asmākam |

1so 'bhūtyāḥ pāśān mā moci ||3||

16,8.19c tasmād amuṃ nir bhajāmo 'mum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putram asau yaḥ |
16,8.19e sa māsānāṃ pāśān mā moci ||19||

16,8.20a jitam asmākam udbhinnam asmākam ṛtam asmākaṃ tejo 'smākaṃ brahmāsmākaṃ svar asmākaṃ yajño 'smākaṃ paśavo 'smākaṃ prajā asmākaṃ vīrā asmākam |
16,8.20c tasmād amuṃ nir bhajāmo 'mum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putram asau yaḥ |
16,8.20e so 'rdhamāsānāṃ pāśān mā moci ||20||

16,8.21a jitam asmākam udbhinnam asmākam ṛtam asmākaṃ tejo 'smākaṃ brahmāsmākaṃ svar asmākaṃ yajño 'smākaṃ paśavo 'smākaṃ prajā asmākaṃ vīrā asmākam |
16,8.21c tasmād amuṃ nir bhajāmo 'mum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putram asau yaḥ |
16,8.21e so 'horātrayoḥ pāśān mā moci ||21||

16,8.22a jitam asmākam udbhinnam asmākam ṛtam asmākaṃ tejo 'smākaṃ brahmāsmākaṃ svar asmākaṃ yajño 'smākaṃ paśavo 'smākaṃ prajā asmākaṃ vīrā asmākam |
16,8.22c tasmād amuṃ nir bhajāmo 'mum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putram asau yaḥ |
16,8.22e so 'hnoḥ saṃyatoḥ pāśān mā moci ||22||

16,8.23a jitam asmākam udbhinnam asmākam ṛtam asmākaṃ tejo 'smākaṃ brahmāsmākaṃ svar asmākaṃ yajño 'smākaṃ paśavo 'smākaṃ prajā asmākaṃ vīrā asmākam |
16,8.23c tasmād amuṃ nir bhajāmo 'mum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putram asau yaḥ |
16,8.23e sa dyāvāpṛthivyoḥ pāśān mā moci ||23||

16,8.24a jitam asmākam udbhinnam asmākam ṛtam asmākaṃ tejo 'smākaṃ brahmāsmākaṃ svar asmākaṃ yajño 'smākaṃ paśavo 'smākaṃ prajā asmākaṃ vīrā asmākam |
16,8.24c tasmād amuṃ nir bhajāmo 'mum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putram asau yaḥ |
16,8.24e sa indrāgnyoḥ pāśān mā moci ||24||

16,8.25a jitam asmākam udbhinnam asmākam ṛtam asmākaṃ tejo 'smākaṃ brahmāsmākaṃ svar asmākaṃ yajño 'smākaṃ paśavo 'smākaṃ prajā asmākaṃ vīrā asmākam |
16,8.25c tasmād amuṃ nir bhajāmo 'mum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putram asau yaḥ |
16,8.25e sa mitrāvaruṇayoḥ pāśān mā moci ||25||

16,8.26a jitam asmākam udbhinnam asmākam ṛtam asmākaṃ tejo 'smākaṃ brahmāsmākaṃ svar asmākaṃ yajño 'smākaṃ paśavo 'smākaṃ prajā asmākaṃ vīrā asmākam |
16,8.26c tasmād amuṃ nir bhajāmo 'mum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putram asau yaḥ |
16,8.26e sa rājño varuṇasya pāśān mā moci ||26||

16,8.27a jitam asmākam udbhinnam asmākam ṛtam asmākaṃ tejo 'smākaṃ brahmāsmākaṃ svar asmākaṃ yajño 'smākaṃ paśavo 'smākaṃ prajā asmākaṃ vīrā asmākam ||27||



1jitam asmākam udbhinnam asmākam abhy aṣṭhāṃ viśvāḥ pṛtanā arātīḥ ||1||

1tad agnir āha tad u soma āha pūṣā mā dhāt sukṛtasya loke ||2||

1aganma svaḥ svar aganma saṃ sūryasya jyotiṣāganma ||3||

1vasyobhūyāya vasumān yajño vasu vaṃsiṣīya vasumān bhūyāsaṃ vasu mayi dhehi ||4||



1viṣāsahiṃ sahamānaṃ sāsahānaṃ sahīyāṃsam |
1sahamānaṃ sahojitaṃ svarjitaṃ gojitaṃ saṃdhanājitam |
1īḍyaṃ nāma hva indram āyuṣmān bhūyāsam ||1||

1viṣāsahiṃ sahamānaṃ sāsahānaṃ sahīyāṃsam |
1sahamānaṃ sahojitaṃ svarjitaṃ gojitaṃ saṃdhanājitam |
1īḍyaṃ nāma hva indram priyo devānāṃ bhūyāsam ||2||

1viṣāsahiṃ sahamānaṃ sāsahānaṃ sahīyāṃsam |
1sahamānaṃ sahojitaṃ svarjitaṃ gojitaṃ saṃdhanājitam |
1īḍyaṃ nāma hva indram priyaḥ prajānāṃ bhūyāsam ||3||

1viṣāsahiṃ sahamānaṃ sāsahānaṃ sahīyāṃsam |
1sahamānaṃ sahojitaṃ svarjitaṃ gojitaṃ saṃdhanājitam |
1īḍyaṃ nāma hva indram priyaḥ paśūnāṃ bhūyāsam ||4||

1viṣāsahiṃ sahamānaṃ sāsahānaṃ sahīyāṃsam |
1sahamānaṃ sahojitaṃ svarjitaṃ gojitaṃ saṃdhanājitam |
1īḍyaṃ nāma hva indram priyaḥ samānānāṃ bhūyāsam ||5||

1ud ihy ud ihi sūrya varcasā mābhyudihi |
1dviṣaṃś ca mahyaṃ radhyatu mā cāhaṃ dviṣate radhaṃ taved viṣṇo bahūdhā vīryāni |
1tvaṃ naḥ pṛṇīhi paśubhir viśvarūpaiḥ sudhāyāṃ mā dhehi parame vyoman ||6||

1ud ihy ud ihi sūrya varcasā mābhyudihi |
1āṃś ca paśyāmi yāṃś ca na teṣu mā sumatiṃ kṛdhi taved viṣṇo bahūdhā vīryāni |
1tvaṃ naḥ pṛṇīhi paśubhir viśvarūpaiḥ sudhāyāṃ mā dhehi parame vyoman ||7||

1mā tvā dabhant salile apsv antar ye pāśina upatiṣṭhanty atra |
1hitvāśastiṃ divam ārukṣa etāṃ sa no mṛḍa sumatau te syāma taved viṣṇo bahūdhā vīryāni |
1tvaṃ naḥ pṛṇīhi paśubhir viśvarūpaiḥ sudhāyāṃ mā dhehi parame vyoman ||8||

1tvaṃ na indra mahate saubhagāyādabdhebhiḥ pari pāhy aktubhis taved viṣṇo bahūdhā vīryāni |
1tvaṃ naḥ pṛṇīhi paśubhir viśvarūpaiḥ sudhāyāṃ mā dhehi parame vyoman ||9||

17,1.10a tvaṃ na indrotibhiḥ śivābhiḥ śaṃtamo bhava |
17,1.10c ārohaṃs tridivaṃ divo gṛṇānaḥ somapītaye priyadhāmā svastaye taved viṣṇo bahūdhā vīryāni |
17,1.10e tvaṃ naḥ pṛṇīhi paśubhir viśvarūpaiḥ sudhāyāṃ mā dhehi parame vyoman ||10|| {1}

17,1.11a tvam indrāsi viśvajit sarvavit puruhūtas tvam indra |
17,1.11c tvam indremaṃ suhavaṃ stomam erayasva sa no mṛḍa sumatau te syāma taved viṣṇo bahūdhā vīryāṇi |
17,1.11e tvaṃ naḥ pṛṇīhi paśubhir viśvarūpaiḥ sudhāyāṃ mā dhehi parame vyoman ||11||

17,1.12a adabdho divi pṛthivyām utāsi na ta āpur mahimānam antarikṣe |
17,1.12c adabdhena brahmaṇā vāvṛdhānaḥ sa tvaṃ na indra divi saṃ charma yacha taved viṣṇo bahūdhā vīryāṇi |
17,1.12e tvaṃ naḥ pṛṇīhi paśubhir viśvarūpaiḥ sudhāyāṃ mā dhehi parame vyoman ||12||

17,1.13a yā ta indra tanūr apsu yā pṛthivyāṃ yāntar agnau yā te indra pavamāne svarvidi |
17,1.13c yayendra tanvā 'ntarikṣaṃ vyāpitha tayā na indra tanvā śarma yacha taved viṣṇo bahūdhā vīryāṇi |
17,1.13e tvaṃ naḥ pṛṇīhi paśubhir viśvarūpaiḥ sudhāyāṃ mā dhehi parame vyoman ||13||

17,1.14a tvām indra brahmaṇā vardhayantaḥ sattraṃ ni ṣedur ṛṣayo nādhamānās taved viṣṇo bahūdhā vīryāṇi |
17,1.14c tvaṃ naḥ pṛṇīhi paśubhir viśvarūpaiḥ sudhāyāṃ mā dhehi parame vyoman ||14||

17,1.15a tvaṃ tṛtaṃ tvaṃ pary eṣy utsaṃ sahasradhāraṃ vidathaṃ svarvidaṃ taved viṣṇo bahūdhā vīryāṇi |
17,1.15c tvaṃ naḥ pṛṇīhi paśubhir viśvarūpaiḥ sudhāyāṃ mā dhehi parame vyoman ||15||

17,1.16a tvaṃ rakṣase pradiśaś catasras tvaṃ śociṣā nabhasī vi bhāsi |
17,1.16c tvam imā viśvā bhuvanānu tiṣṭhasa ṛtasya panthām anv eṣi vidvāṃs taved viṣṇo bahūdhā vīryāṇi |
17,1.16e tvaṃ naḥ pṛṇīhi paśubhir viśvarūpaiḥ sudhāyāṃ mā dhehi parame vyoman ||16||

17,1.17a pañcabhiḥ parāṅ tapasy ekayārvāṅ aśastim eṣi sudine bādhamānas taved viṣṇo bahūdhā vīryāṇi |
17,1.17c tvaṃ naḥ pṛṇīhi paśubhir viśvarūpaiḥ sudhāyāṃ mā dhehi parame vyoman ||17||

17,1.18a tvam indras tvam mahendras tvaṃ lokas tvaṃ prajāpatiḥ |
17,1.18c tubhyaṃ yajño vi tāyate tubhyaṃ juhvati juhvatas taved viṣṇo bahūdhā vīryāṇi |
17,1.18e tvaṃ naḥ pṛṇīhi paśubhir viśvarūpaiḥ sudhāyāṃ mā dhehi parame vyoman ||18||

17,1.19a asati sat pratiṣṭhitaṃ sati bhūtaṃ pratiṣṭhitam |
17,1.19c bhūtam ha bhavya āhitaṃ bhavyaṃ bhūte pratiṣṭhitaṃ taved viṣṇo bahūdhā vīryāṇi |
17,1.19e tvaṃ naḥ pṛṇīhi paśubhir viśvarūpaiḥ sudhāyāṃ mā dhehi parame vyoman ||19||

17,1.20a śukro 'si bhrājo 'si |
17,1.20c sa yathā tvaṃ bhrājatā bhrājo 'sy evāhaṃ bhrājatā bhrājyāsam ||20|| {2}

17,1.21a rucir asi roco 'si |
17,1.21c sa yathā tvaṃ rucyā roco 'sy evāhaṃ paśubhiś ca brāhmaṇavarcasena ca ruciṣīya ||21||

17,1.22a udyate nama udāyate nama uditāya namaḥ |
17,1.22c virāje namaḥ svarāje namaḥ samrāje namaḥ ||22||

17,1.23a astaṃyate namo 'stameṣyate namo 'stamitāya namaḥ |
17,1.23c virāje namaḥ svarāje namaḥ samrāje namaḥ ||23||

17,1.24a ud agād ayam ādityo viśvena tapasā saha |
17,1.24c sapatnān mahyaṃ randhayan mā cāhaṃ dviṣate radhaṃ taved viṣṇo bahūdhā vīryāṇi |
17,1.24e tvaṃ naḥ pṛṇīhi paśubhir viśvarūpaiḥ sudhāyāṃ mā dhehi parame vyoman ||24||

17,1.25a āditya nāvam ārukṣaḥ śatāritrāṃ svastaye |
17,1.25c ahar māty apīparo rātriṃ satrāti pāraya ||25||

17,1.26a sūrya nāvam ārukṣaḥ śatāritrāṃ svastaye |
17,1.26c rātriṃ māty apīparo 'haḥ satrāti pāraya ||26||

17,1.27a prajāpater āvṛto brahmaṇā varmaṇāhaṃ kaśyapasya jyotiṣā varcasā ca |
17,1.27c jaradaṣṭiḥ kṛtavīryo vihāyāḥ sahasrāyuḥ sukṛtaś careyam ||27||

17,1.28a parivṛto brahmaṇā varmaṇāham kaśyapasya jyotiṣā varcasā ca |
17,1.28c mā mā prāpann iṣavo daivyā yā mā mānuṣīr avasṛṣṭāḥ vadhāya ||28||

17,1.29a ṛtena gupta ṛtubhiś ca sarvair bhūtena gupto bhavyena cāham |
17,1.29c mā mā prāpat pāpmā mota mṛtyur antar dadhe 'haṃ salilena vācaḥ ||29||

17,1.30a agnir mā goptā pari pātu viśvataḥ udyant sūryo nudatāṃ mṛtyupāśān |
17,1.30c vyuchantīr uṣasaḥ parvatā dhruvāḥ sahasraṃ prāṇā mayy ā yatantām ||30|| {3}



1o cit sakhāyaṃ sakhyā vavṛtyāṃ tiraḥ puru cid arṇavaṃ jaganvān |
1pitur napātam ā dadhīta vedhā adhi kṣami prataraṃ dīdhyānaḥ ||1||

1na te sakhā sakhyaṃ vaṣṭy etat salakṣmā yad viṣurūpā bhavati |
1mahas putrāso asurasya vīrā divo dhartāra urviyā pari khyan ||2||

1uśanti ghā te amṛtāsa etad ekasya cit tyajasaṃ martyasya |
1ni te mano manasi dhāyy asme janyuḥ patis tanvam ā viviṣyāḥ ||3||

1na yat purā cakṛmā kad dha nūnam ṛtaṃ vadanto anṛtaṃ rapema |
1gandharvo apsv apyā ca yoṣā sā nau nābhiḥ paramaṃ jāmi tan nau ||4||

1garbhe nu nau janitā dampatī kar devas tvaṣṭā savitā viśvarūpaḥ |
1nakir asya pra minanti vratāni veda nāv asya pṛthivī uta dyauḥ ||5||

1ko adya yuṅkte dhuri gā ṛtasya śimīvato bhāmino durhṛṇāyūn |
1āsanniṣūn hṛtsvaso mayobhūn ya eṣāṃ bhṛtyām ṛṇadhat sa jīvāt ||6||

1ko asya veda prathamasyāhnaḥ ka īṃ dadarśa ka iha pra vocat |
1bṛhan mitrasya varuṇasya dhāma kad u brava āhano vīcyā nṝn ||7||

1yamasya mā yamyaṃ kāma āgant samāne yonau sahaśeyyāya |
1jāyeva patye tanvaṃ riricyāṃ vi cid vṛheva rathyeva cakrā ||8||

1na tiṣṭhanti na ni miṣanty ete devānāṃ spaśa iha ye caranti |
1anyena mad āhano yāhi tūyaṃ tena vi vṛha rathyeva cakrā ||9||

18,1.10a rātrībhir asmā ahabhir daśasyet sūryasya cakṣur muhur un mimīyāt |
18,1.10c divā pṛthivyā mithunā sabandhū yamīr yamasya vivṛhād ajāmi ||10|| {1}

18,1.11a ā ghā tā gachān uttarā yugāni yatra jāmayaḥ kṛṇavann ajāmi |
18,1.11c upa barbṛhi vṛṣabhāya bāhum anyam ichasva subhage patiṃ mat ||11||
18,1.12a kiṃ bhrātāsad yad anāthaṃ bhavāti kim u svasā yan nirṛtir nigachāt |
18,1.12c kāmamūtā bahv etad rapāmi tanvā me tanvaṃ saṃ pipṛgdhi ||12||

18,1.13a na te nāthaṃ yamy atrāham asmi na te tanūṃ tanvā sam papṛcyām |
18,1.13c anyena mat pramudaḥ kalpayasva na te bhrātā subhage vaṣṭy etat ||13||

18,1.14a na vā u te tanūṃ tanvā saṃ pipṛcyāṃ pāpam āhur yaḥ svasāraṃ nigachāt |
18,1.14c asaṃyad etan manaso hṛdo me bhrātā svasuḥ śayane yac chayīya ||14||

18,1.15a bato batāsi yama naiva te mano hṛdayaṃ cāvidām ā |
18,1.15c anyā kila tvāṃ kakṣyeva yuktaṃ pari ṣvajātau libujeva vṛkṣam ||15||

18,1.16a anyam ū ṣu yamy anya u tvāṃ pari ṣvajātau libujeva vṛkṣam |
18,1.16c tasya vā tvaṃ mana ichā sa vā tavādhā kṛṇuṣva saṃvidaṃ subhadrām ||16||

18,1.17a trīṇi chandāṃsi kavayo vi yetire pururūpaṃ darśataṃ viśvacakṣaṇam |
18,1.17c āpo vātā oṣadhayas tāny ekasmin bhuvana ārpitāni ||17||
18,1.18a vṛṣā vṛṣṇe duduhe dohasā divaḥ payāṃsi yahvo aditer adābhyaḥ |
18,1.18c viśvaṃ sa veda varuṇo yathā dhiyā sa yajñiyo yajati yajñiyāṃ ṛtūn ||18||

18,1.19a rapad gandharvīr apyā ca yoṣaṇā nadasya nāde pari pātu no manaḥ |
18,1.19c iṣṭasya madhye aditir ni dhātu no bhrātā no jyeṣṭhaḥ prathamo vi vocati ||19||

18,1.20a so cit nu bhadrā kṣumatī yaśasvaty uṣā uvāsa manave svarvatī |
18,1.20c yad īm uśantam uśatām anu kratum agniṃ hotāraṃ vidathāya jījanan ||20|| {2}

18,1.21a adha tyaṃ drapsaṃ vibhvaṃ vicakṣanaṃ vir ābharad iṣiraḥ śyeno adhvare |
18,1.21c yadī viśo vṛṇate dasmam āryā agniṃ hotāram adha dhīr ajāyata ||21||

18,1.22a sadāsi raṇvo yavaseva puṣyate hotrābhir agne manuṣaḥ svadhvaraḥ |
18,1.22c viprasya vā yac chaśamāna ukthyo vājaṃ sasavāṃ upayāsi bhūribhiḥ ||22||

18,1.23a ud īraya pitarā jāra ā bhagam iyakṣati haryato hṛtta iṣyati |
18,1.23c vivakti vahniḥ svapasyate makhas taviṣyate asuro vepate matī ||23||

18,1.24a yas te agne sumatiṃ marto akhyat sahasaḥ sūno ati sa pra śṛṇve |
18,1.24c iṣaṃ dadhāno vahamāno aśvair ā sa dyumāṃ amavān bhūṣati dyūn ||24||

18,1.25a śrudhī no agne sadane sadhasthe yukṣvā ratham amṛtasya dravitnum |
18,1.25c ā no vaha rodasī devaputre mākir devānām apa bhūr iha syāḥ ||25||

18,1.26a yad agna eṣā samitir bhavāti devī deveṣu yajatā yajatra |
18,1.26c ratnā ca yad vibhajāsi svadhāvo bhāgaṃ no atra vasumantaṃ vītāt ||26||

18,1.27a anv agnir uṣasām agram akhyad anv ahāni prathamo jātavedāḥ |
18,1.27c anu sūrya uṣaso anu raśmīn dyāvāpṛthivī ā viveśa ||27||

18,1.28a praty agnir uṣasām agram akhyat praty ahāni prathamo jātavedāḥ |
18,1.28c prati sūryasya purudhā ca raśmīn prati dyāvāpṛthivī ā tatāna ||28||

18,1.29a dyāvā ha kṣāmā prathame ṛtenābhiśrāve bhavataḥ satyavācā |
18,1.29c devo yan martān yajathāya kṛṇvant sīdad dhotā pratyaṅ svam asuṃ yan ||29||

18,1.30a devo devān paribhūr ṛtena vahā no havyaṃ prathamaś cikitvān |
18,1.30c dhūmaketuḥ samidhā bhāṛjīko mandro hotā nityo vācā yajīyān ||30|| {3}
18,1.31a arcāmi vāṃ vardhāyāpo ghṛtasnū dyāvābhūmī śṛṇutaṃ rodasī me |
18,1.31c ahā yad devā asunītim āyan madhvā no atra pitarā śiśītām ||31||

18,1.32a svāvṛg devasyāmṛtaṃ yadī gor ato jātāso dhārayanta urvī |
18,1.32c viśve devā anu tat te yajur gur duhe yad enī divyaṃ ghṛtam vāḥ ||32||

18,1.33a kiṃ svin no rājā jagṛhe kad asyāti vrataṃ cakṛmā ko vi veda |
18,1.33c mitras cid dhi ṣmā juhurāṇo devāṃ chloko na yātām api vājo asti ||33||

18,1.34a durmantv atrāmṛtasya nāma salakṣmā yad viṣurūpā bhavāti |
18,1.34c yamasya yo manavate sumantv agne tam ṛṣva pāhy aprayuchan ||34||

18,1.35a yasmin devā vidathe mādayante vivasvataḥ sadane dhārayante |
18,1.35c sūrye jyotir adadhur māsy aktūn pari dyotaniṃ carato ajasrā ||35||

18,1.36a yasmin devā manmani saṃcaranty apīcye na vayam asya vidma |
18,1.36c mitro no atrāditir anāgānt savitā devo varuṇāya vocat ||36||

18,1.37a sakhāya ā śiṣāmahe brahmendrāya vajriṇe |
18,1.37c stuṣa ū ṣu nṛtamāya dhṛṣṇave ||37||

18,1.38a śavasā hy asi śruto vṛtrahatyena vṛtrahā |
18,1.38c maghair maghono ati śūra dāśasi ||38||

18,1.39a stego na kṣām aty eṣi pṛthivīṃ mahī no vātā iha vāntu bhūmau |
18,1.39c mitro no atra varuṇo yujamāno agnir vane na vy asṛṣṭa śokam ||39||

18,1.40a stuhi śrutaṃ gartasadaṃ janānāṃ rājānaṃ bhīmam upahatnum ugram |
18,1.40c mṛḍā jaritre rudra stavāno anyam asmat te ni vapantu senyam ||40|| {4}

18,1.41a sarasvatīṃ devayanto havante sarasvatīm adhvare tāyamāne |
18,1.41c sarasvatīṃ sukṛto havante sarasvatī dāśuṣe vāryaṃ dāt ||41||

18,1.42a sarasvatīṃ pitaro havante dakṣinā yajñam abhinakṣamāṇāḥ |
18,1.42c āsadyāsmin barhiṣi mādayadhvam anamīvā iṣa ā dhehy asme ||42||

18,1.43a sarasvati yā sarathaṃ yayāthokthaiḥ svadhābhir devi pitṛbhir madantī |
18,1.43c sahasrārgham iḍo atra bhāgaṃ rāyas poṣaṃ yajamānāya dhehi ||43||

18,1.44a ud īratām avara ut parāsa un madhyamāḥ pitaraḥ somyāsaḥ |
18,1.44c asuṃ ya īyur avṛkā ṛtajñās te no 'vantu pitaro haveṣu ||44||

18,1.45a āhaṃ pitṝnt suvidatrāṃ avitsi napātaṃ ca vikramaṇaṃ ca viṣṇoḥ |
18,1.45c barhiṣado ye svadhayā sutasya bhajanta pitvas ta ihāgamiṣṭhāḥ ||45||

18,1.46a idaṃ pitṛbhyo namo astv adya ye pūrvāso ye aparāsa īyuḥ |
18,1.46c ye pārthive rajasy ā niṣaktā ye vā nūnaṃ suvṛjanāsu dikṣu ||46||

18,1.47a mātalī kavyair yamo aṅgirobhir bṛhaspatir ṛkvabhir vāvṛdhānaḥ |
18,1.47c yāṃś ca devā vāvṛdhur ye ca devāṃs te no 'vantu pitaro haveṣu ||47||

18,1.48a svāduṣ kilāyaṃ madhumāṃ utāyaṃ tīvraḥ kilāyaṃ rasavāṃ utāyam |
18,1.48c uto nv asya papivāṃsam indraṃ na kaś cana sahata āhaveṣu ||48||

18,1.49a pareyivāṃsaṃ pravato mahīr iti bahubhyaḥ panthām anupaspaśānam |
18,1.49c vaivasvataṃ saṃgamanaṃ janānāṃ yamaṃ rājānaṃ haviṣā saparyata ||49||

18,1.50a yamo no gātuṃ prathamo viveda naiṣā gavyūtir apabhartavā u |
18,1.50c yatrā naḥ pūrve pitaraḥ paretā enā jajñānāḥ pathyā anu svāḥ ||50|| {5}

18,1.51a barhiṣadaḥ pitara ūty arvāg imā vo havyā cakṛmā juṣadhvam |
18,1.51c ta ā gatāvasā śaṃtamenādhā naḥ śaṃ yor arapo dadhāta ||51||

18,1.52a ācyā jānu dakṣiṇato niṣadyedaṃ no havir abhi gṛṇantu viśve |
18,1.52c mā hiṃsiṣṭa pitaraḥ kena cin no yad va āgaḥ puruṣatā karāma ||52||

18,1.53a tvaṣṭā duhitre vahatuṃ kṛṇoti tenedaṃ viśvaṃ bhuvanaṃ sam eti |
18,1.53c yamasya mātā paryuhyamānā maho jāyā vivasvato nanāśa ||53||

18,1.54a prehi prehi pathibhiḥ pūryāṇair yenā te pūrve pitaraḥ paretāḥ |
18,1.54c ubhā rājānau svadhayā madantau yamaṃ paśyāsi varuṇaṃ ca devam ||54||

18,1.55a apeta vīta vi ca sarpatāto 'smā etaṃ pitaro lokam akran |
18,1.55c ahobhir adbhir aktubhir vyaktaṃ yamo dadāty avasānam asmai ||55||

18,1.56a uśantas tvedhīmahy uśantaḥ sam idhīmahi |
18,1.56c uśann uśata ā vaha pitṝn haviṣe attave ||56||

18,1.57a dyumantas tvedhīmahi dyumantaḥ sam idhīmahi |
18,1.57c dyumān dyumata ā vaha pitṝn haviṣe attave ||57||

18,1.58a aṅgiraso naḥ pitaro navagvā atharvāṇo bhṛgavaḥ somyāsaḥ |
18,1.58c teṣāṃ vayaṃ sumatau yajñiyānām api bhadre saumanase syāma ||58||

18,1.59a aṅgirobhir yajñiyair ā gahīha yama vairūpair iha mādayasva |
18,1.59c vivasvantaṃ huve yaḥ pitā te 'smin barhiṣy ā niṣadya ||59||

18,1.60a imaṃ yama prastaram ā hi rohāṅgirobhiḥ pitṛbhiḥ saṃvidānaḥ |
18,1.60c ā tvā mantrāḥ kaviśastā vahantv enā rājan haviṣo mādayasva ||60||

18,1.61a ita eta udāruhan divas pṛṣṭhānv āruhan |
18,1.61c pra bhūrjayo yathā pathā dyām aṅgiraso yayuḥ ||61|| {6}



1yamāya somaḥ pavate yamāya kriyate haviḥ |
1yamaṃ ha yajño gachaty agnidūto araṃkṛtaḥ ||1||

1yamāya madhumattamaṃ juhotā pra ca tiṣṭhata |
1idaṃ nama ṛṣibhyaḥ pūrvajebhyaḥ pūrvebhyaḥ pathikṛdbhyaḥ ||2||

1yamāya ghṛtavat payo rājñe havir juhotana |
1sa no jīveṣv ā yamed dīrgham āyuḥ pra jīvase ||3||

1mainam agne vi daho mābhi śūśuco māsya tvacaṃ cikṣipo mā śarīram |
1śṛtaṃ yadā karasi jātavedo 'them enaṃ pra hiṇutāt pitṝṃr upa ||4||

1yadā śṛtaṃ kṛṇavo jātavedo 'themam enaṃ pari dattāt pitṛbhyaḥ |
1yado gachāty asunītim etām atha devānāṃ vaśanīr bhavāti ||5||

1trikadrukebhiḥ pavate ṣaḍ urvīr ekam id bṛhat |
1triṣṭub gāyatrī chandāṃsi sarvā tā yama ārpitā ||6||

1sūryaṃ cakṣuṣā gacha vātam ātmanā divaṃ ca gacha pṛthivīṃ ca dharmabhiḥ |
1apo vā gacha yadi tatra te hitam oṣadhīṣu prati tiṣṭhā śarīraiḥ ||7||

1ajo bhāgas tapasas taṃ tapasva taṃ te śocis tapatu taṃ te arciḥ |
1yās te śivās tanvo jātavedas tābhir vahainaṃ sukṛtām u lokam ||8||

1yās te śocayo raṃhayo jātavedo yābhir āpṛṇāsi divam antarikṣam |
1ajaṃ yantam anu tāḥ sam ṛṇvatām athetarābhiḥ śivatamābhiḥ śṛtaṃ kṛdhi ||9||

18,2.10a ava sṛja punar agne pitṛbhyo yas ta āhutaś carati svadhāvān |
18,2.10c āyur vasāna upa yātu śeṣaḥ saṃ gachatāṃ tanvā suvarcāḥ ||10|| {7}

18,2.11a ati drava śvānau sārameyau caturakṣau śabalau sādhunā pathā |
18,2.11c adhā pitṝnt suvidatrāṃ apīhi yamena ye sadhamādaṃ madanti ||11||

18,2.12a yau te śvānau yama rakṣitārau caturakṣau pathiṣadī nṛcakṣasā |
18,2.12c tābhyāṃ rājan pari dhehy enaṃ svasty asmā anamīvaṃ ca dhehi ||12||

18,2.13a urūṇasāv asutṛpāv udumbalau yamasya dūtau carato janāṃ anu |
18,2.13c tāv asmabhyaṃ dṛśaye sūryāya punar dātām asum adyeha bhadram ||13||

18,2.14a soma ekebhyaḥ pavate ghṛtam eka upāsate |
18,2.14c yebhyo madhu pradhāvati tāṃś cid evāpi gachatāt ||14||

18,2.15a ye cit pūrva ṛtasātā ṛtajātā ṛtāvṛdhaḥ |
18,2.15c ṛṣīn tapasvato yama tapojāṃ api gachatāt ||15||

18,2.16a tapasā ye anādhṛṣyās tapasā ye svar yayuḥ |
18,2.16c tapo ye cakrire mahas tāṃś cid evāpi gachatāt ||16||

18,2.17a ye yudhyante pradhaneṣu śūrāso ye svar tanūtyajaḥ |
18,2.17c ye vā sahasradakṣiṇās tāṃ cid evāpi gachatāt ||17||

18,2.18a sahasraṇīthāḥ kavayo ye gopāyanti sūryam |
18,2.18c ṛṣīn tapasvato yama tapojāṃ api gachatāt ||18||

18,2.19a syonāsmai bhava pṛthivy anṛkṣarā niveśanī |
18,2.19c yachāsmai śarma saprathāḥ ||19||

18,2.20a asaṃbādhe pṛthivyā urau loke ni dhīyasva |
18,2.20c svadhā yāś cakṛṣe jīvan tās te santu madhuścutaḥ ||20|| {8}

18,2.21a hvayāmi te manasā mana ihemān gṛhām upa jujuṣāṇa ehi |
18,2.21c saṃ gachasva pitṛbhiḥ saṃ yamena syonās tvā vātā upa vāntu śagmāḥ ||21||

18,2.22a ut tvā vahantu maruta udavāhā udaprutaḥ |
18,2.22c ajena kṛṇvantaḥ śītaṃ varṣeṇokṣantu bāl iti ||22||

18,2.23a ud ahvam āyur āyuṣe kratve dakṣāya jīvase |
18,2.23c svān gachatu te mano adhā pitṝṃr upa drava ||23||

18,2.24a mā te mano māsor māṅgānāṃ mā rasasya te |
18,2.24c mā te hāsta tanvaḥ kiṃ caneha ||24||

18,2.25a mā tvā vṛkṣaḥ saṃ bādhiṣṭa mā devī pṛthivī mahī |
18,2.25c lokaṃ pitṛṣu vittvaidhasva yamarājasu ||25||

18,2.26a yat te aṅgam atihitaṃ parācair apānaḥ prāṇo ya u vā te paretaḥ |
18,2.26c tat te saṃgatya pitaraḥ sanīḍā ghāsād ghāsaṃ punar ā veśayantu ||26||

18,2.27a apemaṃ jīvā arudhan gṛhebhyas taṃ nir vahata pari grāmād itaḥ |
18,2.27c mṛtyur yamasyāsīd dūtaḥ pracetā asūn pitṛbhyo gamayāṃ cakāra ||27||

18,2.28a ye dasyavaḥ pitṛṣu praviṣṭā jñātimukhā ahutādaś caranti |
18,2.28c parāpuro nipuro ye bharanty agniṣ ṭān asmāt pra dhamāti yajñāt ||28||

18,2.29a saṃ viśantv iha pitaraḥ svā naḥ syonaṃ kṛṇvantaḥ pratiranta āyuḥ |
18,2.29c tebhyaḥ śakema haviṣā nakṣamāṇā jyog jīvantaḥ śaradaḥ purūcīḥ ||29||

18,2.30a yāṃ te dhenuṃ nipṛṇāmi yam u kṣīra odanam |
18,2.30c tenā janasyāso bhartā yo 'trāsad ajīvanaḥ ||30|| {9}

18,2.31a aśvāvatīṃ pra tara yā suśevā rkṣākaṃ vā prataraṃ navīyaḥ |
18,2.31c yas tvā jaghāna vadhyaḥ so astu mā so anyad vidata bhāgadheyam ||31||

18,2.32a yamaḥ paro 'varo vivasvān tataḥ paraṃ nāti paśyāmi kiṃ cana |
18,2.32c yame adhvaro adhi me niviṣṭo bhuvo vivasvān anvātatāna ||32||

18,2.33a apāgūhann amṛtāṃ martyebhyaḥ kṛtvā savarṇām adadhur vivasvate |
18,2.33c utāśvināv abharad yat tad āsīd ajahād u dvā mithunā saraṇyūḥ ||33||

18,2.34a ye nikhātā ye paroptā ye dagdhā ye coddhitāḥ |
18,2.34c sarvāṃs tān agna ā vaha pitṝn haviṣe attave ||34||

18,2.35a ye agnidagdhā ye anagnidagdhā madhye divaḥ svadhayā mādayante |
18,2.35c tvaṃ tān vettha yadi te jātavedaḥ svadhayā yajñaṃ svadhitiṃ juṣantām ||35||

18,2.36a śaṃ tapa māti tapo agne mā tanvaṃ tapaḥ |
18,2.36c vaṇeṣu śuṣmo astu te pṛthivyām astu yad dharaḥ ||36||

18,2.37a dadāmy asmā avasānam etad ya eṣa āgan mama ced abhūd iha |
18,2.37c yamaś cikitvān praty etad āha mamaiṣa rāya upa tiṣṭhatām iha ||37||

18,2.38a imāṃ mātrāṃ mimīmahe yathāparaṃ na māsātai |
18,2.38c śate śaratsu no purā ||38||

18,2.39a premāṃ mātrāṃ mimīmahe yathāparaṃ na māsātai |
18,2.39c śate śaratsu no purā ||39||

18,2.40a apemāṃ mātrāṃ mimīmahe yathāparaṃ na māsātai |
18,2.40c śate śaratsu no purā ||40|| {10}

18,2.41a vīmāṃ mātrāṃ mimīmahe yathāparaṃ na māsātai |
18,2.41c śate śaratsu no purā ||41||

18,2.42a nir imāṃ mātrāṃ mimīmahe yathāparaṃ na māsātai |
18,2.42c śate śaratsu no purā ||42||
18,2.43a ud imāṃ mātrāṃ mimīmahe yathāparaṃ na māsātai |
18,2.43c śate śaratsu no purā ||43||

18,2.44a sam imāṃ mātrāṃ mimīmahe yathāparaṃ na māsātai |
18,2.44c śate śaratsu no purā ||44||

18,2.45a amāsi mātrāṃ svar agām āyuṣmān bhūyāsam |
18,2.45c yathāparaṃ na māsātai śate śaratsu no purā ||45||
18,2.46a prāṇo apāno vyāna āyuś cakṣur dṛśaye sūryāya |
18,2.46c aparipareṇa pathā yamarājñaḥ pitṝn gacha ||46||

18,2.47a ye agravaḥ śaśamānāḥ pareyur hitvā dveṣāṃsy anapatyavantaḥ |
18,2.47c te dyām udityāvidanta lokaṃ nākasya pṛṣṭhe adhi dīdhyānāḥ ||47||

18,2.48a udanvatī dyaur avamā pīlumatīti madhyamā |
18,2.48c tṛtīyā ha pradyaur iti yasyāṃ pitara āsate ||48||

18,2.49a ye na pituḥ pitaro ye pitāmahā ya āviviśur urv antarikṣam |
18,2.49c ya ākṣiyanti pṛthivīm uta dyāṃ tebhyaḥ pitṛbhyo namasā vidhema ||49||

18,2.50a idam id vā u nāparaṃ divi paśyasi sūryam |
18,2.50c mātā putraṃ yathā sicābhy enaṃ bhūma ūrṇuhi ||50|| {11}

18,2.51a idam id vā u nāparaṃ jarasy anyad ito 'param |
18,2.51c jāyā patim iva vāsasābhy enaṃ bhūma ūrṇuhi ||51||

18,2.52a abhi tvorṇomi pṛthivyā mātur vastreṇa bhadrayā |
18,2.52c jīveṣu bhadraṃ tan mayi svadhā pitṛṣu sā tvayi ||52||

18,2.53a agnīṣomā pathikṛtā syonaṃ devebhyo ratnaṃ dadhathur vi lokam |
18,2.53c upa preṣyantaṃ pūṣaṇaṃ yo vahāty añjoyānaiḥ pathibhis tatra gachatam ||53||

18,2.54a pūṣā tvetaś cyāvayatu pra vidvān anaṣṭapaśur bhuvanasya gopāḥ |
18,2.54c sa tvaitebhyaḥ pari dadat pitṛbhyo 'gnir devebhyaḥ suvidatriyebhyaḥ ||54||

18,2.55a āyur viśvāyuḥ pari pātu tvā pūṣā tvā pātu prapathe purastāt |
18,2.55c yatrāsate sukṛto yatra ta īyus tatra tvā devaḥ savitā dadhātu ||55||

18,2.56a imau yunajmi te vahnī asunītāya voḍhave |
18,2.56c tābhyāṃ yamasya sādanaṃ samitiś cāva gachatāt ||56||

18,2.57a etat tvā vāsaḥ prathamaṃ nv āgann apaitad ūha yad ihābibhaḥ purā |
18,2.57c iṣṭāpūrtam anusaṃkrāma vidvān yatra te dattaṃ bahudhā vibandhuṣu ||57||

18,2.58a agner varma pari gobhir vyayasva saṃ prorṇuṣva medasā pīvasā ca |
18,2.58c net tvā dhṛṣṇur harasā jarhṛṣāṇo dadhṛg vidhakṣan parīṅkhayātai ||58||

18,2.59a daṇḍaṃ hastād ādadāno gatāsoḥ saha śrotreṇa varcasā balena |
18,2.59c atraiva tvam iha vayaṃ suvīrā viśvā mṛdho abhimātīr jayema ||59||

18,2.60a dhanur hastād ādadāno mṛtasya saha kṣatreṇa varcasā balena |
18,2.60c samāgṛbhāya vasu bhūri puṣṭam arvāṅ tvam ehy upa jīvalokam ||60|| {12}



1iyaṃ nārī patilokaṃ vṛṇānā ni padyata upa tvā martya pretam |
1dharmaṃ purāṇam anupālayantī tasyai prajāṃ draviṇaṃ ceha dhehi ||1||

1ud īrṣva nāry abhi jīvalokaṃ gatāsum etam upa śeṣa ehi |
1hastagrābhasya dadhiṣos tavedaṃ patyur janitvam abhi saṃ babhūtha ||2||

1apaśyaṃ yuvatiṃ nīyamānāṃ jīvāṃ mṛtebhyaḥ pariṇīyamānām |
1andhena yat tamasā prāvṛtāsīt prākto apācīm anayaṃ tad enām ||3||

1prajānaty aghnye jīvalokaṃ devānāṃ panthām anusaṃcarantī |
1ayaṃ te gopatis taṃ juṣasva svargaṃ lokam adhi rohayainam ||4||

1upa dyām upa vetasam avattaro nadīnām |
1agne pittam apām asi ||5||

1yaṃ tvam agne samadahas tam u nir vāpaya punaḥ |
1kyāmbūr atra rohatu śāṇḍadūrvā vyalkaśā ||6||

1idaṃ ta ekam pura ū ta ekaṃ tṛtīyena jyotiṣā saṃ viśasva |
1saṃveśane tanvā cārur edhi priyo devānāṃ parame sadhasthe ||7||

1ut tiṣṭha prehi pra dravaukaḥ kṛṇuṣva salile sadhasthe |
1tatra tvaṃ pitṛbhiḥ saṃvidānaḥ saṃ somena madasva saṃ svadhābhiḥ ||8||

1pra cyavasva tanvaṃ saṃ bharasva mā te gātrā vi hāyi mo śarīram |
1mano niviṣṭam anusaṃviśasva yatra bhūmer juṣase tatra gacha ||9||

18,3.10a varcasā māṃ pitaraḥ somyāso añjantu devā madhunā ghṛtena |
18,3.10c cakṣuṣe mā prataraṃ tārayanto jarase mā jaradaṣṭiṃ vardhantu ||10|| {13}

18,3.11a varcasā māṃ sam anaktv agnir medhāṃ me viṣṇur ny anaktv āsan |
18,3.11c rayiṃ me viśve ni yachantu devāḥ syonā māpaḥ pavanaiḥ punantu ||11||

18,3.12a mitrāvaruṇā pari mām adhātām ādityā mā svaravo vardhayantu |
18,3.12c varco ma indro ny anaktu hastayor jaradaṣṭiṃ mā savitā kṛṇotu ||12||

18,3.13a yo mamāra prathamo martyānāṃ yaḥ preyāya prathamo lokam etam |
18,3.13c vaivasvataṃ saṃgamanaṃ janānāṃ yamaṃ rājānaṃ haviṣā saparyata ||13||

18,3.14a parā yāta pitara ā ca yātāyaṃ vo yajño madhunā samaktaḥ |
18,3.14c datto asmabhyaṃ draviṇeha bhadraṃ rayiṃ ca naḥ sarvavīraṃ dadhāta ||14||

18,3.15a kaṇvaḥ kakṣīvān purumīḍho agastyaḥ śyāvāśvaḥ sobhary arcanānāḥ |
18,3.15c viśvāmitro 'yaṃ jamadagnir atrir avantu naḥ kaśyapo vāmadevaḥ ||15||

18,3.16a viśvāmitra jamadagne vasiṣṭha bharadvāja gotama vāmadeva |
18,3.16c śardir no atrir agrabhīn namobhiḥ susaṃśāsaḥ pitaro mṛḍatā naḥ ||16||

18,3.17a kasye mṛjānā ati yanti ripram āyur dadhānāḥ prataraṃ navīyaḥ |
18,3.17c āpyāyamānāḥ prajayā dhanenādha syāma surabhayo gṛheṣu ||17||

18,3.18a añjate vy añjate sam añjate kratuṃ rihanti madhunābhy añjate |
18,3.18c sindhor ucchvāse patayantam ukṣaṇaṃ hiraṇyapāvāḥ paśum āsu gṛhnate ||18||

18,3.19a yad vo mudraṃ pitaraḥ somyaṃ ca teno sacadhvaṃ svayaśaso hi bhūta |
18,3.19c te arvāṇaḥ kavaya ā śṛṇota suvidatrā vidathe huyamānāḥ ||19||

18,3.20a ye atrayo aṅgiraso navagvā iṣṭāvanto rātiṣāco dadhānāḥ |
18,3.20c dakṣiṇāvantaḥ sukṛto ya u sthāsadyāsmin barhiṣi mādayadhvam ||20|| {14}

18,3.21a adhā yathā naḥ pitaraḥ parāsaḥ pratnāso agna ṛtam āśaśānāḥ |
18,3.21c śucīd ayan dīdhyata ukthaśasaḥ kṣāmā bhindanto aruṇīr apa vran ||21||

18,3.22a sukarmānaḥ suruco devayanto ayo na devā janimā dhamantaḥ |
18,3.22c śucanto agniṃ vāvṛdhanta indram urvīm gavyāṃ pariṣadaṃ no akran ||22||

18,3.23a ā yūtheva kṣumati paśvo akhyad devānāṃ janimānty ugraḥ |
18,3.23c martāsaś cid urvaśīr akṛpran vṛdhe cid arya uparasyāyoḥ ||23||

18,3.24a akarma te svapaso abhūma ṛtam avasrann uṣaso vibhātīḥ |
18,3.24c viśvaṃ tad bhadraṃ yad avanti devā bṛhad vadema vidathe suvīrāḥ ||24||

18,3.25a indro mā marutvān prācyā diśaḥ pātu bāhucyutā pṛthivī dyām ivopari |
18,3.25c lokakṛtaḥ pathikṛto yajāmahe ye devānāṃ hutabhāgā iha stha ||25||

18,3.26a dhātā mā nirṛtyā dakṣiṇāyā diśaḥ pātu bāhucyutā pṛthivī dyāṃ ivopari |
18,3.26c lokakṛtaḥ pathikṛto yajāmahe ye devānāṃ hutabhāgā iha stha ||26||

18,3.27a aditir mādityaiḥ pratīcyā diśaḥ pātu bāhucyutā pṛthivī dyām ivopari |
18,3.27c lokakṛtaḥ pathikṛto yajāmahe ye devānāṃ hutabhāgā iha stha ||27||

18,3.28a somo mā viśvair devair udīcyā diśaḥ pātu bāhucyutā pṛthivī dyām ivopari |
18,3.28c lokakṛtaḥ pathikṛto yajāmahe ye devānāṃ hutabhāgā iha stha ||28||

18,3.29a dhartā ha tvā dharuṇo dhārayātā ūrdhvaṃ bhānuṃ savitā dyām ivopari |
18,3.29c lokakṛtaḥ pathikṛto yajāmahe ye devānāṃ hutabhāgā iha stha ||29||

18,3.30a prācyāṃ tvā diśi purā samvṛtaḥ svadhāyām ā dadhāmi bāhucyutā pṛthivī dyām ivopari |
18,3.30c lokakṛtaḥ pathikṛto yajāmahe ye devānāṃ hutabhāgā iha stha ||30|| {15}

18,3.31a dakṣiṇāyāṃ tvā diśi purā samvṛtaḥ svadhāyām ā dadhāmi bāhucyutā pṛthivī dyām ivopari |
18,3.31c lokakṛtaḥ pathikṛto yajāmahe ye devānāṃ hutabhāgā iha stha ||31||

18,3.32a pratīcyāṃ tvā diśi purā saṃvṛtaḥ svadhāyām ā dadhāmi bāhucyutā pṛthivī dyām ivopari |
18,3.32c lokakṛtaḥ pathikṛto yajāmahe ye devānāṃ hutabhāgā iha stha ||32||

18,3.33a udīcyāṃ tvā diśi purā samvṛtaḥ svadhāyām ā dadhāmi bāhucyutā pṛthivī dyām ivopari |
18,3.33c lokakṛtaḥ pathikṛto yajāmahe ye devānāṃ hutabhāgā iha stha ||33||

18,3.34a dhruvāyāṃ tvā diśi purā saṃvṛtaḥ svadhāyām ā dadhāmi bāhucyutā pṛthivī dyām ivopari |
18,3.34c lokakṛtaḥ pathikṛto yajāmahe ye devānāṃ hutabhāgā iha stha ||34||

18,3.35a ūrdhvāyāṃ tvā diśi purā samvṛtaḥ svadhāyām ā dadhāmi bāhucyutā pṛthivī dyām ivopari |
18,3.35c lokakṛtaḥ pathikṛto yajāmahe ye devānāṃ hutabhāgā iha stha ||35||

18,3.36a dhartāsi dharuno 'si vaṃsago 'si ||36||

18,3.37a udapūr asi madhupūr asi vātapūr asi ||37||

18,3.38a itaś ca māmutaś cāvatāṃ yame iva yatamāne yad aitam |
18,3.38c pra vāṃ bharan mānuṣā devayanto ā sīdatāṃ svam u lokaṃ vidāne ||38||

18,3.39a svāsasthe bhavatam indave no yuje vāṃ brahma pūrvyaṃ namobhiḥ |
18,3.39c vi śloka eti pathyeva sūriḥ śṛṇvantu viśve amṛtāsa etat ||39||

18,3.40a trīṇi padāni rupo anv arohac catuṣpadīm anv etad vratena |
18,3.40c akṣareṇa prati mimīte arkam ṛtasya nābhāv abhi saṃ punāti ||40|| {16}

18,3.41a devebhyaḥ kam avṛṇīta mṛtyuṃ prajāyai kim amṛtaṃ nāvṛṇīta |
18,3.41c bṛhaspatir yajñam atanuta ṛṣiḥ priyāṃ yamas tanvam ā rireca ||41||

18,3.42a tvam agna īḍito jātavedo 'vāḍ ḍhavyāni surabhīṇi kṛtvā |
18,3.42c prādāḥ pitṛbhyaḥ svadhayā te akṣann addhi tvaṃ deva prayatā havīṃṣi ||42||

18,3.43a āsīnāso aruṇīnām upasthe rayiṃ dhatta dāśuṣe martyāya |
18,3.43c putrebhyaḥ pitaras tasya vasvaḥ pra yachata ta ihorjaṃ dadhāta ||43||

18,3.44a agniṣvāttāḥ pitara eha gachata sadaḥsadaḥ sadata supraṇītayaḥ |
18,3.44c atto havīṃṣi prayatāni barhiṣi rayiṃ ca naḥ sarvavīraṃ dadhāta ||44||

18,3.45a upahūtā naḥ pitaraḥ somyāso barhiṣyeṣu nidhiṣu priyeṣu |
18,3.45c ta ā gamantu ta iha śruvantv adhi bruvantu te 'vantv asmān ||45||

18,3.46a ye naḥ pituḥ pitaro ye pitāmahā anūjahire somapīthaṃ vasiṣṭhāḥ |
18,3.46c tebhir yamaḥ samrarāṇo havīṃṣy uśann uśadbhiḥ pratikāmam attu ||46||

18,3.47a ye tātṛṣur devatrā jehamānā hotrāvidaḥ stomataṣṭāso arkaiḥ |
18,3.47c āgne yāhi sahasraṃ devavandaiḥ satyaiḥ kavibhir ṛṣibhir gharmasadbhiḥ ||47||

18,3.48a ye satyāso havirado haviṣpā indreṇa devaiḥ sarathaṃ tureṇa |
18,3.48c āgne yāhi suvidatrebhir arvāṅ paraiḥ pūrvair ṛṣibhir gharmasadbhiḥ ||48||

18,3.49a upa sarpa mātaraṃ bhūmim etām uruvyacasaṃ pṛthivīṃ suśevām |
18,3.49c ūrṇamradāḥ pṛthivī dakṣiṇāvata eṣā tvā pātu prapathe purastāt ||49||

18,3.50a uc chvañcasva pṛthivi mā ni bādhathāḥ sūpāyanāsmai bhava sūpasarpaṇā |
18,3.50c mātā putraṃ yathā sicābhy enaṃ bhūma ūrṇuhi ||50|| {17}

18,3.51a ucchvañcamānā pṛthivī su tiṣṭhatu sahasraṃ mita upa hi śrayantām |
18,3.51c te gṛhāso ghṛtaścutaḥ syonā viśvāhāsmai śaraṇāḥ santv atra ||51||

18,3.52a ut te stabhnāmi pṛthivīṃ tvat parīmaṃ logaṃ nidadhan mo aham riṣam |
18,3.52c etāṃ sthūṇāṃ pitaro dhārayanti te tatra yamaḥ sādanā te kṛṇotu ||52||

18,3.53a imam agne camasaṃ mā vi jihvaraḥ priyo devānām uta somyānām |
18,3.53c ayaṃ yaś camaso devapānas tasmin devā amṛtā mādayantām ||53||

18,3.54a atharvā pūrṇam camasam yam indrāyābibhar vājinīvate |
18,3.54c tasmin kṛṇoti sukṛtasya bhakṣaṃ tasmin induḥ pavate viśvadānim ||54||

18,3.55a yat te kṛṣṇaḥ śakuna ātutoda pipīlaḥ sarpa uta vā śvāpadaḥ |
18,3.55c agniṣ ṭad viśvād agadaṃ kṛṇotu somaś ca yo brāhmaṇāṃ āviveśa ||55||

18,3.56a payasvatīr oṣadhayaḥ payasvan māmakaṃ payaḥ |
18,3.56c apāṃ payaso yat payas tena mā saha śumbhatu ||56||

18,3.57a imā nārīr avidhavāḥ supatnīr āñjanena sarpiṣā saṃ spṛśantām |
18,3.57c anaśravo anamīvāḥ suratnā ā rohantu janayo yonim agre ||57||

18,3.58a saṃ gachasva pitṛbhiḥ saṃ yameneṣṭāpūrtena parame vyoman |
18,3.58c hitvāvadyaṃ punar astam ehi saṃ gachatāṃ tanvā suvarcāḥ ||58||

18,3.59a ye naḥ pituḥ pitaro ye pitāmahā ya āviviśur urv antarikṣam |
18,3.59c tebhyaḥ svarād asunītir no adya vathāvaśaṃ tanvaḥ kalpayāti ||59||

18,3.60a śaṃ te nīhāro bhavatu śaṃ te pruṣvāva śīyatām |
18,3.60c śītike śītikāvati hlādike hlādikāvati |
18,3.60e maṇḍūky apsu śaṃ bhuva imaṃ sv agniṃ śamaya ||60|| {18}

18,3.61a vivasvān no abhayaṃ kṛṇotu yaḥ sutrāmā jīradānuḥ sudānuḥ |
18,3.61c iheme vīrā bahavo bhavantu gomad aśvavan mayy astu puṣṭam ||61||

18,3.62a vivasvān no amṛtatve dadhātu paraitu mṛtyur amṛtaṃ na aitu |
18,3.62c imān rakṣatu puruṣān ā jarimṇo mo sv eṣām asavo yamaṃ guḥ ||62||

18,3.63a yo dadhre antarikṣe na mahnā pitṝṇāṃ kaviḥ pramatir matīnām |
18,3.63c tam arcata viśvamitrā havirbhiḥ sa no yamaḥ prataraṃ jīvase dhāt ||63||

18,3.64a ā rohata divam uttamām ṛṣayo mā bibhītana |
18,3.64c somapāḥ somapāyina idaṃ vaḥ kriyate havir aganma jvotir uttamam ||64||

18,3.65a pra ketunā bṛhatā bhāty agnir ā rodasī vṛṣabho roravīti |
18,3.65c divaś cid antād upamām ud ānaḍ apām upasthe mahiṣo vavardha ||65||

18,3.66a nāke suparṇam upa yat patantaṃ hrdā venanto abhyacakṣata tvā |
18,3.66c hiraṇyapakṣaṃ varuṇasya dūtaṃ yamasya yonau śakunaṃ bhuranyum ||66||

18,3.67a indra kratuṃ na ā bhara pitā putrebhyo yathā |
18,3.67c śikṣā ṇo asmin puruhūta yāmani jīvā jyotir aśīmahi ||67||
18,3.68a apūpāpihitān kumbhān yāṃs te devā adhārayan |
18,3.68c te te santu svadhāvanto madhumanto ghṛtaścutaḥ ||68||

18,3.69a yās te dhānā anukirāmi tilamiśrā svadhāvatīḥ |
18,3.69c tās te santu vibhvīḥ prabhvīs tās te yamo rājānu manyatām ||69||

18,3.70a punar dehi vanaspate ya eṣa nihitas tvayi |
18,3.70c yathā yamasya sādana āsātau vidathā vadan ||70||

18,3.71a ā rabhasva jātavedas tejasvad dharo astu te |
18,3.71c śarīram asya saṃ dahāthainaṃ dehi sukṛtām u loke ||71||
18,3.72a ye te pūrve parāgatā apare pitaraś ca ye |
18,3.72c tebhyo ghṛtasya kulyaitu śatadhārā vyundatī ||72||

18,3.73a etad ā roha vaya unmṛjānaḥ svā iha bṛhad u dīdayante |
18,3.73c abhi prehi madhyato māpa hāsthāḥ pitṝnāṃ lokaṃ prathamo yo atra ||73|| {19}



1ā rohata janitrīṃ jātavedasaḥ pitṛyānaiḥ saṃ va ā rohayāmi |
1avāḍ ḍhavyeṣito havyavāha ījānaṃ yuktāḥ sukṛtāṃ dhatta loke ||1||

1devā yajñam ṛtavaḥ kalpayanti haviḥ puroḍāśaṃ sruco yajñāyudhāni |
1tebhir yāhi pathibhir devayānair yair ījānāḥ svargaṃ yanti lokam ||2||

1ṛtasya panthām anu paśya sādhv aṅgirasaḥ sukṛto yena yanti |
1tebhir yāhi pathibhiḥ svargaṃ yatrādityā madhu bhakṣayanti tṛtīye nāke adhi vi śrayasva ||3||

1trayaḥ suparṇā uparasya māyū nākasya pṛṣṭhe adhi viṣṭapi śritāḥ |
1svargā lokā amṛtena viṣṭhā iṣam ūrjaṃ yajamānāya duhrām ||4||

1juhūr dādhāra dyām upabhṛd antarikṣaṃ dhruvā dādhāra pṛthivīṃ pratiṣṭhām |
1pratīmāṃ lokā ghṛtapṛṣṭhāḥ svargāḥ kāmaṃkāmaṃ yajamānāya duhrām ||5||

1dhruva ā roha pṛthivīṃ viśvabhojasam antarikṣam upabhṛd ā kramasva |
1juhu dyāṃ gacha yajamānena sākaṃ sruveṇa vatsena diśaḥ prapīnāḥ sarvā dhukṣvāhṛṇyamānaḥ ||6||
1tīrthais taranti pravato mahīr iti yajñakṛtaḥ sukṛto yena yanti |
1atrādadhur yajamānāya lokaṃ diśo bhūtāni yad akalpayanta ||7||

1aṅgirasām ayanaṃ pūrvo agnir ādityānām ayanaṃ gārhapatyo dakṣiṇānām ayanaṃ dakṣiṇāgniḥ |
1mahimānam agner vihitasya brahmaṇā samaṅgaḥ sarva upa yāhi śagmaḥ ||8||

1pūrvo agniṣ ṭvā tapatu śaṃ purastāc chaṃ paścāt tapatu gārhapatyaḥ |
1dakṣiṇāgniṣ ṭe tapatu śarma varmottarato madhyato antarikṣād diśodiśo agne pari pāhi ghorāt ||9||

18,4.10a yūyam agne śaṃtamābhis tanūbhir ījānam abhi lokaṃ svargam |
18,4.10c aśvā bhūtvā pṛṣṭivāho vahātha yatra devaiḥ sadhamādaṃ madanti ||10|| {20}

18,4.11a śam agne paścāt tapa śaṃ purastāc cham uttarāc cham adharāt tapainam |
18,4.11c ekas tredhā vihito jātavedaḥ samyag enaṃ dhehi sukṛtām u loke ||11||

18,4.12a śam agnayaḥ samiddhā ā rabhantāṃ prājāpatyaṃ medhyaṃ jātavedasaḥ |
18,4.12c śṛtaṃ kṛṇvanta iha māva cikṣipan ||12||

18,4.13a yajña eti vitataḥ kalpamāna ījānam abhi lokaṃ svargam |
18,4.13c tam agnayaḥ sarvahutaṃ juṣantāṃ prājāpatyaṃ medhyaṃ jātavedasaḥ ||13||

18,4.14a ījānaś citam ārukṣad agniṃ nākasya pṛṣṭhād divam utpatiṣyan |
18,4.14c tasmai pra bhāti nabhaso jyotiṣīmānt svargaḥ panthāḥ sukṛte devayānaḥ ||14||

18,4.15a agnir hotādhvaryuṣ ṭe bṛhaspatir indro brahmā dakṣiṇatas te astu |
18,4.15c huto 'yaṃ saṃsthito yajña eti yatra pūrvam ayanaṃ hutānām ||15||

18,4.16a apūpavān kṣīravāṃś carur eha sīdatu |
18,4.16c lokakṛtaḥ pathikṛto yajāmahe ye devānāṃ hutabhāgā iha stha ||16||

18,4.17a apūpavān dadhivāṃś carur eha sīdatu |
18,4.17c lokakṛtaḥ pathikṛto yajāmahe ye devānāṃ hutabhāgā iha stha ||17||

18,4.18a apūpavān drapsavāṃś carur eha sīdatu |
18,4.18c lokakṛtaḥ pathikṛto yajāmahe ye devānāṃ hutabhāgā iha stha ||18||

18,4.19a apūpavān ghṛtavāṃś carur eha sīdatu |
18,4.19c lokakṛtaḥ pathikṛto yajāmahe ye devānāṃ hutabhāgā iha stha ||19||

18,4.20a apūpavān māṃsavāṃś carur eha sīdatu |
18,4.20c lokakṛtaḥ pathikṛto yajāmahe ye devānāṃ hutabhāgā iha stha ||20|| {21}

18,4.21a apūpavān annavāṃś carur eha sīdatu |
18,4.21c lokakṛtaḥ pathikṛto yajāmahe ye devānāṃ hutabhāgā iha stha ||21||

18,4.22a apūpavān madhumāṃś carur eha sīdatu |
18,4.22c lokakṛtaḥ pathikṛto yajāmahe ye devānāṃ hutabhāgā iha stha ||22||

18,4.23a apūpavān rasavāṃś carur eha sīdatu |
18,4.23c lokakṛtaḥ pathikṛto yajāmahe ye devānāṃ hutabhāgā iha stha ||23||

18,4.24a apūpavān apavāṃś carur eha sīdatu |
18,4.24c lokakṛtaḥ pathikṛto yajāmahe ye devānāṃ hutabhāgā iha stha ||24||

18,4.25a apūpāpihitān kumbhān yāṃs te devā adhārayan |
18,4.25c te te santu svadhāvanto madhumanto ghṛtaścutaḥ ||25||

18,4.26a yās te dhānā anukirāmi tilamiśrāḥ svadhāvatīḥ |
18,4.26c tās te santūdbhvīḥ prabhvīs tās te yamo rājānu manyatām ||26||

18,4.27a akṣitiṃ bhūyasīm ||27||

18,4.28a drapsaś caskanda pṛthivīm anu dyām imaṃ ca yonim anu yaś ca pūrvaḥ |
18,4.28c samānaṃ yonim anu samcarantaṃ drapsam juhomy anu sapta hotrāḥ ||28||

18,4.29a śatadhāraṃ vāyum arkaṃ svarvidaṃ nṛcakṣasas te abhi cakṣate rayim |
18,4.29c ye pṛnanti pra ca yachanti sarvadā te duhrate dakṣiṇāṃ saptamātaram ||29||

18,4.30a kośaṃ duhanti kalaśaṃ caturbilam iḍāṃ dhenuṃ madhumatīṃ svastaye |
18,4.30c ūrjaṃ madantīm aditiṃ janeṣv agne mā hiṃsīḥ parame vyoman ||30|| {22}

18,4.31a etat te devaḥ savitā vāso dadāti bhartave |
18,4.31c tat tvaṃ yamasya rājye vasānas tārpyaṃ cara ||31||

18,4.32a dhānā dhenur abhavad vatso asyās tilo 'bhavat |
18,4.32c tāṃ vai yamasya rājye akṣitām upa jīvati ||32||

18,4.33a etās te asau dhenavaḥ kāmadughā bhavantu |
18,4.33c enīḥ śyenīḥ sarūpā virūpās tilavatsā upa tiṣṭhantu tvātra ||33||

18,4.34a enīr dhānā hariṇīḥ śyenīr asya kṛṣṇā dhānā rohiṇīr dhenavas te |
18,4.34c tilavatsā ūrjam asmai duhānā viśvāhā santv anapasphurantīḥ ||34||

18,4.35a vaiśvānare havir idaṃ juhomi sāhasraṃ śatadhāram utsam |
18,4.35c sa bibharti pitaraṃ pitāmahān prapitāmahān bibharti pinvamānaḥ ||35||

18,4.36a sahasradhāraṃ śatadhāram utsam akṣitaṃ vyacyamānaṃ salilasya pṛṣṭhe |
18,4.36c ūrjaṃ duhānam anapasphurantam upāsate pitaraḥ svadhābhiḥ ||36||

18,4.37a idaṃ kasāmbu cayanena citaṃ tat sajātā ava paśyateta |
18,4.37c martyo 'yam amṛtatvam eti tasmai gṛhān kṛṇuta yāvatsabandhu ||37||

18,4.38a ihaivaidhi dhanasanir ihacitta ihakratuḥ |
18,4.38c ihaidhi vīryavattaro vayodhā aparāhataḥ ||38||

18,4.39a putraṃ pautram abhitarpayantīr āpo madhumatīr imāḥ |
18,4.39c svadhāṃ pitṛbhyo amṛtaṃ duhānā āpo devīr ubhayāṃs tarpayantu ||39||

18,4.40a āpo agniṃ pra hiṇuta pitṝṃr upemaṃ yajñaṃ pitaro me juṣantām |
18,4.40c āsīnām ūrjam upa ye sacante te no rayiṃ sarvavīraṃ ni yachān ||40|| {23}

18,4.41a sam indhate amartyaṃ havyavāhaṃ ghṛtapriyam |
18,4.41c sa veda nihitān nidhīn pitṝn parāvato gatān ||41||

18,4.42a yaṃ te manthaṃ yam odananaṃ yan māṃsaṃ nipṛṇāmi te |
18,4.42c te te santu svadhāvanto madhumanto ghṛtaścutaḥ ||42||

18,4.43a yās te dhānā anukirāmi tilamiśrāḥ svadhāvatīḥ |
18,4.43c tās te santūdbhvīḥ prabhvīs tās te yamo rājānu manyatām ||43||

18,4.44a idaṃ pūrvam aparaṃ niyānaṃ yenā te pūrve pitaraḥ paretāḥ |
18,4.44c purogavā ye abhisāco asya te tvā vahanti sukṛtām u lokam ||44||

18,4.45a sarasvatīṃ devayanto havante sarasvatīm adhvare tāyamāne |
18,4.45c sarasvatīṃ sukṛto havante sarasvatī dāśuṣe vāryaṃ dāt ||45||

18,4.46a sarasvatīṃ pitaro havante dakṣiṇā yajñam abhinakṣamāṇāḥ |
18,4.46c āsadyāsmin barhiṣi mādayadhvam anamīvā iṣa ā dhehy asme ||46||

18,4.47a sarasvati yā sarathaṃ yayāthokthaiḥ svadhābhir devi pitṛbhir madantī |
18,4.47c sahasrārgham iḍo atra bhāgaṃ rāyas poṣaṃ yajamānāya dhehi ||47||

18,4.48a pṛthivīṃ tvā pṛthivyām ā veśayāmi devo no dhātā pra tirāty āyuḥ |
18,4.48c parāparaitā vasuvid vo astv adhā mṛtāḥ pitṛṣu saṃ bhavantu ||48||

18,4.49a ā pra cyavethām apa tan mṛjethāṃ yad vām abhibhā atrocuḥ |
18,4.49c asmād etam aghnyau tad vaśīyo dātuḥ pitṛṣv ihabhojanau mama ||49||

18,4.50a eyam agan dakṣiṇā bhadrato nā anena dattā sudughā vayodhāḥ |
18,4.50c yauvane jīvān upapṛñcatī jarā pitṛbhya upasaṃparāṇayād imān ||50|| {24}

18,4.51a idaṃ pitṛbhyaḥ pra bharāmi barhir jīvaṃ devebhya uttaraṃ stṛṇāmi |
18,4.51c tad ā roha puruṣa medhyo bhavan prati tvā jānantu pitaraḥ paretam ||51||

18,4.52a edaṃ barhir asado medhyo 'bhūḥ prati tvā jānantu pitaraḥ paretam |
18,4.52c yathāparu tanvaṃ saṃ bharasva gātrāṇi te brahmaṇā kalpayāmi ||52||

18,4.53a parṇo rājāpidhānaṃ carūṇām ūrjo balaṃ saha ojo na āgan |
18,4.53c āyur jīvebhyo vidadhad dīrghāyutvāya śataśāradāya ||53||

18,4.54a ūrjo bhāgo ya imaṃ jajānāśmānnānām ādhipatyaṃ jagāma |
18,4.54c tam arcata viśvamitrā havirbhiḥ sa no yamaḥ prataraṃ jīvase dhāt ||54||

18,4.55a yathā yamāya harmyam avapan pañca mānavāḥ |
18,4.55c evā vapāmi harmyaṃ yathā me bhūrayo 'sata ||55||

18,4.56a idaṃ hiraṇyaṃ bibhṛhi yat te pitābibhaḥ purā |
18,4.56c svargaṃ yataḥ pitur hastaṃ nir mṛḍḍhi dakṣiṇam ||56||

18,4.57a ye ca jīvā ye ca mṛtā ye jātā ye ca yajñiyāḥ |
18,4.57c tebhyo ghṛtasya kulyaitu madhudhārā vyundatī ||57||

18,4.58a vṛṣā matīnāṃ pavate vicakṣaṇaḥ sūro ahnāṃ pratarītoṣasāṃ divaḥ |
18,4.58c prāṇaḥ sindhūnāṃ kalaśāṃ acikradad indrasya hārdim āviśan manīṣayā ||58||

18,4.59a tveṣas te dhūma ūrṇotu divi ṣaṃ chukra ātataḥ |
18,4.59c sūro na hi dyutā tvaṃ kṛpā pāvaka rocase ||59||

18,4.60a pra vā etīndur indrasya niṣkṛtiṃ sakhā sakhyur na pra mināti saṃgiraḥ |
18,4.60c marya iva yoṣāḥ sam arṣase somaḥ kalaśe śatayāmanā pathā ||60|| {25}

18,4.61a akṣann amīmadanta hy ava priyāṃ adhūṣata |
18,4.61c astoṣata svabhānavo viprā yaviṣṭhā īmahe ||61||

18,4.62a ā yāta pitaraḥ somyāso gambhīraiḥ pathibhiḥ pitṛyāṇaiḥ |
18,4.62c āyur asmabhyaṃ dadhataḥ prajāṃ ca rāyaś ca poṣair abhi naḥ sacadhvam ||62||

18,4.63a parā yāta pitaraḥ somyāso gambhīraiḥ pathibhiḥ pūryāṇaiḥ |
18,4.63c adhā māsi punar ā yāta no gṛhān havir attuṃ suprajasaḥ suvīrāḥ ||63||

18,4.64a yad vo agnir ajahād ekam aṅgaṃ pitṛlokaṃ gamayaṃ jātavedāḥ |
18,4.64c tad va etat punar ā pyāyayāmi sāṅgāḥ svarge pitaro mādayadhvam ||64||

18,4.65a abhūd dūtaḥ prahito jātavedāḥ sāyaṃ nyahna upavandyo nṛbhiḥ |
18,4.65c prādāḥ pitṛbhyaḥ svadhayā te akṣann addhi tvaṃ deva prayatā havīṃṣi ||65||

18,4.66a asau hā iha te manaḥ kakutsalam iva jāmayaḥ |
18,4.66c abhy enaṃ bhūma ūrṇuhi ||66||

18,4.67a śumbhantāṃ lokāḥ pitṛṣadanāḥ pitṛṣadane tvā loka ā sādayāmi ||67||

18,4.68a ye asmākaṃ pitaras teṣāṃ barhir asi ||68||

18,4.69a ud uttamaṃ varuṇa pāśam asmad avādhamaṃ śrathāya |
18,4.69c adhā vayam āditya vrate tavānāgaso aditaye syāma ||69||

18,4.70a prāsmat pāśān varuṇa muñca sarvān yaiḥ samāme badhyate yair vyāme |
18,4.70c adhā jīvema śaradaṃ śatāni tvayā rājan gupitā rakṣamāṇāḥ ||70|| {26}

18,4.71a agnaye kavyavāhanāya svadhā namaḥ ||71||

18,4.72a somāya pitṛmate svadhā namaḥ ||72||

18,4.73a pitṛbhyaḥ somavadbhyaḥ svadhā namaḥ ||73||

18,4.74a yamāya pitṛmate svadhā namaḥ ||74||
18,4.75a etat te pratatāmaha svadhā ye ca tvām anu ||75||

18,4.76a etat te tatāmaha svadhā ye ca tvām anu ||76||

18,4.77a etat te tata svadhā ||77||

18,4.78a svadhā pitṛbhyaḥ pṛthiviṣadbhyaḥ ||78||

18,4.79a svadhā pitṛbhyo antarikṣasadbhyaḥ ||79||

18,4.80a svadhā pitṛbhyo diviṣadbhyaḥ ||80|| {27}

18,4.81a namo vaḥ pitara ūrje namo vaḥ pitaro rasāya ||81||

18,4.82a namo vaḥ pitaro bhāmāya namo vaḥ pitaro manyave ||82||

18,4.83a namo vaḥ pitaro yad ghoraṃ tasmai namo vaḥ pitaro yat krūraṃ tasmai ||83||

18,4.84a namo vaḥ pitaro yac chivaṃ tasmai namo vaḥ pitaro yat syonaṃ tasmai ||84||

18,4.85a namo vaḥ pitaraḥ svadhā vaḥ pitaraḥ ||85||

18,4.86a ye 'tra pitaraḥ pitaro ye 'tra yūyaṃ stha yuṣmāṃs te 'nu yūyaṃ teṣāṃ śreṣṭhā bhūyāstha ||86||

18,4.87a ya iha pitaro jīvā iha vayaṃ smaḥ |
18,4.87c asmāṃs te 'nu vayaṃ teṣāṃ śreṣṭhā bhūyāsma ||87||

18,4.88a ā tvāgna idhīmahi dyumantaṃ devājaram |
18,4.88c yad gha sā te panīyasī samid dīdayati dyavi |
18,4.88e iṣaṃ stotṛbhya ā bhara ||88||

18,4.89a candramā apsv antar ā suparṇo dhāvate divi |
18,4.89c na vo hiraṇyanemayaḥ padaṃ vindanti vidyuto vittaṃ me asya rodasī ||89|| {28}



1saṃsaṃ sravantu nadyaḥ saṃ vātāḥ saṃ patatriṇaḥ |
1yajñam imaṃ vardhayatā giraḥ saṃsrāvyeṇa haviṣā juhomi ||1||

1imaṃ homā yajñam avatemaṃ saṃsrāvaṇā uta yajñam imaṃ vardhayatā giraḥ saṃsrāvyeṇa haviṣā juhomi ||2||

1rūpaṃrūpaṃ vayovayaḥ saṃrabhyainaṃ pari ṣvaje |
1yajñam imaṃ catasraḥ pradiśo vardhayantu saṃsrāvyeṇa haviṣā juhomi ||3||


1śaṃ ta āpo haimavatīḥ śam u te santūtsyāḥ |
1śaṃ te saniṣyadā āpaḥ śam u te santu varṣyāḥ ||1||

1śaṃ ta āpo dhanvanyāḥ śaṃ te santv anūpyāḥ |
1śaṃ te khanitrimā āpaḥ śaṃ yāḥ kumbhebhir ābhṛtāḥ ||2||

1anabhrayaḥ khanamānā viprā gambhīre apasaḥ |
1bhiṣagbhyo bhiṣaktarā āpo achā vadāmasi ||3||
1apām aha divyānām apāṃ srotasyānām |
1apām aha praṇejane 'śvā bhavatha vājinaḥ ||4||

1tā apaḥ śivā apo 'yakṣmaṃkaraṇīr apaḥ |
1yathaiva tṛpyate mayas tās ta ā datta bhesajīḥ ||5||



1divas pṛthivyāḥ pary antarikṣād vanaspatibhyo adhy oṣadhībhyaḥ |
1yatrayatra vibhṛto jātavedās tata stuto juṣamāṇo na ehi ||1||

1yas te apsu mahimā yo vaneṣu ya oṣadhīṣu paśuṣv apsv antaḥ |
1agne sarvās tanvaḥ saṃ rabhasva tābhir na ehi draviṇodā ajasraḥ ||2||

1yas te deveṣu mahimā svargo yā te tanuḥ pitṛṣv āviveśa |
1puṣṭir yā te manuṣyeṣu paprathe 'gne tayā rayim asmāsu dhehi ||3||

1śrutkarṇāya kavaye vedyāya vacobhir vākair upa yāmi rātim |
1yato bhayam abhayaṃ tan no astv ava devānāṃ yaja heḍo agne ||4||



1yām āhutiṃ prathamām atharvā yā jātā yā havyam akṛṇoj jātavedāḥ |
1tāṃ ta etāṃ prathamo johavīmi tābhiṣ ṭupto vahatu havyam agnir agnaye svāha ||1||

1ākūtiṃ devīṃ subhagāṃ puro dadhe cittasya mātā suhavā no astu |
1yām āśām emi kevalī sā me astu videyam enāṃ manasi praviṣṭām ||2||

1ākūtyā no bṛhaspata ākūtyā na upā gahi |
1atho bhagasya no dhehy atho naḥ suhavo bhava ||3||

1bṛhaspatir ma ākūtim āṅgirasaḥ prati jānātu vācam etām |
1yasya devā devatāḥ saṃbabhūvuḥ sa supraṇītāḥ kāmo anv etv asmān ||4||



1indro rājā jagataś carṣaṇīnām adhi kṣami viṣurūpaṃ yad asti |
1tato dadāti dāśuṣe vasūni codad rādha upastutaś cid arvāk ||1||



1sahasrabāhuḥ puruṣaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapāt |
1sa bhūmiṃ viśvato vṛtvāty atiṣṭhad daśāṅgulam ||1||

1tribhiḥ padbhir dyām arohat pād asyehābhavat punaḥ |
1tathā vy akrāmad viṣvaṅ aśanānaśane anu ||2||

1tāvanto asya mahimānas tato jyāyāṃś ca pūruṣaḥ |
1pādo 'sya viśvā bhūtāni tripād asyāmṛtaṃ divi ||3||

1puruṣa evedaṃ sarvaṃ yad bhūtaṃ yac ca bhāvyam |
1utāmṛtatvasyeśvaro yad anyenābhavat saha ||4||

1yat puruṣaṃ vy adadhuḥ katidhā vy akalpayan |
1mukhaṃ kim asya kim bāhū kim ūrū pādā ucyate ||5||

1brāhmaṇo 'sya mukham āsīd bāhū rājanyo 'bhavat |
1madhyaṃ tad asya yad vaiśyaḥ padbhyāṃ śūdro ajāyata ||6||

1candramā manaso jātaś cakṣoḥ sūryo ajāyata |
1mukhād indraś cāgniś ca prāṇād vāyur ajāyata ||7||

1nābhyā āsīd antarikṣaṃ śīrṣṇo dyauḥ sam avartata |
1padbhyāṃ bhūmir diśaḥ śrotrāt tathā lokāṃ akalpayan ||8||

1virāḍ agre sam abhavad virājo adhi pūruṣaḥ |
1sa jāto aty aricyata paścād bhūmim atho puraḥ ||9||

19,6.10a yat puruṣeṇa haviṣā devā yajñam atanvata |
19,6.10c vasanto asyāsīd ājyaṃ grīṣma idhmaḥ śarad dhaviḥ ||10||

19,6.11a taṃ yajñaṃ prāvṛṣā praukṣan puruṣaṃ jātam agraśaḥ |
19,6.11c tena devā ayajanta sādhyā vasavaś ca ye ||11||

19,6.12a tasmād aśvā ajāyanta ye ca ke cobhayādataḥ |
19,6.12c gāvo ha jajñire tasmāt tasmāj jātā ajāvayaḥ ||12||

19,6.13a tasmād yajñāt sarvahuta ṛcaḥ sāmāni jajñire |
19,6.13c chando ha jajñire tasmād yajus tasmād ajāyata ||13||

19,6.14a tasmād yajñāt sarvahutaḥ saṃbhṛtaṃ pṛṣadājyam |
19,6.14c paśūṃs tāṃś cakre vāyavyān āraṇyā grāmyāś ca ye ||14||

19,6.15a saptāsyāsan paridhayas triḥ sapta samidhaḥ kṛtāḥ |
19,6.15c devā yad yajñaṃ tanvānā abadhnan puruṣaṃ paśum ||15||

19,6.16a mūrdhno devasya bṛhato aṃśavaḥ sapta saptatīḥ |
19,6.16c rājñaḥ somasyājāyanta jātasya puruṣād adhi ||16||



1citrāṇi sākaṃ divi rocanāni sarīsṛpāṇi bhuvane javāni |
1turmiśaṃ sumatim ichamāno ahāni gīrbhiḥ saparyāmi nākam ||1||

1suhavam agne kṛttikā rohiṇī cāstu bhadraṃ mṛgaśiraḥ śam ārdrā |
1punarvasū sūnṛtā cāru puṣyo bhānur āśleṣā ayanaṃ maghā me ||2||

1puṇyaṃ pūrvā phalgunyau cātra hastaś citrā śivā svāti sukho me astu |
1rādhe viśākhe suhavānurādhā jyeṣṭhā sunakṣatram ariṣṭa mūlam ||3||

1annaṃ pūrvā rāsatāṃ me aṣādhā ūrjaṃ devy uttarā ā vahantu |
1abhijin me rāsatāṃ puṇyam eva śravaṇaḥ śraviṣṭhāḥ kurvatāṃ supuṣṭim ||4||

1ā me mahac chatabhiṣag varīya ā me dvayā proṣṭhapadā suśarma |
1ā revatī cāśvayujau bhagaṃ ma ā me rayiṃ bharaṇya ā vahantu ||5||



1yāni nakṣatrāṇi divy antarikṣe apsu bhūmau yāni nageṣu dikṣu |
1prakalpayaṃś candramā yāny eti sarvāṇi mamaitāni śivāni santu ||1||

1aṣṭāviṃśāni śivāni śagmāni saha yogaṃ bhajantu me |
1yogaṃ pra padye kṣemaṃ ca kṣemaṃ pra padye yogaṃ ca namo 'horātrābhyām astu ||2||

1svastitaṃ me suprātaḥ susāyaṃ sudivaṃ sumṛgaṃ suśakunaṃ me astu |
1suhavam agne svasty amartyaṃ gatvā punar āyābhinandan ||3||

1anuhavaṃ parihavaṃ parivādaṃ parikṣavam |
1sarvair me riktakumbhān parā tānt savitaḥ suva ||4||

1apapāpaṃ parikṣavaṃ puṇyaṃ bhakṣīmahi kṣavam |
1śivā te pāpa nāsikāṃ puṇyagaś cābhi mehatām ||5||

1imā yā brahmaṇas pate viṣucīr vāta īrate |
1sadhrīcīr indra tāḥ kṛtvā mahyaṃ śivatamās kṛdhi ||6||

1svasti no astv abhayaṃ no astu namo 'horatrābhyām astu ||7||



1śāntā dyauḥ śāntā pṛthivī śāntam idam urv antarikṣam |
1śāntā udanvatīr āpaḥ śāntā naḥ santv oṣadhīḥ ||1||

1śāntāni pūrvarūpāṇi śāntaṃ no astu kṛtākṛtam |
1śāntaṃ bhūtaṃ ca bhavyaṃ ca sarvam eva śam astu naḥ ||2||

1iyaṃ yā parameṣṭhinī vāg devī brahmasaṃśitā |
1yayaiva sasṛje ghoraṃ tayaiva śāntir astu naḥ ||3||

1idaṃ yat parameṣṭhinaṃ mano vāṃ brahmasaṃśitam |
1yenaiva sasṛje ghoraṃ tenaiva śāntir astu naḥ ||4||

1imāni yāni pañcendriyāni manaḥṣaṣṭhāni me hṛdi brahmaṇā saṃśitāni |
1yair eva sasṛje ghoraṃ tair eva śāntir astu naḥ ||5||

1śaṃ no mitraḥ śaṃ varuṇaḥ śaṃ viṣṇuḥ śaṃ prajāpatiḥ |
1śaṃ na indro bṛhaspatiḥ śaṃ no bhavatv aryamā ||6||

1śaṃ no mitraḥ śaṃ varuṇaḥ śaṃ vivasvāṃ cham antakaḥ |
1utpātāḥ pārthivāntarikṣāḥ śaṃ no divicarā grahāḥ ||7||

1śaṃ no bhūmir vepyamānā śam ulkā nirhataṃ ca yat |
1śaṃ gāvo lohitakṣīrāḥ śaṃ bhūmir ava tīryatīḥ ||8||

1nakṣatram ulkābhihataṃ śam astu naḥ śaṃ no 'bhicārāḥ śam u santu kṛtyāḥ |
1śaṃ no nikhātā valgāḥ śam ulkā deśopasargāḥ śam u no bhavantu ||9||

19,9.10a śaṃ no grahāś cāndramasāḥ śam ādityaś ca rāhuṇā |
19,9.10c śaṃ no mṛtyur dhūmaketuḥ śaṃ rudrās tigmatejasaḥ ||10||

19,9.11a śaṃ rudrāḥ śaṃ vasavaḥ śam ādityāḥ śam agnayaḥ |
19,9.11c śaṃ no maharṣayo devāḥ śaṃ devāḥ śaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ ||11||

19,9.12a brahma prajāpatir dhātā lokā vedāḥ saptaṛṣayo 'gnayaḥ |
19,9.12c tair me kṛtaṃ svastyayanam indro me śarma yachatu brahmā me śarma yachatu |
19,9.12e viśve me devāḥ śarma yachantu sarve me devāḥ śarma yachantu ||12||

19,9.13a yāni kāni cic chāntāni loke saptaṛṣayo viduḥ |
19,9.13c sarvāṇi śaṃ bhavantu me śaṃ me astv abhayaṃ me astu ||13||

19,9.14a pṛthivī śāntir antarikṣaṃ śāntir dyauḥ śāntir āpaḥ śāntir oṣadhayaḥ śāntir vanaspatayaḥ śāntir viśve me devāḥ śāntiḥ sarve me devāḥ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ śāntiḥ śāntibhiḥ |
19,9.14c yad iha ghoraṃ yad iha krūraṃ yad iha pāpaṃ tac chāntaṃ tac chivaṃ sarvam eva śam astu naḥ ||14||



1śaṃ na indrāgnī bhavatām avobhiḥ śaṃ na indrāvaruṇā rātahavyā |
1śam indrāsomā suvitāya śaṃ yoḥ śaṃ na indrāpūṣaṇā vājasātau ||1||

1śaṃ no bhagaḥ śam u naḥ śaṃso astu śaṃ naḥ puraṃdhiḥ śam u santu rāyaḥ |
1śaṃ naḥ satyasya suyamasya śaṃsaḥ śaṃ no aryamā purujāto astu ||2||

1śaṃ no dhātā śam u dhartā no astu śaṃ na urūcī bhavatu svadhābhiḥ |
1śaṃ rodasī bṛhatī śaṃ no adriḥ śaṃ no devānāṃ suhavāni santu ||3||

1śaṃ no agnir jyotiranīko astu śaṃ no mitrāvaruṇāv aśvinā śam |
1śaṃ naḥ sukṛtāṃ sukṛtāni santu śaṃ na iṣiro abhi vātu vātaḥ ||4||

1śaṃ no dyāvāpṛthivī pūrvahūtau śam antarikṣaṃ dṛśaye no astu |
1śaṃ na oṣadhīr vanino bhavantu śaṃ no rajasas patir astu jiṣṇuḥ ||5||

1śaṃ na indro vasubhir devo astu śam ādityebhir varuṇaḥ suśaṃsaḥ |
1śaṃ no rudro rudrebhir jalāṣaḥ śaṃ nas tvaṣṭā gnābhir iha śṛṇotu ||6||

1śaṃ naḥ somo bhavatu brahma śaṃ naḥ śaṃ no grāvāṇaḥ śam u santu yajñāḥ |
1śaṃ naḥ svarūnāṃ mitayo bhavantu śaṃ naḥ prasvaḥ śam v astu vediḥ ||7||

1śaṃ naḥ sūrya urucakṣā ud etu śaṃ no bhavantu pradiśaś catasraḥ |
1śaṃ naḥ parvatā dhruvayo bhavantu śaṃ naḥ sindhavaḥ śam u santv āpaḥ ||8||

1śaṃ no aditir bhavatu vratebhiḥ śaṃ no bhavantu marutaḥ svarkāḥ |
1śaṃ no viṣṇuḥ śam u pūṣā no astu śaṃ no bhavitraṃ śam v astu vāyuḥ ||9||

19,10.10a śaṃ no devaḥ savitā trāyamāṇaḥ śaṃ no bhavantūṣaso vibhātīḥ |
19,10.10c śaṃ naḥ parjanyo bhavatu prajābhyaḥ śaṃ naḥ kṣetrasya patir astu śaṃbhuḥ ||10||



1śaṃ naḥ satyasya patayo bhavantu śaṃ no arvantaḥ śam u santu gāvaḥ |
1śaṃ na ṛbhavaḥ sukṛtaḥ suhastāḥ śaṃ no bhavatu pitaro haveṣu ||1||

1śaṃ no devā viśvadevā bhavantu śaṃ sarasvatī saha dhībhir astu |
1śam abhiṣācaḥ śam u rātiṣācaḥ śaṃ no divyāḥ pārthivāḥ śaṃ no apyāḥ ||2||

1śaṃ no aja ekapād devo astu śam ahir budhnyaḥ śaṃ samudraḥ |
1śaṃ no apāṃ napāt perur astu śaṃ naḥ pṛṣṇir bhavatu devagopā ||3||

1ādityā rudrā vasavo juṣantām idaṃ brahma kriyamāṇaṃ navīyaḥ |
1sṛṇvantu no divyāḥ pārthivāso gojātā uta ye yajñiyāsaḥ ||4||

1ye devānām ṛtvijo yajñiyāso manor yajatrā amṛtā ṛtajñāḥ |
1te no rāsantām urugāyam adya yūyaṃ pāta svastibhiḥ sadā naḥ ||5||

1tad astu mitrāvaruṇā tad agne śaṃ yor asmabhyam idam astu śastam |
1aśīmahi gādham uta pratiṣṭhāṃ namo dive bṛhate sādanāya ||6||



1uṣā apa svasus tamaḥ saṃ vartayati vartaniṃ sujātatā |
1ayā vājaṃ devahitaṃ sanema madema śatahimāḥ suvīrāḥ ||1||



1indrasya bāhū sthavirau vṛṣāṇau citrā imā vṛṣabhau pārayiṣṇū |
1tau yokṣe prathamo yoga āgate yābhyāṃ jitam asurāṇāṃ svar yat ||1||

1āśuḥ śiśāno vṛṣabho na bhīmo ghanāghanaḥ kṣobhaṇaś carṣaṇīnām |
1saṃkrandano 'nimiṣa ekavīraḥ śataṃ senā ajayat sākam indraḥ ||2||

1saṃkrandanenānimiṣeṇa jiṣṇunāyodhyena duścyavanena dhṛṣṇunā |
1tad indreṇa jayata tat sahadhvaṃ yudho nara iṣuhastena vṛṣṇā ||3||

1sa iṣuhastaiḥ sa niṣaṅgibhir vaśī saṃsraṣṭā sa yudha indro gaṇena |
1saṃsṛṣṭajit somapā bāhuśardhy ugradhanvā pratihitābhir astā ||4||
1balavijñāyaḥ sthaviraḥ pravīraḥ sahasvān vājī sahamāna ugraḥ |
1abhivīro abhiṣatvā sahojij jaitram indra ratham ā tiṣṭha govidam ||5||

1imaṃ vīram anu harṣadhvam ugram indraṃ sakhāyo anu saṃ rabhadhvam |
1grāmajitaṃ gojitaṃ vajrabāhuṃ jayantam ajma pramṛṇantam ojasā ||6||

1abhi gotrāṇi sahasā gāhamāno 'dāya ugraḥ śatamanyur indraḥ |
1duścyavanaḥ pṛtanāṣāḍ ayodhyo 'smākaṃ senā avatu pra yutsu ||7||

1bṛhaspate pari dīyā rathena rakṣohāmitrāṃ apabādhamānaḥ |
1prabhañjaṃ chatrūn pramṛṇann amitrān asmākam edhy avitā tanūnām ||8||

1indra eṣāṃ netā bṛhaspatir dakṣiṇā yajñaḥ pura etu somaḥ |
1devasenānām abhibhañjatīnāṃ jayantīnāṃ maruto yantu madhye ||9||

19,13.10a indrasya vṛṣṇo varuṇasya rājña ādityānāṃ marutāṃ śardha ugram |
19,13.10c mahāmanasāṃ bhuvanacyavānāṃ ghoṣo devānāṃ jayatām ud asthāt ||10||

19,13.11a asmākam indraḥ samṛteṣu dhvajeṣv asmākaṃ yā iṣavas tā jayantu |
19,13.11c asmākaṃ vīrā uttare bhavantv asmān devāso 'vatā haveṣu ||11||



1idam ucchreyo 'vasānam āgāṃ śive me dyāvāpṛthivī abhūtām |
1asapatnāḥ pradiśo me bhavantu na vai tvā dviṣmo abhayaṃ no astu ||1||



1yata indra bhayāmahe tato no abhayaṃ kṛdhi |
1maghavaṃ chagdhi tava tvaṃ na ūtibhir vi dviṣo vi mṛdho jahi ||1||

1indraṃ vayam anūrādhaṃ havāmahe 'nu rādhyāsma dvipadā catuṣpadā |
1mā naḥ senā araruṣīr upa gur viṣūcir indra druho vi nāśaya ||2||

1indras trātota vṛtrahā parasphāno vareṇyaḥ |
1sa rakṣitā caramataḥ sa madhyataḥ sa paścāt sa purastān no astu ||3||

1uruṃ no lokam anu neṣi vidvānt svar yaj jyotir abhayaṃ svasti |
1ugrā ta indra sthavirasya bāhū upa kṣayema śaraṇā bṛhantā ||4||

1abhayaṃ naḥ karaty antarikṣam abhayaṃ dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe ime |
1abhayaṃ paścād abhayaṃ purastād uttarād adharād abhayaṃ no astu ||5||

1abhayaṃ mitrād abhayam amitrād abhayaṃ jñātād abhayaṃ puro yaḥ |
1abhayaṃ naktam abhayaṃ divā naḥ sarvā āśā mama mitraṃ bhavantu ||6||



1asapatnaṃ purastāt paścān no abhayaṃ kṛtam |
1savitā mā dakṣiṇata uttarān mā śacīpatiḥ ||1||

1divo mādityā rakṣatu bhūmyā rakṣantv agnayaḥ |
1indrāgnī rakṣatāṃ mā purastād aśvināv abhitaḥ śarma yachatām |
1tiraścīn aghnyā rakṣatu jātavedā bhūtakṛto me sarvataḥ santu varma ||2||



1agnir mā pātu vasubhiḥ purastāt tasmin krame tasmiṃ chraye tāṃ puraṃ praimi |
1sa mā rakṣatu sa mā gopāyatu tasmā ātmānaṃ pari dade svāhā ||1||

1vāyur māntarikṣeṇaitasyā diśaḥ pātu tasmin krame tasmiṃ chraye tāṃ puraṃ praimi |
1sa mā rakṣatu sa mā gopāyatu tasmā ātmānaṃ pari dade svāhā ||2||

1somo mā rudrair dakṣiṇāyā diśaḥ pātu tasmin krame tasmiṃ chraye tāṃ puraṃ praimi |
1sa mā rakṣatu sa mā gopāyatu tasmā ātmānaṃ pari dade svāhā ||3||

1varuṇo mādityair etasyā diśaḥ pātu tasmin krame tasmiṃ chraye tāṃ puraṃ praimi |
1sa mā rakṣatu sa mā gopāyatu tasmā ātmānam pari dade svāhā ||4||

1sūryo mā dyāvāpṛthivībhyāṃ pratīcyā diśaḥ pātu tasmin krame tasmiṃ chraye tāṃ puraṃ praimi |
1sa mā rakṣatu sa mā gopāyatu tasmā ātmānaṃ pari dade svāhā ||5||

1āpo mauṣadhīmatīr etasyā diśaḥ pāntu tāsu krame tāsu śraye tāṃ puraṃ praimi |
1tā mā rakṣantu tā mā gopāyantu tābhya ātmānaṃ pari dade svāhā ||6||

1viśvakarmā mā saptaṛṣibhir udīcyā diśaḥ pātu tasmin krame tasmiṃ chraye tāṃ puraṃ praimi |
1sa mā rakṣatu sa mā gopāyatu tasmā ātmānaṃ pari dade svāhā ||7||

1indro mā marutvān etasyā diśaḥ pātu tasmin krame tasmiṃ chraye tāṃ puraṃ praimi |
1sa mā rakṣatu sa mā gopāyatu tasmā ātmānaṃ pari dade svāhā ||8||

1prajāpatir mā prajananavānt saha pratiṣṭhayā dhruvāyā diśaḥ pātu tasmin krame tasmiṃ chraye tāṃ puraṃ praimi |
1sa mā rakṣatu sa mā gopāyatu tasmā ātmānaṃ pari dade svāhā ||9||
19,17.10a bṛhaspatir mā viśvair devair ūrdhvāyā diśaḥ pātu tasmin krame tasmiṃ chraye tāṃ puraṃ praimi |
19,17.10c sa mā rakṣatu sa mā gopāyatu tasmā ātmānaṃ pari dade svāhā ||10||



1agniṃ te vasuvantam ṛchantu |
1ye māghāyavaḥ prācyā diśo 'bhidāsān ||1||

1vāyuṃ te 'ntarikṣavantam ṛchantu |
1ye māghāyava etasyā diśo 'bhidāsān ||2||

1somaṃ te rudravantam ṛchantu |
1ye māghāyavo dakṣiṇāyā diśo 'bhidāsān ||3||

1varuṇaṃ ta ādityavantam ṛchantu |
1ye māghāyava etasyā diśo 'bhidāsān ||4||

1sūryaṃ te dyāvāpṛthivīvantam ṛchantu |
1ye māghāyava pratīcyā diśo 'bhidāsān ||5||

1apas ta oṣadhīmatīr ṛchantu |
1ye māghāyava etasyā diśo 'bhidāsān ||6||

1viśvakarmāṇaṃ te saptaṛṣivantam ṛchantu |
1ye māghāyava udīcyā diśo 'bhidāsān ||7||

1indraṃ te marutvantam ṛchantu |
1ye māghāyava etasyā diśo 'bhidāsān ||8||

1prajāpatiṃ te prajananavantam ṛchantu |
1ye māghāyavo dhruvāyā diśo 'bhidāsān ||9||

19,18.10a bṛhaspatiṃ te viśvadevavantam ṛchantu |
19,18.10c ye māghāyava ūrdhvāyā diśo 'bhidāsān ||10||



1mitraḥ pṛthivyod akrāmat tāṃ puraṃ pra ṇayāmi vaḥ |
1tām ā viśata tāṃ pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yachatu ||1||

1vāyur antarikṣeṇod akrāmat tāṃ puraṃ pra ṇayāmi vaḥ |
1tām ā viśata tāṃ pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yachatu ||2||

1sūryo divod akrāmat tāṃ puraṃ pra ṇayāmi vaḥ |
1tām ā viśata tāṃ pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yachatu ||3||

1candramā nakṣatrair ud akrāmat tāṃ puraṃ pra ṇayāmi vaḥ |
1tām ā viśata tāṃ pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yachatu ||4||

1soma oṣadhībhir ud akrāmat tāṃ puraṃ pra ṇayāmi vaḥ |
1tām ā viśata tāṃ pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yachatu ||5||

1yajño dakṣiṇābhir ud akrāmat tāṃ puraṃ pra ṇayāmi vaḥ |
1tām ā viśata tāṃ pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yachatu ||6||

1samudro nadībhir ud akrāmat tāṃ puraṃ pra ṇayāmi vaḥ |
1tām ā viśata tāṃ pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yachatu ||7||

1brahma brahmacāribhir ud akrāmat tāṃ puraṃ pra ṇayāmi vaḥ |
1tām ā viśata tāṃ pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yachatu ||8||

1indro vīryeṇod akrāmat tāṃ puraṃ pra ṇayāmi vaḥ |
1tām ā viśata tāṃ pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yachatu ||9||

19,19.10a devā amṛtenod akrāmaṃs tāṃ puraṃ pra ṇayāmi vaḥ |
19,19.10c tām ā viśata tāṃ pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yachatu ||10||

19,19.11a prajāpatiḥ prajābhir ud akrāmat tāṃ puraṃ pra ṇayāmi vaḥ |
19,19.11c tām ā viśata tāṃ pra viśata sā vaḥ śarma ca varma ca yachatu ||11||



1apa nyadhuḥ pauruṣeyaṃ vadhaṃ yam indrāgnī dhātā savitā bṛhaspatiḥ |
1somo rājā varuṇo aśvinā yamaḥ pūṣāsmān pari pātu mṛtyoḥ ||1||

1yāni cakāra bhuvanasya yas patiḥ prajāpatir mātariśvā prajābhyaḥ |
1pradiśo yāni vasate diśaś ca tāni me varmāṇi bahulāni santu ||2||

1yat te tanūṣv anahyanta devā dyurājayo dehinaḥ |
1indro yac cakre varma tad asmān pātu viśvataḥ ||3||

1varma me dyāvāpṛthivī varmāhar varma sūryaḥ |
1varma me viśve devāḥ kran mā mā prāpat pratīcikā ||4||



1gāyatry uṣṇig anuṣṭub bṛhatī paṅktis triṣṭub jagatyai ||1||



1āṅgirasānām ādyaiḥ pañcānuvākaiḥ svāhā ||1||

1ṣaṣṭhāya svāhā ||2||

1dvitīyebhyaḥ śaṅkhebhyaḥ svāhā ||9||

19,22.21c bhūtānāṃ brahmā prathamota jajñe tenārhati brahmaṇā spardhituṃ kaḥ ||21||



1ātharvaṇānāṃ caturṛcebhyaḥ svāhā ||1||
