1yena devaṃ savitāraṃ pari devā adhārayan |
1tenemaṃ brahmaṇas pate pari rāṣṭrāya dhattana ||1||

1parīmam indram āyuṣe mahe kṣatrāya dhattana |
1yathainaṃ jarase nayāj jyok kṣatre 'dhi jāgarat ||2||

1parīmam indram āyuṣe mahe śrotrāya dhattana |
1yathainaṃ jarase nayāj jyok śrotre 'dhi jāgarat ||3||

1pari dhatta dhatta no varcasemaṃ jarāmṛtyuṃ kṛṇuta dīrgham āyuḥ |
1bṛhaspatiḥ prāyachad vāsa etat somāya rājñe paridhātavā u ||4||
1jarāṃ su gacha pari dhatsva vāso bhavā gṛṣṭīnām abhiśastipā u |
1śataṃ ca jīva śaradaḥ purūcī rāyaś ca poṣam upasaṃvyayasva ||5||

1parīdaṃ vāso adhithāḥ svastaye 'bhūr vāpīnām abhiśastipā u |
1śataṃ ca jīva śaradaḥ purūcīr vasūni cārur vi bhajāsi jīvan ||6||

1yogeyoge tavastaraṃ vājevāje havāmahe |
1sakhāya indram ūtaye ||7||

1hiraṇyavarṇo ajaraḥ suvīro jarāmṛtyuḥ prajayā saṃ viśasva |
1tad agnir āha tad u soma āha bṛhaspatiḥ savitā tad indraḥ ||8||



1aśrāntasya tvā manasā yunajmi prathamasya ca |
1utkūlam udvaho bhavoduhya prati dhāvatāt ||1||


1agneḥ prajātaṃ pari yad dhiraṇyam amṛtaṃ dadhre adhi martyeṣu |
1ya enad veda sa id enam arhati jarāmṛtyur bhavati yo bibharti ||1||

1yad dhiraṇyaṃ sūryeṇa suvarṇam prajāvanto manavaḥ pūrva īṣire |
1tat tvā candraṃ varcasā saṃ sṛjaty āyuṣmān bhavati yo bibharti ||2||

1āyuṣe tvā varcase tvaujase ca balāya ca |
1yathā hiraṇyatejasā vibhāsāsi janāṃ anu ||3||

1yad veda rājā varuṇo veda devo bṛhaspatiḥ |
1indro yad vṛtrahā veda tat ta āyuṣyaṃ bhuvat tat te varcasyaṃ bhuvat ||4||


1gobhiṣ ṭvā pātv ṛṣabho vṛṣā tvā pātu vājibhiḥ |
1vāyuṣ ṭvā brahmaṇā pātv indras tvā pātv indriyaiḥ ||1||

1somas tvā pātv oṣadhībhir nakṣatraiḥ pātu sūryaḥ |
1mādbhyas tvā candro vṛtrahā vātaḥ prāṇena rakṣatu ||2||

1tisro divas tisraḥ pṛthivīs trīṇy antarikṣāṇi caturaḥ samudrān |
1trivṛtaṃ stomaṃ trivṛta āpa āhus tās tvā rakṣantu trivṛtā trivṛdbhiḥ ||3||

1trīn nākāṃs trīn samudrāṃs trīn bradhnāṃs trīn vaiṣṭapān |
1trīn mātariśvanas trīnt sūryān goptṝn kalpayāmi te ||4||

1ghṛtena tvā sam ukṣāmy agne ājyena vardhayan |
1agneś candrasya sūryasya mā prāṇaṃ māyino dabhan ||5||

1mā vaḥ prāṇaṃ mā vo 'pānaṃ mā haro māyino dabhan |
1bhrājanto viśvavedaso devā daivyena dhāvata ||6||

1prāṇenāgniṃ saṃ sṛjati vātaḥ prāṇena saṃhitaḥ |
1prāṇena viśvatomukhaṃ sūryaṃ devā ajanayan ||7||

1āyuṣāyuḥkṛtāṃ jīvāyuṣmān jīva mā mṛthāḥ |
1prāṇenātmanvatām jīva mā mṛtyor ud agā vaśam ||8||

1devānāṃ nihitaṃ nidhiṃ yam indro 'nvavindat pathibhir devayānaiḥ |
1āpo hiraṇyaṃ jugupus trivṛdbhis tās tvā rakṣantu trivṛtā trivṛdbhiḥ ||9||

19,27.10a trayastriṃśad devatās trīṇi ca vīryāṇi priyāyamāṇā jugupur apsv antaḥ |
19,27.10c asmiṃś candre adhi yad dhiraṇyaṃ tenāyaṃ kṛṇavad vīryāṇi ||10||

19,27.11a ye devā divy ekādaśa stha te devāso havir idaṃ juṣadhvam ||11||

19,27.12a ye devā antarikṣa ekādaśa stha te devāso havir idaṃ juṣadhvam ||12||

19,27.13a ye devā pṛthivyām ekādaśa stha te devāso havir idaṃ juṣadhvam ||13||

19,27.14a asapatnaṃ purastāt paścān no abhayaṃ kṛtam |
19,27.14c savitā mā dakṣiṇata uttarān mā śacīpatiḥ ||14||

19,27.15a divo mādityā rakṣantu bhūmyā rakṣantv agnayaḥ |
19,27.15c indrāgnī rakṣatāṃ mā purastād aśvināv abhitaḥ śarma yachatām |
19,27.15e tiraścīn aghnyā rakṣatu jātavedā bhūtakṛto me sarvataḥ santu varma ||15||



1imaṃ badhnāmi te maṇiṃ dīrghāyutvāya tejase |
1darbhaṃ sapatnadambhanaṃ dviṣatas tapanaṃ hṛdaḥ ||1||

1dviṣatas tāpayan hṛdaḥ śatrūṇāṃ tāpayan manaḥ |
1durhārdaḥ sarvāṃs tvaṃ darbha gharma ivābhīnt saṃtāpayan ||2||

1gharma ivābhitapan darbha dviṣato nitapan maṇe |
1hṛdaḥ sapatnānāṃ bhinddhīndra iva virujaṃ balam ||3||

1bhinddhi darbha sapatnānāṃ hṛdayaṃ dviṣatāṃ maṇe |
1udyan tvacam iva bhūmyāḥ śira eṣāṃ vi pātaya ||4||

1bhinddhi darbha sapatnān me bhinddhi me pṛtanāyataḥ |
1bhinddhi me sarvān durhārdo bhinddhi me dviṣato maṇe ||5||

1chinddhi darbha sapatnān me chinddhi me pṛtanāyataḥ |
1chinddhi me sarvān durhārdo chinddhi me dviṣato maṇe ||6||

1vṛśca darbha sapatnān me vṛśca me pṛtanāyataḥ |
1vṛśca me sarvān durhārdo vṛśca me dviṣato maṇe ||7||

1kṛnta darbha sapatnān me kṛnta me pṛtanāyataḥ |
1kṛnta me sarvān durhārdo kṛnta me dviṣato maṇe ||8||

1piṃśa darbha sapatnān me piṃśa me pṛtanāyataḥ |
1piṃśa me sarvān durhārdo piṃśa me dviṣato maṇe ||9||

19,28.10a vidhya darbha sapatnān me vidhya me pṛtanāyataḥ |
19,28.10c vidhya me sarvān durhārdo vidhya me dviṣato maṇe ||10||



1nikṣa darbha sapatnān me nikṣa me pṛtanāyataḥ |
1nikṣa me sarvān durhārdo nikṣa me dviṣato maṇe ||1||

1tṛnddhi darbha sapatnān me tṛnddhi me pṛtanāyataḥ |
1tṛnddhi me sarvān durhārdo tṛnddhi me dviṣato maṇe ||2||

1runddhi darbha sapatnān me runddhi me pṛtanāyataḥ |
1runddhi me sarvān durhārdo runddhi me dviṣato maṇe ||3||

1mṛṇa darbha sapatnān me mṛṇa me pṛtanāyataḥ |
1mṛṇa me sarvān durhārdo mṛṇa me dviṣato maṇe ||4||

1mantha darbha sapatnān me mantha me pṛtanāyataḥ |
1mantha me sarvān durhārdo mantha me dviṣato maṇe ||5||

1piṇḍḍhi darbha sapatnān me piṇḍḍhi me pṛtanāyataḥ |
1piṇḍḍhi me sarvān durhārdo piṇḍḍhi me dviṣato maṇe ||6||

1oṣa darbha sapatnān me oṣa me pṛtanāyataḥ |
1oṣa me sarvān durhārdo oṣa me dviṣato maṇe ||7||

1daha darbha sapatnān me daha me pṛtanāyataḥ |
1daha me sarvān durhārdo daha me dviṣato maṇe ||8||

1jahi darbha sapatnān me jahi me pṛtanāyataḥ |
1jahi me sarvān durhārdo jahi me dviṣato maṇe ||9||



1yat te darbha jarāmṛtyu śataṃ varmasu varma te |
1tenemaṃ varmiṇaṃ kṛtvā sapatnāṃ jahi vīryaiḥ ||1||

1śataṃ te darbha varmāṇi sahasraṃ vīryāṇi te |
1tam asmai viśve tvāṃ devā jarase bhartavā aduḥ ||2||

1tvām āhur devavarma tvāṃ darbha brahmaṇas patim |
1tvām indrasyāhur varma tvaṃ rāṣṭrāṇi rakṣasi ||3||

1sapatnakṣayaṇaṃ darbha dviṣatas tapanaṃ hṛdaḥ |
1maṇiṃ kṣatrasya vardhanaṃ tanūpānaṃ kṛṇomi te ||4||

1yat samudro abhyakrandat parjanyo vidyutā saha |
1tato hiranyayo bindus tato darbho ajāyata ||5||



1audumbareṇa maṇinā puṣṭikāmāya vedhasā |
1paśūṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ sphātiṃ goṣṭhe me savitā karat ||1||

1yo no agnir gārhapatyaḥ paśūnām adhipā asat |
1audumbaro vṛṣā maṇiḥ saṃ mā sṛjatu puṣṭyā ||2||

1karīṣiṇīṃ phalavatīṃ svadhām irāṃ ca no gṛhe |
1audumbarasya tejasā dhātā puṣṭiṃ dadhātu me ||3||

1yad dvipāc ca catuṣpāc ca yāny annāni ye rasāḥ |
1gṛhṇe 'haṃ tv eṣāṃ bhūmānaṃ bibhrad audumbaraṃ maṇim ||4||
1puṣṭiṃ paśūnām pari jagrabhāhaṃ catuṣpadāṃ dvipadāṃ yac ca dhānyam |
1payaḥ paśūnāṃ rasam oṣadhīnāṃ bṛhaspatiḥ savitā me ni yachāt ||5||

1ahaṃ paśūnām adhipā asāni mayi puṣṭaṃ puṣṭapatir dadhātu |
1mahyam audumbaro maṇir draviṇāni ni yachatu ||6||

1upa maudumbaro maṇiḥ prajayā ca dhanena ca |
1indreṇa jinvito maṇir ā māgant saha varcasā ||7||

1devo maṇiḥ sapatnahā dhanasā dhanasātaye |
1paśor annasya bhūmānaṃ gavāṃ sphātiṃ ni yachatu ||8||

1yathāgre tvaṃ vanaspate puṣṭhyā saha jajñiṣe |
1evā dhanasya me sphātim ā dadhātu sarasvatī ||9||

19,31.10a ā me dhanaṃ sarasvatī payasphātiṃ ca dhānyam |
19,31.10c sinīvāly upā vahād ayaṃ caudumbaro maṇiḥ ||10||

19,31.11a tvaṃ maṇīṇām adhipā vṛṣāsi tvayi puṣṭaṃ puṣṭapatir jajāna |
19,31.11c tvayīme vājā draviṇāni sarvaudumbaraḥ sa tvam asmat sahasvārād ārād arātim amatiṃ kṣudhaṃ ca ||11||

19,31.12a grāmaṇīr asi grāmaṇīr utthāya abhiṣikto 'bhi mā siñca varcasā |
19,31.12c tejo 'si tejo mayi dhārayādhi rayir asi rayiṃ me dhehi ||12||

19,31.13a puṣṭir asi puṣṭyā mā sam aṅgdhi gṛhamedhī gṛhapatiṃ mā kṛṇu |
19,31.13c audumbaraḥ sa tvam asmāsu dhehi rayiṃ ca naḥ sarvavīraṃ ni yacha rāyas poṣāya prati muñce ahaṃ tvām ||13||

19,31.14a ayam audumbaro maṇir vīro vīrāya badhyate |
19,31.14c sa naḥ saniṃ madhumatīṃ kṛṇotu rayiṃ ca naḥ sarvavīram ni yachāt ||14||



1śatakāṇḍo duścyavanaḥ sahasraparṇa uttiraḥ |
1darbho ya ugra oṣadhis taṃ te badhnāmy āyuṣe ||1||

1nāsya keśān pra vapanti norasi tāḍam ā ghnate |
1yasmā achinnaparṇena darbhena śarma yachati ||2||

1divi te tūlam oṣadhe pṛthivyām asi niṣṭhitaḥ |
1tvayā sahasrakāṇḍenāyuḥ pra vardhayāmahe ||3||

1tisro divo aty atṛṇat tisra imāḥ pṛthivīr uta |
1tvayāhaṃ durhārdo jihvāṃ ni tṛṇadmi vacāṃsi ||4||

1tvam asi sahamāno 'ham asmi sahasvān |
1ubhau sahasvantau bhūtvā sapatnān sahiṣīvahi ||5||

1sahasva no abhimātiṃ sahasva pṛtanāyataḥ |
1sahasva sarvān durhārdaḥ suhārdo me bahūn kṛdhi ||6||

1darbheṇa devajātena divi ṣṭambhena śaśvad it |
1tenāhaṃ śaśvato janāṃ asanaṃ sanavāni ca ||7||

1priyaṃ mā darbha kṛṇu brahmarājanyābhyām śūdrāya cāryāya ca |
1yasmai ca kāmayāmahe sarvasmai ca vipaśyate ||8||

1yo jāyamānaḥ pṛthivīm adṛṃhad yo astabhnād antarikṣaṃ divaṃ ca |
1yaṃ bibhrataṃ nanu pāpmā viveda sa no 'yaṃ darbho varuṇo divā kaḥ ||9||

19,32.10a sapatnahā śatakāṇḍaḥ sahasvān oṣadhīnāṃ prathamaḥ saṃ babhūva |
19,32.10c sa no 'yaṃ darbhaḥ pari pātu viśvatas tena sākṣīya pṛtanāḥ pṛtanyataḥ ||10||



1sahasrārghaḥ śatakāṇḍaḥ payasvān apām agnir vīrudhāṃ rājasūyam |
1sa no 'yaṃ darbhaḥ pari pātu viśvato devo maṇir āyuṣā saṃ sṛjāti naḥ ||1||

1ghṛtād ullupto madhumān payasvān bhūmidṛṃho 'cyutaś cyāvayiṣṇuḥ |
1nudant sapatnān adharāṃś ca kṛṇvan darbhā roha mahatām indriyeṇa ||2||

1tvaṃ bhūmim aty eṣy ojasā tvaṃ vedyāṃ sīdasi cārur adhvare |
1tvāṃ pavitram ṛṣayo 'bharanta tvaṃ punīhi duritāny asmat ||3||
1tīkṣṇo rājā viṣāsahī rakṣohā viśvacarṣaṇiḥ |
1ojo devānāṃ balam ugram etat taṃ te badhnāmi jarase svastaye ||4||

1darbheṇa tvaṃ kṛṇavad vīryāṇi darbhaṃ bibhrad ātmanā mā vyathiṣṭhāḥ |
1atiṣṭhāya varcasādhānyānt sūrya ivā bhāhi pradiśaś catasraḥ ||5||



1jāṅgiḍo 'si jaṅgiḍo rakṣitāsi jaṅgidaḥ |
1dvipāc catuṣpād asmākaṃ sarvaṃ rakṣatu jaṅgidaḥ ||1||
1yā gṛtsyas tripañcāśīḥ śataṃ kṛtyākṛtaś ca ye |
1sarvān vinaktu tejaso 'rasāṃ jaṅgidas karat ||2||

1arasaṃ kṛtrimaṃ nādam arasāḥ sapta visrasaḥ |
1apeto jaṅgiḍāmatim iṣum asteva śātaya ||3||
1kṛtyādūṣaṇa evāyam atho arātidūṣaṇaḥ |
1atho sahasvāñ jaṅgiḍaḥ pra na āyumṣi tāriṣat ||4||

1sa jaṅgiḍasya mahimā pari ṇaḥ pātu viśvataḥ |
1viṣkandhaṃ yena sāsaha saṃskandham oja ojasā ||5||

1triṣ ṭvā devā ajanayan niṣṭhitaṃ bhūmyām adhi |
1tam u tvāṅgirā iti brāhmaṇāḥ pūrvyā viduḥ ||6||

1na tvā pūrvā oṣadhayo na tvā taranti yā navāḥ |
1vibādha ugro jaṅgiḍaḥ paripāṇaḥ sumaṅgalaḥ ||7||

1athopadāna bhagavo jāṅgiḍāmitavīrya |
1purā ta ugrā grasata upendro vīryaṃ dadau ||8||

1ugra it te vanaspata indra ojmānam ā dadhau |
1amīvāḥ sarvāś cātayaṃ jahi rakṣāṃsy oṣadhe ||9||

19,34.10a āśarīkaṃ viśarīkaṃ balāsaṃ pṛṣṭyāmayam |
19,34.10c takmānaṃ viśvaśāradam arasāṃ jaṅgiḍas karat ||10||



1indrasya nāma gṛhṇanta ṛsayo jaṅgidaṃ daduḥ |
1devā yaṃ cakrur bheṣajam agre viṣkandhadūṣaṇam ||1||

1sa no rakṣatu jaṅgiḍo dhanapālo dhaneva |
1devā yaṃ cakrur brāhmaṇāḥ paripāṇam arātiham ||2||

1durhārdaḥ saṃghoraṃ cakṣuḥ pāpakṛtvānam āgamam |
1tāṃs tvaṃ sahasracakṣo pratībodhena nāśaya paripāṇo 'si jaṅgiḍaḥ ||3||

1pari mā divaḥ pari mā pṛthivyāḥ pary antarikṣāt pari mā vīrudbhyaḥ |
1pari mā bhūtāt pari mota bhavyād diśodiśo jaṅgiḍaḥ pātv asmān ||4||

1ya ṛṣṇavo devakṛtā ya uto vavṛte 'nyaḥ |
1sarvāṃ stān viśvabheṣajo 'rasāṃ jaṅgiḍas karat ||5||



1śatavāro anīnaśad yakṣmān rakṣāṃsi tejasā |
1ārohan varcasā saha maṇir durṇāmacātanaḥ ||1||

1śṛṅgābhyāṃ rakṣo nudate mūlena yātudhānyaḥ |
1madhyena yakṣmaṃ bādhate nainaṃ pāpmāti tatrati ||2||

1ye yakṣmāso arbhakā mahānto ye ca śabdinaḥ |
1sarvāṃ durṇāmahā maṇiḥ śatavāro anīnaśat ||3||

1śataṃ vīrān ajanayac chataṃ yakṣmān apāvapat |
1durṇāmnaḥ sarvān hatvāva rakṣāṃsi dhūnute ||4||

1hiraṇyaśṛṅga ṛṣabhaḥ śātavāro ayaṃ maṇiḥ |
1durṇāmnaḥ sarvāṃs tṛdhvāva rakṣāṃsy akramīt ||5||

1śatam ahaṃ durṇāmnīnāṃ gandharvāpsarasāṃ śatam |
1śatam śaśvanvatīnāṃ śatavāreṇa vāraye ||6||


1idaṃ varco agninā dattam āgan bhargo yaśaḥ saha ojo vayo balam |
1trayastriṃśad yāni ca vīryāṇi tāny agniḥ pra dadātu me ||1||

1varca ā dhehi me tanvāṃ saha ojo vayo balam |
1indriyāya tvā karmaṇe vīryāya prati gṛhṇāmi śataśāradāya ||2||

1ūrje tvā balāya tvaujase sahase tvā |
1abhibhūyāya tvā rāṣṭrabhṛtyāya pary ūhāmi śataśāradāya ||3||

1ṛtubhyaṣ ṭvārtavebhyo mādbhyaḥ saṃvatsarebhyaḥ |
1dhātre vidhātre samṛdhe bhūtasya pataye yaje ||4||



1na taṃ yakṣmā arundhate nainaṃ śapatho aśnute |
1yaṃ bheṣajasya gulguloḥ surabhir gandho aśnute ||1||

1viṣvañcas tasmād yakṣmā mṛgā aśvā iverate |
1yad gulgulu saindhavaṃ yad vāpy asi samudriyam ||2||

1ubhayor agrabhaṃ nāmāsmā ariṣṭatātaye ||3||



1aitu devas trāyamāṇaḥ kuṣṭho himavatas pari |
1takmānaṃ sarvaṃ nāśaya sarvāś ca yātudhānyaḥ ||1||

1trīṇi te kuṣṭha nāmāni nadyamāro nadyāriṣaḥ |
1nadyāyaṃ puruṣo riṣat |
1yasmai paribravīmi tvā sāyaṃprātar atho divā ||2||

1jīvalā nāma te mātā jīvanto nāma te pitā |
1nadyāyaṃ puruṣo riṣat |
1yasmai paribravīmi tvā sāyaṃprātar atho divā ||3||

1uttamo asy oṣadhīnām anaḍvān jagatām iva vyāghraḥ śvapadām iva |
1nadyāyaṃ puruṣo riṣat |
1yasmai paribravīmi tvā sāyaṃprātar atho divā ||4||

1triḥ śāmbubhyo aṅgirebhyas trir ādityebhyas pari |
1trir jāto viśvadevebhyaḥ |
1sa kuṣṭho viśvabheṣajaḥ sākaṃ somena tiṣṭhati |

1aśvattho devasadanas tṛtīyasyām ito divi |
1tatrāmṛtasya cakṣaṇaṃ tataḥ kuṣṭho ajāyata |
1sa kuṣṭho viśvabheṣajaḥ sākaṃ somena tiṣṭhati |

1hiraṇyayī naur acarad dhiraṇyabandhanā divi |
1tatrāmṛtasya cakṣaṇaṃ tataḥ kuṣṭho ajāyata |
1sa kuṣṭho viśvabheṣajaḥ sākaṃ somena tiṣṭhati |

1yatra nāvaprabhraṃśanaṃ yatra himavataḥ śiraḥ |
1tatrāmṛtasya cakṣaṇaṃ tataḥ kuṣṭho ajāyata |
1sa kuṣṭho viśvabheṣajaḥ sākaṃ somena tiṣṭhati |

1yaṃ tvā veda pūrva ikṣvāko yaṃ vā tvā kuṣṭha kāmyaḥ |
1yaṃ vā vaso yam ātsyas tenāsi viśvabheṣajaḥ ||9||

19,39.10a śīrṣaśokaṃ tṛtīyakaṃ sadaṃdir yaś ca hāyanaḥ |
19,39.10c takmānaṃ viśvadhāvīryādharāñcaṃ parā suva ||10||


1yan me chidraṃ manaso yac ca vācaḥ sarasvatī manyumantaṃ jagāma |
1viśvais tad devaiḥ saha saṃvidānaḥ saṃ dadhātu bṛhaspatiḥ ||1||

1mā na āpo medhāṃ mā brahma pra mathiṣṭana |
1suṣyadā yūyaṃ syandadhvam upahūto 'haṃ sumedhā varcasvī ||2||

1mā no medhāṃ mā no dīkṣāṃ mā no hiṃsiṣṭaṃ yat tapaḥ |
1śivā naḥ śaṃ santv āyuṣe śivā bhavantu mātaraḥ ||3||

1yā naḥ pīparad aśvinā jyotiṣmatī tamas tiraḥ |
1tām asme rāsatām iṣam ||4||



1bhadram ichanta ṛṣayaḥ svarvidas tapo dīkṣām upaniṣedur agre |
1tato rāṣṭraṃ balam ojaś ca jātaṃ tad asmai devā upasaṃnamantu ||1||



1brahma hotā brahma yajñā brahmaṇā svaravo mitāḥ |
1adhvaryur brahmaṇo jāto brahmaṇo 'ntarhitaṃ haviḥ ||1||

1brahma sruco ghṛtavatīr brahmaṇā vedir uddhitā |
1brahma yajñasya tattvaṃ ca ṛtvijo ye haviṣkṛtaḥ |
1śamitāya svāhā ||2||

1aṃhomuce pra bhare manīṣām ā sutrāvṇe sumatim āvṛṇānaḥ |
1imam indra prati havyaṃ gṛbhāya satyāḥ santu yajamānasya kāmāḥ ||3||

1aṃhomucaṃ vrṣabhaṃ yajñiyānāṃ virājantaṃ prathamam adhvarāṇam |
1apāṃ napātam aśvinā huve dhiya indriyeṇa ta indriyaṃ dattam ojaḥ ||4||



1yatra brahmavido yānti dīkṣayā tapasā saha |
1agnir mā tatra nayatv agnir medhā dadhātu me |
1agnaye svāhā ||1||

1yatra brahmavido yānti dīkṣayā tapasā saha |
1vāyur mā tatra nayatu vāyuḥ praṇān dadhātu me vāyave svāhā ||2||

1yatra brahmavido yānti dīkṣayā tapasā saha |
1sūryo mā tatra nayatu cakṣuḥ sūryo dadhātu me |
1sūryāya svāhā ||3||

1yatra brahmavido yānti dīkṣayā tapasā saha |
1candro mā tatra nayatu manaś candro dadhātu me |
1candrāya svāhā ||4||

1yatra brahmavido yānti dīkṣayā tapasā saha |
1somo mā tatra nayatu payaḥ somo dadhātu me |
1somāya svāhā ||5||

1yatra brahmavido yānti dīkṣayā tapasā saha |
1indro mā tatra nayatu balam indro dadhātu me |
1indrāya svāhā ||6||

1yatra brahmavido yānti dīkṣayā tapasā saha |
1āpo mā tatra nayatv amṛtam mopa tiṣṭhatu |
1adbhyaḥ svāhā ||7||

1yatra brahmavido yānti dīkṣayā tapasā saha |
1brahmā mā tatra nayatu brahmā brahma dadhātu me |
1brahmaṇe svāhā ||8||



1āyuṣo 'si prataraṇaṃ vipraṃ bheṣajam ucyase |
1tad āñjana tvaṃ śaṃtāte śam āpo abhayaṃ kṛtam ||1||

1yo harimā jāyānyo 'ṅgabhedo viṣalpakaḥ |
1sarvaṃ te yakṣmam aṅgebhyo bahir nir hantv āñjanam ||2||

1āñjanaṃ pṛthivyāṃ jātaṃ bhadraṃ puruṣajīvanam |
1kṛṇotv apramāyukaṃ rathajūtim anāgasam ||3||

1prāṇa prāṇaṃ trāyasvāso asave mṛḍa |
1nirṛte nirṛtyā naḥ pāśebhyo muñca ||4||

1sindhor garbho 'si vidyutāṃ puṣpam |
1vātaḥ prāṇaḥ sūryaś cakṣur divas payaḥ ||5||

1devāñjana traikakuda pari mā pāhi viśvataḥ |
1na tvā taranty oṣadhayo bāhyāḥ parvatīyā uta ||6||

1vīdaṃ madhyam avāsṛpad rakṣohāmīvacātanaḥ |
1amīvāḥ sarvāś cātayan nāśayad abhibhā itaḥ ||7||

1bahv idaṃ rājan varuṇānṛtam āha pūruṣaḥ |
1tasmāt sahasravīrya muñca naḥ pary aṃhasaḥ ||8||

1yad āpo aghnyā iti varuṇeti yad ūcima |
1tasmāt sahasravīrya muñca naḥ pary aṃhasaḥ ||9||

19,44.10a mitraś ca tvā varuṇaś cānupreyatur āñjana |
19,44.10c tau tvānugatya dūraṃ bhogāya punar ohatuḥ ||10||



1ṛṇād ṛṇam iva saṃ naya kṛtyāṃ kṛtyākṛto gṛham |
1cakṣurmantrasya durhārdaḥ pṛṣṭīr api śṛṇāñjana ||1||

1yad asmāsu duṣvapnyaṃ yad goṣu yac ca no gṛhe |
1anāmagas taṃ ca durhārdaḥ priyaḥ prati muñcatām ||2||

1apām ūrja ojaso vāvṛdhānam agner jātam adhi jātavedasaḥ |
1caturvīraṃ parvatīyaṃ yad āñjanaṃ diśaḥ pradiśaḥ karad ic chivās te ||3||

1caturvīraṃ badhyata āñjanaṃ te sarvā diśo abhayās te bhavantu |
1dhruvas tiṣṭhāsi saviteva cārya imā viśo abhi harantu te balim ||4||

1ākṣvaikaṃ maṇim ekaṃ krṇuṣva snāhy ekenā pibaikam eṣām |
1caturvīraṃ nairṛtebhyaś caturbhyo grāhyā bandhebhyaḥ pari pātv asmān ||5||

1agnir māgnināvatu prāṇāyāpānāyāyuṣe varcasa ojase |
1tejase svastaye subhūtaye svāhā ||6||

1indro mendriyeṇāvatu prāṇāyāpānāyāyuṣe varcasa ojase |
1tejase svastaye subhūtaye svāhā ||7||

1somo mā saumyenāvatu prāṇāyāpānāyāyuṣe varcasa ojase |
1tejase svastaye subhūtaye svāhā ||8||

1bhago ma bhagenāvatu prāṇāyāpānāyāyuṣe varcasa ojase |
1tejase svastaye subhūtaye svāhā ||9||

19,45.10a maruto mā gaṇair avantu prāṇāyāpānāyuṣe varcasa ojase tejase |
19,45.10c svastaye subhūtaye svāhā ||10||


1prajāpatiṣ ṭvā badhnāt prathamam astṛtaṃ vīryāya kam |
1tat te badhnāmy āyuṣe varcasa ojase ca balāya cāstṛtas tvābhi rakṣatu ||1||

1ūrdhvas tiṣṭhatu rakṣann apramādam astṛtemam mā tvā dabhan paṇayo yātudhānāḥ |
1indra iva dasyūn ava dhūnuṣva pṛtanyataḥ sarvāṃ chatrūn vi ṣahasvāstṛtas tvābhi rakṣatu ||2||

1śataṃ ca na praharanto nighnanto na tastire |
1tasminn indraḥ pary adatta cakṣuḥ prāṇam atho balam astṛtas tvābhi rakṣatu ||3||

1indrasya tvā varmaṇā pari dhāpayāmo yo devānām adhirājo babhūva |
1punas tvā devāḥ pra ṇayantu sarve 'stṛtas tvābhi rakṣatu ||4||

1asmin maṇāv ekaśataṃ vīryāṇi sahasraṃ prāṇā asminn astṛte |
1vyāghraḥ śatrūn abhi tiṣṭha sarvān yas tvā pṛtanyād adharaḥ so astv astṛtas tvābhi rakṣatu ||5||

1ghṛtād ullupto madhumān payasvānt sahasraprāṇaḥ śatayonir vayodhāḥ |
1śambhūś ca mayobhūś corjasvāṃś ca payasvāṃś cāstṛtas tvābhi rakṣatu ||6||

1yathā tvam uttaro 'so asapatnaḥ sapatnahā |
1sajātānām asad vaśī tathā tvā savitā karad astṛtas tvābhi rakṣatu ||7||



1ā rātri pārthivaṃ rajaḥ pitur aprāyi dhāmabhiḥ |
1divaḥ sadāṃsi bṛhatī vi tiṣṭhasa ā tveṣaṃ vartate tamaḥ ||1||

1na yasyāḥ pāraṃ dadṛśe na yoyuvad viśvam asyāṃ ni viśate yad ejati |
1ariṣṭāsas ta urvi tamasvati rātri pāram aśīmahi bhadre pāram aśīmahi ||2||

1ye te rātri nṛcakṣaso draṣṭāro navatir nava |
1aśītiḥ santy aṣṭā uto te sapta saptatiḥ ||3||

1ṣaṣṭiś ca ṣaṭ ca revati pañcāśat pañca sumnayi |
1catvāraś catvāriṃśac ca trayas triṃśac ca vājini ||4||

1dvau ca te viṃśatiś ca te rātry ekādaśāvamāḥ |
1tebhir no adya pāyubhir nu pāhi duhitar divaḥ ||5||

1rakṣā mākir no aghaśaṃsa īśata mā no duḥśaṃsa īśata |
1mā no adya gavāṃ steno māvīnāṃ vṛka īśata ||6||

1māśvānāṃ bhadre taskaro mā nṛṇāṃ yātudhānyaḥ |
1paramebhiḥ pathibhi steno dhāvatu taskaraḥ |
1pareṇa datvatī rajjuḥ pareṇāghāyur arṣatu ||7||

1adha rātri tṛṣṭadhūmam aśīrṣāṇam ahiṃ kṛṇu |
1hanū vṛkasya jambhayā stenaṃ drupade jahi ||8||

1tvayi rātri vasāmasi svapiṣyāmasi jāgṛhi |
1gobhyo naḥ śarma yachāśvebhyaḥ puruṣebhyaḥ ||9||



1atho yāni ca yasmā ha yāni cāntaḥ parīṇahi |
1tāni te pari dadmasi ||1||

1rātri mātar uṣase naḥ pari dehi |
1uṣā no ahne pari dadātv ahas tubhyaṃ vibhāvari ||2||
1yat kiṃ cedaṃ patayati yat kiṃ cedaṃ sarīsṛpam |
1yat kiṃ ca parvatāyāsatvaṃ tasmāt tvaṃ rātri pāhi naḥ ||3||

1sā paścāt pāhi sā puraḥ sottarād adharād uta |
1gopāya no vibhāvari stotāras ta iha smasi ||4||

1ye rātrim anutiṣṭhanti ye ca bhūteṣu jāgrati |
1paśūn ye sarvān rakṣanti te na ātmasu jāgrati te naḥ paśuṣu jāgrati ||5||

1veda vai rātri te nāma ghṛtācī nāma vā asi |
1tāṃ tvāṃ bharadvājo veda sā no vitte 'dhi jāgrati ||6||



1iṣirā yoṣā yuvatir damūnā rātrī devasya savitur bhagasya |
1aśvakṣabhā suhavā saṃbhṛtaśrīr ā paprau dyāvāpṛthivī mahitvā ||1||

1ati viśvāny aruhad gambhiro varṣiṣṭham aruhanta śraviṣṭhāḥ |
1uśatī rātry anu sā bhadrābhi tiṣṭhate mitra iva svadhābhiḥ ||2||

1varye vande subhage sujāta ājagan rātri sumanā iha syām |
1asmāṃs trāyasva naryāṇi jātā atho yāni gavyāni puṣṭyā ||3||

1siṃhasya rātry uśatī pīṃṣasya vyāghrasya dvīpino varca ā dade |
1aśvasya bradhnaṃ puruṣasya māyuṃ puru rūpāṇi kṛṇuṣe vibhātī ||4||

1śivāṃ rātrim anusūryaṃ ca himasya mātā suhavā no astu |
1asya stomasya subhage ni bodha yena tvā vande viśvāsu dikṣu ||5||

1stomasya no vibhāvari rātri rājeva joṣase |
1asāma sarvavīrā bhavāma sarvavedaso vyuchantīr anūṣasaḥ ||6||

1śamyā ha nāma dadhiṣe mama dipsanti ye dhanā |
1rātrīhi tān asutapā ya steno na vidyate yat punar na vidyate ||7||

1bhadrāsi rātri camaso na viṣṭo viṣvaṅ gorūpaṃ yuvatir bibharṣi |
1cakṣuṣmatī me uśatī vapūmṣi prati tvaṃ divyā na kṣām amukthāḥ ||8||

1yo adya stena āyaty aghāyur martyo ripuḥ |
1rātrī tasya pratītya pra grīvāḥ pra śiro hanat ||9||

19,49.10a pra pādau na yathāyati pra hastau na yathāśiṣat |
19,49.10c yo malimlur upāyati sa saṃpiṣṭo apāyati |
19,49.10e apāyati svapāyati śuṣke sthāṇāv apāyati ||10||



1adha rātri tṛṣṭadhūmam aśīrṣāṇam ahiṃ kṛṇu |
1akṣau vṛkasya nir jahyās tena taṃ drupade jahi ||1||

1ye te rātry anaḍvāhas tīkṣṇaśṛṅgāḥ svāśavaḥ |
1tebhir no adya pārayāti durgāṇi viśvahā ||2||

1rātriṃrātrim ariṣyantas tarema tanvā vayam |
1gambhīram aplavā iva na tareyur arātayaḥ ||3||

1yathā śāmyākaḥ prapatann apavān nānuvidyate |
1evā rātri pra pātaya yo asmāṃ abhyaghāyati ||4||

1apa stenaṃ vāsayo goajam uta taskaram |
1atho yo arvataḥ śiro 'bhidhāya ninīṣati ||5||

1yad adya rātri subhage vibhajanty ayo vasu |
1yad etad asmān bhojaya yathed anyān upāyasi ||6||

1uṣase naḥ pari dehi sarvān rātry anāgasaḥ |
1uṣā no ahne ā bhajād ahas tubhyaṃ vibhāvari ||7||



1ayuto 'ham ayuto ma ātmāyutaṃ me cakṣur ayutaṃ me śrotram |
1ayuto me prāṇo 'yuto me 'pāno 'yuto me vyāno 'yuto 'haṃ sarvaḥ ||1||

1devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ prasūta ā rabhe ||2||



1kāmas tad agre sam avartata manaso retaḥ prathamaṃ yad āsīt |
1sa kāma kāmena bṛhatā sayonī rāyas poṣaṃ yajamānāya dhehi ||1||

1tvaṃ kāma sahasāsi pratiṣṭhito vibhur vibhāvā sakha ā sakhīyate |
1tvam ugraḥ pṛtanāsu sasahiḥ saha ojo yajamānāya dhehi ||2||

1dūrāc cakamānāya pratipāṇāyākṣaye |
1āsmā aśṛṇvann āśāḥ kāmenājanayant svaḥ ||3||

1kāmena mā kāma āgan hṛdayād dhṛdayaṃ pari |
1yad amīṣām ado manas tad aitūpa mām iha ||4||

1yat kāma kāmayamānā idaṃ kṛṇmasi te haviḥ |
1tan naḥ sarvaṃ sam ṛdhyatām athaitasya haviṣo vīhi svāhā ||5||



1kālo aśvo vahati saptaraśmiḥ sahasrākṣo ajaro bhūriretāḥ |
1tam ā rohanti kavayo vipaścitas tasya cakrā bhuvanāni viśvā ||1||

1sapta cakrān vahati kāla eṣa saptāsya nābhīr amṛtaṃ nv akṣaḥ |
1sa imā viśvā bhuvanāny añjat kālaḥ sa īyate prathamo nu devaḥ ||2||

1pūrṇaḥ kumbho 'dhi kāla āhitas taṃ vai paśyāmo bahudhā nu santam |
1sa imā viśvā bhuvanāni pratyaṅ kālaṃ tam āhuḥ parame vyoman ||3||

1sa eva saṃ bhuvanāny ābharat sa eva saṃ bhuvanāni pary ait |
1pitā sann abhavat putra eṣāṃ tasmād vai nānyat param asti tejaḥ ||4||

1kālo 'mūṃ divam ajanayat kāla imāḥ pṛthivīr uta |
1kāle ha bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ ceṣitaṃ ha vi tiṣṭhate ||5||

1kālo bhūtim asṛjata kāle tapati sūryaḥ |
1kāle ha viśvā bhūtāni kāle cakṣur vi paśyati ||6||

1kāle manaḥ kāle prāṇaḥ kāle nāma samāhitam |
1kālena sarvā nandanty āgatena prajā imāḥ ||7||

1kāle tapaḥ kāle jyeṣṭham kāle brahma samāhitam |
1kālo ha sarvasyeśvaro yaḥ pitāsīt prajāpateḥ ||8||

1teneṣitaṃ tena jātaṃ tad u tasmin pratiṣṭhitam |
1kālo ha brahma bhūtvā bibharti parameṣṭhinam ||9||

19,53.10a kālaḥ prajā asṛjata kālo agre prajāpatim |
19,53.10c svayaṃbhūḥ kaśyapaḥ kālāt tapaḥ kālād ajāyata ||10||



1kālād āpaḥ sam abhavan kālād brahma tapo diśaḥ |
1kālenod eti sūryaḥ kāle ni viśate punaḥ ||1||

1kālena vātaḥ pavate kālena pṛthivī mahī |
1dyaur mahī kāla āhitā ||2||

1kālo ha bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ ca putro ajanayat purā |
1kālād ṛcaḥ sam abhavan yajuḥ kālād ajāyata ||3||

1kālo yajñaṃ sam airayad devebhyo bhāgam akṣitam |
1kāle gandharvāpsarasaḥ kāle lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ ||4||

1kāle 'yam aṅgirā devo 'tharvā cādhi tiṣṭhataḥ |
1imaṃ ca lokaṃ paramaṃ ca lokaṃ puṇyāṃś ca lokān vidhṛtīś ca puṇyāḥ |
1sarvāṃl lokān abhijitya brahmaṇā kālaḥ sa īyate paramo nu devaḥ ||5||



1rātriṃrātrim aprayātaṃ bharanto 'śvāyeva tiṣṭhate ghāsam asmai |
1rāyas poṣeṇa sam iṣā madanto mā te agne prativeśā riṣāma ||1||

1yā te vasor vāta iṣuḥ sā ta eṣā tayā no mṛḍa |
1rāyas poṣeṇa sam iṣā madanto mā te agne prativeśā riṣāma ||2||

1sāyaṃsāyaṃ gṛhapatir no agniḥ prātaḥprātaḥ saumanasasya dātā |
1vasorvasor vasudāna edhi vayaṃ tvendhānās tanvaṃ puṣema ||3||

1prātaḥprātar gṛhapatir no agniḥ sāyaṃsāyaṃ saumanasasya dātā |
1vasorvasor vasudāna edhīndhānās tvā śataṃhimā ṛdhema ||4||

1apaścā dagdhānnasya bhūyāsam |
1annādāyānnapataye rudrāya namo agnaye |
1sabhyaḥ sabhāṃ me pāhi ye ca sabhyāḥ sabhāsadaḥ ||5||

1tvām indrā puruhūta viśvam āyur vy aśnavan |
1aharahar balim it te haranto 'śvāyeva tiṣṭhate ghāsam agne ||6||



1yamasya lokād adhy ā babhūvitha pramadā martyān pra yunakṣi dhīraḥ |
1ekākinā sarathaṃ yāsi vidvānt svapnaṃ mimāno asurasya yonau ||1||

1bandhas tvāgre viśvacayā apaśyat purā rātryā janitor eke ahni |
1tataḥ svapnedam adhy ā babhūvitha bhiṣagbhyo rūpam apagūhamānaḥ ||2||

1bṛhadgāvāsurebhyo 'dhi devān upāvartata mahimānam ichan |
1tasmai svapnāya dadhur ādhipatyaṃ trayastriṃśāsaḥ svar ānaśānāḥ ||3||

1naitāṃ viduḥ pitaro nota devā yeṣāṃ jalpiś caraty antaredam |
1trite svapnam adadhur āptye nara ādityāso varuṇenānuśiṣṭāḥ ||4||

1yasya krūram abhajanta duṣkṛto 'svapnena sukṛtaḥ puṇyam āyuḥ |
1svar madasi parameṇa bandhunā tapyamānasya manaso 'dhi jajñiṣe ||5||

1vidma te sarvāḥ parijāḥ purastād vidma svapna yo adhipā ihā te |
1yaśaśvino no yaśaseha pāhy ārād dviṣebhir apa yāhi dūram ||6||


1yathā kalāṃ yathā śaphaṃ yathā rṇaṃ samnayanti |
1evā duṣvapnyaṃ sarvam apriye saṃ nayāmasi ||1||

1saṃ rājāno aguḥ sam ṛṇāmy aguḥ saṃ kuṣṭhā aguḥ saṃ kalā aguḥ |
1sam asmāsu yad duṣvapnyaṃ nir dviṣate duṣvapnyaṃ suvāma ||2||

1devānāṃ patnīnāṃ garbha yamasya kara yo bhadraḥ svapna |
1sa mama yaḥ pāpas tad dviṣate pra hiṇmaḥ |
1mā tṛṣṭānām asi kṛṣṇaśakuner mukham ||3||

1taṃ tvā svapna tathā saṃ vidma sa tvaṃ svapnāśva iva kāyam aśva iva nīnāham |
1anāsmākaṃ devapīyuṃ piyāruṃ vapa yad asmāsu duṣvapnyaṃ yad goṣu yac ca no gṛhe ||4||

1anāsmākas tad devapīyuḥ piyārur niṣkam iva prati muñcatām |
1navāratnīn apamayā asmākaṃ tataḥ pari |
1duṣvapnyaṃ sarvaṃ dviṣate nir dayāmasi ||5||



1ghṛtasya jūtiḥ samanā sadevā saṃvatsaraṃ haviṣā vardhayantī |
1śrotraṃ cakṣuḥ prāṇo 'chinno no astv achinnā vayam āyuṣo varcasaḥ ||1||
1upāsmān prāṇo hvayatām upa prāṇaṃ havāmahe |
1varco jagrāha pṛthivy antarikṣaṃ varcaḥ somo bṛhaspatir vidhattā ||2||

1varcaso dyāvāpṛthivī saṃgrahaṇī babhūvathur varco gṛhītvā pṛthivīm anu saṃ carema |
1yaśasam gāvo gopatim upa tiṣṭhanty āyatīr yaśo gṛhītvā pṛthivīm anu saṃ carema ||3||

1vrajaṃ kṛṇudhvaṃ sa hi vo nṛpāṇo varmā sīvyadhvaṃ bahulā pṛthūni |
1puraḥ kṛṇudhvam āyasīr adhṛṣṭā mā vaḥ susroc camaso dṛṃhata tam ||4||

1yajñasya cakṣuḥ prabhṛtir mukhaṃ ca vācā śrotreṇa manasā juhomi |
1imaṃ yajñaṃ vitataṃ viśvakarmaṇā devā yantu sumanasyamānāḥ ||5||
1ye devānām ṛtvijo ye ca yajñiyā yebhyo havyaṃ kriyate bhāgadheyam |
1imaṃ yajñaṃ saha patnībhir etya yāvanto devās taviṣā mādayantām ||6||



1tvam agne vratapā asi deva ā martyeṣv ā |
1tvaṃ yajñeṣv īḍyaḥ ||1||

1yad vo vayaṃ pramināma vratāni viduṣāṃ devā aviduṣṭarāsaḥ |
1agniṣ ṭad viśvād ā pṛṇātu vidvānt somasya yo brāhmaṇāṃ āviveśa ||2||

1ā devānām api panthām aganma yac chaknavāma tad anupravoḍhum |
1agnir vidvānt sa yajāt sa id dhotā so 'dhvarānt sa ṛtūn kalpayāti ||3||



1vāṅ ma āsan nasoḥ prāṇaś cakṣur akṣṇoḥ śrotraṃ karṇayoḥ |
1apalitāḥ keśā aśoṇā dantā bahu bāhvor balam ||1||
1ūrvor ojo jaṅghayor javaḥ pādayoḥ |
1pratiṣṭhā ariṣṭāni me sarvātmānibhṛṣṭaḥ ||2||



1tanūs tanvā me sahe dataḥ sarvam āyur aśīya |
1syonaṃ me sīda puruḥ pṛṇasva pavamānaḥ svarge ||1||


1priyaṃ mā kṛṇu deveṣu priyaṃ rājasu mā kṛṇu |
1priyaṃ sarvasya paśyata uta śūdra utārye ||1||



1ut tiṣṭha brahmaṇas pate devān yajñena bodhaya |
1āyuḥ prāṇaṃ prajāṃ paśūn kīrtiṃ yajamānaṃ ca vardhaya ||1||


1agne samidham āhārṣaṃ bṛhate jātavedase |
1sa me śraddhāṃ ca medhāṃ ca jātavedāḥ pra yachatu ||1||

1idhmena tvā jātavedaḥ samidhā vardhayāmasi |
1tathā tvam asmān vardhaya prajayā ca dhanena ca ||2||

1yad agne yāni kāni cid ā te dārūṇi dadhmasi |
1sarvaṃ tad astu me śivaṃ taj juṣasva yaviṣṭhya ||3||

1etās te agne samidhas tvam iddhaḥ samid bhava |
1āyur asmāsu dhehy amṛtatvam ācāryāya ||4||



1hariḥ suparṇo divam āruho 'rciṣā ye tvā dipsanti divam utpatantam |
1ava tāṃ jahi harasā jātavedo 'bibhyad ugro 'rciṣā divam ā roha sūrya ||1||



1ayojālā asurā māyino 'yasmayaiḥ pāśair aṅkino ye caranti |
1tāṃs te randhayāmi harasā jātavedaḥ sahasraṛṣṭiḥ sapatnān pramṛṇan pāhi vajraḥ ||1||



1paśyema śaradaḥ śatam ||1||

1jīvema śaradaḥ śatam ||2||

1budhyema śaradaḥ śatam ||3||

1rohema śaradaḥ śatam ||4||

1pūṣema śaradaḥ śatam ||5||

1bhavema śaradaḥ śatam ||6||

1bhūṣema śaradaḥ śatam ||7||

1bhūyasīḥ śaradaḥ śatam ||8||



1avyasaś ca vyacasaś ca bilaṃ vi ṣyāmi māyayā |
1tābhyām uddhṛtya vedam atha karmāṇi kṛṇmahe ||1||



1jīvā stha jīvyāsaṃ sarvam āyur jīvyāsam ||1||

1upajīvā sthopa jīvyāsaṃ sarvam āyur jīvyāsam ||2||

1saṃjīvā stha saṃ jīvyāsaṃ sarvam āyur jīvyāsam ||3||

1jīvalā stha jīvyāsaṃ sarvam āyur jīvyāsam ||4||



1indra jīva sūrya jīva devā jīvā jīvyāsam aham |
1sarvam āyur jīvyāsam ||1||



1stutā mayā varadā vedamātā pra codayantāṃ pāvamānī dvijānām |
1āyuḥ prāṇaṃ prajāṃ paśuṃ kīrtiṃ draviṇaṃ brahmavarcasam |
1mahyaṃ dattvā vrajata brahmalokam ||1||



1yasmāt kośād udabharāma vedaṃ tasminn antar ava dadhma enam |
1kṛtam iṣṭaṃ brahmaṇo vīryeṇa tena mā devās tapasāvateha ||1||



2indra tvā vṛṣabhaṃ vayaṃ sute some havāmahe |
2sa pāhi madhvo andhasaḥ ||1||

2maruto yasya hi kṣaye pāthā divo vimahasaḥ |
2sa sugopātamo janaḥ ||2||

2ukṣānnāya vaśānnāya somapṛṣṭhāya vedhase |
2stomair vidhemāgnaye ||3||



2marutaḥ potrāt suṣṭubhaḥ svarkād ṛtunā somaṃ pibantu ||1||

2agnir āgnīdhrāt suṣṭubhaḥ svarkād ṛtunā somaṃ pibatu ||2||

2indro brahmā brāhmaṇāt suṣṭubhaḥ svarkād ṛtunā somaṃ pibatu ||3||

2devo draviṇodāḥ potrāt suṣṭubhaḥ svarkād ṛtunā somaṃ pibatu ||4||



2ā yāhi suṣumā hi ta indra somaṃ pibā imam |
2edaṃ barhiḥ sado mama ||1||

2ā tvā brahmayujā harī vahatām indra keśinā |
2upa brahmāṇi naḥ śṛṇu ||2||

2brahmāṇas tvā vayaṃ yujā somapām indra sominaḥ |
2sutāvanto havāmahe ||3||


2ā no yāhi sutāvato 'smākaṃ suṣṭutīr upa |
2pibā su śiprinn andhasaḥ ||1||

2ā te siñcāmi kukṣyor anu gātrā vi dhāvatu |
2gṛbhāya jihvayā madhu ||2||

2svāduṣ ṭe astu saṃsude madhumān tanve tava |
2somaḥ śam astu te hṛde ||3||


2ayam u tvā vicarṣaṇe janīr ivābhi saṃvṛtaḥ |
2pra soma indra sarpatu ||1||

2tuvigrīvo vapodaraḥ subāhur andhaso sade |
2indro vṛtrāṇi jighnate ||2||

2indra prehi puras tvaṃ viśvasyeśāna ojasā |
2vṛtrāṇi vṛtrahaṃ jahi ||3||

2dīrghas te astv aṅkuśo yenā vasu prayachasi |
2yajamānāya sunvate ||4||

2ayaṃ ta indra somo nipūto adhi barhiṣi |
2ehīm asya dravā piba ||5||

2śācigo śācipūjanāyaṃ raṇāya te sutaḥ |
2ākhaṇḍala pra hūyase ||6||

2yas te śṛṅgavṛṣo napāt praṇapāt kuṇḍapāyyaḥ |
2ny asmin dadhra ā manaḥ ||7||



2indra tvā vṛṣabhaṃ vayaṃ sute some havāmahe |
2sa pāhi madhvo andhasaḥ ||1||

2indra kratuvidaṃ sutaṃ somaṃ harya puruṣṭuta |
2pibā vṛṣasva tātṛpim ||2||

2indra pra ṇo dhitāvānaṃ yajñaṃ viśvebhir devebhir |
2tira stavāna viśpate ||3||

2indra somāḥ sutā ime tava pra yanti satpate |
2kṣayaṃ candrāsa indavaḥ ||4||

2dadhiṣvā jaṭhare sutaṃ somam indra vareṇyam |
2tava dyukṣāsa indavaḥ ||5||

2girvaṇaḥ pāhi naḥ sutaṃ madhor dhārābhir ajyase |
2indra tvādātam id yaśaḥ ||6||

2abhi dyumnāni vanina indraṃ sacante akṣitā |
2pītvī somasya vāvṛdhe ||7||

2arvāvato na ā gahi parāvataś ca vṛtrahan |
2imā juṣasva no giraḥ ||8||

2yad antarā parāvatam arvāvataṃ ca hūyase |
2indreha tata ā gahi ||9||



2ud ghed abhi śrutāmaghaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ naryāpasam |
2astāram eṣi sūrya ||1||

2nava yo navatiṃ puro bibheda bāhvojasā |
2ahiṃ ca vṛtrahāvadhīt ||2||

2sa na indraḥ śivaḥ sakhāśvāvad gomad yavamat |
2urudhāreva dohate ||3||

2indra kratuvidaṃ sutaṃ somaṃ harya puruṣṭuta |
2pibā vṛṣasva tātṛpim ||4||



2evā pāhi pratnathā mandatu tvā śrudhi brahma vāvṛdhasvota gīrbhiḥ |
2āviḥ sūryaṃ kṛṇuhi pīpihīṣo jahi śatrūṃr abhi gā indra tṛndhi ||1||

2arvāṅ ehi somakāmaṃ tvāhur ayaṃ sutas tasya pibā madāya |
2uruvyacā jaṭhara ā vṛṣasva piteva naḥ śṛṇuhi hūyamānaḥ ||2||

2āpūrṇo asya kalaśaḥ svāhā sekteva kośaṃ siṣice pibadhyai |
2sam u priyā āvavṛtran madāya pradakṣiṇid abhi somāsa indram ||3||



2taṃ vo dasmam ṛtīṣaham vasor mandānam andhasaḥ |
2abhi vatsaṃ na svasareṣu dhenava indraṃ gīrbhir navāmahe ||1||

2dyukṣaṃ sudānuṃ taviṣībhir āvṛtaṃ giriṃ na purubhojasam |
2kṣumantaṃ vājaṃ śatinaṃ sahasriṇaṃ makṣū gomantam īmahe ||2||

2tat tvā yāmi suvīryaṃ tad brahma pūrvacittaye |
2yenā yatibhyo bhṛgave dhane hite yena praskaṇvam āvitha ||3||

2yenā samudram asṛjo mahīr apas tad indra vṛṣṇi te śavaḥ |
2sadyaḥ so asya mahimā na saṃnaśe yaṃ kṣoṇīr anucakrade ||4||



2ud u te madhumattamā gira stomāsa īrate |
2satrājito dhanasā akṣitotayo vājayanto rathā iva ||1||

2kaṇvā iva bhṛgavaḥ sūryā iva viśvam id dhītam ānaśuḥ |
2indraṃ stomebhir mahayanta āyavaḥ priyamedhāso asvaran ||2||



2indraḥ pūrbhid ātirad dāsam arkair vidadvasur dayamāno vi śatrūn |
2brahmajūtas tanvā vāvṛdhāno bhūridātra āpṛṇad rodasī ubhe ||1||

2makhasya te taviṣasya pra jūtim iyarmi vācam amṛtāya bhūṣan |
2indra kṣitīnām asi mānuṣīṇāṃ viśāṃ daivīnām uta pūrvayāvā ||2||

2indro vṛtram avṛṇoc chardhanītiḥ pra māyinām aminād varpaṇītiḥ |
2ahan vyaṃsam uśadhag vaneṣv āvir dhenā akṛṇod rāmyāṇām ||3||

2indraḥ svarṣā janayann ahāni jigāyośigbhiḥ pṛtanā abhiṣṭiḥ |
2prārocayan manave ketum ahnām avindaj jyotir bṛhate raṇāya ||4||

2indras tujo barhaṇā ā viveśa nṛvad dadhāno naryā purūṇi |
2acetayad dhiya imā jaritre premaṃ varṇam atirac chukram āsām ||5||

2maho mahāni panayanty asyendrasya karma sukṛtā purūṇi |
2vṛjanena vṛjinānt saṃ pipeṣa māyābhir dasyūṃr abhibhūtyojāḥ ||6||

2yudhendro mahnā varivaś cakāra devebhyaḥ satpatiś carṣaṇiprāḥ |
2vivasvataḥ sadane asya tāni viprā ukthebhiḥ kavayo gṛṇanti ||7||

2satrāsāhaṃ vareṇyaṃ sahodāṃ sasavāṃsaṃ svar apaś ca devīḥ |
2sasāna yaḥ pṛthivīṃ dyām utemām indraṃ madanty anu dhīraṇāsaḥ ||8||

2sasānātyāṃ uta sūryaṃ sasānendraḥ sasāna purubhojasaṃ gām |
2hiraṇyayam uta bhogaṃ sasāna hatvī dasyūn prāryaṃ varṇam āvat ||9||

20,11.10a indra oṣadhīr asanod ahāni vanaspatīṃr asanod antarikṣam |
20,11.10c bibheda balaṃ nunude vivāco 'thābhavad damitābhikratūnām ||10||

20,11.11a śunaṃ huvema maghavānam indram asmin bhare nṛtamaṃ vājasātau |
20,11.11c śṛṇvantam ugram ūtaye samatsu ghnantaṃ vṛtrāṇi saṃjitaṃ dhanānām ||11||


2ud u brahmāṇy airata śravasyendraṃ samarye mahayā vasiṣṭha |
2ā yo viśvāni śavasā tatānopaśrotā ma īvato vacāṃsi ||1||

2ayāmi ghoṣa indra devajāmir irajyanta yac churudho vivāci |
2nahi svam āyuś cikite janeṣu tānīd aṃhāṃsy ati parṣy asmān ||2||

2yuje rathaṃ gaveṣaṇaṃ haribhyām upa brahmāṇi jujuṣāṇam asthuḥ |
2vi bādhiṣṭa sya rodasī mahitvendro vṛtrāṇy apratī jaghanvān ||3||

2āpaś cit pipyu staryo na gāvo nakṣann ṛtaṃ jaritāras ta indra |
2yāhi vāyur na niyuto no achā tvaṃ hi dhībhir dayase vi vājān ||4||

2te tvā madā indra mādayantu śuṣmiṇaṃ tuvirādhasaṃ jaritre |
2eko devatrā dayase hi martān asmin chūra savane mādayasva ||5||

2eved indraṃ vṛṣaṇaṃ vajrabāhuṃ vasiṣṭhāso abhy arcanty arkaiḥ |
2sa na stuto vīravad dhātu gomad yūyaṃ pāta svastibhiḥ sadā naḥ ||6||

2ṛjīṣī vajrī vṛṣabhas turāṣāṭ chuṣmī rājā vṛtrahā somapāvā |
2yuktvā haribhyām upa yāsad arvāṅ mādhyaṃdine savane matsad indraḥ ||7||



2indraś ca somaṃ pibataṃ bṛhaspate 'smin yajñe mandasānā vṛṣaṇvasū |
2ā vāṃ viśantv indavaḥ svābhuvo 'sme rayiṃ sarvavīraṃ ni yachatam ||1||

2ā vo vahantu saptayo raghuṣyado raghupatvānaḥ pra jigāta bāhubhiḥ |
2sīdatā barhir uru vaḥ sadas kṛtaṃ mādayadhvaṃ maruto madhvo andhasaḥ ||2||

2imaṃ stomam arhate jātavedase ratham iva saṃ mahemā manīṣayā |
2bhadrā hi naḥ pramatir asya saṃsady agne sakhye mā riṣāmā vayaṃ tava ||3||

2aibhir agne sarathaṃ yāhy arvāṅ nānārathaṃ vā vibhavo hy aśvāḥ |
2patnīvatas triṃśataṃ trīṃś ca devān anuṣvadham ā vaha mādayasva ||4||



2vayam u tvām apūrvya sthūraṃ na kac cid bharanto 'vasyavaḥ |
2vāje citraṃ havāmahe ||1||

2upa tvā karmann ūtaye sa no yuvograś cakrāma yo dhṛṣat |
2tvām id dhy avitāraṃ vavṛmahe sakhāya indra sānasim ||2||

2yo na idamidaṃ purā pra vasya ānināya tam u va stuṣe |
2sakhāya indram ūtaye ||3||

2haryaśvaṃ satpatiṃ carṣaṇīsahaṃ sa hi ṣmā yo amandata |
2ā tu naḥ sa vayati gavyam aśvyaṃ stotṛbhyo maghavā śatam ||4||



2pra maṃhiṣṭhāya bṛhate bṛhadraye satyaśuṣmāya tavase matiṃ bhare |
2apām iva pravaṇe yasya durdharaṃ rādho viśvāyu śavase apāvṛtam ||1||

2adha te viśvam anu hāsad iṣṭaya āpo nimneva savanā haviṣmataḥ |
2yat parvate na samaśīta haryata indrasya vajraḥ śnathitā hiraṇyayaḥ ||2||

2asmai bhīmāya namasā sam adhvara uṣo na śubhra ā bharā panīyase |
2yasya dhāma śravase nāmendriyaṃ jyotir akāri harito nāyase ||3||

2ime ta indra te vayaṃ puruṣṭuta ye tvārabhya carāmasi prabhūvaso |
2nahi tvad anyo girvaṇo giraḥ sadhat kṣoṇīr iva prati no harya tad vacaḥ ||4||

2bhūri ta indra vīryaṃ tava smasy asya stotur maghavan kāmam ā pṛṇa |
2anu te dyaur bṛhatī vīryaṃ mama iyaṃ ca te pṛthivī nema ojase ||5||

2tvaṃ tam indra parvataṃ mahām uruṃ vajreṇa vajrin parvaśaś cakartitha |
2avāsṛjo nivṛtāḥ sartavā apaḥ satrā viśvaṃ dadhiṣe kevalaṃ sahaḥ ||6||



2udapruto na vayo rakṣamāṇā vāvadato abhriyasyeva ghoṣāḥ |
2giribhrajo normayo madanto bṛhaspatim abhy arkā anāvan ||1||

2saṃ gobhir aṅgiraso nakṣamāṇo bhaga ived aryamaṇaṃ nināya |
2jane mitro na dampatī anakti bṛhaspate vājayāśūṃr ivājau ||2||

2sādhvaryā atithinīr iṣirā spārhāḥ suvarṇā anavadyarūpāḥ |
2bṛhaspatiḥ parvatebhyo vitūryā nir gā ūpe yavam iva sthivibhyaḥ ||3||

2āpruṣāyan madhunā ṛtasya yonim avakṣipann arka ulkām iva dyoḥ |
2bṛhaspatir uddharann aśmano gā bhūmyā udneva vi tvacaṃ bibheda ||4||

2apa jyotiṣā tamo antarikṣad udnaḥ śīpālam iva vāta ājat |
2bṛhaspatir anumṛśyā valasyābhram iva vāta ā cakra ā gāḥ ||5||

2yadā valasya pīyato jasuṃ bhed bṛhaspatir agnitapobhir arkaiḥ |
2dadbhir na jihvā pariviṣṭam ādad āvir nidhīṃr akṛṇod usriyāṇām ||6||

2bṛhaspatir amata hi tyad āsāṃ nāma svarīṇāṃ sadane guhā yat |
2āṇḍeva bhitvā śakunasya garbham ud usriyāḥ parvatasya tmanājat ||7||

2aśnāpinaddhaṃ madhu pary apaśyan matsyaṃ na dīna udani kṣiyantam |
2niṣ ṭaj jabhāra camasaṃ na vṛkṣād bṛhaspatir viraveṇā vikṛtya ||8||

2soṣām avindat sa svaḥ so agniṃ so arkeṇa vi babādhe tamāṃsi |
2bṛhaspatir govapuṣo valasya nir majjānaṃ na parvaṇo jabhāra ||9||

20,16.10a himeva parṇā muṣitā vanāni bṛhaspatinākṛpayad valo gāḥ |
20,16.10c anānukṛtyam apunaś cakāra yāt sūryāmāsā mitha uccarātaḥ ||10||

20,16.11a abhi śyāvaṃ na kṛśanebhir aśvaṃ nakṣatrebhiḥ pitaro dyām apiṃśan |
20,16.11c rātryāṃ tamo adadhur jyotir ahan bṛhaspatir bhinad adriṃ vidad gāḥ ||11||

20,16.12a idam akarma namo abhriyāya yaḥ pūrvīr anv ānonavīti |
20,16.12c bṛhaspatiḥ sa hi gobhiḥ so aśvaiḥ sa vīrebhiḥ sa nṛbhir no vayo dhāt ||12||



2achā ma indraṃ matayaḥ svarvidaḥ sadhrīcīr viśvā uśatīr anūṣata |
2pari ṣvajante janayo yathā patiṃ maryaṃ na śundhyuṃ maghavānam ūtaye ||1||

2na ghā tvadrig apa veti me manas tve it kāmaṃ puruhūta śiśraya |
2rājeva dasma ni ṣado 'dhi barhiṣy asmint su some 'vapānam astu te ||2||

2viṣūvṛd indro amuter uta kṣudhaḥ sa id rāyo maghavā vasva īśate |
2tasyed ime pravaṇe sapta sindhavo vayo vardhanti vṛṣabhasya śuṣmiṇaḥ ||3||

2vayo na vṛkṣaṃ supalāśam āsadant somāsa indraṃ mandinaś camūṣadaḥ |
2praiṣām anīkaṃ śavasā davidyutad vidat svar manave jyotir āryam ||4||

2kṛtaṃ na śvaghnī vi cinoti devane saṃvargaṃ yan maghavā sūryaṃ jayat |
2na tat te anyo anu vīryaṃ śakan na purāṇo maghavan nota nūtanaḥ ||5||

2viśaṃviśaṃ maghavā pary aśāyata janānāṃ dhenā avacākaśad vṛṣā |
2yasyāha śakraḥ savaneṣu raṇyati sa tīvraiḥ somaiḥ sahate pṛtanyataḥ ||6||

2āpo na sindhum abhi yat samakṣarant somāsa indraṃ kulyā iva hradam |
2vardhanti viprā maho asya sādane yavaṃ na vṛṣṭir divyena dānunā ||7||

2vṛṣā na kruddhaḥ patayad rajaḥsv ā yo aryapatnīr akṛṇod imā apaḥ |
2sa sunvate maghavā jīradānave 'vindaj jyotir manave haviṣmate ||8||

2uj jāyatāṃ paraśu jyotiṣā saha bhūyā ṛtasya sudughā purāṇavat |
2vi rocatām aruṣo bhānunā śuciḥ svar na śukraṃ śuśucīta satpatiḥ ||9||

20,17.10a gobhiṣ ṭaremāmatiṃ durevāṃ yavena kṣudhaṃ puruhūta viśvām |
20,17.10c vayaṃ rājabhiḥ prathamā dhanāny asmākena vṛjanenā jayema ||10||

20,17.11a bṛhaspatir naḥ pari pātu paścād utottarasmād adharād aghāyoḥ |
20,17.11c indraḥ purastād uta madhyato naḥ sakhā sakhibhyaḥ varivaḥ kṛṇotu ||11||

20,17.12a bṛhaspate yuvam indraś ca vasvo divyasyeśāthe uta pārthivasya |
20,17.12c dhattaṃ rayiṃ stuvate kīraye cid yūyaṃ pāta svastibhiḥ sadā naḥ ||12||


2vayam u tvā taditarthā indra tvāyantaḥ sakhāyaḥ |
2kaṇvā ukthebhir jarante ||1||

2na ghem anyad ā papana vajrinn apaso naviṣṭau |
2taved u stomaṃ ciketa ||2||

2ichanti devāḥ sunvantaṃ na svapnāya spṛhayanti |
2yanti pramādam atandrāḥ ||3||

2vayam indra tvāyavo 'bhi pra ṇonumo vṛṣan |
2viddhi tv asya no vaso ||4||

2mā no nide ca vaktave 'ryo randhīr arāvne |
2tve api kratur mama ||5||

2tvaṃ varmāsi saprathaḥ puroyodhaś ca vṛtrahan |
2tvayā prati bruve yujā ||6||



2vārtrahatyāya śavase pṛtanāṣāhyāya ca |
2indra tvā vartayāmasi ||1||

2arvācīnaṃ su te mana uta cakṣuḥ śatakrato |
2indra kṛṇvantu vāghataḥ ||2||

2nāmāni te śatakrato viśvābhir gīrbhir īmahe |
2indrābhimātiṣāhye ||3||

2puruṣṭutasya dhāmabhiḥ śatena mahayāmasi |
2indrasya carṣaṇīdhṛtaḥ ||4||

2indraṃ vṛtrāya hantave puruhūtam upa bruve |
2bhareṣu vājasātaye ||5||

2vājeṣu sāsahir bhava tvām īmahe śatakrato |
2indra vṛtrāya hantave ||6||

2dyumneṣu pṛtanājye pṛtsutūrṣu śravaḥsu ca |
2indra sākṣvābhimātiṣu ||7||



2śuṣmintamaṃ na ūtaye dyumninaṃ pāhi jāgṛvim |
2indra somaṃ śatakrato ||1||

2indriyāṇi śatakrato yā te janeṣu pañcasu |
2indra tāni ta ā vṛṇe ||2||

2agann indra śravo bṛhad dyumnaṃ dadhiṣva duṣṭaram |
2ut te śuṣmaṃ tirāmasi ||3||

2arvāvato na ā gahy atho śakra parāvataḥ |
2u loko yas te adriva indreha tata ā gahi ||4||

2indro aṅgaṃ mahad bhayam abhi ṣad apa cucyavat |
2sa hi sthiro vicarṣaṇiḥ ||5||

2indraś ca mṛlayāti no na naḥ paścād aghaṃ naśat |
2bhadraṃ bhavāti naḥ puraḥ ||6||

2indra āśābhyas pari sarvābhyo abhayaṃ karat |
2jetā śatrūn vicarṣaṇiḥ ||7||



2ny ū ṣu vācaṃ pra mahe bharāmahe gira indrāya sadane vivasvataḥ |
2nū cid dhi ratnaṃ sasatām ivāvidan na duṣṭutir draviṇodeṣu śasyate ||1||

2duro aśvasya dura indra gor asi duro yavasya vasuna inas patiḥ |
2śikṣānaraḥ pradivo akāmakarśanaḥ sakhā sakhibhyas tam idaṃ gṛṇīmasi ||2||

2śacīva indra purukṛd dyumattama taved idam abhitaś cekite vasu |
2ataḥ saṃgṛbhyābhibhūta ā bhara mā tvāyato jarituḥ kāmam ūnayīḥ ||3||

2ebhir dyubhir sumanā ebhir indubhir nirundhāno amatiṃ gobhir aśvinā |
2indreṇa dasyuṃ darayanta indubhir yutadveṣasaḥ sam iṣā rabhemahi ||4||

2sam indra rāyā sam iṣā rabhemahi saṃ vājebhiḥ puruścandrair abhidyubhiḥ |
2saṃ devyā pramatyā vīraśuṣmayā goagrayāśvāvatyā rabhemahi ||5||

2te tvā madā amadan tāni vṛṣṇyā te somāso vṛtrahatyeṣu satpate |
2yat kārave daśa vṛtrāṇy aprati barhiṣmate ni sahasrāṇi barhayaḥ ||6||

2yudhā yudham upa ghed eṣi dhṛṣṇuyā purā puraṃ sam idaṃ haṃsy ojasā |
2namyā yad indra sakhyā parāvati nibarhayo namuciṃ nāma māyinam ||7||

2tvaṃ karañjam uta parṇayaṃ vadhīs tejiṣṭhayātithigvasya vartanī |
2tvaṃ śatā vaṅgṛdasyābhinat puro 'nānudaḥ pariṣūtā ṛjiśvanā ||8||
2tvam etāṃ janarājño dvir daśābandhunā suśravasopajagmuṣaḥ |
2ṣaṣṭiṃ sahasrā navatiṃ nava śruto ni cakreṇa rathyā duṣpadāvṛṇak ||9||

20,21.10a tvam āvitha suśravasaṃ tavotibhis tava trāmabhir indra tūrvayāṇam |
20,21.10c tva asmai kutsam atithigvam āyuṃ mahe rājñe yūne arandhanāyaḥ ||10||

20,21.11a ya udṛcīndra devagopāḥ sakhāyas te śivatamā asāma |
20,21.11c tvāṃ stoṣāma tvayā suvīrā drāghīya āyuḥ prataraṃ dadhānāḥ ||11||



2abhi tvā vṛṣabhā sute sutaṃ sṛjāmi pītaye |
2tṛmpā vy aśnuhī madam ||1||

2mā tvā mūrā aviṣyavo mopahasvāna ā dabhan |
2mākīṃ brahmadviṣo vanaḥ ||2||

2iha tvā goparīṇasā mahe mandantu rādhase |
2saro gauro yathā piba ||3||

2abhi pra gopatiṃ girendram arca yathā vide |
2sūnuṃ satyasya satpatim ||4||

2ā harayaḥ sasṛjrire 'ruṣīr adhi barhiṣi |
2yatrābhi saṃnavāmahe ||5||

2indrāya gāva āśiraṃ duduhre vajriṇe madhu |
2yat sīm upahvare vidat ||6||



2ā tū na indra madryag ghuvānaḥ somapītaye |
2haribhyāṃ yāhy adrivaḥ ||1||

2satto hotā na ṛtviyas tistire barhir ānuṣak |
2ayujran prātar adrayaḥ ||2||

2imā brahma brahmavāhaḥ kriyanta ā barhiḥ sīda |
2vīhi śūra purolāśam ||3||

2rārandhi savaneṣu ṇa eṣu stomeṣu vṛtrahan |
2uktheṣv indra girvaṇaḥ ||4||

2matayaḥ somapām uruṃ rihanti śavasas patim |
2indraṃ vatsaṃ na mātaraḥ ||5||

2sa mandasvā hy andhaso rādhase tanvā mahe |
2na stotāraṃ nide karaḥ ||6||

2vayam indra tvāyavo haviṣmanto jarāmahe |
2uta tvam asmayur vaso ||7||

2māre asmad vi mumuco haripriyārvāṅ yāhi |
2indra svadhāvo matsveha ||8||

2arvāñcaṃ tvā sukhe rathe vahatām indra keśinā |
2ghṛtasnū barhir āsade ||9||



2upa naḥ sutam ā gahi somam indra gavāśiram |
2haribhyāṃ yas te asmayuḥ ||1||

2tam indra madam ā gahi barhiṣṭhāṃ grāvabhiḥ sutam |
2kuvin nv asya tṛpṇavaḥ ||2||

2indram itthā giro mamāchāgur iṣitā itaḥ |
2āvṛte somapītaye ||3||

2indraṃ somasya pītaye stomair iha havāmahe |
2ukthebhiḥ kuvid āgamat ||4||

2indra somāḥ sutā ime tān dadhiṣva śatakrato |
2jathare vājinīvaso ||5||

2vidmā hi tvā dhanaṃjayaṃ vājeṣu dadhṛṣaṃ kave |
2adhā te sumnam īmahe ||6||

2imam indra gavāśiraṃ yavāśiraṃ ca naḥ piba |
2āgatyā vṛṣabhiḥ sutam ||7||

2tubhyed indra sva okye somaṃ codāmi pītaye |
2eṣa rārantu te hṛdi ||8||

2tvāṃ sutasya pītaye pratnam indra havāmahe |
2kuśikāso avasyavaḥ ||9||



2aśvāvati prathamo goṣu gachati suprāvīr indra martyas tavotibhiḥ |
2tam it pṛṇakṣi vasunā bhavīyasā sindhum āpo yathābhito vicetasaḥ ||1||

2āpo na devīr upa yanti hotriyam avaḥ paśyanti vitataṃ yathā rajaḥ |
2prācair devāsaḥ pra ṇayanti devayuṃ brahmapriyaṃ joṣayante varā iva ||2||

2adhi dvayor adadhā ukthyaṃ vaco yatasrucā mithunā yā saparyataḥ |
2asaṃyatto vrate te kṣeti puṣyati bhadrā śaktir yajamānāya sunvate ||3||

2ād aṅgirāḥ prathamaṃ dadhire vaya iddhāgnayaḥ śamyā ye sukṛtyayā |
2sarvaṃ paṇeḥ sam avindanta bhojanam aśvāvantaṃ gomantam ā paśuṃ naraḥ ||4||

2yajñair atharvā prathamaḥ pathas tate tataḥ sūryo vratapā vena ājani |
2ā gā ājad uśanā kāvyaḥ sacā yamasya jātam amṛtaṃ yajāmahe ||5||

2barhir vā yat svapatyāya vṛjyate 'rko vā ślokam āghoṣate divi |
2grāvā yatra vadati karur ukthyas tasyed indro abhipitveṣu raṇyati ||6||

2progrāṃ pītiṃ vṛṣṇa iyarmi satyāṃ prayai sutasya haryaśva tubhyam |
2indra dhenābhir iha mādayasva dhībhir viśvābhiḥ śacyā gṛṇānaḥ ||7||



2yogeyoge tavastaraṃ vājevāje havāmahe |
2sakhāya indram ūtaye ||1||

2ā ghā gamad yadi śravat sahasriṇībhir ūtibhiḥ |
2vājebhir upa no havam ||2||

2anu pratnasyaukaso huve tuvipratiṃ naram |
2yaṃ te pūrvaṃ pitā huve ||3||

2yuñjanti bradhnam aruṣaṃ carantaṃ pari tasthuṣaḥ |
2rocante rocanā divi ||4||

2yuñjanti asya kāmyā harī vipakṣasā rathe |
2śoṇā dhṛṣṇū nṛvāhasā ||5||

2ketuṃ kṛṇvann aketave peśo maryā apeśase |
2sam uṣadbhir ajāyathāḥ ||6||



2yad indrāhaṃ yathā tvam īśīya vasva eka it |
2stotā me goṣakhā syāt ||1||

2śikṣeyam asmai ditseyaṃ śacīpate manīṣiṇe |
2yad ahaṃ gopatiḥ syām ||2||

2dhenuṣ ṭa indra sūnṛtā yajamānāya sunvate |
2gām aśvaṃ pipyuṣī duhe ||3||

2na te vartāsti rādhasa indra devo na martyaḥ |
2yad ditsasi stuto magham ||4||

2yajña indram avardhayad yad bhūmiṃ vy avartayat |
2cakrāṇa opaśaṃ divi ||5||

2vāvṛdhānasya te vayaṃ viśvā dhanāni jigyuṣaḥ |
2ūtim indrā vṛṇīmahe ||6||



2vy antarikṣam atiran made somasya rocanā |
2indro yad abhinad valam ||1||

2ud gā ājad aṅgirobhya āviṣ krṇvan guhā satīḥ |
2arvāñcaṃ nunude valam ||2||

2indreṇa rocanā divo dṛlhāni dṛṃhitāni ca |
2sthirāṇi na parāṇude ||3||

2apām ūrmir madann iva stoma indrājirāyate |
2vi te madā arājiṣuḥ ||4||



2tvaṃ hi stomavardhana indrāsy ukthavardhanaḥ |
2stotṝṇām uta bhadrakṛt ||1||

2indram it keśinā harī somapeyāya vakṣataḥ |
2upa yajñaṃ surādhasam ||2||

2apāṃ phenena namuceḥ śira indrod avartayaḥ |
2viśvā yad ajaya spṛdhaḥ ||3||

2māyābhir utsisṛpsata indra dyām ārurukṣataḥ |
2ava dasyūṃr adhūnuthāḥ ||4||

2asunvām indra saṃsadaṃ viṣūcīṃ vy anāśayaḥ |
2somapā uttaro bhavan ||5||



2pra te mahe vidathe śaṃsiṣaṃ harī pra te vanve vanuṣo haryataṃ madam |
2ghṛtaṃ na yo haribhiś cāru secata ā tvā viśantu harivarpasaṃ giraḥ ||1||

2hariṃ hi yonim abhi ye samasvaran hinvanto harī divyaṃ yathā sadaḥ |
2ā yaṃ pṛṇanti haribhir na dhenava indrāya śūśaṃ harivantam arcata ||2||

2so asya vajro harito ya āyaso harir nikāmo harir ā gabhastyoḥ |
2dyumnī suśipro harimanyusāyaka indre ni rūpā haritā mimikṣire ||3||

2divi na ketur adhi dhāyi haryato vivyacad vajro harito na raṃhyā |
2tudad ahiṃ hariśipro ya āyasaḥ sahasraśokā abhavad dharimbharaḥ ||4||

2tvaṃtvam aharyathā upastutaḥ pūrvebhir indra harikeśa yajvabhiḥ |
2tvaṃ haryasi tava viśvam ukthyam asāmi rādho harijāta haryatam ||5||



2tā vajriṇaṃ mandinaṃ stomyaṃ mada indraṃ rathe vahato haryatā harī |
2purūṇy asmai savanāni haryata indrāya somā harayo dadhanvire ||1||

2araṃ kāmāya harayo dadhamire sthirāya hinvan harayo harī turā |
2arvadbhir yo haribhir joṣam īyate so asya kāmaṃ harivantam ānaśe ||2||

2hariśmaśārur harikeśa āyasas turaspeye yo haripā avardhata |
2arvadbhir yo haribhir vājinīvasur ati viśvā duritā pāriṣad dharī ||3||

2śruveva yasya hariṇī vipetatuḥ śipre vājāya hariṇī davidhvataḥ |
2pra yat kṛte camase marmṛjad dharī pītvā madasya haryatasyāndhasaḥ ||4||

2uta sma sadna haryatasya pastyor atyo na vājaṃ harivāṃ acikradat |
2mahī cid dhi dhiṣaṇāharyad ojasā bṛhad vayo dadhiṣe haryatas cid ā ||5||



2ā rodasī haryamāṇo mahitvā navyaṃnavyaṃ haryasi manma nu priyam |
2pra pastyam asura haryataṃ gor āviṣ kṛdhi haraye sūryāya ||1||

2ā tvā haryantaṃ prayujo janānāṃ rathe vahantu hariśipram indra |
2pibā yathā pratibhṛtasya madhvo haryan yajñaṃ sadhamāde daśoṇim ||2||

2apāḥ pūrveṣāṃ harivaḥ sutānām atho idaṃ savanaṃ kevalaṃ te |
2mamaddhi somaṃ madhumantam indra satrā vṛṣaṃ jathara ā vṛṣasva ||3||



2apsu dhūtasya harivaḥ pibeha nṛbhiḥ sutasya jaṭharaṃ pṛṇasva |
2mimikṣur yam adraya indra tubhyaṃ tebhir vardhasva madam ukthavāhaḥ ||1||

2progrāṃ pītiṃ vṛṣṇa iyarmi satyāṃ prayai sutasya haryaśva tubhyam |
2indra dhenābhir iha mādayasva dhībhir viśvābhiḥ śacyā gṛṇānaḥ ||2||

2ūtī śacīvas tava vīryeṇa vayo dadhānā uśija ṛtajñāḥ |
2prajāvad indra maṃso duroṇe tasthur gṛṇantaḥ sadhamādyāsaḥ ||3||



2yo jāta eva prathamo manasvān devo devān kratunā paryamūṣat |
2yasya śuṣmād rodasī abhyasetāṃ nṛmṇasya mahnā sa janāsa indraḥ ||1||

2yaḥ pṛthivīṃ vyathamānām adṛṃhad yaḥ parvatān prakupitāṃ aramṇāt |
2yo antarikṣaṃ vimame varīyo yo dyām astabhnāt sa janāsa indraḥ ||2||

2yo hatvāhim ariṇāt sapta sindhūn yo gā udājad apadhā valasya |
2yo aśmanor antar agniṃ jajāna saṃvṛk samatsu sa janāsa indraḥ ||3||

2yenemā viśvā cyavanā kṛtāni yo dāsaṃ varṇam adharaṃ guhākaḥ |
2śvaghnīva yo jigīvāṃ lakṣam ādad aryaḥ puṣṭāni sa janāsa indraḥ ||4||

2yaṃ smā pṛchanti kuha seti ghoram utem āhur naiṣo astīty enam |
2so aryaḥ puṣṭīr vija ivā mināti śrad asmai dhatta sa janāsa indraḥ ||5||

2yo radhrasya coditā yaḥ kṛśasya yo brahmaṇo nādhamānasya kīreḥ |
2yuktagrāvṇo yo 'vitā suśipraḥ sutasomasya sa janāsa indraḥ ||6||

2yasyāśvāsaḥ pradiśi yasya gāvo yasya grāmā yasya viśve rathāsaḥ |
2yaḥ sūryaṃ ya uṣasaṃ jajāna yo apāṃ netā sa janāsa indraḥ ||7||

2yaṃ krandasī saṃyatī vihvayete pare 'vare ubhayā amitrāḥ |
2samānaṃ cid ratham ātasthivāṃsā nānā havete sa janāsa indraḥ ||8||

2yasmān na ṛte vijayante janāso yaṃ yudhyamānā avase havante |
2yo viśvasya pratimānaṃ babhūva yo acyutacyut sa janāsa indraḥ ||9||
20,34.10a yaḥ śasvato mahy eno dadhānān amanyamānāṃ charvā jaghāna |
20,34.10c yaḥ śardhate nānudadāti śṛdhyāṃ yo dasyor hantā sa janāsa indraḥ ||10||

20,34.11a yaḥ śambharaṃ parvateṣu kṣiyantaṃ catvāriṃśyāṃ śarady anvavindat |
20,34.11c ojāyamānaṃ yo ahiṃ jaghāna dānuṃ śayānaṃ sa janāsa indraḥ ||11||

20,34.12a yaḥ śambharaṃ paryatarat kasībhir yo 'cārukāsnāpibat sutasya |
20,34.12c antar girau yajamānaṃ bahuṃ janaṃ yasminn āmūrchat sa janāsa indraḥ ||12||

20,34.13a yaḥ saptaraśmir vṛṣabhas tuviṣmān avāsṛjat sartave sapta sindhūn |
20,34.13c yo rauhiṇam asphurad vajrabāhur dyām ārohantaṃ sa janāsa indraḥ ||13||

20,34.14a dyāvā cid asmai pṛthivī mamete śuṣmāc cid asya parvatā bhayante |
20,34.14c yaḥ somapā nicito vajrabāhur yo vajrahastaḥ sa janāsa indraḥ ||14||

20,34.15a yaḥ sunvantam avati yaḥ pacantaṃ yaḥ śaṃsantaṃ yaḥ śaśamānam ūtī |
20,34.15c yasya brahma vardhanaṃ yasya somo yasyedaṃ rādhaḥ sa janāsa indraḥ ||15||

20,34.16a jāto vy akhyat pitror upasthe bhuvo na veda janituḥ parasya |
20,34.16c staviṣyamāṇo no yo asmad vratā devānāṃ sa janāsa indraḥ ||16||

20,34.17a yaḥ somakāmo haryaśvaḥ sūrir yasmād rejante bhuvanāni viśvā |
20,34.17c yo jaghāna śambaraṃ yaś ca śuṣṇaṃ ya ekavīraḥ sa janāsa indraḥ ||17||

20,34.18a yaḥ sunvate pacate dudhra ā cid vājaṃ dardarṣi sa kilāsi satyaḥ |
20,34.18c vayaṃ ta indra viśvaha priyāsaḥ suvīrāso vidatham ā vadema ||18||



2asmā id u pra tavase turāya prayo na harmi stomaṃ māhināya |
2ṛcīṣamāyādhrigava oham indrāya brahmāṇi rātatamā ||1||

2asmā id u praya iva pra yaṃsi bharāmy āngūṣaṃ bādhe suvṛkti |
2indrāya hṛdā manasā manīṣā pratnāya patye dhiyo marjayanta ||2||

2asmā id u tyam upamaṃ svarṣāṃ bharāmy āṅgūṣam āsyena |
2maṃhiṣṭham achoktibhir matīnāṃ suvṛktibhiḥ sūriṃ vāvṛdhadhyai ||3||

2asmā id u stomaṃ saṃ hinomi rathaṃ na taṣṭeva tatsināya |
2giraś ca girvāhase suvṛktīndrāya viśvaminvaṃ medhirāya ||4||

2asmā id u saptim iva śravasyendrāyārkaṃ juhvā sam añje |
2vīram dānaukasaṃ vandadhyai purāṃ gūrtaśravasaṃ darmāṇam ||5||

2asmā id u tvaṣṭā takṣad vajraṃ svapastamaṃ svaryaṃ raṇāya |
2vṛtrasya cid vidad yena marma tujann īśānas tujatā kiyedhāḥ ||6||

2asyed u mātuḥ savaneṣu sadyo mahaḥ pituṃ papivāṃ cārv annā |
2muṣāyad viṣṇuḥ pacataṃ sahīyān vidhyad varāhaṃ tiro adrim astā ||7||

2asmā id u gnāś cid devapatnīr indrāyārkam ahihatya ūvuḥ |
2pari dyāvāpṛthivī jabhra urvī nāsya te mahimānaṃ pari ṣṭaḥ ||8||

2asyed eva pra ririce mahitvaṃ divas pṛthivyāḥ pary antarikṣāt |
2svarāl indro dama ā viśvagūrtaḥ svarir amatro vavakṣe raṇāya ||9||

20,35.10a asyed eva śavasā śuśantaṃ vi vṛścad vajreṇa vṛtram indraḥ |
20,35.10c gā na vrāṇā avanīr amuñcad abhi śravo dāvane sacetāḥ ||10||

20,35.11a asyed u tveṣasā ranta sindhavaḥ pari yad vajreṇa sīm ayachat |
20,35.11c īśānakṛd dāśuṣe daśasyan turvītaye gādhaṃ turvaṇiḥ kaḥ ||11||

20,35.12a asmā id u pra bharā tūtujāno vṛtrāya vajram īśānaḥ kiyedhāḥ |
20,35.12c gor na parva vi radā tiraśceṣyann arṇāṃsy apāṃ caradhyai ||12||

20,35.13a asyed u pra brūhi pūrvyāṇi turasya karmāṇi navya ukthaiḥ |
20,35.13c yudhe yad iṣṇāna āyudhāny ṛghāyamāṇo niriṇāti śatrūn ||13||

20,35.14a asyed u bhiyā girayaś ca dṛlhā dyāvā ca bhūmā januṣas tujete |
20,35.14c upo venasya joguvāna oṇiṃ sadyo bhuvad vīryāya nodhāḥ ||14||

20,35.15a asmā id u tyad anu dāyy eṣām eko yad vavne bhūrer īśānaḥ |
20,35.15c praitaśaṃ sūrye paspṛdhānaṃ sauvaśvye suṣvim āvad indraḥ ||15||

20,35.16a evā te hāriyojanā suvṛktīndra brahmāṇi gotamāso akran |
20,35.16c aiṣu viśvapeśasaṃ dhiyaṃ dhāḥ prātar makṣū dhiyāvasur jagamyāt ||16||



2ya eka id dhavyaś carṣaṇīnām indraṃ taṃ gīrbhir abhy arca ābhiḥ |
2yaḥ patyate vṛṣabho vṛṣṇyāvānt satyaḥ satvā purumāyaḥ sahasvān ||1||

2tam u naḥ pūrve pitaro navagvāḥ sapta viprāso abhi vājayantaḥ |
2nakṣaddābhaṃ taturiṃ parvateṣṭhām adroghavācaṃ matibhiḥ śaviṣṭham ||2||

2tam īmahe indram asya rāyaḥ puruvīrasya nṛvataḥ purukṣoḥ |
2yo aṣkṛdhoyur ajaraḥ svarvān tam ā bhara harivo mādayadhyai ||3||

2tan no vi voco yadi te purā cij jaritāra ānaśuḥ sumnam indra |
2kas te bhāgaḥ kiṃ vayo dudhra khiduḥ puruhūta purūvaso 'suraghnaḥ ||4||

2taṃ pṛchantī vajrahastaṃ ratheṣṭhām indraṃ vepī vakvarī yasya nū gīḥ |
2tuvigrābhaṃ tuvikūrmiṃ rabhodāṃ gātum iṣe nakṣate tumram acha ||5||

2ayā ha tyaṃ māyayā vāvṛdhānaṃ manojuvā svatavaḥ parvatena |
2acyutā cid vīlitā svojo rujo vi dṛlhā dhṛṣatā virapśin ||6||

2tam vo dhiyā navyasyā śaviṣṭham pratnaṃ pratnavat paritaṃsayadhyai |
2sa no vakṣad animānaḥ suvahnendro viśvāny ati durgahāṇi ||7||

2ā janāya druhvaṇe pārthivāni divyāni dīpayo 'ntarikṣā |
2tapā vṛṣan viśvataḥ śociṣā tān brahmadviṣe śocaya kṣām apaś ca ||8||

2bhuvo janasya divyasya rājā pārthivasya jagatas tveṣasaṃdṛk |
2dhiṣva vajraṃ dakṣiṇa indra haste viśvā ajurya dayase vi māyāḥ ||9||

20,36.10a ā saṃyatam indra ṇaḥ svastiṃ śatrutūryāya bṛhatīm amṛdhrām |
20,36.10c yayā dāsāny āryāṇi vṛtrā karo vajrint sutukā nāhuṣāṇi ||10||

20,36.11a sa no niyudbhiḥ puruhūta vedho viśvavārābhir ā gahi prayajyo |
20,36.11c na yā adevo varate na deva ābhir yāhi tūyam ā madryadrik ||11||



2yas tigmaśṛṅgo vṛṣabho na bhīmaḥ ekaḥ kṛṣṭīś cyavayati pra viśvāḥ |
2yaḥ śaśvato adāśuṣo gayasya prayantāsi suṣvitarāya vedaḥ ||1||

2tvaṃ ha tyad indra kutsam āvaḥ śuśrūṣamāṇas tanvā samarye |
2dāsaṃ yac śuṣṇam kuyavaṃ ny asmā arandhaya ārjuneyāya śikṣan ||2||

2tvaṃ dhṛṣṇo dhṛṣatā vītahavyaṃ prāvo viśvābhir ūtibhiḥ sudāsam |
2pra paurukutsiṃ trasadasyum āvaḥ kṣetrasātā vṛtrahatyeṣu pūrum ||3||

2tvaṃ nṛbhir nṛmaṇo devavītau bhūrīṇi vṛtrā haryaśva haṃsi |
2tvaṃ ni dasyuṃ cumuriṃ dhuniṃ cāsvāpayo dabhītaye suhantu ||4||

2tava cyautnāni vajrahasta tāni nava yat puro navatiṃ ca sadyaḥ |
2niveśane śatatamāviveṣīr ahaṃ ca vṛtraṃ namucim utāhan ||5||

2sanā tā ta indra bhojanāni rātahavyāya dāśuṣe sudāse |
2vṛṣṇe te harī vṛṣaṇā yunajmi vyantu brahmāṇi puruśāka vājam ||6||

2mā te asyāṃ sahasāvan pariṣṭāv aghāya bhūma harivaḥ parādau |
2trāyasva no 'vṛkebhir varūthais tava priyāsaḥ sūriṣu syāma ||7||

2priyāsa it te maghavann abhiṣṭau naro madema śaraṇe sakhāyaḥ |
2ni turvaśaṃ ni yādvaṃ śiśīhy atithigvāya śaṃsyaṃ kariṣyan ||8||

2sadyaś cin nu te maghavann abhiṣṭau naraḥ śaṃsanty ukthaśāsa ukthā |
2ye te havebhir vi paṇīṃr adāśann asmān vṛṇīṣva yujyāya tasmai ||9||

20,37.10a ete stomā narāṃ nṛtama tubhyam asmadryañco dadato maghāni |
20,37.10c teṣām indra vṛtrahatye śivo bhūḥ sakhā ca śūro 'vitā ca nṛṇām ||10||

20,37.11a nū indra śūra stavamāna ūtī brahmajūtas tanvā vāvṛdhasva |
20,37.11c upa no vājān mimīhy upa stīn yuyaṃ pāta svastibhiḥ sadā naḥ ||11||



2ā yāhi suṣumā hi ta indra somaṃ pibā imam |
2edaṃ barhiḥ sado mama ||1||

2ā tvā brahmayujā harī vahatām indra keśinā |
2upa brahmāṇi naḥ śṛṇu ||2||

2brahmāṇas tvā vayaṃ yujā somapām indra sominaḥ |
2sutāvanto havāmahe ||3||

2indram id gāthino bṛhad indram arkebhir arkiṇaḥ |
2indraṃ vāṇīr anūṣata ||4||

2indra id dharyoḥ sacā saṃmiśla ā vacoyujā |
2indro vajrī hiraṇyayaḥ ||5||

2indro dīrghāya cakṣasa ā sūryaṃ rohayad divi |
2vi gobhir adrim airayat ||6||



2indraṃ vo viśvatas pari havāmahe janebhyaḥ |
2asmākam astu kevalaḥ ||1||

2vy antarikṣam atiran made somasya rocanā |
2indro yad abhinad valam ||2||

2ud gā ājad aṅgirobhya āviṣ kṛṇvan guhā satīḥ |
2arvāñcaṃ nunude valam ||3||

2indreṇa rocanā divo dṛlhāni dṛṃhitāni ca |
2sthirāṇi na parāṇude ||4||

2apām ūrmir madann iva stoma indrājirāyate |
2vi te madā arājiṣuḥ ||5||



2indreṇa saṃ hi dṛkṣase saṃjagmāno abibhyuṣā |
2mandū samānavarcasā ||1||

2anavadyair abhidyubhir makhaḥ sahasvad arcati |
2gaṇair indrasya kāmyaiḥ ||2||

2ād aha svadhām anu punar garbhatvam erire |
2dadhānā nāma yajñiyam ||3||



2indro dadhīco asthabhir vṛtrāṇy apratiṣkutaḥ |
2jaghāna navatīr nava ||1||

2ichan aśvasya yac chiraḥ parvateṣv apaśritam |
2tad vidac charyaṇāvati ||2||

2atrāha gor amanvata nāma tvaṣṭur apīcyam |
2itthā candramaso gṛhe ||3||



2vācam aṣṭāpadīm ahaṃ navasraktim ṛtaspṛśam |
2indrāt pari tanvam mame ||1||

2anu tvā rodasī ubhe krakṣamāṇam akṛpetām |
2indra yad dasyuhābhavaḥ ||2||

2uttiṣṭhann ojasā saha pītvī śipre avepayaḥ |
2somam indra camū sutam ||3||



2bhindhi viśvā apa dviṣaḥ bādho jahī mṛdhaḥ |
2vasu spārhaṃ tad ā bhara ||1||

2yad vīlāv indra yat sthire yat parśāne parābhṛtam |
2vasu spārhaṃ tad ā bhara ||2||

2yasya te viśvamānuṣo bhūrer dattasya vedati |
2vasu spārhaṃ tad ā bhara ||3||



2pra samrājaṃ carṣaṇīnām indraṃ stotā navyaṃ gīrbhiḥ |
2naraṃ nṛṣāhaṃ maṃhiṣṭham ||1||

2yasminn ukthāni raṇyanti viśvāni ca śravasya |
2apām avo na samudre ||2||

2taṃ suṣṭutyā vivāse jyeṣṭharājaṃ bhare kṛtnum |
2maho vājinaṃ sanibhyaḥ ||3||



2ayam u te sam atasi kapota iva garbhadhim |
2vacas tac cin na ohase ||1||

2stotraṃ rādhānāṃ pate girvāho vīra yasya te |
2vibhūtir astu sūnṛtā ||2||

2ūrdhvas tiṣṭhā na ūtaye 'smin vāje śatakrato |
2sam anyeṣu bravāvahai ||3||



2praṇetāram vasyo achā kartāraṃ jyotiḥ samatsu |
2sāsahvāṃsam yudhāmitrān ||1||

2sa naḥ papriḥ pārayāti svasti nāvā puruhūtaḥ |
2indro viśvā ati dviṣaḥ ||2||

2sa tvaṃ na indra vājobhir daśasyā ca gātuyā ca |
2achā ca naḥ sumnaṃ neṣi ||3||



2tam indraṃ vājayāmasi mahe vṛtrāya hantave |
2sa vṛṣā vṛṣabho bhuvat ||1||

2indraḥ sa dāmane kṛta ojiṣṭhaḥ sa made hitaḥ |
2dyumnī ślokī sa somyaḥ ||2||

2girā vajro na saṃbhṛtaḥ sabalo anapacyutaḥ |
2vavakṣa ṛṣvo astṛtaḥ ||3||

2indram id gāthino bṛhad indram arkebhir arkiṇaḥ |
2indraṃ vāṇīr anūṣata ||4||

2indra id dharyoḥ sacā saṃmiśla ā vacoyujā |
2indro vajrī hiraṇyayaḥ ||5||

2indro dīrghāya cakṣasa ā sūryaṃ rohayad divi |
2vi gobhir adrim airayat ||6||

2ā yāhi suṣumā hi ta indra somaṃ pibā imam |
2edaṃ barhiḥ sado mama ||7||

2ā tvā brahmayujā harī vahatām indra keśinā |
2upa brahmāṇi naḥ śṛṇu ||8||

2brahmāṇas tvā vayaṃ yujā somapām indra sominaḥ |
2sutāvanto havāmahe ||9||

20,47.10a yuñjanti bradhnam aruṣaṃ carantaṃ pari tasthuṣaḥ |
20,47.10c rocante rocanā divi ||10||

20,47.11a yuñjanty asya kāmyā harī vipakṣasā rathe |
20,47.11c śoṇā dhṛṣṇū nṛvāhasā ||11||

20,47.12a ketuṃ kṛṇvann aketave peśo maryā apeśase |
20,47.12c sam uṣadbhir ajāyathāḥ ||12||
20,47.13a ud u tyaṃ jātavedasaṃ devaṃ vahanti ketavaḥ |
20,47.13c dṛśe viśvāya sūryam ||13||

20,47.14a apa tye tāyavo yathā nakṣatrā yanty aktubhiḥ |
20,47.14c sūrāya viśvacakṣase ||14||

20,47.15a adṛśrann asya ketavo vi raśmayo janāṃ anu |
20,47.15c bhrājanto agnayo yathā ||15||

20,47.16a taraṇir viśvadarśato jyotiṣkṛd asi sūrya |
20,47.16c viśvam ā bhāsi rocana ||16||

20,47.17a pratyaṅ devānāṃ viśaḥ pratyaṅṅ ud eṣi mānuṣīḥ |
20,47.17c pratyaṅ viśvaṃ svar dṛśe ||17||

20,47.18a yenā pāvaka cakṣasā bhuraṇyantaṃ janāṃ anu |
20,47.18c tvaṃ varuṇa paśyasi ||18||

20,47.19a vi dyām eṣi rajas pṛthv ahar mimāno aktubhiḥ |
20,47.19c paśyaṃ janmāni sūrya ||19||

20,47.20a sapta tvā harito rathe vahanti deva sūrya |
20,47.20c śociṣkeśam vicakṣaṇam ||20||

20,47.21a ayukta sapta śundhyuvaḥ sūro rathasya naptyaḥ |
20,47.21c tābhir yāti svayuktibhiḥ ||21||



2abhi tvā varcasā giraḥ siñcanty ā caraṇyuvaḥ |
2abhi vatsaṃ na dhenavaḥ ||1||

2tā arṣanti śubhriyaḥ pṛñcatīr varcasā payaḥ |
2jātaṃ janir yathā hṛdā ||2||

2vajrāpavasādhyaḥ kīrtir mriyamāṇam āvahan |
2mahyam āyur ghṛtaṃ payaḥ ||3||

2āyaṃ gauḥ pṛśnir akramīd asadan mātaraṃ puraḥ |
2pitaraṃ ca prayant svaḥ ||4||

2antaś carati rocanā asya prāṇād apānataḥ |
2vy akhyan mahiṣaḥ svaḥ ||5||

2triṃśad dhāmā vi rājati vāk pataṅgo aśiśriyat |
2prati vastor ahar dyubhiḥ ||6||



2yac chakrā vācam āruhann antarikṣaṃ siṣāsathaḥ |
2saṃ devā amadan vṛṣā ||1||

2śakro vācam adhṛṣṭāyor uvāco adhṛṣṇuhi |
2maṃhiṣṭha ā madardivi ||2||

2śakro vācam adhṛṣṇuhi dhāmadharman vi rājati |
2vimadan barhir āsaran ||3||

2taṃ vo dasmam ṛtīṣahaṃ vasor mandānam andhasaḥ |
2abhi vatsaṃ na svasareṣu dhenava indraṃ gīrbhir navāmahe ||4||

2dyukṣaṃ sudānuṃ taviṣībhir āvṛtam giriṃ na purubhojasam |
2kṣumantaṃ vājaṃ śatinaṃ sahasriṇaṃ makṣū gomantam īmahe ||5||

2tat tvā yāmi suvīryaṃ tad brahma pūrvacittaye |
2yenā yatibhyo bhṛgave dhane hite yena praskaṇvam āvitha ||6||

2yenā samudram asṛjo mahīr apas tad indra vṛṣṇi te śavaḥ |
2sadyaḥ so asya mahimā na saṃnaśe yaṃ kṣoṇīr anucakrade ||7||



2kan navyo atasīnāṃ turo gṛṇīta martyaḥ |
2nahī nv asya mahimānam indriyaṃ svar gṛṇanta ānaśuḥ ||1||

2kad u stuvanta ṛtayanta devata ṛṣiḥ ko vipra ohate |
2kadā havaṃ maghavann indra sunvataḥ kad u stuvata ā gamaḥ ||2||



2abhi pra vaḥ surādhasam indram arca yathā vide |
2yo jaritṛbhyo maghavā purūvasuḥ sahasreṇeva śikṣati ||1||

2śatānīkeva pra jigāti dhṛṣṇuyā hanti vṛtrāṇi dāśuṣe |
2girer iva pra rasā asya pinvire datrāṇi purubhojasaḥ ||2||

2pra su śrutaṃ surādhasam arcā śakram abhiṣṭaye |
2yaḥ sunvate stuvate kāmyaṃ vasu sahasreṇeva maṃhate ||3||

2śatānīkā hetayo asya duṣṭarā indrasya samiṣo mahīḥ |
2girir na bhujmā maghatsu pinvate yad īṃ sutā amandiṣuḥ ||4||



2vayaṃ gha tvā sutāvanta āpo na vṛktabarhiṣaḥ |
2pavitrasya prasravaṇeṣu vṛtrahan pari stotāra āsate ||1||

2svaranti tvā sute naro vaso nireka ukthinaḥ |
2kadā sutaṃ tṛṣāṇa oka ā gama indra svabdīva vaṃsagaḥ ||2||

2kaṇvebhir dhṛṣṇav ā dhṛsad vājaṃ darṣi sahasriṇam |
2piśaṅgarūpaṃ maghavan vicarṣaṇe makṣū gomantam īmahe ||3||



2ka īṃ veda sute sacā pibantaṃ kad vayo dadhe |
2ayaṃ yaḥ puro vibhinatty ojasā mandānaḥ śipry andhasaḥ ||1||

2dānā mṛgo na vāraṇaḥ purutrā carathaṃ dadhe |
2nakiṣ ṭvā ni yamad ā sute gamo mahāś carasy ojasā ||2||

2ya ugraḥ sann aniṣṭṛta sthiro raṇāya saṃskṛtaḥ |
2yadi stotur maghavā śṛṇavad dhavaṃ nendro yoṣaty ā gamat ||3||



2viśvāḥ pṛtanā abhibhūtaraṃ naraṃ sajūs tatakṣur indraṃ jajanuś ca rājase |
2kratvā variṣṭhaṃ vara āmurim utogram ojiṣṭhaṃ tavasaṃ tarasvinam ||1||

2sam īṃ rebhāso asvarann indraṃ somasya pītaye |
2svarpatiṃ yad īṃ vṛdhe dhṛtavrato hy ojasā sam ūtibhiḥ ||2||

2nemiṃ namanti cakṣasā meṣaṃ viprā abhisvarā |
2sudītayo vo adruho 'pi karṇe tarasvinaḥ sam ṛkvabhiḥ ||3||



2tam indraṃ johavīmi maghavānam ugraṃ satrā dadhānam apratiṣkutaṃ śavāṃsi |
2maṃhiṣṭho gīrbhir ā ca yajñiyo vavartad rāye no viśvā supathā kṛṇotu vajrī ||1||

2yā indra bhuja ābharaḥ svarvāṃ asurebhyaḥ |
2stotāram in maghavann asya vardhaya ye ca tve vṛktabarhiṣaḥ ||2||

2yam indra dadhiṣe tvam aśvaṃ gāṃ bhāgam avyayam |
2yajamāne sunvati dakṣiṇāvati tasmin taṃ dhehi mā paṇau ||3||



2indro madāya vāvṛdhe śavase vṛtrahā nṛbhiḥ |
2tam in mahatsv ājiṣūtem arbhe havāmahe sa vājeṣu pra no 'viṣat ||1||

2asi hi vīra senyo 'si bhūri parādadiḥ |
2asi dabhrasya cid vṛdho yajamānāya śikṣasi sunvate bhūri te vasu ||2||

2yad udīrata ājayo dhṛṣṇave dhīyate dhanā |
2yukṣvā madacyutā harī kaṃ hanaḥ kaṃ vasau dadho 'smāṃ indra vasau dadhaḥ ||3||

2mademade hi no dadir yūthā gavām ṛjukratuḥ |
2saṃ gṛbhāya puru śatobhayāhastyā vasu śiśīhi rāya ā bhara ||4||

2mādayasva sute sacā śavase śūra rādhase |
2vidmā hi tvā purūvasum upa kāmānt sasṛjmahe 'thā no 'vitā bhava ||5||

2ete ta indra jantavo viśvaṃ puṣyanti vāryam |
2antar hi khyo janānām aryo vedo adāśuṣāṃ teṣāṃ no veda ā bhara ||6||



2surūpakṛtnum ūtaye sudughām iva goduhe |
2juhūmasi dyavidyavi ||1||

2upa naḥ savanā gahi somasya somapāḥ piba |
2godā id revato madaḥ ||2||

2athā te antamānāṃ vidyāma sumatīnām |
2mā no ati khya ā gahi ||3||

2śuṣmintamaṃ na ūtaye dyumninaṃ pāhi jāgṛvim |
2indra somaṃ śatakrato ||4||

2indriyāṇi śatakrato yā te janeṣu pañcasu |
2indra tāni ta ā vṛṇe ||5||

2agann indra śravo bṛhad dyumnaṃ dadhiṣva duṣṭaram |
2ut te śuṣmaṃ tirāmasi ||6||

2arvāvato na ā gahy atho śakra parāvataḥ |
2u loko yas te adriva indreha tata ā gahi ||7||

2indro aṅga mahad bhayam abhī ṣad apa cucyavat |
2sa hi sthiro vicarṣaniḥ ||8||

2indraś ca mṛlayāti no na naḥ paścād aghaṃ naśat |
2bhadraṃ bhavāti naḥ puraḥ ||9||

20,57.10a indra āśābhyas pari sarvābhyo abhayaṃ karat |
20,57.10c jetā śatrūn vicarṣaṇiḥ ||10||

20,57.11a ka īṃ veda sute sacā pibantaṃ kad vayo dadhe |
20,57.11c ayaṃ yaḥ puro vibhinatty ojasā mandānaḥ śipry andhasaḥ ||11||

20,57.12a dānā mṛgo na vāraṇaḥ purutrā carathaṃ dadhe |
20,57.12c nakiṣ ṭvā ni yamad ā sute gamo mahāṃś carasy ojasā ||12||

20,57.13a ya ugraḥ sann aniṣṭṛta sthiro raṇāya saṃskṛtaḥ |
20,57.13c yadi stotur maghavā śṛṇavad dhavaṃ nendro yoṣaty ā gamat ||13||

20,57.14a vayaṃ gha tvā sutāvanta āpo na vṛktabarhiṣaḥ |
20,57.14c pavitrasya prasravaṇeṣu vṛtrahan pari stotāra āsate ||14||

20,57.15a svaranti tvā sute naro vaso nireka ukthinaḥ |
20,57.15c kadā sutaṃ tṛṣāṇa oka ā gama indra svabdīva vaṃsagaḥ ||15||

20,57.16a kaṇvebhir dhṛṣṇav ā dhṛṣad vājaṃ darṣi sahasriṇam |
20,57.16c piśaṅgarūpaṃ maghavan vicarṣaṇe makṣū gomantam īmahe ||16||



2śrāyanta iva sūryaṃ viśved indrasya bhakṣata |
2vasūni jāte janamāna ojasā prati bhāgaṃ na dīdhima ||1||

2anarśarātiṃ vasudām upa stuhi bhadrā indrasya rātayaḥ |
2so asya kāmaṃ vidhato na roṣati mano dānāya codayan ||2||

2baṇ mahāṃ asi sūrya baḍ āditya mahāṃ asi |
2mahas te sato mahimā panasyate 'ddhā deva mahāṃ asi ||3||

2baṭ sūrya śravasā mahāṃ asi satrā deva mahāṃ asi |
2mahnā devānām asuryaḥ purohito vibhu jyotir adābhyam ||4||



2ud u tye madhu mattamā gira stomāsa īrate |
2satrājito dhanasā akṣitotayo vājayanto rathā iva ||1||

2kaṇvā iva bhṛgavaḥ sūrya iva viśvam id dhītam ānaśuḥ |
2indraṃ stomebhir mahayanta āyavaḥ priyamedhāso asvaran ||2||

2ud in nv asya ricyate 'ṃśo dhanaṃ na jigyusaḥ |
2ya indro harivān na dabhanti taṃ ripo dakṣaṃ dadhāti somini ||3||

2mantram akharvaṃ sudhitaṃ supeśasaṃ dadhāta yajñiyeṣv ā |
2pūrvīś cana prasitayas taranti taṃ ya indre karmaṇā bhuvat ||4||


2evā hy asi vīrayur evā śūra uta sthiraḥ |
2evā te rādhyaṃ manaḥ ||1||

2evā rātis tuvīmagha viśvebhir dhāyi dhātṛbhiḥ |
2aghā cid indra me sacā ||2||

2mo ṣu brahmeva tandrayur bhuvo vājānāṃ pate |
2matsvā sutasya gomataḥ ||3||

2evā hy asya sūnṛtā virapśī gomatī mahī |
2pakvā śākhā na dāśuṣe ||4||

2evā hi te vibhūtaya ūtaya indra māvate |
2sadyaś cit santi dāśuṣe ||5||

2evā hy asya kāmyā stoma ukthaṃ ca śaṃsyā |
2indrāya somapītaye ||6||



2taṃ te madaṃ gṛṇīmasi vṛṣaṇaṃ pṛtsu sāsahim |
2u lokakṛtnum adrivo hariśriyam ||1||

2yena jyotīmṣy āyave manave ca viveditha |
2mandāno asya barhiṣo vi rājasi ||2||

2tad adyā cit ta ukthino 'nu ṣṭuvanti pūrvathā |
2vṛṣapatnīr apo jayā divedive ||3||

2tam v abhi pra gāyata puruhūtaṃ puruṣṭutam |
2indraṃ gīrbhis taviṣam ā vivāsata ||4||
2yasya dvibarhaso bṛhat saho dādhāra rodasī |
2girīṃr ajrāṃ apaḥ svar vṛṣatvanā ||5||

2sa rājasi puruṣṭutaṃ eko vṛtrāṇi jighnase |
2indra jaitrā śravasya ca yantave ||6||



2vayam u tvām apūrvya sthūraṃ na kac cid bharanto 'vasyavaḥ |
2vāje citraṃ havāmahe ||1||

2upa tvā karmann ūtaye sa no yuvograś cakrāma yo dhṛṣat |
2tvām id dhy avitāraṃ vavṛmahe sakhāya indra sānasim ||2||

2yo na idamidaṃ purā pra vasya ānināya tam u va stuṣe |
2sakhāya indram ūtaye ||3||

2haryaśvaṃ satpatiṃ carṣaṇīsahaṃ sa hi ṣmā yo amandata |
2ā tu naḥ sa vayati gavyam aśvyaṃ stotṛbhyo maghavā śatam ||4||

20,62.10c indra jaitra śravasya ca yantave ||10||


2imā nu kaṃ bhuvanā sīṣadhāmendraś ca viśve ca devāḥ |
2yajñaṃ ca nas tanvaṃ ca prajāṃ cādityair indraḥ saha cīkḷpāti ||1||

2ādityair indraḥ sagaṇo marudbhir asmākaṃ bhūtv avitā tanūnām |
2hatvāya devā asurān yad āyan devā devatvam abhirakṣamāṇāḥ ||2||

2pratyañcam arkam anayaṃ chacībhir ād it svadhām iṣirāṃ pary apaśyan |
2ayā vājaṃ devahitaṃ sanema madema śatahimāḥ suvīrāḥ ||3||

2ya eka id vidayate vasu martāya dāśuṣe |
2īśāno apratiṣkuta indro aṅga ||4||

2kadā martam arādhasaṃ padā kṣumpam iva sphurat |
2kadā naḥ śuśravad gira indro aṅga ||5||

2yaś cid dhi tvā bahubhya ā sutāvāṃ āvivāsati |
2ugraṃ tat patyate śava indro aṅga ||6||

2yenā haṃsi ny attriṇaṃ tam īmahe ||7||

2yenā samudram āvithā tam īmahe ||8||

2yena sindhuṃ mahīr apo rathāṃ iva pracodayaḥ |
2panthām ṛtasya yātave tam īmahe ||9||



2endra no gadhi priyaḥ satrājid agohyaḥ |
2girir na viśvatas pṛthuḥ patir divaḥ ||1||

2abhi hi satya somapā ubhe babhūtha rodasī |

2tvaṃ hi śaśvatīnām indra dartā purām asi |

2ed u madhvo madintaraṃ siñca vādhvaryo andhasaḥ |
2evā hi vīra stavate sadāvṛdhaḥ ||4||

2indra sthātar harīṇāṃ nakiṣ te pūrvyastutim |

2aprāyubhir yajñebhir vāvṛdhenyam ||6||



2eto nv indraṃ stavāma sakhāya stomyaṃ naram |
2kuṣṭīr yo viśvā abhy asty eka it ||1||

2yasyāmitāni vīryā na rādhaḥ paryetave |

2stuhīndraṃ vyaśvavad anūrmiṃ vājinaṃ yamam |
2aryo gayaṃ maṃhamānaṃ vi dāśuṣe ||1||

2evā nūnam upa stuhi vaiyaśva daśamaṃ navam |
2suvidvāṃsaṃ carkṛtyaṃ caraṇīnām ||2||

2vetthā hi nirṛtīnāṃ vajrahasta parivṛjam |
2aharahaḥ śundhyuḥ paripadām iva ||3||



2vanoti hi sunvan kṣayaṃ parīṇasaḥ sunvāno hi ṣmā yajaty ava dviṣo devānām ava dviṣaḥ |
2sunvāna it siṣāsati sahasrā vājy avṛtaḥ |
2sunvānāyendro dadāty ābhuvaṃ rayiṃ dadāty ābhuvam ||1||

2mo ṣu vo asmad abhi tāni pauṃsyā sanā bhūvan dyumnāni mota jāriṣur asmat purota jāriṣuḥ |
2yad vaś citraṃ yugeyuge navyaṃ ghoṣād amartyam |
2asmāsu tan maruto yac ca duṣṭaraṃ didhṛtā yac ca duṣṭaram ||2||

2agniṃ hotāram manye dāsvantaṃ vasuṃ sūnuṃ sahaso jātavedasaṃ vipraṃ na jātavedasam |
2ya ūrdhvayā svadhvaro devo devācyā kṛpā |
2ghṛtasya vibhrāṣṭim anu vaṣṭi śociṣājuhvānasya sarpiṣaḥ ||3||

2yajñaiḥ saṃmiślāḥ pṛṣatībhir ṛṣṭibhir yāmaṃ chubhrāso añjiṣu priyā uta |
2āsadyā barhir bharatasya sūnavaḥ potrād ā somaṃ pibatā divo naraḥ ||4||

2ā vakṣi devāṃ iha vipra yakṣi cośan hotar ni ṣadā yoniṣu triṣu |
2prati vīhi prasthitaṃ somyaṃ madhu pibāgnīdhrāt tava bhāgasya tṛsṇuhi ||5||

2eṣa sya te tanvo nṛmṇavardhanaḥ saha ojaḥ pradivi bāhvor hitaḥ |
2tubhyaṃ suto maghavan tubhyam ābhṛtas tvam asya brāhmaṇād ā tṛpat piba ||6||

2yam u pūrvam ahuve tam idaṃ huve sed u havyo dadir yo nāma patyate |
2adhvaryubhiḥ prasthitaṃ somyaṃ madhu potrāt somaṃ draviṇodaḥ piba ṛtubhiḥ ||7||



2surūpakṛtnum ūtaye sudughām iva goduhe |
2juhūmasi dyavidyavi ||1||

2godā id revato madaḥ ||2||

2patayan mandayatsakham ||7||

2dhanānām indra sātaye ||9||

20,68.10a yo rāyo 'vanir mahānt supāraḥ sunvataḥ sakhā |

2sa ghā no yoga ā bhuvat sa rāye sa puraṃdhyām |
2gamad vājebhir ā sa naḥ ||1||

2yasya saṃsthe na vṛṇvate harī samatsu śatravaḥ |
2tasmā indrāya gāyata ||2||

2sutapāvne sutā ime śucayo yanti vītaye |

2tvaṃ sutasya pītaye sadyo vṛddho ajāyathāḥ |

2ā tvā viśantv āśavaḥ somāsa indra girvaṇaḥ |

2vīlu cid ārujatnubhir guhā cid indra vahnibhiḥ |
2avinda usriyā anu ||1||

2devayanto yathā matim achā vidadvasuṃ giraḥ |

2indreṇa saṃ hi dṛkṣase saṃjagmāno abibhyuṣā |

2mahāṃ indraḥ paraś ca nu mahitvam astu vajriṇe |
2dyaur na prathinā śavaḥ ||1||

2samohe vā ya āśata naras tokasya sanitau |
2viprāso vā dhiyāyavaḥ ||2||

2yaḥ kukṣiḥ somapātamaḥ samudra iva pinvate |
2urvīr āpo na kākudaḥ ||3||

2evā hy asya sūnṛtā virapśī gomatī mahī |
2pakvā śākhā na dāśuṣe ||4||

2evā hi te vibhūtaya ūtaya indra māvate |
2sadyaś cit santi dāśuṣe ||5||

2indrāya somapītaye ||6||
