2viśveṣu hi tvā savaneṣu tuñjate samānam ekaṃ vṛṣamaṇyavaḥ pṛthak svaḥ saniṣyavaḥ pṛthak |
2taṃ tvā nāvaṃ na parṣaṇiṃ śūṣasya dhuri dhīmahi |
2indraṃ na yajñaiś catayanta āyava stomebhir indram āyavaḥ ||1||

2vi tvā tatasre mithunā avasyavo vrajasya sātā gavyasya niḥsṛjaḥ sakṣanta indra niḥsṛjaḥ |
2yad gavyantā dvā janā svar yantā samūhasi |
2āviṣ karikrad vṛṣaṇaṃ sacābhuvaṃ vajram indra sacābhuvam ||2||

2uto no asyā uṣaso juṣeta hy arkasya bodhi haviṣo havīmabhiḥ svarṣātā havīmabhiḥ |
2yad indra hantave mṛgho vṛṣā vajriṃ ciketasi |
2ā me asya vedhaso navīyaso manma śrudhi navīyasaḥ ||3||



2tubhyed imā savanā śūra viśvā tubhyaṃ brahmāṇi vardhanā kṛṇomi |
2tvaṃ nṛbhir havyo viśvadhāsi ||1||

2nū cin nu te manyamānasya dasmod aśnuvanti mahimānam ugra |
2na vīryam indra te na rādhaḥ ||2||

2pra vo mahe mahivṛdhe bharadhvaṃ pracetase pra sumatiṃ kṛṇudhvam |
2viśaḥ pūrvīḥ pra carā carṣaṇiprāḥ ||3||

2yadā vajraṃ hiraṇyam id athā rathaṃ harī yamasya vahato vi sūribhiḥ |
2ā tiṣṭhati maghavā sanaśruta indro vājasya dīrghaśravasas patiḥ ||4||

2so cin nu vṛṣṭir yūthyā svā sacāṃ indraḥ śmaśrūṇi haritābhi pruṣṇute |
2ava veti sukṣayaṃ sute madhūd id dhūṇoti vāto yathā vanam ||5||

2yo vācā vivāco mṛdhravācaḥ purū sahasrāśivā jaghāna |
2tattad id asya pauṃsyaṃ gṛṇīmasi piteva yas taviṣīṃ vāvṛdhe śavaḥ ||6||



2yac cid dhi satya somapā anāśastā iva smasi |
2ā tū na indra śaṃsaya goṣv aśveṣu śubhriṣu sahasreṣu tuvīmagha ||1||

2śiprin vājānāṃ pate śacīvas tava daṃsanā |
2ā tū na indra śaṃsaya goṣv aśveṣu śubhriṣu sahasreṣu tuvīmagha ||2||

2ni ṣvāpayā mithūdṛśā sastām abudhyamāne |
2ā tū na indra śaṃsaya goṣv aśveṣu śubhriṣu sahasreṣu tuvīmagha ||3||

2sasantu tyā arātayo bodhantu śūra rātayaḥ |
2ā tū na indra śaṃsaya goṣv aśveṣu śubhriṣu sahasreṣu tuvīmagha ||4||

2sam indra gardabhaṃ mṛṇa nuvantaṃ papayāmuyā |
2ā tū na indra śaṃsaya goṣv aśveṣu śubhriṣu sahasreṣu tuvīmagha ||5||

2patāti kuṇḍṛṇācyā dūraṃ vāto vanād adhi |
2ā tū na indra śaṃsaya goṣv aśveṣu śubhriṣu sahasreṣu tuvīmagha ||6||

2sarvaṃ parikrośaṃ jahi jambhayā kṛkadāśvam |
2ā tū na indra śaṃsaya goṣv aśveṣu śubhriṣu sahasreṣu tuvīmagha ||7||



2vi tvā tatasre mithunā avasyavo vrajasya sātā gavyasya niḥsṛjaḥ sakṣanta indra niḥsṛjaḥ |
2yad gavyanta dvā janā svar yantā samūhasi |
2āviṣ karikrad vṛṣaṇaṃ sacābhuvaṃ vajram indra sacābhuvam ||1||

2viduṣ ṭe asya vīryasya pūravaḥ puro yad indra śāradīr avātiraḥ sāsahāno avātiraḥ |
2śāsas tam indra martyam ayajuṃ śavasas pate |
2mahīm amuṣṇāḥ pṛthivīm imā apo mandasāna imā apaḥ ||2||

2ād it te asya vīryasya carkiran madeṣu vṛṣann uśijo yad āvitha sakhīyato yad āvitha |
2cakartha kāram ebhyaḥ pṛtanāsu pravantave |
2te anyāmanyāṃ nadyaṃ saniṣṇata śravasyantaḥ saniṣṇata ||3||



2vane na vā yo ny adhāyi cākraṃ chucir vāṃ stomo bhuraṇāv ajīgaḥ |
2yasyed indraḥ purudineṣu hotā nṛṇāṃ narvo nṛtamaḥ kṣapāvān ||1||

2pra te asyā uṣasaḥ prāparasyā nṛtau syāma nṛtam asya nṛṇām |
2anu triśokaḥ śatam āvahan nṝn kutsena ratho yo asat sasavān ||2||

2kas te mada indra rantyo bhūd duro giro abhy ugro vi dhāva |
2kad vāho arvāg upa mā manīṣā ā tvā śakyām upamam rādho annaiḥ ||3||

2kad u dyumnam indra tvāvato nṝn kayā dhiyā karase kan na āgan |
2mitro na satya urugāya bhṛtyā anne samasya yad asan manīṣāḥ ||4||

2preraya sūro arthaṃ na pāraṃ ye asya kāmaṃ janidhā iva gman |
2giraś ca ye te tuvijāta pūrvīr nara indra pratiśikṣanty annaiḥ ||5||

2mātre nu te sumite indra pūrvī dyaur majmanā pṛthivī kāvyena |
2varāya te ghṛtavantaḥ sutāsaḥ svādnan bhavantu pītaye madhūni ||6||

2ā madhvo asmā asicann amatram indrāya pūrṇaṃ sa hi satyarādhāḥ |
2sa vāvṛdhe varimann ā pṛthivyā abhi kratvā naryaḥ pauṃsyaiś ca ||7||

2vy ānaḷ indraḥ pṛtanāḥ svojā āsmai yatante sakhyāya pūrvīḥ |
2ā smā rathaṃ na pṛtanāsu tiṣṭha yaṃ bhadrayā sumatyā codayāse ||8||



2ā satyo yātu maghavāṃ ṛjīṣī dravantv asya haraya upa naḥ |
2tasmā id andhaḥ suṣumā sudakṣam ihābhipitvaṃ karate gṛṇānaḥ ||1||

2ava sya śūrādhvano nānte 'smin no adya savane mandadhyai |
2śaṃsāty uktham uśaneva vedhāś cikituṣe asuryāya manma ||2||

2kavir na niṇyaṃ vidathāni sādhan vṛṣā yat sekaṃ vipipāno arcāt |
2diva itthā jījanat sapta kārūn ahnā cic cakrur vayunā gṛṇantaḥ ||3||

2svar yad vedi sudṛśīkam arkair mahi jyotī rurucur yad dha vastoḥ |
2andhā tamāṃsi dudhitā vicakṣe nṛbhyaś cakāra nṛtamo abhiṣṭau ||4||

2vavakṣa indro amitam ṛjiṣy ubhe ā paprau rodasī mahitvā |
2ataś cid asya mahimā vi recy abhi yo viśvā bhuvanā babhūva ||5||

2viśvāni śakro naryāṇi vidvān apo rireca sakhibhir nikāmaiḥ |
2aśmānaṃ cid ye bibhidur vacobhir vrajam gomantam uśijo vi vavruḥ ||6||

2apo vṛtraṃ vavrivāṃsaṃ parāhan prāvat te vajraṃ pṛthivī sacetāḥ |
2prārṇāṃsi samudriyāṇy ainoḥ patir bhavaṃ chavasā śūra dhṛṣṇo ||7||

2apo yad adriṃ puruhūta dardar āvir bhuvat saramā pūrvyaṃ te |
2sa no netā vājam ā darṣi bhūriṃ gotrā rujann aṅgirobhir gṛṇānaḥ ||8||



2tad vo gāya sute sacā puruhūtāya satvane |
2śaṃ yad gave na śākine ||1||

2na ghā vasur ni yamate dānaṃ vājasya gomataḥ |
2yat sīm upa śravad giraḥ ||2||

2kuvitsasya pra hi vrajaṃ gomantaṃ dasyuhā gamat |
2śacībhir apa no varat ||3||



2indra kratuṃ na ā bhara pitā putrebhyo yathā |
2śikṣā ṇo asmin puruhūta yāmani jīvā jyotir aśīmahi ||1||

2mā no ajñātā vṛjanā durādhyo māśivāso ava kramuḥ |
2tvayā vayaṃ pravataḥ śaśvatīr apo 'ti śūra tarāmasi ||2||



2indra jyeṣṭhaṃ na ā bharaṃ ojiṣṭhaṃ papuri śravaḥ |
2yeneme citra vajrahasta rodasī obhe suśipra prāḥ ||1||

2tvām ugram avase carṣaṇīsahaṃ rājan deveṣu hūmahe |
2viśvā su no vithurā pibdanā vaso 'mitrān suṣahān kṛdhi ||2||



2yad dyāva indra te śataṃ śataṃ bhūmir uta syuḥ |
2na tvā vajrint sahasraṃ sūryā anu na jātam aṣṭa rodasī ||1||

2ā paprātha mahinā kṛṣṇyā vṛṣan viśvā śaviṣṭha śavasā |
2asmāṃ ava maghavan gomati vraje vajrim citrābhir ūtibhiḥ ||2||



2yad indra yāvatas tvam etāvad aham īśīya |
2stotāram id didhiṣeya radāvaso na pāpatvāya rāsīya ||1||

2śikṣeyam in mahayate divedive rāya ā kuhacidvide |
2nahi tvad anyan maghavan na āpyaṃ vasyo asti pitā cana ||2||



2indra tridhātu śaraṇaṃ trivarūthaṃ svastimat |
2chardir yacha maghavadbhyaś ca mahyaṃ ca yāvayā didyum ebhyaḥ ||1||

2ye gavyatā manasā śatrum ādabhur abhipraghnanti dhṛṣṇuyā |
2agha smā no maghavann indra girvaṇas tanūpā antamo bhava ||2||



2indrā yāhi citrabhāno sutā ime tvāyavaḥ |
2aṇvībhis tanā pūtāsaḥ ||1||

2indrā yāhi dhiyeṣito viprajutaḥ sutāvataḥ |
2upa brahmāṇi vāghataḥ ||2||

2indrā yāhi tūtujāna upa brahmāṇi harivaḥ |
2sute dadhiṣva naś canaḥ ||3||



2mā cid anyad vi śaṃsata sakhāyo mā riṣaṇyata |
2indram it stotā vṛṣaṇaṃ sacā sute muhur ukthā ca śaṃsata ||1||
2avakrakṣiṇaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ yathājuram gāṃ na carṣaṇīsaham |
2vidveṣaṇaṃ saṃvananobhayaṃkaraṃ maṃhiṣṭham ubhayāvinam ||2||

2yac cid dhi tvā janā ime nānā havanta ūtaye |
2asmākaṃ brahmedam indra bhūtu te 'hā viśvā ca vardhanam ||3||

2vi tartūryante maghavan vipaścito 'ryo vipo janānām |
2upa kramasva pururūpam ā bhara vājaṃ nediṣṭham ūtaye ||4||



2brahmaṇā te brahmayujā yunajmi harī sakhāyā sadhamāda āśū |
2sthiraṃ rathaṃ sukham indrādhitiṣṭhan prajānan vidvāṃ upa yāhi somam ||1||



2adhvaryavo 'ruṇaṃ dugdham aṃśuṃ juhotana vṛṣabhāya kṣitīnām |
2gaurād vedīyāṃ avapānam indro viśvāhed yāti sutasomam ichan ||1||

2yad dadhiṣe pradivi cārv annaṃ divedive pītim id asya vakṣi |
2uta hṛdota manasā juṣāṇa uśann indra prasthitān pāhi somān ||2||

2jajñānaḥ somaṃ sahase papātha pra te mātā mahimānam uvāca |
2endra paprāthorv antarikṣaṃ yudhā devebhyo varivaś cakartha ||3||

2yad yodhayā mahato manyamānān sākṣāma tān bāhubhiḥ śāśadānān |
2yad vā nṛbhir vṛta indrābhiyudhyās taṃ tvayājiṃ sauśravasaṃ jayema ||4||

2prendrasya vocaṃ prathamā kṛtāni pra nūtanā maghavā yā cakāra |
2yaded adevīr asahiṣṭa māyā athābhavat kevalaḥ somo asya ||5||

2tavedaṃ viśvam abhitaḥ paśavyaṃ yat paśyasi cakṣasā sūryasya |
2gavām asi gopatir eka indra bhakṣīmahi te prayatasya vasvaḥ ||6||

2bṛhaspate yuvam indraś ca vasvo divyasyeśāthe uta pārthivasya |
2dhattaṃ rayiṃ stuvate kīraye cid yūyaṃ pāta svastibhiḥ sadā naḥ ||7||



2yas tastambha sahasā vi jmo antān bṛhaspatis triṣadhastho raveṇa |
2taṃ pratnāsa ṛṣayo dīdhyānāḥ puro viprā dadhire mandrajihvam ||1||

2dhunetayaḥ supraketaṃ madanto bṛhaspate abhi ye nas tatasre |
2pṛṣantaṃ sṛpram adabdham ūrvaṃ bṛhaspate rakṣatād asya yonim ||2||

2bṛhaspate yā paramā parāvad ata ā te ṛtaspṛśo ni ṣeduḥ |
2tubhyaṃ khātā avatā adridugdhā madhva ścotanty abhito virapśam ||3||

2bṛhaspatiḥ prathamaṃ jāyamāno maho jyotiṣaḥ parame vyoman |
2saptāsyas tuvijāto raveṇa vi saptaraśmir adhamat tamāṃsi ||4||

2sa suṣṭubhā sa ṛkvatā gaṇena valaṃ ruroja phaligaṃ ravena |
2bṛhaspatir usriyā havyasūdaḥ kanikradad vāvaśatīr ud ājat ||5||

2evā pitre viśvadevāya vṛṣṇe yajñair vidhema namasā havirbhiḥ |
2bṛhaspate suprajā vīravanto vayaṃ syāma patayo rayīṇām ||6||


2asteva su prataraṃ lāyam asyan bhūṣann iva pra bharā stomam asmai |
2vācā viprās tarata vācam aryo ni rāmaya jaritaḥ soma indram ||1||

2dohena gām upa śikṣā sakhāyaṃ pra bodhaya jaritar jāram indram |
2kośaṃ na pūrṇaṃ vasunā nyṛṣṭam ā cyāvaya maghadeyāya śūram ||2||

2kim aṅga tvā maghavan bhojam āhuḥ śiśīhi mā śiśayaṃ tvā śṛṇomi |
2apnasvatī mama dhīr astu śakra vasuvidaṃ bhagam indrā bharā naḥ ||3||

2tvāṃ janā mamasatyeṣv indra saṃtasthānā vi hvayante samīke |
2atrā yujaṃ kṛṇute yo haviṣmān nāsunvatā sakhyaṃ vaṣṭi śūraḥ ||4||

2dhanaṃ na spandraṃ bahulaṃ yo asmai tīvrānt somāṃ āsunoti prayasvān |
2tasmai śatrūnt sutukān prātar ahno ni svaṣṭrān yuvati hanti vṛtram ||5||

2yasmin vayaṃ dadhimā śaṃsam indre yaḥ śiśrāya maghavā kāmam asme |
2ārāc cit san bhayatām asya śatrur ny asmai dyumnā janyā namantām ||6||

2ārāc chatrum apa bādhasva dūram ugro yaḥ śambaḥ puruhūta tena |
2asme dhehi yavamad gomad indra kṛdhī dhiyaṃ jaritre vājaratnām ||7||

2pra yam antar vṛṣasavāso ajman tīvrāḥ somā bahulāntāsa indram |
2nāha dāmānaṃ maghavā ni yaṃsan ni sunvate vahati bhūri vāmam ||8||

2uta prahām atidīvā jayati kṛtam iva śvaghnī vi cinoti kāle |
2yo devakāmo na dhanaṃ ruṇaddhi sam it taṃ rāyaḥ sṛjati svadhābhiḥ ||9||

20,89.10a gobhiṣ ṭaremāmatiṃ durevāṃ yavena vā kṣudhaṃ puruhūta viśve |
20,89.10c vayaṃ rājasu prathamā dhanāny ariṣṭāso vṛjanībhir jayema ||10||

20,89.11a bṛhaspatir naḥ pari pātu paścād utottarasmād adharād aghayoḥ |
20,89.11c indraḥ purastād uta madhyato naḥ sakhā sakhibhyo varīyaḥ kṛṇotu ||11||



2yo adribhit prathamajā ṛtāvā bṛhaspatir āṅgiraso haviṣmān |
2dvibarhajmā prāgharmasat pitā na ā rodasī vṛṣabho roravīti ||1||

2janāya cid ya īvate u lokaṃ bṛhaspatir devahūtau cakāra |
2ghnan vṛtrāṇi vi puro dardarīti jayaṃ chatrūṃr amitrān pṛtsu sāhan ||2||

2bṛhaspatiḥ sam ajayad vasūni maho vrajān gomate deva eṣaḥ |
2apaḥ siṣāsant svar apratīto bṛhaspatir hanty amitram arkaiḥ ||3||



2imāṃ dhiyaṃ saptaśīrṣṇīṃ pitā na ṛtaprajātāṃ bṛhatīm avindat |
2turīyaṃ svij janayad viśvajanyo 'yāsya uktham indrāya śaṃsan ||1||

2ṛtaṃ śaṃsanta ṛju dīdhyānā divas putrāso asurasya vīrāḥ |
2vipraṃ padam aṅgiraso dadhānā yajñasya dhāma prathamaṃ mananta ||2||

2haṃsair iva sakhibhir vāvadadbhir aśmanmayāni nahanā vyasyan |
2bṛhaspatir abhikanikradad gā uta prāstaud uc ca vidvāṃ agāyat ||3||

2avo dvābhyāṃ para ekayā gā guhā tiṣṭhantīr anṛtasya setau |
2bṛhaspatis tamasi jyotir ichan ud usrā ākar vi hi tisra āvaḥ ||4||

2vibhidyā puraṃ śayathem apācīṃ nis trīṇi sākam udadher akṛntat |
2bṛhaspatir uṣasaṃ sūryaṃ gām arkaṃ viveda stanayann iva dyauḥ ||5||

2indro valaṃ rakṣitāraṃ dughānāṃ kareṇeva vi cakartā raveṇa |
2svedāñjibhir āśiram ichamāno 'rodayat paṇim ā gā amuṣṇāt ||6||

2sa īṃ satyebhiḥ sakhibhiḥ śucadbhir godhāyasaṃ vi dhanasair adardaḥ |
2brahmaṇas patir vṛṣabhir varāhair gharmasvedebhir draviṇaṃ vy ānaṭ ||7||

2te satyena manasā gopatiṃ gā iyānāsa iṣaṇayanta dhībhiḥ |
2bṛhaspatir mithoavadyapebhir ud usriyā asṛjata svayugbhiḥ ||8||

2taṃ vardhayanto matibhiḥ śivābhiḥ siṃham iva nānadataṃ sadhasthe |
2bṛhaspatiṃ vṛṣaṇaṃ śūrasātau bharebhare anu madema jiṣṇum ||9||

20,91.10a yadā vājam asanad viśvarūpam ā dyām arukṣad uttarāṇi sadma |
20,91.10c bṛhaspatiṃ vṛṣaṇaṃ vardhayanto nānā santo bibhrato jyotir āsā ||10||

20,91.11a satyam āśiṣaṃ kṛṇutā vayodhai kīriṃ cid dhy avatha svebhir evaiḥ |
20,91.11c paścā mṛdho apa bhavantu viśvās tad rodasī śṛṇutaṃ viśvaminve ||11||

20,91.12a indro mahnā mahato arṇavasya vi mūrdhānam abhinad arbudasya |
20,91.12c ahann ahim ariṇāt sapta sindhūn devair dyāvāpṛthivī prāvataṃ naḥ ||12||



2abhi pra gopatiṃ girendram arca yathā vide |
2sūtuṃ satyasya satpatim ||1||

2ā harayaḥ sasṛjrire 'ruṣīr adhi barhiṣi |
2yatrābhi saṃnavāmahe ||2||

2indrāya gāva āśiraṃ duduhre vajriṇe madhu |
2yat sīm upahvare vidat ||3||

2ud yad bradhnasya viṣṭapaṃ gṛham indraś ca ganvahi |
2madhvaḥ pītvā sacevahi triḥ sapta sakhyuḥ pade ||4||

2arcata prārcata priyamedhāso arcata |
2arcantu putrakā uta puraṃ na dhṛṣṇv arcata ||5||

2ava svarāti gargaro godhā pari saniṣvaṇat |
2piṅgā pari caniṣkadad indrāya brahmodyatam ||6||

2ā yat patanty enyaḥ sudughā anapasphuraḥ |
2apasphuraṃ gṛbhāyata somam indrāya pātave ||7||

2apād indro apād agnir viśve devā amatsata |
2varuṇa id iha kṣayat tam āpo abhy anūṣata vatsaṃ saṃśiśvarīr iva ||8||

2sudevo asi varuṇa yasya te sapta sindhavaḥ |
2anukṣaranti kākudaṃ sūryaṃ suṣirām iva ||9||

20,92.10a yo vyatīṃr aphāṇayat suyuktāṃ upa dāśuṣe |
20,92.10c takvo netā tad id vapur upamā yo amucyata ||10||

20,92.11a atīd u śakra ohata indro viśvā ati dviṣaḥ |
20,92.11c bhinat kanīna odanaṃ pacyamānaṃ paro girā ||11||

20,92.12a arbhako na kumārako 'dhi tiṣṭhann avaṃ ratham |
20,92.12c sa pakṣan mahiṣaṃ mṛgaṃ pitre mātre vibhukratum ||12||

20,92.13a ā tū suśipra daṃpate rathaṃ tiṣṭhā hiraṇyayam |
20,92.13c adha dyukṣaṃ sacevahi sahasrapādam aruṣaṃ svastigām anehasam ||13||

20,92.14a tam ghem itthā namasvina upa svarājam āsate |
20,92.14c arthaṃ cid asya sudhitaṃ yad etave āvartayanti dāvane ||14||

20,92.15a anu pratnasyaukasaḥ priyamedhāsa eṣām |
20,92.15c pūrvām anu prayatiṃ vṛktabarhiṣo hitaprayasa āśata ||15||

20,92.16a yo rājā carṣaṇīnāṃ yātā rathebhir adhriguḥ |
20,92.16c viśvāsāṃ tarutā pṛtanānāṃ jyeṣṭho yo vṛtrahā gṛṇe ||16||

20,92.17a indraṃ taṃ śumbha puruhanmann avase yasya dvitā vidhartari |
20,92.17c hastāya vajraḥ prati dhāyi darśato maho dive na sūryaḥ ||17||

20,92.18a nakiṣ ṭaṃ karmaṇā naśad yaś cakāra sadāvṛdham |
20,92.18c indraṃ na yajñair viśvagūrtam ṛbhvasam adhṛṣṭaṃ dhṛṣṇvojasam ||18||

20,92.19a aṣālham ugraṃ pṛtanāsu sāsahiṃ yasmin mahīr urujrayaḥ |
20,92.19c saṃ dhenavo jāyamāne anonavur dyāvaḥ kṣāmo anonavuḥ ||19||

20,92.20a yad dyāva indra te śataṃ śataṃ bhūmīr uta syuḥ |
20,92.20c na tvā vajrint sahasraṃ sūryā anu na jātam aṣṭa rodasī ||20||

20,92.21a ā paprātha mahinā vṛṣṇyā vṛṣan viśvā śaviṣṭha śavasā |
20,92.21c asmāṃ ava maghavan gomati vraje vajriṃ citrābhir ūtibhiḥ ||21||


2ut tvā mandantu stomāḥ kṛṇuṣva rādho adrivaḥ |
2ava brahmadviṣo jahi ||1||

2padā paṇīṃr arādhaso ni bādhasva mahāṃ asi |
2nahi tvā kaś cana prati ||2||

2tvam īśiṣe sutānām indra tvam asutānām |
2tvaṃ rājā janānām ||3||

2īṅkhayantīr apasyuva indraṃ jātam upāsate |
2bhejānāsaḥ suvīryam ||4||

2tvam indra balād adhi sahaso jāta ojasaḥ |
2tvaṃ vṛṣan vṛṣed asi ||5||

2tvam indrāsi vṛtrahā vy antarikṣam atiraḥ |
2ud dyām astabhnā ojasā ||6||

2tvam indra sajoṣasam arkaṃ bibharṣi bāhvoḥ |
2vajraṃ śiśāna ojasā ||7||

2tvam indrābhibhur asi viśvā jātāny ojasā |
2sa viśvā bhuva ābhavaḥ ||8||



2ā yātv indraḥ svapatir madāya yo dharmaṇā tūtujānas tuviṣmān |
2pratvakṣāṇo ati viśvā sahāṃsy apāreṇa mahatā vṛṣṇyena ||1||

2suṣṭhāmā rathaḥ suyamā harī te mimyakṣa vajro nṛpate gabhastau |
2śībhaṃ rājan supathā yāhy arvāṅ vardhāma te papuso vṛṣṇyāni ||2||

2endravāho nṛpatiṃ vajrabāhum ugram ugrāsas taviṣāsa enam |
2pratvakṣasaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ satyaśuṣmam em asmatrā sadhamādo vahantu ||3||

2evā patiṃ droṇasācaṃ sacetasam ūrja skambhaṃ dharuṇa ā vṛṣāyase |
2ojaḥ kṛṣva saṃ gṛbhāya tve apy aso yathā kenipānām ino vṛdhe ||4||

2gamann asme vasūny ā hi śaṃsiṣaṃ svāśiṣaṃ bharam ā yāhi sominaḥ |
2tvam īśiṣe sāsminn ā satsi barhiṣy anādhṛṣyā tava pātrāṇi dharmaṇā ||5||

2pṛthak prāyan prathamā devahūtayo 'kṛṇvata śravasyāni duṣṭarā |
2na ye śekur yajñiyāṃ nāvam āruham irmaiva te ny aviśanta kepayaḥ ||6||

2evaivāpāg apare santu dūdhyo 'śvā yeṣāṃ duryuga āyuyujre |
2itthā ye prāg upare santi dāvane purūṇi yatra vayunāni bhojanā ||7||
2girīṃr ajrān rejamānāṃ adhārayad dyauḥ krandad antarikṣāṇi kopayat |
2samīcīne dhiṣaṇe vi ṣkabhāyati vṛṣṇaḥ pītvā mada ukthāni śaṃsati ||8||

2imaṃ bibharmi sukṛtaṃ te aṅkuśaṃ yenārujāsi maghavaṃ chaphārujaḥ |
2asmint su te savane astv oktyaṃ suta iṣṭau maghavan bodhy ābhagaḥ ||9||

20,94.10a gobhiṣ ṭaremāmatiṃ durevāṃ yavena kṣudhaṃ puruhūta viśvām |
20,94.10c vayaṃ rājabhiḥ prathamā dhanāny asmākena vṛjanenā jayema ||10||

20,94.11a bṛhaspatir naḥ pari pātu paścād utottarasmād adharād aghayoḥ |
20,94.11c indraḥ purastād uta madhyato naḥ sakhā sakhibhyo varivaḥ kṛṇotu ||11||


2trikadrukeṣu mahiṣo yavāśiraṃ tuviśuṣmas tṛpat somam apibad viṣṇunā sutaṃ yathāvaśat |
2sa īṃ mamāda mahi karma kartave mahām uruṃ sainaṃ saścad devo devaṃ satyam indraṃ satya induḥ ||1||

2pro ṣv asmai puroratham indrāya śūṣam arcata |
2abhīke cid u lokakṛt saṃge samatsu vṛtrahāsmākaṃ bodhi coditā nabhantām anyakeṣāṃ jyākā adhi dhanvasu ||2||

2tvaṃ sindhūṃr avāsṛjo 'dharāco ahann ahim |
2aśatrur indra jajñiṣe viśvaṃ puṣyasi vāryaṃ taṃ tvā pari ṣvajāmahe nabhantām anyakeṣāṃ jyākā adhi dhanvasu ||3||

2vi ṣu viśvā arātayo 'ryo naśanta no dhiyaḥ |
2astāsi śatrave vadhaṃ yo na indra jighāṃsati yā te rātir dadir vasu |
2nabhantām anyakeṣāṃ jyakā adhi dhanvasu ||4||



2tīvrasyābhivayaso asya pāhi sarvarathā vi harī iha muñca |
2indra mā tvā yajamānāso anye ni rīraman tubhyam ime sutāsaḥ ||1||

2tubhyaṃ sutās tubhyam u sotvāsas tvāṃ giraḥ śvātryā ā hvayanti |
2indredam adya savanaṃ juṣāṇo viśvasya vidvāṃ iha pāhi somam ||2||

2ya uśatā manasā somam asmai sarvahṛdā devakāmaḥ sunoti |
2na gā indras tasya parā dadāti praśastam ic cārum asmai kṛṇoti ||3||
2anuspaṣṭo bhavaty eṣo asya yo asmai revān na sunoti somam |
2nir aratnau maghavā taṃ dadhāti brahmadviṣo hanty anānudiṣṭaḥ ||4||

2aśvāyanto gavyanto vājayanto havāmahe tvopagantavā u |
2ābhūṣantas te sumatau navāyāṃ vayam indra tvā śunaṃ huvema ||5||

2muñcāmi tvā haviṣā jīvanāya kam ajñātayakṣmād uta rājayakṣmāt |
2grāhir jagrāha yady etad tasyā indrāgnī pra mumuktam enam ||6||

2yadi kṣitāyur yadi vā pareto yadi mṛtyor antikaṃ nīta eva |
2tam ā harāmi nirṛter upasthād aspārśam enaṃ śataśāradāya ||7||

2sahasrākṣeṇa śatavīryeṇa śatāyuṣā haviṣāhārṣam enam |
2indro yathainaṃ śarado nayāty ati viśvasya duritasya pāram ||8||

2śataṃ jīva śarado vardhamānaḥ śataṃ hemantān chatam u vasantān |
2śataṃ ta indro agniḥ savitā bṛhaspatiḥ śatāyuṣā haviṣāhārṣam enam ||9||

20,96.10a āhārṣam avidaṃ tvā punar āgāḥ punarṇavaḥ |
20,96.10c sarvāṅga sarvaṃ te cakṣuḥ sarvam āyuś ca te 'vidam ||10||
20,96.11a brahmaṇāgniḥ samvidāno rakṣohā bādhatām itaḥ |
20,96.11c amīvā yas te garbhaṃ durṇāmā yonim āśaye ||11||

20,96.12a yas te garbham amīvā durṇāmā yonim āśaye |
20,96.12c agniṣ ṭaṃ brahmaṇā saha niṣ kravyādam anīnaśat ||12||

20,96.13a yas te hanti patayantaṃ niṣatsnuṃ yaḥ sarīsṛpam |
20,96.13c jātaṃ yas te jighāṃsati tam ito nāśayāmasi ||13||

20,96.14a yas ta ūrū viharaty antarā dampatī śaye |
20,96.14c yoniṃ yo antar ārelhi tam ito nāśayāmasi ||14||

20,96.15a yas tvā bhrātā patir bhūtvā jāro bhūtvā nipadyate |
20,96.15c prajāṃ yas te jighāṃsati tam ito nāśayāmasi ||15||

20,96.16a yas tvā svapnena tamasā mohayitvā nipadyate |
20,96.16c prajāṃ yas te jighāṃsati tam ito nāśayāmasi ||16||

20,96.17a akṣībhyāṃ te nāsikābhyāṃ karṇābhyāṃ chubukād adhi |
20,96.17c yakṣmaṃ śīrṣaṇyaṃ mastiṣkāj jihvāyā vi vṛhāmi te ||17||

20,96.18a grīvābhyas ta uṣṇihābhyaḥ kīkasābhyo anūkyāt |
20,96.18c yakṣmaṃ doṣaṇyam aṃsābhyāṃ bāhubhyāṃ vi vṛhāmi te ||18||

20,96.19a hṛdayāt te pari klomno halīkṣṇāt pārśvābhyām |
20,96.19c yakṣmaṃ matasnābhyāṃ plīhno yaknas te vi vṛhāmasi ||19||

20,96.20a āntrebhyas te gudābhyo vaniṣṭhor udarād adhi |
20,96.20c yakṣmaṃ kukṣibhyāṃ plāśer nābhyā vi vṛhāmi te ||20||

20,96.21a ūrubhyāṃ te aṣṭhīvadbhyāṃ pārṣṇibhyāṃ prapadābhyām |
20,96.21c yakṣmaṃ bhasadyaṃ śroṇibhyāṃ bhāsadaṃ bhāṃsaso vi vṛhāmi te ||21||

20,96.22[-]a mehanād vanaṃkaraṇāl lomabhyas te nakhebhyaḥ |
20,96.22[-]c yakṣmaṃ sarvasmād ātmanas tam idaṃ vi vṛhāmi te ||22||

20,96.[-]22a asthibhyas te majjabhyaḥ snāvabhyo dhamanibhyaḥ |
20,96.[-]22b yakṣmaṃ pāṇibhyām aṅgulibhyo nakhebhyo vi vṛhāmi te ||22||

20,96.23a aṅgeaṅge lomnilomni yas te parvaṇiparvaṇi |
20,96.23c yakṣaṃ tvacasyaṃ te vayaṃ kaśyapasya vībarheṇa viṣvañcaṃ vi vṛhāmasi ||23||

20,96.24a apehi manasas pate 'pa kāma paraś cara |
20,96.24c paro nirṛtyā ā cakṣva bahudhā jīvato manaḥ ||24||



2vayam enam idā hyopīpemeha vajriṇam |
2tasmā u adya samanā sutaṃ bharā nūnaṃ bhūṣata śrute ||1||

2vṛkaś cid asya vāraṇa urāmathir ā vayuneṣu bhūṣati |
2semaṃ naḥ stomaṃ jujuṣāṇa ā gahīndra pra citrayā dhiyā ||2||

2kad u nv asyākṛtam indrasyāsti pauṃsyam |
2keno nu kaṃ śromatena na śuśruve januṣaḥ pari vṛtrahā ||3||



2tvām id dhi havāmahe sātā vājasya kāravaḥ |
2tvāṃ vṛtreṣv indra satpatiṃ naras tvāṃ kāṣṭhāsv arvataḥ ||1||

2sa tvaṃ naś citra vajrahasta dhṛṣṇuyā maha stavāno adrivaḥ |
2gām aśvaṃ rathyam indra saṃ kira satrā vājaṃ na jigyuṣe ||2||



2abhi tvā pūrvapītaya indra stomebhir āyavaḥ |
2samīcīnāsa ṛbhavaḥ sam asvaran rudrā gṛṇanta pūrvyam ||1||

2asyed indro vāvṛdhe vṛṣṇyaṃ śavo made sutasya viṣṇavi |
2adyā tam asya mahimānam āyavo 'nu ṣṭuvanti pūrvathā ||2||



adhā hīndra girvaṇa upa tvā kāmān mahaḥ sasṛjmahe |
udeva yanta udabhiḥ ||1||

vār ṇa tvā yavyābhir vardhanti śūra brahmāṇi |
vāvṛdhvāṃsaṃ cid adrivo divedive ||2||

yuñjanti harī iṣirasya gāthayorau ratha uruyuge |
indravāhā vacoyujā ||3||


agniṃ dūtaṃ vṛṇīmahe hotāraṃ viśvavedasam |
asya yajñasya sukratum ||1||

agnimagniṃ havīmabhiḥ sadā havanta viśpatim |
havyavāhaṃ purupriyam ||2||

agne devāṃ ihā vaha jajñāno vṛktabarhiṣe |
asi hotā na īḍyaḥ ||3||



īlenyo namasyas tiras tamāṃsi darśataḥ |
sam agnir idhyate vṛṣā ||1||

vṛṣo agniḥ sam idhyate 'śvo na devavāhanaḥ |
taṃ haviṣmantaḥ īlate ||2||

vṛṣaṇaṃ tvā vayaṃ vṛṣan vṛṣaṇaḥ sam idhīmahi |
agne dīdyataṃ bṛhat ||3||



agnim īliṣvāvase gāthābhiḥ śīraśociṣam |
agniṃ rāye purumīlha śrutaṃ naro 'gniṃ sudītaye chardiḥ ||1||

agna ā yāhy agnibhir hotāraṃ tvā vṛṇīmahe |
ā tvām anaktu prayatā haviṣmatī yajiṣṭhaṃ barhir āsade ||2||

acha hi tvā sahasaḥ sūno aṅgiraḥ srucaś caranty adhvare |
ūrjo napātaṃ ghṛtakeśam īmahe 'gniṃ yajñeṣu pūrvyam ||3||



imā u tvā purūvaso giro vardhantu yā mama |
pāvakavarṇāḥ śucayo vipaścito 'bhi stomair anūṣata ||1||

ayaṃ sahasram ṛṣibhiḥ sahaskṛtaḥ samudra iva paprathe |
satyaḥ so asya mahimā gṛne śavo yajñeṣu viprarājye ||2||

ā no viśvāsu havya indraḥ samatsu bhūṣatu |
upa brahmāṇi savanāni vṛtrahā paramajyā ṛcīṣamaḥ ||3||

tvaṃ dātā prathamo rāghasām asy asi satya īśānakṛt |
tuvidyumnasya yujyā vṛṇīmahe putrasya śavaso mahaḥ ||4||



tvam indra pratūrtiṣv abhi viśvā asi spṛdhaḥ |
aśastihā janitā viśvatūr asi tvaṃ tūrya taruṣyataḥ ||1||

anu te śuṣmaṃ turayantam īyatuḥ kṣoṇī śiśuṃ na mātarā |
viśvās te spṛdhaḥ śnathayanta manyave vṛtraṃ yad indra tūrvasi ||2||

ita ūtī vo ajaraṃ prahetāram aprahitam |
āśuṃ jetāraṃ hetāraṃ rathītamam atūrtaṃ tugryāvṛdham ||3||

yo rājā carṣaṇīnāṃ yātā rathebhir adhriguḥ |
viśvāsāṃ tarutā pṛtanānāṃ jyeṣṭho yo vṛtrahā gṛṇe ||4||

indraṃ taṃ śumbha puruhanmann avase yasya dvitā vidhartari |
hastāya vajraḥ prati dhāyi darśato maho dive na sūryaḥ ||5||


tava tyad indriyaṃ bṛhat tava śuṣmam uta kratum |
vajraṃ śiśāti dhiṣaṇā vareṇyam ||1||

tava dyaur indra pauṃsyaṃ pṛthivī vardhati śravaḥ |
tvām āpaḥ parvatāsaś ca hinvire ||2||

tvāṃ viṣṇur bṛhan kṣayo mitro gṛṇāti varuṇaḥ |
tvāṃ śardho madaty anu mārutam ||3||



sam asya manyave viśo viśvā namanta kuṣṭayaḥ |
samudrāyeva sindhavaḥ ||1||

ojas tad asya titviṣa ubhe yat samavartayat |
indraś carmeva rodasī ||2||

vi cid vṛtrasya dodhato vajreṇa śataparvaṇā |
śiro bibhed vṛṣṇinā ||3||

tad id āsa bhuvaneṣu jyeṣṭhaṃ yato jajña ugras tveṣanṛmṇaḥ |
sadyo jajñāno ni riṇāti śatrūn anu yad enaṃ madanti viśva ūmāḥ ||4||

vāvṛdhānaḥ śavasā bhūryojāḥ śatrur dāsāya bhiyasaṃ dadhāti |
avyanac ca vyanac ca sasni saṃ te navanta prabhṛtā madeṣu ||5||

tve kratum api pṛñcanti bhūri dvir yad ete trir bhavanty ūmāḥ |
svādoḥ svādīyaḥ svādunā sṛjā sam adaḥ su madhu madhunābhi yodhīḥ ||6||

yadi cin nu tvā dhanā jayantaṃ raṇeraṇe anumadanti viprāḥ |
ojīyaḥ śuṣmint sthiram ā tanuṣva mā tvā dabhan durevāsaḥ kaśokāḥ ||7||

tvayā vayaṃ śāśadmahe raṇeṣu prapaśyanto yudhenyāni bhūri |
codayāmi ta āyudhā vacobhiḥ saṃ te śiśāmi brahmaṇā vayāṃsi ||8||

ni tad dadhiṣe 'vare pare ca yasminn āvithāvasā duroṇe |
ā sthāpayata mātaraṃ jigatnum ata invata karvarāṇi bhūri ||9||

20,107.10a stuṣva varṣman puruvartmānaṃ sam ṛbhvāṇam inatamam āptam āptyānām |
20,107.10c ā darśati śavasā bhūryojāḥ pra sakṣati pratimānaṃ pṛthivyāḥ ||10||

20,107.11a imā brahma bṛhaddivaḥ kṛṇavad indrāya śūṣam agniyaḥ svarṣāḥ |
20,107.11c maho gotrasya kṣayati svarājā turaś cid viśvam arṇavat tapasvān ||11||

20,107.12a evā mahān bṛhaddivo atharvāvocat svāṃ tanvam indram eva |
20,107.12c svasārau mātaribhvarī aripre hinvanti caine śavasā vardhayanti ca ||12||

20,107.13a citraṃ devānāṃ ketur anīkaṃ jyotiṣmān pradiśaḥ sūrya udyan |
20,107.13c divākaro 'ti dyumnais tamāṃsi viśvātārīd duritāni śukraḥ ||13||

20,107.14a citraṃ devānām ud agād anīkaṃ cakṣur mitrasya varuṇasyāgneḥ |
20,107.14c āprād dyāvāpṛthivī antarikṣaṃ sūrya ātmā jagatas tasthuṣaś ca ||14||

20,107.15a sūryo devīm uṣasaṃ rocamānāṃ maryo na yoṣām abhy eti paścāt |
20,107.15c yatrā naro devayanto yugāni vitanvate prati bhadrāya bhadram ||15||



tvaṃ na indrā bharaṃ ojo nṛmṇaṃ śatakrato vicarṣaṇe |
ā vīraṃ pṛtanāṣaham ||1||
tvaṃ hi naḥ pitā vaso tvaṃ mātā śatakrato babhūvitha |
adhā te sumnam īmahe ||2||

tvāṃ śuṣmin puruhūta vājayantam upa bruve śatakrato |
sa no rāsva suvīryam ||3||



svādor itthā viṣuvato madhvaḥ pibanti gauryaḥ |
yā indreṇa sayāvarīr vṛṣṇā madanti śobhase vasvīr anu svarājyam ||1||

tā asya pṛśanāyuvaḥ somaṃ śrīṇanti pṛśnayaḥ |
priyā indrasya dhenavo vajraṃ hinvanti sāyakaṃ vasvīr anu svarājyam ||2||

tā asya namasā sahaḥ saparyanti pracetasaḥ |
vratāny asya saścire purūṇi pūrvacittaye vasvīr anu svarājyam ||3||



indrāya madūne sutaṃ pari ṣṭobhantu no giraḥ |
arkam arcantu kāravaḥ ||1||

yasmin viśvā adhi śriyo raṇanti sapta saṃsadaḥ |
indraṃ sute havāmahe ||2||

trikadrukeṣu cetanaṃ devāso yajñam atnata |
tam id vardhantu no giraḥ ||3||



yat somam indra viṣṇavi yad vā gha trita āptye |
yad vā marutsu mandase sam indubhiḥ ||1||

yad vā śakra parāvati samudre adhi mandase |
asmākam it sute raṇā sam indubhiḥ ||2||

yad vāsi sunvato vṛdho yajamānasya satpate |
ukthe vā yasya raṇyasi sam indubhiḥ ||3||


yad adya kac ca vṛtrahann udagā abhi sūrya |
sarvaṃ tad indra te vaśe ||1||

yad vā pravṛddha satpate na marā iti manyase |
uto tat satyam it tava ||2||

ye somāsaḥ parāvati ye arvāvati sunvire |
sarvāṃs tāṃ indra gachasi ||3||



ubhayaṃ śṛṇavac ca na indro arvāg idaṃ vacaḥ |
satrācyā maghavā somapītaye dhiyā śaviṣṭha ā gamat ||1||
taṃ hi svarājaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ tam ojase dhiṣaṇe niṣṭatakṣatuḥ |
utopamānāṃ prathamo ni ṣīdasi somakāmaṃ hi te manaḥ ||2||



abhrātṛvyo'anā tvam anāpir indra januṣā sanād asi |
yudhed āpitvam ichase ||1||

nakī revantaṃ sakhyāya vindase pīyanti te surāśvaḥ |
yadā kṛṇoṣi nadanuṃ sam ūhasy ād it piteva hūyase ||2||



aham id dhi pituṣ pari medhām ṛtasya jagrabha |
ahaṃ sūrya ivājani ||1||

ahaṃ pratnena manmanā giraḥ śumbhāmi kaṇvavat |
yenendraḥ śuṣmam id dadhe ||2||

ye tvām indra na tuṣṭuvur ṛṣayo ye ca tuṣṭuvuḥ |
mamed vardhasva suṣṭutaḥ ||3||


mā bhūma niṣṭyā ivendra tvad araṇā iva |
vanāni ni prajahitāny adrivo duroṣāso amanmahi ||1||

amanmahīd anāśavo 'nugrāsaś ca vṛtrahan |
sukṛt su te mahatā śūra rādhasānu stomaṃ mudīmahi ||2||



pibā somam indra mandatu tvā yaṃ te suṣāva haryaśvādriḥ |
sotur bāhubhyāṃ suyato nārvā ||1||

yas te mado yujas cārur asti yena vṛtrāṇi haryaśva haṃsi |
sa tvām indra prabhūvaso mamattu ||2||

bodhā su me maghavan vācam emāṃ yāṃ te vasiṣṭho arcati praśastim |
imā brahma sadhamāde juṣasva ||3||



śagdhy ū ṣu śacīpata indra viśvābhir ūtibhiḥ |
bhagaṃ na hi tvā yaśasaṃ vasuvidam anu śūra carāmasi ||1||

pauro aśvasya purukṛd gavām asy utso deva hiraṇyayaḥ |
nakir hi dānaṃ parimardhiṣat tve yadyad yāmi tad ā bhara ||2||

indram id devatātaye indraṃ prayaty adhvare |
indraṃ samīke vanino havāmaha indraṃ dhanasya sātaye ||3||

indro mahnā rodasī paprathac chava indraḥ sūryam arocayat |
indre ha viśvā bhuvanāni yemira indre suvānāsa indavaḥ ||4||



astāvi manma pūrvyaṃ brahmendrāya vocata |
pūrvīr ṛtasya bṛhatīr anūṣata stotur meghā asṛkṣata ||1||

turaṇyavo madhumantaṃ ghṛtaścutaṃ viprāso arkam ānṛcuḥ |
asme rayiḥ paprathe vṛṣṇyaṃ śavo 'sme suvānāsa indavaḥ ||2||



yad indra prāg apāg udaṅ nyag vā hūyase nṛbhiḥ |
simā purū nṛṣūto asy ānave 'si praśardha turvaśe ||1||

yad vā rume ruśame śyāvake kṛpa indra mādayase sacā |
kaṇvāsas tvā brahmabhi stomavāhasa indrā yachanty ā gahi ||2||


abhi tvā śūra nonumo 'dugdhā iva dhenavaḥ |
īśānam asya jagataḥ svardṛśam īśānam indra tasthuṣaḥ ||1||

na tvāvāṃ anyo divyo na pārthivo na jāto na janiṣyate |
aśvāyanto maghavann indra vājino gavyantas tvā havāmahe ||2||



revatīr naḥ sadhamāda indre santu tuvivājāḥ |
kṣumanto yābhir madema ||1||

ā gha tvāvān tmanāpta stotṛbhyo dhṛṣṇav iyānaḥ |
ṛṇor akṣaṃ na cakrayoḥ ||2||

ā yad duvaḥ śatakratav ā kāmaṃ jaritṝṇām |
ṛṇor akṣaṃ na śacībhiḥ ||3||



tat sūryasya devatvaṃ tan mahitvaṃ madhyā kartor vitataṃ saṃ jabhāra |
yaded ayukta haritaḥ sadhasthād ād rātrī vāsas tanute simasmai ||1||

tan mitrasya varuṇasyābhicakṣe sūryo rūpaṃ kṛṇute dyor upasthe |
anantam anyad ruśad asya prājaḥ kṛṣṇam anyad dharitaḥ saṃ bharanti ||2||



kayā naś citra ā bhuvad ūtī sadāvṛdhaḥ sakhā |
kayā śaciṣṭhayā vṛtā ||1||

kas tvā satyo madānāṃ maṃhiṣṭho matsad andhasaḥ |
dṛlhā cid āruje vasu ||2||

abhī ṣu naḥ sakhīnām avitā jaritṝṇām |
śataṃ bhavāsy ūtibhiḥ ||3||

imā nu kaṃ bhuvanā sīṣadhāmendraś ca viśve ca devāḥ |
yajñaṃ ca nas tanvaṃ ca prajāṃ cādityair indraḥ saha cīkḷpāti ||4||

ādityair indraḥ sagaṇo marudbhir asmākaṃ bhūtv avitā tanūnām |
hatvāya devā asurān yad āyan devā devatvam abhirakṣamāṇāḥ ||5||

pratyañcam arkam anayaṃ chacībhir ād it svadhām iṣirām pary apaśyan |
ayā vājaṃ devahitaṃ sanema madema śatahimāḥ suvīrāḥ ||6||



apendra prāco maghavann amitrān apāpāco abhibhūte nudasva |
apodīco apa śūrādharāca urau yathā tava śarman madema ||1||

kuvid aṅga yavamanto yavaṃ cid yathā dānty anupūrvaṃ viyūya |
ihehaiṣāṃ kṛṇuhi bhojanāni ye barhiṣo namovṛktiṃ na jagmuḥ ||2||

nahi sthūry ṛtuthā yātam asti nota śravo vivide saṃgameṣu |
gavyanta indraṃ sakhyāya viprā aśvāyanto vṛṣaṇaṃ vājayantaḥ ||3||

yuvaṃ surāmam aśvinā namucāv āsure sacā |
vipipānā śubhas patī indraṃ karmasv āvatam ||4||

putram iva pitarāv aśvinobhendrāvathuḥ kāvyair daṃsanābhiḥ |
yat surāmaṃ vy apibaḥ śacībhiḥ sarasvatī tvā maghavann abhiṣṇak ||5||

indraḥ sutrāmā svavāṃ avobhiḥ sumṛḍīko bhavatu viśvavedāḥ |
bādhatāṃ dveṣo abhayaṃ naḥ kṛṇotu suvīryasya patayaḥ syāma ||6||

sa sutrāmā svavāṃ indro asmad ārāc cid dveṣaḥ sanutar yuyotu |
tasya vayaṃ sumatau yajñiyasyāpi bhadre saumanase syāma ||7||



vi hi sotor asṛkṣata nendraṃ devam amaṃsata |
yatrāmadad vṛṣākapir aryaḥ puṣṭeṣu matsakhā viśvasmād indra uttaraḥ ||1||

parā hīndra dhāvasi vṛṣākaper ati vyathiḥ |
no aha pra vindasy anyatra somapītaye viśvasmād indra uttaraḥ ||2||

kim ayaṃ tvāṃ vṛṣākapiś cakāra harito mṛgaḥ |
yasmā irasyasīd u nv aryo vā puṣṭimad vasu viśvasmād indra uttaraḥ ||3||

yam imaṃ tvaṃ vṛṣākapiṃ priyam indrābhirakṣasi |
śvā nv asya jambhiṣad api karṇe varāhayur viśvasmād indra uttaraḥ ||4||

priyā taṣṭāni me kapir vyaktā vy adūduṣat |
śiro nv asya rāviṣaṃ na sugaṃ duṣkṛte bhuvaṃ viśvasmād indra uttaraḥ ||5||

na mat strī subhasattarā na suyāśutarā bhuvat |
na mat praticyavīyasī na sakthy udyamīyasī viśvasmād indra uttaraḥ ||6||

uve amba sulābhike yathevāṅgaṃ bhaviṣyati |
bhasan me amba sakthi me śiro me vīva hṛṣyati viśvasmād indra uttaraḥ ||7||

kiṃ subāho svaṅgure pṛthuṣṭo pṛthujāghane |
kiṃ śūrapatni nas tvam abhy amīṣi vṛṣākapiṃ viśvasmād indra uttaraḥ ||8||

avīrām iva mām ayaṃ śarārur abhi manyate |
utāham asmi vīriṇīndrapatnī marutsakhā viśvasmād indra uttaraḥ ||9||

20,126.10a saṃhotraṃ sma purā nārī samanaṃ vāva gachati |
20,126.10c vedhā ṛtasya vīriṇīndrapatnī mahīyate viśvasmād indra uttaraḥ ||10||

20,126.11a indrāṇīm āsu nāriṣu subhagām aham aśravam |
20,126.11c nahy asyā aparaṃ cana jarasā marate patir viśvasmād indra uttaraḥ ||11||

20,126.12a nāham indrāṇi rāraṇa sakhyur vṛṣākaper ṛte |
20,126.12c yasyedam apyaṃ haviḥ priyaṃ deveṣu gachati viśvasmād indra uttaraḥ ||12||

20,126.13a vṛsākapāyi revati suputra ād u susnuṣe |
20,126.13c ghasat ta indra ukṣaṇaḥ priyaṃ kācitkaraṃ havir viśvasmād indra uttaraḥ ||13||

20,126.14a ukṣṇo hi me pañcadaśa sākaṃ pacanti viṃsatim |
20,126.14c utāham admi pīva id ubhā kukṣī pṛṇanti me viśvasmād indra uttaraḥ ||14||

20,126.15a vṛṣabho na tigmaśṛṅgo 'ntar yūtheṣu roruvat |
20,126.15c manthas ta indra śaṃ hṛde yaṃ te sunoti bhāvayur viśvasmād indra uttaraḥ ||15||

20,126.16a na seśe yasya rambate 'ntarā sakthyā kapṛt |
20,126.16c sedīśe yasya romaśaṃ niṣeduṣo vijṛmbhate viśvasmād indra uttaraḥ ||16||

20,126.17a na seśe yasya romaśaṃ niṣeduṣo vijṛmbhate |
20,126.17c sedīśe yasya rambate 'ntarā sakthyā kapṛt viśvasmād indra uttaraḥ ||17||

20,126.18a ayam indra vṛṣākapiḥ parasvantaṃ hataṃ vidat |
20,126.18c asiṃ sūnāṃ navaṃ carum ād edhasyāna ācitaṃ viśvasmād indra uttaraḥ ||18||

20,126.19a ayam emi vicākaśad vicinvan dāsam āryam |
20,126.19c pibāmi pākasutvano 'bhi dhīram acākaśaṃ viśvasmād indra uttaraḥ ||19||

20,126.20a dhanva ca yat kṛntatraṃ ca kati svit tā vi yojanā |
20,126.20c nedīyaso vṛṣākape 'stam ehi gṛhāṃ upa viśvasmād indra uttaraḥ ||20||

20,126.21a punar ehi vṛṣākape suvitā kalpayāvahai |
20,126.21c ya eṣa svapnanaṃśano 'stam eṣi pathā punar viśvasmād indra uttaraḥ ||21||

20,126.22a yad udañco vṛṣākape gṛham indrājagantana |
20,126.22c kva sya pulvagho mṛgaḥ kam agaṃ janayopano viśvasmād indra uttaraḥ ||22||

20,126.23a parśur ha nāma mānavī sākaṃ sasūva viṃśatim |
20,126.23c bhadraṃ bhala tyasyā abhūd yasyā udaram āmayad viśvasmād indra uttaraḥ ||23||


idaṃ janā upa śruta narāśaṃsa staviṣyate |
ṣaṣṭiṃ sahasrā navatiṃ ca kaurama ā ruśameṣu dadmahe ||1||

uṣṭrā yasya pravāhaṇo vadhūmanto dvirdaśa |
varṣmā rathasya ni jihīḍate diva īṣamāṇā upaspṛśaḥ ||2||

eṣa iṣāya māmahe śataṃ niṣkān daśa srajaḥ |
trīṇi śatānyarvatāṃ sahasrā daśa gonām ||3||

vacyasva rebha vacyasva vṛkṣe na pakve śakunaḥ |
naṣṭe jihvā carcarīti kṣuro na bhurijoriva ||4||

pra rebhāso manīṣā vṛṣā gāva iverate |
amotaputrakā eṣāmamota gā ivāsate ||5||

pra rebha dhīm bharasva govidaṃ vasuvidam |
devatremāṃ vācaṃ srīṇīhīṣurnāvīrastāram ||6||

rājño viśvajanīnasya yo devomartyāṃ ati |
vaiśvānarasya suṣṭutimā sunotā parikṣitaḥ ||7||

parichinnaḥ kṣemam akarot tama āsanamācaran |
kulāyan kṛṇvan kauravyaḥ patir vadati jāyayā ||8||

katarat ta ā harāṇi dadhi manthāṃ pari śrutam |
jāyāḥ patiṃ vi pṛchati rāṣṭre rājñaḥ parikṣitaḥ ||9||

20,127.10a abhīvasvaḥ pra jihīte yavaḥ pakvaḥ patho bilam |
20,127.10c janaḥ sa bhadram edhati rāṣṭre rājñaḥ parikṣitaḥ ||10||

20,127.11a indraḥ kārum abūbudhad uttiṣṭha vi carā janam |
20,127.11c mamedugrasya carkṛdhi sarva it te pṛṇādariḥ ||11||

20,127.12a iha gāvaḥ pra jāyadhvam ihāśvā iha pūruṣāḥ |
20,127.12c iho sahasradakṣiṇopi pūṣā ni ṣīdati ||12||

20,127.13a nemā indra gāvo riṣan mo āsāṃ gopa rīriṣat |
20,127.13c māsām amitrayurjana indra mā stena īśata ||13||

20,127.14a upa no na ramasi sūktena vacasā vayaṃ bhadreṇa vacasā vayam |
20,127.14c vanād adhidhvano giro na riṣyema kadā cana ||14||


yaḥ sabheyo vidathyaḥ sutvā yajvātha pūruṣaḥ |
sūryaṃ cāmū riśādasas tad devāḥ prāg akalpayan ||1||

yo jāmyā aprathayas tad yat sakhāyaṃ dudhūrṣati |
jyeṣṭho yad apracetās tad āhur adharāg iti ||2||

yad bhadrasya puruṣasya putro bhavati dādhṛṣiḥ |
tad vipro abravīd u tad gandharvaḥ kāmyaṃ vacaḥ ||3||

yaśca paṇi raghujiṣṭhyo yaśca devāṃ adāśuriḥ |
dhīrāṇāṃ śaśvatām ahaṃ tad apāg iti śuśruma ||4||

ye ca devā ayajantātho ye ca parādadiḥ |
sūryo divam iva gatvāya maghavā no vi rapśate ||5||

yo'nāktākṣo anabhyakto amaṇivo ahiraṇyavaḥ |
abrahmā brahmaṇaḥ putrastotā kalpeṣu saṃmitā ||6||
ya āktākṣaḥ subhyaktaḥ sumaṇiḥ suhiraṇyavaḥ |
subrahmā brahmaṇaḥ putrastotā kalpeṣu saṃmitā ||7||

aprapāṇā ca veśantā revāṃ apratidiśyayaḥ |
ayabhyā kanyā kalyāṇī totā kalpeṣu saṃmitā ||8||

suprapāṇā ca veśantā revānt supratidiśyayaḥ |
suyabhyā kanyā kalyāṇī totā kalpeṣu saṃmitā ||9||

20,128.10a parivṛktā ca mahiṣī svastyā ca yudhiṃ gamaḥ |
20,128.10c anāśuraścāyāmī totā kalpeṣu saṃmitā ||10||

20,128.11a vāvātā ca mahiṣī svastyā ca yudhiṃ gamaḥ |
20,128.11c śvāśuraś cāyāmī totā kalpeṣu saṃmitā ||11||

20,128.12a yad indrādo dāśarājñe mānuṣaṃ vi gāhathāḥ |
20,128.12c virūpaḥ sarvasmā āsīt saha yakṣāya kalpate ||12||
20,128.13a tvaṃ vṛṣākṣuṃ maghavann amraṃ maryākaro raviḥ |
20,128.13c tvaṃ rauhiṇaṃ vyāsyo vi vṛtrasyābhinac chiraḥ ||13||

20,128.14a yaḥ parvatān vyadadhād yo apo vyagāhathāḥ |
20,128.14c indro yo vṛtrahānmahaṃ tasmād indra namo 'stu te ||14||

20,128.15a pṛṣṭhaṃ dhāvantaṃ haryor auccaiḥ śravasam abruvan |
20,128.15c svastyaśva jaitrāyendram ā vaha susrajam ||15||

20,128.16a ye tvā śvetā ajaiśravaso hāryo yuñjanti dakṣiṇam |
20,128.16c pūrvā namasya devānāṃ bibhrad indra mahīyate ||16||

vitatau kiraṇau dvau tāvā pinaṣṭi pūruṣaḥ |
na vai kumāri tat tathā yathā kumāri manyase ||1||

mātuṣṭe kiraṇau dvau nivṛttaḥ puruṣānṛte |
na vai kumāri tat tathā yathā kumāri manyase ||2||

nigṛhya karṇakau dvau nirāyachasi madhyame |
na vai kumāri tat tathā yathā kumāri manyase ||3||

uttānāyai śayānāyai tiṣṭhantī vāva gūhasi |
na vai kumāri tat tathā yathā kumāri manyase ||4||
ślakṣṇāyāṃ ślakṣṇikāyāṃ ślakṣṇamevāva gūhasi |
na vai kumāri tat tathā yathā kumāri manyase ||5||

avaślakṣṇamiva bhraṃśad antarlomamati hrade |
na vai kumāri tat tathā yathā kumāri manyase ||6||



ihettha prāgapāgudagadharāg arālāgudabhartsatha ||1||

ihettha prāgapāgudagadharāg vatsāḥ puruṣanta āsate ||2||

ihettha prāgapāgudagadharāk sthālīpāko vi līyate ||3||

ihettha prāgapāgudagadharāk sa vai pṛthu līyate ||4||

ihettha prāgapāgudagadharāg āste lāhaṇi līśāthī ||5||

ihettha prāgapāgudagadharāg akṣlilī puchilīyate ||6||


bhug ity abhigataḥ śalityapakrāntaḥ phalityabhiṣṭhitaḥ |
dundubhim āhananābhyāṃ jaritarothāmo daiva ||1||

kośabile rajani granther dhānam upānahi pādam |
uttamāṃ janimāṃ janyānuttamāṃ janīn vartmanyāt ||2||

alābūni pṛṣātakānyaśvatthapalāśam |
pipīlikāvataśvaso vidyutsvāparṇaśapho gośapho jaritarothāmo daiva ||3||

vīme devā akraṃsatādhvaryo kṣipraṃ pracara |
susatyam id gavām asyasi prakhudasi ||4||

patnī yadṛśyate patnī yakṣyamāṇā jaritarothāmo daiva |
hotā viṣṭīmena jaritar othāmo daiva ||5||

ādityā ha jaritar aṅgirobhyo dakṣiṇām anayan |
tāṃ ha jaritaḥ pratyāyaṃs tām u ha jaritaḥ pratyāyan ||6||

tāṃ ha jaritar naḥ pratyagṛbhṇaṃs tām u ha jaritar naḥ pratyagṛbhṇaḥ |
ahānetarasaṃ na vi cetanāni yajñān etarasaṃ na purogavāmaḥ ||7||

uta śveta āśupatvā uto padyābhir yaviṣṭhaḥ |
utem āśu mānaṃ piparti ||8||

ādityā rudrā vasavas tvenu ta idaṃ rādhaḥ prati gṛbhṇīhy aṅgiraḥ |
idaṃ rādho vibhu prabhu idaṃ rādho bṛhat pṛthu ||9||

20,135.10a devā dadatvāsuraṃ tad vo astu sucetanam |
20,135.10c yuṣmāṃ astu divedive pratyeva gṛbhāyat ||10||

20,135.11a tvam indra śarmariṇā havyaṃ pārāvatebhyaḥ |
20,135.11c viprāya stuvate vasuvaniṃ duraśravase vaha ||11||

20,135.12a tvam indra kapotāya chinnapakṣāya vañcate |
20,135.12c śyāmākaṃ pakvaṃ pīlu ca vārasmā akṛṇor bahuḥ ||12||

20,135.13a araṃgaro vāvadīti tredhā baddho varatrayā |
20,135.13c irāmaha praśaṃsaty anirām apa sedhati ||13||



yad asyā aṃhubhedyāḥ kṛdhu sthūlam upātasat |
muṣkāvidasyā ejato gośaphe śakulāv iva ||1||

yadā sthūlena pasasāṇau muṣkā upāvadhīt |
viṣvañcā vasyā vardhataḥ sikatāsv eva gardabhau ||2||

yad alpikāsvalpikā karkadhūkevaṣadyate |
vāsantikam iva tejanaṃ yanty avātāya vitpati ||3||

yad devāso lalāmaguṃ praviṣṭīminam āviṣuḥ |
sakulā dediśyate nārī satyasyākṣibhuvo yathā ||4||

mahānagnyatṛpnadvi mokradadasthānāsaran |
śaktikānanā svacamaśakaṃ saktu padyama ||5||

mahānagnyulūkhalam atikrāmanty abravīt |
yathā tava vanaspate niraghnanti tathaiveti ||6||

mahānagnyupa brūte bhraṣṭothāpyabhūbhuvaḥ |
yathaiva te vanaspate pippati tathaiveti ||7||

mahānagnyupa brūte bhraṣṭothāpyabhūbhuvaḥ |
yathā vayo vidāhya svarge namavadahyate ||8||

mahānagnyupa brūte svasāveśitaṃ pasaḥ |
itthaṃ phalasya vṛkṣasya śūrpe śūrpaṃ bhajemahi ||9||

20,136.10a mahānagnī kṛkavākaṃ śamyayā pari dhāvati |
20,136.10c ayaṃ na vidma yo mṛgaḥ śīrṣṇā harati dhāṇikām ||10||

20,136.11a mahānagnī mahānagnaṃ dhāvantam anu dhāvati |
20,136.11c imās tad asya gā rakṣa yabha mām addhyaudanam ||11||

20,136.12a sudevas tvā mahānagnīr babādhate mahataḥ sādhu khodanam |
20,136.12c kusaṃ pīvaro navat ||12||

20,136.13a vaśā dagdhām imāṅguriṃ prasṛjatogrataṃ pare |
20,136.13c mahān vai bhadro yabha mām addhyaudanam ||13||

20,136.14a videvas tvā mahānagnīr vibādhate mahataḥ sādhu khodanam |
20,136.14c kumārikā piṅgalikā kārda bhasmā ku dhāvati ||14||

20,136.15a mahān vai bhadro bilvo mahān bhadra udumbaraḥ |
20,136.15c mahāṃ abhikta bādhate mahataḥ sādhu khodanam ||15||

20,136.16a yaḥ kumārī piṅgalikā vasantaṃ pīvarī labhet |
20,136.16c tailakuṇḍamimāṅguṣṭhaṃ rodantaṃ śudam uddharet ||16||



yad dha prācīr ajagantoro maṇḍūradhāṇikīḥ |
hatā indrasya śatravaḥ sarve budbudayāśavaḥ ||1||

kapṛn naraḥ kapṛtham ud dadhātana codayata khudata vājasātaye |
niṣṭigryaḥ putram ā cyāvayotaya indraṃ sabādha iha somapītaye ||2||

dadhikrāvṇo akāriṣaṃ jiṣṇor aśvasya vājinaḥ |
surabhi no mukhā karat pra ṇa āyūṃṣi tāriṣat ||3||

sutāso madhumattamāḥ somā indrāya mandinaḥ |
pavitravanto akṣaran devān gachantu vo madāḥ ||4||

indur indrāya pavata iti devāso abruvan |
vācas patir makhasyate viśvasyeśāna ojasā ||5||

sahasradhāraḥ pavate samudro vācamīṅkhayaḥ |
somaḥ patī rayīṇāṃ sakhendrasya divedive ||6||

ava drapso aṃśumatīm atiṣṭhad iyānaḥ kṛṣṇo daśabhiḥ sahasraiḥ |
āvat tam indraḥ śacyā dhamantam apa snehitīr nṛmaṇā adhatta ||7||

drapsam apaśyaṃ viṣuṇe carantam upahvare nadyo aṃśumatyāḥ |
nabho na kṛṣṇam avatasthivāṃsam iṣyāmi vo vṛṣaṇo yudhyatājau ||8||

adha drapso aṃśumatyā upasthe 'dhārayat tanvaṃ titviṣāṇaḥ |
viśo adevīr abhy ācarantīr bṛhaspatinā yujendraḥ sasāhe ||9||

20,137.10a tvaṃ ha tyat saptabhyo jāyamāno 'śatrubhyo abhavaḥ śatrur indra |
20,137.10c gūlhe dyāvāpṛthivī anv avindo vibhumadbhyo bhuvanebhyo raṇaṃ dhāḥ ||10||

20,137.11a tvaṃ ha tyad apratimānam ojo vajreṇa vajrin dhṛṣito jaghantha |
20,137.11c tvaṃ śuṣṇasyāvātiro vadhatrais tvaṃ gā indra śacyed avindaḥ ||11||

20,137.12a tam indraṃ vājayāmasi mahe vṛtrāya hantave |
20,137.12c sa vṛṣā vṛṣabho bhuvat ||12||

20,137.13a indraḥ sa dāmane kṛta ojiṣṭhaḥ sa made hitaḥ |
20,137.13c dyumnī ślokī sa somyaḥ ||13||

20,137.14a girā vajro na saṃbhṛtaḥ sabalo anapacyutaḥ |
20,137.14c vavakṣa ṛṣvo astṛtaḥ ||14||



mahāṃ indro ya ojasā parjanyo vṛṣṭimāṃ iva |
stomair vatsasya vāvṛdhe ||1||

prajām ṛtasya piprataḥ pra yad bharanta vahnayaḥ |
viprā ṛtasya vāhasā ||2||

kaṇvāḥ indraṃ yad akrata stomair yajñasya sādhanam |
jāmi bruvata āyudham ||3||



ā nūnam aśvinā yuvaṃ vatsasya gantam avase |
prāsmai yachatam avṛkam pṛthu chardir yuyutaṃ yā arātayaḥ ||1||

yad antarikṣe yad divi yat pañca mānuṣāṃ anu |
nṛmnaṃ tad dhattam aśvinā ||2||

ye vām daṃsāṃsy aśvinā viprāsaḥ parimāmṛśuḥ |
evet kāṇvasya bodhatam ||3||

ayaṃ vāṃ gharmo aśvinā stomena pari ṣicyate |
ayaṃ somo madhumān vājinīvasū yena vṛtraṃ ciketathaḥ ||4||

yad apsu yad vanaspatau yad oṣadhīṣu purudaṃsasā kṛtam |
tena māviṣṭam aśvinā ||5||



yan nāsatyā bhuraṇyatho yad vā deva bhiṣajyathaḥ |
ayaṃ vāṃ vatso matibhir na vindhate haviṣmantaṃ hi gachathaḥ ||1||

ā nūnam aśvinor ṛṣi stomaṃ ciketa vāmayā |
ā somaṃ madhumattamaṃ gharmaṃ siñcād atharvaṇi ||2||

ā nūnaṃ raghuvartaniṃ rathaṃ tiṣṭhātho aśvinā |
ā vāṃ stomā ime mama nabho na cucyavīrata ||3||

yad adya vāṃ nāsatyokthair ācucyuvīmahi |
yad vā vāṇībhir aśvinevet kaṇvasya bodhatam ||4||

yad vāṃ kakṣīvāṃ uta yad vyaśva ṛṣir yad vāṃ dīrghatamā juhāva |
pṛthī yad vāṃ vainyaḥ sādaneṣv eved ato aśvinā cetayethām ||5||



yātaṃ chardiṣpā uta paraspā bhūtaṃ jagatpā uta nas tanūpā |
vartis tokāya tanayāya yātam ||1||

yad indreṇa sarathaṃ yātho aśvinā yad vā vāyunā bhavathaḥ samokasā |
yad ādityebhir ṛbhubhiḥ sajoṣasā yad vā viṣṇor vikramaṇeṣu tiṣṭhathaḥ ||2||

yad adyāśvināv ahaṃ huveya vājasātaye |
yat pṛtsu turvaṇe sanas tac chreṣṭham aśvinor avaḥ ||3||

ā nūnaṃ yātam aśvinemā havyāni vāṃ hitā |
ime somāso adhi turvaśe yadāv ime kaṇveṣu vām atha ||4||

yan nāsatyā parāke arvāke asti bheṣajam |
tena nūnaṃ vimadāya pracetasā chardir vatsāya yachatam ||5||



abhutsy u pra devyā sākaṃ vācāham aśvinoḥ |
vy āvar devy ā matiṃ vi rātiṃ martyebhyaḥ ||1||

pra bodhayoṣo aśvinā pra devi sūnṛte mahi |
pra yajñahotar ānuṣak pra madāya śravo bṛhat ||2||

yad uṣo yāsi bhānunā saṃ sūryeṇa rocase |
ā hāyam aśvino ratho vartir yāti nṛpāyyam ||3||

yad āpītāso aṃśavo gāvo na duhra ūdhabhiḥ |
yad vā vāṇīr anuṣata pra devayanto aśvinā ||4||

pra dyumnāya pra śavase pra nṛṣāhyāya śarmaṇe |
pra dakṣāya pracetasā ||5||

yan nūnaṃ dhībhir aśvinā pitur yonā niṣīdathaḥ |
yad vā sumnebhir ukthyā ||6||



taṃ vāṃ rathaṃ vayam adyā huvema pṛthujrayam aśvinā saṃgatiṃ goḥ |
yaḥ sūryāṃ vahati vandhurāyur girvāhasaṃ purutamaṃ vasūyum ||1||

yuvaṃ śriyam aśvinā devatā tāṃ divo napātā vanathaḥ śacībhiḥ |
yuvor vapur abhi pṛkṣaḥ sacante vahanti yat kakuhāso rathe vām ||2||

ko vām adyā karate rātahavya ūtaye vā sutapeyāya vārkaiḥ |
ṛtasya vā vanuṣe pūrvyāya namo yemāno aśvinā vavartat ||3||

hiraṇyayena purubhū rathenemaṃ yajñaṃ nāsatyopa yātam |
pibātha in madhunaḥ somyasya dadhatho ratnaṃ vidhate janāya ||4||

ā no yātaṃ divo acha pṛthivyā hiraṇyayena suvṛtā rathena |
mā vām anye ni yaman devayantaḥ saṃ yad dade nābhiḥ pūrvyā vām ||5||

nū no rayiṃ puruvīraṃ bṛhantaṃ dasrā mimāthām ubhayeṣv asme |
naro yad vām aśvinā stomam āvant sadhastutim ājamīlhāso agman ||6||

iheha yad vāṃ samanā papṛkṣe seyam asme sumatir vājaratnā |
uruṣyataṃ jaritāraṃ yuvaṃ ha śritaḥ kāmo nāsatyā yuvadrik ||7||

madhumatīr oṣadhīr dyāva āpo madhuman no bhavatv antarikṣam |
kṣetrasya patir madhumān no astv ariṣyanto anv enaṃ carema ||8||

panāyyaṃ tad aśvinā kṛtaṃ vāṃ vṛṣabho divo rajasaḥ pṛthivyāḥ |
sahasraṃ śaṃsā uta ye gaviṣṭau sarvāṃ it tāṃ upa yātā pibadhyai ||9||
